# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Accurate identification and measurement of the precipitate area by two-stage deep neural networks in novel chromium-based alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22112)
*Zeyu Xia,Kan Ma,Sibo Cheng,Thomas Blackburn,Ziling Peng,Kewei Zhu,Weihang Zhang,Dunhui Xiao,Alexander J Knowles,Rossella Arcucci*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出 DT-SegNet，一种基于 YOLOv5 和 SegFormer 的两阶段深度学习方案，用于从电子显微镜图像中高效测量铬基高温合金的析出相体积分数与尺寸分布，在多项指标上显著优于 Weka 和 ilastik 等现有分割工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统固定阈值图像处理方法对背景噪声敏感、跨材料泛化能力差且需要大量手动测量，难以满足铬基超合金（chromium-based superalloy）显微结构高效表征的需求；因此需要一种自动、鲁棒的图像分割方案。

Method: 提出 DT-SegNet，一种端到端两阶段深度学习方案：第一阶段基于 YOLOv5 进行目标检测，利用卷积神经网络（convolutional neural network, CNN）的训练效率；第二阶段基于 SegFormer 进行分割，利用视觉 Transformer（Vision Transformer, ViT）的分割精度。

Result: 数值实验表明，DT-SegNet 在准确率（accuracy）、精确率（precision）、召回率（recall）和 F1 分数（F1-score）等指标上显著优于 Weka 和 ilastik 等现有先进分割工具。

Conclusion: DT-SegNet 为合金开发中的显微结构检验提供了有效工具，有助于处理高通量合金开发中产生的大规模数据集。

Abstract: The performance of advanced materials for extreme environments is underpinned by their microstructure, including the size and distribution of reinforcing phases. Chromium-based superalloys are a recently proposed alternative to conventional face-centred-cubic superalloys for high-temperature applications, such as Concentrated Solar Power, and their development requires efficient measurement of precipitate volume fraction and size distribution from electron microscopy images. Traditional fixed-threshold image processing is sensitive to background noise, generalises poorly across materials, and requires substantial manual measurement effort. To address these bottlenecks, this study proposes DT-SegNet, an end-to-end two-stage deep learning scheme based on YOLOv5 and SegFormer for object detection and segmentation in electron microscopy images. The approach combines the training efficiency of convolutional neural networks at the detection stage with the segmentation accuracy of a Vision Transformer. Numerical experiments show that DT-SegNet substantially outperforms state-of-the-art segmentation tools offered by Weka and ilastik across metrics including accuracy, precision, recall, and F1-score. The model provides a useful tool for alloy-development microstructure examinations and helps address the large datasets associated with high-throughput alloy development.

</details>

# physics.plasm-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Geometric numerical discretization of a quasineutral hybrid model of drift-kinetic electrons and fully kinetic ions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21423)
*Nishant Narechania,Guo Meng,Emil Poulsen,Eric Sonnendruecker*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文在几何电磁粒子网格（GEM polymeric PIC）框架GEMPICX的基础上，将其扩展至求解准中性混合Vlasov-Maxwell方程，其中电子采用漂移动力学（drift-kinetic）描述、离子采用完全动力学（fully kinetic）描述。通过引入对偶网格（dual grids）的结构保持有限差分法，推导了该混合模型的离散作用量原理。由于准中性混合模型的动力学系统不显式包含电场的时间演化项，因此平行于背景磁场的电场分量通过隐式求解curl-curl方程获得，垂直分量则基于准中性Ampère方程（不含位移电流）和漂移动力学模型中的电流定义得到。离散后的电场方程构成大规模稀疏线性系统。研究者测试了全显式时间推进方案以及两种隐式-显式（IMEX）方案，并通过验证色散关系中的各类波动模态对数值模型进行了确认。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GEMPICX框架局限于求解传统电磁粒子网格模型，尚未能处理等离子体物理中常见的准中性混合模型（drift-kinetic电子与fully kinetic离子），而该模型在描述低频等离子体现象时具有重要应用价值。

Method: 采用对偶网格上的结构保持有限差分法，构建混合模型的离散作用量原理；对平行电场分量隐式求解curl-curl方程，对垂直电场分量使用不含位移电流的准中性Ampère方程；测试全显式及两种IMEX时间推进方案。

Result: 离散后的电场方程构成大规模稀疏线性系统；通过验证色散关系中的各类波动模态，确认了数值模型的正确性。

Conclusion: 成功将GEMPICX框架扩展至准中性混合Vlasov-Maxwell系统，提出了多套时间推进方案，并通过色散关系验证了模型的准确性，为后续等离子体模拟提供了结构保持的数值工具。

Abstract: We extend the geometric electromagnetic particle-in-cell (PIC) framework, GEMPICX, to solve the quasineutral hybrid Vlasov-Maxwell equations with drift-kinetic electrons and fully kinetic ions. A structure-preserving finite difference method that employs dual grids is used. The discrete action principle for the hybrid model is derived, using the dual nature of the grids. The dynamical system for this hybrid quasineutral model does not explicitly involve the temporal evolution term for the electric field. A curl-curl equation is therefore used to implicitly obtain the component of the electric field that is parallel to the background magnetic field, at every timestep. The perpendicular component of the electric field is obtained using the quasineutral Ampere's equation without the displacement current, combined with the definition of the current in the drift-kinetic model. The discretized versions of the electric field equations are large, sparse linear systems. A fully explicit time-stepping scheme as well as two implicit-explicit (IMEX) schemes are tested. The numerical model is validated by verifying the various waves obtained from the dispersion relation.

</details>

# nucl-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Observation of centrality-dependent dijet transverse momentum imbalance in O+O and Ne+Ne collisions at $\sqrt{s_{NN}}$ = 5.36 TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20463)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: ATLAS实验在5.36 TeV的O+O和Ne+Ne碰撞中观测到了中心度依赖的双喷注横动量失衡现象，该现象与碰撞系统尺寸减小时仍存在的部分子能量损失效应一致，为喷注淬火（jet quenching）的路径长度依赖性和夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）在小核碰撞系统中的起始研究建立了新的实验平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在小于Pb+Pb和Xe+Xe的核碰撞系统中是否仍存在介质诱导的部分子能量损失效应，并检验喷注淬火（jet quenching）现象是否在更小的碰撞系统（如O+O和Ne+Ne）中持续出现。

Method: 基于2025年收集的8.0 nb$^{-1}$ O+O数据、1.0 nb$^{-1}$ Ne+Ne数据以及386 pb$^{-1}$ pp参考数据，在5.36 TeV核子-核子质心系能量下，测量双喷注（dijet）的动量平衡比率x_J（次领头喷注横动量与领头喷注横动量之比）随碰撞中心度的分布。

Result: 对于反方位角背对背（azimuthally back-to-back）的双喷注事件，自归一化的x_J分布随碰撞中心度增加而逐渐偏离pp参考结果，且该中心度依赖性与介质诱导的部分子能量损失模型定性一致，表明在远小于Pb+Pb和Xe+Xe的O+O和Ne+Ne系统中仍存在喷注淬火效应。

Conclusion: 这些结果为研究喷注淬火的路径长度依赖性提供了新工具，并有助于约束夸克-胶子等离子体（QGP）效应在小核碰撞系统中的起始条件，拓展了相对论性重离子碰撞中介质效应的研究范围。

Abstract: The ATLAS experiment presents an observation of a centrality-dependent dijet transverse momentum imbalance in O+O and Ne+Ne collisions at a nucleon-nucleon center-of-mass energy of 5.36 TeV at the Large Hadron Collider. The measurement uses 8.0 nb$^{-1}$ of O+O and 1.0 nb$^{-1}$ of Ne+Ne data collected in 2025, together with 386 pb$^{-1}$ of \textit{pp} data at the same energy used as a reference. The dijet momentum balance is quantified using the ratio of the sub-leading jet transverse momentum to that of the leading jet, $x_J$. For dijets produced azimuthally back-to-back, the self-normalized $x_J$ distributions exhibit increasingly large deviations from the \textit{pp} reference as collisions become more central, corresponding to an increasing overlap of the colliding nuclei. The observed centrality dependence is consistent with medium-induced partonic energy loss in O+O and Ne+Ne collisions, demonstrating that such effects persist in collision systems considerably smaller than Pb+Pb and Xe+Xe. These results establish a new regime for investigating the path-length dependence of jet quenching and constrain the onset of quark-gluon plasma effects in small nuclear collision systems.

</details>

# cond-mat.mes-hall [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Scanning-probe quantum sensing of microwave and static magnetic field response of an on-chip superconducting resonator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20904)
*Senlei Li,Jingcheng Zhou,Zelong Xiong,Hanyi Lu,Hailong Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文引入扫描探针量子显微镜（scanning-probe quantum microscopy），在纳米尺度上对片上铌（Nb）超导谐振器（superconducting resonator）的微波和静磁场环境进行传感。利用拉比振荡（Rabi oscillation）测量，展示了超导谐振器模式产生的微波磁场可用于实现量子自旋传感器的相干控制，并进一步可视化了静电磁场响应下的超导涡旋（superconducting vortex）形成、演化与脱钉过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导谐振器在先进量子电路（如传感、计量和计算）中的应用日益广泛，但其微观电磁性质的详细认知直接关系到电路设计与器件性能的进一步改进，因此需要发展能够在纳米尺度表征其电磁环境的方法。

Method: 引入扫描探针量子显微镜，利用片上铌超导谐振器模式产生的微波磁场，结合拉比振荡测量，实现对量子自旋传感器的相干控制；同时通过该探针可视化静电磁场响应下超导涡旋的形成、演化与脱钉过程。

Result: 成功在纳米尺度上传感了超导谐振器周围的微波和静磁场环境；演示了利用谐振器微波模式对量子自旋传感器进行相干控制；并可视化了磁场诱导的超导涡旋的动态行为。

Conclusion: 研究结果为固态超导谐振器的未来设计、测试与评估提供了洞察，凸显了量子传感器作为局域探针来研究超导量子电路电磁性质的潜力。

Abstract: Superconducting resonators are finding increasing applications in designing advanced quantum circuits for ongoing sensing, metrology, and computing technological revolution. A detailed knowledge of microscopic electromagnetic properties of superconducting resonators is directly relevant for their further improvements on circuitry design and device performance. Here, we introduce scanning-probe quantum microscopy to report nanoscale sensing of microwave and static magnetic field environment of an on-chip niobium (Nb) superconducting resonator. Taking advantage of Rabi oscillation measurements, we show that microwave magnetic fields generated by the superconducting resonator mode can be utilized to achieve coherent control of a quantum spin sensor. We further visualize static electromagnetic field response of the Nb resonator, showing magnetic field-induced formation, evolution, and depinning of superconducting vortices. Our results provide insights into future design, testing and evaluation of solid-state superconducting resonators, highlighting the potential of quantum sensors as a local probe to investigate electromagnetic properties of superconducting quantum circuits.

</details>


### [5] [Observation of Berry curvature fluctuations from incipient polar order in an oxide interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20949)
*S. Avraham,D. Gitman,P. Matus,S. Sandik,E. Raz,S. Jana,M. Dahan,T. Holder,Y. Dagan*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用KTaO₃氧化物界面，发现二阶非线性电阻率存在宏观尺度（200 μm）的介观涨落（mesoscopic fluctuations），并证明其源于界面杂质钉扎的局域铁电极化导致的结构对称性破缺。该工作将量子几何（quantum geometry）与动态晶格有序联系起来，建立了非线性介观输运（nonlinear mesoscopic transport）作为探测隐藏局域有序的新型表征工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 诊断埋藏界面处的隐藏局域有序（hidden local orders）是量子材料设计与表征的核心难题。线性输运无法探测反转对称性破缺项，而二阶电响应（如非线性霍尔效应）可通过布洛赫电子的量子几何直接揭示纳米尺度环境中的此类信息。

Method: 以KTaO₃为研究对象——该材料具有强钽5d自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）和界面反转对称性破缺（interfacial inversion symmetry breaking）。通过测量二次谐波电阻率（second-harmonic resistivities），分析其在宏观尺度器件中的介观涨落行为，并结合温度依赖与热循环实验验证机制。

Result: 二次谐波电阻率表现出大而可重复的介观涨落，该涨落在宏观尺寸（200 μm）器件中依然存在，且在所有研究的表面取向上普遍出现，即使宏观电导严格遵循晶格对称性。信号在10 K以上因相位退相干（phase decoherence）被抑制，超过40 K的热循环则完全消除介观记忆（mesoscopic memory）。

Conclusion: 这些稳健的磁场驱动干涉图案源于局域结构对称性破缺，由钉扎在界面杂质环境中的初生铁电极化（incipient ferroelectric polarization）驱动。非线性介观输运可揭示传统探测手段无法看到的局域极化倾向与隐藏结构有序，成为复杂材料表征的有力新工具。

Abstract: Diagnosing hidden local orders at buried interfaces remains a central challenge in the design and characterization of quantum materials. Second-order electrical responses, such as the nonlinear Hall effect, probe inversion-symmetry-breaking terms invisible to linear transport, offering a direct window into these nanoscale environments via the quantum geometry of Bloch electrons. Here, we utilize $\text{KTaO}_3$, a complex oxide driven by strong tantalum $5d$ spin-orbit coupling and interfacial inversion symmetry breaking, to demonstrate that second-harmonic resistivities exhibit large, reproducible mesoscopic fluctuations. Remarkably, these fluctuations persist in macroscopically large ($200\,μ\text{m}$) devices and are ubiquitous across all studied surface orientations, even where macroscopic conductivity strictly adheres to underlying crystal symmetries. We propose that these robust, magnetic-field-driven interference patterns arise from local structural symmetry breaking, driven by incipient ferroelectric polarization pinned to the interfacial impurity landscape. This defect-pinned polar mechanism is firmly supported by the signal's suppression above $10\text{ K}$ due to phase decoherence, and a complete loss of mesoscopic memory upon thermal cycling above $40\text{ K}$. By linking quantum geometry to dynamic lattice ordering, our findings establish nonlinear mesoscopic transport as a powerful new characterization tool, capable of revealing local polar tendencies and hidden structural orders in complex materials that remain fundamentally invisible to conventional probes.

</details>


### [6] [Observation and Control of Spontaneous Magnon Emission from Spin Ensembles in 2D Hexagonal Boron Nitride](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20996)
*Ling-Jie Zhou,Jayakrishnan M. P. Nair,Senlei Li,Thomas Poirier,Yiran Zhao,Zelong Xiong,Sumedh Rathi,Jingcheng Zhou,Zhigang Jiang,Hailong Wang,James H. Edgar,Benedetta Flebus,Chunhui Rita Du*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文报道了二维六方氮化硼（hBN）中硼空位中心的自发磁振子发射现象，揭示了一种非常规的量子比特-磁振子偶极耦合通道，并通过理论建模定量描述了该过程及其对自旋关联的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索色心（color centers）与磁性材料组成的混合系统中光活性自旋缺陷与量子自由度之间的新型耦合机制，以推动量子技术的发展。

Method: 实验观测二维六方氮化硼（hBN）中硼空位（boron-vacancy）中心的自发磁振子发射（spontaneous magnon emission）；通过改变温度和自旋缺陷密度，研究其与热磁振子效应的竞争以及对自旋关联的影响；结合详细理论建模进行定量分析。

Result: 观察到从发射主导的有效冷磁振子库到热占据自旋浴的交叉行为；增加自旋缺陷密度后，自发磁振子发射有助于在稠密hBN自旋系综中建立量子关联。

Conclusion: 实验结果被理论建模定量捕捉，为理解量子比特-磁振子耦合、关联自旋动力学以及色心在多体量子体系中的物理提供了新见解。

Abstract: Hybrid systems consisting of color centers and magnetic materials provide an appealing solid-state platform for advancing the burgeoning quantum technological revolution. Exploring novel coupling mechanisms between optically active spin defects and quantum degrees of freedom is directly relevant in this context. Here, we report observation and control of spontaneous magnon emission from boron-vacancy centers in 2D hexagonal boron nitride (hBN), an unconventional qubit-magnon dipole coupling channel that dominates in the near-zero temperature limit. The spontaneous magnon emission process starts to be overshadowed by thermal magnon effect as temperature increases, reflecting the crossover from an emission-dominated, effectively cold magnon reservoir to a thermally occupied spin bath where absorption and stimulated processes restore balance. By increasing the spin defect density, we further present that spontaneous magnon emission into a common spin bath could help establish quantum correlations in dense hBN spin ensembles. Our results are quantitatively captured by detailed theoretical modeling, bringing insights into understanding qubit-magnon coupling, correlated spin dynamics, and many-body physics of color centers in the quantum regime.

</details>


### [7] [Electrically Programmable Correlated Topology and Magnetism in a Moiré Trilayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21004)
*Christiano Wang Beach,Courtney Baier,Kaijie Yang,Huiyuan Zheng,Yueyao Fan,Weijie Li,Shuai Yuan,Yifan Zhao,Yue Sun,Chaowei Hu,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Jiun-haw Chu,Liang Fu,Ting Cao,Satoshi Okamoto,Di Xiao,Xiaodong Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在交替扭曲三层MoTe₂中实现了一种电可编程的量子多体系统，通过面外位移场连续调控莫尔能带的层极化、有效晶格和拓扑性质，在单一平台上同时实现了关联磁性与拓扑态（整数和分数量子陈绝缘体）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强电子-电子相互作用是多种量子多体现象（如磁性、超导和电荷分数化）的基础，但亟需在单一平台内实现对晶格几何、带宽和能带拓扑的原位（in situ）控制。

Method: 利用交替扭曲三层MoTe₂材料，通过施加垂直于平面的位移场（displacement field）连续调节层极化、有效晶格和莫尔能带（moiré bands）的拓扑结构。

Result: 零位移场下形成三角晶格，在每个莫尔原胞一个空穴（ν=-1）处出现关联绝缘体；掺杂该态后产生不对称磁响应：|ν|>1时出现双交换类铁磁性，|ν|<1时出现自旋极化子和反铁磁性特征。大位移场下，层间杂化将电子结构重构为具有平坦陈能带（flat Chern band）的蜂窝晶格，支持整数和分数量子陈绝缘体。磁光测量进一步揭示了两个区域交叉点附近的自旋极化费米面能隙闭合和朗道能级形成特征。

Conclusion: 建立了统一的电可调谐平台，使得关联磁性和拓扑态能够从单一可控能带结构中涌现出来。

Abstract: Strong electron-electron interactions underlie a wide range of quantum many-body phenomena, including magnetism, superconductivity, and charge fractionalization. A central goal is to achieve in situ control over lattice geometry, bandwidth, and band topology within a single platform. Here we realize such an electrically programmable quantum many-body system in an alternating twisted trilayer MoTe$_2$, where an out-of-plane displacement field continuously modifies the layer polarization, effective lattice, and topology of the moiré bands. At zero displacement field, the system realizes a triangular lattice hosting a correlated insulator at one hole per moiré unit cell ($ν= -1$). Doping this state produces strongly asymmetric magnetic responses: double-exchange-like ferromagnetism for $|ν| > 1$, and signatures of spin polarons and antiferromagnetism for $|ν| < 1$. At large displacement field, interlayer hybridization reconstructs the electronic structure into a honeycomb lattice with a flat Chern band, supporting integer and fractional Chern insulators. Magneto-optical measurements further reveal the signatures of gap closure and Landau-level formation from a spin-polarized Fermi surface near the crossover between the two regimes. These results establish a unified, electrically tunable platform in which correlated magnetism and topological states emerge from a single controllable band structure.

</details>


### [8] [Mechanically Exfoliated Metallic Delafossite PdCoO2 Nanomembranes: Quantum Transport and Electrical Evaluation Toward Interconnect Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21057)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 制备单晶PdCoO2纳米膜（nanomembranes），在低温下对不同磁场方向测量Shubnikov-de Haas振荡和Aharonov-Bohm振荡，并评估其互连应用相关的电学性能。

Result: 在准二维（quasi two-dimensional）体系中观测到Shubnikov-de Haas和Aharonov-Bohm振荡，提取了电子有效质量（electron effective mass）和电子相位相干长度（electron phase coherence length）。40 nm厚薄片的室温电阻率近乎与厚度无关；击穿电流密度（breakdown current density）高达113 MA cm⁻²，并展现出优异的热稳定性和电迁移抗性（electromigration resistance）。

Abstract: Metallic delafossite oxides have drawn attention for their ultralow resistivity and coherent electronic transport. However, mesoscopic transport studies are hindered by the limited access to high quality nanoscale devices. Here, we report single crystalline PdCoO2 nanomembranes, enabling exploration of quasi two dimensional (2D) transport. Shubnikov de Haas and Aharonov Bohm oscillations under different magnetic field orientations are observed at low temperatures, from which the electron effective mass and electron phase coherence length are extracted. Beyond quantum transport, the electrical performance of PdCoO2 toward interconnect applications is evaluated. A nearly thickness independent room temperature resistivity is observed for flakes down to 40 nm thickness. The nanomembranes exhibit a breakdown current density up to 113 MA cm-2, with excellent thermal stability and electromigration resistance. These results demonstrate that mechanically exfoliated PdCoO2 flakes preserve the high crystalline and electronic quality of bulk crystals in the quasi-2D limit, providing a useful platform for mesoscopic transport studies and interconnect applications.

### [9] [Propagating edge and interfacial states in corrugated graphene: Robustness and configurability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21065)
*Adel Belayadi,Dawei Zhai,Nancy Sandler*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文展示在周期性应变的图案化衬底石墨烯中，应变诱导的赝磁场（pseudomagnetic field）与位移场控制的标量势（scalar potential）协同作用可形成孤立的窄带（narrow bands）和多能隙结构。部分低能带具有非平凡拓扑性质（谷相反陈数），并在无总陈数的情况下出现稳健的传播性带隙边缘态。基于此，提出了电开关零能隙及可空间重构的拓扑界面态器件架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索通过应变工程（strain engineering）在石墨烯中实现类似莫尔（moiré）电子结构的通用路径，并研究赝磁场与标量势协同作用对能带拓扑和边缘态的影响。

Method: 理论分析周期性应变石墨烯在图案化衬底上的电子结构，研究赝磁场与位移场控制的标量势之间的相互作用，并通过不同纳米带几何构型及分栅结构进行验证。

Result: 应变赝磁场与标量势协同形成孤立窄带和多能隙；低能带具有谷相反陈数；尽管总陈数为零，纳米带中存在传播性带隙边缘态；边缘态在超晶格终止变化和中等无序下保持稳健；分栅结构产生可电压重构的拓扑保护界面态。

Conclusion: 应变超晶格（strain superlattice）为在石墨烯中工程化拓扑电子态和电子输运提供了强大平台。

Abstract: Periodically strained graphene on patterned substrates provides a versatile route to realizing moiré-like electronic structures through strain engineering. Here, we show that the interplay between a strain-induced pseudomagnetic field and a displacement-field-controlled scalar potential enables the formation of isolated narrow bands and multiple energy gaps near charge neutrality and at higher energies. Some of the low-energy bands exhibit nontrivial topology, carrying valley-opposite Chern numbers. Remarkably, despite a vanishing total Chern number, propagating in-gap edge states emerge in a wide range of nanoribbon geometries that preserve valley symmetry. We elucidate the distinct mechanisms responsible for edge states in the zero-energy and higher-energy gaps and demonstrate that they remain robust against variations in superlattice termination and moderate disorder, despite lacking conventional topological protection. Leveraging these properties, we propose device architectures in which an externally applied staggered potential electrically switches the zero-energy gap and its associated edge channels on and off. Furthermore, split-gate geometries generate topologically protected interfacial states that coexist with the edge modes and can be spatially reconfigured by gate voltages. These results establish strain superlattices as a powerful platform for engineering topological electronic states and electronic transport in graphene.

### [10] [Moiré-Enhanced Plasmonics in Non-Hermitian Twisted Bilayer Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21186)
*Andrianos Sygrimis,Giorgos P. Tsironis*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在非厄米（non-Hermitian）框架下研究扭转双层石墨烯（twisted bilayer graphene）中的等离激元激发，发现增益与损耗的工程化调控可减小有效空间阻尼并增强传播长度，同时产生高度局域的横磁近场，但其增强效应依赖于莫尔能带重构、双正交光学矩阵元以及非厄米等离激元极点修正的共同作用，而非单纯添加增益所致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非厄米框架下研究扭转双层石墨烯中的等离激元（plasmonic）激发，探索增益与损耗对等离激元色散、传播长度及场局域性的影响，以揭示非厄米性在莫尔量子材料（moiré quantum materials）等离激元响应中的核心作用机制。

Method: 采用Bistritzer–MacDonald连续模型（Bistritzer–MacDonald continuum model）的非厄米推广，结合用于光导率（optical conductivity）的双正交久保形式（biorthogonal Kubo formalism），计算莫尔电子结构（moiré electronic structure）对活性双层等离激元响应的贡献。

Result: 非厄米性改变了集体激发谱，产生光学与声学等离激元分支（optical and acoustic plasmon branches），其中声学分支表现出强亚波长束缚（subwavelength confinement）。在宇称-时间对称（parity-time-symmetric）构型下，增益-损耗工程可减小有效空间阻尼并增强传播长度，同时产生强局域化的横磁（transverse-magnetic）近场。

Conclusion: 增强效应并非单纯添加增益的结果，而是莫尔能带重构、双正交光学矩阵元及非厄米等离激元极点修正共同作用的产物。尽管受无序、衬底损耗、增益饱和及宇称-时间对称稳定性等限制，扭转双层石墨烯仍为可调谐非厄米等离激元学（non-Hermitian plasmonics）提供了一个有前景但实验要求苛刻的平台。

Abstract: We study plasmonic excitations in twisted bilayer graphene within a non-Hermitian framework that incorporates effective gain and loss. Using a non-Hermitian extension of the Bistritzer--MacDonald continuum model together with a biorthogonal Kubo formalism for the optical conductivity, we determine how the moiré electronic structure enters the plasmonic response of the active bilayer. We find that non-Hermiticity modifies the collective spectrum, yielding optical and acoustic plasmon branches, with the acoustic branch exhibiting strong subwavelength confinement. In the parity-time-symmetric configuration, gain--loss engineering can reduce the effective spatial damping and enhance the propagation length within the ideal linear model. The same regime produces strongly localized transverse-magnetic near fields. We argue that the enhancement is not a generic consequence of adding gain to a bilayer, but results from the combined influence of moiré-band reconstruction, biorthogonal optical matrix elements, and non-Hermitian modification of the plasmon pole. We also discuss the limitations imposed by disorder, substrate loss, gain saturation, and stability of the parity-time-symmetric regime. These results identify twisted bilayer graphene as a promising, but experimentally demanding, platform for tunable non-Hermitian plasmonics in moiré quantum materials.

### [11] [Bose-Einstein Condensation of Three-Dimensional Exciton-Polaritons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21219)
*Junhui Cao,Alexey Kavokin*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发展了一套基于能带结构（band-structure-based）的理论，研究掺杂半导体量子点的三维反蛋白石光子晶体（inverse-opal photonic crystal）中的激子-极化激元（exciton-polariton）。研究发现下极化激元带（lower-polariton band）的W点全局最小和X点鞍点（saddle point）分别决定了平衡态玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose-Einstein condensation）阈值和临界温度的重整化。通过调谐激子共振和光-物质耦合，可以实现W-X相对序的重构，进而显著改变临界温度。基于动量分辨的玻尔兹曼模型（Boltzmann model）的非共振泵浦动力学模拟表明，在非平衡驱动-耗散条件下，可以出现W主导凝聚、混合W-X区域或X主导非平衡相干态等多种行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维光子晶体中的极化激元凝聚为研究能带几何（valley geometry）、范霍夫增强相空间（van-Hove-enhanced phase space）和弛豫路径对凝聚控制的综合影响提供了一个尚未充分探索的平台，本工作旨在建立相应的理论框架。

Method: 从对称性选择的光子带隙边缘附近的明亮光子分支出发，构建激子-光子哈密顿量（exciton-photon Hamiltonian），获得下极化激元带；进一步建立动量分辨的玻尔兹曼模型来描述驱动-耗散动力学，并求解平衡态和非平衡条件下的凝聚特性。

Result: 下极化激元带在W点具有全局最小，在X点附近存在范霍夫增强态密度（van-Hove-enhanced density of states）；W谷决定平衡态凝聚阈值，X点鞍点提供有限激发态容量，当W-X能量偏移热可及时重整化临界温度；调谐激子共振与耦合强度可重构W-X相对序，导致临界温度显著变化；非共振泵浦下，储层注入、辐射衰减和区间弛豫可产生W主导、混合W-X或X主导的非平衡相干态。

Conclusion: 三维光子晶体极化激元是一个凝聚受能带最小、谷几何、范霍夫增强相空间和弛豫路径共同调控的平台，为实现多维度操控极化激元凝聚提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We develop a band-structure-based theory of exciton-polaritons in a three-dimensional inverse-opal photonic crystal doped with semiconductor quantum dots. Starting from a symmetry-selected bright photonic branch near the photonic gap edge, we construct an exciton-photon Hamiltonian and obtain a lower-polariton band with a W-point global minimum and a nearby X-point van-Hove-enhanced density of states. We show that the W valleys determine the equilibrium Bose-Einstein condensation threshold, while the X-point saddle provides a finite excited-state capacity that renormalizes the critical temperature when the W-X offset is thermally accessible. By tuning the exciton resonance and the light-matter coupling, the relative W-X ordering can be reconstructed, leading to a strong variation of the critical temperature. We further formulate a momentum-resolved Boltzmann model for driven-dissipative kinetics. Under non-resonant pumping, reservoir feeding, radiative decay, and inter-sector relaxation can produce either W-dominated condensation, a mixed W-X regime, or an X-dominated nonequilibrium coherent state. Our results establish three-dimensional photonic-crystal polaritons as a platform where condensation is controlled not only by the band minimum but also by valley geometry, van-Hove-enhanced phase space, and relaxation pathways.

### [12] [In-plane and out-of-plane magnetic field driven Josephson diode effect in magic-angle twisted four-layer graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21229)
*Marta Perego,Sayan Banerjee,Mohamad Abu El Hija,Clara Galante Agero,Alexandra Mestre-Torà,Giovanni Zhang,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Mathias S. Scheurer,Thomas Ihn,Klaus Ensslin*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在零面外磁场下，随着面内磁场增大，四层扭曲石墨烯结中出现了二极管效应。该效应表明存在强面内轨道耦合（in-plane orbital coupling），且该耦合对结构的层数奇偶性高度敏感。

Conclusion: 这些实验结果为偶数层扭曲石墨烯的对称性破缺机制（symmetry-breaking mechanisms）提供了新的见解，并确立了面内磁场作为揭示其微观性质的关键实验工具。

Abstract: The superconducting diode effect offers a powerful probe into the fundamental symmetries of quantum materials. Recent studies on twisted graphene diodes have predominantly focused on bilayer or trilayer systems under out-of-plane magnetic fields. Here, we demonstrate both out-of-plane and in-plane driven Josephson diode effects in a magic-angle twisted four-layer graphene junction, i.e., an even number of layers. We observe the emergence of a diode effect at zero out-of-plane field, tuned by an increasing in-plane magnetic field. This result points to the presence of strong in-plane orbital coupling, which is highly sensitive to the specific layer parity of the structure. Our findings provide experimental insights into the symmetry-breaking mechanisms of even-layer twisted graphene, establishing in-plane magnetic fields as a vital tool for unravelling their microscopic properties.

### [13] [Topological Hall Effect in Antiferromagnetic Co doped Fe$_3$GaTe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21254)
*Shyam Raj Karullithodi,Yeonkyu Lee,Vadym Kulichenko,W. Kice Brown,Sang-Eon Lee,Chanyoung Lee,Jinyoung Yun,Gregory T. McCandless,Julia Y. Chan,Jeehoon Kim,Luis Balicas*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过磁化测量、电输运测量和磁力显微镜（MFM），确认了Fe$_{3-x}$Co$_x$GaTe$_2$系列随Co掺杂量$x$和温度变化的完整相图，并观察到拓扑霍尔效应（topological Hall effect）与磁场诱导的手性自旋织构（chiral spin textures）密切相关，暗示了从反铁磁（AFM）斯格明子（skyrmions）向铁磁（FM）斯格明子转变的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Fe$_3$GaTe$_2$作为一种范德瓦尔斯（vdW）铁磁体，其Co替代诱导了反铁磁性（AFM），但该体系中可能存在的拓扑自旋织构及其场致演化尚不清楚。本文旨在通过系统实验确认相图并探索磁场诱导的手性自旋织构行为。

Method: 采用磁化测量（magnetization）和电输运测量（electrical transport measurements）表征Fe$_{3-x}$Co$_x$GaTe$_2$系列随Co含量$x$和温度变化的相图；通过反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect）和拓扑霍尔效应（topological Hall effect）分析磁态演化；并利用磁力显微镜（MFM）观测磁畴结构。

Result: 对于$x \simeq 0.6$的样品，霍尔效应模拟磁化行为，并通过变磁转变（metamagnetic transition）出现反常霍尔响应；低温下在$\mu_0H = 4$ T附近或变磁转变场区观测到显著的拓扑霍尔信号。MFM在反铁磁相中揭示了直径约100–200 nm的近圆形磁畴，分析表明拓扑霍尔效应与磁场诱导的磁畴结构（可能具有手性织构）密切相关。

Conclusion: Co掺杂Fe$_3$GaTe$_2$体系中观测到的现象暗示了反铁磁斯格明子（AFM skyrmions）在磁场下向铁磁斯格明子（FM skyrmions）的演化过程，该材料可能为研究斯格明子的反铁磁-铁磁转变及其对拓扑霍尔效应和斯格明子霍尔效应（skyrmion Hall effect）的影响提供平台。

Abstract: Fe$_3$GaTe$_2$ is van der Waals (vdW) ferromagnet with a Curie temperature $T_C$ ranging from 350 K to 380 K, followed upon cooling by a ferrimagnetic transition near room temperature. Substituting Fe with Co was previously reported to induce antiferromagnetism (AFM) at a Co fraction dependent Neel temperature $T_N$. In this work, we confirm the overall phase diagram of the Fe$_{3-x}$Co$_x$GaTe$_2$ series as a function of $x$ and temperature via magnetization and electrical transport measurements. For $x \simeq 0.6$ the Hall effect is observed to mimic the magnetization as the AF ground state is suppressed by the external magnetic field via a metamagnetic transition, thus displaying an anomalous Hall response. At low temperatures, we also observe a pronounced topological Hall signal peaking at $μ_0H$ = 4 T, or within the metamagnetic transition region of fields. This observation points to the presence of magnetic field-induced chiral spin textures, such as skyrmions upon approaching magnetization saturation. Magnetic force microscopy (MFM) reveals the emergence of nearly circular magnetic domains, with diameters on the order of 100 to 200 nm, within the antiferromagnetic phase. A detailed analysis of the MFM images indicates that the topological Hall effect is closely linked to the field-induced stabilization of magnetic domain structures, likely exhibiting chiral textures. This observation suggests the possible formation of skyrmions already in the AFM phase, i.e., AFM skyrmions, that evolve into ferromagnetic (FM) ones upon increasing the magnetic field. Consequently, Co-doped Fe$_3$GaTe$_2$ might provide a platform to investigate the transformation of skyrmions, initially coupled antiferromagnetically into ferromagnetic skyrmions, and to explore its impact on the topological and skyrmion Hall effects.

### [14] [Spin qubit operations by conveyor-mode shuttling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21452)
*M. De Smet,Y. Matsumoto,D. Fernández-Fernández,L. Tryputen,S. L. de Snoo,D. J. Michalak,H. G. J. Eenink,G. Platero,S. Bosco,G. Scappucci,L. M. K. Vandersypen*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文实验演示了通过传送带模式（conveyor-mode）电子穿梭实现自旋量子比特的单比特和两比特相干控制。两种方法——传送带电偶极自旋共振（conveyor EDSR）和传送带绝热通道（conveyor diabatic gates）——分别利用横向磁场梯度和量子化轴倾斜实现高保真度操控；结合绝热传送与运动控制的交换激活，可产生多种有效两比特相互作用。这些结果推动了可重构、传输驱动的自旋量子比特架构范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动态量子比特布线（dynamic qubit routing）是半导体量子处理器中一个有前景的架构方向，但目前基于传送带模式（conveyor-mode）的电子穿梭主要用于自旋传输，其是否也能直接用于量子比特操控尚未被充分探索。本文旨在验证传送带式穿梭本身是否能够实现单比特和双比特的相干控制。

Method: 采用两种概念不同的方法：1) 传送带电偶极自旋共振（conveyor EDSR），通过让自旋共振地穿梭经过横向磁场梯度，在平均拉莫尔频率（Larmor frequency）下实现高保真旋转；2) 传送带绝热通道（conveyor diabatic gates），利用量子化轴（quantization axis）的倾斜实现可调谐的bang-bang控制。同时，将绝热传送运动与交换激活（exchange activation）结合，通过调节穿梭速度和距离选择不同的两比特相互作用。

Result: 实验成功演示了由传送带模式电子穿梭驱动的相干单比特和两比特控制，包括高保真旋转和多种可选择的相互作用，验证了两种不同原理的实现方式。

Conclusion: 这些实验结果支持一种新的架构范式：可重构的、传输驱动的自旋量子比特（reconfigurable and transport-driven spin qubits），为半导体量子处理器的路径提供了新方向。

Abstract: Dynamic qubit routing is emerging as a promising architectural path for semiconductor quantum processors. Charge carriers can be rapidly moved around on a chip using traveling-wave potentials known as conveyors, preserving the spin state with high fidelity. Originally developed for spin transport, conveyor-mode shuttling may also offer opportunities for performing qubit operations directly controlled by the motion itself. Here, we demonstrate coherent single- and two-qubit control by conveyor-mode electron shuttling, using two conceptually different approaches. First, conveyor electric-dipole spin resonance (conveyor EDSR) achieves high-fidelity rotations by resonantly shuttling spins through transverse magnetic-field gradients at their mean Larmor frequency. Second, conveyor diabatic gates exploit quantization-axis tilts for tunable bang-bang control. Combining diabatic conveyor transport with exchange activation controlled by the motion directly yields a variety of effective two-qubit interactions selectable via the shuttling speed and distance. These experimental results motivate an architectural paradigm of reconfigurable and transport-driven spin qubits.

</details>


### [15] [Hyperfine versus exchange interaction in the spin dynamics of spatially indirect excitons in CsPbI$_{3}$ perovskite nanocrystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21469)
*Timur S. Shamirzaev,Nataliia E. Kopteva,Dmitry S. Smirnov,Dmitri R. Yakovlev,Elena V. Kolobkova,Maria S. Kuznetsova,Eugeniyus L. Ivchenko,Yan E. Maidebura,Evgeny A. Zhukov,Manfred Bayer*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了玻璃基质中CsPbI₃纳米晶（nanocrystals, NCs）内激子的复合动力学、光学取向（optical orientation）和光学对准（optical alignment），并针对三重态激子（triplet excitons）发展了极化光致发光理论，揭示了核自旋涨落主导激子精细结构的新物理机制。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解大尺寸CsPbI₃纳米晶中由空间分离的电子和空穴形成的间接激子（indirect excitons）的复合与自旋动力学，以及电子-空穴交换相互作用（exchange interaction）与超精细相互作用（hyperfine interaction）对激子精细结构的影响。

Method: 实验上，通过光致发光测量研究尺寸超过16 nm的CsPbI₃纳米晶中激子的复合动力学、光学取向与光学对准；理论上，发展了一个包含电子-空穴交换相互作用、塞曼效应（Zeeman effect）和与原子核的超精细相互作用的三重态激子极化光致发光模型。

Result: 大纳米晶中低能光致发光来源于纳米晶/玻璃界面处局域的空间分离电子-空穴对形成的间接激子；其复合动力学从数十纳秒延伸至微秒，呈现幂律依赖（power-law dependence）；光学对准和光学取向表现出由交换相互作用变化数个数量级导致的奇特自旋动力学；对于交换分裂最小的激子，精细结构由随机核自旋涨落所主导。

Conclusion: 所发展的理论模型成功揭示了在交换分裂足够小的激子体系中，超精细相互作用取代交换相互作用成为激子精细结构的主导因素，为理解纳米晶中激子的自旋行为提供了重要理论框架。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of recombination, optical orientation, and optical alignment of excitons in ensembles of CsPbI$_{3}$ nanocrystals (NCs), synthesized in a glass matrix. In large NCs with size exceeding 16 nm, the low-energy photoluminescence is contributed by the emission of indirect in real space excitons formed by spatially separated electrons and holes, which are localized at the NC/glass interface. The recombination dynamics of an ensemble of such excitons extends from tens of nanoseconds to microseconds and exhibits a power-law dependence. Their optical alignment and optical orientation reveal a peculiar spin dynamics caused by excitons influenced by the exchange interaction, varying by orders of magnitude. We develop a theory of the polarized photoluminescence of triplet excitons, taking into account the interplay between the electron-hole exchange interaction, their Zeeman effect, and their hyperfine interaction with the nuclei. This model reveals that for the excitons with the smallest exchange splitting we reach the regime, where the exciton fine structure becomes dominated by the hyperfine interaction with the random nuclear spin fluctuations in the NCs.

### [16] [A thermodynamic uncertainty relation for (hybrid) N--S coherent conductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21555)
*Sergi Vidal,Rosa Lopez*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明了混合正常超导导体中电荷流与熵产生之间的热力学不确定关系（thermodynamic uncertainty relation, TUR），通过将非平衡过剩噪声分解为正定表示，建立了适用于任意超导能隙的混合量子热力学不确定关系，将纯安德烈夫量子TUR推广至准粒子和安德烈夫过程共存区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热力学不确定关系（thermodynamic uncertainty relation, TUR）在非平衡体系中建立了电流涨落与熵产生之间的基本界限。在混合正常超导导体中，输运由准粒子透射（quasiparticle transmission）和安德烈夫反射（Andreev reflection）共同主导，现有理论尚未清晰揭示超导相干性如何在这些共存过程中重塑电流涨落并维持普适的耗散-精度约束。

Method: 采用Anantram-Datta散射形式主义（Anantram Datta scattering formalism），将电荷流和零频率噪声分解为安德烈夫（Andreev）、准粒子（quasiparticle）和干涉（interference）三部分贡献，并通过证明非平衡过剩噪声（nonequilibrium excess noise）允许正定表示，推导混合量子热力学不确定关系。

Result: 尽管干涉项阻止了在单个噪声分量层面建立简单的可加性界限，但非平衡过剩噪声的正定表示使得一个适用于任意实超导能隙（superconducting gap）的混合量子热力学不确定关系得以成立。该结果将纯安德烈夫量子TUR推广至准粒子和安德烈夫过程共存的参数区域。

Conclusion: 超导相干性（superconducting coherence）通过准粒子与安德烈夫过程的共存重塑了电流涨落特性，同时在这些混合量子导体中保留了普适的耗散-精度约束（dissipation-precision constraint）。

Abstract: Thermodynamic uncertainty relations establish fundamental bounds between current fluctuations and entropy production in nonequilibrium systems. In hybrid normal superconducting conductors, transport is governed by the coexistence of quasiparticle transmission and Andreev reflection, where electron hole conversion transfers charge through the superconducting condensate. Using the Anantram Datta scattering formalism, we decompose the charge current and zero-frequency noise into Andreev, quasiparticle, and interference contributions. Although the interference term prevents a simple additive bound at the level of individual noise components, we show that the nonequilibrium excess noise admits a positive representation. This allows us to prove a hybrid quantum thermodynamic uncertainty relation valid for an arbitrary real superconducting gap. Our result extends the pure Andreev quantum TUR to regimes where quasiparticle and Andreev processes coexist, clarifying how superconducting coherence reshapes current fluctuations while preserving a universal dissipation precision constraint in hybrid quantum conductors.

### [17] [Assessing Majorana states and qubits through quantum capacitance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21580)
*Rodrigo A. Dourado,Ramón Aguado,Jeroen Danon,Martin Leijnse,Rubén Seoane Souto*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子电容（QC）已被证明可用于拓扑量子比特中马约拉纳束缚态（MBS）的奇偶性读取；本文旨在进一步拓展QC的探测能力，使其能够同时获取器件的多个关键品质因数。

Method: 采用辅助量子点（QD）作为传感器进行量子电容（QC）测量；利用低能有效模型推导偶宇称和奇宇称两个扇区中QC峰值相对位置与幅值的解析表达式，并结合基于量子点（QD）的Kitaev链和量子比特的微观模型进行验证。

Result: QC测量能够同时解析基态能级分裂和马约拉纳束缚态（MBS）重叠这两个基本品质因数；低能有效模型给出了从辅助量子点（QD）能量相关的偶/奇宇称QC峰值推断上述两个量的解析表达式；微观模型验证了这些结果在多种MBS器件中的适用性。

Conclusion: 量子电容（QC）可作为一种保留费米子奇偶性的探针，用于评估马约拉纳束缚态（MBS）质量并优化拓扑器件。

Abstract: Quantum capacitance (QC) has recently emerged as a promising tool for parity readout in topological qubits based on Majorana bound states (MBSs). Here, we show that this capability can be extended further: by employing an auxiliary quantum dot (QD) as a sensor, we demonstrate that QC measurements simultaneously resolve two fundamental figures of merit of the device, the ground-state energy splitting and the MBS overlap, thus providing direct access to the underlying internal degrees of freedom. Using a low-energy effective model, we provide analytic expressions for these two figures of merit that can be determined from the relative position and magnitude of the QC maxima in the even and odd parity sectors as functions of the auxiliary-QD energy. We further validate these results with a microscopic model of QD-based Kitaev chains and qubits, demonstrating their applicability in a wide range of MBS-based devices. Our results establish QC as a probe of MBS quality and a tool for topological-device optimization that preserves fermion parity.

### [18] [Subgap Linear Thermoelectricity in Superconducting Quantum Hall Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21599)
*Leonardo Pierattelli,Fabio Taddei,Alessandro Romito,Alessandro Braggio*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明，在超导体邻近的整数量子霍尔（integer quantum Hall）系统中，当存在三重态超导关联（triplet superconducting correlations）时，线性响应（linear-response）范围内可以出现亚能隙热电效应（subgap thermoelectric effects）。通过最小化模型设计，实现了由Andreev过程介导的非零塞贝克效应（Seebeck effect），其塞贝克系数在量子霍尔平台中心可达 $k_B/e$ 量级。分析表明，三重态关联与自旋极化（spin polarization）对热电效应的出现均不可或缺，且该效应在边缘态线性色散（linear band dispersion）条件下依然存在。研究还刻画了热电响应随哈密顿量参数及系统温区的依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在超导体邻近的整数量子霍尔系统中，如何利用三重态超导关联（triplet superconducting correlations）在亚能隙区域实现线性响应（linear-response）热电效应。该研究旨在揭示边缘态线性色散（linear band dispersion）条件下热电效应的存在条件，并寻找可观测的塞贝克效应（Seebeck effect）物理机制。

Method: 构建一个最小化（minimal）超导邻近整数量子霍尔（integer quantum Hall）模型，通过引入三重态超导关联（triplet superconducting correlations）并分析Andreev过程（Andreev processes）对热电输运的贡献。采用线性响应（linear-response）框架解析推导（analytically show）塞贝克系数（Seebeck coefficient）的表达式，并系统改变哈密顿量参数与温度范围以刻画热电特性的依赖关系。

Result: 发现该体系中可产生由Andreev过程（Andreev processes）介导的非零塞贝克效应（Seebeck effect），其塞贝克系数（Seebeck coefficient）在量子霍尔平台（quantum Hall plateau）中部可达到 $k_B/e$ 量级。三重态超导关联（triplet superconducting correlations）与自旋极化（spin polarization）两者同时存在是热电效应出现的必要条件；该效应在边缘态线性色散（linear band dispersion）条件下依然成立。

Conclusion: 三重态超导关联（triplet superconducting correlations）与自旋极化（spin polarization）的结合为整数量子霍尔（integer quantum Hall）系统中亚能隙热电效应（subgap thermoelectric effects）提供了可行机制。该发现为在量子霍尔平台区实现高效热电转换提供了理论依据，并揭示了超导关联类型与自旋自由度在低维热电输运中的关键作用。

Abstract: We show that an integer quantum Hall setup proximized by superconductors can exhibit subgap thermoelectric effects in the linear-response regime when triplet superconducting correlations are present. We devise a minimal setup that enables a nonzero Seebeck effect mediated by Andreev processes and predict that the corresponding Seebeck coefficient can reach values on the order of $k_B/e$ in the middle of the quantum Hall plateau. We analytically show that both triplet correlations and spin polarization are essential for the emergence of the thermoelectric effect, which arises despite the linear band dispersion of the edge states. We characterize the dependence of the thermoelectric response on the Hamiltonian parameters and the system's temperature regime.

### [19] [Solid-state transcapacitor, a new gain element for logic, memory and interconnects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21772)
*Amrita Mathuriya,Roza Kotlyar,Neal Reynolds,Rafael Rios,Alan Kalitsov,Peter B. Meisenheimer,James Clarkson,Noriyuki Sato,Tanay Gosavi,Ramamoorthy Ramesh,Dmitri E. Nikonov,Sasikanth Manipatruni*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新型三端逻辑元件——固态跨电容器（transcapacitor, TCAP），通过压电-电机械耦合实现位移电流调制，旨在突破传统晶体管在电压、电流密度和电流调制方面的能量缩放极限，有望实现比终级缩放的CMOS器件低两个数量级的能耗，为超低能耗计算提供新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前晶体管决定了逻辑与存储的电压和电荷尺度，而AI系统的能耗瓶颈主要来自片内互连，其电压与电荷尺度仍由晶体管设定。晶体管在同时满足高电流密度、高电流/阻抗调制和降低电压方面面临根本性挑战，因此亟需一种能降低电压和电荷需求的新型逻辑元件。

Method: 提出一种三端固态跨电容器（solid-state transcapacitor, TCAP），它本质上是一种由栅极控制沟道电荷-电压关系的固态位移电流调制器（displacement current modulator）。具体实现采用压电跨电容器（piezoelectric transcapacitor）结构，通过栅控应力施加器（gate-controlled stressor）经电机械耦合（electromechanical coupling）调制极性沟道的电容。

Result: TCAP元件实现了逻辑所必需的反相（inversion）和增益（gain），同时在功能上等效于1T-1C存储单元，可实现高密度存储。基于TCAP的逻辑通过电压缩放（voltage scaling）、电容性能量回收（capacitive energy recovery）以及极性材料的高极化密度，有望实现比终级缩放的CMOS器件低100倍的能耗，且延迟相当。

Conclusion: TCAP通过消除耗散性输运电流、不受玻尔兹曼电流调制极限（Boltzmann current modulation limit）约束，并以极化响应和接触电阻限制的位移电流工作，可同时克服CMOS在电压、电流密度和电流调制方面的极限。该方案为超越晶体管极限的超低能耗计算提供了一条基于电机械学（electro-mechanics）和多铁性材料（multiferroics）的新潜在路径。

Abstract: Today's transistors dictate the voltage and charge scales for both logic and memory. While AI systems are recognized to be limited by memory energy, the dominant share of the energy is expended in the intrachip interconnects whose voltage and charge scales are set by transistors. The energy scaling challenges of transistors can be attributed to simultaneously meeting high current density, high current/impedance modulation, and the inability to lower voltages. Hence, a new logic element that lowers the voltage and charge needs is a priority, not only for lowering logic power but also memory access power. Here, we propose a novel 3-terminal logic element for low energy computing, a solid-state transcapacitor (TCAP). A TCAP is a solid state displacement current modulator realized by a gate which controls the charge-voltage relationship of the channel. Unlike transistors, TCAPs eliminate the dissipative transport current, are not bound by the Boltzmann current modulation limit, and operate with displacement currents limited only by the polarization response and contact resistance. Hence, TCAP circuits may simultaneously overcome the voltage, current density, and current modulation limits of CMOS. We describe a solid state TCAP using a piezoelectric transcapacitor in which a gate-controlled stressor modulates the capacitance of a polar channel via electromechanical coupling. This device achieves inversion and gain, essential for logic, and is functionally equivalent to a 1T-1C memory cell, enabling dense memory. Using voltage scaling, capacitive energy recovery, and high polarization densities of polar materials, the logic based on TCAP offers a pathway to 100 fold lower energy consumption with a delay comparable to ultimately scaled CMOS devices. This approach provides a new potential pathway for low-energy computing beyond the limits of transistors using electro-mechanics and multiferroics.

</details>


### [20] [Antiferromagnetic pseudospintronics without spin splitting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21860)
*Shu-Hui Zhang,Shu-Qi Liu,Dan-Yang Han,Zhan Kong,Ding-Fu Shao,Wen Yang,Kai Chang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在零自旋分裂的反铁磁体（antiferromagnet）中提出并验证了基于子晶格赝自旋（sublattice pseudospin）的“反铁磁赝自旋电子学”（AFM pseudospintronics）新范式，通过部分赝自旋-自旋耦合实现奈尔矢量（Néel vector）对赝自旋极化的调控，并在全功能反铁磁结中展示了奈尔矢量控制的隧穿磁电阻（tunneling magnetoresistance）效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统反铁磁自旋电子学依赖于自旋分裂（spin splitting），这排除了大量具有补偿自旋子晶格（compensated spin sublattices）的共线反铁磁体。作者旨在利用零自旋分裂反铁磁体中的子晶格自由度，拓展自旋电子学的新物理机制。

Method: 以蜂窝状零自旋分裂反铁磁体为研究对象，通过理论分析揭示自旋与子晶格之间的耦合关系，即面外赝自旋极化（out-of-plane pseudospin polarization）具有自旋依赖性，称为部分赝自旋-自旋耦合（partial pseudospin-spin coupling）。通过反转奈尔矢量实现赝自旋极化切换；在特定子晶格引入杂质产生弗里德尔振荡（Friedel oscillations），其子晶格分辨振幅比由赝自旋极化唯一决定，可用于自旋极化扫描隧道显微镜（spin-polarized scanning tunneling microscopy）测量。

Result: 实现了奈尔矢量控制的电荷传输，并在全功能反铁磁结中观测到大非易失性隧穿磁电阻（large nonvolatile tunneling magnetoresistance），该效应在栅极可调（gate-tunable）二维器件中表现出显著的共振增强。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了反铁磁赝自旋电子学新范式，利用零自旋分裂反铁磁体中的子晶格赝自旋，将自旋电子学扩展至传统自旋分裂范式之外。

Abstract: Antiferromagnets (AFMs) are promising for high-density spintronics due to their zero net magnetization, yet conventional AFM spintronics relies on spin splitting-a requirement that excludes many collinear AFMs with compensated spin sublattices. Here we exploit the sublattice degree of freedom in a honeycomb AFM with zero spin splitting. We uncover a coupling between spin and sublattice: the out-of-plane pseudospin polarization is spin-dependent, a mechanism we term partial pseudospin-spin coupling. This allows switching of the pseudospin polarization by reversing the Néel vector. Introducing an impurity into a specific sublattice induces Friedel oscillations with a sublattice-resolved amplitude ratio dictated solely by the pseudospin polarization, which is directly measurable by spin-polarized scanning tunneling microscopy. Furthermore, we demonstrate Néel-vector-controlled transmission and a large nonvolatile tunneling magnetoresistance in an all-in-one AFM junction, with pronounced resonant enhancement in gate-tunable two-dimensional devices. Our work establishes a new paradigm-AFM pseudospintronics-that utilizes the sublattice pseudospin in zero-spin-splitting AFMs, extending spintronics beyond the conventional spin-splitting paradigm.

</details>


### [21] [Effect of weak positional disorder on the miniband structure of spherical quantum dot chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22128)
*R. Ya. Leshko*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文基于紧束缚近似与有效介质方法，建立了一个理论框架，分析弱位置无序对一维球形量子点链中电子微带结构的影响。通过将随机间距涨落映射为哈密顿量参数的重整化，推导出无序重整化参数的解析表达式，揭示了弱无序导致微带展宽及其随晶格周期增大而减小的敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究弱位置无序（weak positional disorder）对一维球形量子点（quantum dots）链中电子微带（miniband）结构的影响，建立相应的理论框架。

Method: 采用紧束缚近似（tight-binding approximation）结合有效介质方法（effective-medium approach），将点间间距的随机涨落映射为关键哈密顿量参数——跳跃积分（hopping integral $B$）、重叠积分（overlap integral $Q$）和格点能移（on-site energy shift $M$）的重整化（renormalization）。通过对窄高斯分布的位置偏差（$σ\ll a$）进行系综平均，推导出无序重整化参数的解析表达式。

Result: 得到的广义色散关系表明，弱位置无序导致微带展宽。在典型 fabrication 涨落 $σ=0.1\,a$ 下，微带宽度增加 8-12%（依赖于平均点间距 $a$）。同时，微带宽度对无序的敏感性随晶格周期增大而迅速降低，这是由于电子波函数的指数衰减。在考虑的弱无序条件下，安德森局域化长度（Anderson localization length）远大于晶格常数，微带态仍保持退局域化（delocalized）。

Conclusion: 弱位置无序主要引起微带展宽而非导致电子态局域化，因此在该体系的实际器件应用中，微带输运特性对一定程度的 fabrication 缺陷具有鲁棒性。

Abstract: A theoretical framework is developed for the electron miniband structure in one-dimensional chains of spherical quantum dots subjected to weak positional disorder. Within the tight-binding approximation combined with the effective-medium approach, the stochastic fluctuations of the inter-dot spacing are mapped onto the renormalization of the key Hamiltonian parameters: the hopping integral $ B $, the overlap integral $ Q $, and the on-site energy shift $ M $. Analytical expressions for these disorder-renormalized parameters are derived by performing an ensemble average over a narrow Gaussian distribution of positional deviations ($ σ\ll a $). The resulting generalized dispersion relation shows that weak positional disorder causes a broadening of the minibands. Specifically, for typical fabrication fluctuations $σ= 0.1\,a $, the miniband width increases by 8-12\% (depending on the mean inter-dot distance $a$). At the same time, the sensitivity of the miniband width to disorder decreases rapidly with increasing lattice period due to the exponential decay of the electron wave functions. In the considered weak-disorder regime, the Anderson localization length significantly exceeds the lattice constant, so the miniband states remain delocalized.

Abstract: Ferroelectricity is a property of materials that exhibit spontaneous charge polarization. Ferroelectricity in 2D materials is interesting because of their applications in memory devices and field-effect transistors. Recently, a new type of ferroelectricity, known as sliding ferroelectricity, has been discovered, in which parallel-stacked bilayers of hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) or transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDCs) develop an out-of-plane electric polarization. In this work, we probe the polarization of small-angle parallel stacked WSe$_2$ by measuring its high-frequency AC response, achieved by embedding it into a half-wave superconducting coplanar waveguide cavity. We observe a hysteretic response in the capacitance of the stack and quality factor of the cavity, confirming ferroelectric switching in the system. ### [23] [Deterministic control of the probabilistic phase dynamics in injection-locked spin-torque nano-oscillators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22208)
*Abderrazak Hakam,Chloé Chopin,Nhat-Tan Phan,Nicolas Mollard,Franck Badets,Louis Hutin,Luana Benetti,Alex S. Jenkins,Ricardo Ferreira,Ursula Ebels,Philippe Talatchian*

TL;DR: 本文证明，尽管自旋扭矩纳米振荡器（STNO）固有地存在热驱动相位涨落，但其占据各相位态的概率可通过注入锁定和弱射频扰动实现确定性与连续性的编程控制，为概率计算与类脑计算提供了硬件基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋扭矩纳米振荡器（STNO）本质上存在热驱动相位涨落（thermally driven phase fluctuations），导致其动力学呈现真随机性。传统观点认为这种内在随机性难以控制，论文旨在探索能否在这种随机性中实现确定性的概率操控。

Method: 实验基于涡旋型（vortex-based）STNO，工作在二次谐波注入锁定（second-harmonic injection-locking）模式下。通过施加一个自由运行频率（free-running frequency）下的弱射频扰动（weak radio-frequency perturbation），在不抑制涨落的前提下调节两个简并吸引子之间的相位跳跃率（phase-jump rates），实现连续的概率控制。

Result: 实现了从无偏极限到接近0或1的连续概率调控。偏置相位（bias phase）决定偏好哪个吸引子，偏置幅度（bias amplitude）设置不平衡强度，提供了两个互补的控制旋钮。基于有效准势（effective quasipotential）的相位约化描述（phase-reduced description）定量解释了实验结果。

Conclusion: 注入锁定STNO可作为可编程随机单元（programmable stochastic elements），为概率计算（probabilistic computing）、伊辛机（Ising machines）和类脑计算架构（brain-inspired computing architectures）提供硬件原语。

Abstract: Spin-torque nano-oscillators (STNOs) inherently exhibit thermally driven phase fluctuations that render their dynamics truly stochastic. Here, we demonstrate that, despite this intrinsic randomness, the probability of occupying each phase state can be deterministically and continuously programmed. We experimentally investigate a vortex-based STNO operating under second-harmonic injection-locking, where the oscillator phase settles into two degenerate attractors separated by $π$ and undergoes thermally activated phase jumps. By applying a weak radio-frequency perturbation at the free-running frequency, we tune the phase-jump rates between the two attractors without suppressing the fluctuations, achieving continuous probability control from the unbiased limit to values approaching 0 or 1. The bias phase selects which attractor is favored while the bias amplitude sets the strength of the imbalance, providing two complementary control knobs within a single nanoscale device. A phase-reduced description based on an effective quasipotential quantitatively accounts for the observations. These results establish injection-locked STNOs as programmable stochastic elements and provide a hardware primitive for probabilistic computing, Ising machines, and brain-inspired computing architectures.

### [24] [Non-equilibrium angular momentum selectivity and filtering in chiral carbon nanotubes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22235)
*Sergio Shmayev,D. R. da Costa,D. A. Bahamon*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文通过系统研究手性碳纳米管（chiral carbon nanotubes）中的非平衡轨道响应，揭示了轨道埃德尔斯坦磁化率（orbital Edelstein susceptibility）强烈依赖于手性和直径，无法用普适标度律描述；手性碳纳米管还可作为高效的轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum）过滤器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对一系列金属性和半导体性手性碳纳米管的非平衡轨道响应进行了系统性研究；在接触自能（contact self-energy）中引入了角度关联（angular correlations），以分析金属接触对轨道电流产生和轨道选择性的影响。

Result: 轨道埃德尔斯坦磁化率强烈依赖于手性和纳米管直径，无法用普适标度律（universal scaling law）描述；不同碳纳米管家族形成由手性包裹矢量（chiral wrapping vector）唯一确定的特征轨道响应分支。金属性碳纳米管在远离接触区时迅速恢复本征轨道响应，而半导体性碳纳米管则表现出由不同角动量输运通道干涉导致的显著振荡行为。手性碳纳米管可作为高效的轨道角动量过滤器（orbital-angular-momentum filter），根据传播能带的晶体角动量选择性透射轨道纹理化的电子态。

Conclusion: 手性碳纳米管的非平衡轨道响应呈现丰富的家族依赖性结构，且其轨道角动量选择性透射能力使其在轨道电子学（orbitronics）领域具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: Carbon nanotubes (CNTs) constitute a highly tunable platform for probing the interplay between structural chirality and quantum transport in quasi-one-dimensional systems. Here, we perform a systematic study of the non-equilibrium orbital response across a broad set of metallic and semiconducting chiral CNTs. We find that the orbital Edelstein susceptibility depends strongly on both chirality and nanotube diameter, revealing that the orbital response cannot be captured by a universal scaling law. Instead, distinct families of CNTs emerge, forming characteristic orbital-response branches uniquely determined by the chiral wrapping vector. We further investigate the role of metallic contacts on orbital-current generation and orbital selectivity. While metallic CNTs rapidly recover their intrinsic orbital response away from the contact region, semiconducting CNTs display pronounced oscillatory behavior arising from interference between transport channels carrying different angular momenta injected by wide-band metallic contacts. Finally, by incorporating angular correlations into the contact self-energy, we demonstrate that chiral CNTs can operate as efficient orbital-angular-momentum filters, selectively transmitting orbitally textured electronic states in accordance with the crystal angular momentum of the propagating bands.

### [25] [Keldysh field theory of spin- and valley-distinguished polariton nonlinearities in transition-metal dichalcogenide monolayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22242)
*Anna M. Grudinina,Nina S. Voronova*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用路径积分（path integral）形式推导了一个非平衡场论（nonequilibrium field-theory）方法，能够追踪强耦合（strong coupling） regime 下所有极化子非线性效应。

Conclusion: 揭示了自旋暗激子在极化子非线性效应中的关键作用，指出其在能级蓝移中贡献显著高于亮激子，表明谷与自旋自由度对TMD基光子器件的性能有重要影响。

Abstract: Electrons in transition-metal dichalcogenides (TMDs) possess valley and spin degrees of freedom, which leads to rich exciton and exciton-polariton physics with nontrivial scattering dynamics and enhanced nonlinearities, presenting a key mechanism for photonic devices. Yet, existing descriptions of bosonization and polariton interactions in TMD-based systems overlook the valley degree of freedom as well as the various particles' spins combinations. In this work, we derive a nonequilibrium field-theory approach in the path integral formalism that allows to track all the polariton nonlinearities in the strong coupling regime. We demonstrate that, when all the bright and dark exciton species are considered, the TMD monolayer-based polariton systems feature sixteen different nonlinear contributions due to interactions and even more saturation-related terms. Strikingly, while the interactions of excitons within one valley are overall dominant, we show that the contribution to the blueshift from spin-dark excitons is much higher than that from bright intravalley excitons.

### [26] [Second-order dc conductivity in the velocity-gauge Keldysh formalism: gauge-invariant decomposition into nonlinear Drude, Berry-curvature-dipole, and quantum-metric responses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22359)
*Junya Shibata*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在速度规范Keldysh格林函数框架下，推导了多带紧束缚系统中二阶直流非线性电导的规范不变分解，将响应分为四个具有不同寿命标度和物理起源的贡献项，并展示了量子度量偶极子（quantum-metric dipole）可作为独立于贝里曲率偶极子（Berry-curvature dipole）的直流响应机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有二阶非线性直流响应理论中，各贡献项的规范不变性及其与量子几何量（如量子度量和贝里曲率）的关系尚不清晰，需要一种严格的分解方法来区分不同物理起源的贡献，并厘清连接依赖项的抵消机制。

Method: 采用速度规范Keldysh格林函数形式（velocity-gauge Keldysh Green's function formalism），在常数弛豫时间近似下对多带紧束缚系统的二阶直流非线性电导进行规范不变分解；通过能带基展开，明确展示了协变量子连接项（covariant-quantum-connection sector）与三贝里连接项（three-Berry-connection sector）之间的精确抵消，并引入实双带模型作为诊断性示例。

Result: 得到了四项分解：非线性Drude项（∝τ²）、贝里曲率偶极子项（∝τ）、带内量子度量偶极子项（∝τ⁰）、带间量子度量偶极子项（∝τ⁰）。带内项是普通能带量子度量（band quantum metric）的费米面偶极子，带间项在现有表示下为涉及能带归一化量子度量的费米海型响应。所有连接依赖的交换子项在协变量子连接项和三贝里连接项之间精确抵消，明确了Peierls接触速度顶点V_{ij}和V_{ijk}的作用。

Conclusion: 建立了量子度量偶极子作为独立于贝里曲率偶极子的直流响应机制；在贝里曲率恒为零的实双带模型中，带内量子度量偶极子仍保持有限，提供了实验上实现纯量子度量直流响应的可行路径。该结果与Ulrich等人（Phys. Rev. B 113, L201107 (2026)）的投影算子推导在考虑指标和约定差异后一致。

Abstract: We derive a gauge-invariant clean-limit decomposition of the second-order dc nonlinear conductivity in multiband tight-binding systems within the velocity-gauge Keldysh Green's function formalism. In the constant-relaxation-time approximation, the dc response separates into four contributions with distinct lifetime $τ$ scalings and physical origins: the nonlinear Drude term $σ^{\mathrm{ND}}_{ijk}\proptoτ^{2}$, the Berry-curvature-dipole term $σ^{\mathrm{BCD}}_{ijk}\proptoτ$, the intraband quantum-metric-dipole term $σ^{\mathrm{intra\text{-}QMD}}_{ijk}\proptoτ^{0}$, and the interband quantum-metric-dipole term $σ^{\mathrm{inter\text{-}QMD}}_{ijk}\proptoτ^{0}$. The intraband term is a Fermi-surface dipole of the ordinary band quantum metric, while the interband term is written, in the present representation, as a Fermi-sea-type response involving a band-normalized quantum metric. Working entirely within the velocity-gauge Keldysh--Kubo framework, we show that all connection-dependent commutator terms generated in the band-basis expansion cancel exactly between the covariant-quantum-connection sector $σ^{\mathcal{C}}_{ijk}$ and the three-Berry-connection sector $σ^{\mathcal{T}}_{ijk}$, making the role of the Peierls contact velocity vertices $V_{ij}$ and $V_{ijk}$ explicit; a complementary projector-based derivation appears in Ulrich et al., Phys. Rev. B 113, L201107 (2026), and our Fermi-surface dc-limit expression agrees with that reference after accounting for index and convention differences. As a diagnostic illustration, we introduce a real two-band model in which the Berry curvature and hence the BCD response vanish identically while the intraband quantum-metric dipole remains finite, establishing a practical route to quantum-metric dc responses not reducible to the Berry-curvature-dipole mechanism.

### [27] [Quantum Metric Bound State of Light Confinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22479)
*Jinchao Zhao,Rongning Liu,Xue-Yang Song,K. T. Law*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出了量子度量束缚态（quantum metric bound state）作为除色散带有效质量束缚和紧凑局域态（CLS）之外的第三种空间束缚机制，证明在无能带色散和无紧凑局域态保护的情况下，束缚态的指数衰减长度由未扰动平带（flat band）的量子度量（quantum metric）下界决定，并通过构建可调平带生成器和多种实际架构验证了该几何极限的紧致性与普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺陷诱导的束缚态传统上由色散带有效质量或平带中紧凑局域态实现，但紧凑局域态依赖于完美的晶格对称性和精细调谐的缺陷轮廓，引入一般性局域杂质会破坏相位匹配条件，导致广泛束缚态的基本长度尺度成为悬而未决的问题。本文旨在建立第三种束缚机制，并揭示其基本长度标度的几何起源。

Method: 提供严格的数学证明，表明在无动能和紧凑局域态保护的条件下，束缚态的指数衰减长度受到未扰动平带量子度量的下界约束。通过构建一族高度可调的平带生成器来演示该几何极限的紧致性，并在多种实际架构中验证其普适性。

Result: 建立了量子度量束缚态这一新的束缚机制，证明了束缚态指数衰减长度的下界由平带的量子度量决定，并验证了该几何极限的紧致性与跨架构的普适性。

Conclusion: 该工作将独立可测的量子度量确立为预测性设计原则，用于在合成波平台（synthetic wave platforms）中工程化受限模式，完成了对束缚态三种机制的完整分类。

Abstract: The spatial confinement of defect-induced bound states is conventionally governed by the effective mass in dispersive bands. More recently, Compact Localized States (CLSs) arising from exact destructive interference have been utilized to achieve confinement in flat bands. However, CLSs rely on pristine lattice symmetries and fine-tuned defect profiles. The introduction of a generic local impurity inevitably breaks these strict phase-matching conditions, resulting in extensive bound states whose fundamental length scale has remained an open question. Here, we establish a third regime of confinement: the quantum metric bound state. We provide a rigorous mathematical proof demonstrating that in the absence of kinetic energy and CLS protection, the exponential decay length of these states is lower-bounded by the quantum metric of the unperturbed flat band. We demonstrate the tightness of this geometric limit by constructing a family of highly tunable flat-band generators, and we verify its universality across diverse realistic architectures. Ultimately, this classification establishes the independently measurable quantum metric as a predictive design principle for engineering confined modes in synthetic wave platforms.

### [28] [Hysteresis-Driven Radiative Mpemba Effect in Phase-Change Nanostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22552)
*Florian Herz*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文首次在辐射系统中实现了姆潘巴效应（Mpemba effect），通过VO₂纳米颗粒在SiC衬底附近的相变滞回现象，证明了初始温度较高的系统冷却得更快。研究推导了启动条件，绘制了相空间图，并发现潜热作为热缓冲可同时产生普通和逆效应，而近场耦合主导弛豫时间并实现了通过衬底反射的外部记忆存储被动效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 姆潘巴效应在对流、传导和量子系统中已被观测到，但其在辐射系统中的类比尚未被探索。本文旨在填补这一空白，研究辐射系统中的姆潘巴效应。

Method: 通过VO₂纳米颗粒在SiC衬底附近的相变滞回（phase-change hysteresis）实现辐射姆潘巴效应，推导了启动条件的解析表达式，并系统绘制了相空间（phase space）图。

Result: 潜热（latent heat）作为热缓冲可同时实现普通姆潘巴效应和逆效应；近场耦合（near-field coupling）主导弛豫时间（relaxation time），并通过衬底反射实现被动外部记忆存储效应。

Conclusion: 该研究首次在辐射系统中证实了姆潘巴效应，揭示了潜热和近场耦合在其中的关键作用，为热调控和热记忆器件提供了新的物理机制。

Abstract: The Mpemba effect states that initially hotter systems cool faster than colder ones. While known in convective, conductive, and quantum systems, its radiative analogue is unexplored. Here, this anomaly is realized via phase-change hysteresis of a VO$_2$ nanoparticle near a SiC substrate. After analytically deriving an onset condition, the phase space is mapped. Crucially, latent heat acts as a thermal buffer enabling both ordinary and inverse effects. Near-field coupling governs the relaxation time and enables a passive effect where memory is stored externally via substrate reflection.

</details>


### [29] [High-Resolution Probing of Molecular Junctions: Vibrational Fingerprinting and Parameter Extraction via Current Noise Spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22663)

Result: 该方法实现了亚热特征映射（sub-thermal feature mapping），能够解析包括高能泛频（high-energy overtones）在内的复杂振动流形。直接从实验数据中提取了模式能量、非谐性（x_e）、解离能（D_e）以及局域环境重组能（E_r）等纳米尺度分子参数。

Conclusion: 这种参数密集的噪声特征（noise signatures）可作为独特的分子指纹（molecular fingerprint），将噪声光谱确立为一种用于先进量子器件中化学传感和识别的高灵敏度平台。

Abstract: The precise realization of molecular electronic devices requires a comprehensive understanding of charge transport mechanisms and the specific interplay between electronic and nuclear degrees of freedom. While average current measurements (I-V characteristics) and conventional Inelastic Electron Tunneling Spectroscopy (IETS) offer valuable insights, they are fundamentally limited by temperature-dependent line-width broadening. This study presents a high-resolution spectroscopic methodology utilizing suspended-wire molecular junctions (SWMJs) based on self-assembled monolayers (SAMs) of 1-decanethiol (C10) and 1,1',4',1''-terphenyl-4-thiol (TPT). By systematically probing the voltage-dependent current noise ($ΔI$), we demonstrate that electronic noise spectroscopy circumvents thermal degradation by probing transition rates between vibrational manifolds rather than simple additions of conductance channels, which enables sub-thermal feature mapping. Leveraging a fast-convolution-based Landauer-Büttiker transport model fitted to experimental data, we map complex vibrational manifolds, including high-energy overtones. This allows for the direct extraction of crucial nanoscale molecular parameters, including mode energies, anharmonicities ($x_e$), dissociation energies ($D_e$), and local environment reorganization energies ($E_r$). These parameter-dense noise signatures act as a unique molecular fingerprint, establishing noise spectroscopy as a highly sensitive platform for chemical sensing and discrimination in advanced quantum devices.

### [31] [Modulating radiative heat and momentum transfer via the thermal Purcell effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22746)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 亚波长约束增强辐射热和角动量传递，但抑制横向力（lateral force）；腔模干涉导致所有传递量随粒子位置发生空间振荡；在腔中心，镜面对称性使电磁涨落产生宇称分解（parity decomposition），横向力消失，而热传递和扭矩通过奇偶模态（even and odd modal contributions）的联合贡献保持有限。

Conclusion: 腔体工程（cavity engineering）可通过结构化电磁涨落（structured electromagnetic fluctuations）实现纳米尺度能量与动量转移的选择性调控。

Abstract: The thermal Purcell effect describes the modification of the local density of states of the fluctuating electromagnetic field induced by a Fabry-Pérot cavity, leading to the enhancement or suppression of radiative transport quantities. Using fluctuational electrodynamics, we investigate nonequilibrium radiative heat, linear-momentum, and angular-momentum exchange between a magneto-optic nanoparticle and a Fabry-Pérot cavity. Analytical expressions for the spectral densities reveal that geometric confinement modifies the electromagnetic local density of states, producing distinct behaviors for different transport quantities. Specifically, sub-wavelength confinement enhances radiative heat and angular-momentum transfer, but suppresses the lateral force. Additionally, interference between cavity modes causes all transfer quantities to oscillate spatially with particle position. At the cavity center, mirror symmetry enforces a parity decomposition of electromagnetic fluctuations resulting in a vanishing lateral force, whereas heat transfer and torque remain finite through combined even and odd modal contributions. These results demonstrate that cavity engineering provides selective control over nanoscale energy and momentum transfer via structured electromagnetic fluctuations.

### [32] [Strongly anisotropic Rytova-Keldysh interaction and the ground state of 2D excitons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23033)
*Andrei Galiautdinov*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Rytova-Keldysh势描述了二维材料中库仑相互作用的非局域介电屏蔽，但仅适用于各向同性情况。尽管已推导出任意面内各向异性的积分形式，数值研究表明有效各向同性近似对高度方向性系统依然稳健，缺少严格的解析基础来解释这一现象。

Method: 应用最速下降法（method of steepest descent）和动量空间坐标缩放（momentum-space coordinate scaling）处理精确的一维积分表示；采用各向异性高斯变分假设（anisotropic Gaussian variational ansatz）求解Wannier方程。

Result: 中间范围屏蔽表现出由最弱极化率方向驱动的非平凡振幅缩放；短程极限产生由主极化率几何平均值决定的各向异性对数势阱；得到了激子基态结合能的闭式解析表达式，显式捕捉有效质量张量与介电张量之间的竞争。

Abstract: The classic Rytova-Keldysh potential describes the non-local dielectric screening of Coulomb interactions in ultrathin two-dimensional (2D) materials. Recently, the corresponding potential for arbitrary in-plane anisotropy was derived in integral form, with numerical studies suggesting that an effective isotropic approximation remains robust for highly directional systems. In this paper we provide the analytical foundation for these observations by mapping the complete spatial landscape of the strongly anisotropic Rytova-Keldysh interaction. By applying the method of steepest descent and momentum-space coordinate scaling to the exact one-dimensional integral representation, we derive closed-form asymptotic expressions for the potential across all spatial regimes. We find that the intermediate-range screening exhibits a non-trivial amplitude scaling driven by the direction of weakest polarizability, while the short-range limit produces an anisotropic logarithmic well governed by the geometric mean of the principal polarizabilities. Finally, utilizing this short-range confinement, we implement an anisotropic Gaussian variational ansatz to solve the Wannier equation, providing a closed-form analytical expression for the exciton ground-state binding energy that explicitly captures the competition between the effective mass and dielectric tensors.

Abstract: Understanding the spatial distribution of carriers is important for interpreting transport in nanoscale devices. Using theory to distinguish between bulk-dominated transport, coherent near-surface transport across facets, and transport confined to individual facets. The measurements are consistent with transport dominated by a near-surface accumulation layer in InAs. Devices with normal contacts show behavior consistent with coherent transport across the nanowire apex, whereas hybrid normal-superconductor devices exhibit signatures of more facet-dependent transport. These results demonstrate how universal conductance fluctuations can be used as a tomographic probe of phase-coherent transport pathways in semiconductor nanostructures.

### [34] [Universality of dimensional crossovers in topological insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23074)
*Lumen Eek,Zeb Osseweijer,Cristiane Morais Smith*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过紧束缚晶格模型，系统研究了三维拓扑绝缘体（3D topological insulator）在几何受限下的维度交叉（dimensional crossover）行为，发现考虑体相受限效应（bulk confinement effects）和边界终止（boundary termination）后，体系会出现强非单调的拓扑相变序列，并揭示了一种超出传统认知的维度约化普适性框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为三维强拓扑绝缘体减薄为薄膜时，表面态杂化会导致其简单交叉到二维量子自旋霍尔相（2D quantum spin Hall phase）。作者旨在证明这一图像不完整，需将体相受限效应与边界终止全面纳入考虑，以揭示更丰富的拓扑相变行为。

Method: 采用最小紧束缚模型（minimal tight-binding model）对三维拓扑绝缘体进行晶格建模，通过改变系统尺寸和微观参数，系统研究拓扑相随厚度和边界终止条件的演化，并分析维度降低过程中拓扑相变的序次。

Result: 发现拓扑对厚度和微观参数呈现强非单调依赖，导致一系列对表面终止高度敏感的拓扑相变；具体观察到从三维拓扑绝缘体到二维量子自旋霍尔相，再到由反演对称性保护（inversion symmetry protected）的Kramers对端态（end states）构成的一维相的级联维度约化；此外，二维和一维拓扑相甚至可以在对应的三维体相为拓扑平庸时出现。

Conclusion: 三维到二维以及二维到一维交叉的相图展现出意想不到的普适性，指向一个统一的维度约化拓扑框架。

Abstract: We investigate dimensional crossovers in minimal tight-binding models of three-dimensional (3D) topological insulators subject to geometric confinement. While thin films are commonly understood to host a crossover from a 3D strong topological insulator to a two-dimensional (2D) quantum spin Hall phase via hybridization of surface states, we demonstrate that this picture is incomplete once bulk confinement effects and boundary termination are fully taken into account. Using lattice models, we show that reducing the system size induces a strongly non-monotonic dependence of the topology on thickness and microscopic parameters, leading to a sequence of topological phase transitions that is highly sensitive to surface termination. In particular, we find a cascade of dimensional reduction from a 3D topological insulator to a 2D quantum spin Hall phase and ultimately to a one-dimensional phase consisting of end states of Kramers pairs protected by inversion symmetry. Remarkably, we show that both the 2D and 1D topological phases can emerge even when the corresponding 3D bulk phase is topologically trivial. Our results reveal an unexpected universality in the phase diagrams of 3D-to-2D and 2D-to-1D crossovers, pointing toward a unified framework for topology under dimensional reduction.

### [35] [Fingerprints of an Imbert-Fedorov-like effect in the tunneling transmission of Rarita-Schwinger semi-metals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23095)
*Otman Bouladiane,Ahmed Jellal,Hocine Bahlouli,A. Al Luhaibi,Michael Vogl*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文研究了旋转对称的Rarita-Schwinger半金属中通过方形势垒的隧穿现象，发现了一种类似于Imbert-Fedorov效应的镜像对称性破缺机制，该机制源于多通道散射态之间的干涉项，而非能带各向异性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在旋转对称（rotationally symmetric）的各向同性多带系统中，隧穿传输是否会出现镜像对称性破缺，以及该效应的物理起源是否可归因于Imbert-Fedorov效应的类比。

Method: 在旋转对称的Rarita-Schwinger半金属（Rarita-Schwinger semi-metal）中建立方形势垒隧穿模型，通过解析方法推导透射振幅，比较单通道注入与两通道（自旋投影 $m=1/2$ 和 $m=3/2$）相干混合入射两种情况下的传输特性。

Result: 单通道注入时，透射在入射角的镜像变换下保持对称；而相干叠加情况下，透射概率出现方向不对称性 $T(k_y)\neq T(-k_y)$。高能隧穿偏向自旋投影 $3/2$ 的散射贡献。该不对称性源于两个自旋投影通道不同的散射相位和势垒传播相位之间的干涉项，而非能带色散的各向异性。

Conclusion: 该工作发现了各向同性多带系统中由界面诱导相位差引起的Imbert-Fedorov效应类比，表明不对称隧穿并非必然归因于显式能带各向异性，在理想化的各向同性多带系统中即可实现。

Abstract: We study tunneling through a square barrier in a rotationally symmetric Rarita-Schwinger semi-metal and identify fingerprints of an Imbert-Fedorov-like effect in the tunneling transmission. The problem is intrinsically multichannel at all energies because there exist two propagating sectors with spin projections $m=1/2$ and $m=3/2$. We derive the transmission amplitudes analytically and compare the single-channel and coherent mixed-incidence cases in the two channels. Interestingly, we observe that tunneling at high energy shows a bias towards scattering into spin projection $3/2$ contributions. For single-channel injection, we find that the transmission remains symmetric under a mirror transformation of the incident angle. In contrast, for the coherent superposition, we find a directional asymmetry in the transmission probability $T(k_y)\neq T(-k_y)$. Importantly, this effect does not originate from an anisotropy of the dispersion. Instead, it arises from the phase structure of the multicomponent scattering states. The two spin projection sectors exhibit different scattering and barrier-propagation phases, which enter as interference terms when both channels appear as a coherent superposition. This interference term is identified as the cause of the broken mirror symmetry. We therefore discover an analog of the Imbert-Fedorov effect, at the level of interface-induced phase differences between internal wave components. Our result demonstrates that asymmetric tunneling can already occur in transport experiments, even in an idealized, isotropic multiband system, and should therefore not be automatically attributed solely to explicit band anisotropy.

</details>


### [36] [Rotating Zeeman field as a tool for Majorana zero mode detection in topological superconducting wire](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23183)
*Piotr Stefański*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文演示了通过分析附着在拓扑线（topological wire）上的量子点（quantum dot, QD）的自旋极化（spin polarization），可以获取关于马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero mode, MZM）形成及拓扑相变（topological phase transition）的有价值信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索利用量子点自旋极化作为探测手段，来识别拓扑线中的马约拉纳零模形成与拓扑相变。

Method: 通过旋转拓扑线中的塞曼场（Zeeman field）方向（保持量子点中塞曼场方向不变），测量量子点费米能级处的有效自旋极化变化。

Result: 存在马约拉纳模时，当线中塞曼场从平行转为垂直于线轴方向，量子点费米能级处的自旋极化显著变化；在平庸态（trivial state）下自旋极化几乎不变；临界磁场值处自旋极化呈现非线性依赖关系，可标识拓扑相变。

Conclusion: 量子点自旋极化分析可作为探测马约拉纳零模及拓扑相变的有效手段，且该特征不依赖于线-点耦合强度及塞曼场角度。

Abstract: We demonstrate that analysis of the spin polarization of a quantum dot (QD) attached to the topological wire can provide valuable insights into Majorana zero mode (MZM) formation and topological phase transition. Detection is realized by rotation of the Zeeman field in the wire, while retaining the Zeeman field direction in the dot intact. In the presence of Majorana mode, the effective QD spin polarization at Fermi energy changes significantly when the direction of the Zeeman field in the wire changes from parallel to perpendicular to the wire axis. It can be opposed to the wire in its trivial state, when spin polarization remains practically constant while the magnetic field is rotated. Similar unaltered spin polarization is observed when QD spin sub-level at Fermi energy mimics MZM. Moreover, the characteristic non-linear dependence of the spin polarization on the magnetic field magnitude at its critical value identifies a topological phase transition in the wire. This feature is observed independently on the coupling strength of the wire to the dot and the angle of the Zeeman field.

</details>


### [37] [Reactive Force Field for P/Sn/I System: Atomistic Insight into the Early Stage of Black Phosphorus and Phosphorene Synthesis Process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23328)
*Djuric Brice Talonpa Tchoffo,Ismail Benabdallah,Petr Neugebauer,Anouar Belhboub,Abdelouahad El Fatimy*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究通过开发PSnI体系的反应力场（reactive force field），并基于ReaxFF分子动力学模拟，揭示了黑磷（black phosphorus）及其二维类似物磷烯（phosphorene）在化学气相传输/沉积合成中成核前期的原子尺度机制，发现碘和密度共同调控磷的复合行为，且高密度条件下可生成类似黑磷的六元环结构，可能作为成核种子（nucleation seeds）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑磷和磷烯的合成通常依赖Sn和I2添加剂进行化学气相传输（chemical vapor transport），但化学气相沉积（chemical vapor deposition）合成机制尚不明确，且实验上难以探究磷传输和早期成核的原子尺度过程。

Method: 基于ReaxFF框架开发了PSnI体系的反应力场，力场参数通过全面的量子力学（quantum mechanical）数据集训练，涵盖键解离、角度和二面角分布、锡凝聚相状态方程以及团簇形成能；利用该力场进行分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，研究黑磷-磷烯生长中成核前（pre-nucleation）的早期阶段。

Result: 碘（iodine）和体系密度共同控制磷的复合：低密度下原子磷主导，几乎无团簇生成；添加I2显著促进P-P复合，形成PxIy结构基元和瞬态SnxPyIz化合物；高密度有利于大Px团簇形成及三元SnxPyIz化合物的生长；最高密度下，系统在SnxPyIz团簇边缘生成类似Hittorf磷的凝聚相结构，以及由碘稳定化的类黑磷六元环结构，可能作为成核种子。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了黑磷合成过程中磷传输和早期成核步骤的原子尺度图像，并提供了一个实用的反应性模型（reactive model），可用于研究黑磷-磷烯气相合成中的生长条件和添加剂效应。

Abstract: Black phosphorus and its two dimensional counterpart, phosphorene, are typically synthesized through chemical vapor transport using Sn and I2 additives. Chemical vapor deposition synthesis of phosphorene and allotropes is still yet not well understood. Investigating the atomistic mechanisms underlying phosphorus transport and early stage processes is difficult experimentally. In this study, a reactive force field for the PSnI system was developed and applied using ReaxFF based molecular dynamics to explore the early stage phase of the pre nucleation relevant to BP-phosphorene growth. The force field parameters were trained on a comprehensive quantum mechanical dataset covering bond dissociation, angle and torsion profiles, and tin condensed phase equation of state and cluster formation energies, showing strong agreement in both gas and condensed phases. We demonstrate that iodine and density together control phosphorus recombination. Under low density, atomic phosphorus dominates with minimal clustering. Adding I2 greatly increases P-P recombination, promotes the formation of PxIy motifs, and transient SnxPyIz compounds. Higher density systems favor the formation of larger Px clusters and support the development of ternary SnxPyIz compounds that grow by capturing transported phosphorus. At the highest density, the system produces condensed, Hittorf like phosphorus structures at the edges of SnxPyIz clusters, along with BP-like hexagons stabilized by iodine that may act as nucleation seeds. These results offer an atomistic view of transport and early stage steps in BP synthesis and provide a practical reactive model for studying growth conditions and additive effects in BP phosphorene vapor synthesis.
