### [38] [Quantum Geometry Driven Finite-Momentum Exciton Fluctuations in Flat-Band Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23598)
*Yi-Chun Hung,Xiaoting Zhou,Arun Bansil*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从理论上证明了晶格几何诱导的平带（如kagome和Lieb晶格）可作为纯量子几何驱动激子绝缘体相的平台，通过Ginzburg-Landau框架将平带量子度规映射到宏观自由能，并预测了在强相互作用下由量子度规诱导的有限动量超流密度涨落态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在动能被抑制的平带系统中，量子度规（quantum metric）成为宏观集体现象的基本驱动力；然而，纯粹由量子几何驱动的激子绝缘体（excitonic insulator, EI）相尚未得到理论阐明，尤其缺乏将平带量子几何与动态集体激发态（如超流相）之间建立严格联系的理论框架。

Method: 采用无自旋-轨道耦合下的面外塞曼场（Zeeman field）解除自旋简并，建立Ginzburg-Landau理论框架，将电子-空穴波函数重叠直接映射为平带量子度规，进而纳入宏观自由能表达式中，并分析该映射对激子绝缘体相和超流相的影响。

Result: 在强相互作用下，量子度规导致振幅模式（amplitude mode）的有效动力学系数（effective kinetic coefficient）变为负值；这并未使均匀凝聚体失稳，反而在有限动量处软化振幅涨落，从而产生有限动量超流密度涨落（finite-momentum superfluid density fluctuation, FMSDF）态，该态可观测为面内磁化涨落的周期调制。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了平带量子几何与动态集体激子态之间的严格联系，并指出共价有机框架（covalent-organic frameworks, COFs）是实现该FMSDF态的理想候选平台。

Abstract: Quantum geometry is instrumental in stabilizing exotic phenomena in systems ranging from topological insulators to superconductors. In dispersionless flat bands, where the kinetic energy is quenched, the quantum metric emerges as the fundamental driver of macroscopic collective phenomena. Here, we theoretically demonstrate that lattice-geometry-induced flat bands, such as those in kagome and Lieb lattices, provide a fertile platform for realizing a purely quantum-geometry-driven excitonic insulator (EI) phase. By applying an out-of-plane Zeeman field to lift spin degeneracy without spin-orbit coupling, we establish a Ginzburg-Landau framework in which the electron-hole wavefunction-overlap directly maps the flat-band quantum metric onto the macroscopic free energy. This mapping plays a key role in both the EI and the associated superfluid phases, with the coherence length and phase stiffness emerging directly from the quantum metric. Our analysis reveals that under strong interactions, the quantum metric induces a negative effective kinetic coefficient for the amplitude mode. Rather than destabilizing the uniform condensate, this softens the amplitude fluctuations at a finite momentum, giving rise to a finite-momentum superfluid density fluctuation (FMSDF) state. This state is observable as a periodically modulated magnitude of in-plane magnetization fluctuations. Our findings establish a rigorous link between flat-band quantum geometry and dynamic collective excitonic states, with promising pathways for realization in covalent-organic frameworks (COFs).

### [39] [Helical Domain-Wall-Ring Networks Reshape Superconducting Correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23599)
*Yi-Chun Hung,Arun Bansil*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究扭转双层蜂窝晶格（twisted bilayer honeycomb lattice）中形成的畴壁环网络（domain-wall-ring networks）内的超导关联（superconducting correlations）。无限大尺寸理论表明环间超导配对隧穿是重整化群（renormalization group）相关的，能增强超导关联；但自洽变分方法显示，有限尺寸效应使得相位锁定尺度（phase-locking scale）被强烈抑制，且超导标度维数（SC scaling dimension）对配对隧穿强度不敏感，揭示了有限环网络与无限大尺寸系统的定性差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 莫尔材料（moiré materials）中扩展的畴壁网络为准一维电子态提供了独特平台，但受限网络中的相互作用驱动有序态尚缺乏研究。本文旨在探索相互作用螺旋畴壁环网络中的超导关联行为。

Method: 首先采用无限大尺寸理论框架分析环间超导配对隧穿的标度行为，然后发展自洽变分方法（self-consistent variational approach）处理由环网络几何结构导致的有限尺寸效应。

Result: 无限大尺寸理论表明环间超导配对隧穿是重整化群相关的，可通过环间相位锁定增强超导关联。但变分分析显示，即使在无限大理论预测强耦合配对隧穿的参数区域，诱导的相位锁定尺度仍被强烈抑制；超导标度维数随扭转角（twist angle）减小而持续降低，且对配对隧穿强度不敏感，与无限大尺寸理论预期存在定性失配。

Conclusion: 环网络并非简单地逼近其无限大尺寸对应系统，而是可能展现出定性不同的集体行为。受限效应与环网络几何结构的相互作用能够重塑超导关联。

Abstract: Extended domain-wall networks emerging in moiré materials provide a distinct platform for quasi-one-dimensional electronic states. However, the interaction-driven orders in confined networks remain largely unexplored. Here, we discuss superconducting (SC) correlations in interacting helical domain-wall-ring networks that emerge in the closed topological domains formed within the moiré patterns of an underlying twisted bilayer honeycomb lattice. We first analyze the system within the framework of an infinite-size theory and show that inter-ring SC-pair tunneling is renormalization-group relevant and thus enhances SC correlations through inter-ring phase locking. To address finite-size effects resulting from the ring-network geometry, we present a self-consistent variational approach. Our analysis shows that even in the regime where the infinite-size theory predicts strongly-coupled pair tunneling, the induced phase-locking scale remains strongly suppressed. In contrast, the SC scaling dimension continues to decrease with decreasing twist angle and remains insensitive to the pair-tunneling strength, revealing a qualitative mismatch from the infinite-size expectation. This discrepancy demonstrates that ring networks do not simply approach their infinite-size counterparts but can exhibit qualitatively distinct collective behavior. Our study highlights how the interplay of confinement effects and ring-network geometry can reshape SC correlations.

### [40] [LLM-Guided Test-Time Discovery of Quantum-Chemical Approximation Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20729)
*Masaya Hagai,Yuta Suzuki,Tomoya Murata,Shuhei Kurita,Masaki Adachi*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出 LADeQ，一种基于大语言模型（LLM）引导的工作流，能够在量子化学代码中于测试时自动发现、实现并评估候选近似算法，从而在保持误差可控的前提下加速电子结构计算（如 CCSD 和 CISD）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子化学模拟（quantum chemistry simulation）受限于高昂的计算成本和对固定近似方案的依赖；现有基础模型（foundation models）和智能体 AI 系统（agentic AI systems）各自存在数据依赖与工具约束，难以适应化学空间前沿中方法创新与稀疏数据的实际需求。

Method: LADeQ 利用现成的大语言模型（LLM），在测试时从空间统计（spatial statistics）、电路模拟（circuit simulation）和核方法（kernel methods）等先前少用于电子结构理论的领域动态构建候选近似方案，并将其直接嵌入现有量子化学代码中执行与基准测试，无需任务特定预训练或人工数据集。

Result: LADeQ 成功加速了耦合簇单双激发（CCSD）和组态相互作用单双激发（CISD）计算，同时将关联能误差（correlation-energy error）控制在用户指定的容差范围内。

Conclusion: LADeQ 展示了在现有电子结构求解器内部实现自主、目标驱动的近似算法发现能力，其透明可追溯的近似误差机制支持对精度-效率权衡（accuracy-efficiency trade-off）的原则性控制。

Abstract: Quantum chemistry simulations underpin modern materials discovery, yet their impact is limited by steep computational cost and dependence on fixed approximation schemes. Foundation models, such as machine-learned interatomic potentials, have accelerated parts of this workflow, but their reliance on large-scale pretraining restricts adaptability at the frontier of chemical space, where methodological innovation and sparse data are the norm. Agentic AI systems can automate existing simulation pipelines, yet they remain constrained by the predefined tools and algorithms they orchestrate. In response, we introduce LADeQ, an LLM-guided workflow that discovers, implements, and benchmarks candidate approximation algorithms at test-time within existing quantum chemistry codes. Rather than selecting from a predefined repertoire, LADeQ constructs candidate approximation schemes on demand, drawing on techniques from disciplines such as spatial statistics, circuit simulation, and kernel methods that have had little prior presence in electronic-structure theory. Because it builds on an out-of-the-box language model, LADeQ requires no task-specific pretraining or curated data, and the resulting implementations are transparent and inspectable, with explicitly traceable approximation errors that enable principled control of accuracy--efficiency trade-offs. We show that LADeQ accelerates coupled cluster singles and doubles (CCSD) and configuration interaction singles and doubles (CISD) calculations while keeping correlation-energy errors within user-specified tolerances, demonstrating autonomous, objective-driven discovery of approximation algorithms inside existing electronic-structure solvers.

</details>


### [41] [Generalized Mpemba effect in diffusion-controlled spin-dependent delayed fluorescence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21003)
*Kazuhiko Seki*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过三线态融合系统中的磁场依赖延迟荧光，展示了由外部控制自旋选择性动力学实现的广义姆潘巴效应（generalized Mpemba effect），并推导了轨迹交叉的动力学判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代姆潘巴效应（Mpemba effect）的广义定义比传统热弛豫解释更宽泛——初始远离平衡的态可能比近平衡态弛豫更快，或弛豫轨迹发生交叉。本文旨在证明这种轨迹交叉现象可以在由扩散控制的成对复合（geminate recombination）及非马尔可夫动力学（non-Markovian kinetics）支配的自旋相关光动力学系统中实现。

Method: 采用Johnson–Merrifield模型的扩散控制成对复合扩展版本，通过数值模拟和解析推导研究三线态融合系统中不同磁场下的延迟荧光弛豫轨迹，并推导出轨迹交叉的紧凑动力学判据。

Result: 当成对融合有效时，不同磁场下的延迟荧光弛豫轨迹会发生交叉；这一交叉现象由中间时间衰减率与长时间幂律振幅之间的竞争决定；最终弛豫态与外部控制参数（磁场）无关，完全弛豫后不存在分离的三线态布居。

Conclusion: 该广义姆潘巴效应源于与成对复合相关的瞬态弛豫路径的重新分配，而体扩散控制过程仅贡献于最终弛豫。研究结果将自旋相关光动力学中的反常弛豫与现代广义姆潘巴效应联系起来，揭示了非马尔可夫动力学系统中轨迹交叉的产生机制。

Abstract: The Mpemba effect is commonly associated with anomalous thermal relaxation, in which a system prepared at a higher temperature reaches equilibrium faster than one prepared at a lower temperature. In modern formulations, however, its defining feature is broader: a state initially farther from equilibrium can relax faster than a closer one, or, equivalently, relaxation trajectories can cross.
  Here, we show that magnetic-field-dependent delayed fluorescence in triplet-fusion systems realizes a generalized Mpemba effect driven by external control of spin-selective kinetics. Using a diffusion-controlled geminate-recombination extension of the Johnson--Merrifield model, we demonstrate that delayed-fluorescence trajectories obtained at different magnetic fields cross when geminate fusion is effective. We further derive a compact kinetic criterion for such crossing in terms of the competition between intermediate-time decay rates and long-time power-law amplitudes. This criterion captures the interplay between effective fast and slow relaxation contributions. Within this kinetic framework, the final state is independent of the external control parameter and is defined as the fully relaxed state in which no separated triplet population remains. The generalized Mpemba effect therefore arises from the redistribution of transient relaxation pathways associated with geminate recombination, whereas bulk diffusion-controlled processes contribute only to the final relaxation.
  These results link anomalous relaxation in spin-dependent photokinetics to modern formulations of the generalized Mpemba effect and show how trajectory crossing can emerge in systems governed by diffusion-controlled geminate recombination and non-Markovian kinetics.

</details>


### [42] [Controlling the phase behaviour of ultraconfined water via bilayer graphene stacking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21490)
*Yixuan Pu,Benjamin X. Shi,Pavan Ravindra,Chris Pickard,Angelos Michaelides,Venkat Kapil*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potentials）计算了双层石墨烯纳米毛细管中受限水的密度-温度相图，发现仅1.4 Å的横向堆叠差异（AA与AB堆叠）就能显著改变受限水的冰多晶型、熔点、质子转移及超离子行为，证明限制壁的原子级结构变化可定性重塑纳米受限水的物理化学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往研究将纳米受限水异常行为的归因于几何约束及降维效应（geometric confinement and reduced dimensionality），但限制拓扑（confinement topology）本身是否足以预测其行为尚未明确。本文旨在检验限制壁的原子级堆叠方式是否对受限水行为具有决定性影响。

Method: 采用具有第一性原理精度（first-principles accuracy）的机器学习原子间势，计算双层石墨烯纳米毛细管中受限水的密度-温度相图，并系统比较AA堆叠与AB堆叠两种仅相差1.4 Å横向位移的构型。

Result: AA堆叠相较于AB堆叠可稳定不同的冰多晶型（ice polymorphs），使熔点提升超过100 K，增强质子转移（proton transfer），并改变超离子行为（superionic behaviour）的起始条件。这些效应源于堆叠诱导的氢键网络（hydrogen-bond network）变化，与自由能地貌（free energy landscape）及相邻O-O间距的修饰相关。

Conclusion: 即使限制壁仅发生细微原子级变化，也能定性重塑纳米受限水的物理和化学行为，这对理解及控制在埃尺度（angstrom-scale）限制下流体的行为具有重要启示。

Abstract: Water confined within nanoscale capillaries exhibits phase behaviour and transport properties that differ substantially from bulk, and these effects are commonly interpreted as consequences of geometric confinement and reduced dimensionality. Here we show that confinement topology alone is insufficient to predict the behaviour of nanoconfined water. Using machine learning interatomic potentials with first-principles accuracy, we compute the density-temperature phase diagram of water confined within bilayer graphene nanocapillaries and compare AA and AB stacking arrangements, which differ only by a lateral shift of 1.4 Å. Despite this minimal structural change, AA stacking can stabilise different ice polymorphs, can increase the melting temperature by more than 100 K, can enhance proton transfer, and alters the onset of superionic behaviour relative to AB stacking. We trace these effects to stacking-induced changes in the hydrogen-bond network associated with modifications to the lateral free energy landscape and neighbouring O-O separations. Our results demonstrate that even subtle atomistic variations in the confining walls can qualitatively reshape the physical and chemical behaviour of nanoconfined water, with implications for the interpretation and control of fluids under angstrom-scale confinement.

### [43] [The impedance of a charged flat-plate electric double-layer capacitor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21980)
*Adrian L. Usler,David Fertig,Mathijs Janssen*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过有限元方法模拟修正的泊松-能斯特-普朗克（Poisson–Nernst–Planck）方程，计算平板双电层（electric double-layer, EDL）电容器的阻抗。研究发现，当施加偏置电压或阴阳离子扩散系数不同时，奈奎斯特（Nyquist）图的中频区会出现斜线；该斜线在这两种情况下均与双极性盐扩散（ambipolar salt diffusion）相关。研究否定了此前关于斜线宽度代表EDL电阻、斜线斜率反映扩散与充电时间尺度比值的两种观点，并提出了两种等效电路模型，分别对应阴阳离子扩散系数不等和偏置电压非零的情形，进而建立了Warburg（Warburg）元件与双极性扩散系数、体电解质化学电容及EDL差分电荷效率之间的定量关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双电层电容器的阻抗谱中频区出现的斜线（slanted line）其物理来源存在争议，此前研究中两种关于斜线宽度和斜率的解释有待验证。该研究旨在澄清斜线产生的物理机制，并为平板电极EDL电容器的定量阻抗分析提供更准确的理论框架。

Method: 采用有限元方法（Finite Element Method, FEM）对修正的泊松-能斯特-普朗克（modified Poisson–Nernst–Planck）方程进行数值模拟，计算平板双电层（EDL）电容器的阻抗谱。通过设置偏置电压非零（U_bias≠0）和阴阳离子扩散系数不等（D_-≠D_+）两种条件，分别考察其对奈奎斯特（Nyquist）图的影响。进一步通过频率相关的浓度扰动分析验证斜线的物理来源，并提出等效电路（equivalent circuit）模型进行定量分析。

Result: 阻抗谱在偏置电压非零或阴阳离子扩散系数不等时，奈奎斯特（Nyquist）图的中频区均出现斜线（slanted line），两种情况下斜线均与双极性盐扩散（ambipolar salt diffusion）相关。研究否定了此前关于斜线宽度代表EDL电阻（R_sl）及斜线斜率（k_sl）反映扩散与充电时间尺度比值（τ_diff/τ_c）的两种观点。针对D_-≠D_+和U_bias≠0两种情形，分别提出了包含Warburg短（Warburg short）和Warburg开（Warburg open）元件的等效电路，并建立了Warburg预因子与双极性扩散系数、体电解质化学电容及EDL差分电荷效率之间的定量关系。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一个理论框架，能够解释斜线宽度在大偏置电压下饱和、在大离子堆积分数（ion packing fraction）下消失的物理原因，并揭示了封闭系统中有限离子数量如何限制系统的整体电容。该框架为平板电极EDL电容器的阻抗谱定量分析提供了更精确的等效电路模型和物理关联。

Abstract: We calculate the impedance of a flat-plate electric double-layer (EDL) capacitor by means of Finite Element Method simulations of modified Poisson--Nernst--Planck equations. In Nyquist representation, the impedance spectra show a slanted line at intermediate frequencies if the capacitor is biased by a voltage, $U_\mathrm{bias}\neq 0$, or if the cation and anion diffusion coefficients differ, $D_-\neq D_+$. By inspecting the concentration perturbations in the relevant frequency range, we confirm that the slanted line is in both cases related to ambipolar salt diffusion. On the basis of our impedance data, we disprove two previously made claims: 1) that the width $R_\mathrm{sl}$ of the slanted-line region represents an EDL resistance; and 2) that the slope $k_\mathrm{sl}$ of the slanted line is a measure of the ratio of the diffusion and charging time scales, $τ_\mathrm{diff}/τ_\mathrm{c}$. For the quantitative analysis of flat-electrode EDL capacitor impedance, we propose instead two equivalent circuits, for the cases $D_-\neq D_+$ and $U_\mathrm{bias}\neq 0$. These two cases give rise to antisymmetric and symmetric salt perturbations, which are best described by a Warburg short and Warburg open element, respectively. From our circuit analysis, we obtain quantitative relations that link the Warburg prefactors to the ambipolar diffusion coefficient, the chemical capacitance of the bulk electrolyte, and the differential charge efficiency of the EDLs. We thus provide a theoretical framework that explains why the width of the slanted line saturates at large biases, why it vanishes for large ion packing fractions, and how the system's overall capacitance is limited by the finite amount of ions in a closed system.

</details>


### [44] [Reaction-Network-Level Discovery of Ammonia Synthesis Catalysts via Ten-Million-Scale Generative Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22926)
*Ruili Li,Rui Qi,Shuoqi Zhang,Qingli Tang,Qingqing Mao,Ritankar Das,Beien Zhu,Yi Gao*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于千万级生成式探索的反应网络级催化剂发现框架，通过耦合吸附物特异性生成式Transformer与高通量机器学习势，系统绘制四种关键中间体的结构-性能图谱，在稀疏相容性空间中识别出279种高潜力氨合成催化剂，并验证了Fe-V（解离路径）和Al-Pd-Zr（缔合路径）两类新型催化剂家族的机制差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氨合成催化剂的发现本质上是反应网络（reaction-network）层面的挑战，因为催化性能由表面与多个不同中间体（intermediate）在竞争性解离与缔合路径上的协调相容性决定，而非单一吸附中间体。传统筛选工作流在面对多中间体约束的超大型化学空间时存在巨大瓶颈。

Method: 该方法将吸附物特异性生成式Transformer（adsorbate-specific generative Transformers）与高通量机器学习势（machine learning potentials）相结合，对四种关键中间体（N*、NH*、NNH*和HNNH*）进行千万级构型生成与结构-性能图谱的系统映射。每个吸附物约生成1500万构型，经过结构压缩和机器学习势预测后识别高潜力目标材料。

Result: 尺度依赖性重叠分析表明，完整的四中间体相容性空间在常规10⁵–10⁶生成尺度下严重欠采样，仅在千万级探索下才显现。最终识别出279种高潜力目标材料，该稀疏相容性空间成功复现了传统的Fe基和Ru基催化剂，同时发现了此前未探索的催化剂家族。DFT计算验证了Fe-V通过显著降低初始N₂解离势垒成为解离路径（dissociative pathway）先导，而Al-Pd-Zr则作为缔合路径（associative pathway）先导有效稳定缔合中间体。

Conclusion: 多中间体反应网络相容性（multi-intermediate reaction-network compatibility）可作为从百万级生成化学空间中发现先进催化剂的稳健判据，千万级生成式探索对于揭示稀疏相容性空间至关重要。

Abstract: Catalyst discovery for ammonia synthesis is inherently a reaction-network challenge because catalytic performance is governed not by a single adsorbed intermediate, but by a surface's orchestrated compatibility with multiple distinct intermediates across competing dissociative and associative pathways. However, navigating ultra-large chemical spaces under such multi-intermediate constraints remains a formidable bottleneck for conventional screening workflows. Here, we report a reaction-network-level catalyst discovery framework driven by ten-million-scale generative exploration. By coupling adsorbate-specific generative Transformers with high-throughput machine learning potentials, we systematically map the structure-property landscapes of four critical intermediates (N*, NH*, NNH*, and HNNH*). Scale-dependent overlap analysis shows that the full four-intermediate compatibility space remains strongly under-sampled at conventional 105-106 generative scales, emerging exclusively under ten-million-scale exploration. By generating approximately 15 million configurations per adsorbate, followed by structural compression and machine-learning-potential predictions, we identified 279 highly potential target materials. This sparse compatibility space successfully recovers traditional Fe- and Ru-based motifs while uncovering previously unexplored catalyst families. Representative DFT calculations validate pathway-dependent mechanisms: Fe-V emerges as a dissociative-pathway lead by significantly lowering the initial N2 dissociation barrier, whereas Al-Pd-Zr efficiently stabilizes associative intermediates as an associative-pathway lead. These findings establish multi-intermediate reaction-network compatibility as a robust criterion for discovering advanced catalysts from multi-million generative chemical spaces.

### [45] [Neural Wavefunctions in Quantum Field Theory I: Asymptotic Freedom](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20791)

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于神经网络参数化波函数的量子场论变分方法，并通过二维非线性σ模型验证了该方法能重现渐近自由、动力学质量生成及步进标度函数等关键特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 变分方法在量子场论（quantum field theory）中的应用长期受到传统挑战的限制，本文旨在利用神经网络波函数（neural-network wavefunctions）与现代机器学习技术克服这些困难，实现有竞争力的变分计算。

Method: 采用神经网络参数化的波函数作为变分拟设（variational ansatz），并结合现代机器学习技术优化变分参数，从而对量子场论进行变分计算。

Result: 在二维非线性σ模型（two-dimensional nonlinear σ-model）上，成功重现了渐近自由（asymptotic freedom）、动力学质量生成（dynamical mass generation）以及模型的步进标度函数（step-scaling function）。

Conclusion: 神经网络波函数与现代机器学习的结合为非平凡场论中的变分计算提供了一条有效路径，有望推动量子场论变分方法的发展。

Abstract: We present a variational approach to quantum field theory based on wavefunctions parameterized by neural networks. While variational methods have a celebrated history across many fields, their application to quantum field theory has been limited by well-known challenges. We show that neural-network wavefunctions, combined with modern machine-learning techniques, enable competitive variational calculations in nontrivial field theories. As a demonstration, we reproduce the essential features of the two-dimensional nonlinear $σ$-model: asymptotic freedom, dynamical mass generation and the model's step-scaling function.

### [46] [Multi-Level Resistive Synapses for On-Chip Neural Networks: A Physics-Based Design of a Memristive Crossbar Fabric with Quasi-Continuous Conductance States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22621)
*David Alejandro Trejo Pizzo*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文基于电阻通信（resistive communication）提出了一种片上神经网络（on-chip neural network）的物理设计，采用多电平忆阻突触（multi-level memristive synapses）支持密集的电导状态谱，建立了基于离子输运物理的状态变量模型，构建了1T1R交叉开关阵列，实现了模拟域中的向量-矩阵乘法（VMM）、原位外积学习规则及多层流水线推理/训练，最终给出一种高密度、模拟式、存内神经处理器的完整硬件原生蓝图，特别适用于大语言模型（LLMs）并远超传统CPU/GPU能效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统CMOS架构和二元ReRAM在支持大语言模型（large language models）时受限于权重移动开销和有限的电导状态密度，亟需一种高密度、低功耗、存内计算（in-memory computing）的物理硬件方案。

Method: 基于离子输运物理学构建状态变量模型，量化热噪声（thermal noise）、漂移（drift）和量子化电导（quantized conductance）下的可存储子电平数；将忆阻器件组装为1T1R交叉开关阵列，推导含线电阻的模拟向量-矩阵乘法线性代数；设计差分突触实现符号权重；在模拟域物理实现推理（inference）、反向传播（backpropagation）和权重更新的多层流水线；推导原位外积学习规则及其在电导晶格上的离散化与量化噪声模型；给出能量、面积、容量和片间互连模型；详述HfO₂基材料堆栈、FEOL/BEOL CMOS代工厂集成流程、SPICE模型、忆阻-FPGA神经形态系统及电流模跨导线性softmax的存内自注意力引擎。

Result: 三元BitNet数据通路（datapath）的每token能效预计比先进CPU或GPU高出数个数量级；设计消除了权重移动，在密度与能效上超越二元ReRAM和传统CMOS方案。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一整套自洽的硬件原生蓝图，证明基于多电平忆阻突触的模拟存内神经处理器在支持大语言模型方面具备显著优势，可作为高密度、存内计算神经形态系统的可行设计参考。

Abstract: Building on resistive communication, this paper presents a physics-based design of an on-chip neural network with multi-level memristive synapses supporting a dense spectrum of conductance states. Derived from ionic transport physics, we develop a state-variable model and quantify storable sub-levels under thermal noise, drift, and quantized conductance. We assemble these devices into a 1T1R crossbar fabric, derive the linear algebra of analog vector-matrix multiplication (VMM) under wire resistance, and design a differential synapse for signed weights. A multilayer pipeline executes inference, backpropagation, and weight updates physically in the analog domain. We derive the in-situ outer-product learning rule, its discretization onto the conductance lattice, and the resulting quantization noise. We provide energy, area, capacity, and inter-tile models, showing this substrate is ideally suited for large language models (LLMs). Our design eliminates weight movement, surpassing binary ReRAM and traditional CMOS. We detail the material stack (HfO_2-based), the FEOL/BEOL CMOS foundry-integration flow, a self-contained SPICE model, the complete memristive-FPGA neuromorphic system, and an in-memory self-attention engine with current-mode translinear softmax. Finally, a ternary BitNet datapath shows projected per-token efficiency orders of magnitude better than advanced CPUs or GPUs. The result is a self-contained hardware-native blueprint for a high-density, analog, in-memory neural processor.

### [47] [Effect of rewiring for a sandpile model on a directed network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22092)
*Alejandro Zamorano,Víctor Muñoz*

Main category: nlin.CG

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维和二维BTW模型在重连（rewiring）网络上的沙堆动力学（sandpile dynamics），发现基尼系数（Gini coefficient）在约85%重连次数时出现一维转变，并在热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下两个维度均表现出转变，而其他拓扑测度（topological measures）不敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究将沙堆动力学从规则网格扩展到网络（network）上，但简单的重连方式可能导致能量无法释放。本文旨在设计一种保证能量始终可释放的重连方案，并系统研究重连对雪崩统计（avalanche statistics）的影响。

Method: 采用一维和二维的BTW模型（BTW model），通过重连节点使得能量释放始终可行；分析雪崩大小分布、节点负载分布的基尼系数、节点间平均距离、介数中心性（betweenness centrality）等统计量，并考察网络规模N及每次重连的负载和雪崩阈值的影响。

Result: 一维情况下，基尼系数在约85%可能重连次数处出现转变，而雪崩大小分布和平均距离等其他测度未显示该转变。二维情况下，能量释放即使在完全重连后仍服从幂律分布（power law），基尼系数以更平滑的方式持续下降。对于一维和二维，基尼系数在热力学极限N→∞时均存在转变，该转变也被介数中心性捕捉到，但其他拓扑测度未显示。

Conclusion: 基尼系数作为负载分布不均匀性的度量，能够揭示重连网络中由拓扑变化引发的隐藏相变（phase transition），其敏感性优于传统雪崩统计和简单拓扑测度。该转变在热力学极限下对两个维度均成立。

Abstract: Several studies have considered sandpile dynamics not over regular grids, but over networks. In this case, avalanches redistribute grains not between neighboring sites in a geometrical sense, but between connected sites, in a topological sense. However, depending on how nodes are connected, grains may never leave the system, preventing energy release. In this work, we study the simplest case, the BTW model in one and two dimensions, rewiring the nodes so that at every rewiring step, the energy release is always possible, and study avalanche statistics as a function of rewiring. In the 1D case, a transition is observed in the Gini coefficient of the load distribution per node at about 85% the number of possible rewirings, a transition which is not evident with other measures, such as the size distribution of avalanches or the mean distance between nodes in the network. In the 2D case, energy release follows a power law even when the grid is fully rewired, while the Gini coefficient, unlike the 1D case, decreases at a steady rate, with a smoother transition. The effect of network size N is studied, finding that there is a transition for the Gini coefficient at the thermodynamic limit N \to \infty for both the 1D and 2D cases, transition which is also observed in the betweenness centrality, but not in other topological measures. Finally, the dependence of the results with the load per rewiring iteration, and the avalanche threshold is studied.

</details>

### [48] [A phase-field model for microbiologically influenced corrosion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22640)
*S. Kovacevic,E. Martínez-Pañeda*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于相场（phase-field）的反应-扩散腐蚀模型，用于预测金属合金中的微生物影响腐蚀（MIC），尤其在厌氧条件下由硫酸盐还原菌（SRB）引起的过程。模型耦合微生物代谢、物质输运、电化学动力学、材料溶解与力学效应，并通过敏感性分析与多尺度案例验证其预测能力，最终应用于海上风电单桩基础的结构完整性评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微生物影响腐蚀（MIC）在厌氧环境中对金属结构造成严重威胁，但现有模型难以同时兼顾微生物活性、电化学过程、力学场耦合及多尺度预测需求，因此亟需建立一种具备预测能力且计算高效的腐蚀损伤评估工具。

Method: 基于相场（phase-field）方法构建反应-扩散腐蚀模型：微生物硫酸盐还原过程采用Monod型表达式描述硫酸盐消耗速率；力学-化学耦合通过增强迁移率关系（enhanced mobility relationship）实现，用以刻画力学场对腐蚀动力学的影响；模型通过实验标定和敏感性分析，量化微生物动力学、物质输运与热力学驱动力之间的竞争关系。

Result: 模型在预测SRB活性下的点蚀动力学方面与实验吻合良好；结果显示更细的晶粒尺寸可降低点蚀严重程度，但在力学加载下会加速缺陷扩展；在结构尺度上，牺牲阳极的阴极保护（CP）可延缓点蚀并抑制裂纹扩展，但其有效性随阳极退化而下降。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一种可预测且计算高效的MIC损伤评估工具，能够覆盖从微观组织到工程尺度的损伤演化过程，适用于在恶劣微生物环境中运行的金属结构完整性及寿命评估。

Abstract: A phase-field-based reaction-diffusion corrosion model is developed to predict microbially influenced corrosion (MIC) in metal alloys, with a focus on anaerobic conditions and sulfate-reducing bacteria (SRB). The formulation couples microbial sulfate reduction, sulfate transport, electrochemical kinetics, material dissolution, and mechanical effects. Microbial activity is modelled using a Monod-type expression for sulfate consumption, whereas the mechano-chemical coupling is incorporated through an enhanced mobility relationship that captures the influence of mechanical fields on corrosion kinetics. The model is calibrated against experiments and shows strong agreement in predicting pitting kinetics under SRB activity. Sensitivity analyses quantify the competing roles of microbial kinetics, transport, and thermodynamic driving forces in governing corrosion behaviour. The capability of the formulation to capture both MIC-induced pitting and stress-assisted corrosion across multiple length scales is demonstrated through case studies that include microstructure-sensitive simulations and structural-scale coupling with a cathodic protection (CP) model. Results show that finer grain sizes reduce pitting severity but promote faster defect propagation under mechanical loading. At the structural scale, coupling with the CP model enables predictions of defect growth under varying electrochemical conditions and over engineering-relevant length scales, as exemplified with the analysis of an offshore wind turbine monopile. CP delays pitting and suppresses crack propagation, although its effectiveness diminishes as sacrificial anodes degrade. The framework provides a predictive and computationally efficient tool for assessing MIC-induced damage over extended times, with potential applications in the integrity and life assessment of metallic structures operating in aggressive microbial environments.

</details>

### [49] [Radio Follow Up of a Sub-threshold GRB in the Sky Localization Area of GW241125](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20885)
*Natalie Gottschlich,Alessandra Corsi,S. Bradley Cenko,Divyajyoti,James DeLaunay,Derek B. Fox,Tanner O'Dwyer,Samuele Ronchini*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究报告了在LIGO第四观测运行期（O4）探测到的一次双黑洞（binary black hole, BBH）合并事件GW241125_010116与Swift BAT-GUANO探测到的一次亚阈值伽马射线暴（gamma-ray burst, GRB）S241125n在时间和空间上的对应关系。通过对该区域进行甚大阵列（VLA）射电后随观测、Swift/XRT数据重新分析及光学上限约束，将可能存在的相对论性喷流（relativistic jet）的各向同性动能（isotropic kinetic energy）限制在≲3×10⁵⁰ erg（n_ISM=1.0 cm⁻³条件下）。本文还讨论了射电后随观测在判断BBH-GRB关联中的挑战与诊断能力，并对未来LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA第五观测运行期（O5）及下一代地面设施时代的相关射电研究给出了展望。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自费米卫星（Fermi satellite）发现与GW150914在时间上对应的候选伽马射线暴（γ-ray burst, GRB）以来，电磁暂现源（electromagnetic transient）与双黑洞（binary black hole, BBH）合并产生的引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）信号之间的关联已有多起报道但争议不断。本研究旨在通过射电后随观测，评估GW241125_010116与亚阈值GRB S241125n之间关联的物理合理性，并约束BBH合并可能发射的相对论性喷流（relativistic jet）的能量。

Method: 利用卡尔·G·央斯基甚大阵列（Karl G. Jansky Very Large Array, VLA）对Swift BAT-GUANO定位区域进行射电后随巡天；重新分析Swift/XRT对该天区的观测数据；结合光学波段的上限观测结果，对可能存在的相对论性喷流（relativistic jet）的各向同性动能（isotropic kinetic energy）进行约束。

Result: 在假设星际介质（interstellar medium, ISM）密度n_ISM=1.0 cm⁻³的条件下，将可能存在的相对论性喷流（relativistic jet）的各向同性动能（isotropic kinetic energy）上限约束为≲3×10⁵⁰ erg。

Conclusion: 下一代探测网络如宇宙探索者（Cosmic Explorer）和爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）结合下一代射电干涉仪如下一代甚大阵列（next-generation VLA）和平方千米阵列（Square Kilometre Array, SKA），将显著增强对双黑洞（binary black hole, BBH）的多信使（multi-messenger）后随观测能力，有望回答BBH是否通过迷你盘吸积（mini-disk accretion）驱动相对论性抛射物（relativistic ejecta）这一关键问题。

Abstract: Since the Fermi satellite's identification of a candidate $γ$-ray burst (GRB) temporally coincident with GW150914, several tentative, and often debated, associations between electromagnetic (EM) transients and gravitational-wave (GW) signals from binary black hole (BBH) mergers have been reported. One such event, S241125n (later confirmed as GW241125_010116), was identified during the fourth observing run (O4) of Advanced LIGO and found to be spatially (within large GW localization uncertainty) and temporally coincident with a subthreshold GRB detected by the Swift Burst Alert Telescope Gamma-ray Urgent Archiver for Novel Opportunities (BAT-GUANO). Here, we present results from a radio follow-up campaign targeting the BAT-GUANO localization region, carried out with the Karl G. Jansky Very Large Array (VLA). We also re-analyze Swift/XRT observations of the field, and combine these results with optical upper limits. Our analysis constrains the isotropic kinetic energy of a putative relativistic jet launched in the BBH merger to $\lesssim 3 \times 10^{50}$ erg for $n_{ISM} = 1.0 cm^{-3}$. We also discuss both the challenges and the diagnostic power of radio follow up in assessing candidate BBH-GRB associations, and present projections for analogous radio studies in the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA observing run 5 (O5), and in the era of next-generation ground-based instrumentation. The enhanced sensitivity and localization capabilities of detector networks such as Cosmic Explorer and the Einstein Telescope, paired with the enhanced sensitivity of next-generation radio interferometers such as the next-generation VLA and the Square Kilometre Array, will significantly strengthen coordinated multi-messenger follow-up of BBHs. These next-generation facilities are likely to provide an answer to whether BBHs host relativistic ejecta powered by mini-disk accretion.

</details>


### [50] [A New Scaling of Neutron Star Tidal Deformability for Directly Probing the Core Equation of State](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21402)
*Jian-Hao Shi,Bao-Jun Cai,Bao-An Li,Yu-Gang Ma*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过微扰方法建立中子星无量纲潮汐形变参数Λ与中心状态方程参数X ≡ P_c/ε_c之间的标度关系，从而允许直接利用引力波观测数据（如GW170817）探测中子星核心物态方程（EOS），无需依赖特定EOS模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究主要利用引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）观测推断的中子星（neutron star, NS）无量纲潮汐形变参数Λ约束近两倍核饱和密度处的致密物质压力，但核心物态方程（equation of state, EOS）在很大程度上难以通过旋近阶段引力波观测直接获取。

Method: 对以缩放内禀变量（scaled intrinsic variables）表示的无量纲恒星结构与潮汐响应方程进行微扰分析（perturbative analysis），无需引入任何具体EOS模型，从而建立Λ与中心EOS参数X ≡ P_c/ε_c之间的标度关系，并通过大量物理可行的EOS集合验证该关系。

Result: 发现了一个对EOS不敏感的（EOS-insensitive）标度关系，将Λ与中心EOS参数X联系起来；将其应用于GW170817等事件推断的潮汐形变参数，可直接确定X的值。此外，推导出了沿稳定质量-半径序列的最大质量中子星的严格下界Λ_{TOV} ≳ 9.2^{+1.2}_{-1.2}，定量表明即使最致密的稳定中子星也明显区别于黑洞（Λ_{BH}=0）。

Conclusion: 该发现揭示了旋近阶段潮汐形变参数与核心EOS之间先前未被认识到的联系，在引力波观测量与强引力框架下超致密物质的微观物理之间建立了直接关联，确立了旋近阶段潮汐形变参数作为中子星核心EOS的直接且对模型不敏感的（model-insensitive）探测工具。

Abstract: The dimensionless tidal deformability, $Λ$, of neutron stars (NSs), inferred from gravitational-wave (GW) observations, has thus far been used primarily to constrain the pressure of dense matter near twice nuclear saturation density, leaving the core equation of state (EOS) largely inaccessible to inspiral-phase GW observations. We show that the core EOS can be probed directly through $Λ$ using a perturbative analysis of the dimensionless stellar-structure and tidal-response equations formulated in terms of scaled intrinsic variables, without invoking any specific EOS model. We uncover a remarkable EOS-insensitive scaling relation between $Λ$ and the central EOS parameter $\mathrm{X}\equiv P_{\rm c}/\varepsilon_{\rm c}$, where $P_{\rm c}$ and $\varepsilon_{\rm c}$ denote the central pressure and energy density, respectively. The relation is validated against a broad ensemble of physically viable EOSs. Applying it to tidal deformabilities inferred from events such as GW170817 enables a direct determination of $\mathrm{X}$. We further derive a tight lower bound, $Λ_{\rm{TOV}}\gtrsim 9.2^{+1.2}_{-1.2}$, for maximum-mass NSs along stable mass-radius sequences, quantitatively demonstrating that even the most compact stable NSs remain distinctly separated from black holes, for which $Λ_{\rm{BH}}=0$. These findings reveal a previously unrecognized connection between inspiral-phase tidal deformability and the core EOS, establishing a direct link between GW observables and the microphysics of ultradense matter in the strong-gravity regime. The resulting scaling establishes inspiral-phase tidal deformability as a direct and largely model-insensitive probe of the EOS of NS cores.

### [51] [Subgrid Modelling for Relativistic Magnetohydrodynamics with Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21659)
*William Cook,Sebastiano Bernuzzi*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个基于机器学习（machine learning）的亚网格模型（subgrid model），用于特殊相对论磁流体力学（special relativistic magnetohydrodynamics），通过神经网络训练，在三维开尔文-亥姆霍兹不稳定性（Kelvin-Helmholtz instability）模拟中，以44倍加速实现了4倍分辨率下的磁场放大效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解磁场不稳定性（magnetic field instabilities）对触发小尺度湍流（small scale turbulent flow）及磁场重排的影响，对于双中子星并合的多信使观测（multimessenger observables）以及中子星和吸积盘中的角动量输运（angular momentum transport）至关重要。直接模拟这些不稳定性不可行，因此需要借助大涡模拟（large-eddy simulations）中的亚网格模型来纳入湍流效应。

Method: 采用神经网络（neural network）训练一个基于机器学习的亚网格模型，专门用于特殊相对论磁流体力学。通过先验测试（a priori tests）和后验测试（a posteriori tests），在三维开尔文-亥姆霍兹不稳定性的在线模拟（online simulations）中评估模型性能。

Result: 在低分辨率模拟中，该模型能够捕获4倍分辨率下模拟的磁场放大（magnetic field amplification）效果，同时实现了44倍的加速比。

Conclusion: 该结果表明，此类基于机器学习的方法可适用于中子星并合的广义相对论模拟（general relativistic simulations）及其他相关场景。

Abstract: Resolving the impact of magnetic field instabilities in triggering small scale turbulent flow and the associated rearrangement of the field is of critical importance in understanding multimessenger observables in binary neutron star mergers, and angular momentum transport in neutron stars and accretion disks. Direct simulation of these instabilities are unfeasible, however large-eddy simulations can incorporate the impact of this turbulence with a subgrid model. We present the first machine-learning-based subgrid model for special relativistic magnetohydrodynamics, trained using a neural network. We demonstrate its performance in online simulations of the 3D Kelvin-Helmholtz instability through both a priori and a posteriori tests. Evaluated in a low resolution simulation, our model captures magnetic field amplification of a simulation at 4 times the resolution with a speed-up of a factor 44. This demonstrates the applicability of such methods in general relativistic simulations of neutron star mergers and other scenarios.

### [52] [Finite-volume scheme for first-order viscoresistive relativistic magnetohydrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22691)
*Ruben Lier,Jay Armas,Oliver Porth*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 基于BDNK理论，本文实现了耗散性相对论性磁流体动力学（dissipative relativistic magnetohydrodynamics）的数值方案，其中一阶修正使方程因果且稳定，无需引入额外动力学变量。通过有限体积法处理能量、动量和磁场的耦合耗散，并在极端相对论极限下添加额外修正项，开发了有效的原始变量恢复方法，并通过解析基准和二维模拟验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相对论性耗散磁流体动力学（dissipative relativistic magnetohydrodynamics）的传统一阶公式（如Navier-Stokes类型）存在非因果性和不稳定性问题。BDNK理论提供了一阶修正方案，但其数值实现尤其在磁场耦合情形下尚不成熟。本文旨在填补这一空白，开发稳定、因果且高效的数值框架。

Method: 基于BDNK理论引入一阶耗散修正，采用有限体积法（finite-volume scheme）离散化方程，将磁场处理为一次形式荷（one-form charge）。在极端相对论极限下增加额外修正项以确保系统的稳定性和因果性，并设计原始变量恢复（primitive-variable recovery）算法。

Result: 极小BDNK项可将扩散型方程转化为电报方程（telegrapher-type equations）；但在极端相对论极限下，需要额外修正才能实现稳定且因果的行为。通过解析基准测试和多种二维模拟验证了数值实现的有效性。

Conclusion: 基于BDNK理论的耗散性相对论磁流体动力学数值方案是可行的，能够在不引入额外动力学变量的条件下保持因果性和稳定性。所提出的原始变量恢复方法高效可靠，数值验证结果支持该框架的适用性。

Abstract: We present a numerical implementation of dissipative relativistic magnetohydrodynamics based on Bemfica-Disconzi-Noronha-Kovtun (BDNK) theory, in which first-order corrections render the equations causal without introducing additional dynamical variables. We show how these corrections can be incorporated in a finite-volume scheme describing the coupled dissipation of energy, momentum, and magnetic field, with the latter treated as a one-form charge. While a minimal set of BDNK terms can convert diffusive equations into telegrapher-type equations, we find that in the ultra-relativistic limit an additional correction is required for the system to behave in a stable and causal manner. With this set of equations, we develop an efficient method for primitive-variable recovery and validate the implementation through an analytical benchmark and various two-dimensional simulations.

</details>


### [53] [Fast targeted gravitational-wave followup search for compact binary mergers using GSTLAL pipeline](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22266)
*Leo Tsukada,Noah Zhang,Surabhi Sachdev,Shomik Adhicary,Chad Hanna,Prathamesh Joshi,Divya Singh*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于GstLAL管道进行引力波（gravitational wave）定向搜寻的方法，通过引入来自外部电磁触发器（electromagnetic triggers）的 sky localization 和 timing 信息，改进了标准似然比（likelihood ratio）排序统计量（ranking statistic），从而提高了对亚阈值（sub-threshold）引力波信号的探测效率。注射研究表明，该方法在保持虚警率（false alarm rate）控制的同时，显著提升了与给定 sky location 和 timing 一致的信号的探测效率，有助于多信使天文学（multi-messenger astronomy）中的快速电磁暂现源（electromagnetic transient）后随观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有标准全天区搜寻（all-sky search）在探测与电磁暂现源（如短伽马射线暴，short gamma-ray bursts）相关联的亚阈值引力波信号时灵敏度不足，亟需一种能利用外部电磁触发器提供的 sky localization 和 timing 信息来增强探测效率的方法。

Method: 在GstLAL检测管道中，修改标准的似然比排序统计量，加入一个 sky localization 先验（prior），从而将分析聚焦于电磁触发器指定的特定天区。该方法同时整合了外部触发器的 timing 信息，实现对亚阈值引力波信号的定向搜寻。

Result: 注射研究（injection studies）表明，与标准全天区搜寻配置相比，该方法对与给定 sky location 和 timing 一致的信号显著提升了探测效率，同时有效控制了虚警率（false alarm rate）。

Conclusion: 该定向搜寻框架能够实现电磁暂现源的快速后随（rapid follow-up），在先进引力波探测器时代有力推动多信使天文学（multi-messenger astronomy）的发展。

Abstract: We present a novel method to conduct targeted gravitational-wave searches for compact binary mergers using the GstLAL inspiral pipeline. By incorporating sky localization and timing information from external electromagnetic triggers, we enhance the sensitivity of the search for sub-threshold gravitational-wave signals associated with events such as short gamma-ray bursts. Our approach modifies the standard likelihood ratio ranking statistic to include a sky localization prior, allowing for a more focused analysis on specific regions of the sky. We demonstrate the effectiveness of this method through injection studies, comparing the performance of the targeted search against the standard all-sky search configuration. The results show a significant improvement in detection efficiency for signals consistent with the provided sky location and timing, while maintaining control over false alarm rates. This targeted search framework enables rapid follow-up of electromagnetic transients, facilitating multi-messenger astronomy efforts in the era of advanced gravitational-wave detectors.

### [54] [Unified Mass-Scaled QPO Signatures of Kerr Sen Black Holes from Stellar Mass to Supermassive Sources](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22446)
*Orhan Donmez,G. Mustafa*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本研究通过数值模拟分析了Kerr-Sen黑洞周围邦迪-霍伊尔-利特尔顿（BHL）吸积过程的激波锥形态、质量吸积率变化及类准周期振荡（QPO）时间行为，发现电荷相关时空形变会改变振荡频率与相干性，产生接近3:2和2:1的共振谐波结构。通过质量反比缩放，模拟频率与多个黑洞候选体的观测QPO数据吻合良好，表明Kerr-Sen黑洞激波锥振荡可能为不同质量黑洞的时变特征提供统一解释框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Kerr-Sen黑洞的电荷相关时空形变如何影响BHL吸积过程的动力学特征（激波锥形态、质量吸积率变化、类QPO时间行为），并检验其能否为不同质量黑洞系统的观测时变特征提供统一理论解释。

Method: 数值模拟Kerr-Sen黑洞在赤道面上的相对论性BHL吸积流，采用两种自旋参数（a = 0.9 M 和 a = 0.5 M）；对数值计算得到的质量吸积率信号计算功率谱密度（PSD）并进行多分量洛伦兹拟合，以识别主导类QPO模式；通过质量反比缩放将模拟频率与恒星质量、中等质量及超大质量黑洞系统的观测QPO进行比较。

Result: Kerr-Sen时空形变会偏移特征频率、改变振荡模式的相干性，并产生接近3:2和2:1的近共振谐波结构。模拟频率与GRS 1915+105、IGR J17091-3624、M82 X-1、NGC 5408 X-1、RE J1034+396、1H 0707-495及ESO 113-G010等多个黑洞候选体的观测QPO数据合理吻合。

Conclusion: Kerr-Sen黑洞激波锥振荡可能为跨质量尺度的黑洞时变特征提供统一解释框架，并有助于约束观测上尚未完全确定的质量与自旋参数。联合流体动力学与时变诊断是一种有前景的方法，可用于评估Kerr-Sen几何偏离Kerr时空的程度是否可在经验上被区分。

Abstract: In this study, we numerically investigate Bondi-Hoyle-Lyttleton (BHL) accretion around Kerr-Sen black holes and examine how the charge-related deformation of the spacetime affects the shock-cone morphology, the variation of the mass accretion rate, and the quasi-periodic oscillation (QPO)-like temporal behavior. The relativistic BHL flow is solved numerically in the equatorial plane for two different black hole spin parameters, a = 0.9 M and a = 0.5 M. From the numerically computed mass accretion rate signal, we calculate the power spectral density (PSD) and perform multi-component Lorentzian fits to identify the dominant QPO-like modes excited around the black hole. The results show that the Kerr-Sen deformation shifts the characteristic frequencies, changes the coherence properties of the oscillation modes, and produces near-resonant harmonic structures close to 3:2 and 2:1. By using inverse mass scaling, the numerically computed frequencies are compared with observed QPOs from stellar-mass, intermediate-mass, and supermassive black hole systems. In particular, reasonable agreement between the numerical simulation results and observations is found for the sources GRS 1915+105, IGR J17091-3624, M82 X-1, NGC 5408 X-1, RE J1034+396, 1H 0707-495, and ESO 113-G010. This comparative analysis indicates that Kerr-Sen black hole shock-cone oscillations may provide a unified framework for interpreting timing features over a broad range of black hole masses and may additionally contribute to constraining the mass and spin parameters of sources whose properties are not yet fully established observationally. These findings further imply that combined hydrodynamical and timing diagnostics constitute a promising approach for assessing the extent to which deviations associated with the Kerr-Sen geometry can be empirically distinguished from those of the Kerr spacetime.

</details>


### [55] [Crust glass formation reveals the neutron star birth properties in IGR J17480-2446](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22227)
*D. A. Baiko,A. I. Chugunov*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文论证了IGR J17480-2446中子星外壳中低热导率玻璃层的形成是吸积导致原始冷晶壳层破裂的自然结果，由此确定吸积物质质量约为2.4×10⁻⁶ M☉，证实该中子星处于极早期吸积阶段，并推测其可能诞生于电子俘获超新星（electron-capture supernova）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释IGR J17480-2446这一低质量X射线双星（low-mass X-ray binary）中反常缓慢的爆发后外壳冷却现象——此前研究提示其外壳存在低热导率层（可能由玻璃构成），但该层的形成机制尚未被阐明。

Method: 基于吸积诱导原始冷晶壳层破裂的物理图像，论证玻璃层的形成是这一过程的自然结果，并利用该模型估算吸积物质质量；同时结合自旋态（spin state）与热态（thermal state）分析推测中子星的诞生属性。

Result: 确定吸积物质质量ΔM ≈ 2.4×10⁻⁶ M☉，确认该中子星处于极早期再循环（recycling）阶段；自旋与热态分析显示其具有通常与“再循环”中子星相关的奇特诞生属性。

Conclusion: IGR J17480-2446的玻璃层形成是吸积导致原始冷晶结构破坏的必然结果；其自旋与热态特征暗示该中子星可能形成于电子俘获超新星。

Abstract: IGR J17480-2446 is a low-mass X-ray binary, harboring an exceptional accreting pulsar (a neutron star) with an unusual spin frequency of 11 Hz and a very slow post-outburst crust cooling. The former may imply that it is observed at an early stage of recycling, while the latter was shown to indicate the presence in the outer crust of a low thermal conductivity layer, possibly made of glass. Here we argue that the glass layer formation is a natural result of accretion induced failure of pristine cold crystal crust. This allows us to determine the mass of the accreted material as $ΔM \approx 2.4\times 10^{-6}~M_\odot$, confirming very early accretion stage for this neutron star. An analysis of spin and thermal state reveals a peculiar set of neutron star birth properties which is commonly associated with `recycled' neutron stars, i.e.\ those that have been experiencing prolonged periods of accretion from a companion. We speculate that such birth properties may represent the outcome of neutron star formation in an electron-capture supernova.

### [56] [Are Cosmological Data Excluding Sterile Neutrinos or Only the Fully Thermalized Limit?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21518)
*Artur Ladeira,Rafael C. Nunes,Eleonora Di Valentino,Stefano Gariazzo*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文对轻惰性中微子（light sterile neutrino）进行了宇宙学再评估，发现当前观测数据并不普遍排除惰性中微子，而是主要压制完全热化（fully thermalized）或高布居场景；部分填充的惰性中微子模型（如Dodelson-Widrow类型）仍然与观测兼容，宇宙学约束主要指向有效丰度的强烈抑制而非物理质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验当前宇宙学观测是否普遍排除惰性中微子（sterile neutrinos），还是仅仅约束完全热化的情况，从而澄清惰性中微子作为一个理论类别是否仍然可行。

Method: 考虑三种惰性中微子场景：完全热化物种（FTS）、温度相对活跃中微子背景受抑制的热遗迹（DTS）以及相空间归一化降低的Dodelson-Widrow-like（DW）惰性中微子。在ΛCDM和CPL动态暗能量框架下，结合Planck CMB、DESI DR2 BAO以及PantheonPlus和Union3 Ia型超新星样本进行约束分析。

Result: 基线数据组合（不含局域H₀先验）下，FTS场景在两种宇宙学模型中都强烈不受支持；加入局域H₀先验后，ΛCDM+FTS可容纳高局域H₀值并与标准ΛCDM在统计上竞争，但惰性中微子质量仍与零一致。DW场景与观测广泛兼容，DTS场景所受宇宙学压力最弱。总体而言，宇宙学数据主要要求强烈抑制有效惰性丰度（m_eff^sterile），而对物理惰性质量约束明显较弱。

Conclusion: 当前观测并不普遍排除惰性中微子，而是对完全热化或高布居场景施加强烈压力，强调在解释宇宙学约束时必须考虑生成历史和相空间分布（phase-space distribution）。

Abstract: We present a cosmological reassessment of light sterile-neutrino scenarios, examining whether current observations exclude sterile neutrinos as a class or primarily constrain the fully thermalized case. We consider three distinct realizations: (i) a fully thermalized sterile species (FTS), (ii) a thermal relic with a suppressed temperature relative to the active neutrino background (DTS), and (iii) a Dodelson-Widrow-like (DW) sterile neutrino with reduced phase-space normalization. Constraints are derived within both LambdaCDM and the CPL dynamical dark-energy framework using combinations of Planck CMB data, DESI DR2 BAO measurements, and the PantheonPlus and Union3 Type Ia supernova samples. For baseline data combinations without a local H0 prior, the FTS scenario is strongly disfavored in both cosmological models. Adding the local H0^DN prior allows LambdaCDM+FTS to accommodate the high local H0 value and become statistically competitive with standard LambdaCDM once SNIa data are included, although the sterile-neutrino mass remains consistent with zero. By contrast, partially populated sterile-neutrino scenarios remain viable: the DW realization is broadly compatible with current observations, while the DTS scenario yields the weakest cosmological pressure among the cases considered. Overall, cosmological data mainly require a strongly suppressed effective sterile abundance, leading to tight constraints on m_eff^sterile while allowing substantially weaker bounds on the physical sterile mass. We conclude that current observations do not generically exclude sterile neutrinos, but rather place strong pressure on fully thermalized or highly populated scenarios, highlighting the importance of production history and phase-space distribution when interpreting cosmological constraints.

</details>


### [57] [Loss-Cone-Limited Dark Matter Accretion onto Early Black Hole Seeds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20964)
*Brian Zhang,Grant J. Mathews*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个无碰撞暗物质（collisionless dark matter）被早期黑洞种子捕获的损失锥（loss-cone）理论框架，发现在典型NFW型暗物质晕（NFW-like halos）中暗物质捕获无法解释早期超大质量黑洞（supermassive black holes, SMBHs）的快速增长；但在稀有致密环境中，高效的角动量再填充可实现辐射暗的上包络增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高红移处超大质量黑洞的迅速出现挑战了标准重子物质增长通道，因此有必要重新评估非重子增长机制的可能性。

Method: 建立了无碰撞暗物质被早期黑洞种子捕获的损失锥框架，具体包括：Eddington反演的NFW型晕（Eddington-inverted NFW-like halos）、相对论直接捕获边界、角动量输运的轨道平均福克-普朗克（orbit-averaged Fokker-Planck）处理；原初黑洞（primordial black holes, PBHs）作为大质量扰动体；三轴或混沌向心轨道（triaxial/chaotic centrophilic orbits）的无碰撞再填充作为现象学上包络通道。

Result: 普通恒星弛豫在基准高红移种子下导致的暗物质驱动增长可忽略不计；原初黑洞驱动的粒状性在足够致密的晕中可实现量级增长，三轴或全损失锥供给可产生早期爆发；但在自洽计算中增长通常受供给限制，低角动量相空间储层耗竭后捕获率崩溃，黑洞质量饱和；固定背景NFW模型会高估持续增长；TNG50校准的NFW基准即使在乐观再填充假设下增长也可忽略不计。

Conclusion: 无碰撞暗物质捕获在一般NFW型晕中不太可能解决早期超大质量黑洞增长问题，但在稀有致密环境中且角动量再填充高效时，可提供辐射暗的上包络增长。

Abstract: The rapid appearance of supermassive black holes at high redshift motivates a reassessment of non-baryonic growth channels. We develop a loss-cone framework for collisionless dark-matter (DM) capture by early black-hole seeds, with particular attention to phase-space depletion and refilling. The calculation combines Eddington-inverted NFW-like halos, a relativistic direct-capture boundary, and an orbit-averaged Fokker-Planck treatment of angular-momentum transport. Primordial black holes (PBHs) are treated as massive perturbers whose refilling strength depends on both their abundance and individual mass. Collisionless refilling by triaxial or chaotic centrophilic orbits is included as a phenomenological upper-envelope channel. We show that ordinary stellar relaxation gives negligible DM-driven growth for the fiducial high-redshift seeds. PBH-driven granularity can yield order-of-magnitude growth in sufficiently compact halos, while triaxial or full-loss-cone supply can produce a rapid early burst. In the self-consistent calculations, however, the evolution generally becomes supply-limited. Once the accessible low-angular-momentum phase-space reservoir is depleted, the capture rate collapses and the black-hole mass saturates. Fixed-background NFW calculations therefore overestimate sustained growth, especially in the full-loss-cone limit. A TNG50-calibrated NFW benchmark gives negligible growth even under optimistic refilling assumptions. Collisionless DM capture is therefore unlikely to solve early SMBH growth in generic NFW-like halos, but it can provide a radiatively dark upper envelope in rare compact environments with efficient angular-momentum refilling.

### [58] [Dark Energy in the DESI Era: A Brief Review of Evidence, Beyond-$Λ$CDM Interpretations, and Tensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21826)
*Tian-Nuo Li,Guo-Hong Du,Hao Wang,Yun-He Li,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本综述基于DESI的重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillation）测量数据，评估了标准ΛCDM模型是否足以描述晚期宇宙膨胀历史。分析表明，当结合宇宙微波背景（cosmic microwave background）和Ia型超新星（type Ia supernova）数据时，观测显示出偏离ΛCDM模型的迹象，表现为动力学暗能量（dynamical dark energy, DDE）行为，其状态方程（equation of state）穿越幻影分界线（phantom divide）。文章讨论了DDE偏好强度对参数化和数据集组合的依赖性，以及残余系统误差与数据集内部张力对解读的影响。此外，综述区分了多种超出ΛCDM的物理机制（如相互作用暗能量、非最小耦合引力、非标准暗物质）在背景层次产生的相似膨胀历史，并指出它们对当前宇宙学张力（特别是H₀、S₈和Σmν）可能有不同的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DESI最新的重子声学振荡测量为检验标准ΛCDM模型是否充分描述晚期宇宙膨胀历史提供了关键新线索。当与宇宙微波背景和Ia型超新星数据结合时，观测显示明显偏离ΛCDM模型，表现为动力学暗能量（DDE）且状态方程穿越幻影分界线（即quintom行为），这促使综述当前证据及其对超出ΛCDM物理的可能含义。

Method: 本综述系统评估了DESI数据引发的DDE迹象的现状，分析了偏好DDE的强度如何依赖于所采用的参数化（parametrization）和数据集组合，以及残余系统误差（residual systematics）或数据集间的内部张力（internal tensions）如何影响其解读。进一步在背景层次（background level）讨论了多种可产生相似膨胀历史的超出ΛCDM的机制。

Result: 研究表明，DESI数据在不同参数化和数据集组合下对DDE的偏好强度存在差异；残余系统误差和数据集内部张力可能影响解读。多种超出ΛCDM的物理场景（包括相互作用暗能量、非最小耦合引力、非标准暗物质）可在背景层面产生相同的有效偏离w=-1的现象，但不同新物理解读对当前宇宙学张力（尤其是H₀、S₈和Σmν）的影响可能不同。

Conclusion: DESI提出的问题不仅在于暗能量是否随时间演化，更关键的是在精确宇宙学（precision cosmology）框架下，如何将新物理场景与系统误差区分开来。

Abstract: Recent baryon acoustic oscillation measurements from DESI provide important new clues for reassessing whether the standard $Λ$CDM model offers a sufficient description of the late-time expansion history of the Universe. When combined with cosmic microwave background and type Ia supernova data, these measurements show an apparent departure from the $Λ$CDM model, commonly described as dynamical dark energy (DDE) with equation of state crossing the phantom divide (i.e., quintom behavior). This review examines the current status of the DESI-motivated indications for DDE and their possible implications for physics beyond $Λ$CDM. We discuss how the strength of the preference for DDE depends on the adopted parametrization and dataset combination, and how residual systematics or internal tensions among datasets may affect its interpretation. At the background level, several mechanisms beyond $Λ$CDM can produce similar expansion histories. We therefore further discuss how the same effective departure from $w=-1$ may arise from physically distinct scenarios, including interacting dark energy, non-minimally coupled gravity, and non-standard dark matter. Meanwhile, these different new-physics interpretations may have different implications for current cosmological tensions, especially those involving $H_0$, $S_8$, and $\sum m_ν$. In conclusion, the question posed by DESI is not merely whether dark energy evolves with time, but rather how, within the framework of precision cosmology, to disentangle new physics scenarios from systematic errors.

### [59] [Wave-optics imprints of dark matter subhalos on strongly lensed gravitational waves. II. Saddle images and detectability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21519)
*Shin'ichiro Ando*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文扩展了强透镜引力波中波光学干涉对暗物质次结构（substructure）的探测方法，从最小像（minimum image）推广至鞍点像（saddle-point image），并提出一种时域数值方法解决鞍点放大因子计算中的数值不稳定性。基于冷暗物质（cold dark matter）次结构蒙卡模拟，发现次结构在两种宇称像中均引入百分比量级的振幅与相位调制，且平均（去）放大率因宇称而异。匹配滤波分析表明，对于LISA（Laser Interferometer Space Antenna）可观测的典型源，62%的实现在5σ以上显著性实现联合探测，乐观强透镜率预测下整个任务期间可获10–20次次结构探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强透镜引力波中的波光学干涉为探测暗物质次结构提供了新的干涉测量探针，但此前仅针对最小像计算了次结构印记；将这一方法推广至鞍点像并评估其在LISA任务中的联合可探测性，是填补该空白的关键动机。

Method: 采用时域方法（time-domain method）计算鞍点像的放大因子，以克服等到达时间轮廓开放及次结构信号为大项小差带来的数值困难；结合冷暗物质次结构实现的蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）系综，对两种宇称像的振幅与相位调制进行统计评估，并通过解调宏像干涉与匹配滤波分析（matched-filter analysis）分离并检验次结构信号。

Result: 次结构在最小像与鞍点像中均产生百分比量级的调制，且宇称分裂表现为最小像净放大、鞍点像净缩小。匹配滤波后联合探测在62%的实现在5σ以上，对应LISA任务期内10–20次次结构探测事件；条件要求源靠近透镜焦散线（caustic），冲击参数y_src ≲ 0.1。

Conclusion: 强透镜引力波是暗物质次结构在10⁴–10⁷ M⊙尺度上的一种灵敏且互补的探针，这一尺度目前电磁观测无法触及；LISA任务有望通过该干涉途径实现显著的次结构探测。

Abstract: Wave-optics interference in strongly lensed gravitational waves is a new interferometric probe of dark matter substructure: a subhalo population threading a galaxy-scale lens imprints frequency-dependent distortions on the amplification factor of each macro image. In a companion paper (arXiv:2603.04267), we computed these imprints for the magnified minimum image. Here, we extend the calculation to the saddle-point image and we assess the detectability of the combined signal with the Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA). Evaluating the amplification factor at a saddle is numerically delicate, because the equal-arrival-time contours are open and the subhalo signal is a small difference of large terms; we present a time-domain method that resolves it. Across a Monte Carlo ensemble of cold dark matter subhalo realizations, subhalos induce percent-level amplitude and phase modulations in both image parities, while the mean (de)magnification splits by parity: the minimum is net magnified and the saddle net demagnified. Demodulating the macro-image interference recovers the per-image modulations, and a matched-filter analysis that projects out the lens parameters yields a combined detection above $5σ$ in $62\%$ of realizations for fiducial massive-black-hole-binary sources of total mass $\sim10^{6}\,M_\odot$ at redshift $1.5$, provided the source lies close to the lens caustic at small impact parameter $y_{\rm src}\lesssim0.1$. Folding these naive per-event significances through optimistic strong-lensing rate forecasts yields $10$-$20$ substructure detections over the LISA mission. Strongly lensed gravitational waves are thus a sensitive, complementary probe of substructure at $10^{4}$-$10^{7}\,M_\odot$ scales inaccessible to electromagnetic observations.

### [60] [Dark Matter as an Inflationary Relic in Warm Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22147)
*Swagat S. Mishra,Umang Kumar,Suratna Das,Varun Sahni*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文发现暖暴涨（warm inflation）在强耗散机制下不会耗尽暴胀子凝聚（inflaton condensate），残留的暴胀子会在势能二次极小值附近演化为冷暗物质（cold dark matter），其质量被暗物质丰度约束在约0.02 MeV。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为暖暴涨通过将暴胀子能量耗散为辐射会完全耗尽暴胀子凝聚，但本文试图检验这一预期是否在观测允许的参数区域内成立。

Method: 在强耗散暖暴涨场景中引入耗散比 $Q=\Upsilon/(3H)$ 在暴胀结束后随系统趋近辐射主导而快速下降的机制，从而抑制向热浴的能量转移；采用最小可重整化势（minimal renormalizable potential）和 $Υ\propto T^3$ 的耗散系数进行分析。

Result: 残留的暴胀子凝聚在势能二次极小值附近表现为冷暗物质；当前宇宙学数据允许强耗散同时暴胀子质量几乎不受暴胀观测量约束；暗物质丰度将其质量固定为 $m \approx 0.02\,{\rm MeV}$，更大质量会导致宇宙过闭合；向类物质标度（matter-like scaling）的转变在太初核合成（BBN）之前完成，避免了长寿命暴胀子暗辐射组分。

Conclusion: 残留暴胀子暗物质将暖暴涨的暴胀后动力学转化为其参数空间上新的晚期宇宙学约束，从而拓展了暖暴涨的检验窗口。

Abstract: Warm inflation is usually expected to completely deplete the inflaton condensate by dissipating its energy into radiation. We show that this expectation fails in a simple and observationally viable regime. In a strongly dissipative warm inflationary scenario, the dissipative ratio, $Q=Υ/(3H)$, can fall rapidly after the end of inflation as the system approaches radiation domination, thereby suppressing further energy transfer to the thermal bath. This leads to a residual inflaton condensate, which subsequently evolves as an effectively non-dissipative scalar field. For potentials with a stable quadratic minimum, this remnant inflaton manifests as a cold dark matter component. We establish this mechanism for the minimal renormalizable potential, with a dissipative coefficient $Υ\propto T^3$. In this case, current cosmological data allow strong dissipation while leaving the inflaton mass weakly constrained by inflationary observables. The observed dark matter abundance then fixes its mass to be $m \approx 0.02\,{\rm MeV}$, while larger masses overclose the Universe. The transition to matter-like scaling occurs well before BBN, avoiding a long-lived inflaton dark radiation component. Relic inflaton dark matter therefore turns the post-inflationary dynamics of warm inflation into a new late time constraint on its parameter space.

### [61] [Phantom-Divide Crossing in Exponentially Coupled Quintessence and the Role of Neutrino-Mass Freedom](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22023)
*Jincheng Wang,Hongwei Yu,Puxun Wu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用Planck CMB、DESI BAO和DES-Dovekie超新星数据，研究了具有指数势和指数耦合至冷暗物质（CDM）的quintessence暗能量模型（CQ-EXP模型）。当中微子质量总和固定为0.06 eV时，数据偏好耦合参数β≠0（>3σ显著性），尤其支持β<0分支，此时有效暗能量状态方程（EoS）穿越phantom divide（w=-1）。当中微子有效质量参数自由时，对耦合的偏好减弱，CQ-EXP模型与w₀wₐCDM模型无法统计区分；当固定中微子质量时，模型偏好phantom-divide crossing；当允许负有效质量时，无crossing的版本也可有效解释观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究具有指数势和指数耦合至冷暗物质的quintessence暗能量模型（CQ-EXP模型）是否被当前宇宙学观测数据所支持，尤其关注中微子质量参数的变化对模型约束的影响。

Method: 使用Planck CMB、DESI BAO和DES-Dovekie超新星观测数据，对CQ-EXP模型进行贝叶斯统计推断，并分别固定中微子质量总和（0.06 eV）和释放有效中微子质量参数两种情况进行分析。

Result: 当固定中微子质量总和时，数据以>3σ显著性偏好非零耦合参数β，尤其支持β<0分支（有效EoS穿越phantom divide）。当释放有效中微子质量参数时，数据偏好负值，同时弱化了耦合偏好；两种符号的β给出几乎相同的χ²_min值，且均略高于w₀wₐCDM模型，表明CQ-EXP模型与w₀wₐCDM模型无法统计区分。

Conclusion: 当中微子质量固定时，当前观测支持具有phantom-divide crossing的CQ-EXP模型。当中微子有效质量允许为负时，无crossing的CQ-EXP版本也可有效解释最新观测数据。

Abstract: We investigate a quintessence dark-energy model with an exponential potential and an exponential coupling to cold dark matter (CDM), hereafter referred to as the CQ-EXP model, using Planck CMB, DESI BAO, and DES-Dovekie supernova observations. We also examine how variations in the neutrino mass sector affect the constraints. When the neutrino mass sum is fixed at $\sum m_ν=0.06$ eV, the data favor a coupling between quintessence and CDM, with the coupling parameter $β$ deviating from zero at more than $3σ$. In particular, the observations favor the $β<0$ branch, where the energy transfer between the two dark sectors changes sign and the effective equation of state (EoS) of dark energy crosses the phantom divide, $w=-1$. When the effective neutrino mass parameter $\sum m_{ν,\mathrm{eff}}$ is treated as a free parameter, the data show a preference for negative values of $\sum m_{ν,\mathrm{eff}}$. This additional freedom weakens the preference for the coupling between quintessence and CDM and leads to nearly identical values of $χ^2_{\rm min}$ for the CQ-EXP models with $β>0$ and $β<0$, corresponding respectively to models without and with phantom-divide crossing in the effective EoS. Both values are slightly larger than that obtained in the $w_0w_a$CDM model, indicating that the CQ-EXP model cannot be statistically distinguished from the $w_0w_a$CDM model with the data considered here. Therefore, when $\sum m_ν$ is fixed, current observations favor the CQ-EXP model with phantom-divide crossing. In contrast, when negative values of $\sum m_{ν,\mathrm{eff}}$ are allowed, a CQ-EXP dark energy without crossing $w=-1$ can also provide an effective explanation of the latest observations.

### [62] [DSWIM:Efficient and Stable Deterministic Computation of Warm Inflation Perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23518)
*Umang Kumar*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过引入基于物理标度矩阵变换的确定性模块DSWIM，扩展了现有的暖暴胀扰动随机计算代码SWIM，在保持原初曲率功率谱精度的同时改善了数值适定性，并解决了随机与确定性实现之间的差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暖暴胀（warm inflation）中扰动由热涨落和量子涨落共同贡献，通常通过扰动方程的随机实现（stochastic realizations）计算（如开源代码SWIM）。基于相关矩阵演化（correlation matrix evolution）的确定性公式虽计算效率高，但当扰动变量在不同尺度上演化时会出现数值病态（ill-conditioned）问题，需要改进。

Method: 提出确定性模块DSWIM，引入基于有效哈勃标度（effective Hubble scaling）的物理标度矩阵变换（scaling matrix transformation），对扰动变量进行重新标度。该变换精确保持原初曲率功率谱（primordial curvature power spectrum），同时显著改善确定性演化方程的数值适定性。

Result: 在代表性暖暴胀模型上的测试表明：标度框架抑制了数值伪影，提高了确定性演化的鲁棒性，在保证精度的前提下实现了显著的计算加速。通过扩散矩阵（diffusion matrix）结构自然引出相关的热噪声贡献，解决了之前随机实现与确定性实现之间的差异。

Conclusion: DSWIM被确立为计算暖暴胀标量扰动（scalar perturbations）的数值鲁棒且计算高效的框架。

Abstract: Warm inflation perturbations are sourced by both thermal and quantum fluctuations and are commonly computed through stochastic realizations of the perturbation equations, as implemented in the publicly available code SWIM. Deterministic formulations based on correlation matrix evolution provide a computationally efficient alternative, but can become numerically ill-conditioned when the perturbation variables evolve over widely different scales. In this work, we extend SWIM by introducing a deterministic module, DSWIM, based on correlation matrix evolution. We introduce a physically motivated scaling matrix transformation derived from the effective Hubble scaling of the perturbation variables. The transformed system preserves the primordial curvature power spectrum exactly while substantially improving the numerical conditioning of the deterministic evolution equations. Using representative warm inflation models, we show that the scaled framework suppresses numerical artifacts, improves the robustness of the deterministic evolution, and yields substantial computational speedups while preserving accuracy. We further show that correlated thermal noise contributions arise naturally through the diffusion matrix structure, resolving previously observed discrepancies between stochastic and deterministic implementations. Our results establish DSWIM as a numerically robust and computationally efficient framework for computing warm inflation scalar perturbations.

</details>


### [63] [Unifying the Dark Sector with the New Generalized Chaplygin Gas: Observational Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23563)
*Abdulla Al Mamon,Andronikos Paliathanasis,Subhajit Saha*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文检验了一个具有红移依赖指数（redshift-dependent exponent）的广义Chaplygin气体模型（generalized Chaplygin gas model），将其作为统一描述宇宙暗能量（dark energy）和暗物质（dark matter）的单一流体组件，并利用Ia型超新星、宇宙计时器和DESI的重子声学振荡等晚期背景观测数据进行贝叶斯分析（Bayesian analysis）。结果表明，尽管该模型在联合似然（combined likelihood）上取值更高，但考虑自由参数数量后，贝叶斯证据（Bayesian evidence）和Akaike信息准则（Akaike Information Criterion）均表明该模型与ΛCDM模型在统计上不可区分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期宇宙学观测对暗能量和暗物质的统一描述提出了新需求，因此需要检验广义Chaplygin气体模型这类统一暗流体（unified dark fluid）框架的可行性。

Method: 将具有红移依赖指数的广义Chaplygin气体作为单一统一组分，利用Ia型超新星数据、宇宙计时器（cosmic chronometers）以及来自暗能量光谱仪器第二次数据发布（DESI DR2）的重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillations, BAO）数据，进行贝叶斯参数估计并与ΛCDM模型比较。

Result: 广义Chaplygin气体模型在联合似然值上系统地高于ΛCDM模型，但计入更多自由参数后，贝叶斯证据和Akaike信息准则均表明两个模型在统计上无法区分。

Conclusion: 在现有晚期背景观测数据约束下，具有红移依赖指数的广义Chaplygin气体模型与ΛCDM模型在统计上无显著差异，暗示其作为暗能量-暗物质统一描述的额外复杂性并未带来统计上的实质性改进。

Abstract: In light of recent cosmological observations, we examine a generalized Chaplygin gas model with a redshift-dependent exponent as a framework for describing the dark energy and dark matter content of the Universe. Specifically, we treat this fluid as a single unified component and test it against late-time background observational data. We employ Type Ia supernova data, cosmic chronometers, and baryon acoustic oscillations from the second data release of the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument. We perform a Bayesian analysis for parameter estimation and compare the model with $Λ$CDM. We find that the generalized Chaplygin gas provides systematically higher values of the combined likelihood; nevertheless, once the larger number of free parameters is taken into account, both the Bayesian evidence and the Akaike Information Criterion suggest that the model is statistically indistinguishable from $Λ$CDM.

### [64] [Mixed memories in Hopfield networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2504.04879)
*Véronique Gayrard*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文针对Hopfield记忆模型的能量函数局部极小值问题，通过构造“混合记忆（mixed memories）”这一构型集合，刻画了不同激活函数下局部极小值的结构，并在经典、密集和现代三种Hopfield模型中给出了保证混合记忆为动力学不动点的存储模式数量增长条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hopfield模型中存储模式（patterns）时会在能量函数中引入非预期的局部极小值，即虚假记忆（false memories）。尽管该现象自早期研究以来便已知晓，但除了一些基础情形外，此前仅依赖于数值模拟和非严格计算。

Method: 针对一般激活函数F，显式构造了一组称为混合记忆（mixed memories）的构型集合，用于刻画能量函数的局部极小值。随后针对三种典型模型（经典Hopfield模型（二次函数）、密集Hopfield模型（多项式函数）和现代Hopfield模型（指数函数）），分析了存储模式数量M随神经元数量N发散时的增长条件。

Result: 给出了三种模型中保证混合记忆为检索动力学（retrieval dynamics）不动点（fixed points）进而成为能量函数精确极小值的存储模式数量增长率条件。在此基础上提出猜想：在该参数条件下，所有局部极小值均为混合记忆。

Conclusion: 本文为Hopfield模型中的虚假记忆问题提供了严格的理论框架，通过混合记忆的构造将局部极小值分类与存储容量条件联系起来，从而在非基础情形下实现了对能量景观的严格刻画。

Abstract: We consider the class of Hopfield models of associative memory with activation function $F$ and state space $\{-1,1\}^N$, where each vertex of the cube describes a configuration of $N$ binary neurons. $M$ randomly chosen configurations, called patterns, are stored using an energy function designed to make them local minima. If they are, which is known to depend on how $M$ scales with $N$, then they can be retrieved using a dynamics that decreases the energy. However, storing the patterns in the energy function also creates unintended local minima, and thus false memories. Although this has been known since the earliest work on the subject, it has only been supported by numerical simulations and non-rigorous calculations, except in elementary cases.
  Our results are twofold. For a generic function $F$, we explicitly construct a set of configurations, called mixed memories, whose properties are intended to characterise the local minima of the energy function. For three prominent models, namely the classical, the dense and the modern Hopfield models, obtained for quadratic, polynomial and exponential functions $F$ respectively, we give conditions on the growth rate of $M$ which guarantee that, as $N$ diverges, mixed memories are fixed points of the retrieval dynamics and thus exact minima of the energy. We conjecture that in this regime, all local minima are mixed memories.

</details>


### [65] [Slot decomposition of continuous Box-Ball Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20948)
*Inés Armendáriz,Pablo Blanc,Pablo A. Ferrari,Davide Gabrielli*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文将离散盒球系统（Box Ball System）中的槽分解（slot decomposition）推广到连续情形，研究一类分段常数函数及其关联游走（walk）的极小值上回程（excursions over past minima）。在权重函数属于 L¹ 空间的条件下，证明了槽分解对应一个泊松过程（Poisson process），并以非对称电报过程（asymmetric telegraph process）为例计算了其强度测度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将离散盒球系统中已建立的槽分解方法推广到连续情形，从而在连续设定下识别孤子（soliton）并刻画其统计性质。

Method: 将分段常数函数 η 对应的关联游走 ξ 的路径分解为极小值上回程（excursions over past minima），每个回程进一步分解为由孤子高度（soliton height）决定的权重乘积形式；引入二维点配置（point configuration），分别以位置和孤子高度为坐标表示每个孤子。

Result: 当权重函数满足 L¹ 条件时，游走 ξ 的槽分解构成一个泊松过程。以 Kac 引入的非对称电报过程为例，给出了该泊松过程的强度测度（intensity measure）的具体表达式。

Conclusion: 本文成功将槽分解方法从离散盒球系统推广到连续情形，建立了连续游走与泊松过程之间的联系，为后续研究动力学性质奠定了基础。

Abstract: We study a piecewise constant function $η:\mathbb R\to\{-1,1\}$ with a finite number of discontinuities in any interval. We assume that the associated walk $ξ:\mathbb R\to\mathbb R$ satisfying $ξ'(x)=η(x)$, pinned by $ξ(0)=0$, has finite length excursions over past minima. This is the continuous generalization of an initial ball configuration in the discrete Box Ball System introduced by Takahashi and Satsuma, where solitons of integer sizes $k\ge1$ are identified.
  We extend the slot decomposition developed by Ferrari, Nguyen, Rolla and Wang in the discrete setting to the continuous case. Each soliton of $ξ$ is represented by a point in two dimensional space, one coordinate for position and the other for the soliton height, mapping $ξ$ to a point configuration.
  We consider a distribution on walks given by a product measure on the decomposition of the path into excursions over past minima. Excursions are distributed as products of their solitons weights, which are determined by the soliton heights. We show that when the weight function is in $L^1$ the slot decomposition of $ξ$ is a Poisson process. This extends to the continuous case an approach of Ferrari and Gabrielli. As an example, we compute the intensity measure of the Poisson process associated to the asymmetric telegraph process introduced by Kac. In a forthcoming paper we discuss the dynamic properties.

</details>

### [67] [Kinetics of template-directed multistate copolymerization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22448)
*Pierre Gaspard*

Main category: q-bio.QM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对分子机器（如聚合酶或核糖体）介导的模板定向多态共聚（template-directed multistate copolymerization）过程的精确求解方法。通过引入矩阵分解（matrix factorization）形式的向后迭代（backward iteration）与向前迭代（forward iteration），该动力学方程在长时间极限下可精确求解平均生长速度、复制链的序列概率、局部单体概率及比例，计算效率显著优于传统数值方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模板定向多态共聚过程涉及多种构象或激活状态的分子机器，其动力学方程通常难以精确解析求解，亟需高效且精确的理论方法以理解其机理。

Method: 采用矩阵分解假设（matrix factorization ansatz）将动力学方程转化为一个迭代矩阵函数系统（iterated matrix function system），由沿模板序列反向迭代与正向迭代两部分构成。

Result: 该方法可精确求解平均生长速度、复制链序列概率、局部单体概率及比例，并通过数值实例证明了其计算速度远优于常规计算方法。

Conclusion: 所提出的矩阵分解迭代方法为分析模板定向多态共聚过程提供了一种高效精确的解析框架，在长时间极限下具有显著的计算优势。

Abstract: We consider processes of template-directed multistate copolymerization by molecular machines such as polymerases or ribosomes, having multiple states of conformation or activation. We show that the kinetic equations of these processes can be exactly solved for the mean growth velocity, the sequence probabilities of the grown copy, and the local probabilities and fractions of monomeric units in the copy. Asymptotically, in the long-time limit, the kinetic equations are solved with a matrix factorization ansatz in terms of a backward iteration, forming an iterated matrix function system, and a complementary forward iteration, both running along the template sequence. The iterative method is very significantly faster than usual computational methods, as demonstrated with a numerical example.

</details>


### [68] [Kinetics of multistate DNA polymerases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22452)
*Pierre Gaspard*

Main category: q-bio.QM

TL;DR: 本文将先前开发的用于模板指导多态共聚动力学（template-directed multistate copolymerization）的迭代数学方法，应用于具有多种结构状态的聚合酶（polymerase）催化DNA复制动力学。针对T7 DNA聚合酶的两态动力学模型，计算了拷贝沿模板生长的平均速度（mean velocity）、DNA复制的错误概率（error probability）以及沿模板序列的碱基配对局部概率（local probabilities）。结果表明，该迭代方法比常规数值模拟方法快百万倍以上，并在模板异质性（template heterogeneities）均匀化近似下也获得了相关结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将已有的多态共聚迭代数学方法拓展至更复杂的生物聚合系统，即具有多结构状态的聚合酶催化的DNA复制过程，以克服传统数值模拟方法计算效率低下的问题。

Method: 采用迭代数学方法对T7 DNA聚合酶的两态动力学模型进行分析，求解拷贝生长平均速度、复制错误概率及碱基配对局部概率等关键动力学量。

Result: 获得了DNA复制过程的平均速度、错误概率和沿模板序列的碱基配对局部概率；该迭代方法的计算速度比常规数值模拟方法快百万倍以上；在模板异质性均匀化近似下也得到了相应结果。

Conclusion: 该迭代数学方法可高效、准确地分析具有多结构状态聚合酶的DNA复制动力学，显著优于传统数值模拟方法，并为理解模板异质性对复制过程的影响提供了近似分析框架。

Abstract: In the present paper, we apply the iterative mathematical method previously developed for the kinetics of template-directed multistate copolymerization to the kinetics of DNA replication by polymerases having multiple structural states. In particular, we study a two-state kinetic model for the T7 DNA polymerase. We obtain the mean velocity for the growth of the copy along the template, the error probability of DNA replication by the polymerase, and the local probabilities of base-pair formation along the template sequence. Furthermore, we show that the iterative method is more than a million times faster than usual numerical simulation methods. Results are also obtained in the approximation of homogenization of template heterogeneities.

</details>

### [69] [Charged kaon and proton multiplicities in semi-inclusive deep-inelastic scattering with 11 GeV electrons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20745)
*P. Bosted,W. Armstrong,H. Bhatt,D. Dutta,R. Ent,D. Gaskell,S. Jia,E. Kinney,H. Mkrtchyan,S. Ali,R. Ambrose,D. Androic,C. Ayerbe Gayoso,A. Bandari,V. Berdnikov,D. Bhetuwal,D. Biswas,M. Boer,E. Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本研究报告了在Jefferson Lab利用电子束轰击液氢和液氘靶进行的半单举深度非弹性散射（SIDIS）实验中，带电Kaon（K⁺, K⁻）和质子（p）的产额倍数（multiplicities）及其方位角调制的测量结果。实验测量了从低横动量（P_t）到“软”中心区域（soft central region）的运动学范围，并将结果与DSS碎裂函数（fragmentation functions）和Lund蒙特卡洛（Lund Monte Carlo）预言进行了比较。结果表明，K⁻的倍数显著低于理论预言，而质子的倍数在低不变质量平方（W²）区域远高于横动量依赖（TMD）预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通过测量带电Kaon和质子的SIDIS产额倍数及其方位角分布，检验横动量依赖因子化（transverse-momentum-dependent factorization）在相关运动学区域的适用性，并利用实验数据验证现有理论模型（如DSS碎裂函数和Lund模型）的准确性。

Method: 在Jefferson Lab Hall C使用10.2和10.6 GeV电子束轰击10厘米长的液氢和液氘靶，利用HMS和SHMS谱仪分别探测电子和强子。测量范围覆盖轻子变量0.3<x<0.6和3<Q²<6 GeV²，以及强子变量0.3<z<0.7和P_t<0.6 GeV。对每个（x, Q², z, P_t）箱内，将产额倍数拟合为M₀[1+Acos(φ^*)+Bcos(2φ^*)]形式，提取常数项M₀和方位角调制系数A、B。

Result: K⁺的M₀值与DSS碎裂函数预言基本一致，但K⁻的M₀值显著低于预言。Kaon的方位角调制系数A和B均与零一致。质子与π介子的倍数比在最低W²区域比TMD预言高出一个数量级以上，随着W²增加差异缩小至约两倍。质子与氘靶结果无显著差异，且这些趋势与Lund蒙特卡洛预言一致。质子的A系数平均约为0.01且恒为正，B系数与零一致。

Conclusion: 实验数据表明，现有DSS碎裂函数对K⁻的产额描述存在偏差；质子在低W²区域的倍数显著高于TMD因子化预言，说明该运动学区域中其他非因子化过程占据主导；所有观察趋势与Lund蒙特卡洛模型一致，显示该模型在该实验条件下具有较好的描述能力。

Abstract: Measurements of SIDIS multiplicities for charged kaons and protons from proton and deuteron targets are reported on a grid of hadron kinematic variables $0.3<z<0.7$ and $P_{t}<0.6$ GeV for leptonic variables $0.3<x<0.6$ and $3<Q^2<6$ GeV$^2$. Data were acquired in 2018-2019 at Jefferson Lab Hall C with 10.2 and 10.6~GeV electron beams impinging on 10-cm-long liquid hydrogen and deuterium targets. Electrons (hadrons) were detected in the HMS (SHMS) spectrometers. Multiplicities were fitted for each bin in $(x,~Q^2,~z,~P_{t})$ as $M_0[1+A\cos(φ^*)+B\cos(2φ^*)]$. The kaon kinematic range spans the regions where transverse-momentum-dependent factorization can be applied in SIDIS, and a `soft' central region where other processes are of critical importance. The kaon to pion ratios of $M_0$ are in reasonable agreement with predictions using the DSS fragmentation functions for $K^+$, but are mostly well below them for $K^-$. The kaon azimuthal modulations are consistent with zero. The kinematic range for protons is centered on the `soft' central region. The proton-to-pion multiplicity ratios are more than an order-of-magnitude larger than TMD predictions at the lowest value of $W^2$, decreasing to as little as a factor of two at the highest value of $W^2$. No significant difference is observed between proton and deuteron targets. These trends are consistent with Lund Monte Carlo predictions. The proton values of $A$ are consistently positive, with an average value of approximately 0.01, while $B$ is consistent with zero.
