Torassa,K. Trabelsi,F. F. Trantou,I. Tsaklidis,M. Uchida,I. Ueda,T. Uglov,K. Unger,Y. Unno,K. Uno,S. Uno,P. Urquijo,Y. Ushiroda,S. E. Vahsen,R. van Tonder,K. E. Varvell,M. Veronesi,A. Vinokurova,V. S. Vismaya,L. Vitale,V. Vobbilisetti,R. Volpe,M. Wakai,S. Wallner,M. -Z. Wang,A. Warburton,M. Watanabe,S. Watanuki,C. Wessel,X. P. Xu,B. D. Yabsley,S. Yamada,W. Yan,W. P. Yan,J. Yelton,K. Yi,J. H. Yin,K. Yoshihara,C. Z. Yuan,J. Yuan,L. Yuan,Y. Yusa,L. Zani,F. Zeng,M. Zeyrek,B. Zhang,X. Zhao,V. Zhilich,J. S. Zhou,Q. D. Zhou,X. Y. Zhou,L. Zhu,R. Žlebčík*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文报告了利用 Belle II 实验首次在 $B^0\toπ^0π^0$ 衰变中测量到混合诱导的电荷-宇称（CP）破坏。通过一种利用 $B^{0}\overline{B}{}^0$ 对量子纠缠的新分析方法，测量了混合诱导 CP 破坏系数 $S_{π^{0}π^{0}}$ 和直接 CP 破坏系数 $C_{π^{0}π^{0}}$，其精度仅需传统分析方法二十分之一的数据量，从而显著改进了对夸克混合矩阵中 CP 破坏相位 $φ_2$ 的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 夸克跃迁中的 CP 破坏测量能为现有理论提供严格检验，并敏感探测超出标准模型的新粒子或相互作用。此前在 $B^0\toπ^0π^0$ 衰变中尚未测量混合诱导的 CP 破坏。

Method: 利用 Belle II 实验在 SuperKEKB 非对称能量电子-正电子对撞机上收集的 190 million 个 $Υ(4S)\to B^{0}\overline{B}{}^0$ 事件。采用一种利用 $B^{0}\overline{B}{}^0$ 对量子纠缠（quantum entanglement）的新方法，能够在无需重建 $B^0 \to π^0π^0$ 衰变位置的情况下进行衰变时间依赖（decay-time-dependent）分析。

Result: 测得混合诱导 CP 破坏系数 $S_{π^{0}π^{0}} = 0.61^{+0.75}_{-0.79}\,(\mathrm{stat}) \pm 0.11\,(\mathrm{syst})$，直接 CP 破坏系数 $C_{π^{0}π^{0}} = 0.05 \pm 0.28\,(\mathrm{stat}) \pm 0.07\,(\mathrm{syst})$。该精度在传统分析方法下需要二十倍的数据量才能达到。

Conclusion: 这些结果利用远少于先前认为必要的数据量，显著改进了来自 $B \to ππ$ 衰变对夸克混合矩阵（quark-mixing matrix）中 CP 破坏相位 $φ_2$ 的约束。

Abstract: Measurements of charge-parity (CP) violation in quark transitions provide stringent tests of the current theory and sensitive probes of particles or interactions beyond it. We report the first measurement of mixing-induced CP violation in $B^0\toπ^0π^0$ decays. The measurement uses 190 million $Υ(4S)\to B^{0}\overline{B}{}^0$ events collected with the Belle II experiment at the SuperKEKB asymmetric-energy electron-positron collider. A new approach that exploits the quantum entanglement of the $B^{0}\overline{B}{}^0$ pair enables a decay-time-dependent analysis without reconstructing the $B^0 \to π^0π^0$ decay position. We measure the mixing-induced CP-violating coefficient to be $S_{π^{0}π^{0}} = 0.61^{+0.75}_{-0.79}\,(\mathrm{stat}) \pm 0.11\,(\mathrm{syst})$, attaining a precision that would require a data set twenty times as large with a conventional analysis. We also measure the direct CP-violating coefficient to be $C_{π^{0}π^{0}} = 0.05 \pm 0.28\,(\mathrm{stat}) \pm 0.07\,(\mathrm{syst})$. These results substantially improve the constraints from $B \to ππ$ decays on the CP-violating phase $φ_2$ of the quark-mixing matrix using far less data than had previously been assumed necessary.

</details>


### [71] [Analysis note: Long-range near-side correlation in $e^+e^-$ with $W$-boson-pair events at 183-209 GeV with ALEPH archived data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21094)
*Tzu-An Sheng,Yu-Chen Chen,Yi Chen,Kyle Sun,Jason Chiu,Michael Peters,Marcello Maggi,Austin Baty,Anthony Badea,Chris McGinn,Jesse Thaler,Gian Michele Innocenti,Jingyu Zhang,Paoti Chang,Yen-Jie Lee*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于ALEPH探测器在LEP2计划中采集的e⁺e⁻对撞数据（质心能量√s = 183–209 GeV），测量了两粒子方位角关联。在高多重数（>50）下观测到类似脊状（ridge-like）的调制结构，与蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo, MC）预测存在偏差。进一步通过傅里叶分解得到谐波系数vₙ，发现多重数≥30时，类v₂符号由负转正，同样偏离MC基准。该结果旨在区分长程近侧关联（long-range near-side correlations）的两种可能起源：W⁺W⁻过程导致的复杂色弦结构，或高多重数本身的末态效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前在LEP2数据（√s ≤ 209 GeV）中发现，高多重数e⁺e⁻对撞事件的两粒子方位角关联与MC预言存在偏差，提示即使在最简单的对撞系统中也可能出现长程近侧关联。然而，这种关联究竟是源于W⁺W⁻过程中的复杂色弦配置，还是仅仅由更高碰撞能量导致的末态粒子数增加所致，尚不明确。本文通过增强W⁺W⁻过程贡献的测量来区分这两种解释。

Method: 利用ALEPH探测器在LEP2计划期间采集的e⁺e⁻对撞数据（√s = 183–209 GeV），测量两粒子方位角关联函数。关联函数在带电粒子多重数（charged-particle multiplicity）分档下，覆盖宽范围的赝快度（pseudorapidity）和全方位角（full azimuth）。进一步将关联函数展开为傅里叶级数（Fourier series），提取谐波系数vₙ并与归档MC样本进行比较。

Result: 在多重数高于50时，观测到类似脊状的调制结构，与MC参考预测存在偏差。多重数从30开始，有符号的类v₂代理量（signed v₂-like proxy）由负值转变为正值，同样偏离MC基准。

Conclusion: 高多重数e⁺e⁻碰撞中观测到的长程关联偏离MC预言，暗示现有MC模型可能未能充分描述相关物理机制。该结果为区分W⁺W⁻过程贡献与高多重数末态效应提供了关键实验依据。

Abstract: Events characterized by a high multiplicity of charged particles have been a central focus in the study of collective behavior across both large and small collision systems. A previous measurement of two-particle angular correlations in $e^+e^-$ collisions at center-of-mass energies up to $\sqrt{s} = 209$ GeV, using LEP2 data, revealed discrepancies with Monte Carlo (MC) predictions at high multiplicity, suggesting the possible emergence of long-range near-side correlations even in the simplest collision system. Unlike at lower energies, where quark-antiquark production dominates, $W^+W^-$ processes become increasingly important at multiplicities above 30. On the one hand, the observed excess in long-range correlations may reflect the more complex color-string configurations arising from $W^+W^-$ production. On the other hand, it can simply arise from the higher final-state multiplicity made possible by the increased collision energy, independent of the underlying production mechanism.
  To discriminate between these competing interpretations, we present a measurement of two-particle angular correlations in $e^+e^-$ collisions at $\sqrt{s} = 183-209$ GeV, with a focus on enhancing the contribution from $W^+W^-$ processes. The analysis uses data collected by the ALEPH detector during the LEP2 program. Correlation functions are evaluated across a broad range of pseudorapidities and full azimuth, in bins of charged-particle multiplicity. A ridge-like modulation is seen for multiplicity above 50, deviating from the MC reference. In addition, the correlation functions are further decomposed into a Fourier series, and the resulting harmonic coefficients $v_n$ are compared with predictions from the archived Monte Carlo sample. For multiplicity starting from 30, the signed $v_2$-like proxy goes from negative to positive, also deviating from the MC baseline.

</details>


### [72] [Towards LLM-Powered Automation of a Dark Matter Constraint Repository](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21658)
*Lanqing Yuan,Karthik Ramanathan*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于大语言模型（LLM）的自动化管线，用于从 arXiv 论文中提取暗物质（dark matter）限制曲线并生成代码形式的整合请求（pull request），在 346 篇论文的基准测试中实现了 90.5% 的耦合类型正确分类率与 0.33 dex 的中位耦合残差，但该管线生成的限制提案尚未被合并，凸显了 AI 生成科学数据的治理挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暗物质约束数据库（dark matter constraint repositories）是社区关键基础设施，为实验学家和理论学家提供共享的现有约束框架。然而，最广泛使用的数据库由个人志愿者维护，随着新结果发布速度加快，这种模式面临可持续性风险。

Method: 作者构建了一个大语言模型（LLM）管线：监控 arXiv，从论文中提取限制曲线（limit curves），将其整合为代码，并自动发起拉取请求（pull request, PR）供人工审核。该方法将每次提取视为带噪声的样本，通过共识投票（consensus voting）进行校准；引入物理约定标准化层（canonicalization layer），借助智能物理助手 Get Physics Done (GPD) 实现；并设计了评分方法，将真正的提取误差与不可比性（non-comparability）区分开。

Result: 在 346 篇论文的基准测试中（以上游维护的数据库本身作为真实标签），管线对耦合类型的正确分类率达 90.5%，中位耦合残差（coupling residual）为 0.33 dex（其中 48% 的曲线误差在 2 倍以内），平均质量范围覆盖率（mass-range coverage）为 76%。困难集中于具有特殊约定的稀有耦合类型（宏平均残差 1.1 dex）。管线已部署并生成了限制提案，但尚未有任何提案被合并。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了 LLM 在自动维护科学数据库方面的潜力，但也揭示了剩余难点主要来自稀有耦合类型的非标准约定。更重要的是，AI 生成科学数据的治理（governance）本身仍是一个未解决的问题。

Abstract: Dark matter constraint repositories are critical community infrastructure, giving experimentalists and theorists a shared landscape of existing bounds. Yet the most widely-used repositories are maintained by individual volunteers, creating a sustainability risk as the pace of new results accelerates. We present a large language model (LLM) pipeline that monitors arXiv, extracts limit curves from papers, integrates them as code, and opens pull requests (PRs) for human review. On a 346-paper benchmark whose ground truth is the upstream-curated repository itself, the pipeline classifies the coupling type correctly for 90.5% of papers and reaches a median coupling residual of 0.33 dex (a factor of two for 48% of curves), with 76% mean mass-range coverage. This is driven by treating each extraction as a noisy sample reconciled through consensus voting, a physics convention canonicalization layer built with the agentic physics assistant Get Physics Done (GPD), and a scoring methodology that separates genuine extraction error from non-comparability. The remaining difficulty is concentrated in rare coupling types with idiosyncratic conventions (macro-averaged residual 1.1 dex). The pipeline is deployed and has generated limit proposals; none have merged. Governance of AI-generated scientific data is itself an unsolved problem.

</details>


### [73] [Accelerating Discovery: Model-Agnostic Likelihoods for the Reinterpretation of Particle Physics Results and their Application to the Belle II $B^{+}\to K^{+}ν\barν$ Measurement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22215)
*Lorenz Gärtner*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本论文开发并验证了一种基于可分发似然函数（distributable likelihoods）的高能物理实验数据重解释方法，该方法通过重新加权重建与运动学变量的联合分布，在保持统计严谨性和系统不确定性的前提下大幅降低计算成本，并成功应用于Belle II实验的B^+→K^+νν̄测量，为模型无关似然函数的公开共享树立了开放科学先例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理实验的结果天然依赖于特定假设（hypothesis-dependent），理论模型的激增导致理论发展与实验验证之间出现速度不匹配，亟需对现有实验结果进行重解释（reinterpretation）。现有方法面临两难：完整的重分析需要巨大的计算资源和实验专业知识，而简化方法则因忽略运动学变化和系统不确定性而牺牲准确性。

Method: 该方法通过重新加权（reweighting）重建与运动学变量的联合分布，权重为备择假设与零假设的理论预测之比。从基于直方图的似然函数（histogram-based likelihood）出发，该方法为任意理论模型生成更新后的模板（templates），同时保持变量间的相关性和系统不确定性（systematic uncertainties）。

Result: 该方法通过示例验证，并应用于Belle II实验的B^+→K^+νν̄测量（该测量与标准模型存在2.7σ的张力）。共呈现两项分析：一是弱有效理论（Weak Effective Theory, WET）重解释，用于约束Wilson系数（Wilson coefficients）；二是通过B^+→K^+X双体衰变寻找轻新物理（light new physics）。

Conclusion: 所生成的模型无关似然函数（model-agnostic likelihoods）的公开共享，为实验粒子物理学中的开放科学（open science）树立了重要先例。该方法通过促进快速理论验证，推动了实验数据访问的民主化，提升了科研投资的科学回报，并推进了高能物理中的FAIR数据原则（FAIR Data principles）。

Abstract: Experimental results in high-energy physics are inherently hypothesis-dependent, as collider analyses are designed to test specific theoretical frameworks. The proliferation of theoretical models creates a mismatch between the pace of theory development and experimental validation, motivating the reinterpretation of existing results in terms of alternative hypotheses. Existing strategies face limitations: full reanalysis requires enormous computational resources and experimental expertise, while simplified methods sacrifice accuracy by neglecting kinematic variations and systematic uncertainties.
  This thesis develops, validates, and applies a novel reinterpretation method that preserves statistical rigour while dramatically reducing computational requirements, enabling rapid inference on alternative theoretical parameters through distributable likelihoods.
  The method reweights the joint distribution of reconstruction and kinematic variables according to the ratio of theoretical predictions of alternative to null hypotheses. Starting from a histogram-based likelihood, this produces updated templates for any theoretical model while preserving correlations and systematic uncertainties. The method is validated through examples and applied to the Belle II $B^+ \to K^+ ν\barν$ measurement ($2.7σ$ tension with the Standard Model). Two analyses are presented: a Weak Effective Theory reinterpretation constraining Wilson coefficients, and a light new physics search via ${B^+ \to K^+ X}$ two-body decays.
  The public release of the resulting model-agnostic likelihoods establishes an important precedent for open science in experimental particle physics. By facilitating rapid theoretical validation, this approach democratizes experimental data access, enhances scientific return on investments, and advances FAIR Data principles in high-energy physics.

</details>

X. Zhou,Y. Z. Zhou,A. N. Zhu,J. Zhu,K. Zhu,K. J. Zhu,K. S. Zhu,L. X. Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,M. Zhuge,J. H. Zou,J. Zu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于BESIII探测器采集的约100.87亿J/ψ事例，通过J/ψ→γη'、η'→π⁺π⁻η过程搜索η→e^±μ^∓这一带电轻子味味破坏衰变，未发现信号，在90%置信水平下给出分支比上限为6.8×10⁻⁷，将此前最好限制提升一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 带电轻子味味破坏（charged lepton flavor violating, CLFV）过程在标准模型（Standard Model）中被强烈压制，实验上观测到任何信号都将是超出标准模型的新物理（new physics）的确凿证据。η→e^±μ^∓衰变是研究轻子味破坏的重要探针之一，摘要旨在通过更高统计量的实验数据搜索该稀有衰变。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器在质心能量√s=3.097 GeV处采集的约(10.087±0.044)×10⁹个J/ψ事例，选取J/ψ→γη'、η'→π⁺π⁻η的级联衰变过程，通过对末态粒子重建和运动学拟合（kinematic fit）筛选候选事件，在信号区域进行无偏统计检验（blind analysis），并在90%置信水平（confidence level, C.L.）下使用CLs方法设定分支比上限。

Result: 未观察到显著信号，在90%置信水平下给出η→e^±μ^∓衰变分支比的上限为6.8×10⁻⁷。与先前实验最好结果相比提升了一个数量级（improved by one order of magnitude）。

Conclusion: 该工作利用BESIII探测器的大统计量J/ψ数据，将η→e^±μ^∓衰变分支比上限从之前水平压低至6.8×10⁻⁷（90% C.L.），是目前该衰变模式最严格的实验限制，进一步缩小了轻子味破坏（lepton flavor violation, LFV）现象的可能参数空间。

Abstract: Based on $(10.087 \pm 0.044) \times 10^{9}~J/ψ$ events collected at the center-of-mass energy $\sqrt{s} = 3.097$~GeV with the BESIII detector, we search for the charged lepton flavor violating decay $η\to e^{\pm}μ^{\mp}$ through the process $J/ψ\to γη'$ with $η' \to π^{+} π^{-} η$. No signal is observed, and an upper limit on the branching fraction is determined to be $\mathcal{B}(η\to e^{\pm}μ^{\mp}) < 6.8 \times 10^{-7}$ at the 90\% confidence level. This result improves the previous best limit by one order of magnitude.

</details>


### [75] [Searches for resonant and nonresonant multi-Higgs production in ATLAS and CMS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22461)
*Emmanouil Vourliotis*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文综述了大型强子对撞机（LHC）上ATLAS和CMS实验关于多希格斯粒子产生（multi-Higgs production）的最新搜索结果，涵盖希格斯玻色子自耦合测量、三重希格斯产生对四次耦合的敏感性，以及重标量粒子共振搜寻等方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 希格斯玻色子自耦合的测量是LHC项目的核心物理目标之一，它直接决定希格斯势能（Higgs potential）的形状，并对超出标准模型（BSM）的新物理具有敏感性，因此系统研究多希格斯产生过程至关重要。

Method: 通过希格斯玻色子对（Higgs pair）产生过程探测三线性自耦合（trilinear self-coupling），通过三重希格斯产生（triple Higgs production）探测四次耦合（quartic coupling）；同时利用重标量衰变到双希格斯或希格斯加新标量的共振搜寻，覆盖多种末态（final states）的共振与非共振产生模式。

Result: 展示了ATLAS和CMS实验在多希格斯产生搜寻方面的最新实验结果，涉及共振（resonant）和非共振（nonresonant）两种产生模式。

Conclusion: 这些多希格斯产生搜寻结果为希格斯势能形状的精确测量和BSM新物理的探寻提供了重要实验约束。

Abstract: The measurement of the Higgs boson self-coupling is one of the key physics goals of the LHC program, providing direct access to the shape of the Higgs potential and offering sensitivity to physics beyond the Standard Model (BSM). Higgs pair production probes the trilinear self-coupling, while triple Higgs production is sensitive to the quartic coupling. In addition, resonant searches for heavy scalars decaying to pairs of Higgs bosons or to a Higgs boson and a new scalar are motivated by a broad class of BSM models. Recent results on multi-Higgs production searches from the ATLAS and CMS experiments at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) are presented, covering both resonant and nonresonant production modes across a variety of final states.

</details>

Zhuge,J. H. Zou,J. Zu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用BESIII探测器在BEPCII对撞机上收集的26 fb⁻¹数据，在3.510至4.946 GeV范围内的47个质心能量点上，通过研究e⁺e⁻ → p p̄反应的玻恩截面（Born cross section），寻找衰变到p p̄末态的粲偶素（charmonium）或其类似态，并分析质子角分布提取电磁形状因子（electromagnetic form factor）。观测到ψ(3770)→p p̄衰变（显著性6.6σ），以及4.2 GeV附近的结构（对ψ(4160)或Y(4230)假设的显著性分别为4.6σ和4.8σ，目前无法区分）。此外，在大类时动量转移（time-like squared momentum transfer）区域，以更高精度提取了形状因子比值|G_E/G_M|和磁形状因子|G_M|的模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索粲偶素（charmonium）及其类似态衰变到p p̄末态的可能性，并通过质子电磁形状因子研究质子的内部结构，为开粲（open charm）能区的衰变机制提供实验约束。

Method: 基于BESIII探测器在BEPCII对撞机上记录的e⁺e⁻碰撞数据，总积分亮度26 fb⁻¹，覆盖3.510至4.946 GeV范围内47个质心能量点。通过测量e⁺e⁻→p p̄反应的玻恩截面寻找候选共振态，并利用质子极角分布（polar angle distribution）提取电磁形状因子比值|G_E/G_M|和磁形状因子|G_M|。

Result: ψ(3770)→p p̄衰变被观测到，显著性为6.6σ（包含系统不确定性）。在4.2 GeV附近观测到一个结构，对ψ(4160)假设的显著性为4.6σ，对Y(4230)假设的显著性为4.8σ（均包含系统不确定性），两种解释目前无法区分。在大类时动量转移区域，以更高精度提取了|G_E/G_M|和|G_M|。

Conclusion: 该研究为开粲能区粲偶素（charmonium）及其类似态的衰变机制以及质子的内部结构提供了重要的实验依据。

Abstract: We search for possible charmonium(-like) states decaying into the $p\bar{p}$ final state by studying the Born cross sections of the $e^+e^-\to p\bar{p}$ reaction, and we determine the proton electromagnetic form factors by analyzing the proton angular distribution. The measurement is performed using a sample of $e^+e^-$ collision data collected at 47 center-of-mass energies from 3.510 to 4.946 GeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 26 fb$^{-1}$, recorded by the BESIII detector collected at the BEPCII collider. The decay $ψ(3770)\to p\bar{p}$ is observed with a significance of 6.6$σ$ including systematic uncertainties. Furthermore, a structure near 4.2 GeV is observed with significances of $4.6σ$ or $4.8σ$ for the $ψ(4160)$ or $Y(4230)$ hypotheses including systematic uncertainties, respectively; these interpretations cannot presently be distinguished. In addition, the moduli of the form factor ratios $|G_{E}/G_{M}|$ and of the magnetic form factors $|G_{M}|$ are extracted by analyzing the proton polar angle distribution with higher precision at large time-like squared momentum transfer. These results provide important experimental insights into both the decay mechanisms of charmonium(-like) states in the open charm region and the internal structure of proton.

</details>

Zhuge,J. H. Zou,J. Zu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用BESIII探测器在BEPCII对撞机上收集的26 fb⁻¹积分亮度数据，采用能量扫描技术，在3.510至4.946 GeV之间的47个质心能量点测量了e⁺e⁻ → p p̄反应的玻恩截面（Born cross section）和有效形状因子（effective form factor）。首次在高时间动量转移（timelike momentum transfer）区域高精度地确定了电磁形状因子比率|G_E/G_M|的模和磁形状因子|G_M|的模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解粲偶素（charmonium）及其类粲偶素（charmonium-like）态在开粲阈值以上的性质，以及质子电磁形状因子（electromagnetic form factor）背后的动力学机制，是强子物理领域的重要问题。现有实验数据在这些方面仍存在不足，亟需高精度测量以提供关键约束。

Method: 采用能量扫描（energy-scan technique）技术，基于BESIII探测器在BEPCII对撞机上采集的等效积分亮度为26 fb⁻¹的实验数据，在3.510至4.946 GeV范围内选取47个质心能量（center-of-mass energy）点进行测量。通过分析质子极角（polar angle）的分布，提取电磁形状因子比率|G_E/G_M|和磁形状因子|G_M|的模。

Result: 在47个不同质心能量点上系统测量了e⁺e⁻ → p p̄反应的玻恩截面和有效形状因子。首次在大时间动量转移区域高精度地确定了电磁形状因子比率|G_E/G_M|的模和磁形状因子|G_M|的模。

Conclusion: 这些高精度测量结果为理解开粲阈值以上的粲偶素及类粲偶素态的本质提供了关键见解，并深化了对质子电磁形状因子背后动力学机制的认识。

Abstract: We report a measurement of the Born cross section and the effective form factor for the $e^+e^-\to p\bar{p}$ reaction at 47 center-of-mass energies between 3.510 and 4.946 GeV. The measurement is performed using the energy-scan technique and is based on data corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 26 fb\(^{-1}\) collected with the BESIII detector at the BEPCII collider. For the first time, the moduli of the electromagnetic form factor ratio $|G_{E}/G_{M}|$ and of the magnetic form factor $|G_{M}|$ are determined with high precision by analyzing the distribution of the polar angle of the proton at a large timelike momentum transfer.
  These results provide essential insights into the nature of charmonium(-like) states above the open-charm threshold and the dynamics underlying the proton electromagnetic form factors.

</details>


### [78] [Ferromagnetic broadband sensing of axionlike dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22814)
*Chenhao Peng,Dmitry Budker,Yuanning Gao,Xinran Li,Jia Liu,Wei Ji,Jing Shu,Zhenxing Tang,Liheng Wang*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种基于双共振模式（double-resonance mode）的悬浮磁体磁力计，其有效线宽比此前方案宽约三个数量级。结合硬磁体阵列与软铁磁屏蔽构成的混合铁磁平台（hybrid ferromagnetic platform），在40–3000 Hz频率范围内搜索轴子类暗物质（axionlike dark matter）的光子耦合$g_{a\gamma}$，在276 Hz附近达到最佳灵敏度$0.7\,\mathrm{fT}$，对应的$g_{a\gamma}$上限约为$10^{-7}\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$，比此前直接极限提高了四个数量级以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 悬浮粒子系统因其极低的耗散（dissipation）而对磁场和加速度具有超高灵敏度，在基础物理研究（尤其是轴子（axion）及轴子类粒子探测）中潜力巨大。现有方案虽灵敏度极高，但带宽受限；而轴子类暗物质（axionlike dark matter）搜索既要求高灵敏度，也需要大带宽（large bandwidth），因此需要开发同时满足这两者的新型磁力计。

Method: 设计并构建了一个基于工程化双共振模式（engineered double-resonance mode）的悬浮磁体磁力计（levitated magnet magnetometer），其有效线宽（effective linewidth）在最佳灵敏度下比此前方案宽约三个数量级。系统中引入硬磁体阵列（hard-magnet array）以增强轴子诱导信号（axion-induced signal），并采用软铁磁屏蔽（soft-ferromagnetic shielding）抑制环境磁噪声，从而形成一套混合铁磁平台（hybrid ferromagnetic platform）。

Result: 在40–3000 Hz频率范围内搜索轴子类暗物质的光子耦合$g_{a\gamma}$，建立了该频段新的直接极限。最佳灵敏度位于约276 Hz的上共振附近，磁力计达到0.7 fT的磁场分辨率，对应的$g_{a\gamma}$极限约为$10^{-7}\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$，比此前直接极限提升超过四个数量级。

Conclusion: 所展示的高带宽悬浮传感器（high-bandwidth levitated sensor）不仅为轴子类暗物质搜索提供了显著提升的灵敏度，还可能广泛应用于生物传感（biological sensing）和精密测量（precision measurements）等领域。

Abstract: Levitated particles have demonstrated ultrahigh sensitivity to magnetic fields and accelerations owing to their extremely low dissipation. Such systems have strong potential for fundamental physics research, particularly for the detection of axions and axionlike particles, well-motivated dark matter candidates spanning a broad mass range. In this context, both high sensitivity and large bandwidth are essential. Here, we demonstrate a levitated magnet magnetometer based on an engineered double-resonance mode, achieving an effective linewidth at its optimal sensitivity that is approximately three orders of magnitude broader than those of previous approaches. Together with a hard-magnet array that enhances the axion-induced signal and soft-ferromagnetic shielding that suppresses environmental magnetic noise, this system constitutes a hybrid ferromagnetic platform for axionlike dark matter searches. We search for axionlike dark matter through its photon coupling $g_{aγ}$ over the $40$-$3000\,\mathrm{Hz}$ frequency range and establish new direct limits in this frequency band. The best sensitivity is achieved near the upper resonance around $276\,\mathrm{Hz}$, where the magnetometer reaches a magnetic-field resolution of $0.7\,\mathrm{fT}$, corresponding to a limit of $g_{aγ}\sim10^{-7}\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$. At this frequency, this result improves upon previous direct limits by more than four orders of magnitude. The demonstrated high-bandwidth levitated sensor may also enable a broad range of applications, including biological sensing and precision measurements.

</details>


### [79] [Observations of Low-Energy-Electron Production and Experimental Characterization of the Test-Mass Charging Process in the LISA Gravitational Reference Sensor with the BART Experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22979)
*Francesco Dimiccoli,Francesco Venturelli,Valerio Ferroni,Antonella Cavalleri,Teodoro Klaser,Matteo Tomasi,Davide Dal Bosco,Enrico Verroi,Rita Dolesi William J. Weber*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本论文通过粒子加速器实验直接测试了低能二次电子（LEE）发射机制对LISA-like引力参考传感器中测试质量充电的影响，发现该机制是导致LISA Pathfinder实测充电噪声显著高于预发射模拟的关键物理过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LISA Pathfinder的测量结果表明，测试质量的泊松充电噪声远大于发射前模拟的预测值，说明早期模型缺少某些关键物理过程。低能二次电子（LEE）发射被提出作为影响充电和传感器静电响应的关键机制，但尚未被直接实验验证。

Method: 研究采用基于粒子加速器的实验，在LISA-like引力参考传感器（Gravitational Reference Sensor）几何结构中，测量质子诱导的测试质量充电随测试质量静电势的变化，以直接检验LEE假说。

Result: 实验证实了低能二次电子（LEE）发射机制的存在及其对测试质量充电过程的显著影响，解释了LISA Pathfinder观测到的充电噪声与预发射模拟之间的偏差。

Conclusion: LEE发射是影响LISA-like引力参考传感器中测试质量充电的关键物理过程，必须在未来的LISA任务中将其纳入准确的噪声建模，以降低加速度噪声并提高引力波探测灵敏度。

Abstract: The Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) is a space-based gravitational-wave observatory that uses free-falling test masses as inertial references to detect milliHertz frequency signals. Interactions between test masses and galactic or solar energetic particles cause charge buildup and Coulomb forces, source of acceleration noise that must be accurately modeled. LISA Pathfinder measurements showed that the Poissonian test mass charging noise was considerably larger than that in pre launch simulations, indicating missing physical processes in early models. Emission of low energy secondary electrons (LEE) from test mass and housing surfaces has been proposed as a key mechanism affecting charging and the sensor electrostatic response. We report a particle accelerator based experiment that directly tests the LEE hypothesis by measuring proton induced test mass charging in a LISA like Gravitational Reference Sensor geometry as a function of the test mass electrostatic potential.

### [80] [Recent Hadron Spectroscopy Results from the Belle and Belle II experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23170)
*Elisabetta Prencipe*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文报告了Belle~II实验在强子谱学（hadron spectroscopy）方面的最新进展，包括底偶素（bottomonium）、粲偶素（charmonium）、五夸克态（pentaquark）以及重子谱（baryon spectroscopy）的研究成果，并展示了Belle与Belle~II联合数据集（超过1.5 ab⁻¹）在实现前所未有精度方面的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用Belle~II实验积累的大统计量数据（积分亮度达575 fb⁻¹，已超过BaBar和Belle），结合Belle与Belle~II的联合数据集（超过1.5 ab⁻¹），推动强子谱学研究达到前所未有的精度，并探索新型强子态（如五夸克态）和激发态重子的结构。

Method: 在SuperKEKB非对称能量正负电子对撞机（asymmetric-energy e⁺e⁻ collider）上，Belle~II探测器采集数据，并与Belle数据集进行联合分析，利用大统计量样本进行强子谱学测量。

Result: 展示了Υ(10753)结构研究的新成果，进行了隐藏粲（hidden-charm）和隐藏奇异数（hidden-strangeness）五夸克态的搜索，并在重子谱学方面获得了Ω(2012)和激发的Λ_c态的最新研究进展。

Conclusion: Belle与Belle~II联合数据集具有显著的解析潜力，能够产出前所未有精度的结果，为未来强子谱学分析开辟了广阔前景。

Abstract: The Belle~II experiment, the major upgrade of the Belle detector, is currently collecting data at the SuperKEKB asymmetric-energy $e^+e^-$ collider in Tsukuba, Japan. With an integrated luminosity of 575\,fb$^{-1}$, Belle~II has already surpassed the maximum luminosity accumulated by both BaBar and Belle. Recent analyses combining Belle and Belle~II data sets have delivered results of unprecedented precision, demonstrating the strong potential of the unified data sample, which now exceeds 1.5\,ab$^{-1}$.
  In this contribution, recent advances in hadron spectroscopy are presented. Highlights include new results in bottomonium and charmonium physics, with particular emphasis on the structure of the $Υ(10753)$, searches for hidden-charm and hidden-strangeness pentaquarks, and the latest developments in baryon spectroscopy, including studies of the $Ω(2012)$ and excited $Λ_c$ states. Prospects for future spectroscopy analyses exploiting the full Belle and Belle~II data sets are also discussed.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Neutrino-nucleus cross-section measurements are needed to improve interaction modeling and to enable precision neutrino oscillation measurements in upcoming experiments such as the Deep Underground Neutrino Experiment (DUNE), Hyper-Kamiokande, and the Short-Baseline Neutrino program. Baryon-resonance neutrino interactions constitute a dominant contribution near the peak of the DUNE neutrino energy spectrum. We present the first measurement of muon neutrino charged-current resonance-like interactions on argon using transverse kinematic imbalance variables with the MicroBooNE detector. These observables are highly sensitive to the modeling of final-state interactions. This measurement probes kinematic imbalances using the reconstructed momenta of the muon, leading proton, and neutral pion. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,Z. Xu,S. Yadav,K. Yang,X. Yang,Y. Yang,Y. Yang,Z. Yang,Z. Yang,H. Yeung,H. Yin,X. Yin,C. Y. Yu,J. Yu,K. Yu,X. Yuan,Y Yuan,J. A. Zamora Saa,M. Zavertyaev,M. Zdybal,F. Zenesini,C. Zeng,M. Zeng,S. H Zeng,C. Zhang,C. Zhang,D. Zhang,J. Zhang,L. Zhang,Q. Z. Zhang,R. Zhang,S. Zhang,S. L. Zhang,Y. Zhang,Z. Zhang,J. Zhao,Y. Zhao,A. Zhelezov,S. Z. Zheng,X. Z. Zheng,Y. Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani,G. Zunica,X. Zuo*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于LHCb实验收集的9 fb⁻¹质子-质子对撞数据，对B±→π±μ+μ-衰变的分支比和CP不对称性进行了随双缪子质量平方q²变化的分段测量，并报告了与B±→K±μ+μ-衰变的分支比比值。测量结果与标准模型预测在1.4σ至3.8σ范围内一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: B±→π±μ+μ-衰变过程是味改变中性流（flavor-changing neutral current, FCNC）过程，在标准模型中仅通过圈图（loop-level）发生，对可能的新物理（new physics）信号敏感。通过分支比和CP不对称性（CP asymmetry）的分段（differential）测量，可严格检验标准模型预测并寻找超出标准模型（beyond the Standard Model, BSM）的迹象。

Method: 利用LHCb探测器记录的质心能量为7 TeV、8 TeV和13 TeV的质子-质子对撞数据，总积分亮度（integrated luminosity）为9 fb⁻¹。将双缪子质量平方q²划分为若干区间，分别测量B±→π±μ+μ-衰变的分支比（branching fraction）和CP不对称性，并在相同q²区间内报告与B±→K±μ+μ-衰变的分支比比值。

Result: 测量得到的分支比在统计上与标准模型（Standard Model, SM）预测相容，但一致性程度因模型假设的不同而在1.4倍标准差（σ）至3.8倍标准差之间变化。

Conclusion: 当前测量未发现与标准模型预测存在显著偏差，但一致性范围较宽，表明模型假设对结论有重要影响。这一结果为进一步精确检验标准模型和约束新物理参数空间提供了实验依据。

Abstract: Differential measurements of the branching fraction and $C\!P$ asymmetry of the decay $B^\pm\to π^\pmμ^+μ^-$ are performed in intervals of the dimuon mass squared, $q^2$, using proton-proton collision data corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 9 fb$^{-1}$ recorded by the LHCb experiment at centre-of-mass energies of 7 TeV, 8 TeV and 13 TeV. The ratios of the branching fractions of $B^\pm\to π^\pmμ^+μ^-$ and $B^\pm\to K^\pmμ^+μ^-$ decays are also reported in the same $q^2$ intervals. The measured branching fractions are compatible with the predictions of the Standard Model, with consistency varying between 1.4$σ$ and 3.8$σ$ depending on the model assumptions.

</details>


<div id='physics.acc-ph'></div>

# physics.acc-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [83] [Quantum noninvasive three-component beam-spin polarimetry in the Hadron Storage Ring of the Electron-Ion Collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22265)
*Frank Rathmann*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于SQUID的非侵入式极化计，利用束团集体磁偶极矩而非散射过程，在电子-离子对撞机（EIC）强子储存环（HSR）中实现对极化质子束的全斯托克斯矢量（P_x, P_y, P_z）实时监测，结合静态连续监测与动态自由感应衰减（FID）精测模式，可在约18秒（注入）至5分钟（平顶）内达到1%的极化测量精度，并可推广至氘核与³He束流及储存环电偶极矩（EDM）搜索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有极化测量依赖单粒子散射过程，无法获得纵向极化分量P_z（受宇称守恒限制），且对束流具有破坏性。亟需一种非侵入式、可连续监测且能完整重构三维极化矢量的方法，以服务于EIC高能极化物理实验及储存环电偶极矩（electric dipole moment, EDM）搜索需求。

Method: 利用六蛇（six-snake）晶格下同步粒子自旋调谐（spin tune）ν_s=1/2的性质，使面内自旋进动信号位于半倍回旋频率（~39 kHz），落入直流超导量子干涉仪（DC SQUID）频段。设计三通道拾取线圈——余弦-θ与正弦-θ鞍形环路测量横向分量，同轴轴向梯度计测量纵向分量——重构完整极化矢量。提供两种运行模式：静态模式（默认）实现连续非侵入监测，逐束团读取三个极化分量；动态模式通过纵向偏转器（longitudinal kicker）产生小角度倾转，触发自由感应衰减（free-induction-decay, FID）信号，经多次锁相倾转-π脉冲-回波-恢复循环及匹配滤波（matched filter）相干累加，实现高精度极化幅度测量，单次循环损耗仅约10⁻⁴。

Result: 设定倾转角α=30 mrad、极化度P=0.7、有效的均方根自旋调谐展宽σ_{ν_s}^{eff}=10⁻³（相干时间约2 ms）条件下，达到δP/P=1%测量精度所需的积分时间在注入阶段约为18秒，在平顶阶段约为5分钟。该方法可推广至氘核与³He束流，只需根据各粒子特有的自旋-磁因子进行调整。

Conclusion: 该SQUID极化计为非侵入式、连续运行的束流极化监测提供了完整解决方案，克服了传统散射极化测量法无法获得纵向极化分量的根本局限，且可扩展至多种核子束流，在储存环EDM搜索等前沿物理研究中具有重要应用前景。

Abstract: We propose a noninvasive SQUID-based polarimeter for the polarized proton beam in the Electron-Ion Collider (EIC) Hadron Storage Ring (HSR), exploiting the collective magnetic dipole moment of the bunches rather than scattering. The six-snake HSR lattice has synchronous-particle spin tune $ν_s = 1/2$, placing the in-plane spin-precession signal at half the revolution frequency ($\sim$39 kHz), in the DC SQUID band. Three pickup channels (cosine-$θ$ and sine-$θ$ saddle loops for the transverse components, a coaxial axial gradiometer for the longitudinal one) reconstruct the full polarization vector $(P_x, P_y, P_z)$ in two complementary modes. Static mode, the default for continuous noninvasive monitoring, reads all three components: $P_y$ at the revolution frequency and the residual in-plane components at $ν_s f_\mathrm{rev}$, bunch by bunch over an hours-long fill, including $P_z$, inaccessible to single-spin scattering polarimetry by parity conservation. Dynamic mode gives a precise polarization-magnitude measurement: a longitudinal kicker tips a small fraction of the polarization into the horizontal (ring) plane to produce a free-induction-decay (FID) signal, and many phase-locked tip-$π$-echo-restore cycles are summed coherently via a matched filter across all bunches, with $\mathcal{O}(α^2/π^2) \sim 10^{-4}$ loss per cycle, negligible over a full $δP/P = 1\%$ measurement. For tipping angle $α= 30$ mrad, polarization $P = 0.7$, and effective rms spin-tune spread $σ_{ν_s}^\mathrm{eff} = 10^{-3}$ (coherence time $\sim$2 ms), the integration time to reach $δP/P = 1\%$ is about 18 s at injection and 5 min at flattop. The architecture extends to deuteron and $^3$He beams via species-specific spin-magnetic factors, with applications to storage-ring EDM searches.

</details>


### [84] [Powder Spreading and Layer Deposition in Metal Powder Bed Fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22989)
*Antonello Astarita*

Main category: physics.acc-ph

TL;DR: 本章系统综述了粉末床熔融（Powder Bed Fusion, PBF）技术中粉末铺展与层沉积的机理，分析了粉末特性、工艺参数与设备架构对粉末床质量的影响，并讨论了离散元法（Discrete Element Method, DEM）建模、粉末循环利用以及基于数字孪生与数据驱动的未来优化方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粉末铺展与层沉积是粉末床熔融（PBF）技术的基础阶段，直接决定工艺稳定性与最终构件质量。深入理解粉末床形成机理对于提升金属增材制造（additive manufacturing）的可靠性与性能具有关键意义。

Method: 本章采用综述性分析方法，系统考察粉末特性（粒径分布、形貌、内聚力、流动性）、工艺参数（层厚、刮刀速度）及环境条件对粉末床质量的影响机制；同时评述了离散元法（Discrete Element Method, DEM）在粉末铺展建模与粉末床质量指标量化中的应用。

Result: 粉末床被定义为一种过程状态变量（process state variable），其关键特征——包括堆积密度（packing density）、表面覆盖率（surface coverage）、有效层厚（effective layer thickness）及空间均匀性（spatial homogeneity）——直接影响能量吸收、熔池稳定性（melt-pool stability）、缺陷形成与力学性能。

Conclusion: 粉末工程（powder engineering）在先进金属增材制造中的重要性日益凸显。未来发展方向包括过程监控、数字孪生（digital twins）及数据驱动优化策略，同时粉末循环利用与生命周期管理也是关键议题。

Abstract: Powder spreading and layer deposition are fundamental stages of Powder Bed Fusion (PBF) technologies and play a critical role in determining process stability and final component quality. This chapter examines the mechanisms governing powder-bed formation, highlighting the interactions between powder characteristics, process parameters, and machine architecture. Particular attention is devoted to the influence of particle size distribution, morphology, cohesion, flowability, layer thickness, recoater velocity, and environmental conditions on powder-bed quality. The resulting powder-bed is discussed as a process state variable whose characteristics, including packing density, surface coverage, effective layer thickness, and spatial homogeneity, directly affect energy absorption, melt-pool stability, defect formation, and mechanical performance. The chapter also reviews the application of the Discrete Element Method (DEM) for modelling powder spreading phenomena and quantifying powder-bed quality metrics. Finally, the role of powder reuse, lifecycle management, and future developments involving process monitoring, digital twins, and data-driven optimization strategies is discussed, emphasizing the growing importance of powder engineering in advanced metal additive manufacturing.

</details>

### [85] [Revisiting Theoretical Modeling of Seebeck Coefficient of Semiconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21879)
*Yuchao Hua*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文指出传统塞贝克系数（Seebeck coefficient）封闭模型中存在的热力学缺陷，包括电化学势与电势混淆、分布函数空间梯度计算中忽略导带底和费米能级依赖性，以及不当的热流表达。作者提出一种基于漂移-扩散方程（drift-diffusion equation）和索瑞效应（Soret effect）的替代方法，在开路条件下推导塞贝克系数模型。在近平衡情况下，该可逆模型（reversible model）消除了电子速度和弛豫项，理论上给出塞贝克系数下界，其声子拖曳项与基于玻尔兹曼输运方程（Boltzmann transport equation, BTE）的形式一致。对高掺杂硅的案例研究表明，该可逆模型预测与实验数据吻合良好，因其理论严谨、形式简洁且计算成本低，可作为可逆和近平衡条件下评估热电性质的有效替代方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有塞贝克系数封闭模型存在热力学缺陷，如电化学势（electrochemical potential）与电势（electrical potential）混淆、分布函数空间梯度计算中不合理地忽略导带底和费米能级依赖性，以及热流表达不当，需要提出一种理论上更严谨的替代模型。

Method: 基于漂移-扩散方程（drift-diffusion equation）和索瑞效应（Soret effect），在开路条件下推导塞贝克系数模型；在近平衡情况下恢复出可逆模型，消除电子速度和弛豫项；对高掺杂硅进行案例研究，将可逆模型、弹道模型（Landauer formulation）和BTE模型与实验数据对比。

Result: 可逆模型在理论上给出塞贝克系数的下界；声子拖曳项与基于BTE的形式一致；对高掺杂硅的案例研究表明，可逆模型的预测与实验数据吻合良好。

Conclusion: 该可逆模型具有理论严谨性、形式简洁和计算成本低的优点，可作为可逆和近平衡条件下评估热电性质（thermoelectric properties）的简洁替代方案。

Abstract: We revisit the closed-form models of Seebeck coefficient, and identify the thermodynamic flaws in those extensively-used methodologies, essentially including the confusion of electrochemical potential and electrical potential within the definition, arbitrarily neglecting the dependence on conduction band bottom and Fermi level when calculating distribution function spatial gradient, and the improper heat flux presentation. Here, an alternative methodology is presented, which derives the Seebeck coefficient model based on the drift-diffusion equation with the Soret effect in the open circuit condition. The reversible model that eliminates the electron velocity and relaxation terms in the formulation is recovered for the band term in the near-equilibrium case, and it can give the lower bound of Seebeck coefficient in theory, while the phonon-drag term is of the identical form to the Boltzmann transport equation(BTE)-based one. A case study is performed for highly-n-doped Silicon, where the reversible, ballistic(based on Landauer formulation) and BTE models are compared with each other and with the experimental data. The reversible model gives the fairly-good predictions for the experiments. Given its theoretical-soundness, simple form and low computation cost, the reversible model can serve as a concise alternative for evaluating thermoelectric properties in both the reversible and near-equilibrium cases.

</details>


### [86] [Physics-governed executable modelling of triboelectric nanogenerators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23051)
*Hongfa Zhao,Baiqiao Wang,Tiancong Zhao,Chun Jin,Hanlin Zhou,Mingrui Shu,Minyi Xu,Liwei Lin,Wenbo Ding,Zhong Lin Wang*

TL;DR: 本文针对摩擦纳米发电机（TENG）预测建模中分析理论、有限几何求解器与仿真工作流相互割裂的问题，提出电荷定义建模框架并实现为TENG-CLAW平台。该框架建立自洽静电层级结构，以摩擦电荷、预充电荷和补偿电极电荷为状态变量，连接无限平板解析极限与有限几何数值公式，将用户研究请求转化为物理上可接受的仿真任务，为TENG机制解释和可重复仿真研究提供了严格计算基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有TENG预测建模方法分散于分析理论（analytical theories）、有限几何求解器（finite-geometry solvers）和非连通的仿真工作流（disconnected simulation workflows）之中，缺乏统一的可执行框架，阻碍了定量化TENG研究的发展。

Method: 提出电荷定义建模框架（charge-defined modelling framework），并实现为TENG-CLAW物理驱动仿真平台。框架建立自洽静电梯级结构（self-consistent electrostatic hierarchy），以摩擦电荷（triboelectric charges）、预充电荷（pre-charging charges）和补偿电极电荷（compensating electrode charges）为定义状态变量，连接近均匀场下的无限平板解析极限与边缘主导器件所需的有限几何数值公式。

Result: TENG-CLAW可将用户定义的研究请求转化为物理上可接受的仿真任务，生成的输出与明确电荷状态、边界条件、求解器路径以及跨空间、时间、场级、比较和报告工作流的可复用工件（reusable artifacts）相关联。

Conclusion: 该工作为解释TENG机制建立了严格的计算基础，并为仿真和物理引导器件设计提供了可重复的研究基础设施（reproducible research infrastructure）。

Abstract: Predictive modelling of triboelectric nanogenerators (TENGs) remains fragmented across analytical theories, finite-geometry solvers and disconnected simulation workflows. These disparate approaches must be unified into an executable framework to advance quantitative TENG research.Here we introduce a charge-defined modelling framework and implement it as TENG-CLAW, a physics-governed platform for traceable TENG simulation. The framework establishes a self-consistent electrostatic hierarchy in which triboelectric charges, pre-charging charges and compensating electrode charges serve as defining state variables.This hierarchy connects the infinite plate analytical limit for near-uniform fields with finite-geometry numerical formulations required for edge-dominated devices. Built on this basis, TENG-CLAW converts user-defined research requests into physically admissible simulation tasks, so that generated outputs are tied to explicit charge states, boundary conditions, solver routes and reusable artifacts across spatial, temporal, field-level, comparative and reporting workflows. This work establishes a rigorous computational basis for interpreting TENG mechanisms and provides reproducible research infrastructure for simulation and physics-guided device design.

### [87] [An FFT-based solver with general boundary conditions for stationary diffusion problems based on Chebyshev collocation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21410)
*Juan M. Quecedo,Javier Segurado*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于切比雪夫配置法（Chebyshev collocation）的高效鲁棒FFT求解器，用于处理具有一般纽曼（Neumann）和狄利克雷（Dirichlet）边界条件的扩散型问题。该方法结合切比雪夫多项式逼近与基于FFT的算子，实现离散微分算子的无矩阵（matrix-free）计算，并通过LGMRES求解线性系统。针对细网格收敛问题，提出基于模态延拓（modal prolongation）的分层细化策略，可处理大规模三维问题。数值实验表明，该方法在均匀与非均匀域、线性和非线性本构方程中均适用，计算复杂度保持FFT的O(n log n)标度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散型问题在实际中常遇到一般Neumann和Dirichlet边界条件，而现有的快速傅里叶变换（Fast Fourier Transform, FFT）类求解器多局限于周期边界条件。设计一种既能保持FFT计算效率，又能灵活处理多种边界条件的鲁棒求解器具有理论和应用价值。

Method: 采用Chebyshev配置法，在Chebyshev-Gauss-Lobatto点上构建离散微分算子，并利用FFT实现无矩阵（matrix-free）计算；线性系统使用LGMRES迭代求解；针对细网格收敛困难，提出基于模态延拓（modal prolongation）的分层细化策略。

Result: 在均匀1D和3D域上求解Poisson方程，数值解在少量迭代内收敛至解析解，误差小于DCT/DST方法；借助分层细化策略实现了高达256^3的离散网格；在非均匀域中精度和效率与标准周期FFT方法相当；所有测试案例的计算复杂度均保持O(n log n)的FFT标度。

Conclusion: 该FFT求解器在兼顾通用边界条件处理能力的同时，保持了FFT的高效计算复杂度，适用于大规模三维问题及均匀/非均匀、线性/非线性扩散问题。

Abstract: An efficient and robust FFT-based solver is proposed for diffusion-type problems with general Neumann and Dirichlet boundary conditions, based on a Chebyshev collocation framework. The method combines Chebyshev polynomial approximations with FFT-based operators to provide a matrix-free implementation of the discrete differential operator at the Chebyshev-Gauss-Lobatto points. The linear system of equations resulting from the Chebyshev discretization is solved using LGMRES. To overcome convergence problems on fine grids, a hierarchical refinement strategy based on modal prolongation is proposed, enabling the solution of very large 3D problems. The methodology is applicable to homogeneous and heterogeneous domains, as well as to linear and nonlinear constitutive equations.
  The accuracy of the proposed method is analyzed by solving the Poisson equation in homogeneous 1D and 3D domains with general boundary conditions, using manufactured analytical solutions as references. Convergence to the analytical solution is achieved in a few iterations, with smaller errors than those obtained using DCT/DST approaches. Discretizations of up to $256^3$ are achieved thanks to the hierarchical refinement strategy. In the case of heterogeneous domains, the accuracy and efficiency obtained are similar to those of a standard periodic FFT approach. It is found that the computational complexity of the method preserves the FFT scaling, of order $n\log n$, in all the cases studied.

</details>

Method: 采用直接计算方法（direct computations）推导局部双哈密顿结构，并基于此构造具有非平直单位元的半单广义Frobenius流形。

Result: 成功推导了RR2T的局部双哈密顿结构，并构造了一个$(n+1)$维半单广义Frobenius流形，其主层次恰好包含该约化的无色散流。

### [89] [Computing Gaussian and exponential integrals in ${\Bbb R}^n$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23556)
*Alexander Barvinok*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文针对形如 $E\exp\{\sum_{i=1}^m φ_i\}$ 的期望值，在 $φ_i$ 为依赖少数坐标的 Lipschitz 函数且服从高斯或对称指数分布的条件下，给出了该积分非零的充分条件（基于 Lipschitz 常数与依赖关系组合结构），并证明了其可被高效计算逼近；应用涉及高维凸体体积计算与整数点计数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维积分（high-dimensional integral）的精确计算通常面临指数级复杂度（curse of dimensionality），需要寻找可高效近似且保证非平凡（非零）结果的充分条件。

Method: 利用函数 $φ_i$ 的 Lipschitz 常数（Lipschitz constant）以及各函数之间依赖关系的组合结构（combinatorial dependency structure），建立积分非零的充分性判据；期望分别针对标准高斯测度（standard Gaussian measure）与对称指数测度（symmetric exponential measure）进行分析。

Result: 给出了保证积分 $E\exp\{\sum φ_i\}$ 远离零（separated from 0）的充分条件，并由此推导出该积分存在计算高效（computationally efficient）的近似方法。

Conclusion: 该理论可应用于 ${\Bbb R}^n$ 中凸体体积（volume of bodies）的计算以及多面体中整数点（integer points in polyhedra）的统计问题，为高维几何与组合计数中的积分近似提供理论依据。

Abstract: We consider expectations of the type $E\ \exp \left\{\sum_{i=1}^m φ_i \right\}$, where $φ_i: {\Bbb R}^n \longrightarrow {\Bbb C}$ are functions, each depending on a few coordinates of a point in ${\Bbb R}^n$, and the expectation is taken with respect to the standard Gaussian or symmetric exponential probability measures. We prove sufficient conditions, in terms of the Lipschitz constants of $φ_i$ and the combinatorics of their dependencies, for the integral to be separated from 0, and, consequently, to be amenable to a computationally efficient approximation. We discuss applications to computing volumes of bodies and statistics on integer points in polyhedra in ${\Bbb R}^n$.

</details>

### [90] [The Sustainability Paradox of Biodegradable Packaging: A Life Cycle Perspective on Chitosan-Based Food Packaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20654)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 通过综合各阶段交互作用，该综述揭示了可持续发展论述中常被忽视的关键权衡关系（critical trade-offs），并检验了壳聚糖基纳米材料在食品包装应用中是否能提供净环境效益（net environmental benefits）。

Conclusion: 壳聚糖基纳米材料的可持续性并非自明，其环境表现取决于原料来源、加工方式、功能性能与末端处置之间的复杂权衡。该综述为更全面、审慎地评估这类材料的净环境效益提供了分析框架。

Abstract: Chitosan-based nanomaterials are being increasingly explored as sustainable alternatives to petroleum-derived food packaging, yet their environmental performance across the full life cycle remains insufficiently understood. This review critically evaluates these systems from a life cycle perspective and examines how material origin, processing pathways, functional performance, and end-of-life behavior collectively influence sustainability outcomes. Beginning with chitin extraction from crustacean waste, key processing steps, including demineralization, deproteinization, and nanoparticle synthesis, are assessed in terms of chemical intensity, energy demand, and associated emissions. Manufacturing routes, including solvent-based and green synthesis approaches, are compared with those of conventional plastics to identify relative environmental burdens. The use phase is analyzed with respect to antimicrobial functionality, shelf life extension, and potential reductions in food waste. End-of-life pathways, including biodegradation and composting, are evaluated alongside uncertainties related to degradation behavior and nanoparticle fate. By synthesizing these stagewise interactions, this review highlights critical trade-offs that are often overlooked in sustainability narratives and examines whether chitosan-based nanomaterials provide net environmental benefits in food packaging applications.

### [91] [Distance from home matters: Investigation of a basic movement strategy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22025)
*Mohsen Ghasemi Nezhadhaghighi,Yahya Khalili,Behafarid Hemmatpour,Abolfazl Ramezanpour*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于行程端点距离关联的人类移动性模型，仅通过单一智能体（agent）在二维格点上的供需驱动行程，即可定性复现包括旅行距离幂律分布（power-law distribution）在内的关键经验统计特征，且该结果对智能体间队列交互及更现实的供需分布具有鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发现生成人类流动性（human mobility）主要统计特征的基本动力学规则，对于理解此类过程的底层机制至关重要。尽管已有探索与偏好返回模型（exploration and preferential return model）及其推广成功复现了多项经验发现，但行程端点距离之间的强相关性尚未被充分挖掘利用。

Method: 考虑一个运动过程，每个用户在二维格点（two-dimensional lattice）上执行一系列行程以满足一组需求，行程目的地（destination）的选择概率取决于该地点到用户原点（home）的初始距离与最终距离之比。模型中首先考察具有均匀需求与均匀供应商分布的单一智能体，随后引入智能体间的队列交互（queues）以及更现实的需求与供应商分布。

Result: 即使采用均匀需求与均匀供应商分布，单一智能体模型也能定性复现关键经验统计量，例如旅行距离的幂律分布。引入智能体间的队列交互以及更符合现实的需求和供应商分布后，上述结果仍保持鲁棒（robust）。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了行程端点距离相关性在生成人类流动性统计规律中的核心作用，为理解人类移动性的基本动力学机制提供了新的简洁框架，且模型具有较好的扩展性和稳健性。

Abstract: Discovering the fundamental dynamical rules that generate the main statistical features of human mobility is essential for understanding the mechanisms underlying such processes. A prominent example is the exploration and preferential return model and its generalizations, which successfully reproduce several empirical findings. Here, we exploit another observation: the endpoint distances of a trip from the trajectory's starting point are strongly correlated. We consider a movement process in which each user performs a sequence of trips to satisfy a set of demands, given a spatial distribution of suppliers on a two-dimensional lattice. In each trip, destinations are chosen with a probability that depends on the ratio of the initial and final distances from the user's origin (home). We show that even a single agent with uniformly distributed demands and suppliers qualitatively reproduces key empirical statistics, such as the power-law distribution of traveled distances. The results are also robust to introducing interactions between agents via queues and incorporating more realistic demand and supplier distributions.

</details>

### [92] [On Potentials and Complementary Potentials in One-Dimensional Nonlocal Integral Formulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22202)
*Marko Čanađija,Ante Skoblar*

Main category: physics.class-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一维非局部积分公式（nonlocal integral formulations）中的势能（potential）与互补势能（complementary potential），分别用于纯应力驱动和纯应变驱动两种非局部公式，并通过勒让德变换（Legendre transformation）证明其等价性，进而提出一种混合应力-应变势能（mixed stress-strain potential），但发现其与原纯应变驱动公式一样病态（ill-conditioned）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 应变驱动非局部公式中使用的势能是已知的，但其互补势能尚未在文献中出现；同样，应力驱动公式中的对应问题也未被探讨。本研究旨在填补这一空白，建立并证明基于势能与互补势能的等效非局部公式。

Method: 采用勒让德变换推导纯应力驱动与纯应变驱动非局部公式中势能与互补势能之间的关系，并证明其等价性。在此基础上，提出一种混合应力-应变势能并进行理论分析。

Result: 证明了应力驱动与应变驱动两种非局部公式在势能与互补势能框架下的等价性；在此基础上提出的混合应力-应变势能，在理论上是可行的，但与纯应变驱动公式一样存在病态性。

Conclusion: 通过一个示例在实践层面验证了基于势能及其互补势能推导出的应力驱动公式的等价性，确认了理论推导的正确性。

Abstract: The present research presents potentials and complementary potentials used in the one-dimensional nonlocal integral formulations. The pure stress and the pure strain nonlocal formulations were considered. While the potential used in the strain driven formulation is well known, the complementary potential has not yet been presented in the literature. The same applies to the stress driven formulation. The equivalent formulations are obtained by resorting to the Legendre transformation, and their equivalence is proved. It is also shown that these results can be used to postulate a novel potential, i.e. a kind of mixed stress-strain potential, which is, however, as ill-conditioned as the pure strain-driven formulation. Finally, an example is given that practically confirms that the stress-driven formulations resulting from the potential and the complementary potential are equivalent.

</details>

### [93] [Enhanced approach to calculation of cluster integrals for lattice models of matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22123)

TL;DR: 该研究通过两种优化方案（简化被积函数计算与去除物理等效构型），改进了晶格模型（lattice models）中迈耶展开（Mayer's expansion）团簇积分（cluster integrals）的现有计算方法，并基于此获得了若干二维和三维晶格模型的高阶团簇积分新数据。

Result: 针对多个二维和三维晶格模型，基于上述优化获得了新的高阶团簇积分数据。

Abstract: The study is devoted to enhancing the existing techniques of calculating Mayer's expansion cluster integrals for lattice models of matter. Two important optimizations are proposed: simplifying the calculation of the integrand at each integration point and reducing the number of such integration points due to eliminating physically identical configurations. Based on those optimizations, new data on high-order cluster integrals are obtained for a number of 2D and 3D lattice models.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 选取人、小鼠、鸡三种生物的病毒相关网络，构建有向加权连接（directed and weighted connections）；计算拓扑特征和从邻接谱导出的热力学量；设计两种节点删除场景——目标删除最 influential 节点与随机删除，以模拟不同扰动。

Result: 谱热力学函数中出现类似相变的过渡行为，结构度量也呈现特征性变化，表明不同删除策略对网络稳定性有显著不同的影响。

Conclusion: 研究结果为评估将热力学框架应用于病毒-宿主网络的可行性提供了支持，并推动了对病毒-宿主网络动力学的深入理解。

Abstract: Understanding virus-host interactions is crucial for predicting the stability of networks under various perturbations. In this study, we present an analysis of virus-related networks for several organisms (Homo sapiens, Mus musculus, Gallus gallus), encompassing directed and weighted connections. We compute a range of network parameters, including topological characteristics and thermodynamic quantities derived from adjacency spectra, to gain insights into the structural robustness and dynamic behavior of the networks. To assess stability, we model two distinct node removal scenarios: targeted elimination of the most influential nodes and random removal. Our findings reveal transition-like behavior in spectral thermodynamic functions and characteristic changes in structural measures, contributing to evaluating the potential of a thermodynamic framework for studying virus-host networks and advancing a deeper understanding of their dynamics.

### [95] [Nonlinear Static Screening of Positive Charges in an Electron Gas: Contact Hartree Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23065)
*M. Sherafati,G. Rodway-Gant,A. X. Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了均匀电子气中静态质子的电子屏蔽问题，重点研究了接触哈特里能量 U_H(0) 作为非局部量的表达式，并对比了多种线性与非线性模型。通过验证 Estreicher–Meier LDA 参数化与直接 DFT 计算结果的一致性，建立了质子杂质在凝胶模型（jellium）中的单中心非线性屏蔽基准，为凝聚态低能聚变等两中心屏蔽问题提供了基线参考。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金属中正电荷的电子屏蔽在静态近场区域表现出最强的非线性行为。本文旨在重新审视静态单质子电荷在均匀电子气（homogeneous electron gas）中的屏蔽问题，澄清接触哈特里能量 U_H(0) 的局部性争议，并为线性响应理论提供一个紧凑的非线性基准。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density-functional theory, DFT）框架，明确将 U_H(0) 表述为由全诱导密度的径向矩决定的非局部量。对比了 Thomas–Fermi、Lindhard/随机相位近似（random-phase-approximation, RPA）以及局域场修正的介电模型与非线性 DFT 基准。还利用 Friedel 求和规则约束下的变分相散射公式分析了 Yukawa、氢原子型（hydrogenic）和 Hulthén 屏蔽库仑势。

Result: Estreicher–Meier 局域密度近似（local-density-approximation, LDA）参数化再现了直接 LDA 计算以及 Almbladh 等人的自洽结果，验证了统一的 U_H(0) 实现。接触哈特里能量将氢原子型密度分布与不可忽略的 Friedel 振荡分离。Corradini–Del Sole–Onida–Palummo 和 Kaplan–Kukkonen 参数化在接触屏蔽上不可区分。变分相散射势无法单独重现非线性 DFT 的接触哈特里能量。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了凝胶模型中质子杂质的单中心非线性屏蔽基准，澄清了接触屏蔽的非局部本质，并为未来处理两中心屏蔽问题（如凝聚态低能聚变）提供了必要的基线。

Abstract: Electron screening of positive charges in metals is most strongly nonlinear in the static near-field regime. We revisit screening of a static single protonic charge in a homogeneous electron gas, focusing on the induced density and the contact Hartree energy $U_{\text{H}}(0)$. Although evaluated at the impurity position, $U_{\text{H}}(0)$ is not purely local: our formulation makes it explicit as a nonlocal quantity set by a radial moment of the full induced density, applicable to both linear-response and nonlinear density-functional-theory (DFT) descriptions. We compare Thomas--Fermi, Lindhard/random-phase-approximation, and local-field-corrected dielectric models with nonlinear DFT benchmarks. The Estreicher--Meier local-density-approximation (LDA) parametrization reproduces the contact Hartree energy from our direct LDA calculations and the self-consistent results of Almbladh \emph{et al.} [\href{https://doi.org/10.1103/PhysRevB.14.2250}{Phys. Rev. B \textbf{14}, 2250 (1976)}]. This validates the unified $U_{\text{H}}(0)$ implementation, separates the hydrogenic density profile from non-negligible Friedel oscillations, and provides a compact nonlinear reference for linear-response theory. Testing modern local-field factors, the Corradini--Del Sole--Onida--Palummo and Kaplan--Kukkonen parametrizations yield indistinguishable contact screening despite differing near $q\simeq 2k_F$. We also analyze Yukawa, hydrogenic, and Hulthén screened Coulomb potentials via a variable-phase scattering formulation constrained by the Friedel sum rule; these give a useful phase-shift representation of static screening but cannot alone reproduce the nonlinear DFT contact Hartree energy. The results establish a one-center nonlinear screening benchmark for proton impurities in jellium and clarify the baseline needed before treating two-center screening relevant to low-energy fusion in condensed matter.

</details>


### [96] [Synchronization in coherently and dissipatively coupled spinor polariton time crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23311)
*I. Carraro-Haddad,A. Ramos-Pérez,G. Usaj,A. Bruchhausen,K. Biermann,P. V. Santos,A. S. Kuznetsov,A. A. Reynoso,A. Fainstein*

Method: 实验上，研究耦合阱中的极化激元凝聚体，通过光学激发功率调控个体及相对赝自旋取向；理论上，考虑激子库以及阱间相干与长程耗散耦合（coherent and long-range dissipative inter-trap coupling）的作用。

Result: 在CTC相中观察到赝自旋GHz时域动力学的相互诱导与同步，实现了铁磁（ferro）与反铁磁（anti-ferro）动力学构型的光学可调。

Conclusion: 将时间平移对称性破缺的研究拓展到更复杂的非厄米系统（non-hermitian systems），为研究非线性量子凝聚体晶格（lattices of non-linear quantum condensates）中的自持集体动力学（self-sustained collective dynamics）开辟了路径。

Abstract: The spinor degree of freedom associated to exciton-polariton condensates can spontaneously self-oscillate breaking time translation symmetry, thus showing a continuous time-crystal (CTC) behavior. An open question in such driven-dissipative and non-linear quantum open systems is what happens when CTCs are brought together to interact. Here we experimentally study polariton condensates in coupled traps, evidencing mutual induction and synchronization of the pseudospin temporal GHz dynamics in the CTC phase. The individual and relative orientation of the (limit cycle) precessing pseudospins can be tuned by the optical excitation power, displaying both ferro and anti-ferro dynamical configurations. We theoretically show that the exciton reservoir, and both the coherent and long-range dissipative inter-trap coupling, play important roles in the CTC dynamics. The investigation of time-broken symmetry is thus extended here to more complex non-hermitian systems opening the path to study self-sustained collective dynamics in lattices of non-linear quantum condensates.

### [97] [Semi-Analytical Pricing for General Default Intensity Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21800)
*Ryan Parker,Mark Stedman,Luca Capriotti*

TL;DR: 本文基于路径积分形式（path-integral formalism）为一般类别的违约强度（default intensity）模型开发了一种精确且易于计算的半解析近似方法。该方法在Black-Karasinski模型上表现出色，即使在高波动率和多年时间范围内仍保持高精度，为计量经济学和衍生品定价（包括信用产品的XVA计算）提供了全数值方案的有效替代。文章以随机违约强度和外汇贬值模型下的双币信用违约互换（CDS）定价作为实际应用示例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用路径积分形式（path-integral formalism），针对一般类别的违约强度模型构建半解析近似（semi-analytical approximation）。该近似方法易于计算，并通过Black-Karasinski模型验证其准确性，同时应用于双币信用违约互换（quanto Credit Default Swap, CDS）的定价，涉及随机违约强度与外汇贬值模型。

Result: 所提出的近似方法在Black-Karasinski模型上提供了极其精确的结果，即使在高波动率（high volatility）和多年时间范围（multi-year time horizons）等挑战性设定下依然保持高精度。在双币信用违约互换定价的实际案例中，该方法同样表现出良好的适用性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的半解析近似方法兼具准确性与计算效率，可作为全数值方案（fully numerical schemes）的有效替代，适用于计量经济学和衍生品定价中的多种应用场景，包括信用衍生品的XVA计算。

Abstract: Using the path-integral formalism, we develop an accurate and easy-to-compute semi-analytical approximation for a general class of {default intensity} models. We illustrate the accuracy of the method by presenting results for the Black-Karasinski model for which the proposed approximation provides remarkably accurate results, even in regimes of high volatility and multi-year time horizons. The accuracy and the computational efficiency of the proposed approximation makes it a viable alternative to fully numerical schemes for a variety of applications in econometrics and derivatives pricing, including the computation of XVA for credit products. As a practical example, we consider the pricing of a quanto Credit Default Swap (CDS) under stochastic intensity of default and an FX devaluation model.

Conclusion: 该构型通过支持融合等离激元（plasmon）、激子（exciton）和扩展腔场（extended cavity field）贡献的新型杂化等离激元激子态（hybrid plexcitonic states），为在纳米尺度定制光-物质相互作用开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Strong coupling between molecules and electromagnetic fields has emerged as a powerful strategy to modify the physical and chemical properties of molecules, enabled by the formation of hybridized energy levels through strong light-matter interactions. Rather than purely photonic or plasmonic modes, hybrid cavity fields that integrate plasmonic and photonic contributions provide versatile platforms with distinct advantages for tailoring light-matter interactions. Here, we present hybrid modes formed through the coupling between localized surface plasmon resonances of Au nanoparticles and Fabry-Perot microcavity modes.   <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 成功推导出光子体系中能隙陈数的严格上界；该上界适用于色散与非色散两种情形；实现了无需显式拓扑分析即可估计带隙拓扑荷（topological charge of band gaps）。

Abstract: Topology has become a central concept in understanding physical phenomena, leading to important advances in condensed matter and photonics. Here, we generalize this framework to photonic systems, deriving rigorous upper bounds on gap Chern numbers without requiring explicit topological analysis. ### [100] [Mirror-Symmetry-Enforced Photonic Altermagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21545)
*Chong Cao,Xiong-Xiong Xue,Yee Sin Ang,Haiyu Meng*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文在六角晶格上提出了一种光子交替磁体（photonic altermagnet），其螺旋度分裂（helicity splitting）由镜面对称而非旋转对称控制，通过椭圆手性元件的交替排列实现无净磁化的动量依赖能带分裂，并在仿真中展示了光束分裂与方向选择性螺旋度滤波功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有光子交替磁体仅在受四重旋转对称性约束的正方晶格中实现，尚缺少六角晶格等其它晶格对称性类别的探索。本文旨在将光子交替磁体拓展至六角晶格，并引入镜面对称而非旋转对称作为螺旋度分裂的对称性起源。

Method: 在正六边形顶点上交替放置椭圆手性元（chiral elements）作为相反手性（chirality）的子晶格（sublattice），使得两子晶格仅通过手性反转与镜面反射的联合操作相连。采用全波仿真（full-wave simulation）计算能带结构和等频轮廓（isofrequency contours），并在有限结构中分析光束传播行为。

Result: 全波仿真显示两相反螺旋度支在能带结构和等频轮廓中存在镜面对称相关的分裂，反转椭圆取向时对应通道互换。在有限结构中，该分裂可将线偏振光分离为螺旋度分辨的通道，实现光束分裂和方向选择性螺旋度滤波，目标螺旋度输出分数超过0.85，且输出路径可通过椭圆旋转角连续调谐。

Conclusion: 这些结果将光子交替磁性扩展至此前未探索的晶格对称性类别，并建立了镜面对称手性织构（mirror-symmetric chiral textures）作为交替磁性启发的手性光子学（altermagnetism-inspired chiral photonics）的构建模块。

Abstract: Altermagnets host momentum-dependent spin splitting without net magnetization, a symmetry-enforced band phenomenon whose photonic analogues have so far been realized only in square lattices governed by fourfold rotation. Here we introduce a photonic altermagnet on a hexagonal lattice whose helicity splitting is governed by mirror rather than rotational symmetry. Elliptical chiral elements of alternating handedness, placed at the vertices of a regular hexagon, leave the two opposite-chirality sublattices connected only by chirality reversal combined with a mirror reflection. Full-wave simulations reveal mirror-related splitting of the two opposite-helicity branches in the band structure and isofrequency contours, with the channels exchanged when the ellipse orientation is reversed. In finite structures, this splitting separates a linearly polarized beam into handedness-resolved channels, enabling beam splitting and direction-selective helicity filtering with target-helicity output fractions above 0.85 and output paths continuously tunable through the ellipse rotation angle. These results extend photonic altermagnetism to a previously unexplored lattice-symmetry class and establish mirror-symmetric chiral textures as building blocks for altermagnetism-inspired chiral photonics.

</details>


### [101] [Structural and physical properties of gyromorphs and disordered stealthy hyperuniform media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22300)
*Murray Skolnick,Riccardo Franchi,Luca Dal Negro,Paul J. Steinhardt,Salvatore Torquato*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文澄清了gyromorphs与隐形超均匀（stealthy hyperuniform）材料之间的关系，证明gyromorphs实际属于最弱形式的超均匀性（Class III），而非此前认为的非超均匀材料，并验证了其在光子带隙、透明度等物理性能上劣于最强的Class I隐形超均匀材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gyromorphs此前被提出作为隐形超均匀材料的反例，声称无需满足隐形或超均匀条件即可实现甚至超越后者的优异物理性能。本文旨在解决这一矛盾，阐明gyromorphs如何与隐形超均匀研究框架自洽地兼容。

Method: 首先通过结构分析论证gyromorphs实际具有超均匀性（hyperuniform），并在大G极限下属于最弱的Class III超均匀性。随后采用严格的谱格林矩阵方法（spectral Green's matrix method）计算电偶极子阵列中的态密度（density of states, DOS）和Purcell因子（Purcell factors），对比两类材料的物理性能差异。

Result: Gyromorphs显示出依赖于尺寸的赝能隙（pseudogap），其中充斥着局域态，而非像高隐形超均匀材料或确定性结构（如Vogel螺旋和三角晶格）那样拥有平滑的带隙（band gap）。此外，gyromorphs在透明度、可扩展性（spreadability）和扩散性质方面同样表现出相对于隐形超均匀材料的退化。

Conclusion: Gyromorphs属于Class III超均匀性，其物理性能整体劣于属于Class I的隐形超均匀材料，因此并不构成对后者的真正反例，反而与隐形超均匀研究框架保持一致。

Abstract: Disordered stealthy hyperuniform materials combine liquid-like statistical isotropy with crystal-like homogeneity, suppressed density fluctuations at large length scales, bounded holes, and an isotropic structure factor that vanishes for a finite range of wavevectors. This combination yields unusual physical properties, including optical transparency, effective delocalization, ultrafast spreadability, optimal conductivity, and complete isotropic photonic bandgaps. Gyromorphs, point patterns whose structure factor includes rings of Bragg-like peaks arranged with discrete $G$-fold rotational symmetry, were recently introduced as counterexamples: disordered media that can somehow achieve the same physical properties, in some cases with higher performance, without stealthiness or hyperuniformity. In this paper, we resolve the puzzle of how gyromorphs fit consistently with the stealthy hyperuniform studies. We first show that gyromorphs are actually hyperuniform and, in the large-$G$ limit where they become nearly isotropic, belong to the weakest form of hyperuniformity, known as Class III. Thus, gyromorphs should have comparatively degraded physical properties compared to stealthy hyperuniform media, which belong to the strongest form of hyperuniformity, known as Class I. We verify this expectation using the rigorous spectral Green's matrix method for the calculation of the density of states (DOS) and Purcell factors in large arrays of electric dipoles. We find that gyromorphs display size-dependent pseudogaps richly populated by localized states rather than smooth band gaps like those found for highly stealthy hyperuniform materials or in deterministic structures such as Vogel spiral and triangular lattices. Furthermore, we predict similar disorder-induced degradation relative to stealthy hyperuniformity with regard to transparency, spreadability and diffusion properties.

</details>


### [102] [Effusivity-Controlled Interfacial Thermal Transport Revealed by Nanoscale Optical Thermometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22508)
*Adarsh B Vasista,Anita Kumari,Yash P. Mhaske*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文利用时间分辨热光学衍射层析成像（thermal ODT）实现了对界面瞬态温度场的三维时空重建，发现界面热扩散受热渗透率（thermal effusivity）对比控制，并推导出有效界面扩散率（effective interfacial diffusivity）模型。实验表明，具有较低体热扩散率的液体因热渗透率更低，反而表现出更快的界面热扩展，测量结果与理论预测高度一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高时空分辨率的热传输定量成像对于理解非均质系统中的热过程至关重要，然而直接测量材料界面的瞬态温度场仍然具有挑战性。现有技术难以兼顾纳米级空间分辨率与瞬态时间分辨能力，亟需一种能够无标记、三维重建界面温度演化的方法。

Method: 采用时间分辨热光学衍射层析成像（time resolved thermal optical diffraction tomography, thermal ODT），这是一种无标记（label free）纳米级光学测温技术，通过热致折射率变化（thermally induced refractive index changes）重建三维温度场的时空演化。进一步推导了有效界面扩散率模型，并通过有限元仿真在多种液-玻璃界面（liquid-glass interfaces）上进行验证。

Result: 界面热扩散由界面两侧材料的热渗透率对比（thermal effusivity contrast）控制；推导的有效界面扩散率可准确描述热场的横向传播。反直觉地，具有较低体热扩散率（bulk thermal diffusivity）的液体因热渗透率更低，反而表现出更快的界面热扩展。测量扩散率与理论预测在多种材料组合上定量一致。

Conclusion: 本研究通过将体积热成像（volumetric thermal imaging）与界面热传输通用框架相结合，确立了thermal ODT作为一种研究纳米尺度热力学（nanoscale thermodynamics）和工程化异质环境中热流（engineering heat flow）的强大平台。

Abstract: Quantitative imaging of heat transport with high spatial and temporal resolution is essential for understanding thermal processes in heterogeneous systems, yet direct measurements of transient temperature fields at material interfaces remain challenging. Here, we employ time resolved thermal optical diffraction tomography (thermal ODT), a label free nanoscale optical thermometry technique that reconstructs spatio-temporal evolution of three dimensional temperature fields from thermally induced refractive index changes. We show that thermal diffusion along an interface is controlled by their thermal effusivity contrast. We also derive an effective interfacial diffusivity that accurately describes the lateral propagation of thermal fields and validate the model through finite-element simulations across a broad range of liquid-glass interfaces. Surprisingly, liquids with lower bulk thermal diffusivities exhibit faster interfacial thermal spreading due to their lower effusivities. The measured diffusivities agree quantitatively with theoretical predictions over diverse material combinations. By combining volumetric thermal imaging with a general framework for interfacial heat transport, our work establishes thermal ODT as a powerful platform for investigating nanoscale thermodynamics and engineering heat flow in heterogeneous environments.

</details>


### [103] [Integrated Whispering-Gallery Microlaser-Waveguide Platform for On-Chip Electrical Excitation of InGaAs Quantum Dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22626)
*Léo J. Roche,Peter Gschwandtner,Chirag C. Palekar,Setthanat Wijitpatima,Yuhui Yang,Monika Emmerling,Sven Höfling,Tobias Huber-Loyola,Stephan Reitzenstein*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种集成量子光子器件，该器件由电驱动回音壁模式（whispering-gallery-mode）微柱激光器与脊形波导（ridge waveguide）倏逝耦合构成，两者均集成InGaAs量子点（quantum dots, QDs）。通过系统研究微柱激光器与波导间隙距离对激射特性的影响，实现了相干发射到波导的耦合，并利用片上连续波激发在波导末端微柱中获得单光子发射，其二阶关联函数 $g^{(2)}(0) = (3.49 \pm 0.01)\%$，且可通过量子受限斯塔克效应（quantum confined Stark effect）进行光谱调谐。该工作为基于量子点的集成量子光子电路中实现低占用面积、确定性和可扩展的单光子源迈出了重要一步。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于量子点（QDs）的集成量子光子电路需要低占用面积（low-footprint）、确定性和可扩展的单光子源，但现有方案在片上集成和电驱动方面仍存在挑战。本文旨在通过将电驱动微柱激光器与波导集成的方案，实现片上可控的单光子发射。

Method: 制备并表征了一种集成量子光子器件，其核心结构包括一个电驱动回音壁模式（whispering-gallery-mode）微柱激光器与脊形波导（ridge waveguide）倏逝耦合，两者均嵌入InGaAs量子点（QDs）。系统改变微柱-波导间隙距离以研究激射特性，并通过波导将相干发射耦合至末端电接触微柱中的量子点，实现片上连续波（continuous-wave）光学激发。

Result: 在连续波片上激发条件下，在波导末端微柱集成的量子点中观测到单光子发射，其二阶关联函数 $g^{(2)}(0) = (3.49 \pm 0.01)\%$，表明具有极高的单光子纯度。该发射可通过量子受限斯塔克效应（quantum confined Stark effect）进行光谱调谐。

Conclusion: 该集成方案为基于量子点（QDs）的集成量子光子电路提供了一种低占用面积、确定性和可扩展的单光子源实现路径，是推动片上量子光子系统实用化的重要进展。

Abstract: We report the fabrication and characterization of an integrated quantum photonic device consisting of an electrically driven whispering-gallery-mode micropillar laser evanescently coupled to a ridge waveguide, both incorporating InGaAs quantum dots (QDs). The lasing characteristics of microlasers are systematically investigated as a function of the pillar-waveguide gap distance. Coherent emission from the whispering-gallery-mode microlaser coupled into the waveguide enables on-chip optical excitation of QDs embedded in an electrically contacted micropillar at the end of the waveguide. Under continuous-wave on-chip excitation, we observe single-photon emission with $g^{(2)}(0) = (3.49 \pm 0.01) \%$ for a QD integrated in the outcoupling micropillar which can be spectrally tuned-by the quantum confined Stark effect. These results constitute an important step toward low-footprint, deterministic, and scalable single-photon sources for QD-based integrated quantum photonic circuits.

### [104] [Large-Area Patternable Solar-Powered Bistable Organic Film for Nonlinear Optical Communication](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22980)
*Ankur Khapre,Avulu Vinod Kumar,Haseeba Nazreen,Biswajit Kumar Barman,Bedanta Kumar Deka,Shilpa Mangalassery,Sri Ram G Naraharishetty,Rajadurai Chandrasekar*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种基于光致异构分子（E/Z-BTDPA）的太阳光驱动对称性双稳态有机材料，实现了中心对称与非中心对称晶相间的可逆切换，并展示了在柔性薄膜中的二次谐波产生开关、大面积光学图案化及实时非线性光学通信功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶体对称性的可逆控制为可编程光学功能提供了有力途径，但实现中心对称（centrosymmetric）与非中心对称（non-centrosymmetric）晶相之间的固态双稳态（bistability）仍是重大挑战；能够稳定切换二阶非线性光学（second-order nonlinear optical, NLO）响应的材料极为罕见。

Method: 基于光致异构分子（E/Z）-2-(4-(4-溴苯基)噻唑-2-基)-3-(4-(二甲氨基)苯基)丙烯腈（E/Z-BTDPA），利用其可结晶的E型和Z型异构体采用不同的分子堆积排列（molecular packing arrangements），在太阳光驱动下实现光致异构化（photoisomerization），从而在两种晶相间可逆切换。

Result: E型异构体表现出强二次谐波产生（second-harmonic generation, SHG），而Z型异构体无SHG活性且呈现双光子发光（two-photon luminescence）。该双稳态行为可在柔性薄膜中保持，实现太阳光驱动的二阶电极化率（χ⁽²⁾）可逆光开关、大面积光学图案化，以及通过波形生成和文本字符串转录在电信波长下进行实时NLO通信。

Conclusion: 该可持续策略绕过了刚性无机架构，将光致对称双稳态确立为全光计算（all-optical computing）和先进通信网络的可扩展范式。

Abstract: Reversible control of crystal symmetry offers a powerful route to programmable optical functionality. However, achieving solid-state bistability between centrosymmetric and non-centrosymmetric crystalline phases remains a formidable challenge; examples of materials that enable stable switching of second-order nonlinear optical (NLO) responses are exceptionally rare. Here we report a solar-powered, symmetry-bistable organic material based on the photoisomerizable molecule (E/Z)-2-(4-(4-bromophenyl)thiazol-2-yl)-3-(4- (dimethylamino)phenyl)acrylonitrile (E/Z-BTDPA). The crystallizable E- and Z-isomers adopt distinct molecular packing arrangements that reversibly toggle between these states, controlling second-order NLO activity. The E-form exhibits strong second-harmonic generation (SHG), whereas the Z-form is SHG-inactive and displays twophoton luminescence. This bistable behavior is retained in flexible thin films, where sunlight-driven photoisomerization enables reversible photoswitching of the second-order electric susceptibility (\c{hi} 2), large-area optical patterning, and real-time NLO communication via waveform generation and text-string transcription at telecommunication wavelengths. This sustainable strategy bypasses rigid inorganic architectures, establishing photoinduced symmetry bistability as a scalable paradigm for all-optical computing and advanced communication networks.

</details>


### [105] [Hexagonal Boron Nitride Spin Defects for Quantum Photonics: Annealing-Free Generation by Krypton Ion Implantation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23334)
*Ikshvaku Shyam,Raj Singh,Mangababu Akkanaboina,A. M. Sonawane,Muthu Satheeshkumar,Amrita Majumder,Ekta,Janhavi Jayawant Khunte,Akash Khaire,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Gopalan Rajaraman,S. S. Dahiwale,Anshuman Kumar*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文报告了一种利用Kr⁺离子注入在六方氮化硼（hBN）中可控生成近红外发光自旋缺陷的方法，该方法无需退火且具有化学惰性。实验结合SRIM模拟、光致发光（PL）、拉曼光谱、电子顺磁共振（EPR）和密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，证实了VN-CB施主-受主对复合体是观测到的光学与磁学信号的来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在六方氮化硼（hBN）中可控、可重复地生成发光缺陷中心，是实现可扩展量子光子技术的关键挑战。现有方法往往依赖退火步骤或引入化学杂质，亟需一种更简洁、可调且可扩展的替代方案。

Method: 采用Kr⁺离子注入（ion implantation）作为可调、无需退火且化学惰性的方法，通过SRIM蒙特卡罗（Monte Carlo）模拟优化40 keV Kr⁺辐照hBN薄片的参数。对注入样品进行光致发光（photoluminescence, PL）测量（20–300 K）、拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）、电子顺磁共振（electron paramagnetic resonance, EPR）以及密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算。

Result: 注入样品在~830 nm处出现稳定的近红外光致发光（PL）带，其强度随注入通量（10¹¹–10¹⁵ ions/cm²）增加而增强。温度依赖性PL测量显示线宽展宽遵循T³依赖关系，符合声子介导的退相机制。拉曼光谱在~1295 cm⁻¹处出现辐照诱导的缺陷特征峰。EPR测量检测到g因子为2.003的顺磁中心，DFT计算表明空间分离的VN-CB施主-受主对复合体是光学和磁学信号的可行来源。

Conclusion: Kr⁺离子注入提供了一种有效、无需退火且可扩展的平台，用于在hBN中生成稳定的室温发光缺陷，为量子光子学应用提供了一条有前景的路线。

Abstract: Controlled, reproducible generation of luminescent defect centres in hBN remains a key challenge for scalable quantum-photonic technologies. Here, we report Kr$^{+}$ ion implantation as a tunable, annealing-free, and chemically inert route to room-temperature near-infrared luminescent spin defects in hBN, requiring no pre- or post-implantation annealing. SRIM Monte Carlo simulations were used to optimise the parameters for 40 keV Kr$^{+}$ irradiation of hBN flakes. The implanted samples exhibit a stable near-infrared photoluminescence (PL) band centred at $\sim$830 nm whose intensity increases with implantation fluence over $10^{11}$-$10^{15}$ions/cm$^{2}$. Temperature-dependent PL measurements (20-300 K) reveal a linewidth broadening well described by a $T^{3}$ dependence, consistent with acoustic-phonon-mediated dephasing. Raman spectra show the characteristic $E_{2g}$ mode of pristine hBN at $\sim$1366 cm$^{-1}$ alongside an implantation-induced defect feature at $\sim$1295 cm$^{-1}$, confirming irradiation-induced lattice disorder. Electron paramagnetic resonance (EPR) measurements reveal a paramagnetic centre with a $g$-factor of 2.003, and density functional theory (DFT) calculations indicate that a spatially separated $V_{\mathrm{N}}$-$C_{\mathrm{B}}$ donor-acceptor pair complex is a viable origin of the observed optical and magnetic signatures. Overall, Kr$^{+}$ implantation offers an effective, annealing-free, and scalable platform for generating stable room-temperature luminescent defects, providing a promising route toward quantum photonics.

### [106] [Distribution Complexity of Electronic Structure Simulations on Quantum Supercomputers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20805)
*Jason Necaise,Namit Anand,Gaurav Gyawali,K. Grace Johnson,James D. Whitfield,Masoud Mohseni*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种估算混合量子-经典模拟中电子结构哈密顿量分布复杂度的算法，基于双因子分解表示中的低纠缠边界与退相局域化分析，将量子处理单元间通信成本从O(N²)降至O(N)，并刻画了三种硬度区间。该框架旨在推动实用规模量子计算的高效量子-经典应用工作流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强相互作用的费米子体系在量子处理单元（quantum processing units, QPUs）上的高效模拟因非局域模纠缠生成而极具挑战。目前尚未充分理解纠缠结构如何决定大规模量子化学模拟的计算难度以及任务在异构高性能计算架构上的分布开销。

Method: 算法基于双因子分解（double-factorized representation）表示，对张量片段中的轨道旋转与退相诱导局域化进行低纠缠边界（low entanglement boundaries）的高效解析评估。每个片段的纠缠估算复杂度为O(N³)，N为轨道数。

Result: 在QPUs通过量子网络通信时，每个片段的分布成本从O(N²)二次降低至O(N)；在仅有传统高性能计算（HPC）互连的混合量子-经典方法中，最坏情况成本从O(exp(N²))降至O(exp(N))。纠缠模式由相干高斯轨道旋转与无序库仑相互作用共同诱导。基于片段的局域化程度与片段间旋转重叠，引入了可调谐的模型系统，并刻画了分布复杂度与经典可模拟性的三种硬度区间。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架能够支持新型且更高效的量子-经典应用工作流，推动向实用规模量子计算（utility-scale quantum computing）迈进。

Abstract: Efficient simulation of strongly-interacting fermionic systems on quantum processing units (QPUs) is a challenging task due to nonlocal mode entanglement generation. However, it is not yet well understood how the structure of entanglement governs the hardness of large-scale quantum chemistry simulations or the scaling of distributing such workloads. Here, we introduce an algorithm for estimating the distribution complexity of hybrid quantum-classical simulation for electronic structure Hamiltonians over heterogeneous high-performance architectures. Our algorithm relies on efficient analytical evaluation of the low entanglement boundaries for the orbital rotations and dephasing-induced localization within tensor fragments, in a double-factorized representation. Our entanglement estimation scales as $O(N^3)$ for each fragment, where $N$ is the number of orbitals. When QPUs are communicating via a quantum network, the cost of distribution per fragment is reduced quadratically from $O(N^2)$ to $O(N)$. Similarly, for hybrid quantum-classical approaches, with access to only conventional HPC interconnects, the worst-case cost is reduced from $O(\exp(N^2))$ to $O(\exp(N))$. We show that emergent entanglement patterns are induced by the interplay between coherent Gaussian orbital rotations and disordered Coulomb interactions. We discuss the underlying physical mechanisms that govern distribution complexity and introduce model systems that are tunable based on the localizability of fragments and the overlap of interfragment rotations. We characterize three different regimes of hardness for distribution complexity and classical simulability. The framework introduced here enables novel and more efficient quantum-classical application workflows towards utility-scale quantum computing.

Method: 以参数依赖的复Ginibre矩阵系综（complex Ginibre ensemble）为研究对象，针对圆域内谱密度在平均意义下包含有限个本征值的情形，推导了对称性类$\mathbf{A}$系统的参数数协方差（parametric number covariance）的显式闭式表达式。并通过实Ginibre系综、非厄米Bernoulli Wigner矩阵及双酉不变系综（bi-unitarily invariant ensembles）的数值实验提供普适性支持。

Result: 得到了复Ginibre矩阵系综中谱密度参数协方差的解析闭式表达式，数值证据表明该行为在实Ginibre系综、非厄米Bernoulli Wigner矩阵及双酉不变系综中均具有普适性（universality）。

Conclusion: 该工作为理解耗散量子混沌体系中谱密度的参数相关性提供了理论基础，并揭示了其与本征向量非正交性因子分布之间的内在联系。

Abstract: Motivated by the surge of interest in statistics of non-Hermitian random matrices as a framework for description of universal characteristics of dissipative chaotic quantum many-body systems, we address the problem of characterizing the parametric correlations of spectral densities. Considering parameter-dependent ensemble of complex Ginibre matrices we derive an explicit, closed-form expression for the parametric number covariance in the systems of symmetry class $\mathbf{A}$ for eigenvalues in a circular domain containing on average a finite number of eigenvalues in the spectral bulk. This behavior is expected to be universal, as further supported by numerical evidence for the real Ginibre ensemble, non-Hermitian Bernoulli Wigner matrices and bi-unitarily invariant ensembles. We also discuss a relation between parametric correlations of spectral densities and the distribution of the so-called eigenvector non-orthogonality factor, which attracted considerable interest in recent years.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用反应坐标-极化子变换框架（reaction-coordinate polaron-transform framework），将原始强耦合问题映射为有效弱耗散模型；通过谱局域化界（spectral localization bounds）分析所得李乌维超算符（Liouvillian superoperator）的谱结构；辅以含瑟库勒（secular）与非瑟库勒（non-secular）量子主方程的数值模拟。

Result: 在推广的V模型中，强耦合导致有效系统-环境耦合算符出现亮-暗结构（bright-dark structure）：一个集体模式保持强耦合，其余模式逐渐变暗；动力学分离为快慢扇区，有限耦合强度下布居弛豫时间尺度呈现层级结构，数值模拟验证了时间尺度分离和慢弛豫的显著增强。
