Abstract: We investigate the dissipative dynamics of multilevel quantum systems strongly coupled either to a lossy cavity mode or directly to a bosonic environment. By deriving spectral localization bounds, we establish conditions under which strong system-bath coupling gives rise to a hierarchy of population relaxation timescales. Our approach builds on the reaction-coordinate polaron-transform framework. By mapping the original strong-coupling problem onto an effective weakly dissipative model, we analyze the spectrum of the resulting Liouvillian superoperator through localization bounds. For the generalized V model, we find that strong system-bath coupling gives rise to a bright-dark structure in the effective system-bath coupling operator: a single collective mode remains strongly coupled to the environment, while the remaining modes become progressively dark. Consequently, the dynamics separate into fast and slow sectors and, at finite coupling strengths, develop a hierarchy of population relaxation timescales. Numerical simulations based on both secular and non-secular quantum master equations corroborate the emergence of timescale separation and the pronounced slowing down of dissipative dynamics at strong coupling. Our results reveal a general mechanism underlying anomalously slow relaxation in strongly coupled open quantum systems and provide a route for engineering long-lived states through system-environment interactions.

### [110] [Emergence of Boolean Facts from Markovian Coarse-Graining in Relational Quantum Causal Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22127)
*Yipeng Xu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过算子代数（operator algebra）机制，证明经典的布尔记录（Boolean records）可从局域完全正量子操作（local completely positive quantum operations）中涌现，无需预设微观结构。其核心思想是：通过粗粒化（coarse-graining）通道的渐近行为生成交换冯·诺依曼代数（commutative von Neumann algebra），从而自然产生经典事实（classical facts）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典记录如何从量子理论中涌现，而不依赖人为预设的“分裂记录实验室”（split-record laboratories）或微观结构，是量子基础与算子代数研究中的一个关键问题。本文旨在从动力学角度（而非运动学插入）解释非平凡中心（nontrivial centers）的出现。

Method: 定义一个影响代数（influence algebra），其精确事件（exact events）为中心投影（central projections）。采用保态正规单位完全正粗粒化通道（state-preserving normal unital completely positive coarse-graining channels），研究其Cesàro均值收敛到Choi-Effros红外范围（infrared range），并在GNS半范数下渐近交换（asymptotically abelian）的条件。

Result: 若上述条件成立，则红外代数（infrared algebra）为交换冯·诺依曼代数，其投影格构成完全布尔代数（complete Boolean algebra）。进一步给出有限扇区块本原判据（finite-sector block-primitive criterion），该判据基于局域性（locality）与置乱性（scrambling），能保证渐近交换性，并指数压制扇区间相干性（off-sector coherences）与扇区内涨落（intra-sector fluctuations）。

Conclusion: 经典事实不应等同于Type-III局域代数的任意投影，而应被识别为中心投影——它们由渐近交换的完全正红外极限（infrared limit）所选择。这是一项保守的数学陈述：经典性从量子动力学的红外行为中涌现，而非预先植入。

Abstract: We formulate an operator-algebraic mechanism by which exact Boolean records can arise from local completely positive quantum operations without being imposed as microscopic structure. The kinematic input is an algebraic process functional assigning probabilities to local normal completely positive operations in a finite operational context. From the predual response of a target algebra to source interventions, relative to a background strategy class, we define an influence algebra; exact events are then, by definition, the projections in its center. The dynamical question is whether nontrivial centers can be generated by coarse-graining rather than inserted through split-record laboratories. We address this question using state-preserving normal unital completely positive coarse-graining channels. If the Cesaro means of such a channel converge to a Choi-Effros infrared range and the range is asymptotically abelian in the GNS seminorm, then the represented infrared algebra is a commutative von Neumann algebra. Its projection lattice is therefore a complete Boolean algebra. We also give a finite-sector block-primitive criterion, motivated by locality and scrambling, which implies this asymptotic abelianness with exponential suppression of off-sector coherences and intra-sector fluctuations. The result is a conservative mathematical statement: classical facts are not identified with arbitrary projections of a Type-III local algebra, but with central projections selected by an asymptotically abelian completely positive infrared limit.

### [111] [Probing the Weak-Driving Quantum Speed Limit via Drift-Aware Shooting Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22212)
*Denis Janković,Saba Taherpour,Paul-Louis Etienney,Paul-Antoine Hervieux,Christoph Wolf*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出并验证了MAGICARP方法——一种基于庞特里亚金最小值原理（Pontryagin's maximum principle）的打靶法（shooting method），用于生成能效最优且光滑的量子控制脉冲。该方法在无漂移系统基础上扩展到有恒定漂移哈密顿量的封闭系统（以外部磁场中两个交换耦合自旋为例）。与Krotov和GRAPE方法相比，MAGICARP在相同门保真度下能耗最低、脉冲面积守恒、谱权重集中于门相关跃迁，并对交换耦合涨落最鲁棒。此外，大规模统计研究揭示了一个弱驱动量子速度极限（quantum speed limit）：低于临界门时间T*时，低振幅两量子比特量子傅里叶变换的实现消失，最小控制能量服从面积-极点律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子最优控制（quantum optimal control）的核心目标是在实现高保真度的同时降低控制脉冲的能耗。现有方法（如Krotov、GRAPE）虽能独立优化每个时间步的脉冲点以获取高保真度，但往往导致宽带且高能耗的波形。因此，需要一种既能生成光滑、节能脉冲，又能保证高保真度的控制策略。

Method: 将MAGICARP方法从无漂移系统扩展到具有恒定漂移哈密顿量（drift Hamiltonian）的封闭系统，具体针对外部磁场中两个交换耦合自旋（exchange-coupled spins）系统。优化分阶段进行：首先利用漂移哈密顿量的缀饰态（dressed states）结构构建目标；然后在旋转波框架（rotating-wave frame）中进行初始打靶优化；最后在实验室框架（laboratory frame）中进行精确精修。

Result: 在匹配的门保真度（gate infidelity）下，MAGICARP始终实现最低能耗、保守的脉冲面积（pulse area），并将谱权重集中于门相关跃迁，同时对交换耦合（exchange coupling）涨落最为鲁棒。GRAPE可独立收敛至基本相同的脉冲，而Krotov方法则能耗高出一个数量级。大规模统计调查揭示了一个弱驱动量子速度极限：低于由漂移相互作用率设定的临界门时间T*时，两比特量子傅里叶变换的低振幅实现不复存在；最小控制能量在趋近该极限时发散，且该发散服从一个简单的二参数面积-极点律（area-pole law）。

Conclusion: MAGICARP方法在保持高保真度的同时，能够系统性生成能效最优、光谱纯净的量子控制脉冲。研究还揭示了由漂移哈密顿量相互作用率所决定的弱驱动量子速度极限，以及在该极限处的控制能量发散行为，为量子控制中的能量-时间权衡提供了理论依据。

Abstract: A central goal of quantum optimal control is to achieve high-fidelity and low-energy control pulses. When quantum optimal control methods optimize every point of a pulse discretized over small time steps independently this can yield high fidelity control but also results in broadband and energy-hungry waveforms. We extend MAGICARP -- a shooting method inspired by Pontryagin's maximum principle on energy that generates an entire pulse from a small set of parameters, making it smooth and energy-efficient by construction -- from driftless systems to closed systems with the constant drift Hamiltonian of two exchange-coupled spins in an external magnetic field. The optimization proceeds in stages: the dressed states of the drift Hamiltonian structure the target, an initial shooting optimization is performed in the rotating-wave frame, and an exact laboratory-frame refinement follows. Benchmarked against Krotov and GRAPE at matched gate infidelity, MAGICARP consistently achieves the lowest energy and a conserved pulse area, concentrates its spectral weight on the gate-relevant transitions, and is the most robust to fluctuations in the exchange coupling; GRAPE independently converges to essentially the same pulse, while Krotov's method pays an order-of-magnitude energy premium. Moreover, a large statistical survey of unselected optimization runs resolves a weak-driving quantum speed limit for two exchange-coupled electron spins: low-amplitude realizations of the two-qubit quantum Fourier transform cease to exist below a critical gate time $T^*$ set by the drift's interaction rate, and the minimum control energy diverges on approach to this limit. The divergence obeys a simple two-parameter area-pole law, $E_2^{\mathrm{law}}(T)=A/T+B/(T-T^*)$, whose first term is the time-optimal area cost and whose second term is a pole at the speed limit.

Coupled harmonic oscillators are also elucidated in connection with the Wigner phase space. It will be noted that the phase-space picture of quantum mechanics has become an important scientific language for the rapidly expanding field of quantum optics. Here, we mainly focus on the simplest form of the Wigner function, which finds application in many branches of quantum mechanics. We make use of several symmetry groups such as Lorentz groups, the symplectic group in two and four dimensions, and the Euclidean group. ### [113] [Entropic Uncertainty Relations for Mutually Unbiased Operator Frames](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23185)
*Jesni Shamsul Shaari,Stefano Mancini*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在算符的希尔伯特-施密特空间中建立了算符框架（operator-frame）形式的熵不确定关系（entropic uncertainty relation）。通过端点范数估计和Riesz-Thorin插值，推导了连续索引算符框架下系数分布的熵不确定关系；并进一步识别了一类互无偏算符框架（mutually unbiased operator frames），在适当结构条件下其系数振幅由双线性傅里叶变换联系，从而得到更强的Hirschman-Beckner型熵不确定关系。实例涵盖Weyl位移算符、Wigner核以及位置与动量本征态生成的笛卡尔二元框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将熵不确定关系从传统的测量结果（measurement outcomes）推广到算符表示（operator representations）本身，建立一种适用于算符框架（operator frames）的通用理论框架。

Method: 采用算符框架（operator-frame）形式化方法，在希尔伯特-施密特空间（Hilbert-Schmidt space）中处理问题；利用端点范数估计（endpoint norm estimates）结合Riesz-Thorin插值（Riesz-Thorin interpolation）推导一般结果；通过常数模迹重叠（constant-modulus trace overlaps）定义互无偏算符框架，并识别其系数振幅满足的双线性傅里叶变换（bilinear Fourier transform）结构。

Result: 推导了连续索引算符框架下系数分布的一般熵不确定关系，以及一类互无偏算符框架下的Hirschman-Beckner型更强熵不确定关系。Weyl位移算符、Wigner核以及位置与动量本征态框架等实例复现了连续变量傅里叶对偶性（Fourier dualities）。

Conclusion: 本文建立的算符框架熵不确定关系将相关概念从测量结果扩展到算符表示层面，为连续变量量子系统提供了一种更一般的理论工具。

Abstract: We develop an operator-frame formulation of entropic uncertainty relations in the Hilbert-Schmidt space of operators. For general continuous indexed operator frames, we derive an entropic uncertainty relation for the associated coefficient distributions by combining endpoint norm estimates with Riesz-Thorin interpolation. We then identify a distinguished class of mutually unbiased operator frames, defined through constant-modulus trace overlaps. Under suitable structural conditions, the corresponding coefficient amplitudes are related by a bilinear Fourier transform, leading to a stronger Hirschman-Beckner-type entropic uncertainty relation. As canonical realizations, we consider Weyl displacement operators and Wigner kernels, as well as Cartesian dyadic frames generated by position and momentum eigenstates. These examples recover familiar continuous-variable Fourier dualities while extending entropic uncertainty relations beyond measurement outcomes to operator representations themselves.

### [114] [Log-concavity and tunneling: adiabatic quantum optimization for convex functions (with a spike)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23614)
*Arthur Braida,Elie Bermot,Simon Apers*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过建立离散基态对数凹性（log-concavity）的通用框架，将绝热量子优化（Adiabatic Quantum Optimization, AQO）中量子隧穿（quantum tunneling）效应的分析从“汉明重量带尖峰”（HWS）问题推广至更一般的势能函数，并证明了对数凹性可用于扩展微扰分析，从而暗示隧穿效应在凸势能（convex potentials）中的更广泛适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管量子隧穿有望为量子计算提供加速（绝热量子优化所利用的核心现象），但除少数学术概念验证（如HWS问题）外，该效应的算法优势尚未得到充分探索；本文旨在将HWS问题的分析框架推广至更一般的势能函数。

Method: 首先，建立离散基态对数凹性（log-concavity of the ground state）作为关键结构性质，并为一大类离散一维薛定谔算子（Schrödinger operators）设计了对数凹性的证明框架；该框架涵盖凸势能以及某些具有局部极小值的势能。在凸势能情形下，该结果提供了Brascamp与Lieb（1976）连续结果的一个离散版本。其次，利用对数凹性结果将Reichardt（2004）针对HWS的微扰分析（perturbative analysis）推广至具有对数凹基态的更大势能族，并以线性势能到二次势能（quadratic potential）的拓展作为具体实例。

Result: 建立了新的能谱间隙界（spectral gap bounds），超越了Jarret与Jordan（2014）针对凸势能的相关结果；成功将对数凹性用于扩展微扰分析，将HWS分析从严格可解（exactly solvable）的线性势能推广到不可解（no longer solvable）的二次势能。

Conclusion: 本文结果强烈表明，量子隧穿效应在带有尖峰（spike）的凸势能中具有更广泛的适用性。

Abstract: Quantum tunneling is expected to provide a computational speedup in quantum computing, a phenomenon that Adiabatic Quantum Optimization (AQO) aims to leverage. While some academic proofs of concept have been studied, such as the "Hamming weight with a spike" (HWS) problem, the algorithmic gains of this effect remain underexplored. In this work we extend the analysis underlying HWS to more general potentials.
  In the first half of the work, we establish (discrete) log-concavity of the ground state as a key structural property in this context. We devise a framework for establishing log-concavity of the ground state for a large family of discrete, 1-dimensional Schrödinger operators. The family includes convex potentials, but also certain potentials with local minima. In the convex case, this provides a discrete version of a continuous result by Brascamp and Lieb ('76). We demonstrate the utility of our result by establishing new spectral gap bounds, going beyond related results by Jarret and Jordan ('14) for convex potentials.
  In the second half of the work, we use our results on log-concavity to extend the perturbative analysis of HWS by Reichardt ('04) to the larger family of potentials with log-concave ground state. As a concrete instantiation, we use our result to extend the HWS analysis from a linear potential (which is exactly solvable) to a quadratic potential (which is no longer solvable). Our result strongly suggests the broader applicability of tunneling to convex potentials with spikes

</details>


### [115] [Genuine certification of incompatible quantum instruments through sequential communication tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23647)
*Arindam Mitra,Satyaki Manna,Debashis Saha*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过引入一类三方通信任务（发送者、中继者、接收者），建立了量子仪器（quantum instruments）不相容性（incompatibility）的操作意义，并给出了所有兼容仪器所能达到的紧上界，违反该上界即认证了量子仪器的不可兼容性。该认证方案是真正的（genuine），因为它不依赖于仪器所诱导的测量与信道的不相容性，并且识别了实现该认证的最简通信场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子仪器是量子动力学的一般描述，涵盖量子测量与量子信道作为特例，因此量子仪器的不相容性是量子理论中非经典性的基本表现。然而，这一概念的操作意义（operational significance）尚未被充分建立，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 引入一类三方通信任务（涉及发送者、中继者和接收者），推导出所有兼容仪器（compatible instruments）下这些任务品质因数（figure of merits）的紧上界（tight upper bound），该上界与相同维度约束下经典通信中的最优性能一致。违反该上界即可认证中继者执行的量子仪器对是不相容的。

Result: 证明了不相容仪器认证是通信中量子优势的一种体现。该认证是真正的（genuine），因为它能认证一对仪器的不相容性，即使这些仪器所诱导的测量与信道是成对兼容的。此外，研究确定了能够实现不相容量子仪器认证的最简通信场景实例。

Conclusion: 该工作为量子仪器不相容性提供了操作意义上的通信任务支撑，并建立了一种半设备无关（semi-device-independent）的认证协议，揭示了不相容性在量子通信优势中的核心角色。

Abstract: Quantum instruments constitute the general description of quantum dynamics, encompassing both quantum measurements and quantum channels as special cases. Consequently, the incompatibility of quantum instruments represents a fundamental manifestation of nonclassicality in quantum theory. Here, we establish the operational significance of this notion by demonstrating communication tasks with classical inputs and outputs that enable the semi-device-independent certification of incompatible quantum instruments. We introduce a class of three-party communication tasks involving a sender, a relayer, and a receiver, and derive the tight upper bound of the figure of merits of these tasks achievable by all compatible instruments implemented by the relayer and this bound coincides with the optimal performance attainable in a classical communication subject to the same dimensional constraints. Violation of this bound certifies the incompatibility of the pair of quantum instruments implemented by the relayer. This identifies certification of incompatible instruments as a manifestation of quantum advantage in communication. This certification protocol is genuine as it is able to certify the incompatibility of a pair of instruments where the measurements and channels induced by the instruments are pairwise compatible and, therefore it does not depend on the incompability of measurements and channels induced by the instruments. Finally, we identify the simplest instances of our communication scenario that enable the certification of incompatible quantum instruments.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 时间演化的线性性（linearity of time evolution）和量子噪声（quantum noise）等典型量子特征在微观层面阻碍了同步的出现；但量子相干性和量子关联为超越经典同步提供了新颖的增强机制。

Conclusion: 量子同步是一个活跃的前沿研究方向，不仅在基础层面拓展了对同步现象的理解，还为在量子体系中实现更强、更丰富的同步行为提供了可能性。

Abstract: Can synchronization -- the widespread spontaneous emergence of coordinated dynamics in classical nonlinear systems -- also occur in the quantum regime? This question has recently sparked intense research into collective behavior and temporal self-organization in quantum systems. Typical quantum features such as the linearity of time evolution and the presence of quantum noise seem to hinder the appearance of synchrony at the microscopic level. At the same time, quantum coherence and quantum correlations may provide novel mechanisms for enhancing synchronization beyond its classical counterpart. We here survey recent theoretical and experimental advances in quantum synchronization, ranging from the characterization of synchronous oscillations and genuinely nonclassical forms of synchrony to many-body synchronization on quantum networks.

### [117] [Entanglement-entropy analysis of critical and topological quantum phases in a frustrated spin-1/2 Heisenberg ladder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21242)
*Azadeh Ghannadan,Hana Vargová,Jozef Genzor,Roman Krčmár,Andrej Gendiar*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用基于矩阵乘积态（matrix-product state, MPS）框架的密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）计算，通过分析两体纠缠（bipartite entanglement）、磁化强度（magnetization）和自旋关联（spin correlations）来表征量子相。

Conclusion: 纠缠测度的有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）比磁化强度和局域关联函数能更灵敏地统一诊断有能隙（gapped）与无能隙区域；各向异性参数α对相图结构具有关键调控作用。

Abstract: We investigate the ground-state phase diagram of a frustrated spin-1/2 Heisenberg ladder in the transverse magnetic field with an anisotropic inter-rung exchange coupling $α$. This bond-anisotropic parameter continuously interpolates among the Ising-like limit $α=0$, the isotropic point $α=1$, and the XY-dominated regime $α\gg 1$. Using density-matrix renormalization group calculations within a matrix-product-state framework, we analyze bipartite entanglement, magnetization, and spin correlations to characterize the emergent quantum phases. We identify six distinct ground-state phases, including rung-singlet, Haldane-like, Tomonaga-Luttinger liquid, canted Ising-ordered, XY-polarized, and ordered ferromagnetic states. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究玻色约瑟夫森结在突然淬火下的非平衡功统计，特别是初始量子相干性对功分布及可提取功的影响，并探索超越经典界限的功提取可能性。

Method: 采用Holstein-Primakoff近似将系统映射为时间依赖的量子谐振子（time-dependent quantum harmonic oscillator），在弱相互作用区解析表征功统计；对含有能量基相干性的初始叠加态，使用Kirkwood-Dirac拟概率（Kirkwood-Dirac quasiprobabilities, KDQ）描述功分布。

Result: 基态初始化的系统功统计服从负二项分布；初始基态与第二激发态的叠加态下，KDQ功分布出现负值或复数值，体现非经典特征；优化初始状态的相干性可在淬火后提升超越经典界限的可提取功。

Conclusion: 量子相干性在非平衡功统计中扮演关键角色，可被利用来增强功提取，并提出实验干涉测量协议（interferometric protocol）以直接测量功分布的特征函数（characteristic function）。

Abstract: We investigate the non-equilibrium work statistics originating from a sudden quench in a bosonic Josephson junction. In particular, by employing the Holstein-Primakoff approximation, the work statistics are analytically characterized in the weak-interaction regime, where the dynamics map onto a time-dependent quantum harmonic oscillator. For a junction initialized in the ground state of the pre-quench Hamiltonian, we demonstrate that the work statistics are governed by a negative binomial distribution, as occurs in fully-connected models driven across a critical point. Furthermore, we also consider initial superposition states containing quantum coherences in the energy basis. To characterize the corresponding work distributions, we employ Kirkwood-Dirac quasiprobabilities (KDQ). Even in the simplest case, when the junction is initialized in a superposition of the ground and second excited states, the KDQ distribution of work exhibits negative or complex values, reflecting non-classical features. Moreover, the coherence content of the initial state can be optimized to enhance the extractable work extracted from the quench, beyond classical bounds. Finally, we propose an experimental interferometric protocol to directly measure the characteristic function of the work distribution in experimentally accessible settings.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超辐射激光作为一种新型主动光学钟（active optical clock）架构，其强度稳定性对于作为光学频段的频率参考至关重要，因此需要系统分析其稳定边界及潜在的不稳定行为。

Method: 采用平均场（mean-field）理论框架进行分析，推导出失稳的解析判据；并通过与流体湍流中的Bénard失稳（Bénard instability）进行映射对比，结合量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）效应（包括光子输出耦合（photon out-coupling）与原子的重新填充（atom re-filling））修正预期行为。

Result: 发现当腔中光子寿命（photon lifetime）显著短于原子寿命（atom lifetime）时，超辐射激光可能失稳并发展出混沌行为（chaotic behavior）；此外，在大原子数条件下存在规则的自脉冲（self-pulsing）工作机制。

Conclusion: 该稳定性判据有助于优化超辐射激光作为光学频率参考所需的参数，同时指出在失稳区域中，超辐射激光为研究混沌现象提供了一个有趣的新平台。

Abstract: We investigate the intensity stability of the superradiant laser. Our study focuses on the architecture where a continuous beam of atoms in an electronically excited state crosses the mode of a high-finesse Fabry-Perot cavity, which has been proposed as a new architecture of an active optical clock. We show that such superradiant laser can become unstable and develop chaotic behavior. We derive an analytical criterion for this instability and find that it may only occur when the lifetime of photons in the cavity is significantly shorter than the lifetime of atoms. This criterion allows for refining the necessary parameters to run a superradiant laser as a frequency reference in the optical domain. In particular, we point-out the consequences of the instability on intensity fluctuations and laser linewidth. On the other hand, we also point out that the superradiant laser, when in the unstable regime, can become an interesting playground for studying chaos. At the mean-field level, there is a direct mapping to the Bénard instability associated with fluid turbulence; however quantum fluctuations associated with photon out-coupling and atom re-filling substantially modify the expected behaviors. Finally, we point-out the existence of a regular self-pulsing regime at large atom numbers.

### [120] [Prethermal cooling with many-body quantum quenches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21813)
*Jacob F. Steiner,Mohammad Hafezi,Stefan Kehrein,Gil Refael*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在多体量子淬火（quantum quench）中，对系统做正功的淬火反而能有效冷却低能自由度，前提是淬火能量被存储在长寿命的高能激发中。在强耦合费米子哈伯德模型中，淬火产生长寿命的双子（doublon）密度，并形成持续指数长时间的预热态（prethermal state），在此期间有效预热温度降低，类似于绝热去磁的多体推广。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为多体量子淬火通常伴随加热效应。本文试图探究在何种条件下，对系统做正功的淬火反而能实现低能自由度的有效冷却，并给出具体的物理机制与模型验证。

Method: 以半满填充的强耦合费米子哈伯德模型（Fermionic Hubbard model）为具体系统，对跃迁项 t 实施量子淬火。利用该模型中双子（doublon）激发具有极长寿命（时间尺度指数依赖于 (U/t)^2）的特性，分析淬火后预热态的热力学行为。

Result: 预热态的有效温度相对于初始温度降低了终态与初态跃迁振幅比值的平方。对于保双子数（doublon-number conserving）的算符，系统满足一个有效的涨落-耗散关系（fluctuation-dissipation relation）。

Conclusion: 哈伯德系统在淬火后可作为制冷剂来冷却目标系统，前提是耦合过程保双子数。该方案可视为绝热去磁（adiabatic demagnetization）在量子淬火多体系统中的推广。

Abstract: Many-body quantum quenches are typically associated with heating. In this work, we show that quantum quenches that perform positive work on the system can still lead to effective cooling of low-energy degrees of freedom if the quench energy is deposited in long-lived high-energy excitations. We discuss this explicitly for a quench of the hopping term t in the strong-coupling (U >> t) fermionic Hubbard model at half filling, where the quench induces a very long-lived non-equilibrium doublon density. The associated prethermal state persists for a time exponentially large in (U/t)^2. During this time window, we find an effective prethermal temperature that is reduced by the square of the ratio of final to initial hopping amplitude with respect to the initial temperature. This manifests as an effective fluctuation-dissipation relation that holds for doublon-number conserving operators. In a practical implementation the Hubbard system acts as a refrigerant to cool a target system provided the coupling conserves doublon number. Our protocol can be thought of as a quantum quench many-body generalization of adiabatic demagnetization.

### [121] [Transient Information Partition in Coherent Exciton-Phonon-Photon Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22099)
*Kunio Ishida*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用子系统分辨的量子互信息（QMI）分析激子-声子-光子相干系统中的瞬态信息划分，揭示了光学活性不能唯一确定光致瞬态特征，发现了一个隐藏的瞬态关联脊结构，该结构对应于有限能量的极化子激发。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在激子-声子-光子相干系统中，光致瞬态态的特征不能仅由光学吸收决定，缺乏基于关联结构的系统刻画框架。本文旨在发展一个基于量子互信息（QMI）的信息划分方法，以区分不同瞬态响应（如极化激元态与极化子态）并揭示隐藏在静态表征之外的瞬态关联结构。

Method: 采用包含激子、声子和光子自由度的理论模型，在$J$-$\nu$平面（$J$表征激子离域化，$\nu$表征激子-声子耦合强度）上分析动力学。通过比较时间平均的QMI图谱与吸收光子数，利用以激子为中心和以声子为中心的信息划分来刻画信息在子系统间的分配。此外，采用变分强度函数分析（variational strength-function analysis）识别隐藏的关联结构。

Result: 激子中心的信息划分识别出极化激元（polariton-like）与极化子（polaron-like）瞬态响应之间的宽交叉区；声子中心的划分则揭示出零-单激子基态扇区边界附近的一个尖锐边界相邻的重分布脊（boundary-adjacent redistribution ridge）。该脊既非基态扇区边界，也非光学吸收增强，而是在有限能量极化子激发（region-II-like polaronic excitation）中浮现，其主导谱权重位于单声子能量附近。

Conclusion: QMI基的信息划分为表征光与物质自由度量子力学共同参与的光致相干瞬态态提供了基于关联的框架，能够揭示出静态或光学吸收分析无法捕捉的隐藏瞬态关联结构。

Abstract: We study transient information partition in a coherent exciton-phonon-photon system using subsystem-resolved quantum mutual information (QMI). By employing a model with excitonic, phononic, and photonic degrees of freedom, we analyze the dynamics in the $J$-$ν$ plane, where $J$ characterizes excitonic delocalization and $ν$ denotes the exciton-phonon coupling strength. By comparing time-averaged QMI maps with the absorbed photon number, we show that optical activity alone does not determine the character of the light-induced transient state. The exciton-centered information partition identifies a broad crossover between polariton-like and polaron-like transient responses, depending on whether excitonic information is mainly shared with the photon or phonon subsystem. In contrast, the phonon-centered partition reveals a sharper boundary-adjacent redistribution ridge near the boundary between the zero- and one-exciton ground-state sectors. This ridge is absent from both the ground-state sector map and the photon-absorption map, indicating that it is neither a static sector boundary nor an enhancement of optical absorption. A variational strength-function analysis connects the ridge to a region-II-like finite-energy polaronic excitation whose dominant spectral weight lies near the one-phonon energy, and thus the ridge represents a hidden transient correlation structure in which a limited amount of phonon-related information is preferentially shared with the photon subsystem before being predominantly allocated to exciton-phonon dressing. These results show that QMI-based information partition provides a correlation-based framework for characterizing coherent light-induced transient states in which optical and material degrees of freedom jointly participate quantum mechanically.

### [122] [Machine Learning Optimal Quantum Error Correction Thresholds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22194)
*Dominik Seip,Luis Colmenarez,Markus Schmitt,Markus Müller*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了量子相干信息（coherent information, CI）与神经网络解码器训练中交叉熵损失之间的直接联系，证明CI是可实现损失的一个锐利下界；并提出基于Transformer的最大似然解码（maximum likelihood decoding, MLD）网络，在表面码（surface code）上准确预测CI、超越最小权重完美匹配（minimum weight perfect matching, MWPM）解码器，同时引入一种最优且可扩展的软后选择（soft post-selection）策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子纠错码（quantum error correction, QEC）的性能会在超过特定噪声阈值后急剧下降，揭示出保护量子信息的基本极限；需要一种信息论指标来刻画这些极限，并建立其与可训练解码器性能之间的联系。

Method: 建立相干信息（coherent information, CI）与二值交叉熵损失（binary cross-entropy loss）之间的下界关系；开发基于Transformer的最大似然解码（maximum likelihood decoding, MLD）神经网络模型；提出基于MLD陪集（cosets）的软后选择（soft post-selection）方案，并证明其最优性。

Result: 该网络在三种噪声模型（code capacity、phenomenological、circuit-level noise）下准确预测CI，阈值估计与已知理论极限高度吻合；作为解码器，其逻辑错误率（logical error rate）显著优于最小权重完美匹配（MWPM）解码器；所提软后选择方案在逻辑错误率和中止概率（abort probability）两方面均表现出可扩展性。

Conclusion: Transformer架构是量子纠错（quantum error correction, QEC）的有力工具；首次数值验证了基于最大似然解码（MLD）的后选择策略的最优性与可扩展性。

Abstract: As quantum computers remain susceptible to noise, QEC is essential for preserving logical information during computations. However, the performance of QEC codes breaks down beyond certain noise thresholds, revealing fundamental limits on their ability to protect quantum information. These limits can be characterized using information-theoretic measures such as the coherent information, which quantifies the maximum rate at which logical information can be reliably transmitted through a noisy quantum channel. In this work, we establish a direct connection between the CI and the binary cross-entropy loss used when training neural network decoders. Specifically, we show that the CI constitutes a sharp lower bound on the achievable loss for decoders that track logical operators across noisy channels. To this end, we develop a transformer-based neural network model based on maximum likelihood decoding. We train this network to estimate the CI and evaluate its performance on the surface code under three noise models: code capacity, phenomenological, and circuit-level noise. Our results demonstrate that the network accurately predicts CI and yields threshold estimates that closely match known theoretical limits. When used as a decoder, the network significantly outperforms the minimum weight perfect matching decoder in terms of logical error rate. We also introduce a novel soft post-selection scheme that independently treats uncertainty in both logical operators and relies on confidence-based filtering of the network's output. We prove that such post-selection strategies, based on the MLD cosets, are optimal, and demonstrate their scalability in terms of both logical error rate and abort probability. These findings establish transformer-based architectures as powerful tools for QEC and provide the first numerical evidence supporting the optimality and scalability of MLD-based post-selection.

</details>


### [123] [Hierarchy of mixed symmetry protected topological states in extended cluster states under subsystem decoherence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22507)
*Yoshihito Kuno,Takahiro Orito*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究子系统退相干对扩展簇态（一种对称保护拓扑相）的影响，发现退相干可在未被影响的子系统中诱导出层级化的混合态SPT相，并最终演化为Z2强-弱自发对称破缺（SWSSB）态与玻璃态GHZ长程纠缠，揭示了退相干作为诱导而非破坏性过程的系统化路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解子系统退相干（subsystem decoherence）对处于对称保护拓扑（symmetry protected topological, SPT）相的扩展簇态（extended cluster state）的影响，探究退相干能否从混合态中诱导出非平庸的拓扑序。

Method: 研究一个包含多个子系统Z2对称性的扩展簇态模型，通过逐步施加子系统退相干，分析混合态SPT相的层级结构及其表征，利用Rényi-2弦序（Rényi-2 string order）作为序参量刻画这些混合态SPT相。

Result: 子系统退相干在未受影响的子系统中诱导出局部电荷涨落，产生混合态SPT相；逐步退相干下，层级化混合态SPT相最终终止于Z2强-弱自发对称破缺（strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking, SWSSB）态，该态表现为玻璃态GHZ（glassy Greenberger-Horne-Zeilinger, GHZ）长程纠缠态。

Conclusion: 退相干不仅是破坏性过程，还能诱导并组织一系列非平庸混合态，揭示了从混合态SPT序到SWSSB及玻璃态GHZ长程纠缠的系统化演化路径。

Abstract: We study the effect of subsystem decoherence to an extended cluster state which is a symmetry protected topological (SPT) phase. The model includes many subsystem $Z_2$ symmetries. We report that subsystem decoherence induces local charge fluctuations, leading to a mixed SPT state in the unaffected subsystems. If we start from the extended cluster state, hierarchical mixed-state SPT phases emerge in response to step-by-step subsystem decoherences. These mixed-state SPT phases keep strong symmetries the symmetry of which is protecting symmetries for the initial cluster SPT. Moreover, these SPTs can be characterized by Rényi-2 string orders. Then, as the subsystems are progressively decohered, the hierarchy of mixed-state SPT phases terminates in a $Z_2$ strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking (SWSSB) state on the final remaining subsystem, where a long-range entangled state appears, namely a glassy Greenberger-Horne-Zeilinger (GHZ) state. Our work demonstrates that decoherence is not merely a destructive process, but can induce and organize series of nontrivial mixed-states. This reveals a systematic route from mixed-state SPT order to SWSSB with the glassy GHZ-type long-range entanglement.

</details>


### [124] [A single-electron double quantum dot with Rashba spin-orbit interaction as a working substance for heat machines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22733)
*Ivan Romualdo de Oliveira,Vinícius N. A. Lula-Rocha,Moises Rojas*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了在双量子点中由单个电子构成的量子奥托机器，分析了Rashba自旋-轨道耦合（Rashba spin-orbit interaction）作为调控参数如何使系统在热机、制冷机、加热器和加速器四种热力学模式间切换，并揭示了效率与输出功之间存在由参数空间控制的权衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子尺度下热力学循环的调控机制，特别是自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）在量子热机（quantum heat engine）中作为可控参数的可能性。

Method: 采用准静态奥托循环（quasistatic Otto cycle）框架，对一个处于外磁场和Rashba自旋-轨道耦合作用下的双量子点（double quantum dot）中单个电子的哈密顿量进行参数化分析，数值计算热交换、输出功和效率随Zeeman分裂（Zeeman splitting）、隧穿振幅（interdot tunneling amplitude）及Rashba耦合的变化。

Result: Rashba相互作用可有效作为切换热机、制冷机、加热器和加速器四种工作模式的调控参数。最高效率出现在最大温度梯度附近并趋近Carnot界限（Carnot bound），最大输出功则位于参数空间中的不同区域。

Conclusion: 最大效率与最大输出功之间存在明确的权衡关系，该关系由Zeeman分裂、隧穿振幅和Rashba耦合导致的能谱形变（spectral deformation）所决定。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic performance of a quantum Otto machine whose working substance is a single electron confined in a double quantum dot under an external magnetic field and Rashba spin-orbit interaction. The Hamiltonian is controlled by the Zeeman splitting, the interdot tunneling amplitude, and the Rashba coupling, which induces spin-flip tunneling between localized orbital states. Within a quasistatic Otto cycle, we analyze the heat exchanged with the reservoirs, the extracted work, and the efficiency as functions of the Hamiltonian parameters and reservoir temperatures. We show that the Rashba interaction acts as an effective control parameter for switching among heat-engine, refrigerator, heater, and accelerator regimes. A global numerical analysis over the Hamiltonian parameters and reservoir temperatures identifies the optimal operating points for efficiency and work output in the heat-engine regime. The highest efficiencies occur near the maximum temperature gradient explored and approach the Carnot bound, whereas the largest work output appears in a different region of parameter space. The results reveal a clear trade-off between maximum efficiency and maximum extracted work, governed by the spectral deformation induced by the Zeeman splitting, tunneling amplitude, and Rashba coupling.

</details>

### [125] [Revisiting creeping viscoelastic cross-slot flow: Global linear stability and structural sensitivity analyses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21554)
*Kun Zhang,Zhanwen Wang,Lailai Zhu*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟、全局稳定性分析、结构敏感性分析和能量预算分析，揭示了近半个世纪未被解释的交叉槽流（cross-slot flow）黏弹性失稳（viscoelastic instability）的物理起源：该失稳源于拉伸主导区域（extension-dominated regions）内的弹性能量释放（elastic-energy release），而非尖锐拐角或自由中心驻点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交叉槽流的黏弹性失稳虽在近50年前被实验观测、20年前被数值复现，但其物理起源长期未得到解释。

Method: 对二维Oldroyd-B流体（Oldroyd-B fluid）的蠕动流（creeping flow）分别采用直接数值模拟、全局稳定性分析（global stability analysis）、结构敏感性分析（structural sensitivity analysis）和能量预算分析（energy-budget analysis）四种方法联合研究。

Result: 模拟复现了典型的叉型分岔（pitchfork bifurcation），稳定性分析一致预测了阈值和扰动增长率。主导本征模态（eigenmode）由手性速度-应力扰动（chiral velocity–stress perturbation）构成，使拉伸流产生的双折射束（birefringent strand）发生倾斜和旋转。结构敏感性和能量预算分析指出，拉伸流内狭窄的高拉伸率脊（high-extension-rate ridges）既是失稳的空间核心也是能量来源；其中，应力波发生器（stress-based wavemaker）与扰动聚合物应力功率密度（disturbance polymeric stress power density）的正大值共定位。对带圆角和中心圆柱的变体分析表明，尖锐拐角和自由中心驻点均非失稳的必要因素。

Conclusion: 交叉槽流失稳的根本起源在于拉伸主导区域中储存弹性能量向扰动流的局部释放，而非几何上的尖锐拐角或驻点。

Abstract: The viscoelastic instability of cross-slot flow was first observed experimentally almost half a century ago and reproduced numerically two decades ago, yet its physical origin remains unresolved. We revisit this problem for two-dimensional creeping flow of Oldroyd-B fluid by combining direct numerical simulations, global stability analysis, structural sensitivity analysis, and energy-budget analysis. Our simulations reproduce the canonical pitchfork bifurcation, and the stability analysis consistently predicts the threshold and perturbation growth rates. The leading eigenmode consists of a chiral velocity--stress perturbation that tilts and rotates the birefringent strand generated by the extensional flow. Structural sensitivity and energy-budget analyses identify narrow high-extension-rate ridges within the extensional flow as both the spatial core and energetic source of the instability. In these ridges, the stress-based wavemaker co-localizes with large positive disturbance polymeric stress power density, indicating localized transfer of stored elastic energy to the disturbance flow. Analyses of cross-slot variants with rounded corners and with a centered cylinder further reveal that neither sharp corners nor a free central stagnation point is the essential destabilizing ingredient; rather, the instability originates from elastic-energy release in extension-dominated regions characteristic of cross-slot flow.

</details>

### [126] [Cosmology as Representation: Informational Invariance and the Limits of Scientific Realism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21586)
*Stefano Profumo*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 本文挑战了宇宙学通过数学模型逼近本体论（ontology）的传统理解，主张宇宙学的客观内容应被识别为跨表征的信息不变量（cross-representational informational invariants），而非对基础实在的唯一描述；科学进步在于观察性信息结构的渐进精炼，而非朝向固定本体论的收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者旨在质疑宇宙学中一个常见假设，即经验上成功的数学模型能提供对宇宙本体论（ontology）日益精确的描述；其核心动机在于指出经验证据无法唯一确定本体论，甚至无法确定用于表征数据的数学和概念框架。

Method: 采用哲学论证与信息论（information theory）工具相结合的方法，提出以跨表征信息不变量（cross-representational informational invariants）作为宇宙学客观内容的判定标准，并利用费舍尔-拉奥度量（Fisher-Rao metric）等工具在模型空间中进行形式化。

Result: 论证结果表明，宇宙学模型的最佳理解方式是作为观察结构的高效编码（efficient encodings），而非对基础实在拥有特权地位的描述；科学进步应被重新定义为观察可及的信息结构（informational structure accessible to observation）的逐步精细化。

Conclusion: 宇宙学的客观内容应当基于在经验上充分的多种描述中保持不变的信息论特征——包括相关结构（correlation structure）、统计可区分性（statistical distinguishability）和可获取信息（accessible information）的限制——来进行识别，而非依赖于对单一本体论的趋同。

Abstract: Modern cosmology is often taken to provide an increasingly accurate description of the universe's underlying ontology through progressively refined mathematical models. I challenge this interpretation by arguing that the empirical success of cosmology underdetermines not only ontology but also the mathematical and conceptual frameworks used to represent observational data. I propose instead that the objective content of cosmology is best identified with cross-representational informational invariants-features of observational structure that persist across empirically adequate descriptions. These invariants can be characterized in information-theoretic terms, including correlation structure, statistical distinguishability, and limits on accessible information, and formalized using tools such as the Fisher-Rao metric on model space. On this view, cosmological models are best understood as efficient encodings of observational structure rather than uniquely privileged descriptions of fundamental reality. Scientific progress, accordingly, consists not in convergence toward a fixed ontology, but in the progressive refinement of the informational structure accessible to observation.

</details>

*Si Li,Yong Li,Xinxing Tang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文从皮卡-勒夫谢茨理论（Picard-Lefschetz theory）的视角，研究了短时热核渐近展开（short-time heat kernel asymptotics）的重整结构（resurgent structure），证明热核具有1-格弗里（1-Gevrey）小时间展开，其波莱尔变换（Borel transform）能检测超越实测地线扇区的复几何数据。作者在复化路径空间上构造了莫尔斯-弗洛尔型（Morse-Floer type）的无穷维皮卡-勒夫谢茨问题，提出了热核版本的皮卡-勒夫谢茨/异元对应（Picard-Lefschetz/Alien correspondence），并通过双曲平面 $H^2$ 的数值检验验证了该方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统热核渐近展开局限于实测地线扇区（real geodesic sector），难以触及复几何（complex geometry）信息。本文旨在利用重整化（resurgence）理论与皮卡-勒夫谢茨理论，建立热核渐近展开中实扇区与复扇区之间形式上的代数对应关系，从而揭示隐藏在短时热核背后的复几何结构。

Method: 首先证明实解析黎曼流形（real analytic Riemannian manifold）上的热核具有1-格弗里小时间展开，并进行波莱尔变换以提取复几何数据。然后，在复化路径空间（complexified path space）上定义全纯能量泛函（holomorphic energy functional），构造无穷维的莫尔斯-弗洛尔型皮卡-勒夫谢茨问题。在此基础上，提出热核版本的皮卡-勒夫谢茨/异元对应，其中尖点异元算子（pointed alien operators）作用于实测地线对应的渐近展开，产生与其他全纯测地线（holomorphic geodesics）关联的形式热核扇区，系数由莫尔斯流（Morse flow）的连接轨迹（connecting trajectories）的有符号计数给出。

Result: 在双曲平面 $H^2$ 上对这一理论方案进行了具体检验，验证了尖点异元算子通过连接轨迹的计数能够正确生成复扇区热核的渐近形式，从而确认了所提出对应关系的有效性。

Conclusion: 热核的短时渐近展开蕴含着重整结构，可通过皮卡-勒夫谢茨理论与异元微积分（alien calculus）进行系统刻画。这一框架将热核渐近分析与复几何、莫尔斯理论（Morse theory）有机联系起来，为研究几何算子的谱信息和非微扰效应提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We study the resurgent structure of short-time heat kernel asymptotics from the viewpoint of Picard-Lefschetz theory. For a real analytic Riemannian manifold, we show the heat kernel admits a 1-Gevrey small-time expansion whose Borel transform detects complex-geometric data beyond the real geodesic sector. We formulate an infinite-dimensional Picard-Lefschetz problem of Morse-Floer type for the holomorphic energy functional on the complexified path space, and propose a heat-kernel analogue of the Picard-Lefschetz/Alien correspondence. In this framework, pointed alien operators acting on the asymptotic expansion associated with the real geodesic are predicted to produce the formal heat-kernel sectors associated with other holomorphic geodesics, with coefficients given by signed counts of connecting trajectories of the Morse flow. We perform a confirming test of this proposal on the hyperbolic plane $H^2$.

</details>

### [133] [Electromagnetic Characterization of Magnetic Bar: Case of Square Cross-Section Shape](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22117)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于笛卡尔坐标系下的麦克斯韦方程组（Maxwell's equations），结合复数磁导率（complex permeability），利用双曲函数（hyperbolic functions）进行变量分离，推导出互阻抗、内部磁场、磁通量和磁芯损耗的精确数学表达式，并在数学上解耦涡流损耗（eddy current）与磁滞损耗（hysteresis losses）。

Result: 在1 Hz–1 MHz频率范围内，表观相对磁导率从500下降至300；在约700 kHz处出现特征电阻峰值，标志着损耗机制从体积极限（volumetric）向表面主导（surface-dominated）的转变。

Conclusion: 所提出的新表观磁导率参数提供了一种快速、可靠的磁钢表征方法，能够绕过有限元分析的大量处理时间，并为方截面磁性棒材的电磁行为提供完整的解析框架。

Abstract: This paper presents a complete two-dimensional theoretical model for the electromagnetic behavior of square-section solid magnetic bars under sinusoidal loading. Through the application of Maxwell's equations within a Cartesian coordinate system and the integration of complex permeability, exact mathematical expressions are derived for mutual impedance, internal magnetic fields, flux, and core losses. Hyperbolic functions are utilized to separate the variables, enabling the accurate representation of edge flux accumulation and the 2D skin effect. In addition to mathematically decoupling eddy current and hysteresis losses, this formulation yields a new apparent permeability parameter. This parameter establishes a fast, reliable method for magnetic steel characterization that bypasses the extensive processing times associated with Finite Element Analysis (FEA). Numerical results over 1 Hz-1 MHz show the apparent relative permeability decreasing from 500 to 300 and a characteristic resistance peak near 700 kHz, marking the transition from volumetric to surface-dominated loss regimes.

### [134] [Level lines of the Gaussian free field and $c=1$ degenerate conformal blocks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22228)
*Alex Karrila,Eveliina Peltola,Lukas Schoug*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，单连通区域上分段常数狄利克雷边界条件下的高斯自由场（GFF）的等高线穿越概率可由中心荷 $c=1$ 的共形场论（CFT）中的共形块（conformal blocks）确定，亦可表示为融合多 SLE₄ 曲线的配分函数之比；同时证明度量图 GFF 的穿越概率在标度极限下收敛至相同公式，从而揭示两类 GFF 模型涨落几何的 CFT 描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用共形块（conformal blocks）描述穿越概率；将其写为融合多 SLE₄ 曲线（fused multiple SLE₄ curves）的配分函数之比，并借助拉菲、佩尔托拉和鲁西永近期引入的融合 Specht 多项式（fused Specht polynomials）显式表达；对度量图 GFF（metric graph GFF）考虑适当边界条件并证明标度极限收敛。

Result: GFF 等高线穿越概率由 $c=1$ CFT 中每个插入点处退化的初级场（primary fields）共形块决定；对于度量图 GFF，其水平集（level sets）穿越概率在标度极限下收敛至同一公式；并非所有组合边界条件在 GFF 模型中都可行——仅有满足特定单调性约束的广义 Dyck 路径（generalized Dyck paths）标签对应的共形块出现。

Conclusion: 连续 GFF 与度量图 GFF 的水平集逾渗几何（level-set percolation）均可由 $c=1$ 共形块给出 CFT 描述，且这些共形块线性无关并满足任意阶的 Belavin–Polyakov–Zamolodchikov (BPZ) 偏微分方程。

Abstract: We consider Gaussian free field (GFF) on simply connected domains with piecewise constant Dirichlet boundary data. We show that the crossing probabilities for its level lines are determined by conformal blocks of primary fields in a conformal field theory (CFT) with central charge $c = 1$ which are degenerate at each insertion. Alternatively, the crossing probabilities are ratios of explicit partition functions of fused multiple $\mathrm{SLE}_4$ curves, which can be written in terms of fused Specht polynomials introduced recently by Lafay, Peltola, & Roussillon in a representation-theoretic context.
  We also prove that for the metric graph GFF introduced by Lupu, with appropriate boundary conditions, the crossing probabilities for its level sets converge in the scaling limit to our formulas. In particular, the geometry of the level-set percolation for both the continuum GFF and the metric graph GFF has a CFT description in terms of the aforementioned $c=1$ conformal blocks, which are linearly independent and solve the Belavin-Polyakov-Zamolodchikov (BPZ) PDEs of arbitrary orders.
  Interestingly, not all combinatorial boundary conditions are amenable for the GFF models -- while the CFT contains conformal blocks of primary fields labeled by generalized Dyck paths (i.e., semi-standard Young tableaux), the ones appearing in the above models satisfy specific monotonicity constraints.

### [135] [Singular barriers and quartic integrability breaking in the TTW system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22322)
*Adrian M. Escobar Ruiz,Miguel E. Gómez Quintanar,Lidia Jiménez-Lara,Jaume Llibre*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类对称四次形变下的Tempesta-Turbiner-Winternitz（TTW）系统，通过共振平均与Poincaré不可积性判据，证明了在小四次耦合参数κ下系统不存在第二个独立的C^1首次积分，从而建立局域不可积性；在有限耦合下，Poincaré截面与有限时间李雅普诺夫映射展示不变环面破裂与混沌层的增长，并指出TTW系统的奇异壁垒抑制了相空间输运。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究经典TTW系统在四次形变下的可积性转变：该系统插值于最大超可积（maximally superintegrable）的Smorodinsky-Winternitz振子与四次耦合的Contopoulos振子之间。作者希望明确四次耦合项是否破坏系统的可积性，并理解逆向平方势（inverse-square terms）产生的壁垒对相空间结构的影响。

Method: 采用共振平均（resonant averaging）方法分析小幅四次耦合效应，导出相位锁定周期轨道（phase-locked periodic orbit）。在固定能量下构造约化Poincaré映射（reduced Poincaré map），检验其特征乘子（characteristic multiplier）是否为单位模；若否，则依据Poincaré非可积性判据（Poincaré’s nonintegrability criterion）排除第二个独立的C^1首次积分。在有限耦合下，利用Poincaré截面（Poincaré sections）与有限时间李雅普诺夫映射（finite-time Lyapunov maps）数值刻画混沌行为。

Result: 对足够小的非零κ，共振平均得到的周期轨道对应的约化Poincaré映射不存在单位特征乘子，因此在该轨道的任意不变邻域内不存在第二个独立C^1首次积分。有限耦合下，Poincaré截面与有限时间李雅普诺夫映射显示，随能量与四次耦合增强，不变曲线（invariant curves）破裂、混沌层（chaotic layers）增长。相比无壁垒的Contopoulos极限，TTW系统的逆向平方势壁垒抑制了相空间输运（phase-space transport），但并未恢复可积性。

Conclusion: TTW系统的四次形变在相空间中产生局域的不可积性，该不可积性在微扰意义下是成立的；有限耦合时系统呈现混沌特征。奇异壁垒的存在虽然阻碍了全局相空间输运，却不足以使系统回归可积状态。

Abstract: We study a symmetric quartic deformation of the classical ($k=1$) Tempesta-Turbiner-Winternitz system, $H=\frac{1}{2}\left(P_X^2+P_Y^2\right)+X^2+Y^2 +\fracγ{X^2}+\fracγ{Y^2} +κ\,X^2Y^2 $, which interpolates between the maximally superintegrable Smorodinsky-Winternitz oscillator and the quartically coupled Contopoulos oscillator. For $γ>0$, the inverse-square terms generate impenetrable walls at ($X=0$) and ($Y=0$), splitting configuration space into invariant sectors. We show that, for sufficiently small nonzero $κ$, resonant averaging produces a phase-locked periodic orbit whose fixed-energy reduced Poincaré map has no unit characteristic multiplier. The Poincaré's nonintegrability criterion then excludes a second independent $C^1$ first integral in any invariant neighbourhood of this orbit. The result is local in phase space and perturbative in $κ$. At finite coupling, Poincaré sections and finite-time Lyapunov maps show the breakup of invariant curves and the growth of chaotic layers with increasing energy and quartic coupling. Comparison with the barrier-free Contopoulos limit shows that the singular TTW walls suppress phase-space transport without restoring integrability.

Namely, these are asymptotics, the method based on the adiabatic invariance of the action of a trapped wave, and the consideration of the equivalent Hamiltonian system. ### [137] [Minimum Virtual Proper Time and Finite Mass--Charge Matching in QED](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22666)
*Mustafa Bakr*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种有限固有时版本的量子电动力学（finite-proper-time QED），通过引入一个物理性下限的固有时积分，实现了有限且横向的真空极化、精确的Ward-Takahashi恒等式，并在微扰层次上保持了反射正性、幺正性和紫外有限性，同时给出了可计算的有限反常磁矩修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准量子电动力学（QED）中存在紫外发散（ultraviolet divergences），需要重整化（renormalization）处理，且其固有时积分通常被延拓至零。本文旨在构造一个无需移除固有时积分下限的有限QED形式体系，以实现天然有限且物理自洽的理论框架。

Method: 通过构造一个规范协变的生成泛函（gauge-covariant generating functional），规定所有Schwinger固有时积分具有一个物理性下限 s₀=Λ⁻²，且不移除该下限。闭合费米子圈由规范协变的热核行列式（heat-kernel determinant）定义，开端费米子线则通过对同一有限固有时开端核（open-line kernel）进行泛函微分得到。

Result: 证明了Ward-Takahashi恒等式完全由规范协变性导出至所有阶；真空极化是有限且严格横向的；在单圈近似下，选取Λ=13 TeV时给出了0.482 MeV的壳上质量关系；证明了自由有限固有时传播子满足Osterwalder-Schrader反射正性，Källén-Lehmann谱函数为正且无额外鬼态；单圈壳上留数Z₂>0确认了费米子扇区的幺正性；修整传播子的微扰谱函数为正；世界线约束Q≤0确保了固定阶欧氏紫外有限性；单圈顶点修正给出了有限的反常磁矩（anomalous magnetic moment），产生了标准QED中不存在的可计算的O(m²/Λ²)预言。

Conclusion: 该有限固有时QED构建了一个在微扰论下紫外有限、保持规范协变性、反射正性和幺正性的自洽理论框架，并在低能可观测效应（如反常磁矩）中引入了依赖于截断尺度Λ的有限修正。

Abstract: We formulate a finite-proper-time version of QED defined by a gauge-covariant generating functional in which every Schwinger proper-time integral has a physical lower endpoint $s_0=Λ^{-2}$ that is not removed. Closed fermion loops are defined by the gauge-covariant heat-kernel determinant, and open fermion lines are obtained by functional differentiation of the same finite-proper-time open-line kernel. The Ward--Takahashi identity follows exactly from gauge covariance to all orders. The vacuum polarisation is finite and exactly transverse. The on-shell mass relation gives 0.482$$ MeV for an illustrative choice $Λ=13\$ TeV at one loop. The free finite-proper-time propagators are proved to satisfy Osterwalder--Schrader reflection positivity, with a positive Kallen--Lehmann spectral function and no additional ghost states. The on-shell residue $Z_2>0$ at one loop confirms unitarity of the fermion sector, and the perturbative spectral function of the dressed propagator is positive. A worldline bound $Q\le0$ gives fixed-order Euclidean UV finiteness. The one-loop vertex correction gives a finite anomalous magnetic moment, a calculable $O(m^2/Λ^2)$ prediction absent in standard QED.

### [138] [Why Hadamard states?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22767)
*Eleanor March*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了弯曲时空量子场论中Hadamard条件的哲学基础与理论正当性。作者批判了文献中对该条件的既有动机论证，并提出一种替代性辩护：Hadamard条件是定义量子场可观测算子乘积（operator product）的充分必要条件，从而澄清了其在理论中的地位、与等效原理的关系以及Hadamard态为何被视为类似真空（vacuum-like）的理由。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管Hadamard条件在弯曲时空量子场论（quantum field theory on curved spacetime）及局域协变量子场论（locally-covariant quantum field theory）中被广泛视为“物理上合理”态的必要条件，并在从Wick多项式重整化到霍金温度推导等关键应用中发挥核心作用，但其哲学与基础性根基仍然模糊不清，亟需系统澄清。

Method: 采用批判性分析（critical discussion）的方法，首先审视并反驳已有文献中对Hadamard条件的既有动机论证，随后转向论证一种替代性新辩护：证明Hadamard条件是定义一大类可观测量空间上良定义算子乘积的充分必要条件，并满足若干进一步条件——从而确立了一个既有结果的逆命题。

Result: 论证表明，Hadamard条件最好被理解为在足够大的量子场可观测量空间上存在良定义算子乘积（operator product）的充要条件，且该乘积满足一系列附加条件。这一结果相当于证明了此前在该语境下已被讨论的某个结论的逆命题。

Conclusion: 该分析澄清了Hadamard条件的角色与地位，特别是其与等效原理（equivalence principle）的关系、与Wick多项式及应力能量算符期望值等物理量良定义性的关联，以及Hadamard态在何种意义上被视为“类真空态”（vacuum-like）。

Abstract: In quantum field theory on curved spacetime, and in locally-covariant quantum field theory, the Hadamard condition is often presented as a necessary condition on 'physically reasonable' states of the quantum field, and plays a central role in many theoretical and foundational applications - ranging from proofs of the renormalizability of Wick polynomials to derivations of the Hawking temperature. Yet despite this, the philosophical and foundational underpinnings of the Hadamard condition remain murky. I critically discuss existing motivations for the Hadamard condition in the literature, before arguing in favour of an alternative justification for the Hadamard condition, according to which it is best understood as a necessary and sufficient condition for the existence of a well-defined operator product on a sufficiently large space of observables of the quantum field, satisfying a variety of further conditions (thus proving a converse to a result which was already discussed in this context). This clarifies the role and status of the Hadamard condition, including its relationship to the equivalence principle, to well-definedness of physical quantities such as Wick polynomials and the expectation value of the stress-energy operator, and the sense in which Hadamard states are 'vacuum-like'.

</details>


### [139] [Compatible Lie conformal bialgebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22941)
*Lamei Yuan,Jiansen Zhao*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文引入并研究了相容李共形双代数（compatible Lie conformal bialgebras），建立了其与相容共形Manin三元组（compatible conformal Manin triples）和匹配对（matched pairs）的等价关系，并在coboundary情形下刻画了决定该代数结构的张量r，提出了相容共形经典Yang–Baxter方程（compatible conformal CYBE）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将相容李双代数（compatible Lie bialgebras）的框架推广到共形（conformal）情形，为研究具有多个相容结构的无限维代数系统提供理论基础。

Method: 在C[∂]-模上定义相容的李共形括号（Lie conformal brackets）与共形余括号（conformal cobrackets），建立表示（representations）与匹配对理论；引入相容李共形余代数（compatible Lie conformal coalgebras），利用共形对偶（conformal dual）建立其对偶性；在coboundary情形下，通过对称部分的双括号不变性与三类共形Yang–Baxter条件来刻画张量r。

Result: 证明了对于有限秩自由C[∂]-模，相容李共形双代数、标准相容共形Manin三元组与匹配对三者等价。刻画了coboundary情形下张量r需满足的条件：对称部分对两个括号均不变，且满足三个共形Yang–Baxter条件，其中第三个为相容共形Yang–Baxter条件。对比表明，相容共形CYBE的解满足这三个条件，反之则不成立；给出了反例说明前两个条件不能推出第三个，以及三个条件同时成立但r不是相容共形CYBE解的情形。

Conclusion: 本文系统建立了相容李共形双代数的基本理论框架，揭示了其与Manin三元组、匹配对的等价关系，并为coboundary情形提供了精确的刻画条件，同时澄清了与相容共形CYBE之间的包含关系与非等价性。

Abstract: We introduce and study compatible Lie conformal bialgebras as conformal counterparts of compatible Lie bialgebras. Such a structure consists of two compatible Lie conformal brackets and two compatible conformal cobrackets on the same $\C[\partial]$-module, and every simultaneous linear combination of them is again a Lie conformal bialgebra. We develop representations and matched pairs for compatible Lie conformal algebras, introduce compatible Lie conformal coalgebras, and establish their duality through the conformal dual in the finite case. For $\C[\p]$-modules that are free of finite rank, we prove the equivalence among compatible Lie conformal bialgebras, standard compatible conformal Manin triples and matched pairs. In the coboundary case, we characterize the tensors $r$ that determine compatible Lie conformal bialgebras. The characterization requires the symmetric part of $r$ to be invariant with respect to both brackets and three conformal Yang--Baxter conditions to hold. The first two conditions correspond to the two brackets separately, whereas the third is the compatible conformal Yang--Baxter condition. For comparison, we introduce the compatible conformal classical Yang--Baxter equation (CYBE) and show that each of its solutions satisfies these three conditions, while the converse fails. One explicit example shows that the first two conditions do not imply the third. Another shows that all three conformal Yang-Baxter conditions may hold even though $r$ is not a solution of compatible conformal CYBE.

</details>


### [140] [Statistical Physics of Planar Carroll Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23039)
*Fei Huang,Loïc Marsot*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过引入平面上的卡罗尔代数（Carroll algebra）中心扩张并考虑系统角动量，定义了平面卡罗尔系统的统计物理，解决了一般维度下庞加莱统计物理卡罗尔极限不收敛的问题；利用苏里奥几何热力学（Souriau's geometric thermodynamics）计算了均匀旋转圆盘上粒子的配分函数，揭示了旋转对于平面卡罗尔系统热平衡的必要性，并推导了熵和压强等热力学量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究表明，一般维度下庞加莱统计物理（Poincaré statistical physics）的卡罗尔极限（Carroll limit）通常不收敛，因此需要为平面卡罗尔系统建立一套良好定义的统计物理框架。

Method: 利用平面卡罗尔代数的中心扩张（central extensions）和系统角动量（angular momentum）来确保统计物理的定义良好性；采用苏里奥几何热力学计算均匀旋转圆盘上粒子的配分函数（partition function），并基于对称性分析推导有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian）。

Result: 旋转是平面卡罗尔系统达到热平衡（thermal equilibrium）的必要条件，其中一个中心荷（central charge）决定了旋转方向；熵（entropy）与圆盘面积呈对数标度关系（scales logarithmically），压强（pressure）遵循二维理想气体定律（two-dimensional ideal gas law）。

Conclusion: 平面卡罗尔统计物理存在良好定义的形式，其热力学量可由对称性分析直接导出，旋转在系统中具有根本性作用。

Abstract: In this article, we define and study the statistical physics of planar Carrollian systems. While it has been shown recently that, for general dimensions, the Carroll limit of Poincaré statistical physics typically does not converge, we show that thanks to the central extensions of the Carroll algebra in the plane, and by considering systems with angular momentum, there exists a well defined notion of planar Carrollian statistical physics.
  Using Souriau's geometric thermodynamics, we compute the partition function for particles on a uniformly rotating disc, and show that rotation is inevitable for thermal equilibrium of planar Carroll systems, with one of the central charges determining the direction of rotation. We derive thermodynamic quantities in particular entropy, which scales logarithmically with the disc area, and pressure, which follows the two-dimensional ideal gas law. Though all results are obtained from symmetry considerations, we also derive the corresponding effective Hamiltonian.

</details>


### [141] [Jacobi exceptional orthogonal polynomials for extended Scarf I potentials with position-dependent mass](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23264)
*Christiane Quesne*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过点正则变换（point canonical transformation）方法，将具有位置依赖质量（position-dependent mass）的Scarf I势问题映射为常质量Scarf I势问题，进而构造出与$X_m$-Jacobi exceptional正交多项式（类型I、II或III）相关的精确可解有理扩展，并证明了该类系统在变形超对称框架（deformed supersymmetric framework）下具有变形形状不变性（deformed shape invariance property）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 位置依赖质量背景下的量子可解势问题在凝聚态物理、核物理等领域有重要应用，但精确求解较为困难。本文旨在利用点正则变换方法求解质量函数为$m(α;x) = (1 + α\sin x)^{-2}$时的Scarf I势问题，并探讨其代数结构性质。

Method: 采用点正则变换（point canonical transformation）将位置依赖质量背景下的薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）映射为常质量Scarf I势的薛定谔方程；再通过逆点正则变换构造出与$X_m$-Jacobi exceptional正交多项式相关的精确可解有理扩展势；在变形超对称框架（deformed supersymmetric framework）下分析形状不变性（shape invariance property）。

Result: 成功求解了质量函数$m(α;x) = (1 + α\sin x)^{-2}$、$0<α<1$时的Scarf I势问题；构造了与$X_m$-Jacobi exceptional正交多项式（类型I、II或III）相关的有理扩展势；证明了该系统在变形超对称框架下具有变形形状不变性，该性质对类型I和II的扩展势同样成立；并给出了一个简单实例加以验证。

Conclusion: 点正则变换方法可有效求解一类位置依赖质量背景下的Scarf I势问题，并生成异常正交多项式（exceptional orthogonal polynomials）相关的精确可解扩展。变形形状不变性是该类系统的内在代数结构，体现了超对称量子力学（supersymmetric quantum mechanics）框架的推广。

Abstract: We show that the Scarf I potential problem in a position-dependent mass background of the type $m(α;x) = (1 + α\sin x)^{-2}$, $0<α<1$, can be solved by using a point canonical transformation mapping the corresponding Schr\" odinger equation onto that of the Scarf I potential with constant mass. The inverse point canonical transformation then provides some exactly-solvable rational extensions of the Scarf I potential with positive-dependent mass associated with $X_m$-Jacobi exceptional orthogonal polynomials of type I, II, or III. The Scarf I potential problem with position-dependent mass is shown to exhibit a deformed shape invariance property in a deformed supersymmetric framework. Such a property is also valid for extended potentials of type I and II. The results are illustrated with a simple example.

</details>

*Jiawei He,Yuan Shan,Yongjian Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 马赛克几乎马蒂厄算子作为一种准周期模型，自然具有奇异条带-雅可比表示（singular strip-Jacobi representation），但其谱结构尚未被充分理解。本文旨在通过发展新的对偶框架与约化方法，揭示该模型在非临界参数下的谱拓扑性质。

Method: 首先建立对偶框架，并将态密度积分与纤维化旋转数之间的标准对应关系拓展至马赛克几乎马蒂厄算子；进而利用该对应实现向 SL(2,R) 余循环的有效约化；最后综合运用 Aubry 对偶、可约性理论以及 Moser–Pöschel 论证，推导谱集的结构性质。

Result: 对于所有非临界参数（noncritical parameters），马赛克几乎马蒂厄算子的谱集为康托尔集。

Conclusion: 马赛克几乎马蒂厄算子在非临界参数下谱集具有完全的不连通性（即康托尔集结构），这一结论推广了经典几乎马蒂厄算子的相关结果。

Abstract: We study the mosaic Almost Mathieu operator, a quasiperiodic model that naturally admits a singular strip-Jacobi representation. By establishing a duality framework and extending the correspondence between the integrated density of states and the fibered rotation number to this setting, we obtain an effective reduction to $SL(2,\mathbb{R})$ cocycles. As a consequence, combining Aubry duality, reducibility theory, and the Moser--Pöschel argument, we prove that the spectrum is a Cantor set for all noncritical parameters.

Method: 基于规范平移亥姆霍兹算子（gauge-shifted Helmholtz operator）的周期波导网络的散射特性，推导出网络精确透射系数；将晶格电抗（lattice reactance）表示为傅里叶展开，其系数与底层图结构参数（键连接、折射率、长度以及规范相位）建立解析映射关系。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一种闭合形式的解析逆向设计路线，区别于传统数值逆设计方法，可高效地将期望波形映射为实际物理结构，并在图像合成等场景中展现出扩展潜力。

Abstract: We introduce an analytically invertible framework for wavefront construction based on the scattering properties of periodic waveguide networks governed by a gauge-shifted Helmholtz operator. By determining the exact transmission coefficients of the network, we express the lattice reactance as a Fourier expansion whose coefficients are analytically mapped onto the underlying graph architecture, allowing the required bond connections, refractive indices, lengths, and gauge phases to be determined directly from a prescribed target transmission coefficient. In contrast to conventional inverse-design approaches, the present formulation provides a closed-form route from desired wave transmission profiles to physically realisable structures. The framework extends naturally from one-dimensional angular filtering to two-dimensional image synthesis, where arbitrary transmitted intensity patterns are reconstructed through exact spectral control of the network scattering response.

### [144] [Position-Space Renormalization and Half-Space Truncations in $φ^4_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23650)
*Majdouline Borji*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究有质量欧几里得 φ⁴₄ 理论中的半空间可观测量，证明重整化关联子（renormalized correlators）可与半空间截断相乘而无需额外重整化，并建立了紫外截断趋近于无穷时的收敛性及 Besov 空间中的正则性估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子场论中，半空间可观测量（boundary or half-space observables）的定义涉及与不连续函数的乘积，这通常会导致额外的发散，需要新的重整化（renormalization）步骤。本文试图证明，在欧几里得 φ⁴₄ 理论中，这种乘积在无需额外重整化的条件下即可良定义。

Method: 采用基于位置空间的重整化框架（position-space renormalization framework），利用 Wilson–Polchinski 流方程（Wilson–Polchinski flow equation），并引入适应关联子奇异性结构的幂次计数空间（power-counting spaces）层级，从而对重整化关联子建立一致的幂次计数界（uniform power-counting bounds）和 Besov–Hölder 正则性估计（Besov–Hölder regularity estimates）。

Result: 证明了半空间指示函数的光滑近似与重整化关联子的乘积收敛到良定义的分布极限（distributional limits），该收敛在紫外截断（ultraviolet cutoff）下是一致的。随着紫外截断趋于无穷，关联子收敛到明确的极限，且该收敛发生在已显式识别的 Besov 空间（Besov spaces）中。

Conclusion: 在有质量欧几里得 φ⁴₄ 理论中，半空间截断与重整化关联子相乘无需额外重整化步骤；该结果为半空间可观测量的严格构造提供了数学基础，并展示了基于流方程（flow equation）的重整化方法在处理非平凡奇异性结构时的有效性。

Abstract: In this paper, we study half-space observables in the massive Euclidean $φ^4_4$ theory. We prove that the renormalized correlators can be multiplied by half-space truncations without requiring any additional renormalization. More precisely, products with smooth approximations of the half-space indicator converge to well-defined distributional limits, uniformly in the ultraviolet cutoff. The proof relies on a position-space renormalization framework for the Wilson--Polchinski flow equation based on a hierarchy of power-counting spaces adapted to the singularity structure of the correlators. This yields uniform power-counting bounds and Besov--Hölder regularity estimates for the renormalized correlators. As a consequence, the correlators converge as the ultraviolet cutoff tends to infinity, and the convergence takes place in explicitly identified Besov spaces.

</details>

### [145] [The moving Fermi polaron](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21567)
*Johanna Hennebichler,Ruben Erlenstedt,Erich Dobler,Cosetta Baroni,Rudolf Grimm,Matteo Caldara,Georg Bruun,Pietro Massignan*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过结合拉曼加速方案与高精度射频谱学，实验研究了有限动量下运动费米极化子（Fermi polaron）的准粒子色散关系，发现其在低动量区域符合费米液体理论（Fermi liquid theory）的常有效质量图像，在高动量区域趋近弱相互作用裸粒子行为，而中间动量区域则展现出吸引与排斥极化子截然不同的非单调行为，并观测到运动诱导的极化子-分子转变（polaron-molecule transition）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 费米极化子是理解量子多体系统中准粒子概念的重要模型，但以往研究大多局限于零杂质动量情形，有限动量下的性质尚未被充分探索。因此，本文旨在系统研究运动费米极化子在不同动量下的准粒子色散关系。

Method: 实验上采用一种新型拉曼加速方案（Raman acceleration scheme）与高精度射频光谱学（radio-frequency spectroscopy）相结合的方法，在宽动量范围内测量费米极化子的能量移动和谱线宽度，并与微观理论进行定量比较。

Result: 低动量下，极化子能量与具有常有效质量的费米液体图像完全一致；高动量下，极化子接近弱相互作用裸粒子行为，能量移动小且展宽弱。中间动量区域展宽普遍更大，且吸引与排斥极化子行为迥异：排斥极化子呈现光滑连接与单调能量变化，而吸引极化子出现非单调行为——能量偏离常有效质量表达式，展宽突然增大。

Conclusion: 通过将观测与理论对比，表明吸引极化子行为突变的物理机制是：当动量增加时，吸引极化子进入分子-空穴连续谱（molecule-hole continuum），不再是基态，该现象被解释为运动诱导的极化子-分子转变。

Abstract: The Fermi polaron, formed by an impurity interacting with a surrounding Fermi sea, exemplifies the canonical quasiparticle concept as a cornerstone in our description of quantum many-body systems across a wide range of energy scales. Experiments on atomic quantum gases have provided profound insights into the universal nature of the Fermi polaron. While most previous studies have focused on the case of zero impurity momentum, finite-momentum properties have remained largely uncharted. Here, we investigate the moving Fermi polaron by combining a novel Raman acceleration scheme with high-precision radio-frequency spectroscopy, exploring the quasiparticle dispersion relation over a wide range of momenta. We compare our measurements of energy shifts and spectral linewidths with a microscopic theory and reach quantitative agreement for all momenta. For low momenta, we find the energy of the moving polaron to be fully consistent with the Fermi liquid picture of a dressed particle with a constant effective mass. At high momenta, the polaron approaches the behavior of a weakly interacting bare particle, featuring small energy shifts and weak broadening. For intermediate momenta, broadening is generally larger and, most strikingly, the behavior differs for attractive and repulsive polarons. While the repulsive polaron exhibits a smooth connection between both regimes along with a monotonic change of the energy shift, the attractive case shows a peculiar non-monotonic behavior. With increasing momentum, the attractive polaron enters a regime where its energy deviates from the constant effective mass expression and broadening suddenly increases. By comparing this observation with theory, we show that this abrupt behavior coincides with the attractive polaron entering a molecule-hole continuum, where it is no longer the ground state. We interpret this as a motion-induced polaron-molecule transition.

</details>


### [146] [Formation and dynamics of self-bound droplets in dipolar molecular condensate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22503)
*Xinyi Tang,Tianmiao Zhang,Zibin Zhao,Guilong Li,Zhaopin Chen,Bin Liu,Boris A. Malomed,Yongyao Li*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过扩展Gross-Pitaevskii方程结合Lee-Huang-Yang修正，系统研究了非轴对称偶极-偶极相互作用（DDI）主导下的自束缚量子液滴（QD），揭示了其存在区域、化学势等性质对非轴对称DDI强度的非单调依赖，以及碰撞结果的强方向依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有研究表明双微波场可调控极性分子超冷凝聚体中自束缚量子液滴（QD）的对称性和平衡相图，但这些微波场对QD形成及动力学的影响尚未被系统探索。

Method: 采用扩展的Gross-Pitaevskii方程（extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation），并引入Lee-Huang-Yang修正（Lee-Huang-Yang corrections），在非轴对称偶极-偶极相互作用（dipole-dipole interactions, DDIs）主导的框架下对自束缚量子液滴进行理论建模与分析。

Result: 自束缚QD的存在区域被确定，其化学势（chemical potential）、总能量、有效体积、峰值密度和几何各向异性表现出对非轴对称DDI强度的显著非单调依赖；增加凝聚体粒子数导致QD更紧束缚且更各向异性；降低s波散射长度（s-wave scattering length）引发从稳定自束缚态到坍缩（collapse）的转变；沿不同方向运动的QD碰撞展现出从准弹性回弹、合并到碎裂的强烈方向依赖性。

Conclusion: 非轴对称DDI强度是调控QD性质的关键参数，粒子数和散射长度的变化可诱导结构转变与动力学行为多样性，碰撞方向依赖性为实验操控提供了新的自由度。

Abstract: Recent advances in the work with ultracold condensates of polar molecules have enabled the realization of highly tunable self-bound quantum droplets (QDs), with the help of dual microwave fields dressig the dipole-dipole interactions (DDIs) It has been reported that symmetry properties and the equilibrium phase diagram of such QDs can be controlled by parameters of the two microwave fields. However, the effect of these fields on the formation and dynamics of the QD has not yet been systematically explored. Here we address self-bound QDs in a regime dominated by non-axisymmetric DDIs and governed by the extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation with the Lee-Huang-Yang corrections. Within this framework, we identify the existence region of the self-bound QDs and characterize their chemical potential, total energy, effective volume, peak density, and geometric anisotropy. The results reveal a pronounced nonmonotonous dependence on the non-axisymmetric DDI strength, whereas the increase of the number of particles in the condensate leads to tighter bound and more anisotropic QDs. Furthermore, reducing the s-wave scattering length drives a transition from stable self-bound states to the collapse. Collisions between QDs moving along different directions reveal a strong directional dependence, with outcomes ranging from quasi-elastic rebound and merger to fragmentation.

</details>


### [147] [Degeneracy-reshaped spin squeezing in high-spin Fermi-Hubbard systems weakly coupled to light](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23330)
*Hubert Dunikowski,Emilia Witkowska*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究了弱耦合于光的强相互作用高自旋费米-哈伯德系统（Fermi-Hubbard system）中的自旋压缩（spin squeezing）现象，发现内部自旋结构的简并性（degeneracy）会定性改变自旋压缩动力学，并基于布居数本征态（population eigenstates）建立了一个有效理论框架，定量再现了自旋压缩的演化过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解高自旋系统中简并性如何影响自旋压缩动力学，揭示传统最大自旋描述（maximal-spin description）失效的微观根源，并建立能够定量描述该过程的理论框架。

Method: 通过理论分析弱耦合于光的强相互作用高自旋费米-哈伯德系统，识别与内部自旋结构相关的简并性，并基于布居数本征态构建有效理论框架，定量模拟自旋压缩的演化。

Result: 自旋压缩动力学受内部自旋简并性的定性修正；传统最大自旋描述失效的微观起源被确认为这些简并性；基于布居数本征态的有效框架可定量再现自旋压缩演化。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了一种普适机制，即简并性能够重塑集体自旋动力学（collective spin dynamics）。

Abstract: We study spin squeezing in strongly interacting high-spin Fermi-Hubbard systems weakly coupled to light. We show that spin squeezing dynamics is qualitatively modified by the degeneracies associated with the internal spin structure. We identify these degeneracies as the microscopic origin of the breakdown of conventional maximal-spin description and develop an effective framework based on population eigenstates that quantitatively reproduces spin squeezing evolution. Our results uncover a generic mechanism by which degeneracy reshapes collective spin dynamics.

### [148] [Population-based eigenstates of the SU(d) spin-exchange model for high-spin fermions in optical lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23374)
*Hubert Dunikowski,Emilia Witkowska*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文为描述一维光晶格中自旋 s≥1 的超冷费米原子，构建了基于磁子能级布居数（magnetic sub-level populations）的 SU(d) 自旋交换模型本征态表示，并利用该框架通过二阶 Schrieffer–Wolff 变换推导出与光弱耦合的有效哈密顿量，揭示了集体自旋动力学中布居数重排的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高自旋（high-spin）费米子系统中 SU(d) 对称性带来大量简并，需要一种系统化的本征态表示方法来简化有效模型的推导，并理解集体自旋动力学（collective spin dynamics）中布居数重排的作用。

Method: 从强相互作用极限下的费米-哈伯德模型（Fermi-Hubbard model）出发，导出单个格点占据一个原子的 SU(d) 自旋交换模型；基于磁子能级布居数系统构建自旋交换（SE）本征态；利用该表示，通过二阶 Schrieffer–Wolff 变换（second-order Schrieffer–Wolff transformation）投影到布居数本征基上，推导与光弱耦合的有效哈密顿量。

Result: 成功构建了基于布居数的 SE 本征态表示，并推导出包含集体自旋动力学和布居数重排效应的有效哈密顿量。该有效模型与包含光耦合的精确 Fermi–Hubbard 动力学结果一致，验证了布居数本征态框架的有效性。

Conclusion: 所提出的布居数本征态框架是一种描述高自旋量子多体系统（quantum many-body systems）的一致且有效的基表示方法，为研究 SU(d) 对称性下的集体自旋行为提供了可控的理论工具。

Abstract: We investigate the $\mathrm{SU}(d)$ spin exchange model describing ultra-cold fermionic atoms with spin $s\ge 1$ in a one-dimensional optical lattice. The model emerges from the Fermi-Hubbard model in the strongly interacting regime with one atom in each lattice site. The central result of this work is the systematic construction of SE eigenstates in terms of magnetic sub-level populations. This representation provides a natural description of high-spin fermionic systems, where the underlying $\mathrm{SU}(d)$ symmetry gives rise to extensive degeneracies. We illustrate the usefulness of this framework for deriving effective Hamiltonians for a system weakly coupled to light through spin-orbit interactions, using a second-order Schrieffer--Wolff transformation projected onto the introduced population eigenbasis. These effective models provide a controlled description of the collective spin dynamics and capture the role of population redistribution among different collective spin length sectors induced by interactions. The agreement with the exact Fermi--Hubbard with light coupling dynamics confirms the consistency of the population eigenstates framework as a basis for describing high-spin quantum many-body systems.

### [149] [A dipolar Bose-Bose mixture of Dysprosium isotopes with controllable interspecies interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23528)
*M. Duerbeck,L. Reihs,J. P. Marulanda-Serna,B. Choudhari,J. Seifert,N. Werum,G. Meijer,G. Valtolina*

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种由162Dy和164Dy组成的量子简并玻色-玻色混合物的实验实现。两种同位素具有近乎相同的质量和极化率，因此混合物热化效率高，蒸发冷却轨迹接近于单同位素情形。通过利用一个宽的同位素间费什巴赫共振（Feshbach resonance），研究了两玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensates）之间的可混溶-不可混溶转变。混合物间相互作用的可调谐性，结合镝（Dy）的大磁偶极矩，使该平台非常适合探索超冷混合物中的偶极效应，包括多组分超固态（multi-component supersolidity）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 实验上制备了162Dy和164Dy两种同位素的量子简并混合物，利用其近乎相同的质量和极化率实现高效热化与蒸发冷却。通过一个宽的同位素间费什巴赫共振（interspecies Feshbach resonance）来连续调节混合物间的相互作用强度。

Result: 混合物热化效率高，蒸发冷却轨迹与单同位素情形高度一致。利用费什巴赫共振实现了对混合物可混溶-不可混溶转变（miscible-immiscible transition）的调控。

Conclusion: 该同位素混合物平台为研究超冷混合物中的偶极效应提供了高度可控的实验系统，特别适用于探索多组分超固态（multi-component supersolidity）等新奇量子现象。

Abstract: We report on the realization of a quantum-degenerate Bose-Bose mixture of 162Dy and 164Dy. Owing to the near-identical mass and polarizability of the two isotopes, the mixture thermalizes efficiently, with evaporation trajectories closely following those of the single-isotope case. Using a broad interspecies Feshbach resonance, we explore a miscible-immiscible transition between the two Bose-Einstein condensates. The tunability of the interspecies interaction, combined with the large magnetic dipole moment of Dy, makes this platform well suited for exploring dipolar effects in ultracold mixtures, including multi-component supersolidity.

Conclusion: 该工作为矢量玻色子散射的semileptonic末态测量提供了必要的NLO量子色动力学（QCD）与电弱（electroweak）高阶修正理论预言，能够支撑未来LHC及后续实验的精度需求。

Abstract: Vector-boson scattering with semileptonic final states has recently been measured at the LHC, and future experiments are expected to further increase the precision of its measurement, calling for adequate theoretical predictions. ### [152] [Counting axions with IAXO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20826)
*Benjamín Grinstein,Carlos Miró,Pablo Quílez Lasanta*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究多轴子（axion）种类在太阳望远镜实验中的可区分性问题。通过重新分析CAST实验的现有约束并推导IAXO及IAXO+的预测，作者识别了两轴子参数空间中可能产生信号的区域。进一步分析了准简并（quasi-degenerate）与层级（hierarchical）质量区间内轴子味振荡（axion flavor oscillations）的谱特征，指出IAXO在给定探测器能量分辨率下能够区分双轴子信号与单轴子假设。研究表明，这些结论可推广至更一般的N-轴子系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型的多种扩展普遍预言多轴子的存在。如果多个轴子都与光子耦合，它们在太阳望远镜实验中的联合信号可能模拟成一个参数不同的单轴子信号，这提出了一个基础性问题：下一代望远镜（如IAXO）探测到信号时，能否判断其来源于一个还是多个轴子？

Method: 首先重新解读CAST实验的现有约束，并在两轴子参数空间中推导IAXO及IAXO+的投影，识别可观测信号的参数区域。然后分析准简并与层级质量区间中轴子味振荡的谱特征，结合探测器预期的能量分辨率判别双轴子信号与单轴子假设。最后将分析框架推广至N-轴子系统。

Result: 识别了两轴子参数空间中IAXO可观测到信号的区域；展示了在给定探测器能量分辨率条件下，IAXO能够区分双轴子信号与单轴子假设的谱特征条件；证明了这些区分能力可推广至更广泛的N-轴子系统。

Conclusion: 下一代太阳望远镜实验IAXO有望在特定参数区域内区分多轴子信号与单轴子信号，且这一结论对多种轴子种类具有普适性。

Abstract: The existence of multiple axion species is a generic prediction of a number of extensions of the Standard Model. If more than one axion couples to photons, their combined signal in helioscope experiments may mimic that of a single axion with different parameters. This raises a fundamental question: if a next-generation helioscope such as IAXO detected a signal, would we be able to disentangle whether it originated from one or multiple axions? To answer this question, we first recast current CAST bounds and derive IAXO/IAXO+ projections in the two-axion parameter space, identifying the regions where a signal could be observed. Then, we analyze the spectral signatures of axion flavor oscillations in both the quasi-degenerate and hierarchical mass regimes, and point out where IAXO can discriminate a two-axion signal from the single-axion hypothesis given the expected energy resolutions of the detector. Finally, we show that these results extend to a broad class of $N$-axion systems.
