### [153] [When CPT Violation Hides in Plain Sight: How CP Measurements Are Compromised and How to Fix Them](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20830)
*Miaochen Jin,Gabriela Barenboim,Carlos A. Argüelles,Pablo Fernández-Menéndez,Ivan Martinez-Soler*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了CPT对称性破缺对长基线中微子振荡实验中轻子CP破坏相δ_CP测量的影响。研究表明，CPT破缺的参数化形式——中微子与反中微子质量平方差的不对称性δΔm²_31——会引入与δ_CP功能简并的有效相位φ_eff(E)，这可以缓解T2K与NOνA之间的张力，但对DUNE实验可能造成严重偏差。利用IceCube-DeepCore和KM3NeT/ORCA-6的现有数据，研究给出了目前国际上最强的CPT破缺约束，并展望了未来十年内将灵敏度提升至10⁻⁴ eV²水平的前景，从而确保DUNE对δ_CP的测量无歧义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长基线中微子振荡实验（如T2K、NOνA和DUNE）提取轻子CP破坏相δ_CP依赖于CPT守恒假设。然而，T2K与NOνA在CPT守恒假设下最佳拟合的δ_CP值之间存在张力，这暗示CPT可能破缺。因此，需要系统研究CPT破缺对δ_CP测量的影响，并寻找解除简并的独立观测手段。

Method: 将CPT破缺参数化为中微子与反中微子质量平方差的不对称性δΔm²_31，推导其在出现不对称性〈ΔP〉中诱导的有效能量相关相位φ_eff(E)，并展示其与δ_CP的功能简并性。利用IceCube-DeepCore（7.74年）和KM3NeT/ORCA-6（433千吨·年）的大气中微子数据，对δΔm²_31进行约束。

Result: 在CPT破缺真实场景下，T2K与NOνA之间关于δ_CP的张力可显著缓解。对于DUNE实验，若|δΔm²_31| ≳ 0.3×10⁻³ eV²，CPT守恒拟合可能完全错过真实的CP相。现有数据给出CPT破缺的领先约束：|δΔm²_31| ≤ 0.57×10⁻³ eV²（90%置信水平）。未来借助IceCube Upgrade和完整ORCA探测器，可在十年内达到10⁻⁴ eV²的1σ约束。

Conclusion: CPT破缺与δ_CP之间存在根本性的功能简并，这一简并不能仅靠长基线实验自身解除。大气中微子望远镜（IceCube-DeepCore和KM3NeT/ORCA）是解决该简并的自然工具，其提供的独立CPT约束可确保DUNE对δ_CP的测量无歧义。

Abstract: The extraction of the leptonic charge-parity (CP)-violating phase $δ_{\rm CP}$ from long-baseline neutrino oscillation experiments rests on the assumption of charge-parity-time (CPT) conservation. We show that CPT violation, parametrized as an asymmetry $δΔm^2_{31} \equiv Δ\bar{m}^2_{31} - Δm^2_{31}$ between neutrino and antineutrino mass splittings, induces an effective, energy-dependent phase shift $φ_{\rm eff}(E)$ that is functionally degenerate with $δ_{\rm CP}$ in the appearance asymmetry $\langleΔP\rangle$. This has a profound implication for long-baseline experiments, where the tension between T2K and NO$ν$A CPT-conserving best-fit $δ_{\rm CP}$ values can be significantly alleviated by a CPT-violating truth; and a CPT-conserving fit can miss the true CP phase entirely for $|δΔm^2_{31}|\gtrsim 0.3\times10^{-3}~\text{eV}^2$ for DUNE. We then demonstrate that atmospheric neutrino telescopes provide the natural tool to resolve this degeneracy: using existing data from IceCube-DeepCore (7.74 yr) and KM3NeT/ORCA-6 (433 kt-yr), we derive a world-leading constraint on CPT-violation at $| δΔm^2_{31}|\leq 0.57\times10^{-3}~\text{eV}^2$ at 90% CL. With the IceCube Upgrade and full ORCA detector, we can reach a $1σ$ constraint at $10^{-4}~\text{eV}^2$ within a decade, providing the independent CPT constraint needed to ensure that DUNE's $δ_{\rm CP}$ measurement is unambiguous.

</details>


### [154] [Event-Level QCD Inference Framework for Quark-Gluon Imaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20923)
*Patrick Barry,Pi-Yueh Chuang,Ian Cloët,Emil Constantinescu,Arkaprabha Ganguli,Chao Peng*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 提出一种用于夸克-胶子成像的事件级（event-level）分析框架，通过消除探测器效应反解（unfolding）和分箱（binning）两个关键信息损失源，在闭包检验（closure test）中比传统直方图方法表现更好，尤其在小样本和高维微分截面推断场景中优势显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统直方图方法需要先对事件进行分箱（binning）和探测器效应反解（unfolding），这两个步骤会导致信息损失。为此，论文引入并演示了一种事件级（event-level）分析框架，用于夸克-胶子成像（quark-gluon imaging），以消除上述信息损失源。

Method: 基于事件级分析框架（event-level analysis framework），直接从事件数据推断部分子分布函数（parton distribution functions, PDFs），无需分箱和反解。研究使用合成深度非弹性散射（deep inelastic scattering, DIS）数据，并在完美探测器（perfect detector）假设下，将该框架与传统直方图方法进行闭包检验（closure test）对比。

Result: 事件级框架在闭包检验中表现优于传统直方图方法，尤其在小样本场景下优势明显。采用均方误差（mean-squared error, MSE）距离度量时，在中等事件数下事件级框架比传统方法性能提升约35%。

Conclusion: 事件级分析框架在夸克-胶子成像中具有重要优势，其效益应在三维夸克-胶子成像（3D quark-gluon imaging）的推断中进一步增加，因为这类微分截面（differential cross sections）维度更高，且测量事件数显著减少。

Abstract: We introduce and demonstrate an event-level analysis framework for quark-gluon imaging. For a first application we use it for the inference of parton distribution functions from synthetic deep inelastic scattering data. This framework removes the need for unfolding of detector effects and the binning of events, and therefore eliminates two key sources of information loss. We contrast this event-level framework with the traditional histogram approach by performing a closure test for parton distribution functions from event data obtained from a known ground truth. In this study we assume a perfect detector, which makes unfolding straightforward. The elimination of binning in the event-level framework is demonstrated to have important benefits over the traditional histogram approach, and performs better in the closure test, particularly for a smaller number of events. For example, defining a mean-squared error distance metric, we find that the event-level framework performs around $35\%$ better than the traditional approach for a moderate number of events. The benefits of an event-level framework should increase for inference associated with 3D quark-gluon imaging, because these differential cross sections are of higher dimension and the comparative number of measured events is significantly reduced.

</details>


### [155] [Neutrino Dipole Moments and Radiative Signatures from Partial Compositeness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20987)
*Benoît Assi,Pedro A. N. Machado*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种复合中微子（composite neutrino）模型，其中重中微子来自近共形强耦合（near-conformal strongly coupled）束缚态，通过逆跷跷板机制（inverse seesaw mechanism）与标准模型中微子混合，并利用共形动力学（conformal dynamics）产生增强的电磁跃迁偶极算符，导致辐射信号显著强于标准模型预言；通过对MiniBooNE和MINERvA实验的详细模拟，给出了单光子和多光子末态的可观测量预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超越标准模型的中微子质量起源，特别是克服传统狄拉克（Dirac）或马约拉纳（Majorana）模型中辐射衰变分支比过小的困难，寻找实验可探测的新物理信号。

Method: 构建复合中微子模型：将重中微子视为近共形强耦合扇区的束缚态，通过逆跷跷板机制实现与标准模型中微子的混合；引入共形扇区的反常标度维度（anomalous scaling dimensions）自然压低轻中微子质量至亚电子伏特（sub-eV）量级；匹配共形动力学到低能有效理论，得到增强的电磁跃迁偶极算符；对MiniBooNE和MINERvA实验的生产-衰变链 $νX \to \mathcal{U} X \to νγX$ 进行基于事件的详细模拟，计算截面和运动学分布。

Result: 模型的电磁跃迁偶极耦合强度 $d_{μN} \sim 10^{-6}$-$10^{-8}\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$，参数化上远大于最小狄拉克或马约拉纳模型的圈图预言；对于可及的基准参数区间，辐射信号以单光子为主；当复合尺度较轻或束流能量较高时，复合结构的碎裂（fragmentation）可产生多光子末态，成为探测复合动力学（composite dynamics）的新探针。

Conclusion: 该复合中微子模型提供了一种产生实验可观测的辐射中微子信号的理论机制，单光子（single-photon）事件是当前实验的主要信号特征，而多光子（multi-photon）末态则为未来更高能量或更高精度实验提供了区分复合模型与传统模型的独特可观测信号。

Abstract: We investigate composite neutrino models where heavy neutrinos emerge as bound states from a near-conformal strongly coupled sector. Standard Model neutrinos mix with these composite singlets via an inverse seesaw mechanism, where the anomalous scaling dimensions of the composite-sector operators naturally suppress light neutrino masses to sub-eV scales. Matching the conformal dynamics onto low-energy theory yields enhanced electromagnetic transition dipole operators with couplings $d_{μN} \sim 10^{-6}$-$10^{-8}\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$, parametrically larger than the loop-level predictions of minimal Dirac or Majorana models. We carry out a dedicated event-level simulation of the production-and-decay chain $νX \to \mathcal{U} X \to νγX$ and compute the resulting event rates at MiniBooNE and MINERvA within the model, accounting for the composite production cross section and decay kinematics in detail. We further present predictions for the photon energy, angular, and multiplicity distributions. For the benchmark scenarios accessible at these experiments the radiative signal is predominantly single-photon; the composite structure additionally permits fragmentation of the up-scattered state into multiple heavy neutrinos, each decaying as $N\toνγ$, with multi-photon final states emerging for lighter compositeness scales or higher beam energies as a qualitatively new probe of the composite dynamics.

### [156] [Analytic results for heavy-quark contributions to charged-current DIS at NNLO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21702)
*Fabrizio Caola,Giulio Gambuti,Martin Link*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文给出了带电电流深度非弹性散射（charged-current deep-inelastic scattering）中重夸克产生的次次领头阶（next-to-next-to-leading-order, NNLO）QCD修正的解析结果，保留了粲夸克质量的完整依赖。计算了结构函数 $F_2$, $F_L$, $F_3$ 在夸克和胶子通道中的完整部分子系数函数，涵盖了最多三个重夸克末态贡献；通过反向幺正性（reverse-unitarity）框架结合积分-by-部分（integration-by-parts）与规范微分方程（canonical differential-equations）技术，将最多两个末态重夸克的贡献表达为显式实数的Goncharov多重对数（Goncharov polylogarithms），而三夸克贡献则涉及椭圆结构，采用Chen迭代积分（Chen iterated integrals）与快速收敛展开实现高效数值评估，并在多个极限下验证了结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用反向幺正性（reverse-unitarity）框架，结合积分-by-部分（integration-by-parts, IBP）简化多圈积分，并使用规范微分方程（canonical differential-equations）技术求解。对最多两个末态重夸克的贡献，结果表达为Goncharov多重对数（Goncharov polylogarithms）；对三个重夸克末态贡献，采用Chen迭代积分（Chen iterated integrals）与快速收敛级数展开进行处理。

Result: 完成了结构函数 $F_2$, $F_L$, $F_3$ 在夸克和胶子通道的完整部分子系数函数的NNLO计算（含粲夸克质量精确依赖）。所得Goncharov多重对数形式允许鲁棒且高效的数值评估；三夸克贡献的椭圆结构则通过Chen迭代积分与快速收敛展开（适用于微扰区 $Q\gtrsim 5~{\rm GeV}$）实现灵活快速的数值计算。

Conclusion: 通过对比已知的低阶精确结果、无质量NNLO系数函数以及渐近极限下的大 $Q$ 领头幂次展开，对所得结果进行了充分验证。该工作为带电电流深度非弹性散射中的重夸克产生提供了首个完整的NNLO质量依赖理论预言。

Abstract: We present analytic results for the next-to-next-to-leading-order QCD corrections to heavy-quark production in charged-current deep-inelastic scattering, retaining the exact dependence on the charm quark mass. We compute the complete partonic coefficient functions for the structure functions $F_2$, $F_L$, and $F_3$ in the quark and gluon channels, including contributions with up to three heavy quarks in the final state. Working within the reverse-unitarity framework, we use integration-by-parts and canonical differential-equations techniques to express all contributions with at most two final-state heavy quarks in terms of manifestly real Goncharov polylogarithms which allow for a robust and efficient numerical evaluation. The three-heavy-quark contribution involves elliptic structures for which we give a general representation in terms of Chen iterated integrals, as well as expressions in terms of rapidly convergent expansions that are valid in the perturbative $Q\gtrsim 5~{\rm GeV}$ region and also allow for a flexible and fast numerical evaluation. We validate our results against known exact results at lower orders, massless NNLO coefficient functions, and existing leading-power expansions in the asymptotic limit where the virtuality $Q$ is much larger than the charm mass.

### [157] [The feasibility of single $Λ$ production via ${\ell}^{-}$ $+$ $p$ ${\to}$ $Λ$ $+$ $ν_{\ell}$ at $e^{+}e^{-}$ colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21995)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用e⁺e⁻碰撞中产生的共振态（J/ψ, ψ(2S), Υ(1S), Υ(2S), Z⁰）衰变而来的入射轻子，与探测器材料中的静止质子发生散射，计算过程ℓ⁻ + p → ν_ℓ + Λ的微分截面和总截面。重子跃迁形状因子（baryonic transition form factors）采用z-展开方案（z-expansion scheme）进行参数化，并在量子色动力学求和规则（QCD sum rule）和格点QCD（lattice QCD）两种理论框架下分别进行计算。

Result: 截面随质心能量（center-of-mass energy）增加而增大，且对形状因子的选择高度敏感，导致显著的理论不确定性（theoretical uncertainties）。不同理论框架（QCD sum rule与lattice QCD）给出的结果存在差异。

Conclusion: 在e⁺e⁻对撞机中观测LNDIS过程面临显著的实验挑战，亟需改进重子形状因子的精确测定。该研究为未来实验搜索提供了有价值的参考，并指出若观测到异常的Λ超子产生信号，可能预示着新物理（new physics）的存在。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive investigation of single $Λ$ hyperon production via the lepton-nucleon deep inelastic scattering (LNDIS) process, ${\ell}^{-}$ $+$ $p$ ${\to}$ $ν_{\ell}$ $+$ $Λ$, in the experimental environment of electron-positron colliders. Our approach utilizes incident leptons originating from the decays of resonances (${J/ψ}$, $ψ(2S)$, $Υ(1S)$, $Υ(2S)$, and $Z^{0}$) produced in $e^{+}e^{-}$ collisions, which then scatter off stationary protons in the surrounding detector materials. The differential and total cross sections are calculated using baryonic transition form factors parameterized with the $z$-expansion scheme within both the quantum chromodynamics (QCD) sum rule and lattice QCD frameworks. Our results indicate that the cross section increases with center-of-mass energy and is highly sensitive to the choice of form factors, resulting in significant theoretical uncertainties. This study highlights the experimental challenges in observing the LNDIS process at $e^{+}e^{-}$ colliders and underscores the need for improved determination of baryonic form factors. It serves as a valuable reference for future experimental searches and suggests that an anomalous observation of single $Λ$ hyperon production at $e^{+}e^{-}$ colliders could indicate new physics.

### [160] [Angular Analysis of $B \to D^{*}\ell \barν_{\ell}$ from Lattice and Experiment: $|V_{cb}|$ and New Physics Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23410)
*Marzia Bordone,Ollie Heald,Andreas Jüttner*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过联合分析Belle合作的B→D*ℓν̄ℓ角系数实验测量与HPQCD、JLQCD、FNAL/MILC合作组的格点形状因子数据，在标准模型（Standard Model, SM）内外对CKM矩阵元|Vcb|进行确定，并对标量和张量流新物理（new physics, NP）的Wilson系数施加约束。联合贝叶斯拟合得到|Vcb|=0.03997(71)，且标量轻子夸克与矢量轻子夸克/无色标量玻色子介导的新物理分别在1.0 TeV和2.5 TeV有效标度上被排除（68%置信水平）。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Boyd-Grinstein-Lebed（BGL）参数化方案拟合形状因子，以幺正性约束作为贝叶斯先验（Bayesian priors）。对电子和缪子通道分别分析，并与无质量近似进行比较。在标量、矢量和张量流完整表达式下，通过联合贝叶斯拟合（joint Bayesian fit）同时处理实验与格点数据，并纳入SM有效场论（SMEFT）中的Wilson系数重整化群演化（renormalization group evolution）。

Abstract: We present a combined angular analysis within and beyond the Standard Model (SM) of experimental measurements for the $B \to D^{*}\ell \barν_{\ell}$ angular coefficients provided by the Belle collaboration, together with lattice-calculated hadronic form-factor data from the HPQCD, JLQCD, and FNAL/MILC collaborations. We focus on determining the CKM matrix element $|V_{cb}|$ and constraining a set of Wilson coefficients associated with new physics (NP) mediated by scalar and tensor currents. SM predictions for the angular coefficients are obtained using form-factor parameterisations based on the Boyd-Grinstein-Lebed (BGL) ansatz, with unitarity constraints imposed as Bayesian priors. Experimental and theoretical data are analysed jointly by considering the cases $\ell = e, μ$ separately and comparing with the massless approximation. For the latter, we determine $|V_{cb}| = 0.03997(71)$, with no resolution of the exclusive-inclusive puzzle. Using the full expressions for the angular coefficients in the presence of scalar, vector, and tensor currents, the corresponding Wilson coefficients are constrained through a joint Bayesian fit to lattice and experimental data. By including the renormalisation group evolution of the Wilson coefficients in the SM effective field theory (SMEFT), these constraints translate into bounds on the effective scale of potential heavy NP at the TeV scale. We find, at the $68\%$ confidence level, that NP mediated by a scalar leptoquark and a vector leptoquark/colourless scalar boson are excluded at the effective scales 1.0 and 2.5 TeV, respectively.

### [161] [Irrelevance of Anomalous Breaking of Axial U(1) Symmetry and the U(1) Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23578)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为η和η'介子因轴向U(1)反常（axial U(1) anomaly）而非SU(3)_L×SU(3)_R手征对称性自发破缺的Nambu-Goldstone（NG）玻色子；但近期研究表明该反常并非物理实在，因此需要重新审视η和η'介子的本质。

Method: 首先回顾轴向U(1)反常非物理性的论证，然后提出一个新的机制，在该机制中η和η'介子作为NG玻色子出现，同时与轴向U(1)问题（axial U(1) problem）保持一致。

Result: 提出了一种新机制，使得η和η'介子可以成为手征对称性自发破缺的NG玻色子，同时不违反轴向U(1)问题的约束条件。

Conclusion: η和η'介子可能并非如传统认为的那样仅仅源于轴向U(1)反常贡献，而是可以自然地作为手征对称性破缺的NG玻色子被理解。

Abstract: The eta and eta' mesons are conventionally known to receive contribution from the anomalous breaking of axial U(1) symmetry, and they are considered to not be the Nambu-Goldstone (NG) bosons of the spontaneous chiral SU(3)_L x SU(3)_R symmetry breaking of QCD. However, it has recently been shown that this axial U(1) anomaly is not actually physical. In this contribution, we first review this statement and then propose a mechanism in which eta and eta' mesons are indeed NG bosons while being consistent with the axial U(1) problem.

</details>

*Nodoka Yamanaka*

TL;DR: 该论文综述了基本粒子物理中的味对角CP破坏如何贡献于原子、原子核和核子的电偶极矩（EDMs）、T破坏中子光学以及β衰变的角度关联，回顾了CP破坏在超越标准模型新物理搜寻中的基础知识与重要性、相关强子层面CP破坏量化研究的最新进展，以及当前在不引入额外相互作用与场的情况下解决强CP问题的尝试。

Method: 采用综述（review）方法，系统梳理了味对角CP破坏（flavor diagonal CP violation）在电偶极矩（electric dipole moments, EDMs）、T破坏中子光学（T-violating neutron optics）及β衰变（beta decay）角度关联中的贡献机制，并讨论了当前在不引入额外相互作用与场（additional interactions and fields）的条件下解决强CP问题的理论方案。

Result: 总结了强子层面CP破坏量化研究的最新进展，并指出现有理论尝试正在探索无需新粒子或新场即可解决强CP问题的路径。

Conclusion: CP破坏研究对于检验标准模型和发现新物理具有重要意义；强子层面CP破坏的精确量化是连接基本粒子物理与原子核/原子观测量的关键；无需额外自由度解决强CP问题仍是当前活跃的理论探索方向。

Abstract: The flavor diagonal CP violation of elementary particle physics contributes to the atomic, nuclear, and nucleon electric dipole moments (EDMs), T-violating neutron optics, and to the angular correlations of beta decay. In this contribution, we review the basics and the importance of CP violation in the search for new physics beyond the standard model, the recent progress in the quantification of the hadron level CP violation contributing to the aforementioned observables, and finally the current attempt to solve the strong CP problem without additional interactions and fields.

### [163] [Gluon GTMD at strong coupling: fixed-spin saddle factorization and Reggeization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20981)
*Kiminad A. Mamo,Ismail Zahed*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用规范/弦对偶（gauge/string duality）在强耦合下构造了非极化胶子广义横向动量依赖部分子分布（GTMD）的共形矩，揭示了其从局域边界极限到有限分离区间的完整结构，并推导了各种极限下的因子化形式和端点半奇性行为，为强子断层扫描和Regge化研究提供了统一的全息框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义横向动量依赖部分子分布（GTMDs）是QCD中最完整的两部分子关联函数，能够编码强子的联合空间和动量结构，但目前对其在全息对偶框架下的系统性构造尚不充分，本文旨在利用规范/弦对偶填补这一空白。

Method: 采用规范/弦对偶（gauge/string duality）方法，构造非极化胶子GTMDs在强耦合下的共形矩（conformal moments），通过区分局域边界极限（$b_T=0$）和有限分离区间（$b_T>0$），并利用极小世界面（minimal worldsheet）描述半经典振幅。

Result: 在有限分离区间，GTMD矩因子化为一个通用 staple 世界面软因子和一个携带靶依赖的自旋-$j$ Witten振幅；重整化极小面积的尖点生成了快度对数Collins-Soper结构；在$b_T\to0^+$，通过通用交叠核匹配到局域共形矩；大$b_T$下，经尖点/周长减除后因子化为靶投影和红外传递核；不同全息背景（软墙、硬墙、排斥墙）分别产生代数、指数和高斯衰减；解析延拓$j$给出低-$x$Regge区，由全息Pomeron谱曲线主导。

Conclusion: 该框架统一描述了GTMD矩的强子断层扫描（hadron tomography）、横向结构、快度演化和Regge化行为，为电子-离子对撞机（Electron-Ion Collider）相关可观测量提供了全息研究的统一起点。

Abstract: Generalized transverse-momentum-dependent parton distributions (GTMDs) are the most complete two-parton correlation functions in QCD, encoding the joint spatial and momentum structure of hadrons. Through appropriate projections and limits they yield generalized parton distributions (GPDs), transverse-momentum-dependent distributions (TMDs), parton distribution functions (PDFs), and phase-space (Wigner) distributions. We construct conformal moments of unpolarized gluon GTMDs at strong coupling using gauge/string duality. For fixed even conformal spin $j$, we distinguish the local boundary limit at $b_T=0$ from the finite-separation regime $b_T>0$, where the planar semiclassical amplitude is governed by a minimal worldsheet. There the GTMD moment factorizes into a universal staple-worldsheet soft factor and a stripped spin-$j$ Witten amplitude carrying target dependence. The cusp of the renormalized minimal area generates the rapidity-logarithmic Collins-Soper structure. We derive universal ultraviolet and infrared endpoint reductions. As $b_T\to0^+$, the finite-separation sector matches onto the local conformal moment through a universal overlap kernel. At large $b_T$, after cusp/perimeter subtraction, it factorizes into target projections and infrared transfer kernels. The ultraviolet endpoint is universal within the leading saddle, whereas the infrared tail depends on the holographic completion: soft-wall, gap-matched hard-wall, and repulsive-wall backgrounds generate algebraic, exponential, and Gaussian falloffs, respectively. Analytic continuation in $j$ yields the low-$x$ Regge regime governed by the holographic Pomeron spectral curve. The framework describes hadron tomography, transverse structure, rapidity evolution, and Reggeization for GTMD moments and provides a unified starting point for holographic studies of observables relevant to the Electron-Ion Collider.

</details>


### [164] [Theoretical consistency and phenomenology of supercooled cosmological phase transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21380)
*Maciej Kierkla*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本论文研究了早期宇宙中的过冷相变，利用高温量纲约化（dimensional reduction）方法计算了热气泡成核率的次领头阶（NLO）修正，并以SU(2)cSM模型为案例，系统分析了相变动力学、近似方案的局限性以及可观测的引力波信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解早期宇宙中的过冷相变（supercooled phase transition）对于探索超出标准模型的新物理以及解释宇宙的演化至关重要，但精确描述热气泡成核（thermal bubble nucleation）过程在理论上具有挑战性，需要更系统的理论框架和更高精度的计算。

Method: 采用高温量纲约化（high-temperature dimensional reduction, DR）方法，系统计算了热气泡成核率的次领头阶（NLO）修正；通过显式评估涨落行列式（fluctuation determinants），并在SU(2)cSM——共形标准模型（conformal Standard Model）的一个扩展——中首次将DR应用于经典标度不变模型（classically scale-invariant model），推导了相应的三维有效场论（three-dimensional EFT）。

Result: 在SU(2)cSM模型中，过冷相变在整个参数空间内产生足以被激光干涉空间天线（LISA）探测到的强烈引力波信号；同时发现高阶修正（higher-order corrections）对相变动力学和引力波预言均有显著影响。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了热气泡成核的高精度理论描述，验证了SU(2)cSM模型的可实验检验性，并指出高阶修正对于准确预测相变动力学和引力波信号不可或缺。

Abstract: This dissertation investigates a supercooled phase transition (PT) in the early Universe. Using high-temperature dimensional reduction (DR), we compute the NLO thermal bubble nucleation rate. By explicitly evaluating fluctuation determinants, we provide a state-of-the-art description of thermal bubble nucleation. As a case study, we consider the SU(2)cSM, an extension of the conformal Standard Model with an additional SU(2)$_X$ gauge sector and scalar field that acquires a vev through radiative symmetry breaking. This symmetry breaking proceeds via a supercooled first-order phase transition. The first part of the thesis introduces the theoretical framework, including effective actions, RG improvements, finite-temperature quantum field theory, effective field theory techniques, and thermal bubble nucleation. The second part applies these methods to the SU(2)cSM. We establish a consistent power-counting scheme, construct the leading-order effective potential, analyse symmetry breaking and parameter space, derive an RG-improved potential, and incorporate thermal corrections. We then apply high-temperature DR to a classically scale-invariant model for the first time, derive the corresponding three-dimensional EFT, and compute the NLO nucleation rate. A detailed numerical evaluation of fluctuation determinants enables a comparison of different approximation schemes and their limitations. Finally, we present the phenomenological implications. We determine phase transition parameters, perform parameter scans, and predict the resulting gravitational wave signals. We find that the supercooled phase transition in the SU(2)cSM produces a strong signal detectable by LISA throughout the parameter space considered, making the model experimentally testable. We also demonstrate that higher-order corrections can significantly affect both phase transition dynamics and gravitational wave predictions.

### [165] [Globally Charged Vacuum Decay](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21653)
*Giulio Barni,Jose R. Espinosa*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了携带全局守恒荷的标量场在零温下的真空衰变（vacuum decay）问题。当存在全局 $U(1)$ 对称性时，传统的 $O(4)$ 对称Coleman反弹（bounce）不再适用；作者通过两场实欧几里得描述重新表述问题，求解了描述均匀带电介质衰变的二维偏微分方程，发现有限荷破坏了 $O(4)$ 对称性、降低了势垒并提高了衰变率，且气泡膨胀速度在真空中也会降至亚光速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的零温真空衰变理论基于 $O(4)$ 对称的Coleman反弹描述，但当驱动衰变的标量场携带守恒全局荷（global charge）时，该图像定性失效：路径积分需投影到确定荷扇区（charge sector），欧几里得场需满足扭曲边界条件（twisted boundary conditions），且鞍点（saddle）变为复数。本文旨在建立一套适用于该情形的实鞍点形式体系，并定量分析有限电荷对衰变速率及气泡动力学的修正。

Method: 针对最简单的 $U(1)$ 全局对称性情形，作者首先将问题重新表述为一个双场实欧几里得描述（two-field real Euclidean description），从而获得实鞍点（real saddle）。随后将该问题转化为一个二维偏微分方程（two-dimensional partial differential equation），用以描述均匀带电介质通过气泡成核（bubble nucleation）衰变到更深真空的过程。

Result: 有限荷条件下，反弹解不再保持 $O(4)$ 对称性；势垒被降低，真空衰变率随之增大。通过将解延拓到实时（real time）发现，膨胀的气泡壁附近发生电荷重新排布，消耗了相梯度能（phase-gradient energy），导致气泡在真空中也会达到亚光速终端速度（subluminal terminal velocity）。此外，固定荷构造（fixed-charge construction）与有限温度及有限化学势（finite-temperature and finite-chemical-potential）描述之间的衔接关系也得到了阐明。

Conclusion: 守恒全局荷的存在从根本上改变了零温真空衰变的物理图像：不仅衰变率增大，气泡膨胀动力学也出现了电荷诱导的亚光速终端速度效应。本文的双场实欧几里得方法为处理带荷场的非微扰衰变问题提供了有效框架，并建立了与有限温度和化学势描述之间的联系。

Abstract: Vacuum decay at zero temperature is generically described by a real $O(4)$-symmetric Coleman bounce. When the scalar field driving the decay carries a conserved global charge, this picture changes qualitatively: the path integral must be projected onto a definite charge sector, the Euclidean field obeys twisted boundary conditions, and the saddle is complex. For the simplest case of a $U(1)$ global symmetry, we first reformulate this problem in a two-field real Euclidean description with a real saddle. We then solve the resulting two-dimensional partial differential equation problem describing the decay of a homogeneous charged medium to a deeper vacuum via bubble nucleation. At finite charge the bounce departs from $O(4)$ symmetry, the barrier between vacua is lowered, and the decay rate increases. Continuing the solution to real time, we find that charge rearrangement around the expanding wall costs phase-gradient energy and drives the bubble to a subluminal terminal velocity even in vacuum. We also clarify how the fixed-charge construction interfaces with finite-temperature and finite-chemical-potential descriptions.

</details>


### [166] [Dynamics of ($Z_N$) Domain Walls in SU(N) Gauge Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22532)
*Sayanjit Banerjee,Sanatan Digal,Sumit Shaw*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本论文利用Polyakov-loop有效势模型研究SU(N)规范理论中畴壁的碰撞动力学，发现弦连接（string junctions）在Z_N畴壁行为中起关键作用，尤其是在不同碰撞能量下通过涡旋（vortex）与反涡旋（antivortex）对的产生或抑制实现畴壁合并、反弹或散射，揭示了拓扑弦（topological strings）在中心畴壁网络演化中的直接动力学角色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解非阿贝尔规范理论（non-Abelian gauge theories）中Z_N畴壁网络的动力学演化，特别是拓扑缺陷（如弦与涡旋）在畴壁碰撞过程中的作用尚不明确，亟需系统研究。

Method: 采用Polyakov-loop有效势模型（Polyakov-loop effective potential models），对SU(3)和SU(4)规范理论中的Z_3和Z_4畴壁碰撞进行数值模拟与分析，并推广到3+1维情形。

Result: SU(3)中两非平面Z_3畴壁合并时，在2+1维中通过产生涡旋–反涡旋对（vortex–antivortex pair）完成；SU(4)中低能碰撞直接形成单畴壁而无涡旋产生，高能碰撞则可通过涡旋形成导致反弹或散射为另一对畴壁。涡旋–反涡旋对的产生在3+1维中推广为弦环（string loops）的产生。

Conclusion: 拓扑弦在中心畴壁网络（center-domain-wall networks）演化中具有直接的动力学作用，揭示了非阿贝尔规范理论中缺陷动力学（defect dynamics）的新方面。

Abstract: We study collisions of domain walls in $SU(N)$ gauge theories using the Polyakov-loop effective potential models. We find that string junctions play a crucial role in the dynamics of $Z_N$ domain walls. In $SU(3)$ gauge theory, the merger of two non-planar $Z_3$ domain walls into a single wall proceeds via the creation of a vortex--antivortex pair in $2+1$ dimensions. In $SU(4)$ gauge theory, low-energy collisions of $Z_4$ walls result in the formation of a single domain wall without the creation of vortices. At higher collision energies, two $Z_4$ domain walls can either bounce back or scatter into another pair of domain walls through the formation of vortices. The creation of vortex--antivortex pairs generalises to the creation of string loops in $3+1$ dimensions for both gauge theories. These results demonstrate a direct dynamical role for topological strings in the evolution of center-domain-wall networks and reveal a new aspect of defect dynamics in non-Abelian gauge theories.

### [167] [Radiative Lifting of $\mathbb{Z}_3$ Domain-Wall Degeneracy in a Type-III Seesaw Model: Implications for Leptogenesis and Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22642)
*Priya,Labh Singh,B. C. Chauhan,Surender Verma*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个带有Z₃对称性的标准模型扩展，引入三个超荷为零的SU(2)_L费米子三重态（通过Type-III跷跷板机制产生中微子质量）和一个复标量单态χ（通过真空期望值自发破缺Z₃对称性）。Yukawa相互作用的辐射修正产生Coleman-Weinberg真空偏置，解除Z₃真空简并并导致不稳定畴壁湮灭。数值分析符合中微子振荡数据，热轻子生成（thermal leptogenesis）产生观测到的重子不对称性，且引力波谱可被未来探测器观测到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用具有Z₃对称性的标准模型扩展，引入三个超荷为零的SU(2)_L费米子三重态和复标量单态χ。通过Coleman-Weinberg有效势（Coleman-Weinberg effective potential）的辐射修正产生真空偏置（vacuum bias），解除Z₃真空简并并驱动畴壁湮灭。利用Type-III跷跷板机制（Type-III seesaw mechanism）生成中微子质量，并通过轻子三重态的非平衡衰变实现热轻子生成（thermal leptogenesis）。

Result: 数值分析确认了与当前中微子振荡数据一致的参数空间区域。轻子三重态质量在约10⁹ GeV量级时可产生观测到的重子不对称性。预测的引力波谱（gravitational-wave spectrum）在部分参数选择下可被未来天基和地基引力波探测器（gravitational-wave detectors）探测到。

Conclusion: 该框架建立了中微子质量生成、轻子生成、辐射驱动的畴壁不稳定性以及引力波现象学之间的关联，为多物理问题的统一解释提供了可行路径。

Abstract: In this work, we study a $\mathbb{Z}_3$-symmetric extension of the Standard Model with three hyperchargeless $SU(2)_L$ fermion triplets responsible for neutrino mass generation $\textit{via}$ the Type-III seesaw mechanism together with a complex scalar singlet $χ$ whose vacuum expectation value spontaneously breaks the $\mathbb{Z}_3$ symmetry. Radiative corrections induced by the Yukawa interactions between the $SU(2)_L$ fermion triplets and the complex scalar singlet $χ$ generate a Coleman-Weinberg vacuum bias that lifts the degeneracy among the $\mathbb{Z}_3$ vacua, leading to the annihilation of unstable domain-walls. Consequently, the degeneracy among the $\mathbb{Z}_3$ vacua is lifted radiatively through the Coleman-Weinberg effective potential, generating a dynamical bias term that triggers the annihilation of unstable domain walls. We perform a numerical analysis consistent with current neutrino oscillation data and identify viable regions of parameter space accommodating the observed neutrino masses and leptonic mixing parameters. The observed baryon asymmetry of the Universe is generated through thermal leptogenesis $\textit{via}$ the out-of-equilibrium decay of the lightest fermion triplet for masses around $\mathcal{O}(10^{9})\,\mathrm{GeV}$, consistent with the Type-III seesaw framework. Depending on the choice of model parameters, the predicted gravitational-wave spectrum can fall within the sensitivity reach of future space-based and ground-based gravitational-wave detectors. Our framework therefore establishes a correlation between neutrino mass generation, leptogenesis, radiative domain-wall instability, and gravitational-wave phenomenology.

### [168] [Twisting Small-$x$ Gluon Tomography with Orbital Angular Momentum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22871)
*Wei Kou,Xurong Chen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种轨道角动量（Orbital Angular Momentum, OAM）分辨的扩展方法，用于硬衍射双喷注深度非弹性散射（Deep Inelastic Scattering, DIS）中的小-x胶子层析成像（small-x gluon tomography）。通过将平面波轻子流替换为扭曲波包（twisted wave-packet）流，将原本固定的横向读出转变为可调的OAM-贝塞尔（Bessel）投影核，从而得到一族M分辨的椭圆关联量A₂⁽ᴹ⁾(q_T, R_γ)。该可调模式零点是标准平面波读出所不具备的，提供了对同一小-x椭圆几何结构施加不同符号响应或归零的外部投影基。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准平面波设置中，小-x胶子威格纳分布（Wigner distribution）的椭圆分量通过固定的横向读出进行探测，缺乏对轨道角动量（OAM）分辨的灵活调控能力。本文旨在通过引入扭曲波包轻子流，将这种固定读出提升为可调的OAM-贝塞尔投影核，从而扩展小-x胶子层析成像的探测维度。

Method: 将平面波轻子电流替换为扭曲波包电流，使交换虚光子（virtual photon）的OAM依赖性通过轻子电磁流（lepton electromagnetic current）的横向结构引入，而非将虚光子视为渐近涡旋粒子（asymptotic vortex particle）。由此推导出一族M分辨的椭圆关联量A₂⁽ᴹ⁾(q_T, R_γ)，其中q_T表示投影核的横向贝塞尔标度（transverse Bessel scale），而非交换光子的横动量。

Result: 归一化线性响应中包含来自总衍射率（total diffractive rate）形变的减除项。因此，椭圆响应可以在衍射率仍然有限的条件下归零。这种有限率零点（finite-rate null）是目标椭圆胶子分量响应的归一化投影零点，而非衍射现象的消失。该可调模式零点在标准单平面波读出中无法实现。

Conclusion: 该可调OAM-贝塞尔投影核提供了一种外部投影基（external projection basis），使得对同一小-x椭圆几何结构的响应可以以不同符号进行探测，或被调谐至归零。这为小-x胶子层析成像提供了新的实验调控自由度。

Abstract: We propose an orbital-angular-momentum-resolved extension of small-$x$ gluon tomography in hard diffractive dijet deep inelastic scattering. In the standard plane-wave setup, the elliptic correlation between the dijet relative momentum and the target recoil probes the elliptic component of the small-$x$ gluon Wigner distribution through a fixed transverse readout. We show that replacing the plane-wave lepton current by a twisted wave-packet current promotes this readout into a tunable OAM--Bessel projection kernel. The exchanged virtual photon is not treated as an asymptotic vortex particle; the OAM dependence enters through the transverse structure of the lepton electromagnetic current. The resulting observable is a family of $M$-resolved elliptic correlations $A_2^{(M)}(q_T,R_γ)$, where $q_T$ denotes the transverse Bessel scale of the projection kernel, not the transverse momentum of the exchanged photon. We derive the normalized linear response and show that it contains a subtraction from the deformation of the total diffractive rate. Consequently, the elliptic response can vanish while the diffractive rate remains finite. This finite-rate null is a normalized projection zero of the response to the target elliptic gluon component, not a disappearance of diffraction. It is not available as a tunable mode zero in the standard single plane-wave readout, and provides an external projection basis in which the response to the same small-$x$ elliptic geometry can be probed with either sign or tuned to zero.

</details>


### [169] [Remarks on atmospheric effect of D-foam in light of muon puzzle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22855)
*Chengyi Li*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于量子时空泡沫（quantum space-time foam）的弦论模型，论证了该模型引起的亚光速洛伦兹破坏（subluminal Lorentz violation）对广延大气簇射（extensive air shower, EAS）中电子数目的抑制效应，从而可能导致对初级宇宙线粒子能量的低估，并增强簇射中的μ子含量。作者提出，这或可解释多个实验（如Auger和Telescope Array合作组）报道的“μ子过剩”现象，暗示其可能源于量子引力效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者此前在arXiv:2509.00552中基于弦论量子时空泡沫模型提出，该模型诱导的亚光速洛伦兹破坏不会像其他方法那样导致实验上不可接受的粒子簇射变化，但可能在特定条件下通过抑制初级光子在原子核上的对产生（pair creation）来轻微修正电磁级联过程。本附录旨在进一步考察该修正对由超高能宇宙线（ultrahigh-energy cosmic-ray）初级强子（如能量约10^19 eV的质子）引发的EAS探测的影响。

Method: 作者从弦论量子时空泡沫模型出发，分析在初级强子引发的EAS中，次级光子（来自π⁰衰变）的亚簇射（subshowers）如何因泡沫效应而受到抑制。通过论证对产生过程被抑制导致到达探测器的电子数目减少，从而推断初级粒子能量可能被低估，并间接增强μ子含量。

Result: 量子时空泡沫效应将导致EAS中到达地面探测器的电子数量减少，进而使得初级宇宙线粒子的能量被低估。同时，簇射中的μ子含量会相对增强。

Conclusion: 该机制为解释Auger和Telescope Array等多个高能宇宙线实验所报告的“μ子过剩”现象提供了一种基于量子引力效应（quantum-gravitational effect）的候选解释。未来观测将有助于确认该异常是否真实存在。

Abstract: In our recent paper arXiv:2509.00552, we used a stringy model for quantum space-time foam to suggest that the so-induced subluminal Lorentz violation~(LV) for photons would not lead to experimentally unacceptable changes in the developments of particle showers initiated by cosmic $γ$-rays in the Earth's atmosphere, in contrast to other approaches to LV. The result indicated, nonetheless, at the same time that the foam can mildly modify the electromagnetic cascades under certain conditions, by suppressing pair creation on nuclei by primary photons. In this addendum, we consider how this modification affects the detection of extensive air shower~(EAS) initiated by an ultrahigh-energy cosmic-ray particle~(viz., a primary hadron), like proton with $E \sim 10^{19}~\textrm{eV}$, given that secondary photon subshowers following $π^{0}$ decays could be similarly influenced. We argue that fewer electrons would reach the detector and hence the energy of the primary particle may be underestimated due to foam effects, enhancing in such a way the muon content in EASs. This opens up the possibility of interpreting the alleged ``excess'' of muons, as reported by Auger and Telescope Array collaborations recently and many other experiments on high-energy cosmic rays, with a quantum-gravitational effect. Future observations are anticipated to confirm whether this anomaly really exists.

### [170] [AI-accelerated metallized $σ$-bonding screening for superconductor discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21251)
*Zechen Tang,Wen-Han Dong,Baochun Wu,Jian-Feng Zhang,Yuxiang Wang,Yang Li,Honggeng Tao,Qiyu Zeng,Chong Wang,Chen Si,Zhong-Yi Lu,Wenhui Duan,Tao Xiang,Yong Xu*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出基于金属化σ键图像的σ键态密度（σDOS）作为高效物理描述符，结合深度学习密度泛函理论（DFT）哈密顿方法，在不进行显式密度泛函微扰理论（DFPT）计算的前提下，快速筛选高声子介导超导转变温度（Tc）的超导体。通过对200万种材料的筛选，识别出常压超导体候选材料B13Se（预测Tc > 40 K）及B13X家族，验证了该策略的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于金属化σ键图像，引入σ键态密度（σ-bonding density of states, σDOS）作为物理描述符，仅利用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）级别的电子结构即可评估高Tc超导体，无需显式DFPT计算。进一步采用深度学习密度泛函理论哈密顿（deep-learning DFT Hamiltonian）方法加速σDOS评估，实现大规模高通量筛选。

Result: 对200万种材料进行筛选，识别出常压超导体候选材料B13Se，其预测Tc超过40 K，并发现一族高Tc的B13X候选材料，验证了该发现策略的有效性。

Conclusion: 通过将物理先验（physics priors）与人工智能加速相结合，本文提供了一种高效且可推广的计算材料发现路径，适用于人工智能时代的超导体高通量筛选。

Abstract: The computational discovery of phonon-mediated superconductors is hindered by the prohibitive cost of density functional perturbation theory (DFPT). Here, guided by the metallized $σ$-bonding picture, we introduce the $σ$-bonding density of states ($σ$DOS) as an efficient physical descriptor to identify high-transition-temperature ($T_{\mathrm{c}}$) superconductors from density functional theory (DFT)-level electronic structure without explicit DFPT calculations. The evaluation of $σ$DOS can be further accelerated by a deep-learning DFT Hamiltonian method, enabling efficient large-scale screening for superconductors. Screening 2 million materials, we identify B$_{13}$Se as an ambient-pressure superconductor candidate with predicted $T_{\mathrm{c}} > 40$~K, together with a family of high-$T_{\mathrm{c}}$ B$_{13}X$ candidates, supporting the effectiveness of this discovery strategy. By bridging physics priors with AI acceleration, this study delivers an efficient and generalizable route for computational materials discovery in the AI era.

### [171] [Glass-based physical models for tissue mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22281)
*Gopika Madhu,Carolyn Delli-Santi,Jenna Efrein,Prannoy Suraneni,Landolf Rhode-Barbarigos,Vivek N. Prakash*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 玻璃工艺技术提供了一种可控的物理平台，用于研究简单生物体的组织力学（tissue mechanics），但此前缺乏将玻璃物理模型与生物组织变形行为进行系统定量比较的研究。

Method: 在玻璃工作室中将玻璃塑造成类似组织（tissue-like）的单层膜，加热至特定工艺温度后施加受控拉伸，快速冷却冻结变形构型；通过横向和径向拉伸实验量化单个“细胞”的面积和离心率变化，并辅以张拉整体（tensegrity）模型进行模拟。

Result: 拉伸后玻璃模型中单个“细胞”的离心率增加；张拉整体模型捕捉到了实验的主要变形模式，但低估了离心率变化的幅度。

Conclusion: 基于玻璃的物理模型为研究组织尺度的变形和力学行为提供了一个实验上可操作的平台，并支持连接艺术与科学的跨学科研究方法。

Abstract: Techniques from glass art and fabrication provide a controllable physical platform for studying tissue mechanics in simple organisms. Here, we use glass-based physical models to investigate tissue deformation in the marine organism Trichoplax adhaerens. Previous studies have shown that the epithelial tissues in T. adhaerens undergo large deformations and form fracture holes under mechanical loading, exhibiting a ductile-to-brittle transition at fast loading rates. To model these behaviors in a tunable and experimentally accessible system, glass is shaped into tissue-like monolayers in a glass studio, heated to its specific process temperature, and subjected to controlled stretching. Rapid cooling arrests the deformed configurations, providing snapshots of tissue-like strain states under load. Under lateral and radial stretching, we quantify changes in the area and eccentricity of individual "cells" in the glass models, and found that eccentricity increases after stretching. We further use tensegrity-based models to quantify deformations in the cellular geometry of the glass tissues, enabling direct comparison between experiments and simulations. The model captures the principal experimental deformation patterns, but underestimates the magnitude of the observed eccentricity changes. Our results demonstrate that glass-based physical models provide an experimentally accessible platform for studying tissue-scale deformation and mechanical behavior, while supporting interdisciplinary approaches that connect methods in the arts and sciences.

*Pyae Hein Htet,Kenta Ishimoto*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种理论引导的数据驱动方法——Koopman自编码器，从噪声、稀疏且弱周期性的生物形状数据中恢复极限环（limit cycle），提取运动步态（shape gaits）与几何相位（geometric phase），并引入几何相位敏感函数（geometric phase sensitivity function）以仅基于规范场论（gauge theory）结构揭示力学信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 几何相位（geometric phase）通过规范场论（gauge theory）量化耗散介质中的净运动，但将该理论量与实际生物形状数据（噪声大、稀疏、弱周期性）关联存在困难。

Method: 开发了一种理论引导、数据驱动的Koopman自编码器（Koopman autoencoder），用于从不完美的周期数据中恢复极限环（limit cycle），并提取形状步态（shape gaits）与几何相位（geometric phase）；进一步引入几何相位敏感函数（geometric phase sensitivity function），可量化形状扰动（shape perturbations）的响应，并仅利用规范场论结构获取力学信息。

Conclusion: 几何相位敏感函数可在不假设力学定律（mechanical laws）的前提下，仅依赖规范场论结构揭示力学信息（mechanical information）。

Abstract: Geometric phase quantifies net locomotion in dissipative media via gauge theory, but linking this theoretical quantity to noisy, sparse, and weakly periodic biological shape data is challenging. We develop a theory-guided, data-driven Koopman autoencoder to recover the limit cycle embedded in imperfect cyclic data and extract shape gaits and geometric phase from sperm and nematode data. We introduce a geometric phase sensitivity function that quantifies responses to shape perturbations and reveals mechanical information using only gauge-theoretic structure, without assuming mechanical laws.

### [173] [Ambarzumian-type theorems for Hermitian matrices with applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21589)
*Matthias Hofmann,Joachim Kerner*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本论文将逆谱理论（inverse spectral theory）中的Ambarzumian定理推广至有限离散图（finite discrete graphs）上的几类Hermitian矩阵（Hermitian matrices），包括离散拉普拉斯矩阵（discrete Laplacian）和邻接矩阵（adjacency matrix），建立了适用于一般有限图的Ambarzumian型定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Ambarzumian定理指出区间上带非零势的Neumann拉普拉斯算子（Neumann Laplacian）不与无势情形等谱（isospectral）。该文旨在将这一结果推广至有限图上的Hermitian矩阵类，以填补现有Ambarzumian型定理在一般有限离散图上的空白。

Method: 针对不同矩阵类采用不同方法：一方面研究有限图上离散拉普拉斯矩阵等已知矩阵的Ambarzumian型定理；另一方面利用独立方法建立对角元为零的矩阵（如有限图的邻接矩阵）的相应定理。

Result: 成功将Ambarzumian型定理从经典区间情形推广至一般有限离散图，覆盖了离散拉普拉斯矩阵和邻接矩阵等重要矩阵类别。

Conclusion: 该工作统一并扩展了现有关于Ambarzumian型定理的结果，使其适用于一般的有限离散图结构。

Abstract: A foundational result in inverse spectral theory due to Ambarzumian (1929) states that the Neumann Laplacian on an interval is not isospectral to the Neumann Laplacian with an additional non-zero potential. In this note, our aim is to investigate Ambarzumian-type theorems for certain classes of Hermitian matrices, including well-known matrices such as the discrete Laplacian on finite graphs. In addition, using different methods, we establish an Ambarzumian-type theorem for matrices with vanishing diagonal, in particular, the adjacency matrix on finite graphs. In this way, we generalize existing results on Ambarzumian-type theorems to general finite discrete graphs.

### [174] [Digital Beam Pattern Optimisation for the GRAO 32-m Telescope: A Comparative Analysis of FIR Filter Design Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21720)
*Theophilus Ansah-Narh,Nia Imara,Benedicta Woode,Emmanuel Proven Adzri*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于有限脉冲响应（FIR）空间滤波的波束优化框架，将经典数字信号处理方法应用于射电望远镜琼斯场（Jones fields），显著抑制了32米GRAO天线在5 GHz波束模型中的旁瓣、衍射和交叉极化泄漏，提升了定标稳定性与偏振测量精度，并提供了一种可推广至其他单口径和相控阵仪器的非侵入式波束控制方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型单口径射电望远镜的波束模式（beam pattern）稳定性与保真度直接决定其角分辨率、灵敏度和偏振测量精度，而GRAO 32米天线的电磁仿真显示其存在残留旁瓣、结构衍射和交叉极化泄漏（cross-polar leakage），限制了高动态范围和偏振敏感观测的性能。

Method: 通过建立角位移与空间频率之间的等价关系，将经典FIR设计方法（窗函数法与Parks-McClellan算法）直接应用于仿真的琼斯场（Jones fields），构建数字空间滤波框架将波束优化问题转化为数字信号处理问题，从而实现对产生旁瓣和偏振混合的高空间频率伪影的可控抑制。

Result: 在GRAO 5 GHz波束模型上，该方法显著降低了近轴旁瓣波纹（near-in sidelobe ripple），改善了波束平滑度，并将视轴处（boresight）的交叉极化泄漏降至-30 dB以下，从而提升了定标稳定性与偏振测量精度。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种可推广、非侵入式且计算高效的波束控制途径，不仅适用于GRAO，也可扩展至其他单口径和相控阵仪器；数字空间滤波可作为传统光学或机械优化的实用补充，推动电磁建模与信号处理在下一代射电天文仪器中的整合。

Abstract: The scientific utility of large single-dish radio telescopes depends critically on the stability and fidelity of their beam patterns, which govern angular resolution, sensitivity, and polarimetric accuracy. For the 32-m Ghana Radio Astronomy Observatory (GRAO) antenna, electromagnetic simulations reveal residual sidelobes, structural diffraction, and cross-polar leakage that limit performance in high-dynamic-range and polarisation-sensitive observations. To address these limitations, we develop a finite-impulse-response (FIR) spatial filtering framework that reformulates beam optimisation as a digital signal processing problem. By exploiting the equivalence between angular displacement and spatial frequency, classical FIR design methods, window-based and Parks-McClellan algorithms are adapted to operate directly on simulated Jones fields. This approach enables controlled suppression of high spatial frequency artefacts responsible for sidelobes and polarisation mixing, while preserving the telescope's diffraction-limited resolution. Applied to the GRAO 5 GHz beam model, the method achieves substantial reductions in near-in sidelobe ripple, improves beam smoothness, and lowers cross-polar leakage below -30 dB at boresight. These improvements translate into enhanced calibration stability and polarimetric precision, strengthening the telescope's capacity for Very Long Baseline Interferometry, spectral-line surveys, and pulsar timing. Beyond GRAO, the method provides a generalisable, non-invasive, and computationally efficient pathway for beam control applicable to other single-dish and phased-array instruments. The results establish digital spatial filtering as a practical complement to conventional optical or mechanical optimisation, advancing the integration of electromagnetic modelling and signal processing in next-generation radio astronomical instrumentation.

</details>


### [175] [Optimization and robustness of cost-efficient seismic arrays for Newtonian noise cancellation at the Einstein Telescope](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21110)
*Patrick Schillings,Johannes Erdmann*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文研究了爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）中牛顿噪声（Newtonian noise）的抑制策略，优化了地震仪阵列的布设位置。结果表明，每个钻孔中放置多个地震仪的阵列在抑制能力上与更少钻孔但单地震仪阵列相当；在隧道中增设地震仪可进一步提升抑制效果。宽带性能分析显示，大型阵列在3–4 Hz以上频率具有良好且稳定的抑制表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 牛顿噪声是爱因斯坦望远镜低频段的主要噪声源，来源于地震波引起的地面密度涨落。为了有效抑制这一噪声，需要优化地震仪阵列的布置。

Method: 对爱因斯坦望远镜一个完整拐角处的地震仪阵列位置进行优化。比较了单钻孔单地震仪与单钻孔多地震仪两种阵列构型，并评估在干涉仪隧道中增设地震仪的效果。在1–10 Hz范围内量化宽带抑制性能，并检验阵列对位置变化的鲁棒性。

Result: 每钻孔多地震仪阵列的抑制能力与仅略小规模的单钻孔单地震仪阵列相当。在隧道中增设地震仪进一步改善了抑制效果。对于20钻孔每钻孔3地震仪的阵列，抑制因子>6；对于50钻孔每钻孔10地震仪的大型阵列，抑制因子>15。大型阵列在3–4 Hz以上表现出良好的宽带性能。

Conclusion: 采用每钻孔多地震仪并结合隧道内地震仪的阵列构型，可实现成本效益高且稳定的牛顿噪声抑制方案。

Abstract: Newtonian noise is expected to be the dominating noise source for low frequencies at the Einstein Telescope. It originates from seismic waves that cause density fluctuations in the rock around the interferometer. The mitigation strategy for Newtonian noise relies on an array of seismometers, placed at depth in boreholes, which provides measurements of the seismic wave field. We optimize the positions of the individual seismometers for the mitigation capabilities of the array for a full corner of the Einstein Telescope. We find that the mitigation capabilities of arrays with multiple seismometers in each borehole match the capabilities of only somewhat smaller arrays but with only one seismometer per borehole. Mitigation is further improved by extending the array with seismometers in the interferometer tunnels. Such configurations may hence provide a cost-effective way towards realizing an efficient seismic array. In each case, we quantify the broadband mitigation performance in the range from 1 to 10 Hz for arrays that are optimized for a frequency of 10 Hz, as well as the robustness of the arrays with respect to variations from their optimized positions. We find that larger arrays with several seismometers per borehole and additional seismometers in the tunnels provide promising broadband performance above 3 to 4 Hz and that such arrays are particularly stable against variations in the seismometer positions with mitigation factors $>6$ for an array of 20 boreholes with 3 seismometers each and $>15$ for a large array of 50 boreholes with 10 seismometers.

</details>

# cond-mat.stat-mech [[Back]](#toc)

### [176] [A few remarks on hyperstatistics and some applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20735)
*Lucas Squillante,Samuel M. Soares,Guilherme Lepski,Mariano de Souza*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文深入阐述了超统计（hyperstatistics）的理论基础，这是一种处理非玻尔兹曼-吉布斯（non-Boltzmann-Gibbsian）行为系统的一般性统计力学方法，并将其新应用于布朗运动速度自相关函数和脑动力学描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统玻尔兹曼-吉布斯统计力学（Boltzmann-Gibbs statistics）无法描述具有固有非平衡行为的系统，需要发展一种更普适的理论框架。

Method: 采用超统计（hyperstatistics）方法，这是一种针对非玻尔兹曼-吉布斯行为系统提出的统计力学（statistical mechanics）一般性框架。

Result: 超统计方法已被成功应用于RC串联电路电容器放电、闭路循环低温恒温器中$^4$He的泵送、大型强子对撞机（LHC）中$p$-Pb碰撞的中快度数据，以及湍流系统中的加速度分布。本文进一步展示了其在布朗运动速度自相关函数和脑动力学描述中的适用性。

Conclusion: 超统计具有高度的精确性和广泛的适用性，能够有效解决非玻尔兹曼-吉布斯行为系统的统计描述问题，其潜在应用领域涵盖从经典物理到脑动力学的多个方向。

Abstract: In a recent paper [arXiv:2604.24783 (2026)], we have proposed a general approach to treat systems with inherent non-Boltzmann-Gibbsian behaviour. Given the extremely high accuracy of our approach, we have adopted the term hyperstatistics. We have applied such a statistical mechanics approach, i.e., hyperstatistics, to the discharge of a capacitor in a RC series circuit, pumping of $^4$He of a closed cycle cryostat, midrapidity data of $p$-Pb collisions at the LHC, as well as for the distribution of accelerations in turbulent systems. Here, we discuss into more details the ground of hyperstatistics. We demonstrate the versatility of hyperstatistics upon applying it to the velocity autocorrelation function in Brownian motion and also regarding its potential to describe brain dynamics.

</details>


### [177] [Tuning ergodicity breaking: Anomalous diffusion under asymptotic power-law forcing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20807)
*Raul V. B. Morás,M. Florencia Carusela,Luciano C. Lapas*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过广义朗之万方程（Generalized Langevin Equation）中的标度参数η，系统刻画了非马尔可夫系统（non-Markovian systems）在外驱动下的三态相图：热化相（η>0）、非遍历饱和相（η=0）以及力主导失控相（η<0），并揭示了涨落-耗散定理（fluctuation-dissipation theorem）在外力作用下保持形式不变的性质，以及一种选择性的遍历性破缺（selective breaking of ergodicity）机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非马尔可夫系统内部记忆（internal memory）与外部强迫（external forcing）之间的竞争会催生热化、持续遍历性破缺（persistent ergodicity breaking）和能量失控增长等多种不同的动力学相，但缺乏统一的分类框架来理解这些相的涌现条件与转变规律。

Method: 基于具有渐近幂律尾外驱动（external drives with asymptotic power-law tails）的广义朗之万方程（Generalized Langevin Equation），引入标度参数η来刻画相图结构；并在马尔可夫极限（Markovian limit）下进行直接朗之万模拟（Langevin simulations）以验证分类结论。

Result: 标度参数η划分出三个普适扩散过程区域：热化相（η>0）、非遍历饱和相（η=0）和力主导失控相（η<0）。涨落-耗散定理在外力下保持不变，其形式由噪声态密度积分决定。系统呈现出选择性遍历性破缺：微观涨落与驱动解耦，而弛豫过程完全编码了驱动信息，进而控制动力学有效温度（kinetic effective temperature）。马尔可夫极限下的模拟定量确认了该分类，并在临界点捕捉到非热平台（non-thermal plateau）。

Conclusion: 标度参数η为理解非马尔可夫系统中记忆与驱动竞争所导致的动力学相变提供了统一框架，揭示了涨落-耗散关系与遍历性破缺在非平衡系统中的新表现形式。

Abstract: In non-Markovian systems, distinct dynamical phases arise from the competition between internal memory and external forcing, encompassing thermalization, persistent ergodicity breaking, and runaway energy growth. This study shows that the scaling parameter $η$ governs the emergent phase diagram within a system described by the Generalized Langevin Equation, particularly when subjected to external drives with asymptotic power-law tails. Three universal regimes for diffusive processes are delineated by this parameter: thermalization ($η> 0$), non-ergodic saturation ($η= 0$), and a force-dominated runaway phase ($η< 0$). The fluctuation-dissipation theorem, within this framework, is shown to be independent of external force and determined by the integral of noise density of states. A selective breaking of ergodicity is revealed by this formulation; microscopic fluctuations are decoupled from the drive, yet the relaxation completely encodes it, which in turn controls the kinetic effective temperature. Direct Langevin simulations in the Markovian limit quantitatively confirm this classification, capturing the non-thermal plateau at the critical point.

</details>


### [178] [Hydrodynamic tails in chaotic spin chains with quantum group symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20850)
*Luca V. Delacretaz,Victor Gorbenko,Jiaozi Wang,Bernardo Zan,Aleksandr Zhabin*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文证明了量子群对称性（quantum group symmetry）可作为混沌系统中反常流体动力学（anomalous hydrodynamics）的新机制，使携带 U(1) 荷的局域算子在非可积晶格模型中表现出长寿命和超扩散（superdiffusion）行为，且这一现象在哈密顿、Floquet 和经典实现中均成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对称性与热化（thermalization）之间的相互作用支配着非零温度下局域量子与经典多体系统的晚期动力学。当前的研究前沿包括在一般非可积模型中寻找稳健的反常流体动力学（如超扩散），以及从形式上推广全局对称性（global symmetry）的基本概念。本文旨在将这两条前沿联系起来。

Method: 研究具有量子群对称性的非可积晶格模型（包括哈密顿、Floquet 和经典实现）中携带 U(1) 荷的局域算子的动力学。其中一个具体例子是带可积性破缺（integrability breaking）变形的 XXZ 模型中的横向自旋（transverse spin）。

Result: 尽管这类激发在高温下因荷禁戒与常规流体动力学密度（hydrodynamic densities）重叠而预期会快速衰减，但量子群对称性的保护使其成为长寿命模式，即便系统中不存在局域的量子群荷密度或流。该动力学在哈密顿、Floquet 和经典实现中均表现为超扩散，并在极晚期出现异常有限尺寸效应（finite size effects）。

Conclusion: 量子群对称性为混沌系统中的反常流体动力学提供了一种新机制。本文还重新审视了可积 XXZ 模型中的横向自旋动力学。

Abstract: The interplay between symmetry and thermalization governs the late-time dynamics of local quantum and classical many-body systems at nonzero temperature. Recently, two parallel frontiers have emerged: the search for robust anomalous hydrodynamics -- such as superdiffusion -- in generic, non-integrable models, and the formal effort to generalize the fundamental concept of global symmetry. In this paper, we bridge these frontiers by demonstrating that quantum group symmetry provides a novel mechanism for anomalous hydrodynamics in chaotic systems. We study the dynamics of local operators carrying $U(1)$ charge in non-integrable lattice models that also have quantum group symmetry. One example is transverse spin in the XXZ model with integrability breaking deformations. While such excitations are expected to decay very quickly at high temperature because their charge forbids overlap with conventional hydrodynamic densities, we find that protection by the quantum group symmetry makes these modes long-lived, despite the absence of local quantum group charge density or current. Furthermore, the dynamics is superdiffusive across Hamiltonian, Floquet, and classical realizations, and exhibits unusual finite size effects at very late times. We also revisit transverse spin dynamics in the integrable XXZ model.

</details>


### [179] [Asymptotic hydrographs and anomalous dispersion in mass-conserving storage cascades](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21095)
*Henrique Santos Lima,Márk Honti,Balázs Sándor*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究将经典爱尔朗分布（Erlang distribution）中的指数等待时间替换为$q$-指数（$q$-exponential）密度后，质量守恒级联储层系统的渐近行为，证明在$1<q<2$范围内宏观动力学由$α$-稳定Lévy律（$α$-stable Lévy laws）主导，且在临界情形$q=5/3$下大级联流率收敛于经伽利略型变换（Galilean-type transformation）平移的稳定Lévy密度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典概率论中，独立指数随机变量之和导出的爱尔朗分布（Erlang distribution）构成了从指数等待时间到整数形状伽马律（gamma law）的直观概率路径。本文旨在探究当指数等待时间密度被非广延统计（nonextensive statistics）中的$q$-指数密度（$q$-exponential density）替代后，这一经典构造将如何改变。

Method: 本文通过分析质量守恒级联储层（mass-conserving cascade of reservoirs）在$q$-指数等待时间核（waiting-time kernel）驱动下的输出流，推导了大级联极限下流率的解析渐近表达式（analytical asymptotic expression）。

Result: 在临界情形$q=5/3$下，大级联流率收敛于经伽利略型变换（Galilean-type transformation）平移时间的稳定Lévy密度（stable Lévy density），该平移后的Lévy律即级联的渐近水文过程线（asymptotic hydrograph）。对$1<q<2$的整个区间，宏观动力学均由$α$-稳定Lévy律（$α$-stable Lévy laws）支配。

Conclusion: 研究证明，异常的、非高斯色散（anomalous non-Gaussian dispersion）可以从纯质量守恒的卷积链（mass-conserving convolutional chains）中涌现，而无需引入分数阶导数（fractional derivatives）。

Abstract: Sums of independent exponential random variables lead to the Erlang distribution, providing a direct probabilistic route from exponential waiting times to the integer-shape gamma law. This paper investigates how this classical construction changes when the exponential waiting-time density is replaced by the $q$-exponential density of nonextensive statistics. Our main result is an analytical asymptotic expression for the outflow of a mass-conserving cascade of reservoirs driven by a $q$-exponential waiting-time kernel. In the critical case $q=5/3$, the large-cascade flow rate converges to a stable Lévy density whose time argument is shifted by a Galilean-type transformation. This shifted Lévy law gives the asymptotic hydrograph of the cascade. We also found that for the entire regime $1<q<2$ the macroscopic dynamics are governed by $α$-stable Lévy laws. This proves that anomalous non-Gaussian dispersion can emerge from pure mass-conserving convolutional chains without invoking fractional derivatives.

</details>


### [180] [From Landau Equation and Large Deviations to Efficient Simulations of Dynamical Fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21318)
*Anwar El Rhirhayi,Jean-Baptiste Fouvry,Julien Barré*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文基于大偏差理论（Large Deviation Theory）建立了一组与朗道方程（Landau equation）相容的朗之万方程（Langevin equations），既能恢复平均朗道动力学（mean Landau dynamics），又能准确描述不同实现之间的动力学涨落（dynamical fluctuations）。通过罗斯托克原理（Rostoker's principle）在弱两体偏转极限下推导得出，并利用直接N体模拟进行了验证，结果吻合极好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定性朗道方程虽然能够捕捉长程相互作用有限N体系统的平均长期演化，但该动力学方程从根本上忽略了动力学涨落。需要建立一个物理上自洽的框架，既能保留朗道方程的平均动力学描述，又能同时准确刻画不同实现之间的涨落行为。

Method: 基于大偏差理论框架，构建一组朗之万方程；从罗斯托克原理出发，在弱两体偏转（weak two-body deflections）极限下推导出该朗之万方程组。最后通过定制的直接N体模拟（direct N-body simulations）对理论预测进行定量验证。

Result: 所提出的朗之万方程组能够同时恢复平均朗道动力学，并准确捕捉有限N体系统动力学演化中的涨落特征。与直接N体模拟的对比显示出极好的一致性（exquisite level of agreement）。

Conclusion: 本文构建的基于大偏差理论的朗之万方程框架为描述长程相互作用有限N体系统的涨落动力学提供了物理自洽的理论工具，弥补了朗道方程忽略涨落的根本缺陷，且得到了数值模拟的有力支持。

Abstract: The (deterministic) Landau equation captures the mean long-term evolution of dynamically hot long-range interacting finite-$N$ systems. Though successful, this kinetic equation fundamentally ignores dynamical fluctuations. Building upon Large Deviation Theory, we present a physically-consistent system of Langevin equations that simultaneously recovers the mean Landau dynamics and accurately captures the corresponding fluctuations among different realizations. We show in particular how these Langevin equations can be derived from Rostoker's principle in the limit of weak two-body deflections. We extensively validate these equations against tailored direct $N$-body simulations, showing an exquisite level of agreement.

</details>


### [181] [Giant Fluctuations in Self-Propelled Particles with Age-Dependent Switching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22209)
*Shabnam Sohrabi,Farhad H. Jafarpour*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种具有年龄依赖相位切换机制的自推进粒子系统，通过生成函数和矩递推方法精确求解了传播子及长时间渐近行为；发现在临界点处系统方差呈弹道标度（带对数修正），表明慢衰减重取向概率会导致中心极限定理的边缘失效，从而产生极高方差的探索动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解在偏置环境中具有年龄依赖（age-dependent）重取向机制的自推进粒子的输运与涨落特性，特别是长期记忆效应对中心极限定理（Central Limit Theorem, CLT）有效性的影响。

Method: 构建由马尔可夫（Markovian）下游相与半马尔可夫（semi-Markovian）上游相交替的动力学模型，上游相的年龄依赖危险概率（hazard probability）$a/(b+c)$ 随内部时钟 $c$ 衰减；采用生成函数方法（generating-function methods）和离散时间矩递推（discrete-time moment recurrences）推导传播子及各阶矩的精确表达式。

Result: 时间平均速度（order parameter）在 $a=1$ 处呈现连续转变，将系统划分为上游主导的弹道区（$a<1$）和遍历扩散区（$a>1$）；在临界点 $a=1$ 处方差呈弹道标度但带有对数修正，即 $\mathrm{Var}(x_T) \propto T^2 / \log T$，表现出巨涨落（giant fluctuations）现象。

Conclusion: 慢衰减的重取向概率会导致中心极限定理在边缘情形下失效，使偏置环境中的系统能够展现出极高方差的异常探索动力学。

Abstract: We investigate the transport and fluctuation properties of self-propelled particles whose motion is governed by an age-dependent phase-switching mechanism. The dynamics alternate between a Markovian downstream phase with a constant switching probability $r$ and a semi-Markovian upstream phase in which the age-dependent hazard probability $a/(b+c)$ decays with the internal clock $c$, representing persistent orientation. The time-averaged velocity, as an order parameter, shows a continuous transition at $a=1$ which separates an upstream-dominated ballistic regime ($a<1$) from an ergodic diffusive regime ($a>1$). Through generating-function methods and discrete-time moment recurrences, we derive exact expressions for the propagator and determine the long-time asymptotics of the mean displacement and variance. At the critical point $a=1$, the system exhibits giant fluctuations, with the variance scaling ballistically up to a logarithmic correction, $\mathrm{Var}(x_T) \propto T^2 / \log T$. These results demonstrate how slowly decaying reorientation probabilities lead to a marginal breakdown of the Central Limit Theorem, enabling unusually high-variance exploratory dynamics in biased environments.

</details>


### [182] [Nonreciprocal Disorder Prevents Zero-Temperature Freezing in a Ferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21582)
*Noah Grodzinski,Robert L. Jack,Sarah A. M. Loos*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究具有随机分布非互易键（nonreciprocal bonds）的二维伊辛模型（2d Ising model），发现即使在零温下也存在连续的非平衡相变（nonequilibrium transition），且零温动力学呈现非热稀有区域翻转（athermal rare-region reversals）和对数“激活”粗化（logarithmic "activated" coarsening）等反常行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非互易相互作用（nonreciprocal interactions）是多种非平衡现象的基础，但淬火非互易性（quenched nonreciprocity）在扩展系统（extended systems）中的效应尚未被充分探索，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用二维伊辛模型，在其中以密度 p 随机分布非互易键（nonreciprocal bonds），通过规范不变性论证（gauge-invariance argument）推导相图约束，并运用平均场理论（mean-field theory）进行定性预测。

Result: 发现该系统存在连续的非平衡相变，在有限密度 p_c 下相变可延伸至 T=0 温度；零温动力学保持活跃，出现非热稀有区域翻转和对数“激活”粗化行为。

Conclusion: 规范不变性论证给出 p_c(T) ≤ 1/2 的上界，平均场理论能定性正确地预测相图；与平衡无序模型（equilibrium disordered models）不同，该系统的零温动力学并不冻结。

Abstract: Nonreciprocal interactions underpin diverse nonequilibrium phenomena, yet the effects of quenched nonreciprocity in extended systems remain largely unexplored. We study a $2d$ Ising model with randomly distributed nonreciprocal bonds at density $p$, finding a continuous nonequilibrium transition down to $T=0$ with finite $p_c$. A gauge-invariance argument yields $p_c(T)\leq1/2$, and mean-field theory predicts a qualitatively correct phase diagram. Unlike equilibrium disordered models, the zero-temperature dynamics remains active, with athermal rare-region reversals and logarithmic "activated" coarsening.

</details>


### [183] [Heavy-Tailed Dispersal Kernels from Stopped Subdiffusive Fractional Brownian Motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21681)
*Luis F. Gordillo,Priscilla E. Greenwood*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出一个异质性停止速率模型，通过将次扩散分数布朗运动（subdiffusive fractional Brownian motion）与Gamma分布停止速率相结合，同时实现了局部聚集和重尾分布（heavy-tailed distribution），以模拟种子传播等过程中同时出现的聚集与长距离扩散现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 次扩散分数布朗运动在粒子以指数分布时间停止时能产生局部聚集，但无法描述数据尾部中同时观测到的长距离扩散事件（long-distance dispersal events），因为其再分布核（redistribution kernel）仅具有指数衰减尾部，而实际应用（如种子传播）需要更重的尾部。

Method: 在次扩散粒子以指数分布时间停止的框架下，引入一个Gamma分布的速率参数（rate parameter），使不同粒子的停止速率具有异质性（heterogeneity），从而在保持次扩散分数布朗运动强局部聚集特性的同时生成重尾分布。

Result: 该模型使得最终径向位置（final radial positions）的密度呈现出重尾分布，能够在保持次扩散分数布朗运动局部聚集特征的基础上，产生用于模拟长距离扩散所需的重尾。

Conclusion: 所提出的异质性停止速率模型成功兼顾了次扩散过程中的局部聚集与长距离扩散特性，为同时存在这两种现象的实际应用（如种子传播）提供了更贴合数据的建模方案。

Abstract: Subdiffusive fractional Brownian motions produce localized aggregation when particles are stopped at exponentially distributed times. In applications where clumping and long-distance dispersal events are observed simultaneously, such as in some instances of seed dispersal, this model fails to describe the tails of the data. The resulting redistribution kernel has only an exponentially decaying tail, whereas a heavier tail is needed for modeling the long-distance dispersal observed. Here we propose a model in which subdiffusive particles stop at exponentially distributed times, but with a rate parameter that is Gamma distributed. This heterogeneity in stopping rates causes the density of final radial positions to have a heavy-tailed distribution. Our model retains the strong localized clumping characteristic of subdiffusive fractional Brownian motion while simultaneously generating the heavy tails required for realistic long-distance dispersal.

</details>


### [184] [Skewness tunes the small-drift record rate of random walks and Lévy flights](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23553)
*José Ricardo G. Mendonça*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文推导了带有微小正漂移的随机游走创纪录速率 λ(μ) 在漂移 μ→0 时的渐近行为：λ(μ) ∼ K μ^{(1-ρ)/ν}，其中 ν=1-1/α，ρ 为步骤分布的正性参数。该结果通过 Spitzer-Baxter 恒等式中调和和的 Mellin 变换统一处理了扩散、重尾和偏斜随机游走，并同时给出了主项、前因子和修正阶梯。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究微小正漂移随机游走中创纪录速率 λ(μ) 在漂移趋于零时的渐近行为，尤其是当随机游走步长属于稳定律（stable law）吸引域时的精确标度律。

Method: 对 Spitzer-Baxter 恒等式中的调和和（harmonic sum）进行一次 Mellin 变换（Mellin transform），将问题分解为核变换（kernel transform）与黎曼 ζ 因子（Riemann ζ factor）的乘积；通过分析极点的贡献同时得到主项标度律、前因子及修正阶梯。

Result: 创纪录速率满足 λ(μ) ∼ K μ^{(1-ρ)/ν}，其中 ν=1-1/α，指数仅由正性参数 ρ 决定，在偏度变化时扫过区间 [1, 1/(α-1)]；对于高斯步长恢复线性律（斜率 √2），对称重尾情形恢复 μ^{α/2(α-1)} 的幂律；前因子 K 在严格稳定步长下显式给出。

Conclusion: 该 Mellin 变换方法统一处理了扩散、重尾和偏斜随机游走的创纪录问题，并可直接推广到期望最大值、Kingman 的重流量排队律（heavy-traffic law for queues）和 Siegmund 的修正扩散常数（corrected-diffusion constant）等邻近问题。

Abstract: A random walk with small positive drift $μ$ sets new records at a rate $λ(μ)$ that vanishes as $μ\to 0$. For centered steps attracted to a stable law $Y$ with index $1 < α\leq 2$ and positivity parameter $ρ= P(Y>0)$, we find $λ(μ) \sim Kμ^{(1-ρ)/ν}$, $ν=1-1/α$, as $μ\to 0$. The result is exact for Gaussian and strictly stable steps, and extends at the leading-power level to their domains of attraction. The exponent is set by the asymmetry only through $ρ$, sweeping the interval $[1,\,1/(α-1)]$ as the skewness varies. It recovers the Gaussian linear law with slope $\sqrt{2}$ and, for symmetric heavy tails, the power $μ^{α/2(α-1)}$; beyond the stable tail ratio, distributional details enter through the prefactor $K$, which is explicit for strictly stable steps. The result follows directly from one Mellin transform of the harmonic sum in the Spitzer-Baxter identity, which factorizes into a kernel transform and a Riemann $ζ$ factor whose poles deliver at once the leading law, its prefactor, and a correction ladder, unifying diffusive, heavy-tailed, and skewed walks. The same transform also yields the expected maximum, recovering Kingman's heavy-traffic law for queues and Siegmund's corrected-diffusion constant as adjacent poles.

</details>

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模分子动力学模拟和非局域分数阶KPZ理论，揭示了驱动晶界在屈服点处从淬火Edwards-Wilkinson普适类（H≈0.33）向反常fKPZ态（H≈0.8）的突变，并表明长程1/r弹性相互作用和雪崩噪声共同调控了晶界形貌的分数阶弛豫与非高斯自仿射行为。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 驱动晶界的粗糙化行为由非局域弹性核（nonlocal elastic kernels）主导，其形貌转变本质上是一种普适类跃迁，且与动态断裂共享同一普适类，为理解晶界动力学与材料力学行为提供了统一视角。

Abstract: The kinetic roughening of driven grain boundaries (GBs) is fundamentally mediated by the collective behavior of disconnections, whose long-range $1/r$ elastic interactions distinguish them from conventional growing surfaces. Through large-scale molecular dynamics simulations and a nonlocal fractional Kardar-Parisi-Zhang (fKPZ) theory, we demonstrate that driven GBs undergo a sharp transition of morphology at the yield point, from the quenched Edwards-Wilkinson universality class ($H \approx 0.33$) to an anomalous fKPZ regime ($H \approx 0.8$), while the 1/r nonlocal elasticity manifests as the fractional relaxation of GB morphology. The results show that the avalanche noise arrests the gradient catastrophe induced by the KPZ nonlinearity. Governed by the nonlocal elastic kernels, the resulting morphology breaks the Gaussian self-affinity and parallels the universality class of dynamic fracture.

Method: 资产根据收益率符号编码为二元自旋变量（binary spin variables），资产间相关性决定有效相互作用强度；采用基于相关性的广度优先搜索（correlation-based breadth-first search, CBFS）程序将169种加密货币嵌入13×13晶格，构建类似伊辛模型的哈密顿量（Ising-like Hamiltonian），称为“市场晶体”（Market Crystal）。

Conclusion: 该框架为研究金融系统中的集体行为提供了一种统计力学视角，有望推广至其他金融市场分析。

Abstract: Collective dynamics in financial markets can emerge through synchronized movements of large groups of assets. Motivated by analogies with interacting many-body systems, we introduce a spin-lattice representation for analyzing collective states in cryptocurrency markets. In this framework, assets are encoded as binary spin variables according to the sign of their returns, while correlations between assets determine effective interaction strengths. A correlation-based breadth-first search (CBFS) procedure embeds 169 cryptocurrencies into a $13 \times 13$ lattice, enabling the construction of an Ising-like Hamiltonian describing the market configuration, which we call the \emph{Market Crystal}. Macroscopic observables such as magnetization and energy provide a statistical-mechanical characterization of collective market states. ### [187] [Internal-state criticality in Bayesian-inverse-Bayesian inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22109)
*Kazuto Sasai,Yukio-Pegio Gunji*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出贝叶斯-逆贝叶斯（BIB）推理作为重复博弈中的最小生成模型，将贝叶斯推理、统计力学（statistical mechanics）与重尾统计（heavy-tailed statistics）联系起来。在循环主导石头-剪刀-布的模拟中，BIB动力学始终处于内部临界态（critical state），且argmax-持久性分布呈现指数约1.43的重尾幂律（power law）。BIB通过不断重构假设空间边界达到临界性，无需调整外部参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有重复博弈模型在面对如循环主导石头-剪刀-布这样的离散设定时，纳什均衡（Nash equilibrium）导向的算法会退化为均匀随机策略，使得任何非平凡动力学必须源于内部机制。因此，需要一个能够从内部生成非平凡动力学、并连接贝叶斯推理与统计力学框架的最小生成模型。

Method: 提出贝叶斯-逆贝叶斯（Bayesian-inverse-Bayesian, BIB）推理框架，并在重复的N手循环主导石头-剪刀-布游戏中模拟实现。通过跨设计（design）、窗口（window）和对手条件（opponent conditions）的多轴扫描，分析BIB动力学的argmax-持久性分布（argmax-persistence distribution）和层流可观测量（laminar observables），并与纯贝叶斯（Bayes-only）推理进行对比。

Result: BIB动力学在所有条件下均处于同一内部临界态，在规范窗口下argmax-持久性分布为指数约1.43的重尾幂律。沿窗口和字母（alphabet）轴，指数随有限样本残差（finite-sample residual）(N-1)/(2m)趋零而向普适的3/2漂移。纯贝叶斯推理无此普适性和幂律行为。临界态在假设计数（hypothesis count）N_h下不变，截断时间和后验展宽（posterior spread）满足有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）。

Conclusion: 在普通贝叶斯推理基础上添加逆贝叶斯松弛步骤（假设更新，hypothesis renewal）足以使动力学达到临界态，无需外部参数调整。BIB并非自组织到一个吸收态（absorbing state），而是通过不断重构假设空间边界（hypothesis-space boundary）实现临界性，这一机制与自组织临界性（self-organized criticality, SOC）互补，且能在自然参数范围内保持稳健。

Abstract: We propose Bayesian-inverse-Bayesian (BIB) inference in repeated games as a minimal generative model linking Bayesian inference, statistical mechanics, and heavy-tailed statistics. As a concrete instantiation we simulate repeated $N$-hand cyclic-dominance rock-paper-scissors, a discrete setting in which Nash-targeting algorithms collapse to uniform random play, so that any non-trivial dynamics must originate internally. Across a multi-axis sweep of design, window, and opponent conditions, the BIB dynamics remain in the same internal critical state, the argmax-persistence distribution staying a heavy-tailed power law with exponent $α\approx 1.43$ at the canonical window. Along the window and alphabet axes the exponent is not constant but drifts toward the universal $3/2$ as the finite-sample residual $(N-1)/(2m)$ vanishes. Bayes-only inference, which lacks the inverse step, shows no analogous universality and no power law. Because the argmax and laminar observables are first-passage reads of one driftless log-posterior walk, what is robust across conditions is the critical, zero-drift state itself, evidenced by the cross-design data collapse rather than by any particular exponent value. The state is also invariant across the hypothesis count $N_h$, with the cutoff time and posterior spread obeying finite-size scaling. Adding an inverse-Bayesian relaxation step (hypothesis renewal) to ordinary Bayesian inference is by itself enough to render the dynamics critical, with no external parameter adjustment. Rather than self-organizing toward an absorbing state, BIB reaches criticality by continually reconstructing the hypothesis-space boundary, a mechanism complementary to self-organized criticality that makes the criticality robust across a natural parameter range.

*Zhiyi Li,Zhijie Fan,Kun Chen,Youjin Deng*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子模拟器的实验进展表明长程相互作用（LR interactions）能够重塑量子临界性（quantum criticality）并稳定超出短程（short-range, SR）范式的奇异相。本文旨在系统研究长程量子临界行为，并提出统一的理论框架。

Method: 采用微扰重整化群（renormalization-group, RG）展开，通过设定d=3-ε和σ=2-δ，在LR-SR边界附近展开。在双圈（two-loop）计算中，获得了关联长度指数ν、频率反常维度（anomalous dimension）η_ω和动量反常维度η_k关于ε、δ和n的显式表达式。

Result: 计算得到的指数在σ=2d/3时还原为长程高斯标度（long-range Gaussian scaling），在σ→2极限下还原为短程量子Wilson-Fisher标度（SR quantum Wilson-Fisher scaling），从而在受控的3-ε展开中确定σ_*=2为LR-SR边界。

Conclusion: 结合RG结果、标度边界（scaling boundaries）和经典长程类比，本文提出了铁磁长程量子O(n)临界性的(d,σ)普适性图，并用作组织长程量子自旋链相图的框架。

Abstract: Experimental progress in quantum simulators highlights the role of long-range (LR) interactions in reshaping quantum criticality and stabilizing exotic phases beyond the short-range (SR) paradigm. We study ferromagnetic long-range quantum $O(n)$ models with interactions decaying as $1/r^{d+σ}$ and develop a perturbative renormalization-group expansion around the LR--SR boundary by setting $d=3-ε$ and $σ=2-δ$. In this parametrization, the full interacting LR window $2d/3<σ<2$ becomes $0<δ<2ε/3$, and is therefore perturbatively controlled. A two-loop calculation yields explicit expressions, in terms of $ε$, $δ$, and $n$, for the correlation-length exponent $ν$ and for the frequency and momentum anomalous dimensions $η_ω$ and $η_k$. The resulting exponents reduce to long-range Gaussian scaling at $σ=2d/3$ and to SR quantum Wilson-Fisher scaling in the $σ\to 2$ limit, thereby identifying $σ_*=2$ as the LR--SR boundary within the controlled $3-ε$ expansion. Combining the RG results with scaling boundaries and classical LR analogies, we propose a $(d,σ)$ universality diagram for ferromagnetic long-range quantum $O(n)$ criticality and use it as an organizing framework for the phase diagram of long-range quantum spin chains.

Abstract: Detailed balance underlies conventional Markov-chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) algorithms. Here we show that irreversibility provides a new route to improving the recent quantum-enhanced MCMC (QEMC), which combines quantum proposals with classical acceptance. ### [191] [Thermodynamic inference from noisy single-molecule time series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23619)
*Todd R. Gingrich,Oleg A. Igoshin,Anatoly B. Kolomeisky,Dmitrii E. Makarov*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本论文系统研究了有限时空分辨率对从微观轨迹中辨识和量化时间箭头（arrow of time）能力的影响，证明噪声退化观测会导致熵产生（entropy production）估计的下界，并揭示时空分辨率之间存在非平凡相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单分子或单粒子追踪测量本质上会产生带噪声的微观轨迹，这些轨迹常受到衍射极限（diffraction limit）和光子发射计数速率的显著限制。本文旨在系统研究有限空间和时间分辨率对从微观轨迹中辨识和量化时间箭头能力的影响。

Method: 给定一个被噪声退化的实验时间序列 Y(t)，本文考虑两种估计对应微观变量 X(t) 熵产生的策略：第一种策略先尝试从 Y(t) 推断 X(t) 的统计性质，再估计熵产生；第二种策略直接将实验可观测量 Y(t) 作为真实微观观测量的代理，将熵产生估计器直接应用于 Y(t)。

Result: 本文证明两种策略都会得到真实熵产生的下界（lower bounds）。噪声退化的可观测量 Y(t) 即使 X(t) 是马尔可夫过程（Markovian），也会呈现非马尔可夫动力学（non-Markovian dynamics），此时非马尔可夫熵产生估计器具有优势。此外，时空分辨率之间存在非平凡相互作用：在存在探测噪声的情况下，仅提高时间分辨率可能导致熵产生估计变差而非变好。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了有限时空分辨率对微观不可逆性量化的重要影响，指出了噪声退化和非马尔可夫效应对熵产生估计的关键作用，并强调提高时间分辨率并不总是改善估计效果。

Abstract: Single-molecule or single-particle tracking measurements inherently yield noisy microscopic trajectories, often significantly constrained by the diffraction limit and by the finite rate at which photons are emitted and counted. Here we study systematically the resulting effects of finite spatial and temporal resolution on one's ability to discern and quantify the arrow of time in microscopic trajectories. Given an experimental time series Y(t) degraded by noise, we consider the problem of estimating the entropy production associated with the corresponding microscopic variable X(t) using two strategies. The first attempts to infer the statistical properties of X(t) from those of Y(t) before estimating the entropy production. The second uses the experimental observable as a proxy for the true microscopic observable, with the entropy production estimator applied directly to Y(t). We prove that both strategies result in lower bounds on the true entropy production. Importantly, noise-degraded observables Y(t) undergo non-Markovian dynamics even when X(t) are Markovian, and non-Markovian entropy production estimators are advantageous. We further note nontrivial interplay between spatial and temporal resolution: in the presence of detection noise, improving the temporal resolution alone may lead to poorer rather than better entropy production estimates.

</details>


### [192] [Effective hyperuniformity in time-integrated stochastic Turing patterns](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23677)
*Anirban Mukherjee,Hong-Yan Shih*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本论文证明，确定性稳定的反应-扩散系统（reaction-diffusion systems）中，由人口噪声（demographic noise）可产生随机图灵斑图（stochastic Turing patterns），并通过对Levin-Segel模型的分析与数值验证，揭示了该机制下涌现的大尺度组织行为，最终发现一种无需精细调谐的有效超均匀（hyperuniform）新态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统图灵斑图理论通常要求反应-扩散系统在确定性意义上处于失稳状态；本文旨在探索在确定性稳定条件下，仅靠内在的人口噪声（demographic noise）能否驱动系统形成有序的大尺度斑图，并刻画其统计特征。

Method: 采用解析推导与数值模拟相结合的方法，以Levin-Segel模型为研究对象，通过对构型的时间积分（temporal integration of configurations）来分析系统的空间组织；同时利用窗口大小为R的密集数方差（intensive number variance）这一统计量来刻画标度行为。

Result: 在确定性稳定的参数区域内，人口噪声仍能诱导出随机图灵斑图（stochastic Turing patterns）。当窗口大小R >> 1时，密集数方差以1/R的标度律趋近于一个有限的反应动力学下限（reaction-kinetic floor），且该标度行为在空间尺度上跨越多个数量级，持续增长直至接近图灵失稳点。

Conclusion: 该结果揭示了一种此前在非守恒多物种随机系统（non-conserved multispecies stochastic systems）中未被识别的有效超均匀（hyperuniform）态，且该态无需精细调谐参数即可出现，为噪声驱动的斑图形成提供了一种全新的理论框架。

Abstract: Demographic noise generates stochastic Turing patterns even when reaction-diffusion systems are deterministically stable. We show analytically and verify numerically in the Levin-Segel model that temporal integration of configurations reveals emergent large-scale organization. The intensive number variance in a window of size $R \gg 1$ approaches a finite reaction-kinetic floor as $1/R$, over a spatial range growing by orders of magnitude near the Turing instability. This yields an effectively hyperuniform, fine-tuning-free regime previously unidentified in non-conserved multispecies stochastic systems.

### [193] [Two stages of magnetic filament formation in the solar convective zone](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20992)
*Evgeny Kuznetsov,Evgeny Mikhailov,Vlada Khvoshchinskaia*

Main category: astro-ph.SR

TL;DR: 本文综述了太阳对流区（solar convection zone）中磁丝（magnetic filament）形成的两阶段过程：第一阶段中，磁场在对流胞边界的双曲区域（hyperbolic regions）被冻结并聚集；第二阶段中，强磁场的压力梯度反作用于对流，使磁丝横向扩张直至磁能与动能密度相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解太阳对流区中磁丝的形成机制，对于揭示太阳磁活动（solar magnetic activity）的起源和演化具有重要意义。本文旨在通过综述已有的研究，区分并刻画磁丝形成与发展的两个不同阶段。

Method: 论文采用综述性分析方法，基于磁流体动力学（MHD）方程的运动学近似（kinematic approximation），并利用磁雷诺数（magnetic Reynolds number）约10^6的条件分析磁场冻结效应。通过对流胞边界双曲区域的流动行为以及自由边界（free boundary）上的磁场法向分量进行分析，推演磁丝的形成与饱和过程。

Result: 第一阶段中，磁丝在对流胞边界双曲区域形成，磁场可视为冻结（frozen-in）状态；磁场增长和饱和可通过分析自由边界（可近似为平面）上的磁场行为确定。第二阶段中，强磁场的压力梯度阻碍对流，使双曲区域沿自由表面移动，磁丝横向尺寸增大，直至磁能与动能密度相当。

Conclusion: 磁丝的形成不依赖于对流胞的内部结构，而由自由表面附近的对流行为决定。两个阶段的转变由磁场强度增长引发的动力学反馈驱动，最终达到磁能与动能之间的平衡。

Abstract: This paper presents a brief overview of studies of magnetic filament formation in the solar convection zone. Two stages of magnetic filament formation and development are distinguished. The first stage can be described within the kinematic approximation for the MHD equation, since the average kinetic energy of convective motion exceeds the average magnetic field energy. Moreover, magnetic Reynolds number is on the order of $10^6$. Therefore, at the initial stage of magnetic filament formation, the magnetic field can be considered frozen-in. It turns out that at this stage, magnetic filaments begin to form at the boundaries of convective cells in hyperbolic regions of the flow. These regions act as attractors for the magnetic field. At the free boundary of the convective zone near the interfaces between convective cells, the magnetic field has a predominantly normal component relative to the boundary. As the magnetic field increases, the field's frozen-in nature in the filament is disrupted, and saturation occurs due to finite conductivity. It is important to note that the magnetic field growth and saturation in the filament at this stage can be determined by analyzing the behavior of the magnetic field at the free boundary, which, according to observations, can be considered flat. Moreover, the formation of magnetic filaments is independent of the internal structure of the convective cells and is determined by the behavior of the convective flow along the free surface. In the next stage, when the magnetic field in the filament is sufficiently strong, the magnetic field pressure gradient begins to impede the convective flow, leading to a shift of the hyperbolic regions toward the convective flow along the free surface. As a result, the transverse size of the filament increases and stops when the kinetic energy density and the magnetic field energy density become comparable.

</details>
