### [194] [Partition function zeros of quantum many-body systems: perturbative results](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20808)
*Muhammad Sedik,B Sriram Shastry*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出并应用一种基于微扰论的系统方法，用于寻找量子多体系统的杨-李配分函数零点，并在一维哈伯德模型中验证了该方法，同时提出了实验探测方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找量子多体系统的杨-李配分函数零点（Yang-Lee partition function zeros）是一项重要但困难的任务，现有方法通常局限于小规模系统或精确解。本文旨在利用微扰论（perturbation theory）建立一种可推广的系统性方法，并探索其实验可探测性。

Method: 基于arXiv:2504.01880中提出的方法，通过有限温度微扰论获取依赖于波矢和温度的复数虚能量（complex virtual energies），该虚能量可从热电子格林函数（thermal electronic Green's function）导出。对所有波矢$\vec{k}$的虚能量进行收集得到杨-李零点。将该方法应用至一维哈伯德模型（one-dimensional Hubbard model），并考察不同边界条件。在微扰论展开至二阶后，结果与精确对角化（exact diagonalization）进行比较。此外，提出了一个用于实验探测哈伯德环（Hubbard ring）中这些零点的可观测量。

Result: 在微扰论二阶近似下，该方法得到的杨-李零点与精确对角化结果一致；通过8位点哈伯德环的精确对角化示例，展示了所提出的实验探测方法的可行性。

Conclusion: 基于微扰论的杨-李零点系统性方法在哈伯德模型中有效，且有望通过实验观测实现，为有限温度下量子多体系统的相变研究提供了新的分析工具。

Abstract: A systematic method to find the Yang-Lee partition function zeros of quantum many-body systems based on perturbation theory at finite temperatures was recently introduced in arXiv:2504.01880. This method identifies wave-vector and temperature-dependent complex virtual energies obtainable from the thermal electronic Greens function. The collection of virtual energies over all $\vec{k}$ yield the Yang-Lee zeroes. We apply this approach to the one-dimensional Hubbard model for different boundary conditions. We compare the results obtained by this method up to second-order in perturbation theory with the results found by exact diagonalization. We also propose a quantity that could be used for experimental detection of these zeros of a Hubbard ring. An example of the detection method is presented using exact diagonalization of the 8-site Hubbard ring.

</details>


### [195] [Displacement-Field-Driven Semimetal-Superconductor Transition in Magic-Angle Twisted Trilayer Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20849)
*Bokai Liang,Jing-Yu Zhao,Ya-Hui Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过奴隶粒子理论（slave-particle theory）研究魔角三层石墨烯（MATTG）在位移场调控下的电子行为，发现位移场的主要效应是诱导狄拉克锥能移和自掺杂，驱动从半金属（semimetal）到超导态（superconducting state）的转变，并解释了超导电性增强、莫特行为（Mottness）及重费米子（heavy-fermion-like）行为的统一图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 魔角三层石墨烯（MATTG）中存在丰富的位移场（displacement field, D）调控的关联现象，但位移场如何影响其电子结构及驱动量子相变尚不明确。传统重费米子（heavy fermion）图像因TBG Hubbard能带具有动量选择性（momentum-selective）的莫特隙（Mott gap），且在Γ点能隙很小，因此刚性局域磁矩描述（Kondo lattice model）不适用，亟需新的理论解释。

Method: 采用奴隶粒子理论（slave-particle theory）对MATTG在填充数ν=±2时的电子态进行具体计算，分析位移场D对狄拉克锥（Dirac cone）与扭转双层石墨烯（TBG）平带（flat band）杂化（hybridization）的影响。

Result: 位移场D的主要效应是诱导狄拉克锥能移（energy shift）并导致TBG扇区的自掺杂（self-doping）。增大D会驱动从半金属（semimetal）向超导态（superconducting state）的转变。在ν=±2附近，D可增强超导电性，且相图呈现粒子-空穴不对称性（particle-hole asymmetry）。

Conclusion: 研究结果提供了一个统一的图像，用以理解MATTG中电场可调超导电性（electric-field-tunable superconductivity）、莫特行为（Mottness）及类重费米子行为（heavy-fermion-like behavior）。

Abstract: Magic-angle twisted trilayer graphene(MATTG) hosts versatile displacement-field-tuned correlated phenomena. MATTG consists of a dispersive Dirac cone which hybridizes with the flat band from a twisted bilayer graphene (TBG) sector. The hybridization strength increases with the displacement field $D$ and naively one may expect D-driven heavy fermion physics. However, the TBG Hubbard bands have a momentum-selective Mott gap, which is small at the $Γ$ point due to the band topology, and a rigid local moment description as in the familiar Kondo lattice model is invalid. Here we show that the dominant effect of the displacement field is to induce an energy shift of the Dirac cone and self-doping into the TBG sector. We illustrate this picture in a concrete calculation using a slave-particle theory at the filling $ν=\pm 2$. We find that increasing $D$ drives a transition from a semimetal into a superconducting state. We also discuss the enhancement of the superconductivity by $D$ near $ν=\pm2$ and the particle-hole asymmetry of the phase diagram. Our results provide a unified picture for electric-field-tunable superconductivity, Mottness, and heavy-fermion-like behavior in MATTG.

### [196] [Importance of effective Coulomb interactions for $T_c$ in cuprates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21323)
*Jakša Vučičević,Upendra Kumar,Chia-Nan Yeh,Miguel A. Morales,Malte Rösner*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模系统性研究，结合数据收集、第一性原理计算（DFT）和统计分析方法，对约40种铜酸盐超导体的晶体结构参数与实验超导转变温度（T_c）之间的关联进行了全面分析，发现单带Hubbard模型中的次近邻跃迁参数t'以及三带Emery模型中氧p轨道上的库仑耦合强度与T_c存在显著相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铜酸盐超导体（cuprate superconductors）在常压下表现出最高的超导转变温度（superconducting T_c），但不同铜酸盐之间的T_c差异很大。目前尚不清楚晶体结构的哪些特性对T_c影响最强，而这种理解是指导高T_c材料设计的基础。

Method: 研究采用了大规模系统性方法，包括从文献和数据库中收集约40种铜酸盐化合物的T_c及晶体结构数据；利用全自动流程计算DFT能带结构（DFT bandstructure），并基于最大局域化Wannier函数（MLWFs）和约束随机相位近似（cRPA）方法，将能带下折叠（downfold）到两个常用低能晶格模型（单带Hubbard模型和三带Emery模型）上；最后进行彻底的、无偏的统计分析，探究实验T_c与模型计算参数之间的相关性。

Result: 数据分析表明，可能需要更复杂的模型才能统一描述所有铜酸盐体系。但研究发现T_c与模型参数的简单函数存在良好标度关系。研究确认了单带模型中次近邻跃迁参数t'与实验T_c的相关性趋势，并发现T_c在t'低于某个有限值时消失，这与近期Hubbard模型的基态计算结果一致。同时，在整个数据集中，T_c与三带模型中p轨道上的库仑耦合（Coulomb coupling）相关性最强，凸显了铜氧面中氧位点（oxygen sites）的重要性。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了铜酸盐超导体中晶体结构参数与T_c之间的定量关联，特别是氧p轨道库仑耦合对T_c的主导性影响，为理解高温超导机制和指导高T_c材料设计提供了关键线索。

Abstract: Cuprate superconductors exhibit the highest observed superconducting $T_c$ at atmospheric pressure. However, the magnitude of $T_c$ varies significantly between different cuprates. At present, it is unclear what properties of the crystal structure affect $T_c$ most strongly, yet such an understanding must underpin any efforts toward high-$T_c$ materials design. To address this issue, we perform a large scale systematic study, employing a combination of data collection, state-of-the-art numerical methods, and statistical analysis. We identify about 40 different cuprate compounds, and we compile detailed data about their $T_c$'s and crystal structures from literature and the available databases. Using a fully automated procedure, for each compound we compute the DFT bandstructure and downfold it to two of the most commonly studied low-energy lattice models, namely the single-band Hubbard and the three-band Emery models. The downfolding is based on the approach of MLWFs and cRPA. Finally, we apply a thorough and unbiased statistical analysis to investigate the correlations between the experimentally measured $T_c$'s and the computed parameters of our theoretical models. Our data indicates that more sophisticated models might be needed to describe all cuprates on the same footing. Nevertheless, we find that $T_c$ scales well with simple functions of model parameters. We confirm a previously observed trend that $t'$ in the single-band model correlates with the experimental $T_c$, and we find that $T_c$ appears to vanish below a finite value of $t'$, in agreement with recent ground-state calculations for the Hubbard model. However, we find that the coupling strength also plays a role: throughout our entire dataset, $T_c$ correlates the most with the Coulomb coupling on the $p$-orbitals in the 3-band model, highlighting the importance of the oxygen sites in the copper-oxide planes.

</details>


### [197] [Localization pattern of a mobile impurity in the disordered Kitaev chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21499)
*A. V. Sadovnikov,A. N. Rubtsov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 研究耦合到具有化学势无序的Kitaev链上的移动杂质，通过精确对角化（exact diagonalization）和密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）计算，发现杂质的局域化行为可以区分宿主系统的拓扑（topological）与平凡（trivial）相区，但两者之间不存在严格的——对应关系，仅存在间接关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨耦合到Kitaev链上的移动杂质（mobile impurity）是否能够区分宿主系统的不同相区（深拓扑区与深平凡区），从而为探测拓扑物质（topological matter）提供一种基于杂质响应的替代途径。

Method: 针对小周期链使用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）计算，针对强相互作用下的开放链使用密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）方法。从马约拉纳-二聚体（Majorana-dimer）结构出发进行解析解释，并引入化学势无序（chemical-potential disorder）进行扰动分析。

Result: 深拓扑区中杂质仅部分局域化，IPR_d平滑增长；深平凡区中杂质经历尖锐转变至近单点局域化。Kitaev sweet spot附近观察到边缘局域化杂质密度，随着化学势增加杂质权重扩散到体态并趋于均匀。马约拉纳-二聚体结构解释了边缘偏好：体态杂质重组两个相邻二聚体，边缘杂质仅影响一个。无序与清洁边缘偏差竞争，可将杂质钉扎在体态中。

Conclusion: 杂质对宿主系统的相区敏感，但其局域化模式与宿主拓扑之间不存在严格的——对应关系。无序平均行为仅表明杂质局域化与链的底层相之间仅存在间接关联（indirect correlation）。

Abstract: We study a mobile impurity coupled to a Kitaev chain with chemical-potential disorder and ask whether the impurity behavior distinguishes different regimes of the host system. Exact diagonalization calculations for small periodic chains shows that in the deep topological regime the impurity localizes only partially, with a smooth increase of $\mathrm{IPR}_d$, whereas in the deep trivial regime it undergoes a much sharp transition to nearly single-site localization. For open chains at strong interaction, DMRG shows edge-localized impurity density near the Kitaev sweet spot. With increasing chemical potential, the impurity weight spreads into the bulk and eventually becomes almost uniform. We explain the edge preference analytically from the Majorana-dimer structure: a bulk impurity rearranges two neighboring dimers, while an edge impurity affects only one. Disorder competes with this clean edge bias and can pin the impurity in the bulk. Thus, the impurity is sensitive to the regime of the host system, although we do not find a strict one-to-one correspondence between the impurity localization pattern and the host topology. Instead, the disorder-averaged behavior suggests only an indirect correlation between impurity localization and the underlying phase of the chain.

### [198] [Many-body quantum geometric effects and entanglement at the 3D metal-insulator quantum phase transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21648)
*Jason Y. Yan,Xiaoyu Guo,R. Bhandia,T. F. Rosenbaum,Natalia Drichko,N. P. Armitage*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过光学电导的第一个负矩（与量子Fisher信息成正比）作为实验探针，测量了磷掺杂硅中三维金属-绝缘体量子相变（quantum phase transition）的量子几何（quantum geometry）。提取的量子几何长度ℓ在远离相变时接近玻尔半径，在接近临界点时跳跃式地变为无穷大，反映了三维体系中求和规则的紫外主导特性，并为Herzfeld金属化判据提供了量子力学基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子几何（quantum geometry）已成为凝聚态物理中的一个统一概念，但其在多体无序相互作用体系中的实验探测仍面临挑战。该研究旨在寻找一种通过光学测量来实验探测量子几何的方法，特别是跨越三维金属-绝缘体量子相变（metal-insulator quantum phase transition）时的行为。

Method: 研究利用光学电导（optical conductivity）的第一个负矩作为实验探针，该量在零温下与量子Fisher信息（quantum Fisher information）成正比，从而作为多体纠缠（multipartite entanglement）的一个上界。通过提取量子几何长度ℓ来表征局域波函数，并对磷掺杂硅（phosphorus-doped silicon）样品进行实验测量。

Result: 远离相变时，量子几何长度ℓ几乎与磷施主的氢原子玻尔半径（Bohr radius）一致，反映了原子尺度的量子几何。接近临界点时，ℓ被增强但并不像关联长度（correlation length）那样连续发散，而是在临界点不连续地跳跃至无穷大。这种增强展示了施主极化率体积（polarizability volume）的“膨胀”（puffing），该膨胀具有量子几何起源。

Conclusion: 量子几何长度的增强行为反映了三维体系中求和规则（sum rule）的紫外主导特性，使其无法响应驱动介电常数和关联长度发散的临界涨落（critical fluctuations）。该结果提供了一个量子几何修正的Clausius-Mossotti描述，与发散介电响应更吻合，并为已有百年历史的Herzfeld金属化判据（Herzfeld metallization criterion）提供了量子力学基础。

Abstract: Quantum geometry has emerged as a unifying concept across condensed matter physics, underlying phenomena from nonlinear topological response to flat-band superconductivity. While usually formulated within band theory, quantum geometry remains meaningful in disordered interacting systems~\cite{resta1999electron}. Here we show that the first negative moment of the optical conductivity -- proportional to the zero temperature quantum Fisher information as a bound on the multipartite entanglement -- provides an experimental probe of quantum geometry across the three-dimensional metal-insulator quantum phase transition in phosphorus-doped silicon. We extract a quantum geometric length $\ell$ that characterizes the local wavefunctions. Far from the transition, this length is almost coincident with the Bohr radius of the hydrogenic phosphorus donors, reflecting their atomic-scale quantum geometry. Approaching the transition, $\ell$ is enhanced, but does not diverge continuously like a correlation length; it jumps discontinuously to infinity at the critical point. This reflects the UV domination of the sum rule in three dimensions that renders it insensitive to the critical fluctuations driving the diverging dielectric constant and correlation length. Its enhancement demonstrates a ``puffing" of the donor polarizability volume of quantum geometric origin, which yields a quantum geometric corrected Clausius-Mossotti description in closer agreement with the diverging dielectric response and provides a quantum mechanical foundation for the century-old Herzfeld metallization criterion.

</details>


### [199] [Trial wavefunction for fractional quantum spin Hall insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21652)
*Omri Lesser,Chao-Ming Jian*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文针对占据半填充共轭陈带的相反自旋费米子体系，提出了一个具有Z4拓扑序（Z_4 topological order）的分数量子自旋霍尔态（fractional quantum spin Hall state）的变分波函数（variational wavefunction），该波函数基于任意子激子凝聚（anyonic exciton condensation）机制，并通过蒙特卡罗（Monte Carlo）采样在球面几何上评估了其能量学，发现在参数空间中该态在较大区域内能量上优于其他竞争态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半填充共轭陈带（conjugate Chern bands）中的相反自旋费米子表现出与多分量朗道能级（multi-component Landau levels）截然不同的相互作用物理，原因在于不可避免的种间碰撞排除了Halperin型波函数的存在。因此需要构造新的变分波函数来描述这类体系中可能出现的分数量子自旋霍尔相。

Method: 基于解耦的一对Moore-Read Pfaffian态及其共轭态中的中性费米子激发形成的任意子激子（anyonic exciton）的凝聚来构建Z4拓扑序的变分波函数；通过耦合与两种自旋成分相关的手征和反手征Ising共形场论（conformal field theory），引入变分质量参数（variational mass parameter）以同时捕捉复合费米子（composite fermions）的种间s波配对和种内p波配对；采用蒙特卡罗采样在球面几何上评估能量，并显式计算由朗道能级混合（Landau-level mixing）导致的动能惩罚。

Result: 相图（phase diagram）表明，所提出的Z4态在参数空间的较大区域内能量上优于解耦的共轭Pfaffian态对以及另一种激子凝聚态（exciton condensate state），因此在能量上是有利的。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了Z4分数量子自旋霍尔相的具体微观波函数实现，并为构建更多此类态族提出了可行路径。

Abstract: Fermions with opposite spins occupying half-filled conjugate Chern bands exhibit interaction physics distinct from their multi-component Landau-level counterparts with the same chirality. This is largely due to unavoidable inter-species collisions that preclude the Halperin-type wavefunctions available in multi-component Landau levels. In this work, we propose and evaluate a variational wavefunction for a fractional quantum spin Hall state with Z_4 topological order in a pair of conjugate Landau levels. This Z_4 topological order has previously been shown to be the minimal topological order compatible with charge conservation, $S_z$ conservation, time-reversal symmetry, and the fractional spin Hall conductance 1/2 suggested by previous twisted MoTe$_2$ experiments. Our construction is based on the condensation of an anyonic exciton formed by the neutral fermionic excitations in a decoupled pair of Moore-Read Pfaffian state and its conjugate. By coupling the chiral and anti-chiral Ising conformal field theories associated with the two spin species, we introduce a variational mass parameter in the Z_4 trial wavefunction that captures the inter-spin-species s-wave pairing of composite fermions alongside the intra-spin-species p-wave pairing. We assess the energetics of this trial state using Monte Carlo sampling on a spherical geometry. Because the coupled state intrinsically involves Landau-level mixing, we explicitly evaluate the resulting kinetic energy penalty. Our phase diagram reveals that the proposed Z_4 state becomes energetically favorable in a sizable region of parameter space, over both the decoupled pair of conjugate Pfaffian states and an alternative exciton condensate state. These results provide a concrete microscopic wavefunction realization of this Z_4 fractional quantum spin Hall phase, and propose a route to constructing additional families of such states.

Conclusion: 该双合金体系能够在最小化无序影响的前提下精细调控晶体结构、基态和电子色散性质，为进一步理解Kagome晶格的性质及其新奇量子态和相互作用开辟了道路。

Abstract: Kagome lattice crystal systems present interesting symmetry-protected band structure features such as flat bands, van Hove singularities, and linearly dispersing Dirac/Weyl points that provide a rich playground for strongly correlated electron physics. Using a novel growth technique, the synthesis of high quality crystals with extended length along the crystallographic $c$-axis allows us to follow the gradual suppression of charge density wave (CDW) order with Y substitution, and observe quantum oscillations in both magnetoresistance and magnetization throughout the series. We review the evolution of Fermi surfaces, effective masses and quasiparticle dispersion through the alloy series, revealing a decrease in size of Fermi surfaces that trends with both substitutions, and a scaling between effective mass and Fermi wavevector that suggests a regime with Dirac-like dispersion. The ability to fine-tune crystallographic, ground state and electronic dispersion properties of the \lit\ system with minimal impact of disorder opens a path torward further understanding the nature of the kagome lattice and its novel states and interactions.

### [201] [Spectroscopic fingerprints of a ferroaxial charge density wave](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21872)
*Jiangchang Zheng,Zhongyi Zhang,Fazhi Yang,Josh Leeman,Luanjing Li,Zihan Lin,Zijian Fei,Tianhao Guo,Siyu Heng,Xin Liang,Leslie M. Schoop,Junzhang Ma,Hoi Chun Po,Berthold Jäck*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用线偏振角分辨光电子能谱（linearly polarized angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）和扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM）测量，并结合基于原子散射中心选择性沉积的准粒子干涉（quasiparticle interference, QPI）映射技术。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一种基于单个原子散射的光谱学方法，可利用STM和ARPES测量识别和表征量子材料中的隐藏多组分电子序。

Abstract: Unconventional charge density waves (CDWs) with complex order parameters can host exotic collective modes and non-trivial topologies. They have emerged as a new frontier in the study of quantum matter. Recent experiments on rare-earth tritellurides have reported evidence for a ferroaxial CDW through the detection of characteristic Raman modes. This phase, often regarded as a hidden order, has been recognized to arise from the coupling between charge and orbital degrees of freedom in these materials. Yet, spectroscopic insight into its underlying electronic structure and the explicit form of its order parameter symmetry has remained elusive. Here, we present results from linearly polarized angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES) and scanning tunneling microscopy (STM) measurements of the CDW phase in LaTe$_3$. Our ARPES measurements reveal a complex landscape of spectral gaps across the reconstructed Fermi surface, while our STM-based quasiparticle interference (QPI) mapping, enhanced through the selective deposition of atomic scattering centers, directly reveals an inter-orbital CDW with mixed $p_x$-$p_z$ orbital character. The detailed analysis of the QPI characteristics in terms of the order parameter symmetry within the orbital subspace of the Fermi surface suggests a mixed CDW phase with substantial ferroaxial component, which breaks all vertical mirror symmetries. More broadly, our work establishes a powerful spectroscopic pathway, based on scattering off individual atoms, for identifying and characterizing hidden, multi-component electronic orders in quantum materials using STM and ARPES measurements.

### [202] [Magneto-ionic control of topological transport in SrRuO3 via band topology engineering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21999)
*Xuanchi Zhou,Xiaohui Yao,Xiaomei Qiao,Guowei Zhou,Wenjing Huo,Shuang Li,Huihui Ji,Xiaohong Xu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用磁离子控制，在具有强自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）和巡游铁磁性（itinerant ferromagnetism）的4d轨道SrRuO₃体系中，通过可控的质子化（protonation）或氧空位（oxygen vacancy）掺入实现能带填充调控（band filling control），进而引起费米能级相对于能带避让交叉点（avoided band crossings）的上移。

Result: 实现了反常霍尔效应（AHE）极性的可调反转温度（reversal temperature）；通过广泛离子掺杂观察到可逆切换的驼峰状霍尔异常（hump like Hall anomalies），该现象与AHE极性无关，表明其来源于反演对称性破缺（broken inversion symmetry）驱动的拓扑霍尔效应（THE）信号，而非双通道AHE。

Conclusion: 研究为Berry曲率工程（Berry curvature engineering）提供了可行的调控手段，能够在强SOC铁磁体中实现拓扑输运的按需控制，从而推动低功耗、可重构的全氧化物自旋电子器件（all oxide spintronic devices）的发展。

Abstract: The interplay between spin-orbit coupling (SOC) and nontrivial band topology in ferromagnets gives rise to a rich landscape of topological transport phenomena such as anomalous Hall effect (AHE) and topological Hall effect (THE). One central goal in modern spintronics lies in the realization of the active control over topological transport phenomena in a reversible fashion, while unambiguously disentangling respective contributions of THE and AHE to the net Hall effect remains a formidable challenge. Here we establish magneto ionic control as a powerful paradigm for dynamically engineering topological transports in a 4d-orbital SrRuO3 system with sizable SOC and itinerant ferromagnetism. Harnessing controllable protonation or oxygen vacancy incorporation, the Fermi-level upshift relative to avoided band crossings are realized through band filling control, giving rise to tunable reversal temperature of AHE polarity. Of particular note is the emergence of hump like Hall anomalies through extensive ionic doping that can be reversibly switched, irrespective of AHE polarity, providing evidence for a THE signal driven by broken inversion symmetry rather than a two channel AHE. Our findings provide a viable tuning knob for Berry curvature engineering, enabling on demand control of topological transports in strong SOC ferromagnets for low power, reconfigurable all oxide spintronic devices.

### [203] [Emergent Andreev Reflection from a Lattice Duality Defect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23684)
*Atsushi Ueda,Tokiro Numasawa,Boris De Vos,Masataka Watanabe*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文证明，纯粹晶格对偶缺陷可以产生一种类似于安德烈夫反射（Andreev reflection）的电荷共轭边界条件，并通过马约拉纳表示中的平移缺陷将这一现象与手征费米子宇称缺陷、双通道近藤问题以及轴向U(1)_A对称性下的电荷翻转边界联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 安德烈夫反射通常被认为与超导界面绑定，本文旨在探索是否存在非超导的纯粹晶格机制也能实现类似的电荷共轭边界条件，从而将这一现象推广到更广泛的物理场景。

Method: 从横向场伊辛链（transverse-field Ising chain）的马约拉纳表示（Majorana representation）出发，构造了一个折叠晶格模型（folded lattice model），其中边界马约拉纳杂质实现交错马约拉纳链的单格点平移。在连续极限下，该平移转化为手征费米子宇称缺陷（chiral fermion-parity defect），导致左移马约拉纳模式翻转符号而右移模式不变。在折叠几何中重组成复合费米子后，该符号翻转即变为类似安德烈夫的边界条件。

Result: 该晶格公式为两通道近藤问题（two-channel Kondo problem）中Emery–Kivelson边界和Maldacena–Ludwig单极散射提供了微观解释，并将该边界识别为Kitaev链SPT相（Kitaev-chain SPT phase）与无能隙链之间的界面。此外，同一马约拉纳平移缺陷还实现了轴向U(1)_A对称性下的电荷翻转边界（charge-flip boundary）的晶格版本。

Conclusion: 晶格对偶缺陷可以产生与超导界面类似的电荷共轭边界条件，其根源在于马约拉纳模式的手征性符号翻转，这为理解多种强关联和拓扑系统中的边界现象提供了统一的微观框架。

Abstract: Andreev reflection converts an incoming fermion into an outgoing hole and is usually tied to a superconducting interface. We show that an analogous charge-conjugating boundary condition emerges from a purely lattice duality defect. Starting from a Majorana representation of the transverse-field Ising chain, we construct a folded lattice model in which a boundary Majorana impurity implements a one-site translation of a staggered Majorana chain. In the continuum, this translation becomes a chiral fermion-parity defect: it flips the sign of the only left-moving Majorana mode while leaving the right-moving mode unchanged. When the two Majorana modes are recombined into a complex fermion in the folded geometry, this sign flip becomes the Andreev-like boundary condition. Our lattice formulation gives a microscopic interpretation of the Emery--Kivelson boundary of the two-channel Kondo problem and of Maldacena--Ludwig monopole scattering, while identifying the boundary as the interface between a Kitaev-chain SPT phase and a gapless chain. The same Majorana translation defect also provides a lattice realization of an axial $U(1)_A$-symmetric charge-flip boundary.

Abstract: Multiple-$Q$ magnetism in itinerant electron systems enables complex spin crystals and noncoplanar textures even in centrosymmetric settings. Using simulated annealing, we obtain the field-dependent phase diagram and identify successive transitions among single-$Q$, double-$Q$, and multiple inequivalent quadruple-$Q$ states. Our results demonstrate that momentum-space frustration and biquadratic coupling provide an efficient route to stabilizing diverse quadruple-$Q$ spin crystals, offering a general framework for higher-order spin textures in centrosymmetric itinerant magnets.

### [205] [Van Hove Singularity and Phase Instability: Exploring the Role of Electron Correlation in the Magnetic Behavior of $\mathrm{Fe}_{16}\mathrm{N}_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22256)

Conclusion: van Hove 奇点这一拓扑异常与计算磁性质之间的关联揭示了该相亚稳态性（metastability）背后的电子机制，为理解 Fe₁₆N₂ 中关联驱动的磁行为提供了理论框架，并为优化其在实际应用中的稳定性和性能指明了路径。

We demonstrate that the electronic structure exhibits high sensitivity to these parameters, specifically uncovering a van Hove singularity near the Fermi level ($E_F$), inherently tied to the material's structural and thermal phase instability. By linking this topological anomaly to the calculated magnetic properties, we demonstrate that the selection of $U$ not only tunes $M_s$ and MCA energy towards experimental values but also reveals an underlying electronic mechanism potentially responsible for the phase's metastability. This provides a framework for understanding the correlation-driven magnetic behavior of $\mathrm{Fe}_{16}\mathrm{N}_2$ and offers a pathway for optimizing its stability and performance in practical applications.

*M. Manikandan,R. Mahendiran*

TL;DR: 本文通过微波快速合成（<1小时）制备了多晶SrRu1-xCoxO3（x=0, 0.05）和CaRuO3，研究了其磁学、磁电阻、热膨胀和磁致伸缩性质，发现SrRuO3在居里温度（TC=160 K）处呈现铁磁相变和负磁电阻，伴随因瓦效应（invar-like effect）和正磁体积效应（positive magnetovolume effect），而Co掺杂会削弱自发热膨胀并使低温磁致伸缩呈现各向异性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 快速合成钙钛矿型氧化物并探索其磁-结构耦合特性，特别是磁体积效应（magnetovolume effect）与RuO6八面体倾斜/旋转及Co掺杂自旋-轨道相互作用（spin-orbit interaction）之间的关联。

Method: 采用微波辐照（microwave irradiation）氧化物粉末法快速合成多晶样品，并利用磁学测量、磁电阻（magnetoresistance）、线性热膨胀（linear thermal expansion）和磁致伸缩（magnetostriction）等手段进行表征。

Result: 微波合成的SrRuO3在TC=160 K处出现铁磁转变、金属型电阻和负磁电阻，其性能与传统24小时加热合成的样品相当；低温下热膨胀从顺磁态的常规收缩转变为铁磁态的自发膨胀（因瓦效应）；外加磁场导致各向同性长度膨胀（正磁体积效应），体积磁致伸缩在10 K和50 kOe下为40 ppm，在TC附近达最大值60 ppm；Co掺杂（x=0.05）削弱了自发热膨胀，并在10 K时引入各向异性磁致伸缩，但80 K以上恢复各向同性。

Conclusion: SrRu1-xCoxO3中的磁体积效应与RuO6八面体的稳健倾斜/旋转（tilting/rotation）和掺杂Co2+离子的自旋-轨道相互作用之间的竞争有关。

Abstract: Polycrystalline SrRu1-xCoxO3 (x = 0.0, 0.05) and CaRuO3 were rapidly synthesized (< 1 hour) by microwave irradiation of oxide powders, and their magnetic, magnetoresistance, thermal expansion, and magnetostriction properties were investigated. The microwave-synthesised SrRuO3 exhibits a ferromagnetic transition at TC = 160 K, metallic-type resistivity, and negative magnetoresistance, with magnitudes comparable to those of a sample synthesized by conventional heating over 24 hours. Upon lowering the temperature from 300 K, the linear thermal expansion shows a transition from the usual contraction in the paramagnetic state to spontaneous expansion in the ferromagnetic state (invar-like effect). The application of an external magnetic field at a fixed temperature results in isotropic expansion of the length, implying a positive magnetovolume effect. The volume magnetostriction is 40 ppm at 10 K in a magnetic field of 50 kOe, and it reaches a maximum value of 60 ppm close to TC. The spontaneous thermal expansion is diminished in SrRu0.95Co0.05O3. While the magnetostriction is anisotropic at 10 K, the isotropic behaviour is recovered above 80 K, and the maximum value of the positive magnetovolume is comparable to that of the parent compound. Our results suggest that the magnetovolume effect in SrRu1-xCoxO3 is related to competition between robust tilting/rotation of RuO6 octahedra and spin-orbit interaction of the doped Co2+ ions

</details>


### [207] [Evolution of anisotropic magnetostriction in LaMn1-xCoxO3 (x= 0.1-0.9)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22268)
*M. Manikandan,R. Mahendiran*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 通过微波辐照法合成了 LaMn1-xCoxO3 系列多晶样品（x=0.1-0.9），系统研究了其磁性与磁致伸缩性质。结果表明各组分中磁致伸缩以各向异性晶格畸变为主导，x=0.5 时各向异性磁致伸缩最大（1221 ppm），归因于高自旋 Co2+ 离子及其轨道磁矩的最大贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用微波辐照（microwave irradiation）氧化物前驱体法合成多晶样品；测量平行（l_par）和垂直（l_per）于磁场的磁致伸缩，估算各向异性磁致伸缩（l_anis）与体积磁致伸缩（l_vol）。

Conclusion: x=0.5 处最大各向异性磁致伸缩归因于高自旋 Co2+ 离子（high-spin Co2+）及其非零轨道磁矩（orbital moment）的最大占比；Mn3+/4+ 或 Co3+ 离子作用较小。磁致伸缩的组分依赖性源于结构、Mn 和 Co 离子价态及磁相互作用的变化。

Abstract: Polycrystalline samples of LaMn1-xCoxO3 series over a wide compositional range (x = 0.1 - 0.9) were synthesized by microwave irradiation of oxide precursors and their magnetic and magnetostrictive properties were investigated. Magnetostrictions parallel (l_par) and perpendicular (l_per) to the applied magnetic field were measured to estimate anisotropic(l_anis) and volume magnetostrictions(l_vol). In all the compositions, l-par (l_per) is negative (positive) and (l_anis) >> (l_vol), suggesting dominance of anisotropic lattice distortion under a magnetic field. The value of l_anis at 10 K for H = 50 kOe initially increases with x from 178 ppm for x = 0.1 to a maximum of 1221 ppm at x = 0.5 before decreasing for higher x. The composition dependence of magnetostriction is asymmetric about x = 0.5, the decrease for x > 0.5 is more steeper than for x < 0.5 whereas saturation magnetization decreases monotonically with increasing x except for an abrupt change at x = 0.6. The largest anisotropic magnetostriction observed for x = 0.5 is attributed to the presence of high-spin Co2+ ions with a non-zero orbital moment in the maximum fraction whereas Mn3+/4+ or Co3+ ions play minor roles. The composition dependence of magnetostriction is suggested to arise from changes in the structure, valence states of Mn and Co ions and magnetic interactions among them.

Method: 利用自旋-费米子对应（spin-fermion correspondence）在对称点将模型映射到锯齿格点（zigzag lattice）上的横场Ising模型（transverse field Ising model），并结合数值模拟分析含时可观测量的动力学行为。

Abstract: We study the peculiar dynamics of the Kitaev chain induced by nearest-neighbor (NN) interaction. We show that a strong NN interaction suppresses single-particle hopping but enhances pairing, resulting in a Wannier-Stark ladder. Based on the spin-fermion correspondence at the symmetry point, the model maps to a transverse field Ising model on a zigzag lattice, providing a clear physical picture and guiding experimental verification. The Wannier-Stark state corresponds to a localized domain wall between ferromagnetic and antiferromagnetic phases. It exhibits Bloch oscillation even in the absence of a longitudinal field, in contrast to previous works. Numerical simulations of time-dependent observables verify these conclusions. Our findings provide an example demonstrating emergent Stark many-body localization.

### [209] [Neural Polaron: Learning Quasiparticle Operators in Quantum Many-Body Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22644)
*Shang-Shun Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出一种神经极化子拟设（neural polaron ansatz），通过神经多体算符（neural many-body operator）作用于相关基态来表征准粒子激发（quasiparticle excitations），从而将神经量子态（neural quantum states）从基态性质扩展至动力学响应。在方形晶格 $J_1$-$J_2$ 海森堡模型（Heisenberg model）上的基准测试表明，该方法能准确再现从弱阻挫到强阻挫范围内的磁振子色散（magnon dispersions）和谱权重（spectral weights），特别是捕捉到了 $(π,0)$ 反常（anomaly）及其随 $J_2/J_1$ 增大而渐进软化（progressive softening）的非平庸多体特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解量子多体系统（quantum many-body systems）的动力学性质是一个核心挑战，因为激发（excitations）通常需要超越基态波函数（ground-state wave function）的信息。现有方法难以高效且物理透明地刻画激发态。

Method: 方法引入神经极化子拟设，它不是独立学习一个激发态波函数，而是通过一个定义在预训练基态网络特征图（feature map）上的紧凑神经头（compact neural head），参数化一个局域缀饰算符（local dressing operator）。该基于算符（operator-based）的构造内嵌了平移对称性（translation symmetry）、动量分辨（momentum resolution）和准粒子局域性（quasiparticle locality），同时将基态关联（ground-state correlations）与激发特异性缀饰（excitation-specific dressing）分离开来。

Result: 在方形晶格 $J_1$-$J_2$ 海森堡模型上的基准测试显示，该方法在宽泛的阻挫（frustration）范围内准确再现了磁振子色散和谱权重。特别地，它成功捕捉了 $(π,0)$ 反常及其随 $J_2/J_1$ 增大而渐进软化的非平庸多体特征。

Conclusion: 这些结果确立了神经算符（neural operators）作为一种物理透明的途径，可将神经量子态从基态性质扩展至动力学响应。

Abstract: Understanding dynamical properties of quantum many-body systems remains a central challenge because excitations generally require information beyond a ground-state wave function. Here we introduce a neural polaron ansatz that represents quasiparticle excitations by neural many-body operators acting on a correlated ground state. Instead of learning an independent excited-state wave function, the method parameterizes a local dressing operator through a compact neural head defined on the feature map of a pretrained ground-state network. This operator-based construction builds in translation symmetry, momentum resolution, and quasiparticle locality, while separating ground-state correlations from excitation-specific dressing. We benchmark the method on the square-lattice $J_1$-$J_2$ Heisenberg model, where it accurately reproduces magnon dispersions and spectral weights over a broad range of frustration. In particular, it captures nontrivial many-body features including the $(π,0)$ anomaly and its progressive softening with increasing $J_2/J_1$. These results establish neural operators as a physically transparent route for extending neural quantum states from ground-state properties to dynamical response.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对FeTe薄膜施加拉伸应变，实现对体系电子结构的精确调控，避免化学掺杂带来的杂质干扰；结合角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）测量电子能带结构。

Conclusion: 研究结果强调了外延应变（epitaxial strain）与FeTe中电子结构演化之间存在直接关联，为理解强关联电子体系中的轨道选择性及其应变调控提供了新视角。

Abstract: Iron chalcogenides exhibit rich phenomena which are governed by orbital-dependent electronic interactions and strong electronic correlation. In particular, many studies have explored orbital selectivity in FeTe through Se doping. Here, applying tensile strain to thin films allows us to precisely control the system without other impurities that may arise from chemical doping to investigate the emergent behaviors in FeTe. Using angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, we observe a spectral weight transfer between $d_{\rm xy}$ and $d_{\rm z^{2}}$ orbitals, evidence of an orbital-selective Mott phase (OSMP). Beyond OSMP, we reveal hitherto unobserved strain-induced effects, distinct from chemical doping. The evolution of $d_{\rm xz}$ orbital demonstrates how electron hopping mechanism plays an important role in defining the electronic properties of the system. Our findings highlight a direct correlation between epitaxial strain and the evolution of electronic structures in FeTe.

### [211] [Isometrization of Tensor Network States via Gauge Propagation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22816)
*Zhiyu Jiang,Hiroshi Ueda*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种规范传播（gauge propagation）方法，可将通用张量网络态（tensor-network state）近似转换为具有指定正交中心（orthogonality center）的等距张量网络态（isometric tensor-network state, isoTNS）。一维情形下传播精确，高维网络中则通过结构化近似处理局部不可分残余因子；通过增加保留项或扩大局域簇可逐步降低误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维张量网络中的规范传播面临局部步骤存在多个出射方向，残余因子不可分离为单键（single-bond）独立贡献的阻碍，需要一种近似策略来构建等距形式以支持后续算法。

Method: 将局部张量或收缩后的局域簇（local cluster）近似分解为等距因子与出射支路（output-leg）因子张量积的结构化项；等距因子保留在原位，出射支路因子沿传播方向吸收到相邻张量中。可通过增加保留项数量或扩大局域簇规模实现精细化。

Result: 随机张量及Kitaev自旋液体（Kitaev spin liquid）的环气张量表示（loop-gas tensor representation）上的基准测试显示，该精细化策略同时降低了局部残差（local residual）与累积传播误差。环气张量中两个结构化项即可将局部残差降至数值精度；将局域对象从2入2出（2-in-2-out）扩大至4入2出及6入2出簇，可同时降低局域截断误差与有限六角格点规范传播中的累积误差。

Conclusion: 传播兼容的局域分解（propagation-compatible local decomposition）是近似等距化（approximate isometrization）的有效构建模块，并可作为变分等距张量网络态算法（variational isoTNS algorithms）的初始化器（initializer）或预处理器（preconditioner）。

Abstract: We introduce a gauge-propagation approach for approximately converting generic tensor-network states into an isometric tensor-network state form with a prescribed orthogonality center. In one dimension, this propagation is exact because the non-isometric factor produced by a QR or singular-value decomposition is supported on a single virtual bond. In higher-dimensional networks, however, a local step can have several outgoing directions, and the residual factor is generally not separable into independent single-bond contributions. We address this local obstruction by approximating a local tensor, or a contracted local cluster, by structured terms consisting of an isometric factor multiplied by a tensor product of output-leg factors. The isometric factor is retained at the current site or cluster, while the output-leg factors are absorbed into neighboring tensors along the propagation directions. This construction provides a local truncation criterion for gauge propagation and a practical route to refinement by increasing the number of retained terms or enlarging the local cluster. Benchmarks on random tensors and on the loop-gas tensor representation of the Kitaev spin liquid show that this refinement reduces both local residuals and accumulated propagation errors. For the loop-gas tensor, two structured terms reduce the local residual to numerical precision, and enlarging the local object from 2-in-2-out to 4-in-2-out and 6-in-2-out clusters lowers both local truncation errors and accumulated errors in finite honeycomb gauge propagation. These results identify propagation-compatible local decomposition as a useful building block for approximate isometrization and as a potential initializer or preconditioner for variational isoTNS algorithms.

</details>


### [212] [Spiral spin liquid resilient to quantization in the frustrated honeycomb antiferromagnet GdZnPO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23007)
*Xun Chen,Rui Bian,Yuqian Zhao,Haijun Liao,Weiqiang Yu,Yi Cui,Yuesheng Li*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用核磁共振（NMR）技术研究了自旋-7/2 蜂窝状反铁磁体 GdZnPO，发现其在中间磁场区域（~3 T 至 ~12 T）表现出无对称性破缺的自旋液体（spin-liquid）行为，而在低磁场（< 3 T）下则出现弱条状序（stripe order）并伴随强涨落，证明高自旋阻挫磁体可实现自旋液体现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阻挫磁体中的强量子涨落可能抑制传统磁有序并产生自旋液体等新奇量子相，但对于高自旋体系（如自旋-7/2）中自旋液体是否可能存在尚不清楚。GdZnPO 近期被提出为一种螺旋自旋液体（spiral spin-liquid）候选材料，但缺乏直接的微观磁性和自旋动力学实验证据。

Method: 利用核磁共振（nuclear magnetic resonance, NMR）技术，通过测量局域磁化强度（local magnetization）和自旋动力学（spin dynamics），在不同外磁场和温度（低至 0.033 K）条件下研究 GdZnPO 的磁态演化。

Result: 在 ~3 T 至饱和场（~12 T）的中间磁场区间，观察到空间均匀的磁化强度和持续的低能自旋动力学，温度低至 0.033 K 时未检测到对称性破缺，证实存在自旋液体态。在低于 ~3 T 的磁场下，温度低于 ~0.25 K 时出现弱条状序，但自旋-晶格弛豫率（spin-lattice relaxation rate）在低温极限下几乎与温度无关且异常大，表明强涨落仍然存在。

Conclusion: 自旋-7/2 量子化仅微弱地解除螺旋态的简并，稳定了微弱的磁有序，同时保留了强动力学和自旋液体现象学。GdZnPO 为在可达到的最低温度下探索高自旋阻挫磁体中的自旋液体提供了有前景的平台。

Abstract: Frustrated magnets host strong quantum fluctuations that can suppress conventional magnetic order and give rise to exotic quantum phases such as spin liquids. In some cases, however, quantum fluctuations lift classical degeneracies and stabilize ordered states via an order-by-quantum-disorder mechanism. The spin-7/2 honeycomb antiferromagnet GdZnPO has recently been proposed as a spiral spin-liquid candidate arising from cooperative fluctuations among a subextensively degenerate manifold of spiral states. Here, we investigate the local magnetization and spin dynamics in GdZnPO using nuclear magnetic resonance. In an intermediate field regime between $\sim$3 T and the saturation field ($\sim$12 T), we observe a spatially uniform magnetization and persistent low-energy spin dynamics down to 0.033 K, with no detectable symmetry breaking, providing spectroscopic evidence for a spin-liquid state. At lower fields below $\sim$3 T, a weak stripe order emerges below $\sim$0.25 K; however, strong fluctuations persist, as indicated by a nearly temperature-independent and unusually large spin-lattice relaxation rate in the low-temperature limit. Our results demonstrate that spin-7/2 quantization weakly lifts the spiral degeneracy, stabilizing subtle magnetic order while preserving robust dynamics and spin-liquid phenomenology. These findings establish GdZnPO as a promising platform for exploring spin liquids in high-spin frustrated magnets down to the lowest accessible temperatures.

### [213] [Angular-time evolution and edge-spin dynamics in the Haldane phase of the S=1 bilinear-biquadratic chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23117)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究由纠缠哈密顿量（entanglement Hamiltonian）生成的参数时间演化——角时间演化（angular-time evolution）在自旋系统基态中的动力学行为，及其与纠缠谱对称性（$\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2$）和边缘自旋动力学的关联。

Method: 采用矩阵乘积态（matrix-product-state, MPS）表示基态波函数，计算Haldane相中的角时间自旋关联函数（angular-time spin correlation functions）$\langle S_n^{α}(τ)S_{n'}^{α}(0)\rangle$；进一步对系统部分施加均匀磁场（uniform magnetic field），计算有效边缘自旋动力学（effective edge-spin dynamics），并通过比较子体系尺寸依赖的振幅来检验其与主导角时间模式的一致性。

Result: 在Haldane相中，角时间自旋关联函数的主导振荡模式可归因于与$\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2$对称性相关的纠缠谱的准二重简并性；系统部分在均匀磁场下的边缘自旋动力学与主导角时间模式之间存在精确对应关系。

Conclusion: 本文数值验证了在磁场作用下，系统部分的实际边缘自旋动力学与主导角时间模式之间的对应关系，通过精确比较两者的子体系尺寸依赖行为，确认了纠缠谱（entanglement spectrum）的准二重简并性（nearly two-fold degeneracy）作为该现象的微观起源。

Abstract: We investigate the angular-time evolution -- a parameter-time evolution generated by the entanglement Hamiltonian -- for the bipartitioned ground state of the S=1 bilinear-biquadratic chain under the open boundary condition with the up edge spin. Using a matrix-product-state representation of the ground-state wavefunction, we calculate the angular-time spin correlation functions $\langle S_n^{α}(τ)S_{n'}^{α}(0)\rangle$ in the Haldane phase, and extract its dominant oscillation mode attributed to the nearly two-fold-degenerate entanglement spectrum associated with the $\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry. We also compute the effective edge-spin dynamics under a uniform magnetic field applied to the system part and numerically verify its correspondence to the dominant angular-time mode by precisely comparing the subsystem-size dependence of their amplitudes.

</details>


### [214] [Wess-Zumino terms in 0+1 SU(N) superspin systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23234)
*J. S. Morales,M. N. Kiselev*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文系统介绍了量子系统中具有SU(N)对称性的Wess-Zumino（WZ）项，从SU(2)自旋相干态路径积分出发，通过几何与拓扑视角阐明WZ项与Berry相位、第一陈类等概念的关联，并扩展到SU(N)团簇（superspin）相干态构造及其在凝聚态物理中的应用，涵盖SU(N)海森堡模型、SU(4)自旋-轨道系统、多极交换作用等。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在具有SU(N)对称性的量子系统中，WZ项（Wess-Zumino term）是连接几何、拓扑与凝聚态物理应用的关键结构，但缺乏一个从基础到前沿的自包含（self-contained）导引。本文旨在填补这一空白，系统阐述WZ项的几何起源、拓扑分类及其在更高SU(N)对称性系统中的具体构造与物理实现。

Method: 首先从SU(2)自旋相干态路径积分（spin coherent-state path integral）入手，将Berry相位（Berry phase）解释为WZ项，该WZ项编码了Bloch球面（Bloch sphere）的辛结构（symplectic structure）。随后建立其与积分上同调类（integral cohomology classes）及Berry曲率（Berry curvature）作为第一陈类（first Chern class）的几何对应。进一步扩展到0+1维SU(N)超自旋（superspin）相干态构造，将相空间（phase space）识别为复射影空间CP^{N-1}，并显式导出SU(3)和SU(4)的局域WZ项。附录提供多极生成元基（multipolar generator bases）和SU(4)参数化等代数字典。

Result: 给出了SU(2)自旋系统中WZ项与Berry相位的几何对应关系；建立了WZ项与积分上同调类、第一陈类之间的严格联系；讨论了其在磁量子点（magnetic quantum dots）中绝热Berry相位和几何量子噪声（geometric quantum noise）等物理实现；针对SU(N)海森堡模型（Heisenberg models）、SU(4)自旋-轨道系统（spin-orbital systems）、自旋-赝自旋系统（spin-pseudospin systems）、多极交换作用（multipolar exchange interactions）及高阶自旋多极序（higher-spin multipolar orders）等凝聚态系统提供了理论框架；导出了SU(3)和SU(4)的超自旋相干态局域WZ显式表达式。

Conclusion: WZ项是理解具有SU(N)对称性量子系统中拓扑项与几何相位的基础工具，通过超自旋相干态路径积分方法可以系统地将SU(2)的几何结构推广到更高对称性系统，为凝聚态物理中多轨道、多自旋自由度系统中的拓扑效应研究提供了统一的理论语言和计算方法。

Abstract: These notes present a self-contained introduction to Wess-Zumino (WZ) terms in quantum systems with $SU(N)$ symmetry, emphasizing the interplay between geometry, topology, and condensed-matter applications. We begin with the $SU(2)$ spin coherent-state path integral, where the Berry phase appears as a WZ term encoding the symplectic structure of the Bloch sphere. This example is then used to introduce the geometric origin of topological terms, their relation to integral cohomology classes, and the role of Berry curvature as the first Chern class of the canonical $U(1)$ bundle. We next discuss physical realizations in which such geometric terms affect dynamics, including adiabatic Berry phases and geometric quantum noise in magnetic quantum dots. A substantial part of the notes is devoted to the condensed-matter motivation for higher $SU(N)$ symmetries, covering $SU(N)$ Heisenberg models, $SU(4)$ spin-orbital and spin-pseudospin systems, multipolar exchange interactions, and higher-spin multipolar orders. Finally, we develop the 0+1-dimensional $SU(N)$ superspin coherent-state construction, identify the phase space with $CP^{N-1}$, and derive explicit local WZ terms for $SU(3)$ and $SU(4)$. The appendices provide algebraic dictionaries connecting the abstract superspin language with concrete physical embeddings, including multipolar generator bases and several useful $SU(4)$ parametrizations.

</details>


### [215] [Signatures of unconventional magnetism in the layered metallic ferromagnet LaCrSb$_3$ from ferromagnetic resonance spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23413)
*J. J. Abraham,S. Samanta,R. Kolay,V. Singh,R. Nath,B. Büchner,V. Kataev,A. Alfonsov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过变温X射线衍射、静态磁化、电子自旋共振（ESR）和铁磁共振（FMR）实验，系统研究了层状金属铁磁体LaCrSb₃的电子与磁性质，发现强磁弹耦合、远超居里温度（T_C ≈ 126 K）的准静态短程关联，以及双磁性子格子的FMR模式，验证了正交铁磁/反铁磁子格子相互作用模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开展了变温X射线衍射（temperature-dependent x-ray diffraction）、静态磁化测量，以及在宽频率、磁场和温度范围内的电子自旋共振（electron spin resonance, ESR）和铁磁共振（ferromagnetic resonance, FMR）实验。

Result: X射线数据未发现低至15 K的结构相变，但在铁磁转变温度T_C ≈ 126 K附近检测到强磁弹耦合（magneto-elastic coupling）。ESR结果表明远高于T_C的温度下仍存在准静态短程关联（quasi-static short-range correlations），这是低维磁性（low-dimensional magnetism）的典型特征。T_C以下的FMR频率-场图强烈表明存在两个磁性子格子（magnetic sublattices）。基于正交铁磁与反铁磁子格子相互作用的现象学模型定量解释了FMR激发。

Conclusion: FMR结果证实了此前中子衍射提出的正交铁磁/反铁磁子格子共存模型，能够解释LaCrSb₃中异常强烈的自旋倾斜。这为进一步发展该材料非常规磁性的微观理论模型提供了实验依据。

Abstract: LaCrSb$_{3}$ is a metallic ferromagnet with a layered crystal structure demonstrating intriguing electronic and magnetic properties, such as large anomalous Hall effect, strong canting of the spin lattice, and a peculiar spin-reorientation transition. Here, we report the results of the temperature-dependent x-ray diffraction, static magnetization, and in particular electron spin resonance (ESR) and ferromagnetic resonance (FMR) experiments carried out over a wide range of frequencies, magnetic fields, and temperatures. Though x-ray data reveals no structural transition down to 15 K, a strong magneto-elastic coupling is detected across the ferromagnetic transition at $T_{\rm C} \simeq 126$ K. ESR results indicate a presence of the quasi-static short-range correlations extending far above $T_{\rm C}$, which is a typical fingerprint of the low-dimensional magnetism. The frequency-field diagram of the FMR modes mapped below $T_{\rm C}$ strongly suggests presence of two magnetic sublattices in LaCrSb$_{3}$. A quantitative understanding of the FMR excitations was achieved within a phenomenological model of interacting orthogonal ferro- and antiferromagnetic sublattices which was earlier proposed to explain unusually strong spin canting observed by neutron diffraction [E.~Granado et al., Phys. Rev. Lett. 89, 107204 (2002)]. The FMR results corroborate this scenario and call for the development of the underlying microscopic model of unconventional magnetism in LaCrSb$_{3}$.

### [216] [Resolving support-mismatch by local basis rotation in variational Monte Carlo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23657)
*Jia-Lin Chen,Zhen Fan,Canhui Yan,Yantao Wu,Tao Xiang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文针对变分蒙特卡洛（variational Monte Carlo）计算中，由带电局域算符（charged local operator）引发的支撑失配（support mismatch）问题，提出了一种局域基旋转采样方案（local basis-rotation sampling scheme）。该方案通过在局域层面旋转采样基来恢复缺失的支撑，无需改变潜在的变分动力学。基准测试表明，该方法能准确捕获长时间量子动力学，实现一维动力学结构因子和二维局域算符淬火动力学的无偏计算，并有望推广至基态变分蒙特卡洛计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 带电局域算符引发的局域淬火（local quench）后的实时动力学编码了光谱实验中的响应函数，但变分蒙特卡洛计算长期受困于此。核心障碍在于支撑失配：带电局域算符的投影作用导致指数级多的构型在采样中消失，而这些构型本应对动力学有贡献，从而导致估计量偏置并冻结演化。

Method: 提出局域基旋转采样方案，通过对采样基进行局域旋转来恢复缺失的支撑。该方案不改变底层变分动力学，可便捷地集成到现有变分蒙特卡洛算法中。

Result: 基准测试表明，旋转采样能准确捕获长时间量子动力学；实现了一维动力学结构因子（dynamical structure factor）的计算以及二维无偏局域算符淬火动力学（local-operator quench dynamics）的计算。

Conclusion: 支撑失配问题的解决不局限于实时动力学，还可能有助于基态变分蒙特卡洛计算。

Abstract: Real-time dynamics after a local quench by a charged operator encodes the response functions measured in spectroscopic experiments, yet they have long posed a challenge for variational Monte Carlo calculations. The obstacle is a support mismatch: the projective action by a charged local operator forces an exponentially large number of configurations to vanish, but these configurations may still contribute to the dynamics, biasing the estimators and freezing the evolution at the very first step. This difficulty is an artifact of the chosen sampling basis, and the support mismatch generated by a charged local operator is itself local. We demonstrate that the missing support can be restored by a local rotation of the sampling basis, without changing the underlying variational dynamics. We propose a local basis-rotation sampling scheme that resolves the support-mismatch problem and can be readily incorporated into existing variational Monte Carlo algorithms. Benchmarks show that rotation sampling accurately captures long-time quantum dynamics, enabling variational Monte Carlo calculations of dynamical structure factors in one dimension and unbiased local-operator quench dynamics in two dimensions. We also show that this resolution of the support-mismatch problem extends beyond real-time dynamics, and may also be helpful for ground state variational Monte Carlo calculations.

</details>

### [217] [Boosting lattice polarization Mixing the perspectives of geometry optimization and cell-augmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20782)
*Pegah Azizi,Rahul Dev Kundu,Xiaojia Shelly Zhang,Stefano Gonella*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出基于拓扑优化（topology optimization, TO）设计拓扑极化力学超材料（topologically polarized mechanical metamaterials）的框架，利用频带与模态形态属性驱动优化算法，突破理想麦克斯韦晶格（Maxwell lattices）的设计限制，发现了基于增广kagome几何的新麦克斯韦桁架（Maxwell trusses）家族，并通过理论与实验验证了强极化特性的实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前仅有少数理想麦克斯韦晶格（Maxwell lattices）被证明具有拓扑极化（topological polarization）导致的边态（edge state）不对称局域化特性，但缺乏设计此类结构系统的系统化准则。本文旨在建立一套通用设计框架，以探索更广阔的几何设计空间。

Method: 利用拓扑优化（topology optimization, TO）框架，以能带（band）和模态（mode）的形态属性作为优化算法驱动力；对优化结果提取关键准则，确保极化对边缘形态扰动（perturbations of the edge morphology）的鲁棒性；通过优化生成格点结构反哺理想晶格设计，识别基于增广kagome几何的新麦克斯韦桁架（Maxwell trusses）家族。

Result: 实现了高达三阶边态失配（three-count edge state mismatch）的强极化特征；在理论、仿真与实验（包括激光测振波测量和水射流切割样品的静态测试）之间取得一致。

Conclusion: 拓扑优化能够解锁超越经典晶格架构的几何自由度，为设计具有极端极化特性的力学超材料提供系统化方法；优化生成的格点结构可作为发现新型理想晶格构型的灵感来源。

Abstract: Topologically polarized mechanical metamaterials enjoy a special built-in asymmetry that manifests as a preferred localization of edge states on selected edges. While this property has been shown for a few ideal Maxwell lattices, we currently lack systematic criteria to design families of structural systems exhibiting polarization. Here, we propose a framework to design polarized structural configurations enabled by topology optimization (TO), using both band and mode morphological properties as drivers of the optimization algorithm. Through the lens of TO, we are able to tap into a vast design space, unlocking geometric freedom far beyond what is achievable with canonical lattice architectures. At the same time, we elucidate important criteria that need to be satisfied, beyond the optimization outcome, to ensure robustness of the achieved polarization against perturbations of the edge morphology. These results provide the inspiration to loop back into the realm of ideal lattices in search of new configurations characterized by extreme polarization. The peculiar shape and connectivity of the TO-generated lattice offer a blueprint for identifying a new family of Maxwell trusses based on augmented kagome geometry. We demonstrate the achievement of strong polarization signatures up to a three-count edge state mismatch. For all the cases studied, we show agreement between theory, simulations, and experiments, which include laser vibrometry wave measurements on a waterjet-cut specimen and static tests on a 3D-printed prototype.

</details>

Abstract: Magnetic materials with square-net sublattices are of great interest due to its potential to realize magnetic frustration. Here we report the crystal growth and structural, magnetic, thermodynamic and electronic transport properties of a new rare-earth-based intermetallic compound, Er3Pt2Sb4.55(5). The new material possesses a distorted square-net framework of Er. Magnetic properties measurements suggest anisotropic behavior, long-range antiferromagnetic ordering and metamagnetic transitions based on a Jeff = 1/2 Er3+ motif. A magnetic structure is proposed based on the observed magnetic and thermodynamic properties. ### [219] [Silicon Nanostructures for Biosensing: From Field-Effect Transistors to Photonic Resonators, and the Long Road to the Clinic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20902)
*Ang Liu,Jun Cao,Zhihao Sun,Jingsong Shang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文综述了硅纳米结构在生物传感器平台中的发展历程，涵盖离子敏感晶体管、纳米线场效应生物传感器、多孔硅膜、微环光子谐振器、悬臂梁、发光量子点和固态纳米孔等多种器件，并系统分析了各平台在临床转化中面临的关键瓶颈（如器件变异性、德拜屏蔽、污染、热漂移等），指出未来十年应聚焦于集成读出、界面工程和系统基准测试，而非发现新型硅纳米结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硅材料因其低成本、原子级平整的天然氧化物、CMOS兼容的制造工艺以及支持多种生物传感换能机制（transduction mechanism）的独特组合，一直是生物传感器平台的重要候选材料。尽管硅纳米结构生物传感器在实验室条件下展现出单分子、单病毒或亚飞摩尔级别的检测能力，但很少被广泛应用于临床检测，因此需要系统回顾和整理各平台的发展现状与瓶颈，以指导未来的研究方向。

Method: 本文采用综述方法，追溯硅生物传感器从早期到当前状态的发展历程，搜索并整理了文献中关于三种最成熟平台（纳米线BioFET、多孔硅、硅光子学）以及一组新兴方向的研究，并对不同平台的性能与瓶颈进行了总结和比较。

Result: 三种最成熟平台各自面临特定瓶颈：纳米线BioFET存在器件变异性和德拜屏蔽（Debye screening）；多孔硅面临污染（fouling）、孔润湿（pore wetting）和表面稳定性问题；硅光子学受限于热漂移（thermal drift）、光谱读取（spectral readout）和封装（packaging）挑战；所有平台共同面临校准（calibration）、可重复性（reproducibility）和真实生物体液中的验证（validation）难题。

Conclusion: 未来十年的进步将主要来自集成读出（integrated readout）、界面工程（interface engineering）和系统基准测试（systematic benchmarking），而非发现新型硅纳米结构。

Abstract: Silicon has a unique combination of properties that makes it one of the best material choices for biosensor platforms: it is inexpensive, its native oxide is atomically smooth, its fabrication processes are CMOS-compatible and have been refined for more than three decades, and it can support many transduction mechanisms in biosensor design. Over the past thirty years, researchers and engineers have used silicon nanostructures to produce ion-sensitive transistors, ultrasensitive nanowire field-effect biosensors, refractive-index-based porous silicon films, microring photonic resonators, suspended cantilevers, luminescent quantum dots, and solid-state nanopores. These device families have demonstrated successful sensing capabilities at the single-molecule, single-virus, or sub-femtomolar level under laboratory conditions; however, they have rarely been widely deployed in clinical assays. This gap is mainly caused by several well-characterized bottlenecks: for nanowire BioFETs, device variability and Debye screening; for porous silicon, fouling, pore wetting, and surface stability; for silicon photonics, thermal drift, spectral readout, and packaging; and across all platforms, calibration, reproducibility, and validation in real biofluids. In this review, we trace the development of silicon biosensors from their early stages to their current state, search and organize the literature focusing on the three most mature platforms and a set of emerging directions, summarize and compare the performance and bottlenecks of different platforms, and argue that progress over the next decade will come primarily from integrated readout, interface engineering, and systematic benchmarking rather than from the discovery of new silicon nanostructures.

### [220] [Persistent structural distortions and absent superconductivity in trilayer nickelate thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20941)
*Abigail Y. Jiang,Maria Bambrick-Santoyo,Lopa Bhatt,Kyeong-Yoon Baek,Yi-Feng Zhao,Dan Ferenc Segedin,Ari B. Turkiewicz,Jenna Hatmin,Grace A. Pan,Suchismita Sarker,Donald A. Walko,Charles M. Brooks,David A. Muller,Berit H. Goodge,Hua Zhou,Antia S. Botana,Julia A. Mundy*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过对n=3 La₄Ni₃O₁₀薄膜的原子级精确合成、输运测量、皮米级电子显微镜和同步辐射X射线衍射研究，发现尽管压应变抑制了密度波序，但即使在最大应变下也未观察到超导现象，识别出一种独特的结构畸变——围绕c轴的持久且层间不等价的八面体旋转——可能抑制了超导。结果表明n=3与n=2体系存在关键差异，n=3中环境压力超导可能需要超越外延应变工程的新方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期在n=2,3 Ruddlesden-Popper镍酸盐中发现高压诱导的超导现象，且压缩应变可在n=2相中实现环境压力超导，但类似应变稳定的超导在n=3相中尚未实现，因此需要探究n=3体系在应变下的行为及其与n=2体系的差异。

Method: 采用原子级精确合成（atomically-precise synthesis）、输运测量（transport）、皮米级电子显微镜（picoscale electron microscopy）和同步辐射X射线衍射（synchrotron X-ray diffraction）对n=3 La₄Ni₃O₁₀薄膜进行系统表征。

Result: 压缩应变虽能抑制密度波（density wave）序，但在最大应变状态下仍未观测到超导；识别出n=3应变薄膜中存在一种独特的结构畸变——围绕c轴的持久且层间不等价的八面体旋转（octahedral rotations），该畸变可能抑制超导。

Conclusion: n=3与n=2体系存在关键结构差异，n=3中实现环境压力超导可能需要采用超出外延应变工程（epitaxial strain engineering）范畴的新方法。

Abstract: A new family of high-temperature superconductors was recently discovered in the $n=2,3$ Ruddlesden-Popper nickelates, where superconductivity emerges concomitant with suppression of parent density waves and structural octahedral rotations under hydrostatic pressure. Intriguingly, compressive strain mimics the structural effects of pressure in the $n=2$ phase, yielding ambient-pressure superconductivity. However, analogous strain-stabilized superconductivity has not been realized in the $n=3$. Here, we use atomically-precise synthesis, transport, picoscale electron microscopy, and synchrotron X-ray diffraction to probe $n=3$ La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$ thin films. Although compressive strain suppresses density wave order, we do not observe superconductivity even under the largest strain state. Importantly, we identify a structural distortion unique to strained $n=3$ thin films that may inhibit superconductivity: persistent, layer-inequivalent octahedral rotations around the $c$-axis. Our results highlight key differences between the $n=3$ and $n=2$ systems, suggesting that ambient-pressure superconductivity in the $n=3$ may require new methods beyond epitaxial strain engineering.

### [221] [Deciphering Noise in tip--sample Interactions: Insights into Nanoscale Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20974)
*Jaime Colchero,Juan F. González-Martínez*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究揭示动态原子力显微镜（DAFM）中，针尖-样品相互作用在环境条件下会引入一种远超热涨落（thermal fluctuations）的非热噪声成分，该噪声源自纳米液颈（nanoscopic liquid necks）的随机形成与断裂，可作为局部润湿性与耗散动力学的光谱信号，并建议采用调频模式（FM-DAFM）进行解耦以实现高分辨率成像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上认为热涨落（thermal fluctuations）是动态原子力显微镜（DAFM）中限制分辨率和灵敏度的主要噪声来源，但环境条件下针尖-样品相互作用可能引入被忽略的额外噪声成分，其物理机制和潜在价值尚不明确，需要系统表征与解析。

Method: 以十二烷基硫酸钠（SDS）在石墨（graphite）上的体系为模型，综合运用力谱（force spectroscopy）、三维成像模式（3D imaging modes）以及开尔文探针力显微镜（KPFM）对噪声进行表征。

Result: 发现一种由纳米液颈（nanoscopic liquid necks）随机形成与断裂引发的非热噪声（non-thermal noise）成分，其强度显著超过热背景；该噪声通道（noise channel）提供的化学衬度（chemical contrast）与KPFM绘制的静电势（electrostatic potential）截然不同且互为补充。

Conclusion: 噪声并非单纯的仪器伪影（instrumental artifact），而是一种富含信息的信号，可直接反映局部润湿性（wettability）与耗散动力学（dissipative dynamics）；调频模式（FM-DAFM）能有效解耦这些耗散效应，为高分辨率成像提供更优方案。

Abstract: Noise sets the fundamental limits of resolution and sensitivity in Dynamic Atomic Force Microscopy (DAFM). While thermal fluctuations are conventionally assumed to be the dominant noise source, this work demonstrates that tip--sample interactions in ambient conditions introduce a non--thermal noise component that significantly exceeds the thermal background. Using a model system of sodium dodecyl sulfate (SDS) on graphite, we characterize this noise through force spectroscopy, 3D imaging modes, and Kelvin Probe Force Microscopy (KPFM). This interaction--induced noise arises from the stochastic formation and rupture of nanoscopic liquid necks, serving as a direct fingerprint of local wettability and dissipative dynamics. Crucially, we find that this ``noise channel'' provides chemical contrast that is distinct from and complementary to the electrostatic potential mapped by KPFM. By deciphering the physical origin of these fluctuations, we establish that noise is not merely an instrumental artifact but a rich spectroscopic signal, and we propose that Frequency Modulation (FM--DAFM) offers a superior approach to decouple these dissipative effects for high--resolution imaging.

### [222] [Quasi-1D Spin Textures: From Chiral Soliton Lattice to Fan State](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21034)
*M. Winter,A. Pignedoli,A. S. Sukhanov,M. Azhar,A. Tahn,B. Achinuq,J. R. Bollard,V. Ukleev,C. Luo,F. Radu,S. Wintz,M. Weigand,A. Mistonov,P. Vir,J. Geck,C. Felser,G. van der Laan,T. Hesjedal,K. Everschor-Sitte,B. Rellinghaus,M. C. Rahn*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 这篇论文报道了在手性磁体Mn₁.₄PtSn中，当磁场垂直于手性晶轴施加时，观察到从零场π-手性孤子晶格（π-chiral soliton lattice）转变为一个扇状态（fan-like state），其中自旋调制传播方向保持横向于磁场，调制长度随场增加而连续减小，最终趋近于场极化态。微磁模拟表明，有限样品中的静磁相互作用对这一行为的稳定起关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大多数螺旋磁体（helimagnets）中，外磁场会使螺旋自旋纹理的传播方向与磁场方向对齐，形成圆锥态（conical state），从而掩盖了螺旋解绕（unwinding）过程。本工作旨在通过各向异性手性磁体Mn₁.₄PtSn（其中晶体对称性约束了自旋调制的传播方向）来探索在外场垂直于调制方向时的互补物理行为。

Method: 使用矢量磁体（vector magnet）中的共振弹性X射线散射（resonant elastic X-ray scattering）技术，追踪沿手性晶轴（chiral crystallographic axis）传播的准一维自旋纹理在外磁场垂直于该方向时的演化，并结合微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulations）进行分析。

Result: 实验发现，系统从零场下的π-手性孤子晶格转变为一种扇状态，在该态中自旋调制的传播方向仍保持与磁场横向，但自旋围绕磁场方向振荡。随磁场增加，调制长度连续减小，最终趋向场极化态（field-polarized state）。模拟表明，有限样品中的静磁相互作用（magnetostatic interactions）对这一行为的稳定至关重要。

Conclusion: 本研究在手性磁体中提供了扇状态存在的实验证据，并凸显了通过调控磁场方向来控制一维自旋纹理（one-dimensional spin textures）的可能性。

Abstract: In most helimagnets, an applied magnetic field aligns the propagation direction of a helical spin texture with the field, resulting in a conical state and obscuring the unwinding process. Here, we access a complementary regime in the anisotropic chiral magnet Mn$_{1.4}$PtSn, where crystal symmetry constrains the propagation direction of the spin modulation. Using resonant elastic X-ray scattering in a vector magnet, we track the evolution of quasi-one-dimensional spin textures that propagate along a chiral crystallographic axis while the magnetic field is applied perpendicular to this direction. Together with micromagnetic simulations, our measurements reveal a transformation from the zero-field $π$-chiral soliton lattice into a fan-like state. In this state, the propagation direction remains transverse to the applied field, while the spins oscillate about the field direction. During magnetization, the modulation length decreases continuously with the field and approaches the field-polarized state. Simulations indicate that magnetostatic interactions in finite samples play a key role in stabilizing this behavior. Our results provide evidence for a fan-like regime in a chiral magnet and highlight how field orientation can be used to control one-dimensional spin textures.

### [223] [SALMON 2.3: Implementation of divide-and-conquer ground-state initialization for large-scale real-time TDDFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21125)
*Shunsuke Yamada,Tomohito Otobe*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文在开源第一性原理计算软件SALMON 2.3中实现了分治密度泛函理论（DC-DFT）方案，并与后续的实时、实空间含时密度泛函理论（real-time TDDFT）模块结合，通过线性标度的基态电子结构预处理解决了大规模实时TDDFT模拟中的计算瓶颈，在含数千原子的无序材料与液体系统中验证了该工作流的准确性与可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模实时含时密度泛函理论（real-time TDDFT）模拟中，基态电子结构的准备往往比后续的时间传播（time propagation）更为昂贵，成为制约具有数千个原子的实际系统（特别是无序材料、液体、纳米结构和异质凝聚态系统）中非平衡电子动力学模拟的主要瓶颈（bottleneck）。非线性与强场现象（如高次谐波产生和光致相变）需要显式的实时处理（explicit real-time treatment），这进一步凸显了预处理效率的重要性。

Method: 本文在开源第一性原理代码SALMON 2.3中实现了分治密度泛函理论（divide-and-conquer DFT, DC-DFT）方案，并结合后处理方法重建整个系统中空间延展的Kohn-Sham轨道（reconstructed global orbitals）。这些全局轨道直接作为初始状态输入到SALMON的标准实时、实空间TDDFT（real-time, real-space TDDFT）模块中，从而形成将高效DC-DFT基态准备与常规实时TDDFT连接起来的工作流（workflow）。

Result: DC-DFT的自洽场（self-consistent-field）过程表现出随系统大小线性标度（linear scaling）的特性。在Fugaku超级计算机上使用Si超胞进行的弱扩展性测试（weak-scaling test）确认了线性标度行为。针对含512个原子的非晶硅（amorphous Si）系统和含4134个原子的体相液态水（bulk H2O liquid）系统的精度测试表明，该工作流能够支持实用的大规模实时TDDFT模拟。

Conclusion: 该工作流通过DC-DFT实现了线性标度的基态预处理，有效解决了大规模电子动力学模拟中的主要瓶颈，同时保留了SALMON已有时间传播方案（time-propagation scheme）的鲁棒性和广泛适用性，使得包含数千个原子的实际系统的实时TDDFT模拟变得可行。

Abstract: In large-scale real-time time-dependent density functional theory (TDDFT), preparing the ground-state electronic structure can be more expensive than the subsequent time propagation, limiting simulations of nonequilibrium electron dynamics in realistic systems containing thousands of atoms. This bottleneck is especially important for disordered materials, liquids, nanostructures, and heterogeneous condensed-matter systems, where nonlinear and strong-field phenomena such as high-harmonic generation and light-induced phase transitions require explicit real-time treatment.
  SALMON is an open-source first-principles code for light-matter interaction simulations based on real-time TDDFT on real-space grids, supporting massively parallel calculations with MPI combined with OpenMP or GPU acceleration. In SALMON 2.3, we implement a divide-and-conquer density functional theory (DC-DFT) scheme and combine it with a postprocessing method that reconstructs spatially extended Kohn-Sham orbitals of the entire system. These reconstructed global orbitals are used directly as initial states for the standard real-time, real-space TDDFT module of SALMON.
  The resulting workflow connects efficient DC-DFT ground-state preparation to conventional real-time TDDFT. The DC-DFT self-consistent-field procedure exhibits linear scaling with system size, addressing a major bottleneck in large-scale electron-dynamics simulations while retaining the robustness and broad applicability of SALMON's established time-propagation scheme. We describe the computational procedure, parallelization strategy, and input/output design. Weak-scaling tests using Si supercells on Fugaku confirm the linear-scaling behavior. Accuracy tests for a 512-atom amorphous Si system and a bulk H2O liquid system containing 4134 atoms demonstrate that the workflow enables practical large-scale real-time TDDFT simulations.

Result: WO₂Cl₂在室温下呈现铁电性，W⁶⁺离子的非中心位移产生大偶极矩（约3 eÅ），宽带隙达2.80 eV；原子层次上直接观察到非共线偶极序（noncollinear dipole order）。

Here we experimentally demonstrate the room-temperature ferroelectricity of van der Waals WO$_2$Cl$_2$ . The well-tested d0 rule inherited from ferroelectric perovskites leads to a large dipole (~3 eÅ) from the off-center displacement of W$^6+$ ion and a wide bandgap of 2.80 eV. Its ferroelectricity is proved by multiple characterizations including second harmonic generation, piezoresponse force microscopy, and ferroelectric hysteresis loops. Our work paves an alternative route for low-dimensional ferroelectrics to pursue excellent ferroelectric performance and distinct physics of polarity.

### [225] [Atomistic Mechanisms of Hard Carbon Formation from Polyvinylidene Chloride](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21196)
*Litong Wu,Zitong Wu,Zakariya El-Machachi,Volker L. Deringer*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硬碳（hard carbon）作为一种广泛用于储能的无序材料，其原子尺度的形成机制（atomistic formation mechanism）长期难以阐明，主要原因在于原位实验表征（in situ experimental characterization）和第一性原理模拟（first-principles simulations）均面临巨大困难。

Method: 采用定制化的机器学习原子间势（machine-learned interatomic potential）模型，对聚偏二氯乙烯（polyvinylidene chloride, PVDC）的热分解过程进行第一性原理精度（first-principles-quality）的模拟。

Result: 模拟结果揭示了一个两阶段（two-stage）过程：第一阶段为自由基介导的脱氯化氢反应（radical-mediated dehydrochlorination），生成反应性不饱和碳位点；第二阶段为渐进式碳-碳交联（carbon-carbon cross-linking），随后通过热激活重排（thermally activated rearrangement）扩展为 sp² 键合网络。

Conclusion: 研究为热解过程中出现的非六元环结构（non-hexagonal ring motifs）提供了原子层面的描述，从而支持了经验理论——即这些结构单元诱导本征曲率（intrinsic curvature），进而阻碍硬碳中的石墨有序化（graphitic ordering）。

Abstract: Hard carbons are a class of disordered materials with widespread application in energy storage. Despite decades of research, their atomistic formation mechanisms have remained elusive, due to the difficulty of both in situ experimental characterization and first-principles simulations. Here, we describe the formation mechanism of hard carbon from the thermal decomposition of polyvinylidene chloride (PVDC), using first-principles-quality simulations with a bespoke machine-learned interatomic potential model. Our results indicate a two-stage process, consisting of (i) radical-mediated dehydrochlorination, which generates reactive unsaturated carbon sites, and (ii) progressive carbon-carbon cross-linking followed by thermally activated rearrangement into an extended sp$^{2}$-bonded network. We provide an atomistic account of non-hexagonal ring motifs emerging during pyrolysis, supporting the empirically-derived theory that these motifs induce the intrinsic curvature that frustrates graphitic ordering in hard carbons.

### [226] [Strain induced magnetic phase transitions in Fe3GeTe2 monolayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21266)
*Anjali Jyothi Bhasu,Satish Kumar,Mátyás Török,Dániel Tibor Pozsár,Bendegúz Nyári,László Udvardi,Gabriel Martínez-Carracedo,Balázs Nagyfalusi,Amador García-Fuente,Jaime Ferrer,Zoltán Tajkov,László Oroszlány,Levente Rózsa,László Szunyogh*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过第一性原理（first-principles）计算与原子自旋动力学（atomistic spin dynamics）模拟，研究了单层Fe₃GeTe₂中晶格常数对磁性的调控作用，发现压缩应变会增强反铁磁耦合、降低居里温度（Curie temperature），并诱导从铁磁态到锥形自旋螺旋态（conical spin-spiral state）的基态转变，揭示了晶格畸变在控制复杂磁性相及其温度演化中的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究单层Fe₃GeTe₂中磁性性质随晶格常数的变化规律，理解晶格畸变如何影响磁有序类型、相变温度及多磁性相之间的竞争关系。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算与原子自旋动力学模拟相结合的方法，计算磁交换相互作用（magnetic exchange interactions），并通过随机朗道-利夫希茨-吉尔伯特（stochastic Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert）模拟预测居里温度和磁基态变化。

Result: 发现铁磁与反铁磁耦合存在竞争，压缩应变显著增强反铁磁耦合；晶格常数减小导致居里温度大幅下降，基态从铁磁构型转变为锥形自旋螺旋态；引入简单自旋模型可解释螺旋相的稳定机制；观察到铁磁态、锥形自旋螺旋态和平面奈尔态（planar Neel state）等多种磁性相变；Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用的缺失显著降低奈尔温度（Neel temperature），但对居里温度影响不大。

Conclusion: 晶格畸变在调控单层Fe₃GeTe₂的复杂磁性相及温度演化中起关键作用，为利用应变工程控制二维磁性材料中的磁序提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We investigate the magnetic properties of a monolayer of Fe3GeTe2 as a function of the lattice constant by combining first-principles calculations with atomistic spin dynamics simulations. The calculated magnetic exchange interactions reveal a competition between ferromagnetic and antiferromagnetic couplings, with the latter being significantly strengthened under compressive strain. Stochastic Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert simulations reveal a substantial decrease in the Curie temperature with decreasing lattice constant, and predict a transition of the magnetic ground state from a ferromagnetic configuration to a conical spin-spiral state. We introduce a simple spin-model which explains the stabilization of the spiral phase due to competing exchange interactions. We found multiple magnetic phase transitions involving ferromagnetic, conical spin-spiral, and planar Neel states, depending on both the lattice constant and the temperature. The absence of Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interactions is found to significantly reduce the Neel temperature, while leaving the Curie temperature largely unaffected. Our findings reveal the importance of lattice distortions in controlling complex magnetic phases and their evolution with temperature.

</details>


### [227] [Floquet-induced anisotropic magnetoresistance and anomalous Hall effect in 2D $d$-wave altermagnets with Rashba spin-orbit coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21281)
*Mohsen Yarmohammadi,Pieter M. Gunnink,Jairo Sinova,James K. Freericks*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文证明了通过Floquet工程在二维d波交变磁体（altermagnet）中可实现平衡态下禁阻的输运响应，包括单色光驱动的纯面外磁化及双色光驱动同时产生的面内与面外磁化，并由此诱导出各向异性磁电阻和反常霍尔效应等输运现象。这些效应可通过光参数调控，所需等效静磁场高达数百特斯拉，远超出静态实验可达范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnet, AM）兼具动量依赖的自旋劈裂（momentum-dependent spin splitting）与净零磁化（zero net magnetization），在自旋电子学（spintronics）中具有重要潜力。然而，如何在不依赖材料特定静态特性的前提下动态调控其对称性并实现新奇的输运响应，仍是一个开放问题。本文旨在利用周期驱动（periodic driving）构成的Floquet工程（Floquet engineering）来突破这一限制。

Method: 理论分析了二维d波交变磁体（具有面外Néel序和Rashba自旋-轨道耦合（Rashba spin-orbit coupling））在外加单色或双色周期光驱动下的Floquet态；通过对比单色与双色驱动产生的不同磁化分量，研究了相应的各向异性磁电阻（anisotropic magnetoresistance, AMR）和反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect）等输运现象。

Result: 单色周期驱动仅产生纯面外磁化（out-of-plane magnetization），从而产生纵向各向异性磁电阻和反常霍尔效应。双色驱动则同时产生面内与面外磁化，并通过次级光束的二次谐波额外激活横向各向异性磁电阻（transverse AMR）。等效的静磁场需求高达数百特斯拉，而Floquet驱动避免了这一实验困难。上述效应在线偏振、圆偏振及混合偏振光下均稳定存在，且可通过光参数调节。

Conclusion: 研究建立了多色Floquet工程作为控制交变磁体中磁化和对称性保护输运（symmetry-protected transport）的有效方法，为动态操控自旋电子学器件中的输运行为提供了新的理论途径。

Abstract: Altermagnets (AMs) combine momentum-dependent spin splitting with zero net magnetization, making them promising for spintronics. Periodic driving enables dynamic symmetry engineering beyond static, material-specific control. We show that Floquet engineering in 2D $d$-wave AMs with out-of-plane Néel order and Rashba spin-orbit coupling unlocks equilibrium-forbidden transport responses. Monochromatic driving produces purely out-of-plane magnetization, yielding longitudinal anisotropic magnetoresistance (AMR) and an anomalous Hall effect, whereas bichromatic driving generates both in-plane and out-of-plane magnetizations and additionally activates transverse AMR via the second harmonic of the secondary beam. Comparable static magnetic fields would require hundreds of tesla, avoided in Floquet driving. These effects persist across linear, circular, and mixed light polarizations and are tunable via light parameters. Our results establish multi-color Floquet engineering for controlling magnetization and symmetry-protected transport in AMs.

*Chunmei Zhang,Jian Zhou,Liang Si*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用第一性原理密度泛函理论（density functional theory）、紧束缚建模（tight-binding modeling）和对称性分析（symmetry analysis）相结合的理论计算方法。

Conclusion: 自发面外体光伏效应广泛适用于多种二维钙钛矿及其他层状氧化物，为相关材料的光电应用提供了新的物理机制和调控途径。

Abstract: Perovskite oxides ABO$_3$ host a rich interplay of charge, spin, lattice, and orbital degrees of freedom, giving rise to diverse quantum phenomena. In low-dimensional ABO$_3$, reduced symmetry can induce exotic quantum effects such as the two-dimensional electron gas and unconventional superconductivity. Using first-principles density functional theory, tight-binding modeling, and symmetry analysis, we show that ultrathin two-dimensional (2D) ABO$_3$ films -- exemplified by SrTiO$_3$ -- naturally break inversion symmetry, producing a spontaneous out-of-plane bulk photovoltaic (BPV) effect. This differs from previous studies on in-plane BPV current signals and is more applicable and experimentally detectable. Such an effect is highly tunable via thickness, strain, surface termination, crystallographic orientation, and Moiré twisting. ### [229] [Machine learning metallic glass critical cooling rates through elemental and molecular simulation based featurization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21467)
*Lane E. Schultz,Benjamin Afflerbach,Paul M. Voyles,Dane Morgan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一个基于计算属性的机器学习模型，用于预测金属玻璃（metallic glasses）的临界冷却速率（critical cooling rates）。模型结合了源于元素性质的简单特征与基于从头算（ab initio）、机器学习势（machine-learning potentials）和经验势分子动力学（empirical potential molecular dynamics）的物理驱动特征。在20个化学体系的34种合金上，最佳模型由1个基于理想熵的元素性质特征和3个模拟特征（凸包以上能量、热容变化、二十面体类Voronoi多面体比例）构成。通过留出完整化学体系作为测试集的交叉验证，模型达到$R^2=0.78$，平均绝对误差为0.76（单位：$log_{10}(K/s)$）。Shapley加性解释分析显示，最具影响力的特征对模型预测具有物理合理的影响。该方法可推广至其他多样化成分材料性质的高通量研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金属玻璃的临界冷却速率是衡量其玻璃形成能力（glass-forming ability, GFA）的关键参数，但实验测定耗时且成本高昂。研究旨在建立一种基于计算属性的机器学习方法，能够高效、准确地预测不同合金体系的临界冷却速率，从而加速新材料的发现与设计。

Method: 研究对比了基于元素性质的简单特征（如合金化学计量比的理想熵）与通过从头算、机器学习势和经验势分子动力学模拟获得的物理驱动特征。针对20个化学体系的34种合金，采用留出完整化学体系作为测试集的交叉验证策略评估模型性能，并使用Shapley加性解释（Shapley additive explanation, SHAP）分析特征重要性。

Result: 最佳模型包含一个元素性质特征（基于合金化学计量比的理想熵）和三个模拟特征（凸包以上的能量、热容变化、二十面体类Voronoi多面体的比例），$R^2$达到0.78，平均绝对误差为0.76（单位：$log_{10}(K/s)$）。SHAP分析表明，最具影响力的特征对模型预测具有物理合理的影响。

Conclusion: 所建立的机器学习方法能够基于计算属性准确预测金属玻璃的临界冷却速率，且特征的物理合理性得到验证。该框架可推广至其他成分多样化材料性质的高通量研究，为计算驱动的新材料筛选提供了可行途径。

Abstract: We have developed a machine learning model for critical cooling rates for metallic glasses based on computational properties. We compare results for features derived from easy-to-compute functions of elemental properties to more complex physically motivated properties using ab initio, machine-learning potentials, and empirical potential molecular dynamics methods. The established approach enables property acquisition across a diverse range of alloys. Analysis of various features for 34 alloys from 20 chemical systems shows that the best model for critical cooling rates was learned from one elemental property-based feature and three simulated features. The elemental property-based feature is an ideal entropy value based on alloy stoichiometry. The simulated features were acquired from estimates of energies above the convex hull, changes in heat capacity, and the fraction of icosahedra-like Voronoi polyhedra. Models were assessed through a demanding cross validation test based on repeatedly leaving out full chemical systems as test sets and had an $R^2$ of 0.78 and a mean average error of 0.76 in units of $[log_{10}(K/s)]$. We demonstrate with Shapley additive explanation analysis that the most impactful features have physically reasonable influence on model predictions. The established methodology can be applied to other high-throughput studies of material properties of diverse compositions.

### [230] [Peripheral Nitrogen Topology as a Defect-Chemical Switch for Electronic and Magnetic States in Graphene: A First-Principles Study of Pyridinic, Pyridazinic, Pyrrolic, and Pyrazolic Configurations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21480)
*Md. Moktadir Billah Tahmid,Indranil Rudra,Jahid Emon,Mohammad Jane Alam Khan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺陷工程与杂原子工程虽已广泛用于调控石墨烯的电子和磁性质，但石墨烯空位周围特定外围氮拓扑（peripheral nitrogen topology）所起的作用尚不明确，因此有必要系统研究不同氮构型的影响。

Method: 采用自旋极化第一性原理计算（spin-polarized first-principles calculations），对四种杂环类外围氮构型——吡啶型（pyridinic）、哒嗪型（pyridazinic）、吡咯型（pyrrolic）和吡唑型（pyrazolic）——修饰的含中心空位石墨烯体系进行结构稳定性、电荷重分布、电子结构及磁响应的系统性分析。

Result: 吡啶型氮在四种构型中提供了最优的结构-能量平衡；键长分析表明氮拓扑强烈控制局部晶格重构；电荷密度、电荷密度差及Bader分析显示外围氮原子充当电子积累中心，重塑空位边缘的局部电子环境。自旋分辨能带结构表明，吡啶型、哒嗪型和吡咯型保持金属性或近金属性缺陷态特征，而吡唑型石墨烯则打开一个窄带隙。磁分析显示吡唑型石墨烯自旋补偿、净磁化为零，其余体系则具有有限的自旋极化磁矩；磁性源于氮调制的空位边缘态，涉及N 2p与邻近C 2p轨道。

Conclusion: 外围氮拓扑不仅是一个结构缺陷描述符，更是一个决定性的缺陷化学开关（defect-chemical switch），通过受控的空位边缘氮配位，可在石墨烯晶格中直接图案化出无金属的自旋电子与半导体功能域。

Abstract: Defect and heteroatom engineering offer powerful routes for tuning the electronic and magnetic properties of graphene, yet the role of specific peripheral nitrogen topologies around graphene voids remains insufficiently understood. Here, spin-polarized first-principles calculations were performed to investigate how four heterocyclic -- like peripheral nitrogen configurations -- pyridinic, pyridazinic, pyrrolic, and pyrazolic modify the structural stability, charge redistribution, electronic structure, and magnetic response of graphene containing a central void. Among the four peripheral N configurations, the pyridinic N provides the most favorable structural-energetic balance among the investigated motifs. Bond-length analysis reveals that nitrogen topology strongly controls local lattice reconstruction. Charge-density, charge-density-difference, and Bader analyses demonstrate that the peripheral N atoms act as electron-accumulating centers and reshape the local electronic environment around the vacancy rim. Spin-resolved band structures show that pyridinic, pyridazinic, and pyrrolic configurations retain metallic or near-metallic defect-state character, whereas pyrazolic graphene opens a narrow band gap. Magnetic analysis further reveals that pyrazolic graphene is spin-compensated, with zero net magnetization, unlike the other systems, which possess finite spin-polarized moments. Spin-density and SPDOS analyses indicate that the magnetism originates from N-modulated vacancy-edge states involving both N 2p and neighboring C 2p orbitals. These findings establish peripheral nitrogen topology not merely as a structural defect descriptor, but as a deterministic defect-chemical switch, offering a metal-free route to pattern active spintronic and semiconducting domains directly into the graphene lattice through controlled vacancy-edge nitrogen coordination.
