In principle, a foundation model for machine-learned interatomic potential (MLIP) can meet these demands. We explore the use of the Universal Models for Atoms (UMA) model, developed by Meta FAIR, for the interactions of oxygen plasma species on a multilayer of WS$_2$, a promising 2D material. Starting from the pretrained uma-s-1p1 model under the Open Catalyst 2020 (OC20) task, we apply an iterative fine-tuning loop with maximally diverse configuration sampling using Smooth Overlap of Atomic Positions (SOAP) and Farthest Point Sampling (FPS); DFT labeling at the PBE+D3+$U$+spin level; and fine-tuning on energy, force, and stress labels. Even in the absence of fine-tuning, the pretrained model reproduces the production-scale observables of interest, namely, chemisorbed S and O coverage under 15eV O$^+$ and O$_2^+$ bombardment. These results were obtained without spin polarization and Hubbard $U$ correction. Nonetheless, fine-tuning reduces the energy and force mean absolute error (MAE) to $4.5\times10^{-3}$eV/atom and $0.076$eV/angstrom, respectively.

We performed first-principles calculations to investigate the stability of isolated point defects in the vicinity of a vertical inversion domain wall (DW). ### [233] [The FAST Framework: Developing a Data-Efficient Machine Learning Potential to Decode Superionic Transition-Induced Thermophysical and Kinetic Anomalies in UO2 under Extreme Conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21796)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出“FAST”（Fine-tuning via Active-learning and Superionic-Targeting）框架，结合超离子转变目标采样（superionic transition-targeted sampling）与主动学习增强探索（active learning-enhanced exploration），仅用500个构型微调基础模型；在密度泛函理论（DFT）标注中严格考虑铀5f电子的强关联性和反铁磁（AFM）基态，训练得到DFT精度的神经进化势（NEP）。

Result: 该NEP在宽温区内对力学、缺陷、热物理及离子扩散等物理性质展现出卓越的预测能力，准确重现了超离子转变引发的线性热膨胀系数（LTEC）λ峰（λ-peak）和“非阿伦尼乌斯”（non-Arrhenius）阴离子扩散等反常行为。

Conclusion: 基于NEP的模拟阐明了这些反常现象的微观根源：氧亚晶格的预熔化（pre-melting）及其导致的U与O离子之间的动力学解耦（kinetic decoupling）。

Abstract: Uranium dioxide ($UO_2$) serves as the predominant nuclear fuel globally. Despite its widespread application, evaluating its mechanical, thermophysical, and species transport behaviors under extreme accident scenarios remains a formidable challenge for conventional experimental and computational methods. To address this, we develop a versatile machine learning interatomic potential (MLIP) for $UO_2$ by proposing an efficient training strategy, termed the "FAST" (Fine-tuning via Active-learning and Superionic-Targeting) framework. Our "FAST" framework integrates superionic transition-targeted sampling with active learning-enhanced exploration to efficiently construct a highly compact dataset comprising only 500 configurations for fine-tuning a foundation model. By rigorously accounting for the strong correlation of uranium 5f electrons and antiferromagnetic (AFM) ground state during DFT labeling, we train a robust DFT-level neuroevolution potential (NEP) for $UO_2$. We demonstrate that this NEP exhibits superior predictive capability for various physical properties, encompassing mechanical, defect, thermophysical, and ionic diffusion over an extensive temperature range. Moreover, this NEP accurately captures the anomalous thermophysical and kinetic behaviors triggered by superionic transition. Specifically, it reproduces both the $λ$-peak in linear thermal expansion coefficient (LTEC) and "non-Arrhenius" anionic diffusion. Crucially, NEP-based simulations elucidate the microscopic origins underlying these anomalies: the pre-melting of oxygen sublattice and resultant kinetic decoupling between U and O ions.

</details>

Method: 采用GW+BSE多体微扰理论（many-body perturbation theory）进行第一性原理计算。

Result: 同质双层MoS₂中存在由配准诱导的对称性破缺（registry-induced symmetry breaking）驱动的可开关层间偶极子；MoS₂/MoSe₂异质界面则因硫与硒之间的本征化学势失配（chemical potential mismatch）而被钉扎。在2L-MoS₂/MoSe₂三层结构中，堆叠顺序可实现对光生电子在中间层与底层MoS₂之间的确定性控制，准粒子带边偏移（quasiparticle band-edge shifts）为60–70 meV。计算预测的36 meV层间激子偏移（interlayer excitonic shift）与实验高度吻合。

Conclusion: 研究结果阐明了原子配准与多体相互作用的微观联系，确立了过渡金属硫族化合物三层结构作为滑动铁电体（sliding ferroelectricity）与可编程光电子功能平台的可行性。

Abstract: The stacking-dependent polarization and excitonic response of MoS$_2$/MoSe$_2$ heterostructures were investigated using GW+BSE many-body perturbation theory. While homobilayer MoS$_2$ exhibited a switchable interlayer dipole driven by registry-induced symmetry breaking, the MoS$_2$/MoSe$_2$ hetero-interface remained pinned by the intrinsic chemical potential mismatch between sulfur and selenium. In 2L-MoS$_2$/MoSe$_2$ trilayers, the stacking sequence enabled a deterministic control of photogenerated electrons between the central and bottom MoS$_2$ layers, governed by internal electric fields and quasiparticle band-edge shifts of 60--70~meV. Our calculations predicted a 36~meV interlayer excitonic shift, in remarkable agreement with recent experiments. These results elucidate the microscopic link between atomic registry and many-body interactions, establishing transition metal dichalcogenide trilayers as a potential platform for sliding ferroelectricity and programmable optoelectronic functionalities.

TL;DR: 本文提出利用本征滑移铁电性（sliding ferroelectricity）调控常规及反常自旋霍尔效应（spin Hall effect），在单层和双层1T'-WTe₂中实现了显著的反常自旋霍尔电导，并发现滑移铁电可逆切换自旋霍尔电导的符号与大小，从而实现无需外磁场的垂直磁化翻转，为自旋电子器件的非易失电控提供了新策略。

Conclusion: 揭示了滑移铁电性与自旋输运之间的强耦合关系，并提出了一种实现自旋电子器件非易失电控的新策略，为无外磁场条件下自旋轨道力矩器件的磁化翻转提供了可行途径。

Abstract: The spin Hall effect, recognized for its high-speed, low-power, and highly controllable characteristics, is a key enabler for next-generation memory and logic devices. However, a primary challenge lies in achieving 180$^{\circ}$ magnetization switching without an external magnetic field in spin-orbit torque devices. Here, we propose a method to tune the conventional and anomalous spin Hall effects by the intrinsic sliding ferroelectricity. Importantly, the anomalous spin Hall effect can enable the field-free switching of perpendicular magnetization. We find a substantial anomalous spin Hall conductivity of $σ_{xy}^{y}$ = 45.62 ($\hbar$/e)S/cm and $σ_{yx}^{y}$ = 56.84 ($\hbar$/e)S/cm in monolayer 1T'-WTe$_2$. More interestingly, the sliding ferroelectricity enables reversible switching of the signs and magnitudes for both the conventional and anomalous spin Hall conductivities. This originates from the fact that the sliding ferroelectric markedly shifts the relative spin Berry curvature contributions from the valence and conduction bands around the $Γ$-X path. Our findings not only reveal a strong coupling between sliding ferroelectricity and spin transport, but also propose a strategy for the nonvolatile electrical control of spintronic devices.

Abstract: Spin-split electronic structures in compensated antiferromagnets are commonly sought in the nonrelativistic limit, where magnetic order lifts spin degeneracy without spin-orbit coupling (SOC). Whether SOC can instead be the indispensable symmetry-breaking ingredient remains largely unexplored. Here we combine quantum oscillations detected by ultrahigh-sensitivity ac magnetostriction, magnetic-symmetry analysis and first-principles calculations to resolve the bulk Fermi-surface evolution of SmBi across two successive antiferromagnetic (AFM) transitions. New oscillation branches emerge below TN and undergo a further reconstruction below T*, whereas isostructural SmSb shows no comparable change. For the candidate noncollinear orders of SmBi, breaking global parity-time symmetry is insufficient in the nonrelativistic limit because residual spin-space symmetries protect twofold band degeneracy; conversely, SOC alone cannot lift the degeneracy of the centrosymmetric paramagnetic (PM) phase. Only the coexistence of noncollinear order and SOC locks spin to the lattice and removes the residual protection. SmBi therefore realizes a cooperative, relativistic route to spin-split Fermi surfaces, broadening unconventional magnetism beyond systems whose splitting is already present in the nonrelativistic limit.

Method: 方法包括三个关键组件：(i) 降维自编码器（autoencoder），用于对高分辨率微观结构图像（256×256×3）进行紧凑特征表示；(ii) 注意力增强的卷积长短期记忆网络（attention-augmented ConvLSTM），用于学习微观结构演化的复杂时空相关性；(iii) 逐切片（slice-by-slice）扩展策略，使模型能够处理三维系统（128×128×128×3）。此外，采用混合模拟策略，由PFM精确捕捉早期快速演化，DL模型高效预测后期粗化动力学。

Result: 训练后的DL模型实现了显著的预测精度，能够保持高达400个时间步（timesteps）的前向预测保真度，并泛化到训练分布之外的成分。研究还捕捉到了早期旋节线分解（spinodal decomposition）阶段在二维和三维中出现的三种不同的相分离机制（phase-separation mechanisms）。

Conclusion: 该框架通过桥接PFM的物理保真度与DL的计算效率，为复杂多组分系统中微观结构演化的预测建模建立了一个稳健的平台。

Abstract: We develop a hybrid framework that integrates a phase-field model (PFM) with an attention-enhanced deep learning (DL) architecture to study ternary spinodal dealloying, a sophisticated self-organization approach used to fabricate three-dimensional bicontinuous, hierarchical nanoporous materials. The study captures three distinct phase-separation mechanisms that emerge during the early stages of spinodal decomposition in both two and three dimensions. The DL workflow consists of three key components: (i) a dimensionality-reducing autoencoder that provides compact representations of high-resolution microstructure images (256x256x3), (ii) an attention-augmented convolutional long short-term memory (ConvLSTM) network that learns complex spatiotemporal correlations governing microstructure evolution, and (iii) a novel slice-by-slice strategy that enables extension of the model to three-dimensional systems (128x128x128x3). We further demonstrate a hybrid simulation strategy in which PFM accurately captures rapid early-stage microstructure evolution, while the DL model efficiently predicts late-stage coarsening dynamics. The trained DL model achieves remarkable predictive accuracy, maintaining fidelity up to 400 timesteps ahead and generalizing to compositions outside the training distribution. By bridging the physical fidelity of PFM with the computational efficiency of DL, this framework establishes a robust platform for predictive modeling of microstructure evolution in complex multicomponent systems.

### [240] [Reversible nonrelativistic magnon spin transport in ferroelastic altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22186)
*Haozhou Cai,Jian Wu,Weiyi Pan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于铁弹转变（ferroelastic transitions）的通用机制，可在二维交变磁体（altermagnets）中实现无磁场、非易失性的磁振子自旋输运主动操控，并通过第一性原理计算和自旋模型分析在CoTe2单层中验证了该机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁绝缘体中的磁振子（magnon）可实现低耗散、无杂散场的自旋输运，但实现非易失性、无外场的磁振子自旋流调控仍是一个难题。

Method: 基于对称性分析（symmetry analysis）提出铁弹转变调控磁振子自旋输运的通用机制；通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和自旋模型分析（spin-model analyses）对交变磁体CoTe2单层进行验证。

Result: 铁弹转变可有效重新取向主晶轴并调制磁交换各向异性，从而实现无需外磁场或贝里曲率（Berry curvature）即可铁弹可切换的非相对论性各向异性自旋输运，导致自旋塞贝克（spin Seebeck）和自旋能斯特（spin Nernst）电导率的符号反转。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一种基于对称性的磁弹性（magnetoelastic）范式，用于二维交变磁体中磁振子自旋输运的非易失性控制，为构建高能效、可重构的反铁磁磁振子器件开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Magnons in antiferromagnetic (AFM) insulators facilitate low-dissipation, stray-field-free spin transport. However, achieving nonvolatile, field-free control over magnon spin currents remains elusive. Here, based on symmetry analysis, we propose a universal mechanism for the active manipulation of magnon spin transport via ferroelastic transitions in two-dimensional (2D) altermagnets (AMs)-a class of unconventional AFMs simultaneously exhibiting compensated magnetization and nonrelativistic spin splitting. We show that these transitions effectively reorient principal crystal axes and modulate the underlying magnetic exchange anisotropy. Consequently, this magnetoelastic coupling drives nonrelativistic anisotropic spin transport that is ferroelastically switchable without the need for external magnetic fields or Berry curvature, leading to sign reversals in the spin Seebeck and spin Nernst conductivities. We validate this mechanism using first-principles calculations and spin-model analyses of an AM CoTe2 monolayer. Our findings establish a symmetry-based magnetoelastic paradigm for the nonvolatile control of magnon spin transport in 2D AMs, opening new avenues toward energy-efficient, reconfigurable AFM magnonic devices.

### [242] [A correlation of structural changes with nanomechanical properties in TiN-AlN multilayer films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22222)
*Nidhin George Mathews,Aidan A. Taylor,Johannes Zechner,Helmut Riedl,Paul H. Mayrhofer,Johann Michler,Vipin Chawla,Gaurav Mohanty*

TL;DR: 本研究探究了反应溅射沉积的TiN-AlN多层薄膜中，AlN层从立方岩盐（cubic rock salt）到六方纤锌矿（hexagonal wurtzite）的相变对整体纳米力学性能的影响。当AlN层厚度超过3 nm时发生相变，导致硬度降低、压痕模量下降，但3 nm AlN多层膜表现出最优的纳米划痕抗性，裂纹偏转带来部分延性破坏，表明立方到六方的相变有利于提高多层膜的损伤容限（damage tolerance）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用反应溅射（reactive sputtering）制备TiN-AlN多层膜，TiN层厚度固定为5 nm，AlN层厚度在1–5 nm之间变化；通过纳米压痕、微柱压缩（micropillar compression）和纳米划痕（nanoindentation scratch）测试表征力学性能。

Abstract: The present work investigates the changes in overall nanomechanical properties of reactively sputtered TiN-AlN multilayer films arising due to phase transformation in the AlN layers. Multilayered TiN-AlN films were sputter deposited with constant TiN layer thickness of 5 nm while the AlN layer thickness varied between 1-5 nm. The AlN underwent a phase transition from cubic rock salt to hexagonal wurtzite above 3 nm thickness due to the lattice strains. Micropillar compression of these multilayers showed a transition from columnar brittle to partially ductile failure associated with crack deflection with increasing AlN film thickness. The crack propagation behavior in scratching showed increased microcracking tendency towards higher AlN film thickness. This shows that cubic to hexagonal transformation in AlN is beneficial for improving the damage tolerance of the multilayer system.

### [243] [Open-quantum-system theory of non-Markovian electron-phonon dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22233)
*Gabriele Riva,Jacopo Simoni,Yuan Ping*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）开放量子动力学形式体系，基于四个耦合运动方程描述非平衡电子-声子相互作用，在保持能量守恒的同时避免了双时关联函数的存储，并在Holstein二聚体强外场问题中通过与精确解的对比验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的非平衡电子-声子相互作用的动力学描述存在局限：马尔可夫近似（Markovian approximation）忽略了记忆效应（memory effects），而非平衡格林函数（nonequilibrium Green's function）方法需要存储复杂的双时关联函数，计算代价高昂。因此，需要一种兼具物理准确性与计算可行性的动力学形式体系。

Method: 该方法基于一组闭合的四个耦合运动方程（equations of motion），分别描述电子单粒子约化密度矩阵（one-body reduced density matrix）、声子密度矩阵（phonon density matrix）、相干声子（coherent phonon）以及电子-声子关联（electron-phonon correlations）。系统通过外部含时场（external time-dependent field）驱动离开平衡态。电子动力学中的记忆效应自然地来源于电子密度矩阵与电子-声子关联方程之间的耦合，超越了马尔可夫近似。

Result: 该形式体系在适当极限下可恢复非平衡格林函数理论中的Fan-Migdal自能、随机相位近似（random-phase-approximation）下的极化自能以及Ehrenfest自能，也能还原Lindblad方程和玻尔兹曼方程（Boltzmann equation），同时避免了双时关联函数的存储。以Holstein二聚体（Holstein dimer）在强外场扰动下的精确解为基准，该非马尔可夫动力学正确捕获了耗散谱展宽（dissipative spectral broadening）和能量守恒。

Conclusion: 该形式体系将相干声子动力学（coherent-phonon dynamics）与耗散展宽（dissipative broadening）置于同等地位处理，特别适用于极化子形成（polaron formation）以及驱动电子激发有限寿命（finite lifetimes）问题的研究，为非平衡电子-声子相互作用的数值模拟提供了一种兼顾效率与准确性的理论框架。

Abstract: We present a non-Markovian open quantum dynamics formalism for the study of nonequilibrium electron-phonon interactions, based on a closed set of four coupled equations of motion for the electronic one-body reduced density matrix, the phonon density matrix, the coherent phonon, and the electron-phonon correlations. Memory effects in the electronic dynamics emerge naturally from the coupling between the electronic density matrix and the electron-phonon correlation equations, beyond the Markovian approximation. The formalism treats coherent-phonon dynamics and dissipative broadening on an equal footing, making it particularly suited to polaron formation and the finite lifetimes of driven electronic excitations. In appropriate limits it recovers the Fan-Migdal, polarization in random-phase-approximation, and Ehrenfest self-energies of nonequilibrium Green's function theory, as well as the Lindblad and Boltzmann equations, while avoiding the storage of two-time correlators. To drive the system out of equilibrium, we study its interaction with an external time-dependent field. As an illustrative application, we benchmark our theory against the exact solution of the Holstein dimer under a strong external perturbation, where the non-Markovian dynamics correctly captures dissipative spectral broadening and energy conservation.

</details>


### [244] [Fine-Tuned Machine-Learned Interatomic Potentials for Structural and Vibrational Properties of Twisted 2D Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22234)
*Viet-Anh Tran,Viet-Hung Nguyen,Wei Chen,Gian-Marco Rignanese,Jean-Christophe Charlier*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过微调通用原子基础模型（fine-tuning universal atomistic foundation models），开发了适用于扭转型范德华双层材料（twisted van der Waals bilayers）的机器学习原子间势（machine-learned interatomic potentials），并利用局部应变张量分析和声子能带展开技术，揭示了三种代表性材料（扭转型双层石墨烯、h-BN、MoS₂）中一致的弛豫诱导应变景观（reconstruction-induced strain landscape），其精度和效率均得到实验验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扭转型范德华双层材料形成的莫尔超晶格（moiré superlattice）的结构与振动性质对局部堆叠序列（local stacking registry）和原子重构程度高度敏感，但在小扭转角下，基于密度泛函理论（DFT）的原子尺度建模计算成本极高，亟需一种兼具精度和效率的计算方法。

Method: 本文以扭转型双层石墨烯、h-BN和MoS₂为代表性材料（覆盖从柔顺到刚性的力学响应范围），通过微调通用原子基础模型来构建机器学习原子间势；采用局部应变张量分析（local strain tensor analysis）和声子能带展开技术（phonon band unfolding technique）对重构后的原子结构和声子谱进行表征。

Result: 微调后的MACE模型在三种材料中一致地揭示出重构诱导的应变景观：扩展的低能堆叠畴（extended low-energy stacking domains）由狭窄的孤子线（soliton lines）分隔，变形集中于孤子线区域；系统在每个畴内逐步优化局部堆叠序列，形成空间结构化的变形场，其振幅随材料机械柔顺度（mechanical compliance）增大而增大，并可通过外部扰动进一步调节。重构原子结构和莫尔声子谱与实验报道吻合良好。

Conclusion: 广泛训练的原子基础模型无法分辨控制原子重构的微妙层间能量关系，微调通用原子基础模型是实现DFT精度层状材料建模的关键；本文提出的方法在大型纳米材料的建模中兼具准确性和计算效率。

Abstract: Twisted van der Waals bilayers form moiré superlattices whose structural and vibrational properties are highly sensitive to variations in local stacking registry and the degree of atomic reconstruction, yet accurate atomistic modeling of these systems at the DFT level remains computationally prohibitive at small twist angles. We investigate machine-learned interatomic potentials for moiré systems, using twisted bilayer graphene, \textit{h}-BN, and MoS$_2$ as representative materials spanning a broad spectrum of mechanical compliance and atomic reconstruction behavior. We show that fine-tuning universal atomistic foundation models is essential to achieve DFT accuracy for layered materials, as broadly trained foundation models prove insufficient for resolving the subtle interlayer energetics that govern atomic reconstruction. Through local strain tensor analysis and the phonon band unfolding technique, our fine-tuned MACE model reveals a consistent reconstruction-induced strain landscape in all three materials, with extended low-energy stacking domains separated by narrow soliton lines where deformation concentrates. The system progressively optimizes the local stacking registry within each domain, giving rise to a spatially structured deformation field whose amplitude scales with the mechanical compliance of the material and can be further tuned by external perturbation. The obtained results of both atomic reconstructed structures and moiré phonon spectra present a good agreement with the reported experiments, thereby demonstrating the accuracy and efficiency of our methodology in modeling of these large scale nanomaterials.

### [245] [Delafossites as an unexpected competing phase to infinite-layer oxides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22243)

Specifically, delafossites and their ordered rock-salt (111) variants stand out as intriguing layered oxides that share the infinite-layer $AB$O$_2$ stoichiometry and simultaneously retain a perovskite-like octahedral motif. This positions them as a unique structural bridge between these two phases and as promising candidates for novel correlated electronic states. We compile a phase diagram that compares the relative stability of these four distinct oxides across the periodic table. Surprisingly, we find that the delafossite structure rivals the infinite-layer phase in thermodynamic stability for the nickelates, and even more for the recently suggested palladate and platinate analogs. Among all candidates, the La-Ni combination stands out as a thermodynamic optimum for stabilizing the infinite-layer motif. Furthermore, we show that hole doping via Ca, Sr, and Ba systematically enhances the stability of the infinite-layer phase in all three transition-metal families. These results reveal fundamental challenges in realizing bulk substrate-free infinite-layer oxides, and simultaneously offer guidance for future experimental synthesis efforts targeting novel superconducting compounds.

### [246] [Lattice-mediated Geometric Frustration Drives Fast Ionic Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22345)
*Jianmin Yang,Lin Xie*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该论文通过建立晶格重整化（lattice-renormalized）自由能景观，将快离子导体（fast ionic conductors）的“软晶格”与“几何阻挫离子亚晶格”两种视角内在统一起来。推导出晶格介导的自由能修正项，揭示局域自俘获（self-trapping）与非局域晶格响应场干涉效应如何重塑阻挫自由能景观，促进关联离子输运（correlated ionic transport）。对立方相Li₇La₃Zr₂O₁₂和AgCrSe₂的大规模原子模拟验证了从势垒降低到集体离子重排的多尺度效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往对快离子导体的描述分别从“软晶格促进离子迁移”和“几何阻挫离子亚晶格提供简并构型”两个独立视角出发，但二者之间的内在联系尚不明确。本文旨在证明这两种图景在单个晶格重整化自由能景观中是本质关联的。

Method: 从耦合离子-晶格哈密顿量（coupled ion-lattice Hamiltonian）出发，通过绝热消除晶格响应（adiabatic lattice response），推导出由离子组态力（configurational forces）在宿主晶格逆刚度（inverse stiffness）上的投影所控制的晶格介导自由能修正。在粗粒化表示（coarse-grained representation）中，该修正分解为局域自俘获项和非局域晶格响应场干涉项。

Result: 对立方相Li₇La₃Zr₂O₁₂和AgCrSe₂的大规模原子模拟显示，上述效应在多尺度上显著，包括势垒降低和集体离子重排（collective ionic reorganization）。晶格软度（lattice softness）、阻挫（frustration）与集体扩散（collective diffusion）均表现为同一自由能景观的不同表达形式。

Conclusion: 快离子输运应被重新理解为一种晶格重整化的几何阻挫问题（lattice-renormalized geometric frustration problem）。晶格软度、阻挫与集体扩散并非独立机制，而是同一自由能景观的不同侧面，为统一理解快离子导体提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Fast ionic conductors are commonly described from two perspectives: soft lattices that facilitate ion migration, and geometrically frustrated ionic sublattices that host multiple nearly degenerate configurations. Here we demonstrate that these two pictures are intrinsically linked within a single lattice-renormalized free-energy landscape. Eliminating the adiabatic lattice response from a coupled ion-lattice Hamiltonian, we derive a lattice-mediated free-energy correction governed by the projection of ionic configurational forces onto the inverse stiffness of the host lattice. In a coarse-grained representation, this correction decomposes into local self-trapping and non-local interference between lattice-response fields. These intertwined effects reshape the frustrated free-energy landscape, redistribute mobile ions, and promote correlated ionic transport. Large-scale atomistic simulations of cubic Li$_7$La$_3$Zr$_2$O$_{12}$ and AgCrSe$_2$ show these effects across scales, from barrier reduction to collective ionic reorganization. The resulting picture recasts fast ionic transport as a lattice-renormalized geometric frustration problem, in which lattice softness, frustration and collective diffusion emerge as different expressions of the same free-energy landscape.

### [247] [Insights of Ammonia Decomposition on W--B Nanoclusters by Computational Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22395)
*Anastasiia V. Iosimovska,Mikhail M. Lukanov,Christian Tantardini,Alexander S. Novikov,Viktor S. Baidyshev,Alexander G. Kvashnin*

TL;DR: 本文通过进化算法结合密度泛函理论（DFT）系统探索了W$_m$B$_n$纳米团簇（原子数≤43）的基态结构与稳定性，发现孤立“魔法”组分（如WB$_{16}$、W$_2$B$_8$、W$_7$B$_{24}$、W$_{11}$B$_{22}$）具有显著的局部稳定性最大值。进一步以氨吸附与解离为探针评估其催化潜力，发现NH$_3$仅在钨位点吸附（能量-0.54至-1.78 eV），N-H键断裂能垒约1.1-1.4 eV，且解离态普遍低于分子吸附态。研究表明W-B纳米团簇可作为可调谐的氨分解催化剂，为其理性设计提供了结构基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钨硼化物纳米团簇（tungsten-boride nanoclusters）在催化应用中具有潜力，但其结构稳定性（structural stability）与反应性（reactivity）尚不明确，亟需系统研究以指导理性设计。

Method: 采用进化算法（evolutionary algorithm）结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）系统搜索原子数≤43的W$_m$B$_n$纳米团簇的基态结构（ground-state structures）与稳定性图谱（stability landscape）。利用微动弹性带方法（nudged elastic band, NEB）计算氨分解中第一个N-H键断裂的能垒。

Result: 稳定性图谱呈现高度非单调（non-monotonic）特征，存在WB$_{16}$等“魔法”组分（magic compositions）。NH$_3$分子吸附仅发生在W位点，吸附能-0.54至-1.78 eV（均值-1.43 eV），与Pt$_n$和Fe$_n$团簇相当。原子氢吸附范围更宽（+0.49至-1.46 eV），体现高位置敏感性（site sensitivity）。N-H键断裂前向能垒（forward barriers）为1.1-1.4 eV，解离态NH$_2^*$ + H$^*$能量普遍低于分子吸附态。

Conclusion: W-B纳米团簇可作为可调谐催化剂（tunable catalysts）用于氨分解，其催化活性与局部环境密切相关，该研究为其理性设计（rational design）提供了结构基础。

Abstract: Tungsten-boride nanoclusters represent a promising class of materials for catalytic applications, yet their structural stability and reactivity remain poorly understood. The evolutionary algorithm combined with density functional theory (DFT) are used to systematically explore the ground-state structures and stability landscape of W$_m$B$_n$ nanoclusters with up to 43 atoms. The resulting stability maps reveal a highly non-monotonic landscape characterized by isolated "magic" compositions, including WB$_{16}$, W$_2$B$_8$, W$_7$B$_{24}$, and W$_{11}$B$_{22}$, which exhibit pronounced local stability maxima. We further investigate the adsorption and initial decomposition step of ammonia on these clusters as a probe of their catalytic potential. Molecular NH$_3$ adsorption occurs exclusively on tungsten sites with energies ranging from -0.54 to -1.78 eV (average -1.43 eV), comparable to Pt$_n$ and Fe$_n$ clusters. Atomic hydrogen adsorption spans a broader range from +0.49 to -1.46 eV, reflecting high site sensitivity. Nudged elastic band calculations for the first N--H bond cleavage reveal forward barriers of 1.1-1.4 eV, with the dissociated NH$_2^*$ + H$^*$ state lying below the molecular adsorption state for most compositions. Notably, the activation barrier depends critically on the local environment available for stabilizing the detached hydrogen atom. These findings establish W--B nanoclusters as tunable catalysts for ammonia decomposition and provide a structural foundation for their rational design.

</details>

Abstract: Nanosized hafnia-zirconia (HfxZr1-xO2) in the form of thin films, multilayers, and nanoparticles are indispensable CMOS-compatible ferroelectric materials for advanced electronic memories and logic devices. Using the Landau-Ginzburg-Devonshire free energy functional with trilinear and biquadratic couplings of polar, nonpolar, and antipolar order parameters, we analyze the pyroelectric and electrocaloric properties of an ensemble of spherical core-shell HfxZr1-xO2 nanoparticles. The observed temperature-dependent behavior of the accumulated charge and its derivative with respect to temperature are in qualitative agreement with the dependences of polarization and pyroelectric coefficient calculated for the ensemble of densely packed spherical core-shell HfxZr1-xO2 nanoparticles. Thus, these results can open the way for creation of CMOS-compatible HfxZr1-xO2 nanoparticles for pyroelectric, electrocaloric, and thermoelectric applications.

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文开发了一个机器学习原子间势（machine-learning interatomic potential）MLIP4SiC-Mg，用于研究含镁（Mg）相关缺陷的3C-SiC材料的声子输运（phonon transport）性质，并结合Green-Kubo分子动力学与力误差校正方法，定量分析了不同缺陷构型对热导率的影响，揭示了Mg嬗变产物在辐照退化SiC中的构型依赖作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 碳化硅（SiC）是先进核能系统的候选材料，但辐照诱导的缺陷和嬗变产物会严重降低其热导率。在聚变环境中，镁（Mg）被预测为SiC中的主要固态嬗变产物，然而不同Mg相关缺陷如何影响声子输运的机制尚不清楚。

Method: 开发了一个机器学习原子间势（machine-learning interatomic potential）MLIP4SiC-Mg，训练于大规模密度泛函理论（DFT）数据集。结合Green-Kubo分子动力学（molecular dynamics）、力误差校正（force-error correction）以及针对稀缺陷陷系统的基于电阻的处理方法，实现了大尺寸缺陷超胞中的定量热导率计算。

Result: 纯净3C-SiC在300 K下的校正热导率为421 W/(mK)，与实验数据吻合良好。所有缺陷均强烈降低热导率，但散射强度高度依赖构型：V_C和Mg_TC是强声子散射体，而孤立Mg_Si相对较弱。残余热阻分析表明，缺陷诱导的热阻与浓度并非严格线性关系，应视为有效的温度和浓度依赖散射度量。Mg_Si-V_C团簇增强了散射但总超额电阻低于空间分离的Mg_Si和V_C缺陷。

Conclusion: 这些结果阐明了镁嬗变在辐照退化SiC中构型依赖的作用，并为量化核陶瓷中缺陷控制的热输运提供了原子级分析框架。

Abstract: Silicon carbide is a leading candidate material for advanced nuclear energy systems, but irradiation-induced defects and transmutation products can severely degrade its thermal conductivity. In fusion environments, Mg is predicted to be a major solid transmutant in SiC, yet it is not well understood how different Mg-related defects affect phonon transport. Here, we develop a machine-learning interatomic potential, MLIP4SiC-Mg, for 3C-SiC containing intrinsic point defects, Mg-related defects, and Mg-defect complexes. The potential is trained on a large DFT dataset and reproduces DFT energies, forces, equation-of-state behavior, phonon dispersions, and lattice thermal conductivities with near-DFT accuracy. Combined with Green-Kubo molecular dynamics, force-error correction, and a resistance-based treatment for dilute defective systems, MLIP4SiC-Mg enables quantitative thermal-conductivity calculations in large defective supercells. The corrected thermal conductivity of pristine 3C-SiC is 421 W/(mK) at 300 K, in good agreement with available experimental data. All defects considered strongly reduce thermal conductivity, but their scattering strengths are highly configuration dependent. V_C and Mg_TC act as strong phonon scatterers, whereas isolated Mg_Si is comparatively weak. Residual thermal resistivity analysis shows that defect-induced thermal resistance is not strictly linear with concentration and should be treated as an effective temperature- and concentration-dependent scattering metric. Mg_Si-V_C clustering enhances scattering relative to isolated Mg_Si, but reduces the total excess resistance relative to spatially separated Mg_Si and V_C defects. These results clarify the configuration-dependent role of Mg transmutation in irradiation-degraded SiC and provide an atomistic framework for quantifying defect-controlled heat transport in nuclear ceramics.

### [250] [Interfacial-melt stability as a thermodynamic prerequisite for solid-state synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22885)
*Zihan Zhang,Mengyi Chen,Qianxiao Li,Peichen Zhong*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出界面熔体稳定性（interfacial-melt stability）可作为热力学筛选描述符，用于判断通过界面熔体介导的固相合成路径的可行性。在Fe-B体系中，尽管FeB4在凸包上热力学稳定，但常压合成失败的原因是富硼界面熔体发生旋节分解（spinodal decomposition）；施加压力可恢复其稳定性，与实验合成边界一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 材料计算筛选常依据生成能凸包（formation energy convex hull）预测热力学稳定的候选相，但大量预测稳定相难以合成。作者试图区分“热力学稳定性”与“实验合成可行性”，并寻找一个可在计算上评估的合成性描述符。

Method: 以经典Fe-B体系为研究对象，采用精细调优的机器学习原子间势（machine-learning interatomic potential）驱动熔体淬火分子动力学（melt-quench molecular dynamics）模拟。通过计算浓度-浓度结构因子（concentration-concentration structure factor）和自由能曲面的曲率来检测界面熔体的旋节分解不稳定性。

Result: 常压下FeB4成分附近的富硼界面熔体展现出凹形自由能曲面（concave free-energy landscape），标志着脱混不稳定性（demixing instability），该特征与低能二十面体（icosahedral）和五角金字塔形硼簇（pentagonal-pyramidal boron motifs）相关。施加压力后，PV项引入凸性贡献，恢复熔体稳定性，与实验高压合成边界相符。

Conclusion: 界面熔体的旋节分解稳定性可作为热力学合成性筛选描述符，用于AI辅助材料发现。原子模拟可通过结构因子发散（structure-factor divergence）评估该稳定性，从而在计算上甄别虽热力学稳定但难以合成的候选相。

Abstract: Computational materials discovery commonly ranks candidate materials by their thermodynamic stability on the formation energy convex hull, yet many predicted-stable phases resist synthesis. We propose that solid-state synthesizability through interfacial-melt-mediated routes requires an additional thermodynamic condition: the interfacial melt at the target composition must itself remain locally stable against spinodal decomposition. We demonstrate this in the classical Fe--B system, where thermodynamically stable FeB$_4$ has been reported under high-pressure synthesis but not in low-pressure synthesis attempts. Using melt--quench molecular dynamics driven by a fine-tuned machine-learning interatomic potential, we find that, at ambient pressure, the B-rich interfacial melt near the FeB$_4$ composition develops a concave free-energy landscape, signaling a demixing instability that is corroborated by the concentration--concentration structure factor and correlated with low-energy icosahedral and pentagonal-pyramidal boron motifs. Applied pressure introduces a convex $PV$ contribution that restores melt stability, consistent with the experimental synthesis boundary. Interfacial-melt stability, which atomistic simulations can assess via structure-factor divergence, is thus proposed as a practical thermodynamic screening descriptor of synthesizability for AI-assisted materials discovery.

### [251] [Coherent seeding and control of dynamical ferroelectricity by phonon anharmonicity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22896)
*Junhan Huang,Yongkang Ju,Xinbo Wang,Li Yue,Hao Wang,Qiaomei Liu,Tianchen Hu,Yuchen Cui,Liyu Shi,Shangfei Wu,Sijie Zhang,Dong Wu,Peizhe Tang,Tao Dong,Nan-Lin Wang*

Method: 利用强太赫兹（terahertz）脉冲激发中心对称PbTe中的软声子模式（soft phonon mode），通过太赫兹驱动的简并横向光学声子之间的非谐耦合（anharmonic coupling）诱导铁电态；并结合双脉冲激发协议实现极化的相干放大与抑制。

Conclusion: 太赫兹驱动的非谐模式耦合可作为控制量子材料中模式介导功能（mode-mediated functionalities）的通用策略，为超快信息处理开辟新路径。

Abstract: Optical control of quantum materials has progressed along two separate directions: creating non-equilibrium states inaccessible at equilibrium, and coherently controlling ultrafast dynamics with multi-pulse protocols. Ferroelectricity is especially attractive in this context because its order parameter, macroscopic polarization, directly links inversion-symmetry breaking to functional response. Yet light-induced ferroelectricity has so far been confined to quantum paraelectrics near the ferroelectric instability, where critical fluctuations obscure the formation of a homogeneous ferroelectric state and complicate its deterministic coherent control. Unifying these capabilities -- preparing a symmetry-broken state and then coherently steering its functionality -- remains a central challenge. Here we show that intense terahertz excitation of a soft phonon mode induces a ferroelectric state in centrosymmetric PbTe, a thermoelectric material with strong lattice anharmonicity but no ferroelectric transition at finite temperature. The light-induced symmetry-broken state can be realized up to about 100 K, without relying on local dipolar fluctuations. Experiment and theory together reveal that terahertz-driven anharmonic coupling between degenerate transverse optical phonons underlies this ferroelectric induction. Furthermore, we demonstrate coherent amplification and suppression of the induced polarization via a double-pulse-excitation protocol. These results establish terahertz-driven anharmonic mode coupling as a general strategy for controlling mode-mediated functionalities in quantum materials, opening a route to ultrafast information processing.

### [252] [Reduced-Order Modelling of Defect Transport using Surrogate Kinetics: Application to U$_x$Pu$_ {1-x}$N](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23128)
*Peter Hatton*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于环境依赖替代动力学（environment-dependent surrogate kinetics）的降阶方法，用于模拟化学无序材料中的缺陷输运。以 U_xPu_1-xN 为例，利用 Hop-Decorate 工作流生成大量迁移能数据，并蒸馏为紧凑替代函数，在晶格动力学蒙特卡洛（lattice kinetic Monte Carlo）模拟中高效计算迁移率，揭示了两种主导的非线性扩散机制。

Abstract: Defect transport in chemically disordered materials is a difficult phenomenon to model since migration energetics depend strongly on the local chemical environment, producing a distribution of transition barriers that cannot be exhaustively enumerated. Here, we develop a reduced-order approach to modelling defect diffusion in compositionally complex materials using environment-dependent surrogate kinetics. Migration energetics for actinide vacancies, nitride vacancies, and actinide-nitride divacancies in U$_x$Pu$_{1-x}$N are generated using the Hop-Decorate workflow across thousands of chemical configurations. These data are distilled into compact surrogate functions that predict migration barriers and energy differences from simple descriptors based on local coordination counts. The surrogate models reproduce the atomistic dataset with low error and enable efficient evaluation of migration rates during lattice kinetic Monte Carlo simulations. Long-time diffusivities computed across temperature and composition reveal strongly non-linear behaviour arising from two dominant mechanisms: species-controlled migration on the actinide sublattice and environment-dependent trapping on the nitride sublattice. Although demonstrated for U$_x$Pu$_{1-x}$N the framework provides a general and computationally efficient approach for modelling defect transport in chemically disordered materials and for integrating atomistic kinetics into higher-scale simulations.

### [253] [Unconventional topological Hall response and anisotropic magnetotransport properties of a helical magnet EuAuAs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23140)
*Anyesh Saraswati,Koyendrila Debnath,Shubhankar Roy,Barun Ghosh,Nitesh Kumar,Prabhat Mandal*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过实验与理论相结合的方式，研究了反铁磁材料EuAuAs的磁性与磁输运性质，发现其电荷输运强烈受局域Eu自旋构型影响，观测到由标量自旋手性（scalar spin chirality）引起的巨拓扑霍尔效应（topological Hall effect），并结合第一性原理计算确认了螺旋磁结构（helical magnetic structure）和费米面（Fermi surface）各向异性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑磁体（topological magnets）因其非平庸自旋织构（spin texture）可展现丰富的涌现量子现象而受到广泛关注，但目前对中心对称螺旋磁体中电子结构与非共面自旋织构之间相互作用的实验研究仍较为缺乏。

Method: 采用实验与理论相结合的方法：实验上测量了EuAuAs在温度与磁场变化下的电阻率（resistivity）和磁化强度（magnetization）；理论上利用Hikami-Larkin-Nagaoka模型和广义Altshuler-Aronov框架分别分析横向磁电阻（TMR）和纵向磁电阻（LMR）中的弱反局域化（WAL）贡献，并通过第一性原理计算（ab-initio calculations）和第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）获取螺旋磁结构与费米面信息。

Result: 在奈尔温度（Néel temperature, $T_\mathrm{N}$）$\sim$ 6 K以下，纵向磁电阻（LMR）和横向磁电阻（TMR）在低场下为正、高场下为大且负值；随温度升高，TMR在60 K以上变为正，而LMR在100 K以下仍为负。低场正LMR和TMR源于弱反局域化（WAL），其中TMR数据符合Hikami-Larkin-Nagaoka模型，LMR数据符合广义Altshuler-Aronov框架。此外观测到由标量自旋手性引起的巨拓扑霍尔效应，并被第一性原理计算支持的螺旋磁结构所佐证。纵向电阻率和磁电阻的各向异性经第一性原理计算确认与EuAuAs费米面特性一致。

Conclusion: 这些结果表明，EuAuAs是一个探索中心对称螺旋磁体中电子结构与非共面自旋织构（noncoplanar spin texture）之间相互作用的独特平台。

Abstract: Topological magnets with nontrivial spin texture have attracted considerable interest because they display a rich spectrum of emergent quantum phenomena. Here, we present a combined experimental and theoretical investigation of the magnetic and magnetotransport properties of EuAuAs, an antiferromagnet with Néel temperature ($T_\mathrm{N}$) $\sim$ 6 K. The temperature and magnetic field dependence of electrical resistivity and magnetization demonstrate that the charge transport in EuAuAs is strongly influenced by the spin configuration of local Eu moments. Below $T_\mathrm{N}$, both longitudinal magnetoresistance (LMR) and transverse magnetoresistance (TMR) are positive at low fields but large and negative at high fields. With increasing temperature, TMR becomes positive above 60 K, whereas LMR remains negative up to 100 K. The low-field positive LMR and TMR originate from weak antilocalization (WAL). The WAL contribution in TMR is well captured by the Hikami-Larkin-Nagaoka model, whereas the LMR data are described by a generalized Altshuler-Aronov framework. Moreover, we observe a giant topological Hall effect arising from the scalar spin chirality, which is further supported by the helical magnetic structure obtained from the ab-initio calculations. The observed anisotropy in longitudinal resistivity and magnetoresistance underscores the very nature of the Fermi surface of the EuAuAs, as confirmed by first-principles calculations. These results establish EuAuAs as a unique platform for exploring the interplay between electronic structure and noncoplanar spin texture in a centrosymmetric helical magnet.

Abstract: The focus of the present work is the development of specialized experimental instrumentation compatible with synchrotron characterization for in-situ and operando symmetric intermediate temperature solid oxide fuel cells (IT-SOFC) studies at maximum temperatures of 800 C , exposed to reducing and oxidizing atmospheres, using fluorescence X-ray absorption spectroscopy (XAS) measurements in combination with electrochemical impedance spectroscopy (EIS) in the multipurpose Quati beamline at CNPEM/SIRIUS synchrotron facility [1]. Method: 将磁盘检测输出的衍射峰位置向量作为聚类算法的输入，通过无监督聚类自动区分来自不同结构组分的衍射图案，进而实现多晶、单晶（含析出相）及非晶/纳米晶体系的自动化分解与成像。

Abstract: If disk detection is applied to nanobeam electron diffraction datasets, then the results are effectively a list of vectors describing the position of every diffraction peak in real and reciprocal space. This is the natural territory for the application of clustering algorithms, and they are shown to be highly effective at decomposing such datasets and automating imaging and analysis. Examples are shown in both polycrystalline and single crystal (with precipitates) systems. Additionally, automated separation of amorphous or deeply nanocrystalline components is also found to be possible allowing composite images of both amorphous and crystalline components in partially crystallised samples to be easily and automatically generated. These advances promise to increase throughput in atomic structure analysis with nanobeam diffraction, and also make finding minor components much easier. They can also serve as a preliminary step towards more detailed crystallographic or crystal size/shape distribution analysis.

### [256] [Universal Interatomic Potentials as Configuration-Space Generators for One-Shot and Iterative Fine-Tuning of Ab Initio-Accurate Material-Specific Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23214)
*Jonas Hänseroth,Aaron Flötotto,Christian Dreßler*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文比较了五种通用机器学习原子间势（universal MLIPs），发现它们在反应性事件等定量建模场景中表现不可靠，并提出一种将通用MLIP用作构型空间生成器、结合DFT重标定与材料专用MLIP微调/训练的实用工作流，仅需少量DFT计算即可在三天内生成纳秒级从头算质量轨迹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通用机器学习原子间势（universal machine-learning interatomic potentials, universal MLIPs）正迅速成为原子模拟的通用工具，但它们在涉及反应性事件的定量材料建模中的作用尚未明确，需要一个系统性的评估与改进方案。

Method: 在七个化学多样性系统中比较五种通用MLIP；提出一个工作流：先用通用MLIP生成长分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）轨迹，再对构型进行子采样并用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）重新标记，最后在从头算（first-principles）数据集上训练或微调材料专用MLIP。对最具挑战性的案例采用迭代自训练（iterative self-training）逐步优化构型空间采样。

Result: 通用MLIP在标准基准上表现优异并不保证目标可观测量预测的准确性，尤其在反应性、输运或高能垒过程上零样本模型不可靠，以MoS₂中硫空位跳跃为例。工作流中2000个DFT重算结构通常足以获得准确的微调或从头训练模型，最复杂的MoS₂案例仅需600次从头算即可恢复DFT势能面。

Conclusion: 提出的工作流能将通用MLIP有效转化为高效构型空间生成器，同时保留从头算参考标签用于模型训练，可在三天内完成包含训练数据生成和模型创建在内的1纳秒从头算质量轨迹的生成。

Abstract: Universal machine-learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) are rapidly becoming general-purpose tools for atomistic simulation, but their role in quantitative materials modeling when reactive events are involved remains unsettled. We compare five universal MLIPs across seven chemically diverse systems and find that strong performance on standard benchmarks does not guarantee accurate predictions of target observables. In particular, zero-shot models do not reliably reproduce reactive, transport, or high-barrier processes, exemplified here in particular by the sulfur-vacancy jump in MoS$_2$. We therefore propose a practical alternative: universal MLIPs are used to generate long molecular dynamics trajectories, the resulting configurations are sub-sampled and relabeled with DFT, and material-specific MLIPs are subsequently trained or fine-tuned on the resulting first-principles datasets. This workflow converts universal models into efficient configuration-space generators while retaining ab initio reference labels for training. Across the tested systems, $2{,}000$ DFT-recalculated structures are often sufficient to obtain accurate fine-tuned or trained-from-scratch models. For the most challenging case, iterative self-training progressively refines the sampled configuration space and recovers the DFT MoS$_2$ potential energy profile with only $600$ first-principles calculations in total. The resulting workflow enables the generation of $1$ ns ab initio-quality trajectories - including training data generation and model creation - within three days.

Method: 在邻位Au(788)表面引入chevron-GNRs进行台阶边缘钝化，利用扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy, STM）观察局部生长构型变化；建立基于拉曼（Raman）光谱的自动化大面积分析框架，依据G模（G mode）和径向呼吸类模（radial breathing-like mode, RBLM）进行像素级分类，评估转移覆盖度和纳米带完整性。

Result: STM观察到chevron-GNRs优先占据台阶边缘，将9-AGNRs推向台面中心。Raman映射显示转移质量高度不均匀，存在大片无GNR信号区域以及RBLM与G模强度比的显著空间变化。样本间转移质量差异大，仅一个样本表现高产，大多数样本转移产率远低于100%。

Conclusion: Chevron钝化虽能局部改变9-AGNRs在Au(788)上的生长构型，但尚无法实现可重复的高质量完整对齐纳米带转移。本文建立的基于Raman的分析框架为系统优化GNR转移策略提供了定量基准。

Abstract: The transfer of aligned graphene nanoribbons from metallic growth surfaces to device-compatible platforms remains a central bottleneck for nanoribbon electronics. Here, we investigate step-edge passivation of vicinal Au(788) by chevron-GNRs as a strategy to improve the transfer of aligned 9-armchair graphene nanoribbons. Scanning tunneling microscopy reveals that chevron-GNRs preferentially occupy step-edges, effectively acting as passivators that displace 9-AGNRs toward terrace centers, thereby altering their local growth configuration. To quantify transfer performance, we establish an automated large-area Raman analysis framework that enables pixel-wise classification based on the G mode and the radial breathing-like mode (RBLM). This approach provides a robust and scalable metric for assessing both transfer coverage and local ribbon integrity across macroscopic areas. Raman mapping uncovers strongly inhomogeneous transfer, characterized by extended regions with no detectable GNR signal and pronounced spatial variability in the RBLM-to-G intensity ratio. Transfer quality varies substantially across the sample series, with only a single high-yield outlier and most samples remaining well below 100% transfer yield. These results demonstrate that while chevron passivation locally modifies the growth configuration of 9-AGNRs on Au(788), it does not yet yield reproducible, high-quality transfer of intact aligned ribbons. The presented Raman-based analysis framework establishes a quantitative benchmark for the systematic optimization of GNR transfer strategies.

Abstract: The bilayer kagome metal Ni$_3$In has recently attracted attention due to the presence of a flat band located near the Fermi level, which has been associated with unconventional thermodynamic and electronic transport properties [Ye et al., Nat. Phys. 20, 610-614 (2024)]. However, further investigation of the intrinsic properties of this system has been hindered by the lack of large, high-quality single crystals. Here, we report the successful growth of Ni$_3$(In, Sn) single crystals using a Pb-flux technique. By optimizing the growth conditions, competing binary phases can be effectively suppressed, enabling the synthesis of single crystals with dimensions reaching several millimeters. We compare the physical properties of our Pb-flux-grown crystals to previously reported samples prepared by iodine-assisted chemical vapor transport and molecular beam epitaxy as well as to first-principles resistivity calculations. We find a significantly lower electrical resistivity in our crystals, in excellent agreement with calculations of resistivity from electron-phonon scattering, a sizeable non-saturating magnetoresistance, and a reduced Sommerfeld coefficient and magnetic susceptibility compared to previous experimental findings, which are likely related to differences in the Fermi level position. Our results establish Pb-flux growth as a reliable route for obtaining large single crystals of the bilayer kagome metals Ni$_3$(In, Sn) that are suitable for further thermodynamic and spectroscopic investigations of their intrinsic electronic and magnetic properties.

### [259] [Atomic-scale theory of robust out-of-plane ferroelectricity in ultrathin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23508)
*Fengbo Yuan,Yujia Teng,Karin M. Rabe,Yubo Qi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个原子尺度理论框架，通过考虑薄膜终止层（termination layer）的功函数（work function），揭示了超薄铁电薄膜中“自极化（self-polarizing）”和“终止层角色切换（switchable role of the termination layer）”两种效应与“特征结构（characteristic structure）”的强关联性，从而解释了HfO₂基氧化物和铋基氧化物在超薄极限下仍能保持稳健铁电性（ferroelectricity）的微观机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究发现，终止层的“自极化效应”和“终止层角色可切换效应”与特征结构存在强关联，共同促成超薄极限下的稳健铁电性。此外，顶部电极（top electrode）对于稳定该类材料的超薄铁电性也至关重要。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一个综合性的超薄薄膜铁电性理论框架，为理解超薄极限下铁电性的存续机制提供了基础性洞见，并为下一代纳米尺度器件（nanoscale devices）的设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Ferroelectricity in ultrathin films, characterized by robust switchable out-of-plane polarization, is key to next-generation nanoelectronics. Although the macroscopic theory of ferroelectricity suggests that ferroelectricity is inevitably suppressed as the film thickness decreases, recent studies have demonstrated robust ultra thin-film ferroelectricity, for certain ferroelectric materials, specifically HfO$_2$-based oxides and bismuth-based oxides. In this work, we develop an atomic-scale theoretical framework for understanding ferroelectricity in this limiting regime. By considering the work function of the termination layers of the film, we find that robust ferroelectricity arises from ``self-polarizing'' and ``switchable role of the termination layer'' effects strongly correlated to the ``characteristic structure.'' This theory also provides further insights on the importance of top electrodes in stabilizing ferroelectricity for this class of materials in the ultrathin limit. This work aims to develop a comprehensive theoretical framework for thin-film ferroelectricity, providing fundamental insights that can guide the design of next-generation nanoscale devices.

### [260] [INCARBench: A Benchmark for Scientific Configuration in VASP INCAR by Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23571)
*Bin Shao,Jixiang Li,Xinyue Zhang,Baishun Yang,Zhiyang Liu,Weichao Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了INCARBench基准，用于评估大语言模型（LLM）在VASP输入配置任务上的能力，涵盖配置生成与修复。实验发现当前前沿模型在语义和政策准确率上表现尚可，但在任务关键正确性（task-critical correctness）上显著偏低，且错误集中于需要同时满足多重约束的物理耦合设置（如DFT+$U$、磁性和关联材料）。修复评估表明，修正错误设置与保留已有正确配置是两种不同的能力，后者仍面临重大挑战。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 前沿模型在高层次语义和政策准确率上表现良好，但任务关键正确性显著偏低，表明参数级正确性（parameter-level correctness）并不等同于科学有效的配置。错误主要集中在DFT+$U$、磁性和关联材料等具有物理耦合（physically coupled）的设置中。此外，修复任务显示，修正错误与保持已有正确配置是两种不同的能力，配置保留（configuration preservation）仍是主要难点。

Conclusion: 科学配置（scientific configuration）可作为一种可测量的LLM能力，本研究为在计算材料科学中开发更可靠的AI系统奠定了基础。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly being integrated into first-principles computational workflows, yet their ability to configure scientific calculations remains poorly understood. Here, we introduce INCARBench, a benchmark for evaluating LLMs on input configuration for the Vienna Ab initio Simulation Package (VASP) through both configuration generation and repair tasks. Evaluating 19 model configurations reveals substantial capability differences among current frontier models. While several models achieve high semantic and policy accuracy, task-critical correctness remains substantially lower, demonstrating that parameter-level correctness does not necessarily imply scientifically valid configurations. Failure analysis shows that errors concentrate in physically coupled settings involving DFT+$U$, magnetism, and correlated materials, where multiple constraints must be satisfied simultaneously. Repair evaluation further reveals that correcting incorrect settings and preserving already-valid configurations are distinct capabilities, with configuration preservation remaining a major challenge. These findings establish scientific configuration as a measurable capability of large language models and provide a foundation for developing more reliable AI systems for computational materials science.

### [261] [Data analysis methods for powder x-ray diffraction intensity under laser-driven dynamic compression at Omega and NIF laser facilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23602)
*Marius Millot,Federica Coppari,Amy Lazicki,Jon H. Eggert*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文介绍了为激光驱动动态压缩下的粉末X射线衍射（PXRD）平台（如Omega的PXRDIP和NIF的TARDIS）所开发的数据分析新方法，旨在提升PXRD强度测定的保真度。方法包括利用准直针孔或未压缩材料层作为原位（in-situ）参考、跨不同X射线源的数据比较，以及考虑热阻尼效应对衍射信号的影响，并以金刚石在约1 TPa下的冲击压缩数据为例进行说明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激光驱动动态压缩下的粉末X射线衍射（PXRD）是研究材料在极端压力、温度和应变率下响应的有力工具，但现有数据分析方法在PXRD强度测定的保真度上仍有提升空间。作者旨在进一步发展数据分析方法，以提高PXRD强度测定的准确性。

Method: 作者提出了几种改进PXRD强度测定的数据分析方法，包括：(1) 利用准直针孔或样品包中未压缩材料层的XRD信号作为原位（in-situ）参考；(2) 比较不同X射线源采集的数据；(3) 考虑热阻尼效应（thermal damping），即当比较冲击压缩的高温材料与常温室温参考材料的XRD信号时，校正高温对衍射强度的影响。这些方法被集成到一个数据分析包中，并以金刚石在约1 TPa下的冲击压缩数据为例进行演示。

Result: 本文主要呈现了方法论的开发与实现，而非具体的实验发现。通过讨论如何在数据分析包中实现这些方法，并应用于金刚石在约1 TPa下的冲击压缩数据，展示了该方法在提升PXRD强度测定保真度方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 所提出的数据分析方法能够有效提升激光驱动动态压缩PXRD平台的强度测定保真度，并适用于不同X射线源和不同温度条件下的数据比较与校正。这些方法有助于更准确地从PXRD数据中提取材料在极端条件下的结构信息。

Abstract: Powder x-ray diffraction (PXRD) under laser-driven dynamic compression is a powerful tool to investigate material response to extreme pressure, temperature and strain rates. Robust PXRD platforms have been developed at kJ and MJ laser facilities worldwide including the Powder X-Ray Diffraction Image Plate (PXRDIP) at the Omega Laser Facility at the Laboratory for Laser Energetics (LLE) and the TARget Diffraction In Situ (TARDIS) at the National Ignition Facility (NIF). Here we present further developments of data analysis methods focused towards improving the fidelity of the PXRD intensity determination for these platforms. We illustrate these methods by discussing how they can be implemented in a data analysis package and applied to shock compression data on diamond near 1 TPa. We discuss using the XRD signal from the collimating pinhole or a layer of un-compressed material in the sample package as \textit{ in-situ} references for XRD intensity. We detail how to compare data collected with different x-ray sources and how to account for thermal damping of XRD signal when comparing XRD from a shock-compressed, hot material with the reference material at ambient.

</details>


### [262] [Two-dimensional stealthy hyperuniform polycrystalline disk packings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23628)
*Carlo Vanoni,Paul J. Steinhardt,Salvatore Torquato*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过集体坐标优化方法生成了超致密、隐身且超均匀（SHU）的二维多晶圆盘堆积，并与标准Lubachevsky–Stillinger（LS）分子动力学模拟得到的非超均匀多晶进行了系统比较。研究发现，SHU多晶堆积在晶粒尺寸分布、扩散能力以及电磁波透过性等方面显著优于LS多晶，尽管这类结构在自然界中难以自发形成，但可通过纳米光刻或3D打印制备为超材料（metamaterials）应用于光学和输运领域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多晶体（polycrystals）由晶粒（grains）和晶界（grain boundaries）组成，尽管完美晶体是超均匀（hyperuniform）的，但由于多晶中晶粒尺寸和取向随机，会产生长波长密度涨落，使其不具备超均匀性。本文旨在探索能否通过优化方法生成具有超均匀性（hyperuniform）的多晶结构，并评估其相较于非超均匀多晶在结构和功能上的优势。

Method: 采用集体坐标优化（collective-coordinate optimization）程序生成二维多晶圆盘堆积，使其同时具有超致密（ultradense）、隐身（stealthy）和超均匀（hyperuniform）特性（称为SHU多晶）。作为对照，使用改进的Lubachevsky–Stillinger快速压缩算法（LS算法）的分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟生成标准的非超均匀多晶堆积。随后对两类堆积进行了广泛的比较，涵盖两点统计（two-point statistics）、晶粒尺寸、比表面积、扩散传播性（diffusion spreadability）以及有效动态介电常数虚部表征的光学响应（optical response）。

Result: SHU多晶堆积展现出独特的晶粒尺寸分布，这是非超均匀情形中所缺失的不同晶粒间长程关联（long-range correlations）的结果。在非局域强对比展开（nonlocal strong-contrast expansion）框架下，由介电材料制成的SHU多晶堆积在小波矢（wave vectors）下对电磁波（electromagnetic waves）完全透明，而LS多晶则不具备这一性质。此外，SHU多晶堆积具有增强的扩散传播性。

Conclusion: 尽管SHU多晶堆积在自然界中无法自发形成，但其独特的光学和输运性能使其可以通过纳米光刻（nanolithography）或3D打印（3D printing）等技术制备为超材料（metamaterials），在功能应用中具有潜在价值。

Abstract: Polycrystals consist of grains of local crystalline order separated by grain boundaries. Their structure is not hyperuniform, even though perfect crystals are, because polycrystals consist of randomly sized and oriented grains that generate appreciable long-wavelength density fluctuations. In this paper, we use a collective-coordinate optimization procedure to generate two-dimensional polycrystalline packings composed of identical disks arranged in a pattern that is ultradense, stealthy, and hyperuniform (hereafter named SHU). We compare them with polycrystalline disk packings obtained via a modified Lubachevsky--Stillinger rapid compression algorithm (hereafter named LS), a molecular dynamics protocol that serves as a standard reference model describing realistic, nonhyperuniform polycrystalline microstructures. We carry out an extensive comparison of polycrystalline SHU and LS packings that includes differences in two-point statistics, grain size, specific surface area, diffusion spreadability, and optical response as quantified by the imaginary part of the effective dynamic dielectric constant. We find that the polycrystalline SHU packings exhibit a distinctive grain-size distribution, a consequence of long-range correlations between different grains that is absent in the nonhyperuniform case. Within the nonlocal strong-contrast expansion, we confirm that polycrystalline SHU packings made of dielectric material are perfectly transparent to electromagnetic waves at small wave vectors, in contrast to LS packings. Moreover, polycrystalline SHU packings offer enhanced diffusion spreadability. Although polycrystalline SHU packings are not expected to form spontaneously in nature, they may be created for applications as metamaterials via nanolithography or 3D printing that take advantage of their distinctive optical and transport properties.

</details>

Result: 成功在开闭同伦代数的Hochschild不变量上构造了微积分结构，并证明了Getzler-Gauss-Manin联络在开闭周期循环链复形上是链同伦平坦的。

Abstract: We establish the calculus structure on Hochschild invariants of open-closed homotopy algebras. We further define the Getzler-Gauss-Manin connection and show that it is flat up to chain homotopy on the open-closed periodic cyclic chain complex.

TL;DR: 本文综述了精确从头算核理论（ab initio nuclear theory）的最新突破，包括将其扩展到重核铅-208、大形变中质量核和滴线附近弱束缚核，以及暗物质直接探测的核响应计算，展示了该方法如何大幅降低超越标准模型物理搜索中的核物理不确定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确从头算核理论时代已经到来，需要系统总结其最新进展，特别是如何从基本核力和电弱流出发，实现经不确定性量化的核结构预测以及对外部探针的相互作用计算，从而为超越标准模型（Beyond the Standard Model）的精密实验提供更稳健的理论解释。

Method: 综述了从头算方法在多个方向的应用：将计算范围扩展至重核铅-208（$^{208}$Pb）、具有复杂形变（complex deformation）的中质量核体系以及滴线（driplines）附近的弱束缚核；同时涵盖了对暗物质直接探测中核响应（nuclear responses）的从头算计算。

Result: 从头算方法已成功应用于从轻核到重核铅-208、形变中质量核和滴线弱束缚核的全范围系统，并能计算暗物质直接探测相关的核响应，显著降低了核物理不确定性。

Conclusion: 从头算方法能够实质性地降低超越标准模型物理搜索中的核物理不确定性，为当前及未来精密实验提供更可靠的理论解释。

Abstract: The era of precision ab initio nuclear theory has arrived, enabling uncertainty-quantified predictions for nuclear structure and for interactions with external probes directly from the underlying nuclear force and electroweak currents. This review highlights recent breakthroughs that extend ab initio calculations to the heavy nucleus $^{208}$Pb, to medium-mass systems with complex deformation, and to weakly-bound nuclei near the driplines. We also summarize ab initio calculations of nuclear responses for dark matter direct detection. Together, these advances demonstrate how ab initio methods can substantially reduce nuclear-physics uncertainties in searches for physics beyond the Standard Model, providing a more robust interpretation of current and forthcoming precision experiments.

### [265] [Gas-induced perturbations on the gravitational wave in-spiral of live post-Newtonian LISA massive black hole binaries: 0.1 disk aspect ratio](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20787)
*Mudit Garg,Alessia Franchini,Alessandro Lupi*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 该研究通过三维流体动力学（3D hydrodynamics）模拟，研究了嵌入在原位共转环双星盘（circumbinary disk, CBD）中、质量为10^6太阳质量、等质量准圆轨道的大质量双黑洞（massive black hole binary, MBHB）的演化，首次在0.1纵横比的盘中同时测量了有无引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）发射时的气体引力矩与吸积力矩，并发现LISA可探测到约0.12 rad的气体诱导轨道相移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大质量双黑洞（MBHB）在演化的晚期会受到周围环双星盘（CBD）气体的影响，而此前对于纵横比为0.1的盘中、引力波（GW）驱动下MBHB的演化过程中气体力矩的具体贡献尚不清楚，因此有必要进行高精度的数值模拟以揭示其动力学细节。

Method: 采用三维流体动力学（3D hydrodynamics）模拟，设置等质量、准圆轨道的10^6太阳质量MBHB嵌入在顺行、局部等温、纵横比为0.1的CBD中；双星演化由气体力矩驱动，动力学引入2.5阶后牛顿（post-Newtonian, PN）修正，从而追踪从55到46个史瓦西半径（Schwarzschild radii）的GW驱动旋入过程。

Result: 首次在0.1纵横比盘中分别报告了有无GW发射时的引力矩与吸积力矩测量结果；发现当GW成为主导演化机制时，吸积时序（accretion time series）的形态发生适度改变；气体诱导的轨道相移（orbital phase-shift）为0.12 rad，覆盖600个轨道周期，LISA可在红移z=1处探测到该信号。

Conclusion: 该结果对多信使天文学（multi-messenger astronomy）具有重要意义：LSST/Roman巡天对吸积率调制的观测与LISA对相移的联合探测，将为揭示MBHB周围复杂环境的关键信息提供重要途径。

Abstract: We perform 3D hydrodynamics simulations of an equal-mass quasi-circular live $10^6~{\rm M}_\odot$ massive black hole binary (MBHB) embedded in a prograde, locally isothermal circumbinary disk (CBD) with $0.1$ aspect ratio. The binary evolution is driven by the gaseous torques and its dynamics is described with $2.5$ post-Newtonian corrections. This approach allows us to track the influence of the CBD on a gravitational-wave (GW) driven MBHB inspiral from $55$ to $46$ Schwarzschild radii, i.e., at its early evolution in the LISA band at redshift $z\sim1$. For the first time for the $0.1$ aspect ratio disk, we report the measurement of gravitational and accretion torques with and without concurrent GW emission. We also report how the morphology of the accretion time series onto the MBHB modestly alters when GW emission is the dominant binary evolutionary mechanism. Lastly, we find that the gas-induced orbital phase-shift is $0.12$ rad over $600$ orbital cycles, which LISA should detect at $z=1$. Our results have implications for multi-messenger astronomy, since observation of accretion rate modulation by LSST/Roman surveys and phase-shift by LISA will provide crucial information on the complex environment surrounding MBHBs.

### [266] [What Do Lorentz-Equivariant Jet Taggers Learn?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21790)
*Jay Agarwal,Siddharth Khare,Dhruv Kumar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了洛伦兹等变（Lorentz-equivariant）喷注标记器（jet taggers）内部学习到的物理特征与代数分级结构（algebraic grade structure），发现等变模型能压制框架依赖的赝快度（pseudorapidity），同时编码喷注质量（jet mass）与N-subjettiness等关键可观测量；通过分级消融（grade ablation）实验，揭示了双向量通道（bivector channels）在顶夸克标记中贡献可忽略，而矢量通道（vector-like channels）虽占主导但变量不稳定，表明网络利用了多重表征路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解洛伦兹等变喷注标记器内部学到了哪些物理特征与代数分级结构，以揭示其判别信息（discriminative information）的来源，为未来模型开发提供指导。

Method: 采用等变性测试（equivariance tests）、线性探针（linear probes）与分级消融（grade ablations）三种分析手段，对L-GATr、L-GATr-slim、LLoCa-T等五种模型进行系统研究。

Result: 线性探针显示等变模型将框架相关的赝快度压制为零，同时强烈编码喷注质量与N-subjettiness；分级消融实验表明L-GATr中双向量通道对顶夸克标记（top-quark tagging）贡献可忽略，矢量通道占主导但种子变量（seed variable），说明网络利用了多重表征路径（multiple representational pathways）。

Conclusion: 这些结果刻画了等变标记器中哪些物理特征与代数分级结构携带判别信息，可为未来此类模型的开发提供参考。

Abstract: We study what Lorentz-equivariant jet taggers learn internally, using equivariance tests, linear probes and grade ablations across five models including L-GATr, L-GATr-slim and LLoCa-T. Linear probes show that equivariant models suppress frame-dependent pseudorapidity to zero while encoding jet mass and N-subjettiness strongly. Grade ablations on L-GATr reveal that bivector channels are negligible for top-quark tagging while vector-like channels are dominant but seed variable, consistent with the network exploiting multiple representational pathways. These results characterize which physical features and algebraic grade structures carry discriminative information in equivariant taggers and may inform future development of such models.

### [267] [Atomistic Language Models Understand and Generate Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21395)
*Sathya Edamadaka,Krithik Ramesh,Ju Li,Rafael Gómez-Bombarelli*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出原子语言模型（ALM），通过连续投影器和分阶段训练统一原子编码器、大语言模型和去噪扩散模型，实现自然语言与原子结构的原生多模态理解与生成，并在晶体结构预测和从头生成任务上取得最优结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期以来，原子尺度结构建模与自然语言处理被分开研究，语言模型要么仅将原子模型作为工具调用，要么基于有损的文本编码进行微调，丢失了原子层面的结构信息。缺乏能够同时理解自然语言和原子结构的统一原生多模态模型。

Method: 提出原子语言模型（Atomistic Language Models, ALMs），通过纯连续投影器（continuous projectors）和分阶段训练（staged training），统一预训练的原子编码器（atomistic encoder）、大语言模型（large language model）和去噪扩散模型（denoising diffusion model）。引入Text-to-Crystal Feynman-Kac (T2C-FK)，一种基于粒子的采样器，在推理时对部分去噪轨迹进行评分，强制执行化学计量比约束。

Result: 在晶体结构预测（crystal structure prediction）和从头生成（de novo generation）任务上取得最优结果（state-of-the-art）。同时构建了ALM Bench，这是首个面向文本条件晶体生成与优化的基准测试。

Conclusion: ALM通过连续桥接实现语言模型嵌入到原子扩散引导空间的直接映射，打破了语言与原子结构之间的模态壁垒，为文本驱动的材料生成与优化提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Atomistic structure and natural language have long been modeled separately, with language models either calling atomistic models as tools or being fine-tuned on lossy textual encodings that discard atomistic information. We introduce Atomistic Language Models (ALMs) to pursue native multimodality, in which a single language backbone understands atomistic structures, generates materials from natural language, and optimizes crystal structures as instructed by text. By unifying a pretrained atomistic encoder, large language model, and denoising diffusion model through purely continuous projectors and staged training, ALMs achieve state-of-the-art results on crystal structure prediction and de novo generation. ALMs are enabled by a continuous bridge that maps language model embeddings directly into the steering space of atomistic diffusion, and are assisted by Text-to-Crystal Feynman-Kac (T2C-FK), a particle-based sampler that scores partial denoising trajectories to enforce stoichiometric targets at inference time. To evaluate the ability of ALMs to optimize and generate materials from natural-language prompts and 3D atom-coordinate inputs, we introduce ALM Bench, the first benchmark for text-conditioned crystal generation and optimization. Code, training data, and model weights will be released soon.

</details>


### [268] [Substitution-Based Analysis of Structural Novelty for Generative Models of Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23166)
*Masahiro Negishi,Aron Walsh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过开发一种工作流评估AI生成的晶体材料是否真正扩展了材料搜索空间，发现81-92%的AI生成晶体要么是训练集的重复结构，要么可通过元素替换得到，表明当前生成模型在高对称区域偏向已知结构原型，但在低对称区域仍可实现一定探索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式人工智能（generative artificial intelligence）模型在无机晶体设计领域取得了快速进展，能够高效生成大量候选化合物。但学术界尚不清楚这类模型是否真正扩展了可搜索的材料空间，抑或只是重复了传统的元素替换（elemental substitution）策略。本文旨在量化评估AI生成晶体的原创性与探索能力。

Method: 开发了一套系统化的评估工作流，将AI生成的晶体分为三类：训练集重复（duplicates）、可通过元素替换从训练结构导出的结构（substitution-derived）、以及不符合上述任一标准的新结构（unmatched）。将该工作流应用于多个具有代表性的生成模型。

Result: 在化学有效且亚稳态（metastable）的AI生成晶体中，81-92%属于训练重复或元素替换导出结构。这一倾向在高对称（high-symmetry）晶系中尤为明显，尽管许多结构原型（structural prototypes）尚未被探索。低对称新结构本质上是训练数据密集区域的插值（interpolation），而高对称重复结构则源于训练稀疏区域的记忆（memorisation）。

Conclusion: 当前生成模型存在局限性：在高对称区域偏向已知结构原型，限制了真正的结构创新；但在低对称结构空间（low-symmetry structural space）中仍具备更广泛的探索能力。研究结果指出了未来改进生成模型的方向。

Abstract: There has been rapid progress in generative artificial intelligence (AI) models for inorganic crystal design, which can efficiently generate large numbers of candidate compounds after being trained on databases of known crystals. However, it remains unclear whether they genuinely expand the accessible materials search space beyond conventional strategies such as elemental substitution within known structure types. We address this question by developing a workflow to assess whether AI-generated crystals are duplicates of training structures, reproducible by elemental substitution, or unmatched by either criterion. Applying this workflow to representative generative models reveals that 81-92% of chemically valid and metastable generated crystals are either training duplicates or substitution-derived structures. This tendency is particularly strong in high-symmetry crystal systems, even though many possible structural prototypes remain unexplored. Further analysis of the underlying structural fingerprints shows that low-symmetry structures beyond duplication or substitution can be interpreted as interpolation in training-data-rich regions, while high-symmetry duplicates appear to result from memorisation in training-sparse regions. Our findings highlight a limitation in the current generation of models that exhibit a bias towards known structural prototypes in the high symmetry regions, but enable wider exploration of the low-symmetry structural space.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.dis-nn'></div>
