### [306] [On background fields and a cutoff in sigma models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23088)
*N. V. Kharuk*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文以海森堡群（Heisenberg group）上的二维非线性 sigma 模型（two-dimensional nonlinear sigma model）为例，比较了两种手征场（chiral field）分解为背景部分与涨落部分的方案。结果表明仅有一种方案与通过引入背景场（background field）构造生成泛函（generating functional）的方式一致。此外，本文进行了量子作用量（quantum action）的单圈重整化（one-loop renormalization）、双圈近似下的幂律奇异性（power-law singularities）计算，并考虑了向扩展经典作用量（extended classical action）的过渡。最后，在背景场方法（background field method）框架下研究了截断（cutoff）与特殊泛函关系的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在手征场理论中，将场分解为背景部分与涨落部分存在不同方案，但并非所有方案都能保证生成泛函构造的自洽性。本文旨在通过具体的二维非线性 sigma 模型实例，比较并验证哪种分解方法与背景场方法的理论框架兼容。

Method: 以海森堡群上的二维非线性 sigma 模型为测试平台，对比两种不同的手征场分解方法；通过背景场方法构造生成泛函，检验分解方案的自洽性；在此基础上进行单圈重整化、双圈近似下的幂律奇异性分析以及向扩展经典作用量的过渡研究；最后在背景场框架内检验截断与特殊泛函关系的相容性。

Result: 两种手征场分解方案中，仅有一种方法与通过背景场引入生成泛函的构造方式一致。在单圈层次上完成了量子作用量的重整化，并在双圈近似下计算了幂律奇异性。同时，论文考察了向扩展经典作用量的过渡，并在背景场方法框架下验证了截断与特殊泛函关系的一致性。

Conclusion: 在手征场分解中，只有正确的分解方案才能保证背景场方法框架下的理论自洽性；本文的分析为非线性 sigma 模型的量子修正和重整化提供了可操作的检验途径。

Abstract: In this paper, using the example of a two-dimensional nonlinear sigma model with the Heisenberg group, we compare two variants of chiral field decomposition into a background part and a fluctuation. It is shown that only one of these methods is consistent with the construction of the generating functional by introducing a background field. Furthermore, we perform a one-loop renormalization of the quantum action, calculate power-law singularities in the two-loop approximation, and consider transition to an extended classical action. Finally, we study the consistency of the cutoff with special functional relations within the framework of the background field method.

</details>


### [307] [Bounds on nonlinear electrodynamics via resummed relative entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23323)
*Pietro Conzinu,Daiki Ueda*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过背景电磁场中的相对熵（relative entropy）研究非线性电动力学有效场论（EFT），发现弱耦合下相对熵非负性对高维算符有限截断施加符号约束，强耦合下的相对熵违反可区分微扰截断失效（perturbative breakdown）与物理不稳定性（如Schwinger效应），并利用重求和相对熵的非负性推导出更广泛的紫外完备化（UV completion）约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 系统性探测非线性电动力学有效场论中高维算符的无穷层级结构，并建立统一框架来诊断微扰一致性与非微扰稳定性。

Method: 在背景电磁场中计算相对熵，综合运用微扰分析、Borel--Laplace重求和（Borel–Laplace resummation）技术以及Schwinger固有时间方法（Schwinger proper-time method）等非微扰方法，研究费米子QED、标量QED和Dirac-Born-Infeld理论。

Result: 弱耦合下相对熵非负性要求有限截断的高维算符满足符号约束，推广了领先EFT系数的正定性界（positivity bounds）；强耦合下微扰分析中的相对熵违反标志EFT截断展开失效，而重求和或非微扰相对熵的违反则指示物理不稳定性（如Schwinger效应）；对于具有阶乘或幂律增长EFT系数的紫外完备化，非负重求和相对熵导出一般性约束。

Conclusion: 相对熵为非线性电动力学有效场论提供了统一诊断工具，同时涵盖微扰一致性和非微扰稳定性的检验。

Abstract: We investigate nonlinear electrodynamic effective field theories (EFTs) through the relative entropy evaluated in suitable background electromagnetic fields. In this setup, the relative entropy encodes information about the infinite tower of higher-dimensional operators and provides a systematic probe of nonlinear EFT effects. We study these features in fermionic QED, scalar QED, and Dirac-Born-Infeld theory using perturbative analyses, resummation techniques such as Borel--Laplace resummation, and non-perturbative approaches including the Schwinger proper-time method. In the weak-coupling regime, we show that the non-negativity of the perturbative relative entropy imposes sign constraints on finite truncations of higher-dimensional operators, generalizing familiar positivity bounds on leading EFT coefficients. We further show that violations of non-negativity in the strong-coupling regime admit qualitatively different interpretations depending on the framework: perturbatively analyzed violations diagnose the breakdown of the truncated EFT expansion, whereas violations in resummed or genuinely non-perturbative relative entropy signal physical instabilities of the system, such as the Schwinger effect. Extending the analysis to broader classes of UV completions, including theories with factorial or power-law growth of EFT coefficients, we derive general constraints on nonlinear electrodynamic EFT effects from the non-negativity of the resummed relative entropy. Our results suggest that relative entropy provides a unified diagnostic of perturbative consistency and non-perturbative stability in nonlinear EFTs.

</details>


### [308] [NLO Angular Impulse and Leading Singularities to all orders in spin for Kerr Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23450)
*Lucas Haiashi,Gabriel Menezes*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用Kosower-Maybee-O'Connell (KMOC)形式论，基于on-shell散射振幅和主导奇点（leading singularities），计算了Kerr黑洞散射中的次领头阶（NLO）角冲量（自旋kick），得到了自旋变量全阶有效的紧凑表达式，并通过多种一致性检验验证了结果的正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在双黑洞散射问题中，精确计算自旋相关的经典可观测量对于引力波物理至关重要。现有方法在自旋效应的高阶处理上存在局限，亟需发展基于振幅的现代方法来自洽地提取自旋贡献。

Method: 采用KMOC形式论，结合on-shell散射振幅和主导奇点技术，直接从量子振幅中提取经典可观测量。在积分核层面推导出自旋变量全阶有效的紧凑表达式，并通过三角主导奇点（triangle leading singularities）提取对应的非相对论引力势。

Result: 获得了Kerr黑洞散射中自旋相关的NLO角冲量（自旋kick）的紧凑表达式，该表达式在自旋变量中保持全阶有效性，并在适当极限下退化为已知结果。保守部分在2PM（post-Minkowskian）阶同时保持了协变自旋补充条件（covariant spin supplementary condition）和自旋大小守恒；二次自旋的保守结果与现有的径向作用量（radial-action）结果一致。

Conclusion: 本研究进一步证实了基于振幅的方法在经典引力动力学中的高效性，凸显了KMOC形式论作为计算双黑洞散射中自旋相关观测量的强大框架。

Abstract: We compute the next-to-leading order (NLO) angular impulse (spin kick) in the scattering of Kerr black holes using the Kosower--Maybee--O'Connell (KMOC) formalism. Our approach is based on on-shell scattering amplitudes and leading singularities, allowing for a direct extraction of classical observables from quantum amplitudes. We derive compact expressions for the spin-dependent angular impulse valid to all orders in the spin variables at the integrand level, and show that these results reduce to known expressions in the appropriate limits. We perform detailed consistency checks: the conservative result preserves both the covariant spin supplementary condition and the spin magnitude through 2PM order, and the quadratic-in-spin conservative result agrees with existing radial-action results after translating between the direct KMOC spin kick and the radial-action observable. In addition, we extract the corresponding non-relativistic gravitational potential from the triangle leading singularities, obtaining a representation that resums spin effects and reproduces the known spin-orbit interaction at linear order. Our results provide further evidence for the efficiency of amplitude-based methods in classical gravitational dynamics, and highlight the KMOC formalism as a powerful framework for computing spin-dependent observables in binary black hole scattering.

</details>


### [309] [Geometric and Statistical Thermo Field Dynamics in de Sitter Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23484)
*D. S. Cabral,L. A. S. Evangelista,J. C. R. de Souza,A. F. Santos*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文基于热场动力学（Thermo Field Dynamics）发展了德西特时空中非最小耦合标量场的热形式理论，揭示了宇宙学视界引起的几何倍增与内禀热浴引起的统计倍增之间的统一框架，并分析了不同观测者参考系下的粒子产生与热力学演化行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 德西特（de Sitter）时空中，共动观测者（comoving observer）与静态观测者（static observer）对同一量子态的真空态和热态感知不同：共动观测者将Bunch–Davies态视为真空，而静态观测者将其视为处于Gibbons–Hawking温度下的热浴。这种观测者依赖性（observer dependence）促使作者发展一种能够同时描述视界诱导效应与内禀热效应的统一热形式框架。

Method: 基于热场动力学（Thermo Field Dynamics）构建热形式理论，将宇宙学视界（cosmological horizon）引起的几何倍增（geometric doubling）与内禀热浴（intrinsic thermal bath）导致的统计倍增（statistical doubling）相结合，分析了Bogoliubov角的时间演化，并在共动和静态两种参考系下计算了对应的粒子数密度。

Result: 在辐射极限（radiation limit）下，共动系中的粒子数密度守恒，其热力学演化与宇宙微波背景辐射（Cosmic Microwave Background）一致；而在静态系中，有限温度效应会激发Parker粒子产生。对于大质量且非最小耦合的场，几何温度与统计温度之间的相互作用产生了一个特征热标度（characteristic thermal scale），并表现出对初始条件的非平凡依赖性。

Conclusion: 倍增程序（doubling procedure）并非纯粹的数学技巧，而是全局因果结构（global causal structure of spacetime）与有限温度效应（finite-temperature effects）的共同体现。该工作为描述同时存在视界诱导热效应与内禀热效应的德西特时空量子场提供了一个统一的理论框架。

Abstract: The dynamics of a massive scalar field non-minimally coupled to gravity in an expanding de Sitter universe are investigated. It is shown that a comoving observer identifies the Bunch--Davies state as the vacuum, whereas a static observer perceives the same state as a thermal bath at the Gibbons--Hawking temperature. Motivated by this observer dependence, a thermal formulation based on Thermo Field Dynamics is developed by combining the geometric doubling associated with the cosmological horizon with the statistical doubling induced by a intrinsec thermal bath. The resulting construction reveals that the doubling procedure is not merely a mathematical artifact, but rather a manifestation of the global causal structure of spacetime together with finite-temperature effects. The temporal evolution of the Bogoliubov angle is analyzed and the corresponding particle number densities are evaluated in both comoving and static frames. In the radiation limit, the comoving number density remains conserved, providing a thermodynamic evolution consistent with that of the Cosmic Microwave Background, whereas in the static frame finite-temperature effects sti\-mulate Parker particle creation. For massive and non-minimally coupled fields, the interplay between geometric and statistical temperatures gives rise to a characteristic thermal scale and a nontrivial dependence on the initial conditions. These results provide a unified framework for describing quantum fields in de Sitter spacetime in the presence of both apparent horizon-induced and intrinsec thermal effects.

</details>


### [310] [Microscopic entropy of de Sitter spacetime and entropic solution to the old cosmological constant problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23522)
*Mariano Cadoni,Lorenzo Herres,Lorenzo Orlando,Mirko Pitzalis*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文通过外尔对称性破缺（Weyl symmetry breaking）将共形引力（conformal gravity）与爱因斯坦引力（Einstein gravity）联系起来，提出一个由德西特（de Sitter）与普朗克尺度之比定义的无量纲耦合常数α可被解释为德西特时空的贝肯斯坦-霍金熵（Bekenstein-Hawking entropy）。结合泛函重整化群（functional renormalization group）、全息原理（holography）和涌现引力（emergent gravity）的思想，论文将α理解为德西特视界微观自由度的度量，并要求其重整化群流（renormalization group flow）在红外方向单调递增，从而得到与观测值一致的宇宙学常数（cosmological constant），提出一种基于熵的旧宇宙学常数问题解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决旧宇宙学常数问题（old cosmological constant problem），即为何观测到的宇宙学常数远小于理论预期值。

Method: 通过研究外尔对称性破缺将共形引力约化为爱因斯坦引力，引入无量纲耦合常数α作为德西特与普朗克尺度之比；结合泛函重整化群、全息原理和涌现引力框架，将α重新解释为德西特视界微观自由度的度量，并分析其重整化群流α(k)的尺度依赖行为。

Result: 发现α可自然解释为德西特时空的贝肯斯坦-霍金熵；要求α(k)的红外重整化群流单调递增，将导致与观测值同量级的宇宙学常数。

Conclusion: 观测到的极小宇宙学常数可直接归因于德西特宇宙中极其庞大的微观自由度数，从而为旧宇宙学常数问题提供了一种基于熵的解释方案。

Abstract: We study the role of Weyl symmetry breaking in conformal gravity and the residual scale symmetry of Einstein gravity. The corresponding action is characterized by a dimensionless coupling $α$, determined by the ratio between the de Sitter and Planck scales. We show that this quantity admits a natural interpretation as the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy of de Sitter spacetime. Combining ideas from the functional renormalization group, holography, and emergent gravity, we propose a microscopic interpretation of $α$ as a measure of the degrees of freedom associated with the de Sitter horizon. In this framework, the renormalization group flow of $α(k)$ encodes the scale dependence of these microscopic degrees of freedom. Requiring this flow to be monotonically increasing toward the infrared leads to a cosmological constant of the same order as the observed one, suggesting an entropic solution to the old cosmological constant problem. This remarkably small value can therefore be understood as a direct consequence of the extraordinarily large number of degrees of freedom in our de Sitter universe.

### [311] [One-loop contributions in Lorentz-violating scalar QED with nonminimal coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23523)
*F. M. Belchior,J. R. Nascimento,A. Yu. Petrov,P. Porfirio*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在微扰洛伦兹破缺（Lorentz-violating, LV）理论框架下，计算了包含量纲为五的CPT奇非最小耦合（CPT-odd nonminimal coupling）的标量QED（scalar QED）的单圈两点函数发散部分，验证了规范不变性（gauge invariance）并给出了LV反项（LV counterterms）结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究洛伦兹破缺（Lorentz-violating, LV）理论中非最小耦合（nonminimal coupling）的微扰性质，特别是包含CPT奇（CPT-odd）量纲为五算符的标量QED（scalar QED）模型，以检验其规范不变性（gauge invariance）和重整化（renormalization）行为。

Method: 模型通过广义协变导数（generalized covariant derivative）定义，该导数包含常数背景矢量（constant background vector）和对偶电磁场强（dual electromagnetic field strength）。展开作用量后，推导出光子和标量自能（self-energy）相关的全部顶点（vertices），包括由规范不变性要求的混合最小-非最小海鸥相互作用图（mixed minimal-nonminimal seagull interaction diagram）。采用维数正规化（dimensional regularization）计算真空极化（vacuum polarization）和标量自能的发散部分。

Result: 完整的光子两点函数（photon two-point function）是横向的（transverse），因为由混合图和纯非最小泡泡图（bubble graphs）产生的质量依赖项与相应的海鸥图（seagull graphs）相互抵消，仅留下高阶导数的CPT奇和CPT偶LV规范反项（LV gauge counterterms）。标量自能（scalar self-energy）产生了LV动能和高阶导数反项（LV kinetic and higher-derivative counterterms）。

Conclusion: 计算确认规范不变性（gauge invariance）得到保持，同时非最小耦合（nonminimal interaction）应在有效场论展开（effective-field-theory expansion）的框架内理解。

Abstract: In the context of pertubative aspects of Lorentz-violating theories, we study the divergent one-loop two-point functions of a Lorentz-violating (LV) extension of scalar QED containing a dimension-five CPT-odd nonminimal coupling. The model is defined through a generalized covariant derivative involving a constant background vector and the dual electromagnetic field strength. After expanding the action, we derive the full set of vertices relevant for the photon and scalar self-energies, including the mixed minimal-nonminimal seagull interaction diagram required by the gauge invariance. Using dimensional regularization, we compute the divergent parts of the vacuum polarization and scalar self-energy. The complete photon two-point function is shown to be transverse since the mass-dependent pieces generated by the mixed and purely nonminimal bubble graphs cancel against the corresponding seagull graphs, leaving higher-derivative CPT-odd and CPT-even LV gauge counterterms. The scalar self-energy generates LV kinetic and higher-derivative counterterms. The calculation confirms that gauge invariance is preserved, while the nonminimal interaction should be understood within an effective-field-theory expansion.

</details>

Method: 通过引入CP^1作用的BPS涡旋，构造一种涡旋变形的Nariai瞬子作为正则欧几里得瞬子，该瞬子的欧几里得几何形如S^2×Σ，其中Σ的几何由涡旋构型决定。

Result: 衰减率受离散拓扑荷控制，证明物质涡旋为de Sitter空间打开了一个拓扑组织的新衰变通道族。

Conclusion: 物质涡旋的存在使得de Sitter空间存在一类新的、受拓扑荷调控的衰变通道，丰富了de Sitter衰变的理论图景。

Abstract: We study the decay of de Sitter space into black holes whose horizons are dressed by BPS vortices of a $\mathrm{CP}^1$ action. The process is mediated by a regular Euclidean instanton obtained as a vortex-deformed generalization of the Nariai instanton. Its Euclidean geometry has the form $S^2\timesΣ$, where $Σ$ is a compact surface whose geometry is shaped by the vortex configuration. The resulting decay rates are controlled by a discrete topological charge, showing that matter vortices open a new topologically organized family of decay channels for de Sitter space.

### [313] [Perturbative Approach to Nonlinear Capacitance Matrix Formulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20821)
*Habib Ammari,Clemens Thalhammer*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究三维高对比度夹杂物中的非线性亥姆霍兹系统，利用狄利克雷-诺伊曼算子和电容形式主义建立了与有限离散非线性电容系统之间的严格双向对应关系，并给出了亚波长和非亚波长区域的高阶修正算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了理解非线性高对比度夹杂物中孤立子（soliton）的涌现机制，特别是在对比度参数δ趋近于零时的行为，需要一个严格的数学框架来衔接连续系统与离散近似。

Method: 通过狄利克雷-诺伊曼算子（Dirichlet-to-Neumann operator）和电容形式主义（capacitance formalism），构建了一个以$\sqrtδ$为幂次的微扰级联展开，将共振频率和场展开。同时引入频率相关的电容矩阵（frequency-dependent capacitance matrix）处理非亚波长区域。

Result: 建立了连续孤立子与有限离散非线性电容系统之间的严格双向对应关系：每个离散解可提升为一个连续孤立子（展开式在$\sqrtδ$中解析收敛），每个满足自然亚波长缩放的连续族可约化为离散解。在对称二聚体（dimer）中数值表征了一个对称性破缺分岔（symmetry-breaking bifurcation）。

Conclusion: 该构造是算法化的，能够给出亚波长（subwavelength）和非亚波长（non-subwavelength）区域的高阶修正，为非线性高对比度系统中的孤立子分析提供了严格且可计算的理论工具。

Abstract: We study a nonlinear Helmholtz system with cubic nonlinearity on high-contrast inclusions in three dimensions, and the solitons that emerge as the contrast $δ$ tends to zero. Using the Dirichlet-to-Neumann operator and a capacitance formalism, we develop a perturbative cascade that expands the resonant frequency and field in powers of $\sqrtδ$. Our main result is a rigorous two-way correspondence with a finite discrete nonlinear capacitance system: every discrete solution lifts to a continuous soliton (a convergent expansion, analytic in $\sqrtδ$), and every continuous family with the natural subwavelength scaling reduces to a discrete one. The construction is algorithmic, giving higher-order corrections in both the subwavelength and non-subwavelength regimes, the latter via a frequency-dependent capacitance matrix. We illustrate the theory numerically and characterise a symmetry-breaking bifurcation in a symmetric dimer.

</details>


### [314] [Advancing fronts for the thin-film equation with null slip and repulsive potentials: the case of partial wetting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20834)
*Riccardo Durastanti,Lorenzo Giacomelli*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明：在部分润湿（partial wetting）条件下，具有零滑移和特定排斥势的薄液膜方程（thin-film equation）存在单参数族的行波解（travelling-wave solutions），该解具有接触线（contact line）且呈对数修正线性行为，从而表明温和排斥势能有效解决无滑移悖论（no-slip paradox）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无滑移边界条件在接触线动力学中会导致非物理的应力奇异性（即“无滑移悖论”），本文旨在证明使用形式上为 $P(h)\approx h^{1-m}$（$m>1$）的排斥势（repulsive potentials）可以在零滑移条件下消除这一奇异性，并提供严格数学证明。

Method: 采用分析动力学方法，研究薄液膜方程（thin-film equation）在部分润湿 regime 下，对零滑移（zero slip）和特定幂律排斥势的定常行进波解（travelling-wave solutions）的存在性与性质，并考察其耗散率与能量有限性条件。

Result: 对于任意 $m>1$，耗散率（rate of dissipation）局部有限；对于任意 $m\in (1,3)$，能量（energy）局部有限。行波解具有对数修正的线性渐近行为（$h\to +\infty$），且接触线条件若 $P\equiv 0$ 则退化为经典固定微观接触角条件。

Conclusion: 温和排斥势能够在零滑移框架下有效消除接触线处的奇异性，从而从数学上确认了基于排斥势的润湿模型可以解决无滑移悖论，且模型具有热力学一致性（thermodynamically consistent）。

Abstract: For negative values of the spreading coefficient (that is, in the so-called ``partial wetting'' regime), we prove that the thin-film equation with zero slip and repulsive potentials $P$ of the form $P(h)\approx h^{1-m}$ as $h\to 0$, $m>1$, admits for any positive speed a one-parameter family of travelling-wave solutions with a contact line and (as in standard slippage models) a logarithmically-corrected linear behaviour as $h\to +\infty$. These waves have locally finite rate of dissipation for any $m>1$ and locally finite energy for any $m\in (1,3)$. The result thus confirms that mildly repulsive potentials effectively resolve the no-slip paradox. The family is parametrized by a thermodynamically consistent contact-line condition which reduces to the classical fixed microscopic contact-angle one if $P\equiv 0$.

</details>


### [315] [On the traces of the L_2-solution of a general linear differential equation in the domain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21612)
*Burskii V. P*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对光滑有界区域上具有光滑系数的一般线性微分方程的边值问题（boundary value problem）提出了新进展，重点探讨了解在边界上的迹（trace）性质，给出了通过迹和方程右端项重构解的条�，并在常系数情形下将这些条件归结为广义矩问题（generalized moment problem）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在推进一般线性微分方程边值问题的通论（general theory），特别是对解在边界上的迹属性进行系统研究，以填补现有理论在边界性质方面的空白。

Method: 采用解析方法研究光滑有界区域上光滑系数的一般线性微分方程，通过分析解在边界上的迹条件（trace conditions），建立从迹和方程右端项重构解的数学框架；在常系数情形下，将所得迹条件转化为广义矩问题的形式。

Result: 给出了解在区域边界上的迹所满足的条件；在常系数情形下，这些条件进一步表现为广义矩问题。

Conclusion: 本文在一般线性微分方程边值问题的通论中取得了新进展，为通过边界迹和方程右端项重构解提供了理论依据，并将常系数情形下的问题与广义矩问题相联系。

Abstract: This paper pertains to the general theory of boundary value problems for general linear differential equations with smooth coefficients in a bounded domain with a smooth boundary and contains new advances in the general theory related to the boundary properties of solutions. Specifically, conditions on the traces of a solution to a general differential equation on the boundary of the domain are found and studied, allowing the solution to be reconstructed from its traces and the right-hand side of the equation. For the case of a general equation with constant coefficients, the resulting conditions on the traces of the solution take the form of a generalized moment problem.

</details>


### [316] [Geometric Structures of Pseudo-Sonic Curves in Self-Similar Solutions of the Euler Equations for Potential Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21793)
*Gui-Qiang G. Chen,Mikhail Feldman,Xin Gao,Wei Xiang*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对势流欧拉方程（Euler equations for potential flow）的二维自相似解（self-similar solutions）中伪声速曲线（pseudo-sonic curve）的几何结构，建立严格的解析分析方法。研究表明，当伪速度（pseudo-velocity）处处垂直于曲线时，伪声速曲线必为圆；在非垂直的一般情形下，分析了曲线附近流线的几何性质。进一步给出了伪速度垂直于曲线的充分条件，并将理论应用于非均匀来流的激波反射-绕射问题（shock reflection-diffraction problem），证明了在均匀来流解的小扰动下伪声速曲线必为圆弧，且解在伪亚声速区域（pseudo-subsonic region）达到$C^{2,\alpha}$正则性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自相似解中伪声速曲线（pseudo-sonic curve）的几何结构是混合型偏微分方程（mixed hyperbolic-elliptic type）的关键退化界面，对其几何特征的严格分析有助于理解非均匀超声速状态下势流欧拉方程（Euler equations for potential flow）解的结构性质。

Method: 建立严格的解析分析方法：首先证明伪速度（pseudo-velocity）处处为曲线法线时伪声速曲线必为圆；然后分析一般情形下曲线附近流线（streamlines）的几何性质；进而建立两个定理给出伪速度垂直于曲线的充分条件；最后将理论应用于激波反射-绕射问题（shock reflection-diffraction problem），考虑$C^2$小扰动情形。

Result: 伪声速曲线在伪速度处处法向时必为圆；在非均匀来流的激波反射-绕射问题中，若解是均匀来流解的$C^2$小扰动，则伪声速曲线必为圆弧，密度和速度分别对应于圆弧的半径和中心；解在伪亚声速区域（pseudo-subsonic region）中达到$C^{2,\alpha}$正则性（在声速圆弧上除点$P_1$外）。

Conclusion: 建立了伪声速曲线几何结构的精确刻画，所发展的解析方法和技术有望应用于其他涉及类似混合型退化（mixed-type degeneracy）的非线性问题。

Abstract: We are concerned with the geometric structures of pseudo-sonic curves in two-dimensional self-similar solutions for the Euler equations for potential flow, allowing for non-uniform supersonic states. Mathematically, the governing second-order potential flow equation is of mixed hyperbolic-elliptic type, with degeneracy occurring along the pseudo-sonic curve. In this paper, we develop rigorous analytical approaches to analyze the geometric structures of pseudo-sonic curves in such self-similar solutions. We first show that the pseudo-sonic curve is necessarily a circle if the pseudo-velocity at each point is a normal to the curve. We then analyze the general case in which the pseudo-velocity on the pseudo-sonic point is not a normal to the curve, and study the geometric properties of streamlines in a neighborhood of the pseudo-sonic curve. Next, we establish two theorems that provide sufficient conditions ensuring that the pseudo-velocity at a pseudo-sonic point is normal to the curve, under natural assumptions on the local behavior of the solution. These results yield a precise characterization of the geometry of pseudo-sonic curves. Finally, we apply the developed theory to the shock reflection-diffraction problem with non-uniform incoming flow. We prove that the pseudo-sonic curve must be an arc if the solution is a $C^2$-small perturbation, either in the pseudo-supersonic or pseudo-subsonic region, of a solution with uniform incoming flow. In particular, the density and velocity must be constant, corresponding to the radius and the center of the pseudo-sonic arc, respectively. Moreover, we prove that the solution is $C^{2,α}$-regular in the pseudo-subsonic region up to the sonic arc (except at point $P_1$). The techniques and ideas developed in this paper are expected to be applicable to other nonlinear problems involving similar mixed-type degeneracies.

</details>


### [317] [Absence of eigenvalues of dissipative operator for strictly convex obstacles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21958)
*Vesselin Petkov*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明了一个猜想：对于具有耗散边界条件的波动方程，在严格凸有界区域外部（奇数维数d≥3），当边界上的耗散系数γ(x)满足0<γ(x)<1时，生成压缩半群V(t)=e^{tG}的算子G不存在特征值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者在先前工作[10]中已证明，当γ为常数且区域为三维单位球外部时，算子G无特征值；本文的目标是将这一结论推广至任意严格凸有界障碍物情形，从而验证此前提出的猜想。

Method: 采用数学分析中的半群理论与边界值问题方法，研究严格凸有界区域外部、奇数维空间（d≥3）中具有耗散边界条件∂_ν u - γ(x) ∂_t u = 0的波动方程，其中0<γ(x)<1。

Result: 成功证明了对于任意严格凸有界障碍物K ⊂ ℝ^d（d≥3且为奇数），在边界耗散系数γ(x)严格介于0和1之间的条件下，压缩半群V(t)的生成元G不存在任何特征值。

Conclusion: 该结论表明，在所述条件下波动方程的解不会出现时间指数增长模式（即无特征值对应的共振态），从而拓展了对耗散边界条件下波动方程谱性质的认知。

Abstract: We study the wave equation in the exterior of a strictly convex bounded domain $K \subset {\mathbb R}^d, d \geq 3,$ odd, with dissipative boundary condition $\partial_ν u - γ(x) \partial_t u = 0$ on the boundary $Γ$ and $0 < γ(x) <1, \:\forall x \in Γ.$ The solutions are described by a contraction semigroup $V(t) = e^{tG}, \: t \geq 0.$ In [10] we established that for $γ\equiv const$ and $K = \{x \in {\mathbb R}^3: \:|x| \leq 1\}$ the operator $G$ has no eigenvalues and we conjectured that the same result holds for every strictly convex obstacle. In this paper we prove this conjecture.

</details>


### [318] [A Classical Elliptic Regularity Approach to Almost Harmonic Maps and Related Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22468)
*Giovanni Di Fratta*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对二维非线性椭圆系统建立了一个统一的内部正则性分析框架，基于Campanato型离散迭代与Caccioppoli型估计，在无需经典对偶、Wente不等式、移动标架或共形均匀化等工具的条件下，自动导出满足离散振荡衰减公理的解映射的局部Hölder连续性，并将该方法应用于几乎调和映射及带一般连接形式的系统，推广了现有理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维非线性椭圆系统（two-dimensional nonlinear elliptic systems）的正则性（regularity）问题长期依赖于$\mathcal{H}^1$–$\mathrm{BMO}$对偶、Wente不等式、移动标架（moving frames）和共形均匀化（conformal uniformization）等复杂技术。这些方法存在适用范围受限、推导繁琐等不足，尤其难以处理超出规范理论（gauge-theoretic）框架的系统。作者旨在建立一种纯解析的统一抽象框架，以简化并推广正则性理论。

Method: 方法的核心是一个基于Campanato型离散迭代方案（Campanato-type discrete iteration scheme）与Caccioppoli型估计（Caccioppoli-type estimate）的抽象框架。通过在允许对$(\boldsymbol{u}, \boldsymbol{f})$上定义离散振荡衰减公理（discrete oscillation-decay axiom），并保证该类在尺度变换下稳定，进而在无需任何几何或调和分析辅助工具的条件下，直接证明$\boldsymbol{u}$的局部Hölder连续性。

Result: 首先，在抽象框架下证明了解映射$\boldsymbol{u}$自动满足局部Hölder连续（locally Hölder continuous），且所得到的Hölder指数（Hölder exponent）是显式的，并最优地达到由源项$\boldsymbol{f}$的Lebesgue可积性（Lebesgue integrability）所决定的经典Morrey–Campanato阈值。其次，将该原理应用于现有规范理论无法覆盖的领域：一是为几乎调和映射（almost harmonic maps）$-\Delta\boldsymbol{u} = |\nabla \boldsymbol{u}|^2 \boldsymbol{u} + \boldsymbol{f}$ 进入$\mathbb{S}^n$的情形给出了直接的正则性证明；二是将系统的连接形式$Ω\in L^2$的几何反对称条件替换为纯解析条件$\mathrm{div}Ω\in L^q\,(q>1)$，推广了体系的适用范围。

Conclusion: 本文提出的抽象框架系统地避免了传统正则性理论中依赖的多种调和分析与几何技术，为二维非线性椭圆系统的内部正则性提供了一种更简洁、统一的路径。该方法不仅能够覆盖已知结果，还可推广到规范理论方法无法处理的新情形，表明基于离散振荡衰减与尺度稳定性的纯解析策略具有广泛的适用性和理论潜力。

Abstract: We establish interior regularity results for a broad class of two-dimensional nonlinear elliptic systems. Our approach isolates the core integrability mechanism within a unified abstract framework built around a Campanato-type discrete iteration scheme coupled with a Caccioppoli-type estimate. Specifically, we show that within any class of admissible pairs $(\boldsymbol{u}, \boldsymbol{f})$ that is stable under rescaling and satisfies a discrete oscillation-decay axiom, the map $\boldsymbol{u}$ is automatically locally Hölder continuous. Furthermore, the resulting Hölder exponent is explicit and optimally attains the classical Morrey--Campanato threshold dictated by the Lebesgue integrability of the source term $\boldsymbol{f}$. This purely analytic framework systematically avoids the $\mathcal{H}^1$--$\mathrm{BMO}$ duality, Wente's inequality, moving frames, and conformal uniformization techniques that underpin existing regularity theories.
  We apply this principle to derive regularity results in regimes lying strictly beyond the reach of existing gauge-theoretic methods. As a foundational example, we provide a new direct proof of local Hölder continuity for almost harmonic maps $-Δ\boldsymbol{u} = |\nabla \boldsymbol{u}|^2 \boldsymbol{u} + \boldsymbol{f}$ into $\mathbb{S}^n$ with $L^q$-integrable tension fields. We then extend the analysis to systems of the form $-Δ\boldsymbol{u} = Ω\cdot \nabla \boldsymbol{u} + \boldsymbol{f}$, replacing geometric antisymmetry assumption on the connection form $Ω\in L^2$ with the purely analytic condition $\mathrm{div} Ω\in L^q$ for some $q>1$...

</details>

### [321] [Study of Cosmic Acceleration of the Universe in the Presence of Bulk Viscous Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20759)
*Dheeraj Singh Rana*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本论文研究了基于非黎曼几何（non-Riemannian geometry）的修正引力理论，特别是包含体粘滞（bulk viscosity）的 f(Q) 引力模型。通过理论推导和观测数据约束，发现粘性 f(Q) 引力模型能够成功解释宇宙晚期加速膨胀，并能再现从物质主导时期到加速膨胀阶段的不同宇宙演化阶段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文在 f(Q) 引力框架内引入体粘滞（bulk viscosity）流体模型，首先探索粘性流体模型在 f(Q) 引力中的精确宇宙学解，并利用观测数据集约束其自由参数；随后对若干类非线性粘性 f(Q) 引力模型进行动力系统（dynamical systems）分析和观测分析。

Result: 所提出的粘性 f(Q) 引力模型能够成功解释宇宙晚期加速膨胀。通过约束后的模型，论文进一步研究了宇宙膨胀的演化历史，并验证了这些模型在宇宙学上的可行性，确认它们能够再现从物质主导时期到加速膨胀阶段的不同演化阶段。

Conclusion: 基于非黎曼几何的粘性 f(Q) 引力模型是广义相对论有潜力的替代方案，能够有效描述宇宙晚期加速膨胀并复现多阶段宇宙演化历史，为修正引力理论的研究提供了新的可行方向。

Abstract: Over the past century, both theoretical advancements and experimental observations have established General Relativity (GR) as the most successful framework for describing gravitational phenomena. However, observations from multiple cosmological probes over the last two decades have provided compelling evidence for the accelerated expansion of the Universe. The rapid progress in observational astronomy and precision cosmology has highlighted several challenges that motivate the search for extensions or alternatives to General Relativity. In this thesis, we investigate alternative formulations of gravity based on non-Riemannian geometry, with particular emphasis on (f(Q)) gravity in the presence of bulk viscosity. We first explore the existence of exact cosmological solutions for viscous fluid models within the framework of (f(Q)) gravity and constrain the free parameters of these solutions using observational datasets. The resulting constrained models are then employed to study the evolutionary history of cosmic expansion. Our analysis demonstrates that the proposed viscous (f(Q)) gravity models can successfully account for the observed late-time acceleration of the Universe. Furthermore, we examine several classes of nonlinear viscous (f(Q)) gravity models through both dynamical systems and observational analyses. Particular attention is given to the cosmological viability of these models and their ability to reproduce the different evolutionary epochs of the Universe, ranging from matter-dominated eras to accelerated expansion phases.

### [322] [Selective enhancement of quantum decay channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20766)
*Pritam Nanda,Kinjalk Lochan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文论证在腔体边界条件（controlled boundary condition）下，产物的模式函数在红外区域获得显著增强，从而提升低能过程的衰变率，并通过共振腔几何的选择替代高能研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在自由空间中，量子粒子衰变在红外区域的模式密度不足，导致低能衰变效率受限；为提升衰变率通常需要高能区间的跃迁概率密度足够丰富。作者试图通过腔体边界调控增强低能过程的衰变率。

Method: 理论分析：比较自由空间与受控边界条件（腔体）下量子场衰变率的表现，重点分析产物场模式函数在红外（infrared）区域的支撑变化以及共振几何（resonant geometry）带来的增强效应。

Result: 腔体几何中，产物场的模式函数在红外区域获得显著支撑，提升低能过程衰变概率与速率；通过选择适当的共振腔几何，可实现衰变率的显著增强。

Conclusion: 精心选择腔体几何可作为高能研究的潜在替代方案，对量子电动力学（QED）过程及奇异新物理（exotic new physics）的研究具有直接意义。

Abstract: In the decay of quantum particles under field theoretic consideration, the decay rate is typically a convolution of the density of modes the primary field is allowed to decay into and the allowed probability density for the field to decay into such modes. In free space, though many such processes show high amplitude of such transitions towards the infrared sector, the depletion of allowed mode density in that regime arrests the efficacy of such decays at low energies. Therefore in free space, in order to enhance the decay rate, one needs the transition probability density to be rich enough towards the high energy sector where mode density support is also high enough to make the rate sufficiently large. In this work we argue that in the controlled boundary condition environment e.g. in a cavity, the mode functions of product field receive significant support towards their infrared sector, boosting the probability (and hence rates) of low energy processes. The cavity geometry offers sweet spots in terms of resonant geometry around which the interaction of a primary field with product fields receives dramatic enhancement, significantly enlarging its decay rates. Therefore, a judicious selection of cavity geometry serves as a potential substitute to studying interesting processes at high energy. The results have direct relevance for the study of QED processes and implications for the study of exotic new physics are also discussed.

</details>


### [323] [The Cosmological Constant Problem: An Accessible Introduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20778)
*Ali Kaya,Adam Lahey*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文以教学性方式介绍了宇宙学常数问题（cosmological constant problem），通过实标量场（real scalar field）展示如何计算平直时空和膨胀宇宙中的量子真空能量密度与压强，并提供了维度正规化、截断正规化和绝热正规化的详细计算。文章指出，尽管常引用的120个数量级差异未考虑正规化与重整化（regularization and renormalization），但量子场论的基本原理仍导致理论与观测的巨大失配；此外，还存在与宇宙膨胀相关的概念性挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙学常数问题是理论物理中一个长期存在的核心难题。本文的目的在于为仅具备量子场论（quantum field theory）和广义相对论（general relativity）基础知识的读者提供该问题的教学性介绍，澄清常见的误解，并指出除了数量级失配之外，还有更深层的概念性挑战。

Method: 本文采用教学性论述方式，以一个有质量实标量场（massive real scalar field）为例，分别在平直时空（flat spacetime）和膨胀宇宙（expanding universe）中计算量子真空能量密度与压强。文中提供了维度正规化（dimensional regularization）、截断正规化（cutoff regularization）和绝热正规化（adiabatic regularization）的详细计算过程。膨胀宇宙背景采用经典处理方式，未涉及量子引力效应（quantum gravitational effects）。

Result: 文章指出，尽管常被引用的120个数量级差异的数值估算并未考虑正规化与重整化过程，但量子场论的基本原理仍会导致理论预言与观测值之间存在巨大的失配。此外，文章还识别出与宇宙膨胀相关的概念性挑战，包括在某些语境中共动尺度（comoving scale）与物理尺度（physical scale）之间的选择问题，以及真空的非唯一性（non-uniqueness of vacuum）。

Conclusion: 宇宙学常数问题不仅表现为理论与观测之间巨大的数量级差异——即便考虑正规化和重整化后依然存在，更包含深层的概念性困难，尤其是膨胀宇宙中真空定义的非唯一性和尺度选择问题。这些挑战在本质上比单纯的数值失配更为根本。

Abstract: We present a pedagogical introduction to the cosmological constant problem that requires only basic knowledge of quantum field theory and general relativity. A massive real scalar field is used to illustrate how the quantum vacuum energy density and pressure can be calculated both in flat spacetime and in an expanding universe. Detailed computations are provided for dimensional, cutoff, and adiabatic regularizations. No attempt is made to address quantum gravitational effects, and the expanding-universe background is treated classically. We point out that although the commonly cited discrepancy of 120 orders of magnitude between theory and observation is based on an estimate that does not account for regularization and renormalization, fundamental principles of quantum field theory nevertheless lead to a huge mismatch. In addition to this large discrepancy, we emphasize that there are also conceptual challenges related to cosmic expansion, such as the choice between comoving and physical scales in certain contexts and the non-uniqueness of vacuum.

</details>

Abstract: We investigate a K-essence like cosmological model whose scalar-field potential is constructed from a negative power-law Sáez--Ballester potential. By means of a suitable field redefinition from $φ$ to $\varphi$, we show that the resulting field equations acquire a mathematical structure analogous to that of a previously solved Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) cosmological model. This correspondence allows us to obtain exact classical solutions for both the scale factor and the scalar field within the Hamiltonian formalism. At the quantum level, the corresponding Wheeler-DeWitt (WDW) equation is derived and exact quantum solutions are obtained. ### [326] [Scattering, Hawking Radiation and Neutrino Energy Deposition in Euler-Heisenberg Black Holes Surrounded by Perfect Fluid Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20931)

Method: 采用十三阶WKB方法辅以Padé resummation计算准正则模（quasinormal modes）频谱，并与基于光子球角频率和Lyapunov指数的eikonal预测对比；通过直接数值积分径向波动方程计算精确灰体因子（greybody factors）并与解析下界比较；同时分析吸收截面、霍金辐射谱以及中微子-反中微子湮灭通道的相对论增强效应。

Abstract: We study the dynamical and scattering properties for the Euler-Heisenberg BH surrounded by perfect fluid dark matter. The geometry contains a compact non-linear electrodynamic correction governed by the EH coupling and a logarithmic dark-matter contribution governed by the surrounding PFDM halo. We study the scalar, electromagnetic and a particular effective axial spin-2 channel constructed on the fixed EH plus PFDM background, acting as a proxy for the gravitational-like perturbation problem and not for the fully coupled gravitational perturbation problem. We compute the quasinormal-mode spectrum employing a thirteenth-order WKB method supplemented with Padé resummation and compare it with the eikonal prediction calculated in terms of the angular frequency of the photon sphere and the Lyapunov exponent. Moreover, we study the near-extremal configurations and derive a purely imaginary branch of quasinormal frequencies in the near-horizon region, whose damping rate increases with the PFDM parameter and is nearly spin-independent. We then compute exact greybody factors by direct numerical integration of the radial wave equation and compare them to analytical lower bounds. We also analyze the absorption cross sections and the Hawking emission spectra. We also calculate the relativistic enhancement of the neutrino-antineutrino annihilation channel outside the EHPFDM black hole. We find that the PFDM parameter contracts the optical structure, increases the oscillation frequency, enhances the damping rate and suppresses transmission. On the other hand, the Euler-Heisenberg correction leads to a weaker near-horizon deformation whose effect becomes relevant for sufficiently large charge. These results provide a common scattering framework for comparing the impact of dark-matter environments and nonlinear electrodynamics

### [327] [Quantum Dust from the Curse of Dimensionality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20943)
*Kenan Oggad*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文指出，多种量子引力方法在最短尺度下都得到时空二维性，可能源于态空间几何中的测度集中现象（concentration of measure），而非动力学机制；该效应使随机样本退化为等距点集（equidistant dust），扩散探针在大样本极限下将其读为二维，这是测量假象（measurement artifact）而非真实维度；通过谱维数（spectral dimension）在零附近的特征值密度分布，可区分真实维度与测量假象。作者在Lean 4中验证了相关数学结论，并提出了谱忠实性（spectral faithfulness）作为跨越涌现映射的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为什么互不相关的量子引力方法在最短尺度下都得出时空二维这一相同结果？现有理论各自在自身动力学框架内解释，本文试图寻找一条不依赖场方程（field equation）、仅基于态空间几何（geometry of the space of states）的运动学（kinematic）路径，以统一理解这一现象。

Method: 利用纯态Fubini-Study几何上的测度集中现象（concentration of measure），证明当维度增长时随机样本的成对距离趋于相等，有限样本退化为等距点集（equidistant dust），其阈值化度量图为完全图（complete graph）；扩散探针（diffusion probe）在样本数趋于无穷时将其读为二维，此为谱维数（spectral dimension）在单个弛豫标度（relaxation scale）处的取值。进一步通过Laplacian谱在零附近的特征值密度，区分真实维度与测量假象，并在Lean 4中验证相关数学结论。

Result: 等距点集的谱维数收敛于2，但这是测量假象而非结构本身的性质。谱维数是否反映真实维度由Laplacian谱在零附近的特征值密度分布决定：幂律尾（power-law tail）对应真实维度；单个标度位于能隙（gap）之上时，在其自身弛豫时间处读出二维；两标度能带（gapped two-scale band）则读出普适线（universal line）。这些分类已在图-Laplacian代理（graph-Laplacian proxies）上运行，但物理非局部算子（nonlocal operator）是否适用尚待验证。

Conclusion: 基于谱测试（spectral test）读取特征值密度在零附近的行为，可以在给定结构上区分测量假象与结构真正表达的维度；单一弛豫标度无法编码区分不同结构的谱维数；谱忠实性（spectral faithfulness）是这种读取能否跨越涌现映射（emergence map）的条件。

Abstract: Why do unrelated approaches to quantum gravity nearly all find spacetime two-dimensional at the shortest scales? Each theory answers only within its own dynamics; we highlight a single kinematic route to the same value, one assuming no field equation and living in the geometry of the space of states alone. That route is concentration of measure on the Fubini-Study geometry of pure states, which forces the pairwise distances of a random sample to equalize as the dimension grows, so any finite sample collapses to an equidistant dust whose thresholded metric graph is the complete graph. Handed this dust, a diffusion probe reads it as two-dimensional in the large-sample limit, the value the running spectral dimension takes at the dust's single relaxation scale, a property of the measurement rather than the structure; this convergence on two is not, by itself, evidence that spacetime is two-dimensional. Whether a given two is such an artifact is governed by the Laplacian spectrum near zero, and whether that reading carries across an emergence map is the condition we call spectral faithfulness; a single relaxation scale encodes no spectral dimension that tells one structure from another. The collapse, the probe value, and the eigenvalue-density criterion are machine-checked in Lean 4 against Mathlib, resting on the standard Beta law of overlaps; a power-law tail of small eigenvalues reads a genuine dimension, a single scale above a gap reads two at its own clock, and a gapped two-scale band reads off the universal line. These classes are run on graph-Laplacian proxies, and whether a link-graph reading carries to the physical nonlocal operator is left open. The spectral test reads the eigenvalue density near zero and separates, on a given structure, a measurement artifact from a dimension the structure genuinely expresses.

</details>

Abstract: We present a systematic, model-agnostic analysis of out-of-equilibrium effects, including viscosity and thermal conductivity, in non-radial oscillations of relativistic stars. Extending the Lindblom-Detweiler formalism, we construct, to our knowledge, the first general framework for linear, non-radial relativistic stellar perturbations that incorporates generic nonequilibrium corrections to the perfect-fluid sector in both the even- and odd-parity channels. Our framework is formulated in terms of the tensorial structure and thermodynamic decomposition of generic corrections without relying on any specific constitutive relations, thereby allowing us to elucidate, at a structural level, how these effects enter the perturbation equations and contribute to geometric deformations and fluid fluctuations. As an application, we consider the Bemfica-Disconzi-Noronha-Kovtun fluid and perturbatively investigate shifts in the frequencies and damping times of modes connected to their perfect-fluid counterparts in the limit of vanishing transport coefficients. We also identify structural features of the closed eigenvalue problem that can give rise to additional mode families. Our formalism provides a unified framework for analyzing how different relativistic fluid theories modify the structure of non-radial stellar perturbations.

Conclusion: 该工作首次展示了量子算法在数值相对论框架下求解爱因斯坦场方程的可行性，为未来利用量子计算加速黑洞时空模拟等强引力物理问题提供了初步依据。

Abstract: In this work, we show how simulations performed on classical computers such as those of Numerical Relativity can be tackled by quantum algorithms for solving systems of partial differential equations. We develop a proof-of-principle quantum algorithm for solving Einstein Field Equations in the Wahlquist-Estabrook-Buchman-Bardeen(WEBB) tetrad Numerical Relativity formalism [1], and test it by evolving the Schwarzschild Black Hole spacetime in the WEBB Numerical Relativity formalism [2], perturbing it to obtain gravitational Quasinormal Modes [3]. We program the algorithm components for a gate-based, digital quantum computer using the Qiskit software [4] and run it on classical simulators and physical IBM quantum computers through the UKRI National Quantum Computing Centre (NQCC) Quantum Access program and quantify the computational resources and runtime.

### [330] [Probing the Circular Unruh Effect with Cavity-Controlled Lamb Shifts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21019)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Unruh效应（Unruh effect）预测加速观察者会感到惯性真空如同充满粒子，但其直接观测因所需加速度极大（1 K对应约10²⁰ m/s²）而面临实验挑战。探索能在更低加速度下敏感探测Unruh效应的替代方案是当前研究的核心动力。

Method: 将原子置于高Q腔中做向心加速运动，利用腔体重塑电磁态密度（electromagnetic density of states），将原本极小的非惯性修正转换为可调的能级移动。通过调节原子角速度与腔失谐量（cavity detuning），实现对Lamb shift的增强、强烈抑制或完全屏蔽。

Result: 在实验可行的参数下，当加速度低至0.5 m/s²时，即可产生约10 Hz的旋转诱导Lamb shift，比传统直接检测Unruh效应所需的加速度尺度低二十多个数量级。

Conclusion: 腔控Lamb shift光谱学（cavity-controlled Lamb-shift spectroscopy）为在超低加速度区间实验检验圆型Unruh效应提供了可行路径。

Abstract: The Unruh effect predicts that accelerated observers perceive the inertial vacuum as populated by particles, providing a flat-spacetime analogue of Hawking radiation. Its direct observation, however, remains experimentally challenging, since an Unruh temperature of $1\,\mathrm{K}$ requires accelerations of order $10^{20}\,\mathrm{m/s^2}$. Here, we show that the Lamb shift of a centripetally accelerated atom inside a high-$Q$ cavity provides a sensitive spectroscopic probe of the Unruh effect at dramatically lower accelerations. The cavity reshapes the electromagnetic density of states and converts otherwise tiny noninertial corrections into tunable level shifts. Depending on the atomic angular velocity and cavity detuning, the Lamb shift can be enhanced, strongly quenched, or completely screened. Remarkably, for experimentally realistic parameters, a rotation-induced shift of order $10\;\mathrm{Hz}$ can arise already at accelerations as low as $0.5\,\mathrm{m/s^2}$, more than twenty orders of magnitude below the acceleration scale conventionally associated with direct Unruh detection. These results identify cavity-controlled Lamb-shift spectroscopy as a viable route toward laboratory tests of the circular Unruh effect in the ultralow-acceleration regime.

</details>


### [331] [An open-source numerical tool for rational orbits and gravitational radiation in static spherically symmetric spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21029)
*Dan Li,Shiyang Hu,Chen Deng,Shijie Tan,Guansheng He*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于Mathematica和OpenMP并行架构开发了一个通用计算框架，用于模拟静态球对称时空中类时粒子的有理轨道及其引力辐射，可计算轨道构型、引力波极化态与特征应变，并在Schwarzschild时空中验证了其有效性，最后展示了一个中等质量黑洞与银心超大质量黑洞组成的极端质量比旋近系统所发射的引力波信号，有望被未来空间探测器识别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 类时轨道是探索弯曲时空内在性质的重要探针，其携带的引力辐射信号为强场引力提供了直接观测窗口。现有工具在轨道模拟与引力波计算的通用性和效率上存在不足，亟需一个高效、一体化且用户友好的数值框架。

Method: 基于Mathematica和OpenMP并行架构，开发了一个通用数值计算工具。用户只需定义协变度规（covariant metric），该工具即可自动计算静态球对称时空中的有理轨道（rational orbits），并输出相应的引力波极化态（gravitational wave polarization states）与特征应变（characteristic strains）。

Result: 以Schwarzschild时空为测试案例，验证了代码在有效势、稳定轨道区域、有理与无理轨道以及引力波信号等关键方面的功能。进一步表明，由中等质量黑洞与银心超大质量黑洞构成的极端质量比旋近（extreme mass ratio inspiral）系统所发射的引力波信号，具备被未来空间探测器识别的潜力。

Conclusion: 该软件包提供了一个高效、全面的一站式解决方案，可用于研究弯曲时空的性质及其潜在观测特征，尤其为强场引力领域中的引力波信号预测与探测提供了有力工具。

Abstract: Timelike orbits constitute a crucial probe for exploring the intrinsic properties of curved spacetimes, and the carried gravitational radiation signals provide a direct window into strong field gravity. In this paper, we develop a versatile computational framework based on Mathematica and the OpenMP parallel architecture to simulate the rational orbits of timelike particles and their gravitational radiation in static spherically symmetric spacetimes. Specifically, requiring only the user defined covariant metric, this numerical tool can efficiently calculate rational orbits across various configurations, as well as the corresponding gravitational wave polarization states and characteristic strains. The package presented here offers a highly efficient and comprehensive one-stop solution for investigating the properties of curved spacetimes and their potential observational signatures. To demonstrate the reliability and capability of our code, we apply it to the Schwarzschild spacetime as a test case, illustrating the functionality of the code across several key aspects, including the effective potential, stable orbital regions, rational and irrational orbits, and gravitational wave signals. Furthermore, we show that the gravitational waves emitted by an extreme mass ratio inspiral system composed of an intermediate mass black hole and the Galactic Center supermassive black hole have the potential to be identified by future space detectors.

### [332] [Population-level correlations in Bayesian statistics: an illustrative model for gravitational-wave astronomy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21076)
*Caroline B. Owen,Alexandre Toubiana,Davide Gerosa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个理想化的解析模型（analytical model），用于研究引力波事件中单事件相关性、系统偏差与群体层面相关性之间的相互作用，并量化了单事件相关性如何增大群体相关性的不确定性、以及波形系统误差如何被错误地吸收为群体相关性，从而产生误报。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着引力波事件数量的增长，群体推断（population inference）已从边缘分布预测转向探索致密双星参数（如质量、自旋、红移）之间的相关性，这些相关性对天体物理学和广义相对论检验具有重要约束力。然而，群体层面相关性的误报风险尚待系统研究。

Method: 作者提出一个基于高斯分布（Gaussian-based）的理想化解析模型，分析单事件层面的参数相关性、系统性偏差与群体层面相关性之间的相互作用，并考察误报产生的条件。

Result: 研究表明：(1) 单事件层面的参数相关会增大群体层面相应相关性的不确定性，可能掩盖真实的群体相关性；(2) 若波形系统误差（waveform systematics）导致的偏差在目录中具有相关性（由于参数空间中某些区域更难建模），则这些偏差可被群体分析有效吸收并被误判为群体相关性。

Conclusion: 该简单的高斯模型可作为未来更详细探索的“广义指南针”（broad compass），帮助理解群体相关性测量中的误报机制。

Abstract: With increasingly large numbers of gravitational-wave events, population inference is now beginning to move beyond predictions of marginal distributions and to probe correlations between compact-binary parameters such as masses, spins, and redshifts. These correlations have strong constraining power for both astrophysics and tests of general relativity. In this paper, we present an idealized analytical model to study the interplay between single-event correlations, systematic biases, and population-level correlations. With this, we investigate the potential emergence of false-positive measurements of population-level correlations. We quantify how the presence of correlations at the single-event level between a pair of parameters increases the uncertainty of population-level correlations for those parameters, potentially obscuring the true underlying population correlation if present. We also find that if waveform systematics lead to biases that are correlated across the catalog (which is likely, because certain regions of the parameter space are more difficult to model), this can be effectively absorbed by a population analysis that targets correlations and can be misinterpreted as such. This simple Gaussian-based model may serve as a broad compass for future, more detailed explorations.

### [333] [Reconstructing the slope of a nearly flat quintessence potential from cosmography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21127)
*Saikat Chakraborty,Peter K. S. Dunsby,Robert J. Scherrer*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在宇宙学图（cosmographic）框架下重新审视了具有近似平坦标量场势的thawing quintessence模型。研究表明，在慢滚（slow-roll）条件成立时，仅需减速参数$q$（和密度参数$Ω_φ$）即可重建势能斜率，但DESI DR2数据与近平坦假设存在潜在张力。模型展现出吸引子（attractor）行为，且所有可行演化轨迹均接近$Λ$CDM极限$j=1$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前研究表明，对一般thawing quintessence模型势能斜率$λ=-(dV/dφ)/V$的宇宙学图重构需要直到jerk参数$j$的宇宙学图参数。本文旨在探索在慢滚条件（slow-roll conditions）下，能否以更低的参数阶数实现重构，并检验近平坦势假设与当前宇宙学图数据（DESI DR2）的兼容性。

Method: 采用宇宙学图（cosmographic）框架对thawing quintessence模型进行分析；利用慢滚条件$[(dV/dφ)/V]^2 \ll 1$和$|(d^2V/dφ^2)/V| \ll 1$简化势能斜率的重构；将模型预测与DESI DR2的宇宙学图数据进行对比；在$w$--$Ω_φ$、$w$--$w'$及$q$--$j$相平面中分析模型的动力学行为（attractor behaviour）。

Result: 在慢滚条件下，只需减速参数$q$（以及密度参数$Ω_φ$）即可重构近平坦势的斜率，无需更高阶的jerk参数$j$。然而，DESI DR2数据与近平坦假设之间存在潜在张力。模型在$w$--$Ω_φ$和$w$--$w'$相平面中展示出吸引子行为，对应早期$w \approx -1$的普适thawing演化。在$q$--$j$平面上，不同宇宙膨胀历史可产生相同的thawing演化，但所有可行轨迹均接近$Λ$CDM极限$j=1$。

Conclusion: 慢滚条件显著降低了thawing quintessence模型势能重构所需的宇宙学图参数阶数，但DESI DR2数据对近平坦假设提出了挑战。模型动力学上存在吸引子行为，且与$Λ$CDM模型（$j=1$）高度接近，表明这类模型在观测上难以与$Λ$CDM显著区分。

Abstract: We revisit thawing quintessence models with nearly flat scalar-field potentials using a cosmographic framework. Earlier work indicates that the cosmographic reconstruction of the slope $λ=-(dV/dφ)/V$ of the quintessence potential in the general case requires the knowledge of the cosmographic paremeters up to the jerk parameter $j$. In this work we show that the slow-roll conditions $[(dV/dφ)/V]^2 \ll 1$ and $|(d^2V/dφ^2)/V| \ll 1$ allow the reconstruction of the slope of a nearly flat potential with knowledge of only the deceleration parameter $q$ (and the density parameter $Ω_φ$). Confronting the assumption of near-flatness with the cosmographic data after DESI DR2, however, reveals possible tension between the two. We further show that these models exhibit attractor behaviour in the $w$--$Ω_φ$ and $w$--$w'$ phase planes, corresponding to a universal thawing evolution with $w \approx -1$ at early times. We also derive the corresponding relation in the cosmographic $q$--$j$ plane and show that different cosmological expansion histories can produce the same thawing evolution. Nevertheless, all viable trajectories remain close to the $Λ$CDM limit $j=1$.

### [334] [Entanglement and firewalls in quantum circuit model of black hole evaporation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21181)
*Yi-Chen Lu,Tien Hsieh,Da-Shin Lee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文重新审视黑洞蒸发的量子电路模型，通过引入带单参数θ的置乱幺正矩阵（scrambling unitary matrix）生成更一般的初始黑洞量子比特态，研究量子单配性（quantum monogamy）在黑洞与辐射之间防火墙形成中的作用。发现防火墙的出现时间依赖于θ和黑洞质量与霍金辐射频率的乘积Mω，且在特定θ范围内信息可被辐射完整携带。最终，初始黑洞量子比特态可从最终辐射态中恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原始量子电路模型（Class. Quantum Grav. 35, 235013 (2018)）仅考虑了特定初始态，本文旨在探索更一般的初始黑洞量子比特态对防火墙形成和量子单配性（quantum monogamy）的影响，以揭示多体纠缠（multipartite entanglement）在黑洞蒸发过程中的性质。

Method: 基于三体系统（黑洞、即时辐射与早期辐射）的量子电路模型，使用带单参数θ的置乱幺正矩阵（scrambling unitary matrix）作用于落入黑洞的量子比特基态，生成更一般的初始黑洞量子比特态。θ=0时无置乱，θ=π/2时达到最大置乱。通过幺正门动力学（unitary gate dynamics）分析纠缠与防火墙的形成。

Result: 防火墙的形成依赖于θ和Mω。当θ=π/2时，防火墙比θ=0时更早出现；黑洞与即时辐射之间也会产生防火墙结构；当θ处于特定解析范围内时，对所有Mω值，信息均可被辐射携带。初始黑洞量子比特态可从最终辐射态中被恢复。

Conclusion: 这些结果揭示了不同初始态下量子电路模型中多体纠缠（multipartite entanglement）的性质，为理解黑洞信息悖论及相关量子引力问题提供了新视角。

Abstract: We reexamine the quantum circuit model of black hole evaporation proposed in Class. Quantum Grav. 35, 235013 (2018). This model incorporates the tripartite systems: black hole, just radiation and early radiation. We apply the scrambling unitary matrix with a single parameter $θ$ to the ground state of the qubits in infalling matter towards a black hole in order to generate initial qubit states of the black hole that are more general than those in Class. Quantum Grav. 35, 235013 (2018). Specifically, the scrambling unitary matrix reduces to no scrambling and maximum scrambling when $θ=0$ and $θ=π/2$, respectively. Our aim is to explore the role of quantum monogamy in the firewall formation between the black hole and radiation. In this model, entanglement and firewall formation depend on the black hole mass $M$ and the frequency of Hawking radiation $ω$. For the initial state with $θ=π/2$, a firewall emerges at an earlier stage of the evolution than with $θ=0$. We also find that a firewall structure emerges between BH and JR, and that the information is carried away by radiation for all values of $Mω$, provided that $θ$ lies within a certain analytically determined range. Following the unitary gate dynamics, the initial black hole qubit state can be retrieved from its imprint on the final radiation state, which was originally hidden behind the black hole's horizon. These results may provide insight into the properties of multipartite entanglement due to the different initial states in the evolution of a quantum circuit model for black hole evaporation.

### [335] [Temperature of free gravitational field: A geometrical perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21183)
*Samarjit Chakraborty,Gareth Amery,Sunil D Maharaj,Rituparno Goswami*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过一种新颖的几何方法，将自由引力场的热力学温度（thermodynamic temperature）与Newman-Penrose标架中实零测地线（null geodesics）的非仿射性（non-affinity）联系起来，在相应极限下自然统一了多种温度函数（如Clifton-Ellis-Tavakol温度、Hawking温度、Unruh温度等），并导出了该温度函数的几何与因果输运方程，最终将其与光沿零测地线传播时的引力红移/蓝移相关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献中存在多种引力场温度定义（如Clifton、Ellis、Tavakol温度、Hawking温度、Unruh温度等），但这些温度函数之间的内在联系尚不明确。本文旨在通过几何方法建立自由引力场热力学温度的统一描述框架。

Method: 采用新颖的几何方法（geometrical approach），在Newman-Penrose标架（Newman Penrose tetrad）中，将引力场的热力学温度与实零测地线的非仿射性建立关联。分析在局部旋转对称性（local rotational symmetry）框架内进行，并展示了结果可推广至其他Petrov D型几何（如Kerr时空）。

Result: 在相应极限下，自然统一了Clifton-Ellis-Tavakol温度、Hawking温度、Unruh温度等多种温度函数。导出了该温度函数的几何与因果输运方程，其形式为带有强迫项（forcing term）的双曲波动方程（hyperbolic wave equation），源项由Weyl曲率（Weyl curvature）和物质（matter）提供。此外，将几何温度与沿零测地线传播的光线的引力红移/蓝移（gravitational red/blue shift）相关联。

Conclusion: 自由引力场的热力学温度可以通过零测地线的非仿射性给出统一的几何解释，且该温度函数满足由曲率和物质驱动的波动方程，并可通过引力红移/蓝移效应获得物理诠释。该结果从局部旋转对称时空推广到了更一般的Petrov D型几何。

Abstract: In this paper, using a novel geometrical approach, we relate the concept of the thermodynamic temperature of the free gravitational field, to the non-affinity of real null geodesics in a Newman Penrose tetrad. This naturally links various temperature functions like Clifton, Ellis and Tavakol temperature, Hawking temperature, Unruh temperature etc., in their respective proper limits. Although our analysis is done within the realm of local rotational symmetry, we show that the result can be extended to other Petrov type D geometries, like the Kerr spacetime. We also obtain the geometrical and causal transport equations for this temperature function, in the form of a hyperbolic wave equation with a forcing term, sourced by Weyl curvature and matter. Finally, as a possible physical interpretation of the non-affinity, we relate the geometrical temperature with the gravitational red/blue shift of light rays travelling along null geodesics.

### [337] [Relativistic effects in extreme-mass-ratio inspirals within scalar clouds: Eccentric and inclined orbits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21439)
*Qi-Xuan Xu,Richard Brito,Riccardo Della Monica,Rodrigo Vicente,Chen Yuan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文采用全相对论性微扰框架，研究了在标量云（scalar cloud）环境中沿偏心且倾斜轨道演化的极端质量比率旋近（EMRI），发现轨道偏心率可在最后一个稳定轨道附近激发密集的共振谱，而轨道倾角会显著改变能量与角动量损失，并存在一个临界倾角使标量云向轨道净传输能量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前关于标量云中EMRI的相对论性研究仅限于圆轨道和赤道面运动，无法涵盖实际天体物理中更为普遍的偏心与倾斜轨道。本文旨在突破这一限制，在史瓦西黑洞背景下系统研究轨道偏心率（eccentricity）和轨道倾角（orbital inclination）对标量云中EMRI动力学的影响。

Method: 采用全相对论性微扰框架（fully relativistic perturbative framework），在以史瓦西黑洞为背景的时空中计算标量能量与角动量向空间无穷远处散射和被事件视界（event horizon）吸收的速率，从而分析偏心与倾斜轨道的演化特征。

Result: 轨道偏心率可在最后一个稳定轨道附近激发密集的共振谱（resonance spectrum），该共振与强相对论性近星点进动（apsidal precession）相关。轨道倾角会显著修改轨道能量与角动量损失：存在一个临界倾角，在该倾角以下且轨道半径足够小时，标量云向轨道净传输能量。对于足够大的偏心率，近星点进动共振在全部倾角范围内持续存在，但顺行（prograde）与逆行（retrograde）轨道的共振结构存在显著差异。

Conclusion: 这些结果为未来在自旋黑洞周围完全一般轨道上研究标量云中EMRI的动力学奠定了基础，表明偏心率与倾角是理解标量云环境影响EMRI引力波信号的关键因素。

Abstract: We study extreme-mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) evolving in a scalar cloud environment that may form through superradiant instabilities, using a fully relativistic perturbative framework that allows for eccentric and inclined orbits. EMRIs, consisting of a stellar-mass compact object inspiraling into a supermassive black hole, are key sources for space-based gravitational-wave detectors such as LISA. Previous relativistic studies of EMRIs in scalar clouds have been restricted to circular, equatorial motion. Here, instead, we focus on a Schwarzschild black hole background to incorporate eccentricity and orbital inclination. By computing the scalar energy and angular momentum scattered off to spatial infinity and absorbed at the event horizon, we show that orbital eccentricity can induce a dense spectrum of resonances near the last stable orbit, associated with strong relativistic apsidal precession. We further find that orbital inclination can significantly modify the orbital energy and angular momentum losses. In particular, we identify a critical inclination angle below which, at sufficiently small orbital radii, there is a net transfer of energy from the scalar cloud to the orbit. Moreover, for sufficiently large eccentricities, resonances associated with relativistic apsidal precession persist across the full range of inclinations, although their structure changes significantly between prograde and retrograde orbits. These results provide a foundation for future studies of EMRIs in scalar cloud environments on fully generic orbits around spinning black holes.

</details>


### [338] [The WDM Time-Frequency Transform in Gravitational-Wave Data Analysis I: Formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21473)
*Aaron Johnson,Katerina Chatziioannou,Jake Summers*

TL;DR: 本文针对引力波数据分析领域，系统阐述了时频方法（time-frequency methods）的理论基础与实现细节，重点聚焦于Wilson-Daubechies-Meyer (WDM)基的正交性、时频局域化、边界效应、正逆变换实现以及噪声协方差矩阵与似然函数等关键概念，旨在为引力波分析者提供一份自洽的时频方法参考文档。

Method: 本文采用理论推导与经验分享相结合的方式，聚焦于Wilson-Daubechies-Meyer (WDM)基这一特定基组。详细推导了该基的正交性（orthogonality）与良好的时频局域化（time-frequency localization）、DC与奈奎斯特频率（Nyquist frequency）处的边界效应（edge effects）、正逆变换及其实际实现，以及时频域中的噪声协方差矩阵（noise covariance matrix）与似然函数（likelihood）。

Result: 本文提供了一套关于WDM基的完整推导文档，阐明了其在时频域中的正交性、局域化性质及边界效应的数学细节，并给出了正逆变换的实践实现方案以及噪声协方差矩阵与似然函数的具体形式。

Conclusion: 本文系统记录了时频方法在引力波数据分析中的关键概念与实现细节，有助于提升该领域研究者对时频方法的理解与使用能力，从而在频域效率与时域通用性之间取得更好的平衡。

Abstract: For slowly-varying noise, time-frequency methods offer a natural middle ground between the efficiency of the frequency domain and the generality of the more expensive time domain. Despite growing adoption, such methods remain less well documented and less familiar in the gravitational-wave literature, compared to the ubiquitous frequency domain. Aimed at gravitational-wave analysts, in this paper we present a self-contained account of time-frequency methods, detail derivations for a specific basis, namely the Wilson-Daubechies-Meyer (WDM) basis, and share intuition and lessons learned. We document key concepts: the orthogonality and good time-frequency localization of the basis, the edge effects at the DC and Nyquist frequencies, the forward and inverse transforms and their practical implementation, and the noise covariance matrix and likelihood in the time-frequency domain.

### [339] [Binary Black Hole Coalescence and the Dynamics of Scalar Hair in Einstein-Maxwell-Scalar Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21549)
*Jean Pierre Díaz,P. A. González,Eleftherios Papantonopoulos,Yerko Vásquez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过数值相对论模拟了爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量（EMS）理论中带电双黑洞的正面并合过程，发现非最小电磁-标量耦合能够动态触发标量化/去标量化的转变，最终是否形成带标量毛发的黑洞取决于耦合强度与残余电荷的竞争。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量（Einstein-Maxwell-Scalar，EMS）理论中，带电双黑洞并合能否动态触发标量化（scalarization）或去标量化（descalarization）转变，以及这些转变的条件。

Method: 采用数值相对论（numerical relativity）方法，基于带电穿刺初始数据（charged puncture initial data）构建两个Reissner-Nordström黑洞，并引入纯动力学标量微扰（purely kinetic scalar perturbation）作为不稳定性种子，然后同步演化引力、电磁和标量三个耦合扇区。

Result: 非最小电磁-标量耦合可动态触发标量毛发（scalar hair）的生长，即使初始单个黑洞不含标量场。弱耦合或并合后电荷抵消导致电磁源被抑制时，标量场被辐射或吸收，系统去标量化；强耦合且残余电荷非零时，标量场持续存在，终态黑洞趋近于标量化构型。标量辐射的时间分布与非线性阶段的主导引力波模式存在定性关联。

Conclusion: 这些结果在EMS理论中实现了标量化/去标量化转变的双黑洞实例，表明标量毛发的命运由标量耦合强度与残余电荷含量之间的相互作用共同决定。

Abstract: We investigate the head-on coalescence of charged binary black holes in Einstein-Maxwell-Scalar (EMS) theory using numerical relativity. The binaries are built from charged puncture initial data representing two Reissner-Nordström black holes immersed in a purely kinetic scalar perturbation: the scalar field initially vanishes, while its conjugate momentum provides a small seed for the instability. We evolve the coupled gravitational, electromagnetic, and scalar sectors and monitor the apparent horizons, the emitted radiation, and the scalar field on the horizons. Our simulations show that the nonminimal electromagnetic-scalar coupling can dynamically trigger the growth of scalar hair even when the individual black holes are initially scalar-free. The subsequent evolution depends on the coupling strength and on the charge retained by the remnant. For weak coupling, or when charge cancellation suppresses the electromagnetic source after merger, the scalar field is radiated away or absorbed by the final horizon and the system dynamically descalarizes. For sufficiently strong coupling and nonzero remnant charge, the scalar field remains finite and the final black hole approaches a scalarized configuration. The coalescence also excites scalar radiation whose time profile is qualitatively correlated with the dominant gravitational-wave mode during the nonlinear stage of the collision. These results provide a binary realization of scalarization/descalarization transitions in EMS theory and show that the fate of scalar hair is controlled by the interplay between the scalar coupling and the charge content of the remnant.

</details>


### [340] [Consistency Conditions and the Derivation of Harmonic Structure in Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21603)
*Bardia H. Fahim,Joshua G. Fenwick*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过分析爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-狄拉顿理论（Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton theory）在任意维度下的场方程，证明在不预先假设基空间几何或度规函数调和形式的条件下，场方程强制要求狄拉顿耦合相等、基空间几何为里奇平坦（Ricci flat），并使度规函数在该基上成为调和函数，从而统一推导出多中心几何、宇宙学解和动力学黑洞等多类解中所共有的调和行为与共形结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦和爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-狄拉顿理论的许多精确解共享一个结构模式，即度规函数由特定空间基（常为平坦基）上的调和函数（harmonic function）构建。该研究旨在不预先假设基空间几何或度规函数的调和形式，直接从场方程出发推导这一结构模式的起源与约束条件。

Method: 在任意维度的爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-狄拉顿理论框架中，考虑狄拉顿场（dilaton field）与麦克斯韦场（Maxwell field）非平凡耦合，并引入与宇宙学参数成比例的刘维尔型势（Liouville-type potential）。不预先设定基空间几何或度规函数的调和形式，直接分析场方程的解分支，分别考察一般分支（generic branch）和纯空间分支（purely spatial branch）下的约束条件。

Result: 在一般分支下，场方程强制要求狄拉顿耦合常数相等，限制空间基几何为里奇平坦（Ricci flat），并使度规函数在该基上成为调和函数，得到的时空可用共形势（conformal potential）表达。在纯空间分支下，耦合常数则受到一个不同的约束。这些结果统一解释了多中心几何、宇宙学解和动力学黑洞等解类中出现的调和行为与共形结构。

Conclusion: 该研究为爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-狄拉顿理论中广泛出现的调和函数结构与共形对称性提供了一个统一的场方程推导视角，揭示了其背后由场方程本身强加的约束条件，从而为理解和构造更多精确解奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: Many exact solutions of Einstein-Maxwell and Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton theory share a common structural pattern in which the metric functions are built from harmonic functions on a specified spatial base, often taken to be flat. We investigate this pattern by considering the Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton theory in arbitrary dimensions, where the dilaton field is non-trivially coupled to the Maxwell field and to a Liouville-type potential proportional to the cosmological parameter. Without imposing either the base geometry or the harmonic form of the metric function in advance, we show that for the generic branch, the field equations force the dilaton couplings to be equal, restrict the spatial base geometry to be Ricci flat, and make the metric function harmonic on this base. The resulting spacetime can then be written in terms of a conformal potential. We also consider a purely spatial branch, which instead leads to a distinct constraint on the coupling constants. These results provide a unified field-equation derivation of the harmonic behavior and conformal structure that appear in several classes of solutions, including multi-center geometries, cosmological solutions, and dynamical black holes.

Abstract: The black mirror spacetime proposed by Tzanavaris, Boyle, and Turok [1] connects the two exterior regions of the extended Schwarzschild black hole directly to each other, with no intervening interior region. Using techniques adapted from previous work on signature change, we reexamine the black mirror spacetime as a model of double signature change, and investigate whether there is a surface layer at the horizon, that is, a distributional curvature singularity corresponding to an impulsive gravitational wave. We confirm that the black mirror spacetime does not contain any such singularity, and compare our result with previous claims that the curvature components are analytic. ### [342] [Quantum Memory in Scalar-Induced Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21835)
*Waqas Ahmed*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 标量诱导引力波（scalar-induced gravitational waves）通常被处理为相位随机曲率扰动（phase-random curvature perturbations）产生的经典随机背景。本文证明，这种描述可能遗漏残余量子信息（residual quantum information）。通过从退相干双模高斯标量态（decohered two-mode Gaussian scalar state）出发，推导出标量反常相干性（scalar anomalous coherence）与诱导张量模式协方差矩阵（covariance matrix of induced tensor modes）之间的显式传递关系。对于局域标量功率谱，普通张量功率由标量功率收缩产生，而对向模式张量相干性（opposite-mode tensor coherence）则由标量反常相干性收缩产生。这种相干性即使在标量纠缠消失后仍能产生非零张量不和谐（tensor discord）和连通张量功率协方差（connected tensor-power covariance）。研究将连通协方差和相位敏感应变关联（phase-sensitive strain correlations）识别为次级引力波背景中原始量子相干性（primordial quantum coherence）的探针，并讨论了它们对未来空间干涉仪和脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing arrays）的可能意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准处理将标量诱导引力波视为经典随机背景，但可能遗漏了其中蕴含的量子信息。本文旨在揭示退相干标量态中残留的量子相干性如何传递给诱导张量模式，并识别能够探测次级引力波背景中原始量子相干性的可观测物理量。

Method: 从退相干双模高斯标量态出发，通过解析推导建立标量反常相干性与诱导张量模式协方差矩阵之间的显式传递关系，分别分析标量功率收缩和标量反常相干性收缩对张量功率和对应张量相干性的贡献。

Result: 局域标量功率谱下，普通张量功率由标量功率收缩贡献，而对向模式张量相干性由标量反常相干性收缩贡献。即使在标量纠缠消失后，该相干性仍会产生非零张量不和谐和连通张量功率协方差。

Conclusion: 连通协方差和相位敏感应变关联可作为次级引力波背景中原始量子相干性的探针，对未来空间干涉仪和脉冲星计时阵列具有潜在意义。

Abstract: Scalar-induced gravitational waves are usually treated as a classical stochastic background sourced by phase-random curvature perturbations. We show that this description can miss residual quantum information. Starting from a decohered two-mode Gaussian scalar state, we derive explicit transfer relations between the scalar anomalous coherence and the covariance matrix of induced tensor modes. For a localized scalar power spectrum, the ordinary tensor power is sourced by scalar power contractions, whereas the opposite-mode tensor coherence is sourced by scalar anomalous-coherence contractions. This coherence can generate nonzero tensor discord and a connected tensor-power covariance even after scalar entanglement has vanished. We identify the connected covariance and phase-sensitive strain correlations as probes of primordial quantum coherence in secondary gravitational-wave backgrounds, and discuss their possible relevance for future space-based interferometers and pulsar timing arrays.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We investigate late-time cosmology in extended symmetric teleparallel gravity coupled to a Dirac-Born-Infeld (DBI) scalar field within $f(Q,T)$ gravity, where $Q$ is the non-metricity scalar and $T$ is the trace of the matter energy-momentum tensor. Working on a spatially flat Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker background and treating the cosmic medium as an effective perfect fluid, we derive the background field equations for $f(Q,T)+\mathrm{DBI}$ gravity and obtain analytic solutions for the linear choice $f(Q,T)=αQ+βT$. The joint posteriors (Tables II and III) are broadly consistent with current late-time constraints and allow a direct comparison with $Λ$CDM, quantifying the departures driven by the $βT$ coupling and the DBI sector. Although the model does not reproduce every observational feature exactly, it provides a statistically viable alternative avenue to the standard paradigm and a useful framework for exploring potential remedies to existing tensions, including the $H_0$ discrepancy, without claiming a definitive resolution.

### [344] [Entanglement, Discord, and Residual Coherence in Scalar-Induced Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21901)
*Waqas Ahmed*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了由原初曲率扰动（primordial curvature perturbations）标量诱导的引力波（scalar-induced gravitational waves）中可能残存的量子信息特征。通过协方差矩阵形式（covariance-matrix formalism），将原初扰动描述为退相干的双模压缩高斯态（decohered two-mode squeezed Gaussian states），发现标量退纠缠后仍可残留反常标量相干性（anomalous scalar coherence），并由此产生具有非平凡协方差和相位结构的关联张量背景，为探测超出纠缠的原初量子关联提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用协方差矩阵形式描述原初曲率扰动为退相干的双模压缩高斯态，识别标量纠缠（scalar entanglement）消失后可能残留的反常标量相干性。随后推导了相反动量（opposite-momentum）诱导张量模式的标量-张量转移关系（scalar-to-tensor transfer relations），并分析了张量相干性对诱导高斯失谐（Gaussian discord）及相位敏感可观测量（phase-sensitive observables）的控制作用。

Result: 普通张量功率（tensor power）由标量功率缩并（scalar power contractions）驱动，而相反模式张量相干性（opposite-mode tensor coherence）由反常标量相干缩并（anomalous scalar-coherence contractions）驱动。该张量相干性产生连接功率协方差（connected power covariance）$κ(k)\propto |γ_k|^2/α_k^2$等可观测量，表明稳健特征并非引力波谱的普遍偏移，而是具有非平凡协方差和相位结构的关联张量背景。

Conclusion: 标量诱导引力波可能提供一种超越纠缠（beyond entanglement）的原初量子关联（primordial quantum correlations）的新探针。文中讨论了现象学模板（phenomenological templates）并给出了未来引力波观测的Fisher估计（Fisher estimate）作为示意。

Abstract: Scalar-induced gravitational waves are usually modeled as a classical stochastic background sourced by primordial curvature perturbations. We investigate whether residual quantum-information properties of the scalar sector can survive decoherence and leave imprints in the induced tensor background. Using the covariance-matrix formalism, we describe primordial curvature perturbations as decohered two-mode squeezed Gaussian states and identify the anomalous scalar coherence that may remain after scalar entanglement has vanished. We then derive the leading scalar-to-tensor transfer relations for opposite-momentum induced tensor modes. The ordinary tensor power is sourced by scalar power contractions, whereas the opposite-mode tensor coherence is sourced by anomalous scalar-coherence contractions. This tensor coherence controls the induced Gaussian discord and generates connected and phase-sensitive observables, including a connected power covariance $κ(k)\propto |γ_k|^2/α_k^2$. Thus the robust signature is not a universal shift of the gravitational-wave spectrum, but a correlated tensor background with nontrivial covariance and phase structure. We discuss phenomenological templates and provide an illustrative Fisher estimate for future gravitational-wave observations. Our results suggest that scalar-induced gravitational waves may offer a new probe of primordial quantum correlations beyond entanglement.

### [345] [Determining Kerr black hole spin and inclination from a segment of the critical curve in black hole images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21921)
*Kenta Hioki,Umpei Miyamoto,Tomohiro Harada*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种方法，利用黑洞图像中临界曲线（critical curve）的局部片段来确定非极端克尔黑洞（non-extremal Kerr black hole）的自旋参数 $a/M$ 和倾角 $i$，无需完整重建临界曲线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临界曲线本身不可直接观测，但高阶光子环（higher-order photon rings）在其附近累积，产生可识别的亮度增强局部片段。因此需要一种方法，从这些局部片段中提取几何信息以约束黑洞的自旋与倾角。

Method: 引入临界曲线的标准化片段（standardized segments），定义三个可观测几何量（observables）描述其几何特征；证明这些可观测量与一个辅助参数 $r_{nl}\in[0,1]$（用于标识片段在临界曲线上的位置）一起，能在所考虑的参数域内唯一确定 $(a/M,i)$。

Result: 即使仅获取临界曲线的一个片段，也包含足够的几何信息来约束黑洞自旋和倾角，无需重建整条临界曲线。

Conclusion: 该框架自然适用于实际观测条件，并可推广到更一般的旋转黑洞时空（rotating black hole spacetimes）。

Abstract: We present a method for determining the spin parameter $a/M$ and inclination angle $i$ of a non-extremal Kerr black hole from segments of the critical curve identified in black hole images. Although the critical curve itself is not directly observable, higher-order photon rings accumulate near it, and in realistic observations localized portions of the resulting brightness enhancement may be available for identifying segments of the critical curve. We introduce standardized segments of the critical curve and define three observables that characterize their geometry. We show that these observables uniquely determine $(a/M,i)$, together with an auxiliary parameter $r_{nl}\in[0,1]$ specifying the location of the identified segment along the critical curve, within the domain considered. Thus, even a segment of the critical curve contains sufficient geometric information to constrain the black hole spin and inclination without reconstructing the full critical curve. The framework is naturally suited to realistic observations and may be extended to more general rotating black hole spacetimes.

</details>


### [346] [Gravitational Radiation and Charges on de Sitter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22060)

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文总结了与Geoffrey Compère和Sk.Jahanur Hoque合作的工作，探讨了在Λ-边界对称性（Λ-BMS）框架下定义类似于邦迪质量损失（Bondi mass loss）的物理量所面临的困难，并通过线性化广义谐和规范（generalized harmonic gauge）下的爱因斯坦方程求解，引入源多极矩（source multipole moments）和绝热近似（adiabaticity）等假设，最终利用全息应力张量（holographic stress tensor）定义电荷流（charge flows），并将结果与记忆效应（memory effect）相连接。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Λ-边界对称性（Λ-BMS）解空间中，定义类似于邦迪质量损失（Bondi mass loss）的物理量并非显然可行，因此需要寻找解决方案。研究线性化引力解及其在广义谐和规范下的描述，能够帮助理解引力辐射与源多极矩的关系，并最终与记忆效应（memory effect）建立联系。

Method: 首先回顾Λ-BMS解空间并分析定义邦迪质量损失（Bondi mass loss）的困难；接着通过研究线性化解（linearized solutions）来解决该问题；然后在广义谐和规范（generalized harmonic gauge）下求解线性化爱因斯坦方程，引入绝热近似（adiabaticity）和远源近似（大距离）等假设，将度规扰动（metric perturbations）用源多极矩（source multipole moments）展开，并讨论多极展开的一致截断（consistent truncation）。进一步分析有限时间间隔内时变源导致的未来无穷远处度规扰动的净变化，并将其与记忆效应（memory effect）关联。最后利用全息应力张量（holographic stress tensor）定义电荷流（charge flows），给出其在二阶扰动下用多极矩表达的形式。

Result: 在Λ-BMS框架下，通过线性化解的方法克服了直接定义邦迪质量损失（Bondi mass loss）的困难；在广义谐和规范下成功将度规扰动用源多极矩展开，并能一致截断多极展开；建立了有限时间源导致的未来无穷远处度规变化与记忆效应（memory effect）的联系；利用全息应力张量（holographic stress tensor）定义了电荷流，并给出了其在二阶扰动下关于多极矩的具体形式。

Conclusion: 该工作为Λ-BMS框架下的引力辐射和记忆效应提供了系统化的描述方法，特别是通过线性化方法和全息对应关系定义了电荷流与多极矩之间的联系，为进一步研究渐近对称性（asymptotic symmetries）和引力记忆效应（gravitational memory effect）奠定了基础。

Abstract: We give a summary of our work [3] and [4] with Geoffrey Compère and Sk.Jahanur Hoque. After quickly reviewing the $Λ$-BMS solution space and why it is not trivial to define an analogue of Bondi mass loss, we discuss how this can be resolved by studying the linearized solutions. Then we describe how to solve the linearized Einstein s equations in the generalized harmonic gauge and the set of assumptions such as adiabaticity and being at a large distance from the source that allows us to write the metric perturbations in terms of the source multipole moments. We point out how to consistently truncate the multipole expansion. We then discuss the net change of the metric perturbation at future infinity due to a source that is time-varying in a finite time interval that will be connected to the memory effect. We explain how to define charge flows using the holographic stress tensor and what form they take in terms of multipole moments at second order in perturbations. We conclude with a some remarks on the results.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展修正Deser-Woodard非局部引力（revised D-W nonlocal gravity）中已有的静态球对称黑洞解，探索更多可能的渐近平坦扩展形式。

Method: 利用场方程的线性性，在Schwarzschild解附近进行一阶展开，证明度规的时间分量与径向分量的倒数均呈线性关系，从而可以按模式进行逐模叠加（mode-by-mode superposition）；随后构造对数型修正与指数型修正两种解析解。

Result: 对数型修正在大半径处产生相对于Schwarzschild解的缓慢衰减偏离，体现出更扩展的非局域效应；指数型修正则局域在视界附近，且当修正振幅为正时使视界向内移动。

Conclusion: 两种修正项具有明确物理动机：对数项可能与量子修正（quantum corrections）效应相关，指数项可能源于有限范围或屏蔽引力效应（finite-range or screened gravitational effects）。

Abstract: In this work, we extend the static spherically symmetric black hole solutions of revised Deser--Woodard (D-W) nonlocal gravity. Due to the linearity of the field equations, we show that the first-order expansion around the Schwarzschild solution is linear in both the temporal metric component and the reciprocal of the radial metric component. Therefore, a mode-by-mode superposition can be properly defined for different types of correction terms. We then further study two additional asymptotically flat extensions, a logarithmically dressed correction and an exponentially suppressed correction. The logarithmically dressed correction gives a slowly decaying deviation from Schwarzschild as the radius becomes large, making it a more extended nonlocal effect, whereas the exponentially suppressed correction is localized near the horizon and shifts the horizon inward for positive correction amplitude. These correction terms are physically motivated by common mechanisms in modified gravity: Logarithmic terms are possibly related to effects of quantum corrections, and exponential terms can arise from finite-range or screened gravitational effects.
