### [348] [Horizon Singularities in the Schwarzschild Geometry of the Teleparallel Equivalent of General Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22121)
*D. F. López,A. A. Coley,R. J. van den Hoogen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文指出，在原初的(TEGR)中，某些挠率标量不变量在史瓦西解视界处发散，阻碍了其作为黑洞时空的解释。作者证明史瓦西TEGR几何可分为两类：正则子类中发散消失，视界属于流形，支持黑洞解释；奇异子类中发散真实存在，视界被排除。通过惯性系条件、穿透视界坐标和视界正则性判据三种方法，确定了允许正则视界的完整洛伦兹扇区函数类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Teleparallel Equivalent of General Relativity (TEGR)中，已知某些挠率标量不变量（torsion scalar invariants）在史瓦西解视界处发散，这阻碍了将其视界解释为黑洞时空的合法性。本研究旨在解决这一发散问题，澄清其来源，并找出使视界正则化的条件。

Method: 首先将史瓦西TEGR几何分为两个子类，由几何的洛伦兹扇区（Lorentz sector）决定——即不包含在度规中但出现在挠率（torsion）中的标架（tetrad）和自旋联络（spin connection）元素。然后采用三种独立方法确定正则视界对应的洛伦兹扇区函数类：(1) 惯性系条件（inertial frame condition）；(2) 穿透视界坐标（horizon-penetrating coordinates）；(3) 视界正则性判据（horizon regularity criterion）。

Result: 正则子类中，发散消失，视界属于流形，支持一致的黑洞解释；奇异子类中，发散是真实的，视界被排除在流形之外。惯性贡献（inertial contributions）本身不能消除视界奇异性，适当的标架（proper frame）也无法单独消除惯性效应。研究确定了使视界正则的完整洛伦兹扇区函数类。

Conclusion: 在该函数类中，所有挠率标量不变量在视界处保持有限，且允许跨视界的解析延拓（analytic extensions）。这表明TEGR中的史瓦西黑洞解释并不必然受阻，关键在于洛伦兹扇区的选择。

Abstract: Certain torsion scalar invariants are known to diverge at the horizon of the Schwarzschild solution in the Teleparallel Equivalent of General Relativity (TEGR), obstructing its interpretation as a black hole spacetime. We show that Schwarzschild TEGR geometries split into two distinct subclasses determined by the Lorentz sector of the geometry -- the elements of the tetrad and spin connection not encoded in the metric but appearing in the torsion. In the regular subclass, the divergences are absent and the horizon belongs to the manifold, supporting a consistent black hole interpretation. In the singular subclass, the divergences are genuine and the horizon is excluded from the manifold. As part of this analysis, we clarify the role of inertial contributions in teleparallel gravity, showing that the proper frame does not, by itself, eliminate inertial effects and that the horizon singularities are independent of the inertial structure of the frame. Using three independent approaches -- the inertial frame condition, horizon-penetrating coordinates, and the horizon regularity criterion -- we determine the complete class of Lorentz sector functions compatible with a regular horizon in Schwarzschild TEGR geometries. For this class, all torsion scalar invariants remain finite at the horizon and analytic extensions across it are admitted.

### [349] [Covariant virtual work and the d'Alembert-Lagrange formulation of general relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22196)
*A. Cuevas,C. Ortiz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文为时空几何建立了一个协变虚功（covariant virtual work）结构及相应的达朗贝尔-拉格朗日原理（d'Alembert-Lagrange principle），从中导出了爱因斯坦场方程（Einstein field equations）和宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）的新诠释，后者作为由整体容许性约束决定的理想反应项（ideal reaction）出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有广义相对论（General Relativity）的变分原理（variational principle）通常基于作用量极值（action extremality），但约束所导致的贡献缺乏协变分类机制。作者旨在通过虚功框架（virtual work framework）提供一种替代性统一描述，并自然涵盖不等式约束情形。

Method: 建立协变虚功结构与对应的达朗贝尔-拉格朗日原理，通过对可容许度量变分（admissible metric variations）令总协变虚功（total covariant virtual work）为零，而非要求作用量取极值。该结构进一步将约束引起的贡献协变地分类为不做虚功的理想反应（ideal reactions）与做虚功的非理想部分（non-ideal sectors）。

Result: 广义相对论作为该原理的一个特例得以重现；爱因斯坦场方程由总协变虚功为零导出。等周约束（isoperimetric constraint）产生宇宙学项，该宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）作为由时空平均值（spacetime averages）固定的全局参数出现，体现了非局域几何起源。

Conclusion: 约束诱导的反应项（reaction terms）在协变虚功框架中得到分类；宇宙学常数得以通过整体的容许性条件（admissibility conditions）被确定，具有内在的非局域几何起源。该框架还自然地延伸至单侧容许性条件（one-sided admissibility conditions），形成协变不等式结构。

Abstract: We develop a covariant virtual work structure and a corresponding d'Alembert-Lagrange principle for spacetime geometry. Within this framework, General Relativity arises as a particular realization of the principle, leading to a covariant d'Alembert-Lagrange formulation in which the Einstein field equations arise from the vanishing of total covariant virtual work on admissible metric variations, rather than from action extremality. The covariant virtual work structure provides a covariant classification of constraint-induced contributions, distinguishing ideal reactions, which perform no virtual work, from non-ideal sectors contribute explicitly to it. The structure extends naturally to one-sided admissibility conditions, yielding a covariant inequality structure. Constraints generate reaction terms. In particular, an isoperimetric constraint produces a cosmological term as an ideal reaction fixed by spacetime averages, so that the cosmological constant emerges as a global parameter determined by admissibility, reflecting an intrinsically nonlocal geometric origin.

Method: 考虑两种 f(Q) 引力（f(Q) gravity）的函数形式：对数模型（logarithmic model）和非线性饱和模型（nonlinear saturation model）。两者通过几何修正（geometric corrections）改变标准膨胀历史，无需引入宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）。模型参数通过贝叶斯 MCMC 分析（Bayesian MCMC analysis）进行约束，使用的观测数据包括宇宙计时器（cosmic chronometers）、Ia 型超新星样本（Pantheon、Pantheon+SH0ES、DES SN5YR）以及 SDSS 和 DESI 的 BAO 测量数据。

Abstract: The persistent discrepancy between early-time and late-Universe measurements of the Hubble constant commonly known as the $H_0$ tension remains one of the most pressing open questions in modern cosmology. In this work, we explore whether modifications to the gravitational sector, specifically within the framework of symmetric teleparallel gravity, can offer a viable pathway toward alleviating this tension. We consider two functional forms of $f(Q)$ gravity: a logarithmic model and a nonlinear saturation model, both of which introduce geometric corrections to the standard expansion history without invoking a cosmological constant. Constraining these models through a Bayesian MCMC analysis against a comprehensive suite of observational data, including cosmic chronometers, Type Ia supernova compilations (Pantheon, Pantheon$+$SH0ES, and DES SN5YR), and BAO measurements from SDSS and DESI, we find that both models remain statistically competitive with $Λ$CDM. The logarithmic model, in particular, consistently infers intermediate values of $H_0$ between the \textit{Planck} and SH0ES benchmarks across all dataset combinations, and carries lower AIC and BIC penalties, establishing it as the more promising candidate for partially easing the $H_0$ tension within a modified gravity framework.

### [351] [Null geodesic defocusing in dynamical black-hole-to-white-hole transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22404)
*Johanna Borissova,Stefano Liberati,Matt Visser*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究动力学非奇异黑洞-白洞转变中零测地线（null geodesics）的发散行为，证明该转变必然违反零收敛条件（null convergence condition），并指出瞬时转变情况需要无界违反，暗示有效连续度规描述的失效及对完整量子引力（quantum gravity）描述的需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索黑洞-白洞转变过程中零测地线的行为，特别是从时空运动学层面分析束缚区域（trapped region）收缩消失与反束缚区域（anti-trapped region）形成膨胀的几何条件，而不依赖具体的引力场方程或奇点消解（singularity resolution）的微观机制。

Method: 首先在一般时空运动学框架下，通过零膨胀（null expansions）在束缚视界（trapping horizon）与反束缚视界（anti-trapping horizon）上的行为，推导零收敛条件必然被违反；然后构建广义Painlevé-Gullstrand坐标下的显式弹跳几何（bouncing geometries），将具有de Sitter核心的静态规则黑洞提升为时变黑洞-白洞转变模型，并以Bardeen型质量函数为例展示违反的局域化特征。

Result: 零收敛条件的违反是黑洞-白洞转变过程的一般性必要条件，与奇点消解的具体机制无关；在Bardeen型质量函数模型中，该违反局域于束缚区域蒸发与反束缚区域形成的中间动力学阶段；瞬时转变极限要求零收敛条件的无界违反。

Conclusion: 瞬时黑洞-白洞转变极限下，无界的零收敛条件违反表明有效连续度规描述失效，必须诉诸完整的量子引力描述才能正确理解该过程。

Abstract: We investigate the defocusing of null geodesics in dynamical, non-singular black-hole-to-white-hole transitions. Working at the level of spacetime kinematics, and without assuming any specific gravitational field equations, we show that the contraction and disappearance of a trapped region, as well as the subsequent formation and expansion of an anti-trapped region, necessarily require a violation of the null convergence condition. This conclusion follows directly from the behaviour of the null expansions across the trapping and anti-trapping horizons, and is therefore independent of the microscopic mechanism responsible for singularity resolution. We then illustrate this general argument by constructing a class of explicit bouncing geometries in generalised Painlevé-Gullstrand coordinates, obtained by promoting static regular black holes with de Sitter cores to time-dependent black-hole-to-white-hole transition models. For a Bardeen-type mass function, we show that the required violation of the null convergence condition is localised within the intermediate dynamical phase in which the trapped region evaporates and the anti-trapped region forms. Finally, we argue that the limiting case of an instantaneous black-hole-to-white-hole transition would require an unbounded violation of the null convergence condition, signalling a breakdown of the effective continuum metric description, and the need to appeal to a full quantum-gravitational description.

### [352] [Starobinsky-inflation in asymptotically safe shift-symmetric scalar-tensor theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22408)

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了标量场驱动暴胀（scalaron-driven inflation）对渐近安全标量-张量理论（asymptotically safe scalar-tensor theories）的约束能力。通过重整化群改进（renormalization group improvement）从Horndeski型理论出发，发现非最小引力-物质耦合参数不仅影响物质-引力扇区，还进入有效高阶导数耦合，进而利用多场暴胀模型（multi-field inflationary models）从宇宙学观测导出对非最小引力-物质耦合的显式界限。结果表明，在三个非高斯不动点中，两个不被观测支持，仅一个给出现象学可行的重整化群（renormalization group）轨迹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动机在于探究渐近安全机制下标量-张量理论中，标量场驱动暴胀对理论参数空间的约束能力，特别是非最小引力-物质耦合（non-minimal gravity-matter coupling）的可观测界限。

Method: 从Horndeski型理论出发，应用重整化群改进（renormalization group improvement）程序生成由微观参数固定的高阶导数耦合；引入多场暴胀模型（multi-field inflationary models）框架分析暴胀动力学，并结合宇宙学观测导出对非最小引力-物质耦合参数的显式边界。

Conclusion: 渐近安全标量-张量理论中的标量场驱动暴胀对非最小引力-物质耦合施加了严格的宇宙学观测约束，进而能够区分不同的非高斯不动点结构，缩小理论可能的紫外完备化方案。

Abstract: We investigate the constraining power of scalaron-driven inflation on asymptotically safe scalar-tensor theories. Starting from a Horndeski-type theory and applying a renormalization group improvement procedure generates higher-derivative couplings which are fixed in terms of the microscopic parameters - a structure that is expected to occur also within first principle computations based on the asymptotic safety mechanism. The latter are taken to be the free parameters appearing at the Gaussian fixed point. We find that the free parameter initially associated with the non-minimal gravity-matter coupling is not confined to the gravity-matter sector of the theory and also enters the effective higher-derivative couplings in the gravitational sector. We review the setting of multi-field inflationary models which is appropriate to analyze the inflationary dynamics in this context and illustrate their applicability by working out the explicit bounds on the non-minimal gravity-matter coupling resulting from cosmological observations. Given the fixed point structure of asymptotically safe scalar-tensor theories, the results indicate that UV-completions by two of the three available non-Gaussian fixed points can be ruled out while pinpointing phenomenologically viable RG trajectories emanating from the third fixed point.

</details>


### [353] [An Interplay Between Fractional Calculus and Holographic Dark Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22431)
*Ayush Bidlan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本论文系统构建了分形全息暗能量（Fractional Holographic Dark Energy, FHDE）框架，通过在黑洞热力学中引入分形（Riesz）导数来扩展全息暗能量（HDE），导出了分数阶Wheeler–DeWitt方程与分数阶Bekenstein–Hawking熵，并基于该熵与Cohen不等式构造了新的暗能量密度。随后在多种引力理论（BD、DGP、EPN、Horndeski）中分析了FHDE的宇宙学演化、有效场描述、状态方程及晚期奇点行为，为超越ΛCDM的宇宙加速机制提供了非局域性量子引力路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准全息暗能量（HDE）在解释晚期宇宙加速时面临哈勃截断（Hubble cutoff）等挑战；将晚期宇宙加速与黑洞热力学中编码的非局域性或记忆效应（通过分形导数实现）联系起来，有望突破标准HDE的局限并回应截断问题。

Method: 在量子几何动力学（quantum geometrodynamics）中，将Riesz分形空间导数引入Schwarzschild黑洞的哈密顿约束，得到分数阶Wheeler–DeWitt方程；其解给出由Lévy指数α（1<α≤2）控制的分数阶Bekenstein–Hawking熵；再利用该熵与Cohen不等式构造新的暗能量密度，定义FHDE框架。随后在Hubble截断下分析其晚期宇宙学行为，通过自旋-0和自旋-1候选者进行有效场重构，并扩展至BD、DGP、EPN及Horndeski理论以推导状态方程与减速参数。

Result: FHDE框架给出了依赖于α的分数阶热力学量和暗能量密度；在Hubble截断下，宇宙学可观测量（状态方程参数、减速参数、有效场动能与势能项）均可表示为红移z和α的函数；在Granda–Oliveros FHDE设定中，宇宙可能经历大撕裂（big rip）、小撕裂（little rip）或伪撕裂（pseudo-rip）等晚期奇点。

Conclusion: FHDE为HDE提供了一种理论上有动机的扩展，在量子引力的非局域性与宇宙晚期动力学之间建立了桥梁，为理解超越ΛCDM模型的宇宙加速机制提供了一条可行途径。

Abstract: This dissertation aims to put forth a systematic construction of a fractional-calculus extension of holographic dark energy (HDE). We show that linking late-time cosmic acceleration to non-local or memory effects encoded in a fractional (Riesz) derivative within black hole thermodynamics produces deviations from standard HDE and can address some challenges of the Hubble cutoff. In particular, a Riesz fractional spatial derivative is introduced into the Hamiltonian constraint of a Schwarzschild black hole in quantum geometrodynamics, leading to a Fractional Wheeler--DeWitt equation whose solutions yield fractionally corrected thermodynamic quantities, notably fractional Bekenstein--Hawking entropy governed by the Lévy index \(α\), with \(1<α\leq2\). Using this entropy with Cohen's inequality, a new dark energy density is constructed, defining the Fractional Holographic Dark Energy (FHDE) framework.
  The cosmological implications of FHDE are then investigated. Within the Hubble cutoff, its late-time evolution is analysed through cosmological observables, and the model is reconstructed using effective field descriptions with spin-\(0\) and spin-\(1\) candidates, allowing kinetic and potential terms to be extracted as functions of redshift \(z\) and \(α\). The framework is then extended to BD, DGP, EPN, and Horndeski theories to derive the equation-of-state and deceleration parameters in terms of \(z\) and \(α\). In addition, the fate of the Universe is studied through late-time singularities, namely the big, little, and pseudo-rip, within the Granda--Oliveros FHDE setting. In short, this dissertation proposes FHDE as a theoretically motivated extension of HDE, bridging non-locality in quantum gravity with the late-time dynamics of the Universe, and offering a route toward understanding cosmic acceleration beyond \(Λ\)CDM.

### [354] [Steering a warp drive without exotic matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22531)
*An T. Le*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文论证了任何渐近平直翘曲驱动器（warp drive）的变向必然伴随辐射（radiation）到零无穷远（null infinity），并构造了一个正能（positive-energy）且可转向的时空——基于Kinnersley光子火箭（photon rocket）匹配外壳的翘曲驱动，其转向机制为光子火箭反冲（recoil），能量条件由Bondi质量损失（Bondi mass loss）支付，且加速存在Buchdahl型上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有翘曲驱动要么是静态或匀速的正能构造，要么加速时需要奇异物质（exotic matter）；Bobrick与Martire指出翘曲驱动“没有任何自然的方式改变速度”。因此，本文旨在从原理和构造两个层面回答：能否实现一个正能的可加速、可转向翘曲驱动。

Method: 首先通过守恒律证明一般性原理：任何渐近平坦（asymptotically flat）、拥有受限主能量源（confined dominant-energy source）且满足标准剥离（standard peeling）的驱动器，其Bondi-Sachs四动量（Bondi–Sachs four-momentum）只能通过向零无穷远的辐射改变，因此转向必须伴随辐射。然后构造一个正能时空：设定乘客世界管（passenger worldtube），取精确Kinnersley光子火箭作为外部解，并求解与之匹配的类时壳（timelike shell）；外部解和转向律为精确形式，壳层通过微扰和数值方法验证。

Result: 得到转向机制为光子火箭反冲作用在潮汐保护（tidally protected）、精确平坦的腔体上；翘曲驱动是解耦的平坦内部，而非翘曲场。外部能量条件简化为n²≥0；转向服从条件-ṁ≥3m|a|，由Bondi质量损失支付。壳层满足表面主能量条件（surface dominant energy condition）的条件为2m/R<24/25；可容许的加速壳层存在于Schwarzschild-Minkowski锚点附近以及慢燃（slow burn）情形下。加速存在Buchdahl型边界：a_max R≤g(2m/R)，下界约0.2，上界为(1/2)(1-2m/R)。在引力波静默类（gravitational-wave–silent class）中，最优机动为Damour偶极（Damour dipole）。壳层边缘为边际稳定（marginally stable），严格稳定可在不牺牲能量条件的前提下实现；完全动力学通量耦合稳定性（fully dynamical flux-coupled stability）仍有待研究。

Conclusion: 该驱动器是因果的（causal）、亚光速的（subluminal），能量成本高但为正能：转向问题本质上是能量预算（energy budget）问题，而非依赖于奇异物质。

Abstract: A useful warp drive must change its velocity, yet known positive-energy constructions are static or constant-velocity, while accelerating ones require exotic matter; Bobrick and Martire noted that warp drives ``do not have any natural way of changing their velocities.'' First, a conservation law settles the principle: for any asymptotically flat drive with a confined dominant-energy source and standard peeling, the Bondi--Sachs four-momentum changes only through radiation to null infinity, so the drive cannot steer without radiating. Second, we construct a positive-energy spacetime that saturates this bound. Prescribing the passenger worldtube, we take the exact Kinnersley photon rocket as exterior and solve for the matching timelike shell; the exterior and steering law are exact, while the shell is certified perturbatively and numerically. The mechanism is photon-rocket recoil on a tidally protected, exactly flat cavity; the warp drive is the decoupled flat interior, not a warp field. The exterior energy conditions reduce to $n^2\ge0$, and steering obeys $-\dot m\ge 3m|a|$, paid for by Bondi mass loss. The shell satisfies the surface dominant energy condition for $2m/R<24/25$; admissible accelerating shells exist near the Schwarzschild--Minkowski anchor and, for slow burns, as time-evolved spacetimes. A Buchdahl-type frontier $a_{\max}R\le g(2m/R)$ caps the acceleration between a numerical lower bound $\sim\!0.2$ and a closed-form ceiling ${1\over2}(1-2m/R)$. On the gravitational-wave--silent class, the optimal maneuver is the Damour dipole. The wall is marginally stable, with strict stability available at no energy-condition cost; fully dynamical flux-coupled stability remains open. The drive is causal, subluminal, and energetically costly but positive-energy: steering is a problem of energy budget, not exotic matter.

</details>


### [355] [Extended parameterized spin expansion formalism for ringdown analysis with GW250114](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22580)
*Jia-Ning Chen,Liang-Bi Wu,Zong-Kuan Guo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文将参数化自旋展开系数（ParSpec）框架扩展为理论无关（theory-agnostic）形式，同时对特征长度尺度 ℓ 和缩放指数 p 进行采样，并应用于GW250114和GW231123的ringdown数据分析。结果表明，当前信噪比（SNR）下数据无法区分不同的缩放行为，对 ℓ 的约束主要来自参数空间几何，且220-only模型比220+221模型提供更具信息量的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ringdown测试通常将ParSpec框架中的缩放指数 p 固定为理论驱动的整数值，缺乏理论无关的描述方式。本文通过同时采样 ℓ 和 p 参数，旨在提供一种更通用的、基于有效场论（effective-field theory）精神的ringdown频谱分析框架，从而不依赖特定理论假设。

Method: 基于ParSpec框架，将原参数 ℓ 和 p 替换为 $\tilde{\ell}$ 和 $\tilde{p}$ 后同时进行采样；利用 pyRing 工具对GW250114应用分析，采用 $M_{\rm f}$ 和 $D_{\rm L}$ 的信息性先验（informative priors），比较220-only与220+221两种模态模型在不同 γ 条件下的表现；通过后验分布和Kullback-Leibler散度（Kullback-Leibler divergence）评估信息增益。

Result: $\tilde{p}$ 的后验分布主要受先验主导，表明当前ringdown数据无法区分不同缩放行为；对 $\tilde{\ell}$ 的约束主要由 γ 条件导致的参数空间几何决定；γ<1 条件下给出 $\tilde{\ell}_{90}\simeq 83\,{\rm km}$ 的稳定但较弱的上限；Kullback-Leibler散度分析显示 $\tilde{\ell}$ 和 $\logγ$ 的数据驱动信息增益很小；220-only模型比220+221模型提供更具信息量的约束；联合分析GW231123后，约束仍由GW250114主导。

Conclusion: 当前ringdown数据信噪比尚不足以区分不同理论中的修正缩放行为，ParSpec扩展框架的有效性受限于参数空间几何和先验影响；220-only模型在当前阶段优于引入更高阶模态的模型；未来需要更高信噪比的数据才能获得有意义的约束。

Abstract: We extend the Parameterized Spin Expansion Coefficients (ParSpec) framework for ringdown tests of black holes by simultaneously sampling the characteristic length scale $\ell$ and the scaling index $p$, where the two parameters are replaced by $\tilde{p}$ and $\tilde{\ell}$ in subsequent analysis, respectively. Unlike previous analyses that fix $\tilde{p}$ to theory-motivated integer values, this extension provides a theory-agnostic description inspired by effective-field theory to the Kerr ringdown spectrum. Using \texttt{pyRing}, we apply the framework to GW250114 with informative priors on $M_{\rm f}$ and $D_{\rm L}$, comparing the $220$-only and $220+221$ mode models under different conditions on $γ$. The posterior distributions of $\tilde{\ell}, \tilde{p}$ and $γ$ are presented with different ringdown start times. We show that the posterior of $\tilde{p}$ remains largely prior dominated, indicating that current ringdown data cannot distinguish different scaling behaviors of the correction. The inferred constraint on $\tilde{\ell}$ is instead mainly controlled by the geometry of the allowed parameter space induced by the $γ$ condition. In particular, $γ<1$ provides the most natural prescription in the $(\tilde{\ell},\tilde{p})$ plane and yields stable but weak upper bounds of $\tilde{\ell}_{90}\simeq 83\, {\rm km}$. An analysis based on the Kullback-Leibler divergence further shows that, after accounting for the effective prior associated with $γ<1$, the data-driven information gain on $\tilde{\ell}$ and $\logγ$ is very small. At the current SNR level, the $220$-only model provides a more informative constraint than the $220+221$ model. We also perform a joint analysis including GW231123 and find that the combined constraint is dominated by GW250114.

Abstract: Cross-correlation searches for gravitational-wave backgrounds depend on the geometrical configuration (physical separation and relative orientation) of the detectors comprising the network. Applying standard techniques to a few simple examples, we illustrate how the relative orientation of a pair of Earth-based L-shaped laser interferometers can drastically impact the detectability of both isotropic and anisotropic gravitational-wave backgrounds.

### [358] [Periodic Timelike Motion and Gravitational Wave Signatures around a Magnetically Charged Black Hole Surrounded by Quintessence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23021)
*R. H. Ali*

Method: 通过有效势（effective potential）分析有质量粒子的运动，确定边际束缚轨道（marginally bound orbit）和最内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbit），并利用zoom-whirl分类法$(z,w,v)$对束缚轨迹进行分类；随后在数值kludge（numerical kludge）近似下建模极端质量比旋进（extreme-mass-ratio inspiral）产生的引力辐射。

Result: 五重态参数$c_q$系统性改变周期性轨道家族的轨道半径、守恒量和转向点结构；引力波波形呈现zoom-whirl运动的爆发状结构，五重态耦合参数影响相位演化、爆发时序和谐波成分；傅里叶谱呈现离散梳状结构，特征应变（characteristic strain）集中在毫赫兹频段，适用于LISA等空间探测器。

Abstract: We investigate timelike geodesics and gravitational wave signatures of periodic motion around a static magnetically charged black hole arising from nonlinear electrodynamics and immersed in a quintessence background. We analyze the effective potential for massive particles, determine the marginally bound and innermost stable circular orbits, and classify the resulting bound trajectories using the zoom-whirl taxonomy $(\mathit{z},\mathit{w},\mathit{v})$. We show that the quintessence parameter $c_q$ systematically shifts the orbital radii, conserved quantities, and turning-point structure associated with representative periodic families.
  We then model the gravitational radiation emitted by periodic extreme-mass-ratio inspirals within the numerical kludge approximation. The resulting waveforms exhibit the characteristic burst-like structure of zoom-whirl motion, while variations in the quintessence coupling parameter modify the phase evolution, burst timing, and harmonic content of the signal. The corresponding Fourier spectra display a discrete comb-like structure, and the characteristic strain is concentrated in the millihertz band relevant for space-based detectors such as LISA. These results indicate that a quintessence background can leave systematic imprints on periodic orbit dynamics and on the associated time and frequency-domain gravitational wave observables.

### [359] [MaxWave Signal: Rapid, coherent maximum likelihood wavelet reconstruction of transient signals in gravitational wave data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23035)
*Sudhi Mathur,Neil J. Cornish*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文扩展了MaxWave快速最大似然小波重构算法，使其能够进行相干多探测器信号重构和瞬态噪声（glitch）抑制。通过构建合成探测器（synthetic detector）以增强相干信号、抑制噪声，算法实现了实时、低延迟、模型无关（model-independent）的引力波信号重构，可提升对弱信号的敏感度并增强现有爆发搜索框架的检测置信度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波探测器灵敏度的提升增加了暂现信号（transient signal）的探测率，急需更快的自动化分析方法来处理持续增长的数据流。

Method: 扩展MaxWave算法，基于所有探测器中共同的小波（wavelet）集进行相干搜索。首先，利用z统计量（z-statistic）的时间与相位偏移以及振幅缩放，相对于主重构（dominant reconstruction）对齐多探测器数据；同时，基于几何平均噪声谱（geometrically averaged noise spectrum）导出自适应噪声权重（adaptive noise weightings）。通过对齐与加权，构建一个合成探测器（synthetic detector），该探测器能够放大非高斯（non-Gaussian）特征、降低高噪声探测器的权重并保留高斯噪声统计特性，进而提取相干信号。

Result: 该算法能提升对弱事件的敏感度，同时抑制那些缺乏一致相位和振幅演化的符合性噪声（coincident glitches）。最终实现实时、低延迟的模型无关信号重构，安全地去噪而不移除暂现信号。

Conclusion: 该方法可通过一种根本不同的途径（fundamentally distinct approach）补充现有的爆发搜索与重构框架，增强检测置信度并改善对不同信号形态（signal morphologies）的灵敏度。

Abstract: Advances in gravitational-wave detector sensitivity have increased the rate of transient signal detections, demanding faster automated analysis. We extend MaxWave, a fast maximum likelihood wavelet reconstruction algorithm, to perform coherent multi-detector signal reconstruction and glitch rejection. We coherently search for a common set of wavelets modeling the signal in all detectors. Multi-detector data are aligned using z-statistic time and phase offsets and amplitude scalings relative to the dominant reconstruction, as well as adaptive noise weightings derived from a geometrically averaged noise spectrum. By aligning and weighting individual detectors, we form a synthetic detector that amplifies non-Gaussian features, down-weights noisy detectors, and preserves Gaussian noise statistics. We extract the coherent signal using this synthetic detector, improving sensitivity to weak events while rejecting coincident glitches that lack consistent phase and amplitude evolution. Our algorithm provides real-time, low-latency, model-independent signal reconstructions, safely denoises gravitational wave data without removing transient signals, and can complement existing burst search and reconstruction frameworks through a fundamentally distinct approach, strengthening detection confidence and improving sensitivity to diverse signal morphologies.

### [360] [Polarization States and Effective Stress Energy Tensor of Gravitational Waves in Metric $f(R)$ Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23056)
*Sakshi Srivastava,Utkal Keshari Dash,Murli Manohar Verma*

TL;DR: 本文在线性化闵氏时空近似下，研究了度规f(R)引力中引力波的极化性质与有效应力-能量张量，揭示了标量自由度激发的横向呼吸模与纵模，并基于Isaacson高频平均形式论推导了包含张量与标量贡献的能量密度，指出大质量标量模的亚光速群速度导致能量通量的频率依赖抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在修正引力理论中，引力波极化模式与能量输运是检验广义相对论（general relativity）之外新物理的关键探针。度规f(R)引力因内含额外标量自由度，其引力波行为与广义相对论存在本质差异，但目前缺乏对其极化-能量统一联系的系统研究。

Method: 采用闵氏时空（Minkowski spacetime）下的线性化近似；利用线性化Riemann张量的电分量推导极化振幅的显式表达式；运用Isaacson高频平均（high-frequency averaging）形式论导出有效应力-能量张量。

Result: 无质量标量场激发横向呼吸模（transverse breathing mode），大质量标量场通过单个传播标量激发同时产生呼吸模与纵模（longitudinal response）；张量与标量扰动均贡献于引力波总能量密度；大质量标量模的亚光速群速度导致标量能量通量出现频率依赖的抑制效应。

Conclusion: 本文建立了度规f(R)引力中引力波极化与能量输运的统一联系，为利用当前和未来引力波探测器检验修正引力理论提供了潜在的可观测特征。

Abstract: We investigate the polarization properties and effective stress--energy tensor of gravitational waves in metric $f(R)$ gravity within the linearized approximation around Minkowski spacetime. Owing to the additional scalar degree of freedom inherent in the theory, gravitational waves exhibit polarization states beyond the two tensor modes predicted by general relativity. Using the electric components of the linearized Riemann tensor, we derive explicit expressions for the polarization amplitudes and show that a massless scalar field excites a transverse breathing mode, whereas a massive scalar field generates both breathing and longitudinal responses through a single propagating scalar excitation. Employing the Isaacson high-frequency averaging formalism, we further derive the effective stress--energy tensor and demonstrate that both tensor and scalar perturbations contribute to the total gravitational-wave energy density. The energy transport associated with the massive scalar mode is reduced by its subluminal group velocity, leading to a frequency-dependent suppression of the scalar energy flux. These results establish a unified connection between gravitational-wave polarization and energy transport in metric $f(R)$ gravity and provide potential observational signatures for testing modified gravity with current and future gravitational-wave detectors.

</details>


### [361] [Dark matter from the quadratic spinor Lagrangian II: A spin-3/2 no-go and the uniqueness of the spin-1/2 candidate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23273)
*Roh-Suan Tung*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明，将复合二次旋量拉格朗日量（QSL）中的旋量1-形式提升为独立狄拉克-矢量场并不会产生有质量的spin-3/2暗物质候选者。通过三项结果构成的不存在定理（no-go theorem），论证了唯一存在的传播激发是复合的spin-1/2狄拉克费米子，该模式可被解读为超对称性破缺产生的戈德斯通费米子（Goldstino），是QSL中唯一的暗物质候选者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索将复合二次旋量拉格朗日量（composite Quadratic Spinor Lagrangian, QSL）中的旋量1-形式$Ψ_μ$提升为独立的狄拉克-矢量（Dirac-vector）场，是否能够产生一个真正的spin-3/2暗物质（dark-matter）候选者。

Method: 通过三项独立结果的结合来证明一个不存在定理（no-go theorem）：(1) 利用克利福德约化（Clifford reduction）精确计算挠率项；(2) 分析二阶形式$2 DΨγ_5 DΨ$中独立场的动能项与交叉项；(3) 考察曲率侧的作用量$S=-\int\barψψR\sqrt{-g}$的二阶变分因子化结构。

Result: 三项结果共同表明不存在有质量的spin-3/2模式。挠率项仅是局限于时间分量区间的框架对齐质量；二阶形式的动能项和交叉项恒为零；曲率侧作用量的二阶变分因子化为线性化度规和标量场的泛函，所有传播极点均落在度规光锥$k^2=0$上——仅包含引力子（graviton）和一个标量粒子（scalar）——不产生任何有质量的spin-3/2模式。

Conclusion: 复合spin-1/2狄拉克费米子是QSL中唯一存在的传播物质激发和唯一的暗物质候选者。通过超SL(2,C)结构（super-SL(2,C) structure），该幸存模式可被自然解读为度规凝聚（metric condensate）破缺局域超对称（local supersymmetry）所产生的戈德斯通费米子（Goldstino），是Pagels和Primack提出的轻引力微子暗物质（light-gravitino dark matter）的复合引力后裔。

Abstract: The composite Quadratic Spinor Lagrangian (QSL) propagates a spin-1/2 Dirac fermion whose mass is generated geometrically by cosmological trace torsion. It is natural to ask whether promoting the spinor 1-form $Ψ_μ$ to an \emph{independent} Dirac-vector field yields a genuine spin-3/2 dark-matter candidate. We prove that it does not. Three results combine into a no-go theorem. First, the torsional term, computed exactly by Clifford reduction, is a frame-aligned mass confined to the time-component sector -- not a uniform spin-3/2 mass. Second, the second-order form $2 DΨγ_5 DΨ$ has identically vanishing kinetic and cross terms for the independent field: as a component expression it is the boundary part of the spinor-curvature identity and carries no bulk dynamics. Third, the genuine dynamics therefore reside in the curvature side of that identity, $S=-\int\barψψR\sqrt{-g}$, in which the metric $g=Ψ\otimes_SΨ$ and the scalar $\barψψ$ are \emph{both} composites of $Ψ$; the second variation consequently factors, $δ^2S=\mathcal Q(h_{μν}[δΨ],δΦ[δΨ])$, through the linearized metric and a scalar, both massless. Every propagating pole therefore lies on the metric light cone $k^2=0$ -- the graviton and a scalar -- and no massive spin-3/2 mode exists, on any background. This is the dynamical completion of the kinematic fact that the composite spinor 1-form has no spin-3/2 part, and it establishes the composite spin-1/2 Dirac fermion as the unique propagating matter excitation, and the unique dark-matter candidate, of the QSL. Through the super-SL(2,C) structure this surviving mode is naturally read as the Goldstino of the local supersymmetry broken by the metric condensate -- a composite, gravitational descendant of the light-gravitino dark matter of Pagels and Primack.

### [362] [Primordial Black Holes from Vector-Induced Curvature Perturbations Sourced by Primordial Magnetic Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23307)
*Chang Han,Zu-Cheng Chen,Hongwei Yu,Puxun Wu*

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的暴胀后（post-inflationary）机制，在刚硬（stiff）或动能主导（kination）时期，通过原初磁场（PMFs）的电磁应力-能量张量激发矢量度规扰动，进而通过二阶标量扰动放大原初曲率扰动，从而有效产生原初黑洞（PBHs），并展示该机制可使PBHs构成暗物质的相当一部分。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出在动能主导（kination）时期，利用原初磁场（PMFs）的电磁应力-能量张量（electromagnetic stress-energy tensor）的矢量分量激发一阶矢量度规扰动（first-order vector modes）；这些矢量模在动能主导时期近似保持常数，作为持久的非线性源驱动二阶标量扰动（second-order scalar perturbations），从而放大曲率扰动。

Result: 矢量诱导的曲率扰动在动能主导波段的红外截断（infrared cutoff）附近被显著放大，并呈现特征标度行为 $\mathcal P_{\mathcal R}(k)\propto k^{-5}$。在Ratra型磁生成（magnetogenesis）场景下，诱导的曲率扰动足以产生足够丰度的原初黑洞，使其构成暗物质的相当一部分。

Conclusion: 本文提出的暴胀后机制为产生原初黑洞提供了一条新路径，表明原初磁场通过矢量-标量耦合可以在动能主导时期有效增强曲率扰动，从而贡献暗物质成分。

Abstract: Generating an appreciable abundance of primordial black holes (PBHs) requires a substantial enhancement of primordial curvature perturbations on small scales. In this work, we propose a new post-inflationary mechanism in which such an enhancement arises during a stiff, or kination, epoch. The mechanism is driven by metric vector perturbations sourced by the vector component of the electromagnetic stress-energy tensor associated with primordial magnetic fields (PMFs). Since these first-order vector modes remain approximately constant during kination, they act as persistent nonlinear sources for second-order scalar perturbations. We show that the resulting vector-induced curvature perturbations are amplified toward the infrared cutoff of the kination band and exhibit the characteristic scaling $\mathcal P_{\mathcal R}(k)\propto k^{-5}$. As a concrete realization, we consider PMFs generated in a Ratra-type magnetogenesis scenario and find that the induced curvature perturbations can produce PBHs with an abundance large enough to constitute a substantial fraction of the dark matter.

### [363] [Scattered wave functions and worldline instantons for particle production in curved spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23389)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用两种互补方法：(1) 将原本用于电磁背景（electromagnetic backgrounds）中粒子对产生的散射波函数（scattered-wave-function, SWF）方法推广至弯曲时空背景；(2) 推导并完善开世界线瞬子（open-worldline-instanton）方法，重点计算其对产生概率的指数前因子（pre-exponential factor）。

Conclusion: 研究所发展的两种新方法为多维引力背景下的粒子对产生提供了有力的理论工具，能够处理许多现有方法无法适用的情形。

Abstract: We study the production of spin-$1/2$ particle-antiparticle pairs in curved spacetimes with nontrivial dependence on more than one coordinate. To this end, we develop two complementary approaches. First, we extend the scattered-wave-function (SWF) method, originally introduced for pair production in electromagnetic backgrounds, to curved spacetime backgrounds. Second, we complete the development of an open-worldline-instanton method by deriving the pre-exponential factor of the pair-production probability. We apply both methods to several two-dimensional metrics and find good agreement between the resulting probabilities. While the SWF approach provides numerically exact results and is particularly efficient for the examples considered here, the instanton approach offers favorable scaling to higher-dimensional backgrounds and more extreme parameter regimes. These methods provide new tools for studying pair production in multidimensional gravitational backgrounds beyond the reach of many existing approaches.

### [364] [High-Stability Deformable Mirrors for Correcting Non-Axisymmetric Residual Aberrations in Thermal Compensation of Future Gravitational Wave Interferometers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23415)

Result: 论文展示了该投影策略的仿真结果以及实验验证，结果表明该方法能够一致地复现（consistent reproduction）所需的强度图案。

Conclusion: 可变形镜结合改进的Gerchberg-Saxton算法能够有效产生非对称强度图案，为引力波探测器中非轴对称波前畸变的校正提供了一种可行方案，有望提升未来高功率干涉仪的稳定性与灵敏度。

Abstract: In gravitational wave detectors, optical aberrations arise mainly from laser absorption in coatings and production process defects in the optics along the laser path. If left uncorrected, these optical path distortions drive the interferometer away from its optimal working point, degrading both stability and sensitivity. Future instruments such as the Einstein Telescope high-frequency detector will operate with unprecedented circulating power, further amplifying the aberration budget. In the current detectors Advanced Virgo and Advanced LIGO, the axisymmetric distortions are corrected using thermal actuators and CO2 laser projectors, however, non-axisymmetric wavefront distortions remain unmitigated. Deformable mirrors are investigated as a flexible solution for mitigating such defects: by shaping the CO2 beam phase upon reflection, they can imprint the required asymmetric intensity pattern on the lensing optics without introducing frequency dependent noise. The target phase map is computed via a modified Gerchberg-Saxton algorithm. We present simulations of this projection strategy and experimental validation demonstrating consistent reproduction of the desired intensity patterns.

### [365] [Spacetime torsion fixes the mass and spin of gravitationally produced dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23418)
*Roh-Suan Tung*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明，在爱因斯坦-嘉当（Einstein–Cartan）框架下的二次旋量拉格朗日量（Quadratic Spinor Lagrangian）表述中，宇宙学旋量凝聚体（cosmological spinor condensate）产生的矢量挠率（vectorial trace torsion）可为随机引力波（stochastic gravitational waves）产生的费米子提供质量，从而无需希格斯（Higgs）机制或自由质量参数。所得狄拉克（Dirac）质量锁定于产生时的哈勃（Hubble）率，其剩余丰度仅由一个参数决定，且该框架唯一预言的暗物质候选者是自旋1/2的狄拉克费米子。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机引力波产生暗物质的过程要求产生的费米子通过未指明的晚期物理学获得质量；本文旨在证明该质量无需引入希格斯扇区（Higgs sector）或自由质量参数，而仅由时空挠率（spacetime torsion）即可提供。

Method: 采用广义相对论的二次旋量拉格朗日量表述，并将其推广至爱因斯坦–嘉当理论；引入宇宙学旋量凝聚体以生成矢量迹挠率（vectorial trace torsion）$K\propto\dotχ/χ$，并通过显式的克利福德约化（Clifford reduction）为产生的自旋1/2费米子赋予纯狄拉克质量。

Result: 产生的费米子获得纯狄拉克质量$M_{\rm eff}=(1/\sqrt6)\,|\dotχ/χ|$，不含赝标量（pseudoscalar）或交叉项（cross terms）；该质量锁定于产生时的哈勃率，$M_{\rm eff}\simeq(c_χ/\sqrt6)H_*$；剩余丰度由单一参数预测，满足$Ωh^2\propto H_*^{5/2}$；框架中不存在传播的自旋3/2模式，唯一的暗物质候选者是复合自旋1/2狄拉克费米子。

Conclusion: 该框架为随机引力波产生暗物质的质量起源提供了一种无需额外自由参数的纯几何机制，且自旋自由度受到严格约束，仅允许自旋1/2狄拉克费米子作为暗物质候选者。

Abstract: The gravitational production of dark matter from stochastic gravitational waves requires the produced fermion to acquire a mass by unspecified late-time physics. We show that this mass is supplied by spacetime torsion alone -- no Higgs sector and no free mass parameter. In the Quadratic Spinor Lagrangian formulation of general relativity, extended to Einstein--Cartan, a cosmological spinor condensate generates a vectorial trace torsion $K\propto\dotχ/χ$; an explicit Clifford reduction confers on the produced spin-1/2 fermion a pure Dirac mass $M_{\rm eff}=(1/\sqrt6)\,|\dotχ/χ|$, with no pseudoscalar or cross terms, locked to the Hubble rate at production, $M_{\rm eff}\simeq(c_χ/\sqrt6)H_*$. The relic abundance is then a one-parameter prediction, $Ωh^2\propto H_*^{5/2}$, and the spin is fixed: the same framework admits no propagating spin-3/2 mode, so the composite spin-1/2 Dirac fermion is its unique dark-matter candidate.

### [366] [Closed and broken electromagnetic orbits in Kerr--Newman spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23446)
*Erasmo Caponio,Giulio Sanzeni,Stefan Suhr*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kerr-Newman时空的时间机器区域中轴向Killing场是类时的，这为因果违反现象提供了可能。本文旨在系统研究该区域中带电粒子的电磁轨道行为，并探索通过带电粒子衰变过程同时实现能量提取与因果违反的机制。

Method: 首先构造与类时轴向Killing场相切的平滑闭合电磁轨道；然后证明赤道时间机器区域中存在球形电磁轨道并推导其半径与荷质比等参数的关系；给出赤道电磁轨道成为飞越轨道（flyby orbit）的充分条件；最后引入破碎电磁轨道（broken electromagnetic orbit）概念，通过连接多段光滑解并施加四动量与电荷守恒条件，构建包含衰变过程的闭合轨道。

Result: 得到了闭合电磁轨道半径与粒子荷质比（charge-to-mass ratio）之间的显式关系，且荷质比须与黑洞电荷符号相反；推导了球形电磁轨道的半径、荷质比、能量与角动量之间的显式关系；给出了飞越轨道径向折返点位于时间机器区域的充分条件；构建了一条包含能量提取过程与因果违反过程的闭合破碎电磁轨道，该轨道位于内视界（inner horizon）内部，由两段飞越分支与一段球形轨道拼接而成。

Conclusion: 在Kerr-Newman时空中，时间机器区域内部存在丰富的电磁轨道结构，且通过破碎电磁轨道机制，带电粒子衰变过程可以在单一轨道中同时实现能量提取与因果违反，这为研究广义相对论框架下的因果破坏与能量动力学提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: We study future-pointing timelike solutions of the Lorentz force equation in the sub-extremal Kerr--Newman spacetime, with special attention to the time-machine region $\mathfrak T$, where the axial Killing field $\partial_φ$ is timelike. We first construct smooth closed electromagnetic orbits tangent to $\partial_φ$ in the positive equatorial part of $\mathfrak T$: the radius of such a circle determines, and is determined by, the charge-to-mass ratio of the particle which must have opposite sign to that of the black hole charge. We then prove the existence of spherical electromagnetic orbits contained in the equatorial time-machine region and derive explicit relations between their radius, charge-to-mass ratio, energy and angular momentum. Next we give sufficient conditions ensuring that an equatorial electromagnetic orbit is a flyby orbit with radial turning point in $\mathfrak T$. Finally, to describe charged-particle decay processes whose fragments have different charge-to-mass ratios, we introduce the notion of a broken electromagnetic orbit: a continuous, piecewise smooth, future-pointing worldline whose smooth pieces solve the Lorentz force equation. Imposing conservation of kinetic four-momentum and electric charge at the decay vertices, we exhibit an energy extraction process followed by a causality-violating one. The latter is realized by a closed broken electromagnetic orbit, which we construct in both the $r$-positive and the $r$-negative regions inside the inner horizon, by concatenating two flyby branches sharing a common radial turning value $\bar r$, and having charge-to-mass ratios with opposite sign to that of the black hole charge, with a spherical electromagnetic orbit of radius $\bar r$.

### [367] [Dark matter from the quadratic spinor Lagrangian I: Geometric mass for a gravitationally produced spin-1/2 fermion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23447)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Maleknejad与Kopp (2026)提出的引力波诱导freeze-in机制能够从随机引力波背景产生暗费米子，但该机制需要额外手段赋予费米子质量。本文旨在通过广义相对论的几何扩展自然提供这一质量，无需引入自由参数。

Method: 发展二次旋量拉格朗日量（Quadratic Spinor Lagrangian, QSL）形式，将其扩展至爱因斯坦-嘉当（Einstein–Cartan）理论。利用单个狄拉克场构建的旋量1-形式（spinor 1-form）具有纯自旋-1/2特性（其伽马无迹部分恒为零），并通过克利福德约化（Clifford reduction）分析旋量凝聚体诱导的矢量挠率（vectorial trace torsion）对费米子质量的影响。

Result: 旋量凝聚体诱导的矢量挠率 $K\propto\dotχ/χ$ 通过克利福德约化给出纯狄拉克质量 $M_{eff}=(1/\sqrt6)\,|\dotχ/χ|$，不含赝标量或交叉项。该质量锁定于产生时的哈勃率 $M_{eff}\simeq(c_χ/\sqrt6)H_*$，使暗物质剩余丰度成为单标度函数 $\Omega h^2\propto H_*^{5/2}$。论文II进一步表明将旋量1-形式提升为独立场不会产生传播的自旋-3/2激发，复合自旋-1/2狄拉克费米子是唯一的QSL暗物质候选者。

Conclusion: QSL形式为引力波诱导freeze-in机制提供了所需的几何质量来源，使暗物质丰度仅依赖于一个基本标度 $H_*$，无需额外自由参数。该工作还讨论了所得暗物质现象学及其与渐近自由标量场宇宙学的联系。

Abstract: The gravitational-wave induced freeze-in of Maleknejad and Kopp (2026) produces dark fermions from a stochastic gravitational-wave background, but requires them to acquire mass by separate means. We develop the Quadratic Spinor Lagrangian (QSL) formulation of general relativity, extended to Einstein--Cartan, as a framework that supplies this mass geometrically. The spinor 1-form built from a single Dirac field is purely spin-1/2 -- its gamma-traceless (spin-3/2) part vanishes identically -- so the propagating excitation is a Dirac fermion, the same content as the produced Weyl fermion. A cosmological spinor condensate sources a vectorial trace torsion $K\propto\dotχ/χ$, and an explicit Clifford reduction shows that this torsion gives the fermion a pure Dirac mass $M_{eff}=(1/\sqrt6)\,|\dotχ/χ|$, with no pseudoscalar or cross terms. The mass is not a free parameter but is locked to the Hubble rate at production, $M_{eff}\simeq(c_χ/\sqrt6)H_*$, making the relic abundance a function of essentially the single scale $H_*$ ($Ωh^2\propto H_*^{5/2}$) and supplying the mass the parent mechanism must postulate. Whether promoting the spinor 1-form to an independent field yields a propagating spin-3/2 candidate is a distinct dynamical question; Paper II shows that it does not -- the QSL channels all propagation into the gravitational sector -- so the composite spin-1/2 Dirac fermion is the unique QSL dark-matter candidate. We discuss the resulting dark-matter phenomenology and its link to asymptotically free scalar-field cosmology.

</details>


### [368] [Affine quantization of the dynamical Reissner--Nordström region](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23552)
*Morteza Bajand,Babak Vakili*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过微超空间约化（minisuperspace reduction）和仿射量子化（affine quantization）研究Reissner–Nordström时空动态区域的量子动力学，发现Wheeler–DeWitt方程可分离，得到Hermite多项式模式和高斯型径向解，并分析了电荷在量子动力学中的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将先前关于Schwarzschild黑洞的仿射量子化研究扩展到带电荷的Reissner–Nordström几何，以理解电荷对量子黑洞动力学的影响。

Method: 采用微超空间约化（minisuperspace reduction）和仿射量子化（affine quantization）——后者天然适用于正定几何变量——对Reissner–Nordström度规的动态区域进行量子化，并构造可归一化的半经典波包（semiclassical wave packets）。

Result: Wheeler–DeWitt方程变为可分离形式，在一扇区得到Hermite多项式（Hermite-polynomial）模式，在另一扇区得到类高斯径向解（Gaussian-like radial solutions）。仿射量子化引入的短距离贡献修改了小半径处的波函数行为。

Conclusion: 仿射量子化方法成功扩展至带电荷的Reissner–Nordström几何，电荷在微超空间中的概率分布和量子动力学中扮演了重要角色。

Abstract: We study the quantum dynamics of the dynamical region of the Reissner--Nordström geometry using a minisuperspace reduction and affine quantization, which is naturally suited for positive-definite geometrical variables. The resulting Wheeler--DeWitt equation becomes separable, yielding Hermite-polynomial modes in one sector and Gaussian-like radial solutions in the other. Affine quantization introduces additional short-distance contributions that modify the small-radius behaviour of the wave function. By constructing normalizable semiclassical wave packets, we analyze the resulting probability distributions in minisuperspace and the role played by the electric charge in the quantum dynamics. Our results extend previous affine-quantization studies of the Schwarzschild case to the charged Reissner--Nordström geometry.

</details>


### [369] [Equatorial Periodic Orbits and Gravitational Wave Phenomenology around Spherically-symmetric vacuum solution in Freund-Nambu scalar-tensor gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23635)
*Dhruba Jyoti Gogoi,Jyatsnasree Bora,Himanshu Chaudhary,M. Yousaf,G. Mustafa*

Method: 基于Janis-Newman-Winicour（JNW）裸奇点的精确球对称真空解，引入几何非线性耦合$q$与直接标量-粒子耦合$g_s$；利用数值Kludge方法模拟极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）的引力波波形，分析轨道动力学参数变化与标量-张量修正对高频引力波爆发产生的时间失谐。

Result: 正标量-粒子耦合$g_s>0$使内稳圆轨道（ISCO）向内移动，同时边缘束缚轨道（MBO）也被系统修正；极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）中的高频引力波爆发出现宏观时间失谐，即使轨道空间拓扑结构保持不变。

Conclusion: 标量-张量修正导致的独特相位偏移可作为未来LISA等空间天文台探测强场引力、约束广义相对论标量-张量扩展的稳健诊断特征。

Abstract: We investigate test particle dynamics and gravitational wave (GW) phenomenology in an exact spherically symmetric vacuum solution of Freund - Nambu scalar - tensor gravity. This framework generalizes the Janis - Newman - Winicour (JNW) naked singularity via a geometric non - linear coupling $q$ and a direct scalar - particle coupling $g_s$. We demonstrate that these parameters systematically modify the Innermost Stable Circular Orbit (ISCO) - which shifts inward for $g_s > 0$ - and the Marginally Bound Orbit (MBO). Furthermore, we classify bound periodic trajectories to isolate extreme zoom - whirl orbits exhibiting intense periapsis precession. By applying the Numerical Kludge method to Extreme Mass - Ratio Inspirals (EMRIs), we reveal that scalar - tensor corrections induce a macroscopic temporal dephasing in high - frequency GW bursts, even when the orbit's spatial topology is preserved. These unique phase shifts offer a robust diagnostic signature for future space-based observatories like LISA to probe the strong - field regime and constrain scalar - tensor extensions of general relativity.

### [370] [On toric self-dual Einstein gravitational instantons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21455)
*Bernardo Araneda,James Lucietti,Virinchi Rallabhandi*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究带有负宇宙常数（negative cosmological constant）的环面自对偶爱因斯坦引力瞬子（toric self-dual Einstein gravitational instanton）的分类问题。证明若与某个环面基灵场（torus Killing field）关联的共形凯勒结构（conformal Kähler structure）是全局的，且可延拓至无额外不动点的ALE流形上，则该自对偶爱因斯坦瞬子必然属于Calderbank、Pedersen与Singer构造的多极解（multipole solutions）无穷类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨带有负宇宙常数的环面自对偶爱因斯坦引力瞬子的分类问题，以明确此类几何对象的结构特征。

Method: 利用自对偶爱因斯坦流形上基灵矢量场（Killing vector field）定义局部共形凯勒结构（local conformal Kähler structure）的已知性质，通过分析该结构的全局延拓性及ALE流形上的不动点条件，进行分类论证。

Result: 若与某个环面基灵场对应的共形凯勒结构是全局的，并能延拓至无额外不动点的ALE流形，则对应的自对偶爱因斯坦瞬子必属于Calderbank、Pedersen与Singer构造的多极解无穷类。

Conclusion: 在特定全局性假设下，带有负宇宙常数的环面自对偶爱因斯坦引力瞬子的分类可归结为已知的多极解无穷类。

Abstract: We consider the classification of toric self-dual Einstein gravitational instantons with negative cosmological constant. As is well known, any Killing vector field on a self-dual Einstein manifold defines a local conformal Kähler structure. We prove that if the conformal Kähler structure associated to one of the torus Killing fields is global and extends to an ALE manifold with no additional fixed points, then the corresponding self-dual Einstein instanton is precisely given by the infinite class of multipole solutions constructed by Calderbank, Pedersen and Singer.

### [371] [Vafa-Witten Equations and Conformal Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22100)
*Teng Huang,Pan Zhang*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了闭四维流形上Vafa-Witten方程非平凡解所施加的几何与分析约束，建立了包含Yamabe常数与自对偶Weyl张量的不等式、Kahler几何刻画条件、降维对应关系以及能量间隙等若干关键结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究闭四维流形上Vafa-Witten方程非平凡解的存在性对流形几何结构（如共形几何、曲率与拓扑）施加何种约束，并推导相关的分析不等式。

Method: 利用共形不变性（conformal invariance）和精细的Bochner型估计（refined Bochner-type estimates）推导不等式；通过降维（dimensional reduction）$S^{1}\times N$ 建立稳定平连接与 $S^{1}$-不变Vafa-Witten解之间的一一对应；在紧化模空间的正则性假设下证明能量间隙（energy gap）。

Result: 得到Yamabe常数与自对偶Weyl张量 $L^2$ 范数的不等式；等号情形下流形必为具有非负标量曲率的Kähler流形且联络可约；正爱因斯坦流形（positive Einstein manifolds）情形下得到尖锐体积界；降维给出Yamabe常数的新估计；正则性假设下证明非平凡解的自对偶曲率 $L^2$ 范数存在正下界。

Conclusion: Vafa-Witten方程的非平凡解对底流形的几何与拓扑施加深刻限制，揭示了该方程与共形几何、Kähler几何以及三维平连接之间的内在联系。

Abstract: In this article, we establish geometric and analytic constraints imposed by the existence of nontrivial solutions to the Vafa-Witten equations on closed 4-manifolds. Using conformal invariance and refined Bochner-type estimates, we first prove an inequality relating the Yamabe constant $Y(g)$ to the $L^{2}$-norm of the self-dual Weyl tensor: $Y(g)\leq 2\sqrt{6}\|W_{g}^{+}\|_{L^2}$; when $Y(g)>0$, this yields a topological lower bound $\int_{M} |W_{g}^{+}|^{2} \geq \frac{4}{3}π^{2}(2χ(M)+3σ(M))$. In the equality case, we show that the manifold must be Kähler with nonnegative scalar curvature and that the connection is reducible. As an application, for positive Einstein manifolds with $\operatorname{Ric}=3g$ admitting an irreducible Vafa-Witten solution, we obtain a sharp volume bound and prove the manifold cannot be Kähler.
  Through dimensional reduction $S^{1}\times N$, we establish a one-to-one correspondence between stable flat connections on a closed 3-manifold $N$ and $S^{1}$-invariant Vafa-Witten solutions, which yields a new estimate for the Yamabe constant $Y(g_{S^{1}\times N})\leq 2\sqrt{6π}\big(\int_{N}|\operatorname{Ric}(g_{N})-\frac{1}{3} R_{g_{N}}g_{N}|^2\big)^{1/2}$. Finally, under a regularity assumption that every anti-self-dual connection in the compactified moduli space is regular, we prove an energy gap: there exists $\varepsilon(g,P)>0$ such that any Vafa-Witten solution satisfies either $F_{A}^{+}\equiv0$ or $\|F_{A}^{+}\|_{L^{2}}\geq\varepsilon$.

</details>


### [372] [Star-Shaped Nakajima Quiver Varieties, Parabolic Higgs Bundle Moduli Spaces, and their Holomorphic Symplectic Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23369)
*Arya Yae*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文在两类超凯勒流形（hyperkähler manifolds）——中心-列维抛物希格斯丛模空间（central-Levi parabolic Higgs bundle moduli spaces）与星形中岛箭图簇（star-shaped Nakajima quiver varieties）之间构造了一个映射 𝒯，证明了该映射保持稳定性，是到具有平凡全纯结构的希格斯丛（Higgs bundles）子空间上的同胚，并且识别了两类空间上的自然全纯辛结构（holomorphic symplectic structures），从而将前人的结果从秩2、全旗、强抛物情形推广到了任意秩、部分旗、弱抛物情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核心动机是将两类看似不同的超凯勒几何对象——中心-列维抛物希格斯丛模空间与星形中岛箭图簇——建立严格的对应关系，并证明这种对应保持其自然的全纯辛结构，从而推动超凯勒对偶（hyperkähler duality）理论的发展。该工作将Biswas等人此前在秩2、全旗、强抛物情况下的结果推广到任意秩、部分旗和弱抛物情形。

Method: 构造了一个从星形箭图簇 𝒳 到中心-列维抛物希格斯丛模空间 ℳ 的映射 𝒯。验证了 𝒯 保持稳定性条件，并通过证明 𝒯 是到具有平凡全纯结构的希格斯丛子空间上的同胚来建立拓扑等价性。进一步证明了主要定理：𝒯 在两类空间上识别出了自然的全纯辛结构。

Result: 映射 𝒯 是从星形中岛箭图簇到中心-列维抛物希格斯丛模空间的同胚，且限制在具有平凡全纯结构的希格斯丛子空间上；两类空间上的自然全纯辛结构在该映射下被识别。

Conclusion: 该定理将Biswas、Florentino、Godinho、Mandini等人的先前结果从秩2、全旗、强抛物情形推广到了任意秩、部分旗、弱抛物（即希格斯场留数投影到各自列维子代数中心）的情形，为更广泛的超凯勒流形之间的对偶关系提供了统一的理论框架。

Abstract: In this paper, we consider two classes of hyperkähler manifolds: moduli spaces of central-Levi parabolic Higgs bundles on the punctured sphere and star-shaped Nakajima quiver varieties. We produce a map $\mathcal T$ from a given star-shaped quiver variety $\mathcal X$ to a central-Levi parabolic Higgs bundle moduli space $\mathcal M$. We verify that $\mathcal T$ preserves stability and we show that it is a homeomorphism onto the locus of Higgs bundles with trivial underlying holomorphic structure. We then prove our main theorem: that $\mathcal T$ identifies the natural holomorphic symplectic structures on the two spaces. This theorem generalizes work by Biswas, Florentino, Godinho, Mandini from the rank 2, full flag, strongly parabolic case to arbitrary rank, partial flag, and weakly parabolic cases -- namely, those whose Higgs field residues project to the centers of their respective Levi subalgebras.

</details>


### [373] [Failure of local equi-Lipschitzness for families of Lorentz distances to Cauchy surface foliations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21997)
*Gregory J. Galloway,Robert J. McCann,Argam Ohanyan*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文指出，沿完整类时线定义的类时距离函数族具有局部等利普希茨连续（locally equi-Lipschitz continuous）性质，但该性质对于沿柯西时间函数（Cauchy temporal function）水平集定义的类时距离函数族一般不再成立；进一步，作者提出了与巴特尼克分裂猜想（Bartnik's splitting conjecture）等价的若干猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典洛伦兹分裂定理（Lorentzian splitting theorems）的证明依赖于沿完整类时线定义的类时距离函数族的局部等利普希茨连续性。本文旨在考察该性质是否对更一般的类时距离函数族（特别是沿柯西时间函数水平集定义者）仍然成立，从而探讨更广义分裂猜想的可能性。

Method: 通过分析类时距离函数（Lorentzian distance functions）沿柯西时间函数水平集的构造，作者证明了该族函数一般不具备局部等利普希茨连续性；并基于宇宙学与类时测地完备时空（timelike geodesically complete spacetimes）中柯西时间函数的存在性，提出了若干与巴特尼克分裂猜想等价的猜想。

Result: 沿完整类时线定义的类时距离函数族具有局部等利普希茨连续性，但该性质对沿柯西时间函数水平集定义的类时距离函数族一般不成立。

Conclusion: 上述性质的缺失表明，若要在更一般的语境下推广洛伦兹分裂定理，需引入额外的条件；作者提出的等价猜想为这一方向提供了理论框架。

Abstract: The families of Lorentzian distance functions to and from points along a complete timelike line in a spacetime are known to be locally equi-Lipschitz continuous in a neighborhood of the line. This is an essential component in the proof of the classical Lorentzian splitting theorems. We show that this property fails in general for families of Lorentzian distances to and from the level sets of a given Cauchy temporal function. Moreover, we formulate conjectures based on the existence of Cauchy temporal functions in cosmological and timelike geodesically complete spacetimes such that the Lorentz distances to its level sets are equi-Lipschitz, which are equivalent to Bartnik's splitting conjecture.

</details>


### [374] [Riemannian Positive Mass Theorem in All Dimensions in the Presence of Low-Codimension Singularities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23529)
*Marcus Khuri,Jian Wang,Jinmin Wang*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文证明了在任意维度下，具有次临界奇异集的渐近平坦$L^\infty$度量的黎曼正质量定理（Riemannian positive mass theorem），包括质量非负性以及仅当流形为欧氏空间时质量为零的刚性结论，是Schoen余维数三猜想在渐近平坦情形下的类比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在广义相对论与几何分析中，正质量定理是核心结论，但经典形式要求度量的高正则性。Schoen提出余维数三猜想（codimension-three conjecture）：标量曲率非负的度量允许的奇异集（singular set）至少应有余维数三。本文旨在将该猜想推广到渐近平坦情形，在允许更低正则性的度量下建立正质量定理。

Method: 证明方法整合了四个关键技术：(1) 奇异渐近平坦度量的密度定理（density theorem）；(2) 跨越奇异集（singular set）的容量估计（capacity estimates）；(3) 受Bi-Hao-He-Shi-Zhu [3]启发的共形爆破（conformal blow-up）；(4) 改编自Brendle-Wang [6]的$\mu$-泡泡（$\mu$-bubble）维数下降论证（dimension-descent argument）。

Result: 对于完整的光滑区域上标量曲率非负的渐近平坦流形，当奇异集的闵可夫斯基维数（Minkowski dimension）小于$n-3+\frac{2}{n}$时，每个渐近平坦末端的ADM质量（ADM mass）非负；当奇异集维数不大于$n-3+\frac{1}{n-1}$时，若某一末端质量为零，则该流形等距于欧氏空间。

Conclusion: 该结果建立了渐近平坦情形下Schoen余维数三猜想的模拟版本，将正质量定理扩展到了更广泛的低正则性背景，并为后续在奇异度规下研究标量曲率刚性提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We prove the Riemannian positive mass theorem in all dimensions for asymptotically flat $L^\infty$-metrics with subcritical singular sets. More precisely, we consider complete asymptotically flat manifolds whose metrics are smooth away from a compact singular set of Minkowski dimension less than $n-3+\frac{2}{n}$, and whose scalar curvature is nonnegative on the regular set. We show that the ADM mass of each asymptotically flat end is nonnegative, and that the mass vanishes in some end only in the Euclidean case. For the rigidity statement, we require additionally that the Minkowski dimension of the singular set is not larger than $n-3+\frac{1}{n-1}$. This gives an asymptotically flat analogue of Schoen's codimension-three conjecture for positive scalar curvature. The proof combines a density theorem for singular asymptotically flat metrics, capacity estimates across the singular set, conformal blow-up inspired by Bi-Hao-He-Shi-Zhu [3], and a $μ$-bubble dimension-descent argument adapted from Brendle-Wang [6].

</details>

### [375] [Quantum Enhancement of Particle-Size Segregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20921)
*Tomás Trewhela*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一种开放量子元胞自动机（open quantum cellular automaton），用于研究双分散颗粒混合物中的尺寸分离。研究发现，量子相干性（quantum coherence）可以增强分离程度，使其超越经典极限。稳态分离度可由两个无量纲数统一描述，分别控制分离、扩散与退相干之间的竞争。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 颗粒材料（granular materials）中，不同尺寸粒子会因分离与扩散混合之间的竞争而形成分离态。经典理论已能描述这一行为，但量子效应是否能在经典极限之外进一步增强分离，尚不明确。本文旨在探索量子相干性对颗粒尺寸分离的作用机制。

Method: 引入一个用于双分散混合物的开放量子元胞自动机（open quantum cellular automaton），将相干输运（coherent transport）与耗散分离（dissipative segregation）相结合。该自动机能够复现实验和连续介质理论中的分离动力学，且分离度符合理论上的Péclet数依赖关系。在弱退相干系统中，相干驱动输运可产生强于经典预测的稳态分离。

Result: 弱退相干（weakly decohering）系统表现出相干驱动的输运机制，其稳态分离程度显著高于经典理论预测。在广泛参数范围内，稳态分离度可由两个无量纲数统一描述，分别反映分离与扩散、以及分离与退相干之间的竞争关系。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，量子相干性可作为增强颗粒尺寸分离（particle-size segregation）的一种新机制。同时，该工作为研究开放多体系统（open many-body systems）中的输运现象建立了一个可推广的分析框架。

Abstract: Segregated states based on particle size emerge in granular materials from the competition between segregation and diffusive remixing. Here, we show that quantum coherence can enhance segregation beyond this classical limit. We introduce an open quantum cellular automaton for bidisperse mixtures that combines coherent transport and dissipative segregation. The automaton reproduces experimental and continuum-theory segregation dynamics, with segregation degrees collapsing onto a theoretical Péclet-dependent relationship. However, weakly decohering systems exhibit a coherence-driven transport regime that produces more strongly segregated steady states than classical predictions. Across a broad parameter range, the steady-state degree of segregation collapses onto two dimensionless numbers governing the competition between segregation, diffusion, and decoherence. These results identify quantum coherence as a mechanism for enhancing particle-size segregation and establish a framework for studying transport phenomena in open many-body systems.

</details>


### [376] [Many-body attractions do not stabilize gas-liquid phase separation in aqueous dispersions of charged colloids within the Poisson-Boltzmann framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21184)
*Thijs ter Rele,René van Roij,Marjolein Dijkstra*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究利用机器学习（machine learning, ML）构建带电胶体（charged colloids）的多体相互作用势（many-body interaction potentials），训练数据来自有限元泊松-玻尔兹曼（Poisson-Boltzmann）计算。结果发现：三体贡献（three-body contribution）为强吸引性，四体贡献（four-body contribution）为排斥性；纳入更高阶多体效应会削弱相互作用的凝聚性（cohesive nature）；通过ML势的分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）可观察到气-液或气-固相分离，但更大团簇训练集会进一步削弱凝聚性并消除宽泛相分离。原始模型（primitive model）模拟得到的平均力势（potential of mean force）与泊松-玻尔兹曼计算结果吻合，验证了后者的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往基于泊松-玻尔兹曼（Poisson-Boltzmann）计算的研究报道了同种电荷胶体（like-charged colloids）在低盐悬浮液中的吸引性三体相互作用，并将其视为驱动胶体团簇化（colloidal clustering）的机制。然而，这些计算通常忽略电荷调节（charge regulation）和高阶多体效应（higher-order many-body effects），因此需要更精确的模型来揭示多体相互作用的完整图景。

Method: 首先，基于有限元泊松-玻尔兹曼计算训练出机器学习多体相互作用势，用于电荷调节胶体（charge-regulating colloids）；随后分别在孤立三体、四面体四体以及13个和48个胶体团簇上计算多体贡献；最后利用原始模型模拟（primitive model simulations）计算胶体对和三体的平均力势（potential of mean force, PMF），并与泊松-玻尔兹曼结果进行对比验证。

Result: 三体贡献呈强吸引性（与以往研究一致），四体贡献（等边金字塔构型）为排斥性；基于13个胶体团簇训练的ML势捕获了削弱凝聚性的高阶效应并可观测到相分离；而加入48个胶体团簇后凝聚性进一步减弱，相分离消失；原始模型模拟的PMF与泊松-玻尔兹曼计算结果高度一致。

Conclusion: 泊松-玻尔兹曼方法可用于确定胶体多体相互作用势，但其预测的三体吸引力在考虑更高阶多体效应后会被显著削弱，甚至导致相分离消失。原始模型模拟结果也支持泊松-玻尔兹曼方法的有效性。

Abstract: Attractive three-body interactions have been reported for like-charged colloids in low-salt suspensions, based on both finite-element Poisson-Boltzmann calculations and direct experimental measurements, and have been proposed as a mechanism to drive colloidal clustering. However, these Poisson-Boltzmann calculations typically neglect charge regulation and higher-order many-body effects. Here, we construct machine-learned (ML) many-body interaction potentials for charge-regulating colloids, trained on finite-element Poisson-Boltzmann calculations, to accurately capture three-body and higher-order contributions. We find that the three-body contribution to the many-body potential as obtained from Poisson-Boltzmann calculations on isolated colloid triplets is strongly attractive, consistent with previous work, whereas the four-body contribution for an equilateral pyramid configuration of four colloids is repulsive. We then construct ML many-body potentials for charged colloids using finite-element Poisson-Boltzmann calculations on clusters of 13 colloids, and find that the incorporation of higher-body interactions weakens the cohesive nature of the interactions. We identify a parameter regime exhibiting gas-liquid or gas-solid phase separation using the ML potentials in molecular dynamics simulations. However, when we include clusters of 48 colloids in the training data, the cohesion diminishes further, and molecular dynamics simulations using these potentials no longer include broad phase separation in aqueous dispersions of charged colloids. Finally, we compute the potential of mean force of pairs and triplets of colloids using primitive model simulations. We find that the resulting potentials are in good agreement with those obtained from the Poisson-Boltzmann calculations, thereby supporting the validity of the Poisson-Boltzmann approach for determining many-body interactions.

### [377] [Thermo-responsive self-oscillating gel: mathematical model and theoretical analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21225)
*Yunjie Wang,Ling Yuan,Lin Ren,Zihao Liu,Qingyu Gao*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过一个最小双变量模型（minimal two-variable model）分析了内部加热的低临界溶解温度（LCST）热响应凝胶的自持振荡（self-sustained oscillations），发现大幅振荡主要由极限环的整体分岔（global bifurcations of limit cycles）控制，而非局部霍普夫分岔（local Hopf bifurcation）；振荡周期由冷却速率主导，振幅由溶胀平衡流形（swelling equilibrium manifold）的几何形状决定。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将凝胶溶胀动力学（gel swelling dynamics）与集总热平衡（lumped thermal balance）耦合，建立最小双变量模型，并采用快慢分析（fast-slow analysis）研究振荡行为。

Result: 稳定的大幅振荡主要受极限环的整体分岔控制；霍普夫分岔在研究的参数范围内是亚临界（subcritical）的，导致稳定不动点与稳定极限环共存的宽共存区域；振荡行为对不同加热门函数（heating-gate functions）具有鲁棒性；局域线性不稳定性（local linear instability）对自振荡既非必要也非充分；振荡周期由冷却速率主导，振幅由溶胀平衡流形的几何形状决定。

Conclusion: 阐明了热响应凝胶振荡的分岔机制，为控制其周期、振幅和波形提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Internally heated LCST thermo-responsive gels can show self-sustained swelling and collapse oscillations through feedback between temperature-induced collapse and collapse-suppressed heating. In this work, a minimal two-variable model is developed by coupling gel swelling dynamics with a lumped thermal balance. The analysis shows that stable large-amplitude oscillations are mainly controlled by global bifurcations of limit cycles, rather than by the local Hopf bifurcation. The Hopf bifurcation is subcritical in the studied parameter range, leading to a broad coexistence region where a stable fixed point and a stable limit cycle are both possible. The oscillatory behavior remains robust for different heating-gate functions, indicating that local linear instability is neither necessary nor sufficient for self-oscillation. Fast-slow analysis further shows that the oscillation period is mainly governed by the cooling rate, while the amplitude is determined by the geometry of the swelling equilibrium manifold. These results clarify the bifurcation mechanism of thermo-responsive gel oscillations and provide guidance for controlling their period, amplitude, and waveform.

### [378] [Exotic topological defects and director fields in free-floating spherical ferroelectric nematic liquid crystal shells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21231)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁电向列液晶具有极性对称性和大极化，展现出传统非极性向列相中不存在的现象。将铁电向列相约束在具有拓扑约束的几何结构（如球形壳层）中，可能揭示其独特的缺陷行为与物理机制，但目前相关研究尚不充分。

Method: 采用自由漂浮的球形壳层约束RM734+DIO液晶，施加切向边界条件（tangential boundary conditions）以强制产生总拓扑缺陷荷（topological defect charge）为+2的构型；在NF相、中间温度反铁电Nx相及高温N相下分别通过偏振光学显微镜和二次谐波产生（second-harmonic generation, SHG）显微术观测缺陷织构。

Result: 在NF相中，液晶形成围绕两个对跖+1弯曲-扭曲缺陷的方位角指向场（azimuthal director field），避免了非极性向列壳层中常见的半整数缺陷；SHG显微术确认了壳层在NF相中的非中心对称性（non-centrosymmetric nature）与方位角指向构型。中间温度的反铁电Nx相产生布满锯齿线的新奇异织构。高温N相则形成位于最薄点附近的四个+1/2向错。

Conclusion: 本研究凸显了球形壳层作为拓扑约束平台在研究奇异液晶行为中的丰富潜力，可能为高响应性铁电向列相的应用开辟新途径。

Abstract: Ferroelectric nematic (NF) liquid crystals exhibit polar symmetry and large polarization, giving rise to phenomena absent in conventional apolar nematics. We investigate NF liquid crystals confined to free-floating spherical shells with tangential boundary conditions, enforcing a total topological defect charge of +2. We conjecture that ferroelectric nematics avoid splayed configurations with half-integer defects, common in apolar nematic shells, instead concentrating the topological charge into escaped azimuthal +1 defects requiring only bend and twist. Indeed, at room temperature in the NF phase, our thin RM734+DIO shells with inner and outer aqueous poly(vinyl alcohol) solutions develop an azimuthal director field around two antipodal +1 bend-twist defects. The non-centrosymmetric nature and the azimuthal director configuration of the shells in the NF phase are confirmed also through second-harmonic generation microscopy. At intermediate temperature the antiferroelectric Nx phase generates a new exotic texture rife in zigzag lines in the shells. In the regular N phase at high temperature, the shells develop the usual four +1/2 disclinations located near the thinnest point. Our study highlights the rich platform offered by spherical shells to study the behavior of exotic liquid crystals subject to topological constraints, possibly opening new paths to apply the highly responsive ferroelectric nematic phase

### [380] [Nonlocal Sensing Drives Hybrid Phase Separation in Brownian Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21464)
*Benchang Wu,Ziluo Zhang,Shutong Guo,Hepeng Zhang,Zhihong You*

TL;DR: 本文通过感知布朗粒子（perceptive Brownian particles）的最小模型，证明非局部感知（nonlocal sensing）可作为非平衡物质（nonequilibrium matter）的一种组织原理，信息获取能够独立于力学相互作用主导相稳定性与有序涌现的动力学路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统认为物质组织依赖力学力，而该研究旨在探究信息获取（information acquisition）本身能否作为非平衡物质的一种基本组织原理，并为此建立最小模型。

Method: 采用纯布朗运动的感知粒子系统，粒子之间无力学相互作用、自驱动、排列或辅助场，仅通过由有限感知区内测量的密度调控的扩散率（diffusivity）实现信息耦合。

Result: 局部感知（local sensing）在失稳时产生常规长波长分相（demixing）；非局部感知（nonlocal perception）重构失稳谱，引入有限波长图案化（finite-wavelength patterning）及非线性气泡不稳定性（bubbling instabilities），并级联组装为混合相分离（hybrid phase separation）——宏观致密相与稀薄背景共存，同时内部保留由感知核（perception kernel）选择对称性、各向异性与长度尺度的有序微观结构。

Conclusion: 信息获取可作为非平衡物质的一个构成性原理（constitutive principle），同时主导相稳定性与有序涌现的动力学路径。

Abstract: Matter can organize not only through forces, but also through the information its constituents acquire from their surroundings. Here we use perceptive Brownian particles as a minimal model to isolate nonlocal sensing as an organizing principle for nonequilibrium matter. The particles undergo purely Brownian motion, with no mechanical interactions, self-propulsion, alignment, or auxiliary fields. Their only coupling is informational, through diffusivity regulated by density measured over a finite perception zone. Whereas local sensing, when unstable, produces conventional long-wavelength demixing, nonlocal perception restructures the instability spectrum, introducing finite-wavelength patterning and nonlinear bubbling instabilities. More fundamentally, it reshapes the ordering pathway by assembling a cascade of instabilities: macroscopic demixing creates dense domains, finite-wavelength modes pattern them internally, and nonlinear feedback hollows them into void bubbles. This produces hybrid phase separation, where a macroscopic dense phase coexists with a dilute background while retaining ordered internal microstructure, whose symmetry, anisotropy, and length scales are selected by the perception kernel. These results establish information acquisition as a constitutive principle of nonequilibrium matter, capable of governing both phase stability and the dynamical pathways through which order emerges.

### [381] [Defect Topology in Colloidal Smectics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21479)
*Chaya Halperin,Hillel Aharoni*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文针对胶体近晶相（colloidal smectics）中常见的90°取向晶界，发展了一套基于层（layer）的拓扑框架。该框架将正交晶界视为基态组成部分而非缺陷，通过将近晶相结构约化为层、半层和畴壁，对二维和三维中的点缺陷与线缺陷进行了拓扑分类，并揭示了向错荷（disclination charge）在二维中非唯一分类、在三维中非拓扑不变量的重要结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胶体近晶相中普遍存在层取向改变90°的晶界，但传统的缺陷理论将其视为例外结构。为了更自然地描述这类现象，需要建立一个新的拓扑框架，将正交晶界纳入基态描述。

Method: 扩展了适用于普通近晶相（ordinary smectics）的基于层的方法（layer-based approach），将近晶相结构约化为层（layers）、半层（half-layers）和畴壁（domain walls），并基于此结构对缺陷拓扑及其组合规则进行分类。在二维中，点缺陷用半有向圈图（semi-directed cycle graphs）描述；在三维中，线缺陷由横向图结构（transverse graph structure）分类。

Result: 在二维中，向错荷（disclination charge）虽是有效的拓扑不变量（topological invariant），但不能唯一分类缺陷，因为不同的半有向圈图可能具有相同的电荷。在三维中，点缺陷行为定性不同，其中刺猬向错荷（hedgehog disclination charge）不是拓扑不变量，而是会在层结构的平滑形变下连续变化。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，将正交晶界纳入基态而非视为缺陷，能够揭示近晶相中更丰富的拓扑结构。向错荷在二维和三维中的不同拓扑性质，对理解胶体近晶相的缺陷行为具有重要理论意义。

Abstract: Colloidal smectics -- layered structures formed in dense suspensions of rod-like particles -- often exhibit grain boundaries, across which the layer orientation changes by $90^{\circ}$. Motivated by this feature, we develop a layer-based topological framework that treats orthogonal grain boundaries as constituents of the ground state rather than as exceptional defect structures. Extending the layer-based approach for ordinary smectics, we reduce the smectic structure to layers, half-layers, and domain walls. We classify the topology of defects and their combination rules based on this structure. In two dimensions, point defects are described by semi-directed cycle graphs. Although the disclination charge remains a valid topological invariant, it does not uniquely classify defects, as distinct graphs may share the same charge. In three dimensions, line defects are classified by their transverse graph structure, while point defects exhibit qualitatively different behavior. In particular, we show that the hedgehog disclination charge is not a topological invariant, but instead varies continuously under smooth deformations of the layer structure.

### [382] [Perspective: Highly stable vapor-deposited glasses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21552)
*M. D. Ediger*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文综述了通过物理气相沉积（physical vapor deposition）制备高稳定性玻璃的最新进展，指出这类玻璃在密度、焓值及动力学稳定性（kinetic stability）方面均优于传统液冷玻璃，并探讨了其与理想玻璃（ideal glass）及深层过冷液体（deeply supercooled liquids）之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统液冷玻璃在性能上存在局限，难以接近理想玻璃的构型空间（configuration space）底部。通过物理气相沉积制备的玻璃展现出更优异的密度、焓值和动力学稳定性，为理解无定形态物质的热力学极限提供了新的可能性。

Method: 本文采用综述性方法，总结近年来关于物理气相沉积制备高稳定性玻璃的实验与理论进展，并分析其与液冷玻璃及深层过冷液体之间的结构、热力学和动力学关联。

Result: 对于给定的分子，气相沉积玻璃（vapor-deposited glasses）能够获得高于液冷玻璃的密度和更低的焓值，同时展现出显著增强的动力学稳定性（kinetic stability）。这些玻璃接近于势能景观（potential energy landscape）中无定形区域的底部，从而提供了接近理想玻璃性能的实验证据。

Conclusion: 稳定玻璃的形成在有机分子中具有普遍性，并有望推广至其他类型的材料。气相沉积玻璃的研究为深入理解玻璃转变（glass transition）及无定形态物质的热力学极限提供了重要视角，同时指出了未来可能的研究方向。

Abstract: This article describes recent progress in understanding highly stable glasses prepared by physical vapor deposition and provides perspective on further research directions for the field. For a given molecule, vapor-deposited glasses can have higher density and lower enthalpy than any glass that can be prepared by the more traditional route of cooling a liquid, and such glasses also exhibit greatly enhanced kinetic stability. Because vapor-deposited glasses can approach the bottom of the amorphous part of the potential energy landscape, they provide insights into the properties expected for the ideal glass. Connections between vapor-deposited glasses, liquid-cooled glasses, and deeply supercooled liquids are explored. The generality of stable glass formation for organic molecules is discussed along with the prospects for stable glasses of other types of materials.

</details>


### [383] [A Topology-Preserving Python Framework for Reliable Initialization of Star and Cyclic Polymer Architectures in Molecular Dynamics (LAMMPS) Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21719)
*Oluwatumininu Emmanuel Ayo-Ojo,Akpevweoghene Ogheneowho Ugono,Nkosinathi Dlamini*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 生成的聚合物结构在初始化时表现出机械稳定性，有效抑制了人为能量尖峰（artificial energy spikes），并在平衡过程中维持一致的热力学行为。与朴素随机放置方案（naive random placement schemes）的基准比较显示，重叠导致的失稳显著减少，结构和动力学可观测量的可再现性显著提升。

Conclusion: 该框架将初始化从随机预处理步骤重新定义为可控物理边界条件（controlled physical boundary condition），从而增强了聚合物分子动力学（MD）模拟的可靠性和可再现性。

Abstract: Accurate initialization of polymer architectures remains a critical yet underappreciated determinant of reliability in molecular dynamics simulations of soft matter systems. Errors in coordinate generation and connectivity assignment frequently introduce artificial stresses, topological inconsistencies, and numerical instabilities that propagate throughout simulation trajectories. Here, we present a topology-preserving Python framework for generating star and cyclic polymer architectures with deterministic bond connectivity, exact ring closure, excluded volume enforcement, and spatial-hashing-based overlap detection. The algorithm produces LAMMPS-compatible data files under atom style full without reliance on third-party libraries. We demonstrate that the generated structures exhibit mechanical stability at initialization, suppressed artificial energy spikes, and consistent thermodynamic behavior during equilibration. Benchmark comparisons against naive random placement schemes reveal significant reductions in overlap-induced instabilities and improved reproducibility of structural and dynamical observables. The presented framework establishes initialization as a controlled physical boundary condition rather than a stochastic preprocessing step, thereby enhancing the reliability and reproducibility of polymer molecular dynamics simulations.

### [384] [Saturation Coverage in Binary Mixtures of Oriented Regular Polygons via Random Sequential Adsorption](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21812)
*Aref Abbasi Moud*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文通过随机顺序吸附（RSA）方法系统研究了二维等面积正多边形二元混合物的饱和覆盖问题，发现中心对称性引发的奇偶效应显著影响堆积效率，并建立了排除面积（excluded area）与饱和覆盖率之间的负相关关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探究二维二元混合物中多边形的形状（而非大小）对随机堆积饱和覆盖率的影响，特别是形状对称性（奇偶性）在其中的作用机制。

Method: 采用基于分离轴定理（Separating Axis Theorem）的精确重叠检测的自适应分割体素（split-voxel）RSA算法，对边数 n ∈ {3,…,23} 的等面积正多边形进行二元混合体系的饱和构型生成与系统分析；排除面积通过闵可夫斯基和（Minkowski sum）解析计算。

Result: 三角形混合物覆盖率最低，轴对齐正方形达到最大观测值 φ_sat ≈ 0.5646；偶数边多边形持续优于相邻奇数边多边形，体现中心对称性（centrosymmetry）驱动的奇偶效应。奇数边纯物种的饱和覆盖率从下方趋近圆盘RSA极限（φ_disk ≈ 0.547），满足 φ_sat(n) = φ_disk - c/n^α，α ≈ 2.41±0.06，接近等周论证预期的 1/n^2 标度；偶数边多边形从上方趋近。排除面积与饱和覆盖率呈负相关。

Conclusion: 形状几何对称性（中心对称性）直接决定了随机堆积的饱和效率，偶数边多边形因中心对称固定排除面积 E_AA = 4A_0 而获得堆积优势，该优势仅在圆极限下消失；平均场RSA描述可以建立排除面积与堆积极限之间的直接联系。

Abstract: We study saturation in two-dimensional binary mixtures of fixed-orientation regular polygons deposited by random sequential adsorption (RSA). Polygons with (n\in{3,\dots,23}) are considered under an equal-area constraint, isolating shape effects from size effects. Saturated configurations are generated using an adaptive split-voxel RSA algorithm with exact overlap detection based on the Separating Axis Theorem, allowing a systematic exploration of all distinct binary shape combinations. Jamming coverage depends strongly on polygon geometry despite identical particle area. Triangle-containing mixtures yield the lowest coverages, whereas axis-aligned squares achieve the maximum observed value, (φ_{\rm sat}\approx0.5646). Even-sided polygons consistently outperform neighboring odd-sided polygons, revealing a parity effect associated with centrosymmetry. For odd (n), the pure-species saturation approaches the disk RSA limit (φ_{\rm disk}\approx0.547) from below according to (φ_{\rm sat}(n)=φ_{\rm disk}-c/n^α), with (α\approx2.41\pm0.06), close to the (1/n^2) scaling expected from isoperimetric arguments. Even-sided polygons instead converge from above, indicating a symmetry-driven packing advantage that disappears only in the circular limit. These trends are explained through the excluded area (E_{AB}=\mathrm{Area}(P_A\oplus(-P_B))), computed analytically via Minkowski sums. Centrosymmetry fixes (E_{AA}=4A_0) for even (n), whereas odd polygons have a larger excluded area that decreases monotonically toward the same limit as (n\to\infty). Saturation coverage is negatively correlated with excluded area, consistent with a mean-field RSA description and directly linking geometric symmetry to jamming efficiency.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在多种通道长度与宽度下，理论与实验在脉冲速度和形状上达成定量一致。窄通道中，一维分数阶波动方程无需拟合参数即可准确预测远端压力信号。宽通道中，二维描述使用单一公共拟合参数集即可解释所有几何效应。

Conclusion: 分数阶波动方程能够有效描述脂质单层中的压力脉冲传播，但由于azoPC光开关产生的脉冲振幅极小，方程中的非线性项在解释观测到的脉冲形状中不起作用。该框架为研究受限几何中生物膜力学响应提供了定量工具。

Abstract: We study pressure pulse generation and propagation in lipid monolayers by an experimental approach employing rapid photoisomerization of photoswitchable lipids (azoPC). This allows us to generate longitudinal surface pressure pulses by optical flash excitation in both free and constrained layer geometries. We compare the observed pulse shapes with a theoretical approach based on a nonlinear fractional wave equation for a surface displacement field, where a fractional time derivative term captures the hydrodynamics of the monolayer subphase. We explore channel geometries of different lengths and widths and find quantitative agreement between theory and experiment regarding pulse speed and pulse shapes. For narrow channels, we employ a one-dimensional version of the fractional wave equation to study pulse propagation without any fit parameters by using the pressure signal at a close pressure sensor as boundary condition to predict the pressure signal at a second far sensor. A full two-dimensional description can capture all effects arising from the channel geometry for wider channels using one common set of fit parameters for the pulse excitation that can be applied to all geometries. The nonlinearity in the fractional wave equation plays no role in explaining the observed pulse shapes because pulse amplitudes generated by azoPC photoswitching remain very small.

Abstract: Remembering here the work of two pioneers of the statistical physics of Coulomb systems, Günter Kelbg, and Ihor Yukhnovskii, we analyze their methods and give some new applications to ionic solutions and quantum plasmas. In particular, we develop applications of the theory to strong electrolytes and to thermal high-temperature plasmas at $T > 0^5$ K using the exponential interaction model. We show the strong structural similarity of these two classes of Coulomb systems, which physics is determined mostly by contributions proportional to $e^4$ and $e^6$. We predict at higher densities a structural transition to oscillating correlations. ### [388] [Quasi-two-dimensional dispersions of Brownian particles with competitive interactions: Dynamical clustering, non-Gaussianity and hydrodynamic correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22250)
*Zihan Tan,Vania Calandrini,Jan K. G. Dhont,Gerhard Nägele*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文基于朗之万动力学（Langevin dynamics, LD）和多粒子碰撞动力学（multiparticle collision dynamics, MPC），对具有竞争性短程吸引（short-range attractive, SA）和长程排斥（long-range repulsive, LR）相互作用的准二维（quasi-two-dimensional, Q2D）布朗粒子分散体系进行了全面的动力学分析，揭示了团簇化导致的亚扩散行为、非高斯动力学特征，以及流体动力学相互作用（hydrodynamic interactions, HIs）对集体动力学的关键影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准二维体系中具有竞争性短程吸引与长程排斥（SALR）相互作用的布朗粒子分散体系的动力学行为尚缺乏系统的理解，尤其是团簇化对扩散、非高斯涨落以及流体动力学相互作用（HIs）的影响机制有待阐明。

Method: 采用朗之万动力学（Langevin dynamics, LD）和多粒子碰撞动力学（multiparticle collision dynamics, MPC）两种模拟方法，对Q2D-SALR体系进行全面的动力学分析，考察吸引强度、粒子浓度等参数对动力学行为的影响。
