Conclusion: Q2D-SALR体系的动力学行为由吸引相互作用与流体动力学相互作用（HIs）共同主导；团簇化显著改变扩散特性、序参量弛豫与非高斯涨落行为；HIs在集体动力学中起关键作用，且其起始时间因团簇化而提前至惯性时间尺度。

Abstract: We conduct a comprehensive dynamical analysis of quasi-two-dimensional (Q2D) dispersions of Brownian particles with competing short-range attractive (SA) and long-range repulsive (LR) interactions using Langevin dynamics (LD) and multiparticle collision dynamics (MPC). As the attractive interaction is strengthened, self-diffusion is significantly suppressed, and clustering gives rise to pronounced subdiffusive behavior. We find that cluster lifetimes are influenced more strongly by attraction strength than by particle concentration. Two dynamical criteria for the transition from non-clustered to clustered phases are identified in terms of the mean cluster lifetime and the relaxation time of local hexagonal order, respectively. Moreover, clustered Q2D-SALR systems exhibit pronounced non-Gaussian dynamics. In particular, the self-van Hove function in the equilibrium-cluster phase displays an approximately exponential form, consistent with an underlying diffusing-diffusivity mechanism. Importantly, MPC simulations reveal the critical role of hydrodynamic interactions (HIs) in collective dynamics. We observe that the anomalously enhanced large-scale collective diffusion characteristic of hydrodynamically interacting Q2D systems is qualitatively preserved in Q2D-SALR dispersions. However, this enhancement suppresses the intermediate-range-order peak in the hydrodynamic function compared to its three-dimensional counterpart. Furthermore, by analyzing the time-dependent evolution of hydrodynamic function and the sound mode in hydrodynamic correlations, we find that clustering in Q2D-SALR systems leads to an earlier onset of HIs than in Q2D hard-sphere reference systems, implying HIs become relevant already on inertial timescales.

### [389] [Higher-Order Topological Phase Transitions in Continuous Hyperelastic Manifolds: From Surface Wrinkles to Zero-Energy Corner States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22710)
*Yu-Xin Xie*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过理论证明连续、均匀的超弹性体在多轴有限变形下会自然产生高阶拓扑相，将高阶拓扑现象从离散超材料推广至连续介质力学中，并提出了基于电活性介电弹性体的实验实现方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有高阶拓扑绝缘体（higher-order topological insulators, HOTIs）的实现完全依赖于离散设计的人工超材料（metamaterials）或周期性声子晶格（phononic lattices），尚未在连续、均匀的介质中发现此类现象。

Method: 将广义Stroh-Lie阻抗形式（Stroh-Lie impedance formalism）扩展至完全耦合的三维有限应变框架，将高度非线性的正交各向异性几何约束映射为Clifford Γ矩阵（Clifford Γ-matrices）张成的四带有效狄拉克哈密顿量，并进一步将静态分叉框架推广至弹性动力学体系。

Conclusion: 连续均质超弹性体在多轴有限变形下内禀地承载高阶拓扑相位，且三类拓扑态（表面褶皱、1D铰链态、0D角态）对应第一至第三阶拓扑相；基于电活性介电弹性体（electro-active dielectric elastomers）可动态编程零维拓扑奇异性，实现实验验证。

Abstract: Higher-order topological insulators (HOTIs) have revolutionized our understanding of wave localization, extending the bulk-boundary correspondence to lower-dimensional hinges and corners. Thus far, the realization of mechanical HOTIs has relied exclusively on discretely engineered metamaterials or periodic phononic lattices. Here, we report a fundamental paradigm shift by demonstrating that continuous, homogeneous hyperelastic manifolds undergoing finite multiaxial deformations naturally harbor intrinsic higher-order topological phases. By extending the generalized Stroh-Lie impedance formalism into a fully coupled 3D finite-strain framework, we map the highly nonlinear orthotropic geometric frustration onto a four-band effective Dirac Hamiltonian spanned by Clifford $Γ$-matrices. We reveal that macroscopic orthogonal stretches act precisely as competing Dirac mass terms, driving the continuous spatial transitions of topological domain walls and triggering a breakdown of $C_{4v}$ spatial symmetry. Remarkably, we analytically prove that beyond classical 2D surface wrinkling (1st-order topology), concurrent multiaxial extreme compression unconditionally triggers the emergence of 1D hinge states (2nd-order) and completely localized 0D zero-energy corner states (3rd-order). We further extend this static bifurcation framework into the elastodynamic regime, proving the existence of mid-gap localized vibrational modes. The theoretically derived topological phase diagram, nested Wilson loops, and fractional corner charges are comprehensively verified. Finally, we propose a concrete experimental realization using electro-active dielectric elastomers, enabling the dynamic programming of 0D topological singularities.

### [390] [Hierarchical Granular Metamaterials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22795)
*James Utama Surjadi,Bastien F. G. Aymon,Ayan Kumar,Lei Wu,Jet Lem,Ken N. Kamrin,Carlos M. Portela*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过引入层级粒状超材料（hierarchical granular metamaterials），在轻质架构化颗粒中设计空心椭圆夹杂、类晶体颗粒堆积以及功能性梯度与缺陷，实现了低密度下冲击能量吸收的提升与透射峰值力的降低，并展示了接触网络的可编程性可独立调控力学响应与输运特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统颗粒材料（granular materials）虽能高效耗散能量，但其无序致密的特性限制了在轻质系统中的精确控制与集成；而架构化材料（architected materials）虽可在低密度下实现可调力学响应，却因应力局部化而导致耗散效率不足。本文旨在调和这两种材料间的权衡，设计兼具低密度与高耗散能力的超材料。

Method: 本文通过三个层级的设计策略构建层级粒状超材料：轻质架构化颗粒（含空心椭圆夹杂）、类晶体颗粒堆积（crystal-inspired grain packings），以及颗粒拼接中的功能梯度与缺陷。采用原位纳米力学实验（in situ nanomechanical experiments）和非线性计算模型（nonlinear computational models）揭示耗散机制，并通过多尺度冲击实验验证其跨尺度、跨材料与跨维度的普适性。

Result: 层级粒状超材料在低密度下同时实现了单位质量冲击能量吸收的提升与透射峰值力的降低，性能优于传统架构化材料。增强的横向颗粒膨胀（lateral grain expansion）驱动邻近颗粒的招募，放大了塑性耗散与摩擦耗散。多尺度实验证实该机制具有跨尺度、跨材料与跨维度的可迁移性。此外，空间可编程的颗粒间接触网络实现了变形的确定性路由，并可独立于堆积几何调控电输运路径。

Conclusion: 本文通过将颗粒材料原理与架构化材料设计相结合，建立了一种多功能力学超材料的新范式，其接触拓扑（contact topology）、力学响应（mechanical response）与输运特性（transport properties）可被独立编程，为多功能超材料的可编程设计提供了理论依据与实验验证。

Abstract: Granular materials dissipate energy efficiently through intergranular interactions, yet their disordered, dense nature precludes precise control and integration into lightweight systems. Architected materials offer tunable mechanical responses at low densities but tend to localize stress, limiting dissipation efficiency. Here, we introduce hierarchical granular metamaterials that reconcile these trade-offs through three levels of design: lightweight architected grains engineered with hollow elliptical inclusions, crystal-inspired grain packings, and functional gradients and defects within grain tessellations. These metamaterials exhibit simultaneous increases in impact energy absorption per unit mass and reductions in transmitted peak force at low densities, outperforming conventional architected materials. In situ nanomechanical experiments and nonlinear computational models reveal that enhanced lateral grain expansion drives recruitment of neighboring grains, amplifying plastic and frictional dissipation. Multiscale impact experiments confirm that these mechanisms persist across length scales, constituent materials, and dimensionalities. Beyond mechanical performance, we demonstrate that spatially programmable inter-grain contact networks enable deterministic routing of deformation, which extends to electrical transport pathways independently of packing geometry. By combining granular principles with architected material design, this work establishes a paradigm for multifunctional metamaterials whose contact topology, mechanical response, and transport properties can be programmed independently.

</details>


### [391] [Hydrodynamic Phase Separation and Morphological Evolution in Chiral Active-Passive Mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22903)
*Mayurakshi Deb,Rajesh Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文通过Ewald求和计算多体流体动力学相互作用，系统研究了手性活性物质（chiral active matter）中活性旋转粒子（active spinners）与被动胶体（passive colloids）混合体系的涌现动力学，发现了独特的相分离形态，包括被动粒子涡旋和大尺度活性-被动条带，并揭示了长程流体动力学耦合在非平衡凝聚态自组织中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 被动粒子在活性手性物质中的集体行为是软物质研究的重要方向，但现有研究多聚焦于外部扭矩施加手性而非内在活动性导致的系统，缺乏对内在活性手性系统中被动组分行为与长程流体动力学耦合的系统理解。

Method: 采用Ewald求和（Ewald summation）方法计算多体流体动力学相互作用（many-body hydrodynamic interactions），系统扫描了面积分数（area fractions）和旋转速度（rotational velocities）等运动学参数（kinematic parameters）的广泛范围，并通过分析特征长度尺度（characteristic length scales）的时间演化和被动粒子的非平衡速度分布（non-equilibrium velocity distributions）来表征底层动力学。

Result: 识别出对系统运动学参数敏感的不同相分离（phase-separation）区域；发现了独特的结构形态，包括相分离活性旋转粒子周围形成的被动粒子涡旋（passive particle vortices），以及大尺度活性-被动条带（active-passive bands）的发展。

Conclusion: 长程流体动力学耦合（long-range hydrodynamic couplings）在控制非平衡凝聚态（non-equilibrium condensed matter）的自组织（self-organization）中发挥关键作用，该研究为理解这一机制提供了新的视角。

Abstract: The collective behavior of passive particles within chiral active matter has emerged as a significant area of soft matter research. However, most existing studies focus on systems where chirality is imposed by external torques rather than intrinsic activity. In this work, we study emergent dynamics in a suspension of active spinners and passive colloids by computing many-body hydrodynamic interactions via Ewald summation. By systematically exploring a broad range of area fractions and rotational velocities, we identify distinct phase-separation regimes sensitive to the system's kinematic parameters. Specifically, we report the emergence of unique structural morphologies, including the formation of passive particle vortices surrounding phase-separated active spinners and the development of large-scale active-passive bands. We characterize the underlying dynamics by analyzing the temporal evolution of characteristic length scales and the non-equilibrium velocity distributions of the passive particles. Our findings provide new insights into the role of long-range hydrodynamic couplings in governing the self-organization of non-equilibrium condensed matter.

</details>


### [392] [Coupling Heterarchical Granular Dynamics and Computational Fluid Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23202)
*Jiahuan Li,Shivakumar Athani,Alistair Gillespie,Matthew J Cleary,Itai Einav,Benjy Marks*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种异质性颗粒-流体动力学（HGFD）框架，通过将异质性颗粒动力学（HGD）与基于流体质量分数的不可压Navier-Stokes求解器双向耦合，实现了对流体环境中颗粒流粒径分离行为的高效模拟。该框架在三种实验场景下得到验证，证明了其在模拟流体耦合颗粒分离动力学方面的有效性和一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型难以高效捕捉环境流体中颗粒流（granular flows）的粒径依赖性分离（grain-size-dependent segregation），尤其是在涉及百万颗以上颗粒的大规模系统中。

Method: 开发了一个双向耦合框架，将异质性颗粒动力学（heterarchical granular dynamics, HGD）与基于流体质量分数的不可压Navier-Stokes求解器（fluid-fraction-weighted incompressible Navier-Stokes solver）相结合。该HGFD模型在先前准静态变形HGD模型的基础上，引入了惯性力平衡驱动的颗粒速度（inertial, force-balance-driven particle velocities）以及一致的流固动量交换。耦合采用交错显式顺序方案（staggered explicit sequential scheme）和共位欧拉场（co-located Eulerian fields）实现。

Result: 通过三种实验场景验证了框架性能：(i) 单颗粒沉降（single-particle settling）验证惯性松弛；(ii) 受阻沉降（hindered settling）再现浓度依赖性沉降和垂向粒径分层；(iii) 三种已报道的分离类型案例评估了流态敏感性。结果表明HGFD是一种高效且一致的模拟方法。

Conclusion: HGFD建立了一种高效且一致的方法，用于模拟流体耦合的颗粒分离动力学（fluid-coupled granular segregation dynamics），为大规模系统下的粒径分离研究提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Granular flows in ambient fluids exhibit grain-size-dependent segregation, which is difficult to capture efficiently with existing models, especially in large-scale systems involving more than a million grains. We develop a two-way coupled framework that integrates heterarchical granular dynamics (HGD) with a fluid-fraction-weighted incompressible Navier-Stokes solver. This heterarchical granular-fluid dynamics (HGFD) model extends a previous HGD model for quasi-static deformations by introducing inertial, force-balance-driven particle velocities and consistent fluid-solid momentum exchange. The coupling between the inertial HGD and the fluid solver is performed using a staggered explicit sequential scheme and co-located Eulerian fields. The framework is evaluated against experimental data of (i) single-particle settling to verify inertial relaxation, (ii) hindered settling to reproduce concentration-dependent settling and vertical size stratification, and (iii) representative cases covering three reported segregation types to assess regime sensitivity. These results establish HGFD as an efficient and consistent approach for simulating fluid-coupled granular segregation dynamics.

</details>


### [393] [Dissociation of NaCl in supercritical aqueous fluids of moderate and high concentrations: A molecular dynamics study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23349)
*Mikhail V. Ivanov,Olga V. Alexandrovich*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过经典分子动力学模拟，系统考察了超临界水-盐（H₂O-NaCl）体系中NaCl在不同浓度（从中等盐度到高浓度）、温度（673.15–1273.15 K）和压力（0.1–2 GPa）下的缔合与解离行为，发现解离度随盐浓度升高呈非单调变化，结构解离离子的摩尔分数在x_NaCl ≈ 0.06–0.10达到峰值；高盐度下以接触离子对（contact pairs）和多离子簇为主。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解超临界水热流体中NaCl的缔合/解离行为对于热力学模型和高温度下氯离子可利用性的评价至关重要，然而目前对广泛浓度范围内解离度的分子尺度约束仍十分缺乏。

Method: 采用经典分子动力学（classical molecular dynamics）模拟，在673.15–1273.15 K、0.1–2 GPa条件下，针对从中等盐度到高浓度的H₂O-NaCl混合物计算了解离度α及对应的理想解离常数K_d；此外还开展了固定密度（1和7 mol/kg）的补充模拟，将温度上限扩展至1673.15 K。

Result: 在中等盐度（约1 mol/kg）下，NaCl解离度α = 0.3–0.7；当NaCl摩尔分数升至0.333（27.8 mol/kg）时，α趋近于零，体系中以Na⁺Cl⁻接触离子对（contact pairs）和多离子簇（multi-ion clusters）为主。结构解离的Na⁺与Cl⁻摩尔分数随盐浓度呈现非单调变化，峰值出现在x_NaCl ≈ 0.06–0.10。

Conclusion: 增加盐度并不必然增加超临界水热流体中结构可用的氯离子丰度；所得浓度依赖性结果为浓缩超临界电解质的热力学描述及高温水热流体中氯离子可利用性的评估提供了分子层面的约束。

Abstract: We report classical molecular dynamics simulations of NaCl association and dissociation in supercritical aqueous fluids over a wide range of salt concentrations, from moderate salinity to highly concentrated H2O-NaCl mixtures attainable at high temperatures. The degree of dissociation a and the corresponding ideal dissociation constant Kd, derived directly from a, were calculated as functions of the stoichiometric NaCl mole fraction at selected pressure-temperature (PT) conditions from 673.15 to 1273.15 K and from 0.1 to 2 GPa. At moderate salinity corresponding to a molality of approximately 1 mol/kg, NaCl remains largely dissociated a = 0.3-0.7 depending on pressure and temperature). In contrast, when the mole fraction of NaCl increases up to xNaCl = 0.333 (27.8 mol/kg), the degree of dissociation tends towards zero, and most ions form Na$^+$Cl$^-$ contact pairs and multi-ion clusters. As a result of these competing trends, the mole fraction of structurally dissociated Na$^+$ and Cl$^-$ ions is a non-monotonic function of the stoichiometric NaCl concentration and typically reaches a maximum at xNaCl = 0.06-0.10. This result shows that increasing salinity does not necessarily increase the abundance of structurally available chloride ions in supercritical aqueous fluids. Additional fixed density simulations at 1 and 7 mol/kg extend the analysis up to 1673.15 K and separate the effects of temperature and density on the associate/dissociate state of the ions. The obtained concentration dependences provide molecular-level constraints for thermodynamic descriptions of concentrated supercritical electrolytes and for evaluating chloride availability in high-temperature aqueous fluids.

</details>


### [394] [Application of Machine Learning for the Identification of 2D Colloidal Assemblies: A Case Study on Particles of Distinct Shapes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23639)
*L. T. Khusainova,S. A. Kolegova,K. S. Kolegov*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文利用YOLO模型对由不同形状粒子（球体、椭球体、长方体、杆状）构成的胶体单层装配（colloidal monolayer assemblies）进行分类识别（孤立粒子、二聚体、链、团簇、环），并使用合成数据集训练模型。在人工图像上识别近乎完美，但在实验图像上平均误差达43.1%，误差随粒子几何形状变化显著（球体20%至长方体58.5%），表明算法对目标几何形状具有选择性敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现对不同形状粒子构成的胶体单层装配（如球体、椭球体、长方体、杆状粒子）的结构分类识别，替代传统人工分析方法。

Method: 采用YOLO模型作为识别方法，针对四种粒子形状分别制备合成数据集（synthetic datasets）训练模型，并将训练后的模型应用于实验图像进行验证与误差分析。

Result: 在人工图像上识别近乎完美；在实验图像上平均误差为43.1%，其中球体误差最低（20%），长方体误差最高（58.5%），显示出算法对目标几何形状的选择性敏感性（selective sensitivity）。

Conclusion: 现有基于合成数据训练的模型在实验图像上表现不足，需进一步构建基于实验图像的训练数据集（datasets based on experimental images）以提升预测效果。

Abstract: This work addresses the problem of identifying colloidal monolayer assemblies using particles of various shapes (two-dimensional coatings): spheres, ellipsoids, cuboids, and rods. The following classification of assemblies is considered: isolated particles, dimers, chains, clusters, and loops. The YOLO model was chosen as the identification method. Synthetic datasets were prepared for each of the four particle shapes to train the models. The paper discusses the application of models trained on synthetic data to experimental images. An analysis was carried out on the feasibility of using such models for recognizing configurations in real images. While recognition on artificial images is nearly perfect, tests on experimental images showed a significant deviation. The average error across all particle types was 43.1%, but a considerable spread in values is observed: from 20% for spheres to 58.5% for cuboids, indicating the algorithm's selective sensitivity to object geometry. The created datasets and trained models are freely available for use. The corresponding modules have been integrated into the previously developed information system (https://isanm.space/). To further improve prediction results, it is necessary to prepare datasets based on experimental images.

</details>

### [395] [Deep-Ocean Application-Specific Neutrino Experiment: a white paper](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20780)
*Takumi Araki,Simran Chauhan,Lyla Choi,Brian C. Crow,Max A. A. Dornfest,John Graham,Misaki Hosoya,John G. Learned,Viacheslav A. Li,William F. McDonough,Takeru Ohno,Takanobu Ono,Taichi Sakai,Jackson Seligman,Nathan Sibert,Shang-Wen Stradleigh,David Vartanyan,Hiroko Watanabe,Zhihao Xu,Jeffrey G. Yepez*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一种用于探测地幔铀钍衰变链产生的地质中微子（geoneutrino）的深海移动实验装置的概念、原型设计、预期成本及科学目标。该装置可将地壳背景噪声降低50-100倍，其独特移动性支持空间热源分布映射，并为地球内部结构的多模态数据采集提供跨学科平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有及已计划的实验均无法直接测量来自地幔的地质中微子，限制了对地球放射性生成热（radiogenic heat production）和地球化学组成（geochemical makeup）的约束。需要一种新型探测方案以显著降低地壳背景噪声，实现对地幔中微子的直接观测。

Method: 提出一种深海移动中微子实验装置设计，利用深海环境实现相对于同等规模陆基探测器50-100倍的地壳背景抑制；通过探测器的可移动性（mobility）获取多个立体投影（stereoscopic projections），从而映射地幔中产热元素的空间分布。

Result: 该设计在同等规模下可降低地壳背景噪声50-100倍，支持直接测量来自地幔的地质中微子。研究团队已在主动原型验证（active prototyping）中获得最新的硬件开发进展。

Conclusion: 该深海移动中微子实验设计具有独特性和跨学科性（multidisplinary），能够服务于物理学与地球科学对地球内部组成和结构的多模态数据（multi-modal data）获取目标，并且具备多用途（multiuse）潜力。

Abstract: This white paper introduces the concept, prototype design, projected costs, and scientific goals of a mobile experiment for detecting geoneutrinos originating from uranium and thorium decay chains in the Earth's mantle. This will constrain the planet's radiogenic heat production and unearth its geochemical makeup. This design of a deep-ocean mobile neutrino experiment, which is not mirrored by any active or planned experiments, supports physics and geoscience's goal of multi-modal data on the Earth's internal composition and structure. Based on geoscientific studies, this design is expected to achieve a 50--100-fold reduction in crustal background compared to similarly sized continental detectors, thereby enabling direct measurements of mantle geoneutrinos. The multiple stereoscopic projections enabled by the detector's unique mobility can map spatial variations in heat-producing elements within the mantle. Beyond discussing the design, we report on our collaboration's most recent hardware developments in the active prototyping of this detector. We briefly highlight the potential multiuse and interdisciplinary nature of this detector.

</details>


### [396] [Multi-scale reconstruction of single-ion damage tracks in diamond via nitrogen-vacancy centers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23621)
*Daniel G. Ang,Jiashen Tang,Maximilian Shen,Michael Titze,Gavishta Liyanage,Jordan Chapman,Chinmay Bharathulwar,Andrew T. Gilpin,Tanguy Terlier,Edward S. Bielejec,Vsevolod Ivanov,Ronald L. Walsworth*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本论文通过氮-空位（NV）中心平台，结合实验与模拟框架，研究了亚MeV碳离子在金刚石中产生的粒子损伤径迹（particle-induced damage tracks），展示了其在稀有事件方向探测和量子缺陷工程中的应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解固体材料中的粒子诱导损伤径迹（particle-induced damage tracks）是稀有事件探测和量子缺陷工程等新兴应用的基础，但多尺度径迹解析（从毫米级事件定位到纳米级形貌重建）仍面临挑战。本文旨在利用金刚石中的氮-空位（NV）中心平台，实现从事件定位到径迹形貌重建的多尺度读出。

Method: 将亚MeV碳离子注入富氮金刚石，通过空间局域化的NV中心形成探测单个反冲事件。开发了一个模拟框架来解释观察到的NV产额，并预测退火后NV分布中保留有方向信息。进一步利用机器学习恢复因缺陷扩散和有限NV产额而损失的信息。

Result: 模拟框架成功解释了观察到的NV产额，并预测退火后NV分布保留方向性信息。机器学习将头尾分类（head-tail classification）性能提升至接近退火前空位径迹的水平。NV自旋相干性测量结果表明，该平台与基于NV应变映射和磁梯度技术的纳米尺度径迹重建兼容。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了NV-金刚石方向探测器在稀有事件探测中的可行路径，同时所建立的径迹建模框架对古探测（paleodetection）和量子材料合成具有更广泛的启示意义。

Abstract: Understanding particle-induced damage tracks in solid-state materials underpins emerging applications in rare-event detection and quantum defect engineering. Resolving these tracks requires multi-scale readout, from event localization at the millimeter scale to track-morphology reconstruction at the nanoscale. Nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers in diamond provide such a platform, combining optical localization with quantum sensing of track morphology. Here, we implant sub-MeV carbon ions into nitrogen-rich diamond and detect individual recoil events via spatially localized NV formation. We develop a simulation framework that explains the observed NV yield and predicts that directional information is retained in the NV distribution after annealing. Machine learning further recovers much of the information lost to defect diffusion and limited NV yield, improving head-tail classification to a level comparable to pre-annealed vacancy tracks. Measurements of NV spin coherence indicate compatibility with nanoscale track reconstruction via NV strain mapping and magnetic gradient-based techniques. These results identify promising pathways toward NV-diamond directional detectors for rare events, while the track-modeling framework has broader implications for paleodetection and quantum material synthesis.

### [397] [Quantum-Geometry-Induced Superconductivity near a Fractional Chern Insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21166)
*Haoyu Hu,Lei Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文利用耦合导线构造（coupled-wire construction）和玻色化（bosonization）方法，解析研究了部分填充陈带（Chern band）中的竞争性关联驱动相。研究表明，分数量子陈绝缘体（FCI）和反分数量子陈绝缘体（aFCI）通道之间的相互作用会产生有效耦合，驱动FCI相附近的超导不稳定性，且该机制同样可能导致电荷密度波（charge-density-wave）相。量子几何（quantum geometry）增强了超导转变温度，并成为调控FCI、aFCI与超导关联之间相互作用的组织原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 莫尔实验和数值研究已在拓扑系统中发现了分数量子陈绝缘体、电荷密度波序和超导等关联驱动相，但这些相如何竞争或交织、量子几何如何塑造它们之间的相互作用仍尚未解决。

Method: 采用耦合导线构造（coupled-wire construction）和玻色化（bosonization）方法对部分填充陈带中的竞争性关联驱动相进行解析研究；通过微扰重整化群（perturbative renormalization-group）分析获取相图。

Result: FCI与aFCI散射通道共存时，两者的相互作用产生有效耦合，在FCI相附近驱动超导不稳定性；相同机制在微观参数变化下也可导致电荷密度波相；量子几何（quantum geometry）增强了超导转变温度。

Conclusion: 量子几何（quantum geometry）是调控FCI、aFCI与超导关联之间相互作用的组织原则（organizing principle）。

Abstract: Recent moiré experiments and numerical studies of interacting Chern bands have revealed fractional Chern insulators, charge-density-wave order, and superconductivity as proximate correlation-driven phases in topological systems. How these phases compete or intertwine, and how quantum geometry shapes their interplay, remain open questions. Here we present an analytic study of competing correlation-driven phases in a partially filled Chern band using a coupled-wire construction and bosonization. The key ingredient is the coexistence of interaction channels that favor, respectively, a fractional Chern insulator (FCI) and a closely related anti-FCI (aFCI) state. The aFCI channel is specific to lattice Chern bands and is enhanced by the quantum geometry of the underlying band structure. We show that when both FCI and aFCI scattering channels are present, their interplay generates an effective coupling that drives a superconducting instability near the FCI phase. The same mechanism can also favor a charge-density-wave phase, depending on microscopic parameters. Using a perturbative renormalization-group analysis, we obtain the phase diagram and identify a superconducting regime adjacent to the FCI phase. We further estimate the superconducting transition temperature and show that it is enhanced by quantum geometry. Our results establish quantum geometry as an organizing principle for the interplay among FCI, aFCI, and superconducting correlations.

### [398] [Nontrivial Boundary-Mediated Superconducting Transport in a TRSB Topological Iron-Based Superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21507)
*Wenyao Liu,Gabriel Natale,Camron Farhang,Michael Geiwitz,Qishuo Tan,Xingyao Guo,Mason Gray,Vincent LambertiJazzmin Victorin,Huairuo Zhang,James L.   <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 极化克尔测量显示TRSB在TKerr（低于Tc）处出现，并在多个组分下与超导共存。在FeTe0.55Se0.45中观测到反常电导平台，该平台要求源漏之间具有连续锐利边缘，在远超体相干长度（coherence length）的微米尺度距离上依然存在，热展宽受到强烈抑制，当漏极移至顶面时平台消失。该平台的温度演化遵循TRSB能标：在T*Kerr以下保持弱展宽，并在TKerr附近而非Tc附近消失。

Conclusion: 这些掺杂选择性、边缘几何依赖性、TRSB关联性以及长程非局域信号建立了在FeTe0.55Se0.45中识别边界介导超导输运的实验判据，并为理解其微观起源的相敏感研究和理论研究提供了动机。

Abstract: The interplay of superconductivity, band topology, and spontaneous time-reversal-symmetry breaking (TRSB) is expected to enable topological superconducting boundary states. FeTe0.55Se0.45 provides a promising single-material platform because it combines superconductivity, nontrivial band topology, and spontaneous magnetization in the superconducting state. Here we report evidence for a boundary-mediated superconducting transport response in exfoliated Fe(Te,Se) devices. Polar Kerr measurements show that TRSB emerges below TKerr < Tc and coexists with superconductivity across multiple compositions, providing an independent symmetry-breaking scale for transport. Using crystallographically sharp, continuous edges and side-surface-dominant contacts, we find that topological FeTe0.55Se0.45 exhibits an anomalous conductance plateau absent in topologically trivial FeTe0.40Se0.60 and Fe1.02Te0.55Se0.45 under comparable measurements. This plateau requires uninterrupted sharp edges connecting source and drain, persists over micrometer-scale separations far exceeding the bulk coherence length, shows strongly suppressed thermal broadening, and collapses when the drain is moved to the top surface. Its temperature evolution follows the TRSB scale: the plateau remains weakly broadened below T*Kerr and disappears near TKerr rather than Tc. These doping-selective, edge-geometry-dependent, TRSB-correlated, and long-range nonlocal signatures establish experimental criteria for identifying boundary-mediated superconducting transport in FeTe0.55Se0.45 and motivate phase-sensitive and theoretical studies of its microscopic origin.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用扩展t-J模型在Kagome晶格上研究超导电性，通过分析布洛赫波函数的对称性约束亚晶格结构以及不同范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularity, vHS）类型（p型、m型、m'型）附近的配对行为。

Conclusion: 被先前忽略的m'型vHS是一条植根于电子关联和镜面对称约束布洛赫波函数的非常规超导电性新路径。

Abstract: The pair-density wave (PDW) state, characterized by Cooper pairing at finite momentum, is a long-sought superconducting phase whose possible realization in Kagome metals is particularly intriguing in the strongly correlated regime. We investigate superconductivity in the extended $t$-$J$ model on the Kagome lattice and show that the symmetry-enforced sublattice structure of the Bloch wavefunctions gives rise to a rich landscape of unconventional pairing states. When the chemical potential is tuned to a sublattice-pure ($p$-type) van Hove singularity (vHS), a PDW state inevitably emerges. Near the $m'$-type vHS, which features opposite mirror eigenvalues to the conventional $m$-type vHS, intraband chiral, uniform, and nematic pairing states compete. When further-neighbor hoppings drive the $p$- and $m'$-type vHSs towards near degeneracy, phase frustration in the interband pairing channel stabilizes a chiral interband state. Our results reveal the previously overlooked $m'$-type vHS as a distinct route to unconventional superconductivity rooted in electronic correlations and mirror-symmetry-constrained Bloch wavefunctions.

### [400] [Non-BCS Pairing by a Singular Dynamical Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21731)
*Artem G. Abanov,Andrey V. Chubukov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文综述了具有奇异动力学电子-电子相互作用的系统中的超导理论，通过与常规BCS超导的对比，揭示了奇异相互作用如何破坏传统能标分离和Cooper对数机制，并基于γ-模型分析了配对与非费米液体行为的竞争，展示了超导仍可发生但其起源本质上不同于BCS理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统BCS超导框架依赖于能标分离和Cooper对数机制，但在奇异动力学相互作用（如量子临界点附近、量子点及局域化转变体系）下这些前提不再成立，因此亟需发展新的理论框架来理解此类系统中的超导现象。

Method: 采用具有奇异动力学相互作用的通用γ-模型，其中相互作用形式为Γ(Ω) ∝ 1/|Ω|^γ，通过分析零温下的能隙方程（gap equation），研究配对倾向与非费米液体行为（non-Fermi liquid behavior）之间的竞争与相互影响。

Result: 发现当配对相互作用超过某一阈值时超导仍可形成，但其配对机制与BCS理论有本质不同；零温能隙方程具有无限多拓扑不等价解（topologically distinct solutions），且当相互作用变得非奇异（有质量，massive）时这些解逐一消失。

Conclusion: 奇异动力学相互作用导致传统BCS框架失效，但超导仍能通过一种质不同的机制出现；这些发现揭示了奇异相互作用下超导的丰富物理内涵，并为未来的理论探索提供了方向。

Abstract: This review examines the theory of superconductivity in systems with {\em singular dynamical} electron-electron interaction and contrasts it with a conventional BCS superconductivity. Examples include metals near a Quantum Critical Point, quantum dots and system near a localization (Mott) transition. We show, that the singular interaction destroys the traditional separation of energy scales, invalidating the significance of Cooper logarithm, and, as the consequence, the whole BCS framework. We explore the universal model with dynamical interaction $Γ(Ω) \propto 1/|Ω|^γ$ (the $γ$-model) and analyze the competition/interplay between the tendency towards pairing and towards non-Fermi liquid behavior. We show that superconductivity still develops once the pairing interaction exceeds a certain threshold, but the origin of the pairing is qualitatively different from that in BCS theory. We show that the gap equation at $T=0$ has an infinite set of topologically distinct solutions. These solution disappear one by one once the pairing interaction becomes non-singular (massive). We review the physics underlying these phenomena and outline future directions.

### [401] [Structural symmetry effects on the competition of density waves and superconductivity in bilayer nickelates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23022)
*Steffen Bötzel,Aiman Al-Eryani,Jun Zhan,Xianxin Wu,Frank Lechermann,Michael M. Scherer,Ilya M. Eremin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示双层镍氧化物La₃Ni₂O₇中自旋密度波（spin-density-wave, SDW）序与超导电性之间的竞争机制，尤其是高压下超导态出现的物理起源。

Method: 采用功能重整化群（functional renormalization group, fRG）方法，对常压和高压晶体结构下的多轨道弱耦合模型进行分析。

Result: 随着Hund耦合增大，体系主导不稳定性从超导转变为SDW序（序矢量为Q₁≈(π/2,π/2)或正交Amam晶胞下的Q_Y≈(0,π)），与实验一致；常压与高压结构在非相互作用磁化率及主导fRG不稳定性上几乎相同；抑制正交性（orthorhombicity）是超导出现的关键，接近四方极限时，与对称性相关的SDW涨落近乎简并，抑制长程磁序并增强配对相互作用。

Conclusion: 晶格对称性（lattice symmetry）是调控双层镍氧化物中竞争有序态的核心参数，通过单轴应变（uniaxial strain）降低正交性，可在常压下稳定体超导态。

Abstract: We investigate the interplay between spin-density-wave (SDW) order and superconductivity in the bilayer nickelate La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ using the functional renormalization group~(fRG) applied to multiorbital weak-coupling models of both the ambient- and high-pressure crystal structures. As Hund's coupling increases, the leading instability evolves from superconductivity to an SDW state with ordering vector $\mathbf{Q}_1 \approx (π/2,π/2)$ (equivalently $\mathbf{Q}_Y \approx (0,π)$ in the orthorhombic $Amam$ unit cell), in agreement with experimental observations. Surprisingly, the ambient- and high-pressure structures exhibit nearly identical non-interacting susceptibilities and leading fRG instabilities, indicating that the emergence of superconductivity under pressure cannot be explained solely by changes in the low-energy electronic structure. Instead, our results identify the suppression of orthorhombicity as a key ingredient for superconductivity. As the system approaches the tetragonal limit, symmetry-related SDW fluctuations become nearly degenerate, frustrating long-range magnetic order while enhancing pairing interactions. These findings highlight lattice symmetry as a central tuning parameter of the competing ordered states in bilayer nickelates and suggest that reducing orthorhombicity through uniaxial strain could stabilize bulk superconductivity already at ambient pressure.

Conclusion: 上述特征若被实验观测到，将为激子超流提供直接证据，并确立激子双层（exciton bilayers）作为中性约瑟夫森器件（neutral Josephson devices）的平台。

Abstract: Obtaining definitive evidence for zero-magnetic-field exciton superfluidity in electron-hole bilayers remains a longstanding challenge because the condensate is electrically neutral and its phase coherence is difficult to probe directly. We propose a direct test based on Shapiro steps in a Dayem-bridge excitonic Josephson junction. We predict clearly resolvable Shapiro plateaus in experimentally accessible current and voltage regimes for double-bilayer graphene and, in the low-density regime, double-layer transition-metal dichalcogenides. Moreover, by tuning the density across the BCS-BEC crossover we show that the Shapiro response acquires a distinct nonmonotonic evolution. The symmetry of the order parameter is of the $d$-wave type. Application of the bias voltage increases the superconducting transition temperature. ### [404] [Magnetic-Free Quantum Interference and Universal Josephson Diode Effect Driven by a Supercurrent Gauge Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23479)
*Haowei Ye,Wenxue He,Kaixuan Fan,Yingpeng Zhang,Shijin Li,Yu Pan,Dechao Geng,Fan Yang,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Hechen Ren*

Method: 在Bi₂O₂Se和双层石墨烯（bilayer graphene）制备的平面约瑟夫森结中，通过高动能电感超导体（high-kinetic-inductance superconductors）和新型器件结构产生并放大超流规范场（supercurrent gauge field, SGF），建立其与磁场的物理等价性，从而替代磁场实现超流干涉控制。

Result: 证明了JDE是约瑟夫森效应的普遍内禀属性；实现了无外磁场的超流干涉控制；揭示了一种普遍的、无磁场JDE机制；实验演示了基于SGF的无磁场相敏技术，用于构建和表征有限动量超导性（finite-momentum superconductivity）。

Abstract: The Josephson effect, a hallmark of superconducting phase coherence, drives modern quantum technologies. However, Josephson-based quantum interference has hitherto been tethered to magnetic fields, despite phase coherence being a quintessential, intrinsic trait of superconductivity. Moreover, the Josephson diode effect (JDE) is typically viewed as an anomalous phenomenon indicative of broken symmetries in exotic phases of matter. Here, in planar Josephson junctions made with $\mathrm{Bi}_2\mathrm{O}_2\mathrm{Se}$ and bilayer graphene, we demonstrate that the JDE is a missing universal property of the Josephson effect. Simultaneously, we present an all-electric technology that replaces magnetic flux for controlling and measuring supercurrent interference. Central to our approach is a supercurrent gauge field (SGF), generated and amplified through high-kinetic-inductance superconductors and novel device architectures. By establishing the physical equivalence between the SGF and a magnetic field, we eliminate the reliance on external fields in quantum interference and reveal a universal, field-free JDE mechanism with broad implications for detecting broken-symmetry states. Finally, we show that the SGF offers capabilities beyond those of a conventional magnetic field by experimentally demonstrating a magnetic-free, phase-sensitive technique to construct and characterize finite-momentum superconductivity, opening new frontiers for exploring novel phases of matter and superconducting quantum architectures.

### [405] [Anomalous charge density wave in a two-dimensional superatomic superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23490)
*Boqin Song,Shuaishuai Sun,Zhongxu Wei,Xinbo Wang,Xiaoping Ma,Kaifa Luo,Lei Wang,Jun Deng,Xu Chen,Tian Qian,Shuya Xing,Zhihai Cheng,Jiangang Guo,Tianping Ying,Xiaolong Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究报告在二维超原子超导体Au₆Te₁₂Se₈中发现了一系列反常电荷密度波（CDW）行为：其CDW由横声子主导，伴随约4Å的超高实空间位移；在微米级厚度下仍表现出奇异的维度响应；CDW转变温度从体相的<2K急剧提升至接近“超原子极限”时的110K。该反常CDW与超导态之间的竞争为探索非常规电子-声子相互作用开辟了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电荷密度波（CDW）是一种与超导、量子霍尔态等共存的基态量子态，传统CDW由纵声学声子介导、晶格畸变仅在皮米量级且接近原子极限时消失。本文旨在探索超越这些常规特征的新型CDW行为，特别是在超原子材料体系中。

Method: 采用液氦温度透射电子显微镜（cryo-TEM）、超快泵浦-探针光谱（ultrafast pump-probe spectroscopy）和输运测量（transport measurements）等手段，对二维超原子超导体Au₆Te₁₂Se₈中的CDW行为进行表征。

Result: 发现该材料中CDW由横声子（transverse phonons）主导，实空间位移高达约4 Å（远超传统的皮米量级）；在微米级厚度下仍保持维度响应；CDW转变温度从体相的<2 K急剧提升至接近“超原子极限”时的110 K。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了CDW和超原子材料的新面貌，反常CDW与超导性的竞争为探索非常规电子-声子相互作用（unconventional electron-phonon interactions）提供了新途径。

Abstract: The spatial modulation of electron density into a wave-like pattern, known as charge density wave (CDW), represents a fundamental quantum state that often coexists with superconductivity, quantum Hall states, axion insulating phases and etc. Conventional CDWs are mediated by longitudinal acoustic phonons, exhibit picometer-scale lattice distortions ($10^{-12}$--$10^{-11}$ m), and typically vanish approaching the atomic limit. Here, we report a series of anomalous CDW behaviors in the 2D superatomic superconductor Au$_6$Te$_{12}$Se$_8$. Remarkably, its CDW is governed by transverse phonons, accompanied by an extraordinarily high real-space displacement of $\sim 4$ Ångström. Furthermore, we observe an exotic dimensional response persisting up to micrometer-scale thickness, a regime where other materials are already considered as bulk. Through liquid helium-temperature transmission electron microscopy, ultrafast pump-probe spectroscopy and transport measurements, we demonstrate a dramatic enhancement of the CDW transition temperature ($T_{\text{CDW}}$) from $<2$ K in the bulk to 110 K in approaching the ``superatomic limit''. Our findings not only reveal novel facets of both CDW and superatomic materials, but the competition between this anomalous CDW and superconductivity opens avenues for exploring unconventional electron-phonon interactions.

</details>


### [406] [Influence of Harris disorder on quantum-critical superconductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23582)
*Serhii Kryhin,Peter Lunts,Aavishkar A. Patel,Subir Sachdev,Pavel A. Nosov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文研究了量子临界金属中由哈里斯无序（Harris disorder）引起的局域化过阻尼玻色子模如何诱导配对不稳定性。通过实空间线性化Usadel方程、数值求解、自洽玻恩近似（self-consistent Born approximation）和Lifshitz尾分析方法，揭示了高温下形成紧凑超导液滴、低温下出现扩展配对本征态但受介观关联效应强烈影响的两种配对机制，其局域配对标度分布呈现幂律尾特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在赫兹理论（Hertz theory）描述的量子临界金属中，费米面与朗道阻尼玻色场（Landau-damped bosonic field）的耦合会产生非费米液体行为并增强库珀配对。然而，对称性保持的无序（即哈里斯无序）会局部地调谐系统趋近或远离临界点，导致有限密度的局域化低能玻色子模。需要理解这些局域化过阻尼玻色子模如何引发配对不稳定性及其具体机制。

Method: 从双粒子传播子的实空间线性化Usadel方程出发，推导出局域化玻色子波函数同时产生空间随机的配对顶点和库珀对的有效随机势。采用数值求解、自洽玻恩近似（self-consistent Born approximation）以及Lifshitz尾分析（Lifshitz-tail analysis）来研究配对不稳定性。

Result: 发现了两种配对不稳定性区域：高温时，配对在最局域化的玻色子模上成核形成紧凑的超导液滴（superconducting puddles）；低温时出现扩展配对本征态，但其转变尺度与空间结构仍受介观关联效应和局域化玻色子胶水（localized bosonic glue）中有利区域回返概率增强的强烈影响。局域配对标度的分布呈幂律尾（power-law tail），与无序BCS超导体中的拉伸指数尾（stretched-exponential tails）形成对比。

Conclusion: 该机制为量子临界金属中宽能隙不均匀性和超导液滴的形成提供了一条路径，并对铜氧化物超导体（cuprates）的扫描隧道显微镜（STM）测量结果提供了一种解释。

Abstract: In the Hertz theory, a quantum critical metal is described by the coupling of a Fermi surface to fluctuations of a Landau-damped bosonic field $φ$, which may represent either an order parameter or a Higgs field for a transition without symmetry breaking. Scattering from $φ$ produces non-Fermi-liquid behavior in the normal state, while the same fluctuations mediate enhanced Cooper pairing. By the Harris criterion, symmetry-preserving disorder couples most strongly to the coefficient of the $φ^2$ term, locally tuning the system toward or away from criticality. This random mass (``Harris disorder'') leads to a finite density of localized low-energy $φ$ modes even when the fermionic states remain extended and continue to provide Landau damping. We study the onset of pairing mediated by these localized overdamped bosonic modes. Starting from a real-space linearized Usadel equation for the two-particle propagator, we show that the localized bosonic wave functions generate both a spatially random pairing vertex and an effective random potential for Cooper pairs. Numerical solution, a self-consistent Born approximation, and Lifshitz-tail analysis reveal two regimes of the pairing instability. At high temperatures, pairing nucleates compact superconducting puddles on the most localized bosonic modes. At lower temperatures, an extended pairing eigenstate appears, but its transition scale and spatial structure remain strongly affected by mesoscopic correlation effects and enhanced probability of returns to favorable regions of the localized bosonic glue. The resulting distribution of local pairing scales has a power-law tail, in contrast to the stretched-exponential tails of disordered BCS superconductors. This mechanism provides a route to broad gap inhomogeneity and superconducting puddles in quantum-critical metals, and offers an interpretation of STM measurements of the cuprates.

</details>


### [407] [Reentrant superconductivity enabled by spin-orbit coupling: Application to UTe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23638)
*Changhee Lee,Nico A. Hackner,Daniel F. Agterberg,P. M. R. Brydon*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的理论机制来解释UTe₂中的再入超导现象（reentrant superconductivity），认为其源于子晶格自由度（sublattice degrees of freedom）与自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的相互作用，在强塞曼场（Zeeman field）下可显著增强反向自旋库珀配对（opposite-spin Cooper pairings），并指出具有B₃ᵤ对称性的配对态能够再现UTe₂再入超导态的高度各向异性相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有再入超导机制（如Jaccarino-Peter场补偿效应或配对相互作用强度变化）无法完全解释UTe₂的非凡相图，因此需要提出一种不依赖于磁性共存或磁量子临界点（magnetic quantum critical point）邻近性的普适理论。

Method: 采用解析处理方法（analytical treatment），研究子晶格自由度与自旋-轨道耦合的相互作用如何在强塞曼场下增强反向自旋库珀配对，并基于该结果构建具有B₃ᵤ对称性的配对态模型。

Result: 解析结果表明，再入超导的起源在于子晶格自由度与自旋-轨道耦合的共同作用，该机制可在强塞曼场下显著增强反向自旋库珀配对；基于该机制，B₃ᵤ对称性的配对态能够成功复现UTe₂再入超导态的高度各向异性相图。

Conclusion: 提出了一种不依赖磁性或磁量子临界点的再入超导普适理论，将UTe₂的异常相图归因于子晶格-自旋轨道耦合效应，为理解重费米子超导体（heavy-fermion superconductor）中的场增强配对现象提供了新视角。

Abstract: Reentrant superconductivity has been understood primarily in terms of the Jaccarino-Peter field-compensation effect or from a change of the strength in the pairing interaction. However, neither mechanism appears able to entirely explain the remarkable phase diagram of UTe$_2$. Here we propose a generic theory of the field-enhancement of opposite-spin Cooper pairings which does not necessitate the coexistence of magnetism or the vicinity of a magnetic quantum critical point. Our analytical treatment shows that the reentrance has its origin in the interplay of the sublattice degrees of freedom and spin-orbit coupling, which can can strikingly enhance opposite-spin Cooper pairings at strong Zeeman fields. Based on these results, we show that a pairing state with B$_{3u}$ symmetry can reproduce the highly anisotropic phase diagram of the reentrant superconducting state of UTe$_2$.

</details>

### [408] [Constituency Optimisation Through Hamiltonian Representation Of Mandates (COTHROM): Algorithmic Redistricting of Irish Election Boundaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20637)
*Ruaidhrí Campion,Matthew Fenlon,Joshua Cooney Mercedal,Casey Farren-Colloty,Eliza Somerville,Michael A. J. Mitchell*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了爱尔兰比例代表制-单一可转移票（PR-STV）选举重划选区的首个计算框架，利用统计物理学的Potts哈密顿量建模宪法目标，结合马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）与模拟退火进行优化，并通过多准则决策分析（MCDA）和帕累托最优性解决目标权重模糊性问题。在科克郡的实验中，COTHROM方法在比例代表性和紧凑性目标上持续优于现有法定选区边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 爱尔兰PR-STV选举制度下的选区重划面临巨大配置空间中选择最优代表边界的挑战，而“代表性”涉及多个相互冲突的宪法目标之间的微妙平衡。现有方法缺乏能够系统量化并优化多重宪法要求的计算框架。

Method: 将选区重划问题映射为统计物理学框架，宪法目标作为Potts哈密顿量（Potts Hamiltonian）中的各项；使用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo, MCMC）方法和模拟退火（simulated annealing）最小化该目标函数，并以耦合常数作为目标权重的代理变量；最后采用多准则决策分析（Multi Criterion Decision Analysis, MCDA）和帕累托最优性（Pareto Optimality）解决不同权重组合选择的不确定性问题。

Result: 在科克郡（County Cork）的实证评估中，COTHROM方法在比例代表性（proportional representation）和紧凑性（compactness）目标上，针对一系列目标权重均持续优于现有的法定选区边界。

Conclusion: 该计算框架首次为爱尔兰选举重划提供了系统优化多重要求并量化权衡的途径，验证了统计物理学方法在选区边界优化问题中的有效性。

Abstract: Electoral redistricting in Ireland's Proportional Representation Single Transferable Vote (PR-STV) system faces the challenge of selecting an optimally representative set of electoral boundaries from an enormous set of possible configurations, and where ``representative'' is a delicate balance of constitutional objectives that are often in tension with one another. We present the first computational framework for Irish electoral redistricting that systematically optimises across multiple constitutional requirements while making trade-offs explicit and quantifiable. The electoral redistricting problem is parsed using statistical physics, where constitutional objectives are considered as terms in a Potts Hamiltonian. Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) methods and simulated annealing are employed to minimise this objective function, systematically exploring this configuration space, with coupling constants as proxies for objective weightings. Multi Criterion Decision Analysis (MCDA) and Pareto Optimality is then utilised to remedy the ambiguity in choosing a certain objective weighting combination over others. With respect to proportional representation and compactness objectives evaluated in County Cork, COTHROM consistently improves on the existing legal constituency boundaries for a range of objective weightings.

</details>


### [409] [SVGym (SciVerseGym): An Environment for Reinforcement Learning and Bayesian Optimization in Crystal Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22425)
*Bin Cao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 SciVerseGym——一个兼容 Gymnasium 的闭环晶体发现环境，将晶体设计形式化为马尔可夫决策过程（Markov decision process），支持通过强化学习、贝叶斯优化、进化搜索和语言代理等多种工作流进行顺序晶体发现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管机器学习原子间势能（machine-learned interatomic potential）已能实现高效的原子尺度材料评估，但闭环晶体搜索（closed-loop crystal search）方法仍分散在各类专用流程中，缺乏统一、可复现且可扩展的测试平台。

Method: 将晶体设计形式化为马尔可夫决策过程（Markov decision process, MDP）：代理观测原子结构，执行具有化学意义的编辑操作，并从可配置评估器接收反馈。支持局部与全局操作（元素替换、晶格扰动、原子位移、空位创建、原子插入）、可配置化学空间、结构池、基于原子和图（graph-based）的观测、自定义奖励、可选弛豫（relaxation）以及稳定性或声子（phonon）相关诊断。每一步返回标准 (obs, reward, terminated, truncated, info) 元组。

Result: SciVerseGym 实现了代理逻辑与材料基础设施的解耦，为强化学习（reinforcement learning）、贝叶斯优化（Bayesian optimization）、进化搜索（evolutionary search）以及语言代理（language-agent）工作流在闭环晶体发现中提供了开放、可复现且可扩展的测试平台。代码已开源。

Conclusion: SciVerseGym 填补了闭环晶体搜索领域缺乏统一环境的空白，通过解耦代理与材料计算基础设施，有望推动基于机器学习的自动化晶体发现方法的发展。

Abstract: Machine-learned interatomic potentials now enable efficient atomistic evaluation for interactive materials discovery, yet closed-loop crystal search methods remain fragmented across bespoke pipelines for editing, relaxation, scoring, constraints, and bookkeeping. We introduce SciVerseGym, a Gymnasium-compatible environment for sequential crystal discovery that frames crystal design as a Markov decision process. Agents observe an atomistic structure, apply chemically meaningful edits, and receive feedback from a configurable evaluator. SciVerseGym supports local and global actions, including elemental substitution, lattice perturbation, atomic displacement, vacancy creation, and atom insertion, along with configurable chemical spaces, structure pools, atomistic and graph-based observations, custom rewards, optional relaxation, and stability or phonon-related diagnostics. Each step applies an edit, evaluates the candidate using a machine-learned interatomic potential or any ASE-compatible calculator, and returns the standard (obs, reward, terminated, truncated, info) tuple. By decoupling agent logic from materials infrastructure, SciVerseGym provides an open, reproducible, and extensible testbed for reinforcement learning, Bayesian optimization, evolutionary search, and language-agent workflows in closed-loop crystal discovery. Code is available at: https://github.com/Bin-Cao/SciVerseGym.

</details>
